Ubuqhophololo beSitrato saseBerners benziwa ngumbhali uTheodore Hook eWestminster (ngoku eyinxalenye yeLondon) ngowe-1810. Emva kweeveki eziliqela zokulungiselela wenza ubhejo oluzenzekelayo nomhlobo wakhe ukuba unokuguqula nayiphi na indawo ibe yeyona dilesi kwathethwa ngayo eLondon. UHook uchithe iiveki ezintandathu ethumela phakathi kwewaka elinesine iileta eziya kubarhwebi kunye namashishini eodola ukuhanjiswa kwempahla kunye neenkonzo zabo kwi-54 Berners Street, eWestminster, ngamaxesha ahlukeneyo ngomhla wama-27 kuNovemba 1810. Abantu abaliqela abaziwayo nabo bamenywa ukuba bafowunele kule dilesi, kuquka noosihlalo beBhanki yaseNgilani kunye neNkampani yase-East India, iDuke yaseLondon yaseGlouce Mayorce. 

UHook nabahlobo bakhe baqeshe amagumbi kwindlu ejongene nenombolo 54 ukuze bajonge inkqubo. Ukutshayela itshimini kwaqalisa ukufika kwidilesi ngeye-5:00 kusasa ngolo suku, kulandelwa ngamakhulu abameli bezorhwebo namashishini aliqela, kuquka abo bathengisa iifandesi, abangcwabi, abathengisa ukutya, abaxheshi, ababhaki, abapheki neengcaphephe zokudanisa; Ukuhanjiswa kwempahla kuquka amalungu omzimba, ifanitshala, amalahle, amaqebengwana omtshato, ukutya, iziselo kunye nebhokisi. Amapolisa abiziwe ukuba azame ukulawula isihlwele kodwa akakwazanga ukususa isitalato de kwaba semva kokuthontelana kokugqibela kweendwendwe ngo-5:00 pm: abasebenzi basekhaya abacinga ukuba baza kudliwano-ndlebe ukuze bafumane umsebenzi. 

UHook wayengachazwanga ngelo xesha, kodwa wavuma ukubandakanyeka kwakhe kwinoveli ye-semi-autobiographical epapashwe kwiminyaka engamashumi amabini anesihlanu emva kwesiganeko. Inkohliso yaphindwa kwiBritani yonke naseParis, kwaye yaphinda yaxelwa eqongeni, ngengoma kunye nangabazobi bekhathuni. 

Imvelaphi kunye nokwakha-up 
Etching of Hook abaneminyaka ejikeleze 22. Unxiba ilokhwe ye-regency kwaye ujonge ngqo kumbukeli. 
Theodore Hook, umenzi wobuqhinga, c. Ngo-1810 
uTheodore Hook wayengumbhali wee-comic operas kunye neefarces zeqonga kunye nombhali weenoveli ezininzi. Wayenecala elikhohlakeleyo kwindalo yakhe kwaye wayesaziwa njenge-prankster kunye ne-hoaxer.[1] Umbhali-mbali uJudith Flanders uphawula ukuba wayesaziwa kakhulu ngeziqhulo zakhe ezisebenzayo njengoko wayesaziwa ngokubhala kwakhe.[2] Ngexesha le-Berners Street hoax wayeneminyaka engama-22 ubudala. 

Ucwangciso lukaHook ngobuqhetseba lwaqala ngo-Oktobha 1810, kwiiveki ezintandathu ngaphambi kokuba kwenzeke eso siganeko, yaye wayenabahlobo ababini ababeza kuncedisa kulo.[4] Akwaziwa ukuba ngoobani abo wayehamba nabo—indoda nebhinqa—kodwa kucingelwa ukuba omnye wabo kamva waba ngumdlali weqonga odumileyo.[5] Inani elikhulu leeleta zathunyelwa kubarhwebi, abathengisi kunye nabaziwayo kusetyenziswa izizathu ezahlukeneyo; Uqikelelo lwenani loonobumba luyahluka ukusuka "kwiwaka ubuncinane"[6] ukuya kumawaka amane.

Iingqinisiso ezisetyenzisiweyo zitshintshile kuxhomekeke ekubeni ngubani owayeqhagamshelwana naye, kodwa zonke zinemiyalelo efanayo: ukubiza uNksk Tottenham, umhlali we-54 Berners Street. abanye bayalele isithuthi, besithi "ucela ukuba i-post-chaise kunye [namahashe] amane abe sekhaya ... ukuze amdlulisele kwinqanaba lokuqala eliya eBhafini". Amanqaku awayesiya koosomashishini afundeka ukuba “wayenqwenela ukuthetha naye ngomcimbi obalulekileyo”;[8] inguqulelo eyathunyelwa kubafundisi-ntsapho bomdaniso yabacela “ukuba bambize ngomso, phakathi kweyure yesibini neyesithathu, njengoko enqwenela ukuba iintombi zakhe zifumane imiyalelo”.[9] Kuthunyelwe iileta koosihlalo beBhanki yaseNgilane kunye ne-East India Company becela ukuba batsalele umnxeba ukuva iinkcukacha zobuqhophololo obuchaphazela imibutho yabo. UMlawuli waseGloucester wathunyelwa incwadi emcela ukuba aye kukhuko lokufa lomgcini wosapho. 

NgoNovemba 1810 Hook kunye nomhlobo babehamba phantsi Berners Street xa walatha, ebonakala ngokungakhethiyo, kwindlu ngenombolo 54 kwaye babheje ukuba angenza ipropathi eyona dilesi ekuthethwa ngayo eLondon. Umhlobo wakhe wamkhwelisa ebhejini kwaye ibheji yayilungiselelwe igwini elinye. 

Isiganeko 
Umboniso oqikelelweyo ukususela kumhla wenkohliso. ISitrato saseBerners sigcwele iikhareji, oosomashishini, abarhwebi, abafana abahambisa iimpahla kunye nababukeleyo. 
IBerners Street hoax 
Hook kunye nabahlobo bakhe baqeshe amagumbi kwindlu ejongene ne-54 Berners Street ukuze babe nokujonga inkqubo yosuku.[2][13] Ngentsimbi yesi-5:00 kusasa nge-27 kaNovemba ka-1810 uthotho lwetshimini zokutshayela zankqonkqoza kumnyango wenombolo 54, zisithi babethunyiwe. Balandelwa liqela leenqwelwana zamalahle, ezizisa imithwalo yazo ukusuka kwiindawo zokuloba zasePaddington; ngaxeshanye, ishumi elinesibini lababhaki beza ukuza kuzisa amaqebengwana omtshato, kulandele uthotho lweebhutsi. [5] [6] [14] Ngokutsho kwe<em>The Times, zalandelwa “ziimpahla ezixhotyiswe ngeenqwelo-mafutha, amalungu, ipiyanoforte, ilinen, izacholo kunye nayo yonke enye inkcazelo yefanitshala, [ezo] zafakwa kufutshane kangangoko kunokwenzeka kumnyango weNo. Ngalinye iliza elitsha labafikayo, isihlwele esasijikeleze loo mhlaba sasikhula, njengoko abaninzi babehleli bejonge ukuba ngubani oza kuba ngolandelayo. Oosihlalo beBhanki yaseNgilani kunye neNkampani yase-East India, kunye neNkosana yaseGloucester, bonke beza emini, njengoko kwenza umngcwabi ngebhokisi eyenziwe kwimilinganiselo kaNksk. 

Imephu yaseWestminster enophawu olubonisa indawo ye-54 Berners StreetMap yaseWestminster enophawu olubonisa indawo ye-54 Berners Street54 Berners Street 
Indawo eqikelelweyo ye-54 Berners Street, London
Ukongezelela kubathengisi beentlanzi abangamashumi amane—abafike bephethe iikreyifishi necod—kunye neebhula ezingamashumi amane, ngamnye enomlenze wegusha, kwakukho abapheki bepastry abangamashumi amahlanu nabangama-2 500 ee raspberry tarts. UJoshua Smith, iNkosi uSodolophu waseLondon-enxibe iimpahla ezipheleleyo kwaye ekhwele kwinqwelo yakhe esemthethweni-wajika, kodwa akazange ayeke. Endaweni yoko waya kwiNkundla kaMantyi yaseMarlborough ukuze amapolisa athunyelwe kwindawo yexhwayelo. [5] [10] [18] Ngokutsho kwengxelo yeThe Times, njengoko amagosa ayefika kwiSitrato saseBerners afumana “amadoda amathandathu angqwabalala ephethe ilungu elithile, ejikelezwe ngabagcini bewayini abaneemvume, abachebi beenwele beneewigi, abenzi be<em>mantua bephethe iibhokisi zomculo, [kunye] noogqirha bamehlo bephethe izinto ezahlukahlukeneyo zorhwebo”.[15] I<em>Morning Post nayo yanikela ingxelo ngaba bazimasi balandelayo: “ababekho, abadwebi bamazinyo, abapeyinti abancinci, abazobi bazo zonke iinkcazo, abadayisi, abangcwabi, abathengisa ukutya, abarhwebi, abarhwebi, abakhweli, iinkukhu, imivundla, amahobe, & c”.[19] Ukuzama ukunqanda le meko, amapolisa avala zombini iziphelo zesitrato, kodwa abantu baqhubeka bejika ukuze baqeshwe, kuquka, ngo-5: 00 ntambama, inani elikhulu labasebenzi basekhaya, bonke ababecinga ukuba baza kudliwano-ndlebe ukuze bafumane umsebenzi.[15][20] Akuzange kube kudala emva kokuba kumnyama apho iindwendwe zayeka ukujika zaza izihlwele zachithakala. 

Emva kwesiphumo 
Amapolisa akhangela umenzi kwaye wafumana umvuzo, kodwa akazange aphumelele.[21] Hook wacinga ukuba bubulumko ukushiya isixeko kwaye bachitha iiveki ezimbalwa emaphandleni.[6] Ngo-1812 uHook warhanelwa ngobuqhetseba; wavuma kuyo kwinoveli yakhe yowe-1835 yesemi-autobiographical uGilbert Gurney 

[T]apha akukho nto ifana nolonwabo – yintoni enye eyenza isiphumo kwiBerner's Street? Ndiyindoda - ndiyenzile ... khuphela isiqhulo, kwaye siyayeka ukuba sinye; -Nasiphi na isidenge sinokuxelisa umzekelo xa usekiwe - kodwa kwimvelaphi yengcinga kunye noyilo, ndicinga ukuba yayigqibelele. 

Inkohliso yaphindaphindwa kwezinye izixeko zaseBritani naseParis. [23] Yaba ngumthombo wempembelelo yeebaladi ezihlekisayo kunye neekhathuni kwaye yabhekiswa kwiipantomime iminyaka eliqela.[24] Emva kokufa kukaHook ngowe-1841 umhlobo wakhe uNancy Matthews—umfazi womdlali weqonga uCharles Matthew—wathi yayingenguye uHook owayenoxanduva lobu buxoki kodwa “indoda eselula, ngoku ... Uqhube wathi ngelixa uHook engazange enze inkohliso kwiSitalato saseBerners, wayekhe wenza iprank efanayo kwisikali esincinci eBedford Street. 

Akuzange kubekho inkcazo malunga nokuba kutheni le nkohliso yenziwe, okanye ukukhethwa kukaNkskz Tottenham-ibhinqa elisisityebi elinobume bentlalontle-njengexhoba leziganeko. [24] [7] UGraeme Harper, ebhala kwiOxford Dictionary of National Biography ngo-2008, uthi ukhetho lwenziwa ngamabona-ndenzile.[1] Umlobi weendaba kunye nombhali uRobert Chambers wabhala ngo-1879 ukuba kwakukho uburhalarhume phakathi kukaNksk Tottenham kunye noHook kunye nabahlobo bakhe, kodwa abazange banike iinkcukacha.




uheodore Edward Hook (22 Septemba 1788 – 24 Agasti 1841) wayeliNgesi ingqondi nomqambi kwaye ngokufutshane wayengumsebenzi waseburhulumenteni eMauritius. Waziwa kakhulu ngeziqhulo zakhe ezisebenzayo, ngakumbi iBerners Street hoax ngo-1810. Iposikhadi yokuqala yehlabathi yafunyanwa nguHook ngo-1840; kusenokwenzeka ukuba wayithumela kuye. 

Ubomi 
bokuqala 
uHook wazalelwa eCharlotte Street, eBedford Square, eLondon. Uyise, uJames Hook (1746–1827), wayengumqambi; umkhuluwa wakhe, okwabizwa ngokuba nguJames Hook (1771–1828), waba yiDini yaseWorcester. 

Wachitha unyaka kwisikolo saseHarrow waza emva koko waphumelela imatriki kwiYunivesithi yaseOxford. Uyise wayonwabile ekuboniseni izipho zenkwenkwe zomculo kunye ne-metrical, kwaye i-precocious Theodore yaba sisilwanyana segumbi eliluhlaza. Xa wayeneminyaka eyi-16, edibene noyise, wafumana impumelelo emangalisayo kunye ne-The Soldier's Return, i-comic opera, kwaye ilandele uthotho lwamalinge athandwayo noJohn Liston kunye noCharles Mathews, kuquka noTekeli. 

UHook ke waba ngumdlali odlalayo kunye neqhula elisebenzayo elaziwa kakhulu ngeBerners Street hoax ngo-1810 apho walungiselela intaphane yabarhwebi, kunye nezinto eziphawulekayo ezifana neNkosi uSodolophu waseLondon, iRhuluneli yeBhanki yaseNgilani, uSihlalo we-East India Company kunye noDuke waseGloucester ukutyelela uNksk. iveki. 

Enye i-prank ephawulekayo yeHook yadlalwa kumdlali we-Robert ("Romeo") uCoates, kwiminyaka embalwa kamva. I-Prince Regent ngelo xesha yayibambe "udumo lobungangamsha obugqwesileyo" eCarlton House, kunye noCoates "kuzuko lwakhe- ebulala uShakespeare eHaymarket"; belinganisa umbhalo weChamberlain, uHook wavelisa itikiti "eyalela ubukho bukaSignor Romeo" kwaye, enxibe i-livery ebomvu ecikizekileyo, wazisa esi simemo simnandi kodwa singeyonyani kuCoates ngokobuqu. UHook walinda ukuze abukele uCoates ekhwela umsitho kwinqwelo yakhe, "ethobela yonke into yakhe entle, ngekrele elinqatyisiweyo ledayimani kunye nomoya kaLouis le Grand". UCoates wamenywa ukuba angene, kodwa ekuvavanyeni itikiti "waxelelwa ngokuchubekileyo ukuba kwenzeke impazamo", wajika. Emva kokuba eyindulule inqwelo yakhe, kwanyanzeleka ukuba alinde kwisikhululo senqwelo saseHackney. INkosana, ibandakanyeka ngokungaziyo kwi-prank kaHook, yazisola ngokuba uCoates ejikiwe, embona ukuba "yindoda ekhohlakeleyo", kwaye ephawula ukuba "ubukho bakhe bunokuzothusa uninzi lweendwendwe, kwaye akukho mntu unokwenzakalisa." INkosana yathumela unobhala wayo kusuku olulandelayo, wamema uCoates ukuba eze kujonga “amalungiselelo nezihombiso” ezazisahleli; UCoates wahamba ngokufanelekileyo. Kwaphawulwa ukuba, "ukumenzela ubulungisa", Hook, ekuyibaliseni kwakhona,"Andizange ndithethe ibali ngaphandle kweempawu ezithile.
"Andizange ndithethe ibali ngaphandle kweempawu ezithile. 
Umsebenzi
Wahlala eSt Mary Hall, kwiYunivesithi yaseOxford, wemka emva kwamaxesha amabini ukuze aqhubeke nobomi bakhe bangaphambili. Isipho sakhe sokuphucula iingoma sithande uMlawuli oyiNkosana ukuba enze isibhengezo sokuba kukho into emayenzelwe uHook, owaqeshwa njengomgcini-mali jikelele kunye nonondyebo waseMauritius ngomvuzo we-£ 2,000 ngonyaka (i-£ 142,325; i-US $ 194,771 ngokwemiqathango ye-2021). Wayebubomi kunye nomphefumlo wesiqithi ukusuka ekufikeni kwakhe ngo-Okthobha 1813, kodwa intsilelo enkulu yafunyanwa kwi-akhawunti ye-treasury ngo-1817, kwaye wabanjwa waza waziswa eNgilani ngetyala lolwaphulo-mthetho. Isixa esimalunga ne-£12,000 (£1,054,500; US$1.44 yezigidi ngokwemiqathango ye-2021) yatsalwa ngusekela-gosa, kwaye iHook yabanjwa uxanduva. 


Hook, c. Ngo-1810 
Ngexesha lokuphononongwa kwebhodi yophicotho, wayehlala ngokufihlakeleyo kwaye wazigcina ngokubhalela amaphephancwadi kunye namaphephandaba. Ngo-1820, wasungula iphephandaba uJohn Bull, intshatsheli yeToryism ephezulu kunye nomchasi okhohlakeleyo kaKumkanikazi uCaroline. Ukugxekwa okuchuliweyo kunye novelwano olungenalusini lukhusele ukusasazwa okukhulu, kwaye iHook ifumene, kunyaka wokuqala ubuncinci, ingeniso ye-£ 2,000. Kodwa ke, wabanjwa okwesibini ngenxa yetyala lakhe kurhulumente, engazange enze nzame zokulihlawula. 

Ngelixa wayevalelwe kwindlu yesiponji ukusuka kowe-1823 ukuya kowe-1825, wabhala imiqulu elithoba yamabali emva koko aqokelelwa phantsi komxholo othi IiNtetho neZinto (1824–1828). Ekuqaleni kwee-1820s, wanceda imvumi uMichael Kelly ukuba aqulunqe i-Reminiscences yakhe, equka iinkcukacha zokusebenza noMozart. Kwiminyaka engama-23 eseleyo yobomi bakhe, wagalela imiqulu engama-38 ngaphandle kwamanqaku, ama-squibs neziketshi. Iinoveli zakhe zinemihlathi ethe gqolo yokubalisa ngorhatyazo kunye nomfanekiso ocacileyo. Baquka uMaxwell (1830), umfanekiso womhlobo wakhe uMfundisi E. Cannon; Uthando nekratshi (1833); i-autobiographical uGilbert Gurney (1835) kunye noGurney Married (1838); UJack Brag (1837) kunye noPeregrine Bunce (1842). Akazange awugqibe umsebenzi wobomi bukaCharles Mathews. Inoveli yakhe yokugqibela ibiyiyokuzalwa, imitshato kunye noKufa (1839). 

Elona khadi leposi lidala ehlabathini lathunyelwa eHook ngo-1840, [1] liphethe isitampu sikaPenny Black. I-Hook mhlawumbi idale kwaye yathumela ikhadi kuye njengehlaya elisebenzayo kwinkonzo yeposi, ekubeni umfanekiso ufana ne-caricature yabasebenzi beposi. Kwi-2002, ikhadi leposi lithengiswa ngerekhodi ye-£ 31,750. 

Kamva ubomi nokufa 
Umsebenzi wayesele eqalisile ukuhlawula impilo yakhe xa Hook wabuyela kwimikhwa yakhe yakudala kunye nomzamo elide lokudibanisa ishishini kunye nokutshatyalaliswa kwaphumela ekuvunyweni ukuba wenziwa kwi-purse, engqondweni nasemzimbeni, ekugqibeleni. Wabhubhela ekhaya eFulham ngomhla wama-24 kuAgasti 1841 eneminyaka engama-52 ubudala. Akazange atshate kodwa wayehlala noMary Anne Doughty; babenabantwana abathandathu.

IHook ikhunjulwa njengomnye wamanani aqaqambileyo ngamaxesha aseGeorgia. Ukhuthaze abalinganiswa bakaLucian Gay kwinoveli kaBenjamin Disraeli ethi Coningsby kunye noMnu Wagg kwiVanity Fair kaThackeray. Isimbo sakhe sabhalwa phantsi ngabantakwethu bakwaSmith kwiiDilesi eziYaliweyo (1812). UColeridge wamncoma ngokuthi "unyanisekile njengengqondo njengoDante". 













Ngommandla obanzi waseLondon, bona iSixeko saseWestminster. Ngolunye usetyenziso, jonga iWestminster (disambiguation). 
IWestminster 

Westminster yeyona ndawo iphambili yokuhlala kwiSixeko saseWestminster kuMbindi weLondon, eNgilani. Isuka kuMlambo iThames ukuya kwisitalato iOxford kwaye ineendawo ezininzi ezidumileyo, kubandakanya iBhotwe laseWestminster, iBuckingham Palace, iWestminster Abbey, iWestminster Cathedral, iTrafalgar Square kunye noninzi lweziko lenkcubeko laseWest End kubandakanya indawo yokuzonwabisa yaseWest End theatre. 

Igama (IsiNgesi sakudala: Westmynstre) [1] lisuka kwinkcazo engacwangciswanga yecawe ye-abbey kunye neyobukhosi obukhethekileyo beSt Peter's (Westminster Abbey), kwintshona yesiXeko saseLondon (kude kube kuHlaziyo lwamaNgesi kukwakho ne-Eastminster abbey, kwelinye icala leSixeko saseLondon, kwi-East End yaseLondon). Imvelaphi ye-abbey isukela phakathi kwe-7th kunye ne-10th inkulungwane, kodwa yaphakama ukuya kwisikhundla esiphakamileyo xa yaphinda yakhiwa ngu-Edward uMvuma ngenkulungwane ye-11. Ngophuhliso lwebhotwe elidala ecaleni kwe-abbey, iWestminster ibilikhaya likarhulumente waseNgilani ukusukela malunga ne-1200, kwaye ukusukela ngo-1707 uRhulumente wase-United Kingdom. Ngowe-1539, yaba sisixeko. 

IWestminster ihlala isetyenziswa njengegama elithetha ukubhekisa kwiPalamente yase-United Kingdom, ehlala kwiBhotwe laseWestminster. 

IJografi 
yoBume beJografi 
ISixeko kunye neNkululeko yaseWestminster kunye namanye amacandelo olawulo eWestminster (ngaphandle kwesiXeko sanamhlanje esibanzi saseWestminster, iLondon Borough eyadalwa ngo-1965) yandiswa ukusuka kuMlambo iThames ukuya kwindlela endala yaseRoma ukusuka kwiSixeko ukuya kwintshona yeNgilani, ngoku ebizwa ngokuba yiOxford Street. 




Westminster ngaphambi kokufudukela ezidolophini. Indlela yaseRoma (iSitrato sanamhlanje iOxford) iboniswe phezulu ihamba ngasentshona. 
Isiqithi saseThorney silele phakathi kweengalo zoMlambo iTyburn wangaphambili ekudibaneni kwawo nomlambo iThames, ngelixa umda osentshona kunye neChelsea wasekwa nguMlambo iWestbourne owalahleka ngendlela efanayo. Umgca womlambo usabumba (nohlaziyo oluncinci kakhulu) imida yommandla wangoku kunye neRoyal Borough yaseKensington kunye neChelsea. 


Amarhamente kunye neNdawo zeSixeko kunye neNkululeko yaseWestminster. Umzantsi weWestbourne wenze inxenye yomda osentshona, kunye nesitalato iOxford esisemantla. 
Emantla, kude nomlambo, iWestminster ibandakanya umhlaba kumacala omabini eWestbourne,ngakumbi iKnightsbridge (kubandakanywa iindawo zeHyde Park kwintshona yechibi iSerpentine (ekuqaleni yayiyilwe ngokugrumba umlambo) kunye noninzi lweeGadi zaseKensington).


I-Westminster ibandakanya izithilana zaseSoho, eSt James, eMayfair, eCovent Garden (ekwabelwana ngayo neCamden engummelwane), iPimlico, iVictoria, iBelgravia kunye neKnightsbridge (ekwabelwana ngayo neKensington engummelwane). 

IsiXeko sangaphambili saseWestminster sadityaniswa neendawo ezingabamelwane zasePaddington kunye neMarylebone ngo-1965 ukuze zenze indawo enkulu yale mihla. Le mimandla ingabamelwane (ngaphandle kwendawo encinci yasePaddington kwinxalenye yeGadi yaseKensington), imi emantla eSitalato iOxford kunye nokuqhubekeka kwayo ngasentshona, iBayswater Road. 


















ISitrato saseBerners sikwindawo esemantla eSitrato iOxford kwisiXeko saseWestminster kwiWest End yaseLondon, eyaqala yaphuhliswa njengendawo yokuhlala phakathi kwenkulungwane ye-18 ngumakhi wepropathi uWilliam Berners, kwaye kamva yanikezelwa kwizakhiwo ezinkulu zorhwebo kunye nesiqingatha semizi-mveliso okanye iibhloko ezinkulu zeeflethi. Inobudlelwane noCharles Dickens, kwaye yayiyindawo yabenzi bezixhobo zomculo kubandakanya ipiyano kunye neehadi, kunye nefenitshala kunye nabenzi befilimu. 


ISitalato iBerners sibaleka malunga neemitha ezingama-315 kwicala elingasemantla ukusuka ekudibaneni kweSitalato iOxford kunye neWardour Street ukuya kuhlangana neMortimer Street (eyayifudula iyiCharles Street) kunye neSibhedlele sangaphambili saseMiddlesex (ngoku esibizwa ngokuba yiFitzroy Place). Isitrato silele kwindawo eyaziwa ngokuba yiFitzrovia kwaye sithathwa ngokwembali ukuba sise-East Marylebone. Imithi engamashumi amabini ananye yongezwa kwisitalato iBerners ngo-2012 


iBerners Street yaqala yaphuhliswa njengendawo yokuhlala yiBerners Estate phakathi kwinkulungwane yeshumi elinesibhozo. 

UJohn Slater, umhloli weBerners Estate, wabhala ngowe-1918

Ngomhla wama-21 kuMeyi ngo-1738, uWilliam Berners wavumela iminyaka engamashumi alithoba anesithoba ukuya kuThomas Huddle yonke i-frontage ye-655 yeenyawo ukuya kwi-Oxford Street kunye ne-100 yeenyawo ubunzulu (ngaphandle kobubanzi obufunekayo kwizitrato ezitsha ezimbini ezicetywayo - eziya kuba zizitrato zangoku zeBerners kunye neNewman kunye nokwandiswa kwe-Wells Lane) kwirenti epheleleyo ye-4s. ngenyawo ngonyaka. UHuddle wayeza kudiliza zonke izakhiwo ezidala aze akhe ezintsha, kwaye iBerners yayiza kwakha umjelo ohambisa amanzi amdaka ukusuka eWells Lane ukuya eRathbone Place. U-Huddle waqala ukwakha izindlu kwisitalato i-Oxford kwangoko, kwaye wabelwa apho irenti, irenti yokuqala yeminyaka engamashumi alithoba anesithoba yanikezelwa ngo-1739. Iyonke irenti yonyaka efunyenwe lilifa lezindlu ze-Oxford Street yayiyi-£135 8s. de kwawa okokugqibela kwingqeshiso endala ngo-1838. Umjelo ophantsi komhlaba ohambisa amanzi amdaka ekubhekiselwa kuwo usahamba ngaphantsi kwezinye izindlu ezikwiSitalato iBerners Street neWells, kodwa ngoku awusasetyenziswa. Phakathi kwe-1750 kunye ne-1763 izitrato ezikhoyo kwi-Estate zandlalwa: indawo yokuqala eyanikezelwa kwi-Newman Street ibhalwe ngo-1750, e-Charles Street, ngoku ebizwa ngokuba yi-Mortimer Street, ngo-1759, e-Castle Street nase-Wells Street ngo-1760, e-Berners Street ngo-1763, kwaye ngoku kwiSakhiwo esise-1763, kwiSakhiwo sase-Suffolk, e-Suffolk. ngokukhawuleza, kuba ngo-1773 kwakukho izindlu ezigqityiweyo ezingamashumi amathandathu eBerners Street, amashumi amabini anesithathu eCastle Street, amashumi amathathu anesihlanu eMortimer Street, ngaphandle kweSibhedlele saseMiddlesex, amashumi alithoba kwisitalato saseNewman, namashumi amabini anesithathu eNassau Street. Uninzi lwezindlu lubonisa ngamandla impembelelo ka-Adam Brothers, kunye nezinye iisilingi, ezintle kakhulu, zaziphantse zivela kuyilo lwazo lokuqala. Isivumelwano seminyaka engama-999 sanikezelwa kwiSibhedlele saseMiddlesex ngo-1754 

u-Edward Walford, wabhala kwi-Old and New London (Umqulu 4), epapashwe ngo-1878 

Berners Street, ebizwa ngokuba yisihloko sosapho somnini-mhlaba, ubalekela emantla kancinane ukuya empuma yesitalato i-Wells. Yakhiwa malunga nombindi wenkulungwane edlulileyo, kwaye ibisoloko ibhiyozelwa njenge "khaya kunye nendawo yokuhlala" yamagcisa, abapeyinti kunye nabakroli. Phakathi kwabahlali bayo bangaphambili kuya kubalwa u-Opie, uFuseli, kunye noMhlekazi uWilliam Chambers, abo bokugqibela esele sibakhankanyile ngokunxulumene neSomerset House. UOpie wangcwatyelwa kwiCathedral yaseSt. Umfazi wakhe wesibini, u-Amelia, i-Quakeress efundileyo, wayesaziwa kakuhle ngemibhalo yakhe, "Amabali oBomi benene," "Imibongo," "iiNtsomi ezilula," njl. Kwesi sitrato yayiyibhanki apho uFauntleroy, umqambi, wayeliqabane 

uWalford erekhoda ukwanda kwamaziko esisa kunye nezonyango eBerners Street ngenkulungwane ye-19.

ISitrato saseBerners senza ikomkhulu lamaziko aliqela angaphandle kunye nesisa, amanye awo asekwa ukusukela kwinkulungwane edlulileyo. Ngo-1788 kwasekwa uMbutho woNcedo lwabahlolokazi kunye neeNkedama zaMadoda oNyango. I-Medical and Chirurgical Society yasungulwa kwi-1805, kwaye ifakwe kwi-1834, ukulima nokukhuthazwa kweyeza kunye nokuhlinzwa. Ibutho labantu linethala leencwadi elisemgangathweni, elinemiqulu emalunga nama-25,000. Apha, kwakhona, nguMbutho Wokubelekisa waseLondon, owasungulwa ngowe-1858; kunye noMbutho wePathological, owasekwa ngo-1846. Uluntu olunegama lokugqibela lwamiselwa umboniso kunye noviwo lwesampulu, imizobo, amalungiselelo e-microscopic, iisasti okanye imizekelo yamalungu agulayo, kunye neenkcazo ezibhaliweyo okanye zomlomo ezikhaphayo, ezibonisa inzululwazi yezifo. Zonke imibutho yezonyango ekhankanywe ngasentla, kunye nenye ebizwa ngokuba yi-Clinical Society yaseLondon, ihlaliswa kwindlu enye (Nombolo 53). Idityaniswe nesi sakhiwo (Nombolo 54) sisibhedlele iSt Peter's for Stone. Eli ziko lesisa lasekwa ngo-1860, kwaye injongo yalo kukuzuza inani elikhulu kangangoko kunokwenzeka abahluphekayo ngokubabonelela, ngaphandle kweleta yengcebiso, iingenelo ngendawo yokulala esibhedlele; ukuphucula ulwazi lwezonyango kunye notyando kwizifundo eziphathwa ngokukodwa apha, ngokuhlanganisa inani elikhulu lezigulana ezithwaxwa zezo zifo, kwaye ngaloo ndlela kunikezelwe ngamathuba oqwalaselo kunye nokuhlelwa; kwaye, kwiimeko zezigulana ezithwaxwa lilitye, ukuphanda ngeyona ndlela ilungileyo yokuphumeza ukususwa kwayo ngeyona ngozi incinci inokwenzeka kubomi besigulane, kwaye, nanini na kuyenzeka, kuthathelwe indawo lithotrity kwi-lithotomy. Inkqubo yesi sibhedlele ivuleleke kubo bonke abafundi kunye namalungu omsebenzi. KwiNombolo yama-22 kukho iiofisi zeLadies’ Sanitary Association, kwanoMbutho Wokukhuthaza Ukuqeshwa Kwamabhinqa. KwiNombolo ye-9 yiBerners Women's Club-enye yeemvavanyo zokuqala kule ndlela. Kwakwindlu enye kukho iiofisi zeKomiti ePhakamileyo yoMbutho weSizwe woLwaphulo-mthetho lwaManina. Umbutho waseLondon woKhuseleko lwezoRhwebo uneofisi yawo ekuNombolo 16. 

Uninzi lwala maziko avela kufutshane neSibhedlele saseMiddlesex.

Kwisitalato iCharles, encotsheni yeSitalato iBerners, imbono esezantsi apho iyalele, siSibhedlele saseMiddlesex. Isakhiwo, esenziwe ngezitena, kwaye sibanzi kakhulu, sineziko kunye namaphiko; ifakwe kwiibhafu, imisebenzi yaselabhoratri, i-shaft yokufaka umoya, kwaye, ngokwenene, zonke izixhobo eziyimfuneko zokuthuthuzela, njl. Isibhedlele siqale malunga neminyaka elishumi okanye engamashumi amabini emva kwesicelo esihle sikaThomas Guy, umthengisi weencwadi osweleyo weSitalato iLombard. Yasekwa okokuqala, ngo-1745, eWindmill Street, eTottenham Court Road, isenzelwa abantu abagulayo nabaziziqhwala, kunye nabafazi abatshatileyo abalele. Yasuswa, ngo-1755, kwindawo ekuyo ngoku, xa yema phakathi kwamasimi aluhlaza kunye neendlela. Ukusukela ngo-1807 abaguli ababebelekisa, ukuya kutsho kwinani eliphantse libe liwaka ngonyaka, endaweni yokuba bamkelwe njengamabanjwa, bazinyaswa kumakhaya abo ngamagosa onyango esibhedlele. Iiwadi zomhlaza zasekwa ngesipho se-£ 4,000 esivela kuMnumzane Samuel Whitbread, kwi-1807, apho ezinye izipho kunye nelifa zongezwa. Isiganeko esiphawulekayo kwimbali yesibhedlele kukuba kwi-1793 yaba yindawo yokusabela kuninzi lwabafuduki baseFransi abafudukayo abaxoshwa eFransi nguJacobin Reign of Terror. Izakhiwo zandiswa ngamaphiko amatsha akhiwa ngo-1775, kwakhona ngowe-1834. ULord Robert Seymour, umhlobo onenzondelelo nowongamileyo weli ziko, wafumana ngenxa yalo inkxaso yasebukhosini kaGeorge IV., eqhubeka nguKumkani wakhe ngoku. Isikolo sobugqirha, esasekwa ngowe-1835, sinodumo oluphakamileyo; ixhotyiswe ngemyuziyam yengqokelela yexabiso. Esi sibhedlele sineebhedi zezigulane ezingaphaya kwamakhulu amathathu. Kula mashumi mabini anesithandathu azinikele ekusungulweni komhlaza, owasungulwa ngonyaka we-1791, apho isigulane sivunyelwe ukuba sihlale "de kube sikhululekile ngobugcisa okanye sikhululwe ngokufa;" ezisibhozo zibekelwe abafazi abaphethwe zizifo ezingaqhelekanga ngokwesini sabo; intsalela yeebhedi ibekelwe bucala iimeko ezahlukeneyo ngokubanzi. Bangaphezulu kwamakhulu alithoba abasetyhini abatshatileyo abajongwa kwiindawo zabo zokuhlala, kwaye ishumi elinesibhozo lamawaka abaguli abangaphandle bayakhululeka minyaka le. Isibhedlele asinampahla. Umrhumo wonyaka ufikelela kwi-£ 2,355, ngelixa iminyaka edlulileyo inkcitho iye yandiswa ngemisebenzi eyimfuneko yokuphucula. Esi sibhedlele sibalwa phakathi koogqirha botyando kunye noogqirha abangamadoda agqwesileyo kwezonyango; ngaphandle koko ibe sisiqalo semisebenzi emininzi ebalaseleyo kutyando. 

U-Edward Walford uvusa into ethile yomoya wentengiso yesitrato kwikona yeSitalato iBerners kunye neCharles Street echazwe ngokucacileyo nguHenry Mayhew ngeminyaka yee-1840s kunye ne-50s.

Icala elisemazantsi eSitalato iCharles, esiqhubeleka nesitalato saseGoodge singene kwiNdlela yeNkundla yaseTottenham, sibonisa ukuxakeka, ngakumbi ngolwesiHlanu nangoMgqibelo ngokuhlwa; kwaye njengenye yeemakethi zezitrato ezimbalwa eziseleyo kwi-West-end, kwaye mhlawumbi imiselwe ukuba ingabikho xesha lide inyamalale, inokubanga isaziso esifutshane. Kuluhlu olude lwabagcini beevenkile kwicala labo elisemazantsi, ababonisa iindawo zabo zokugcina iintlanzi, iziqhamo, kunye nemifuno kwiibhasi eziphathwa ngesandla kunye neengobozi, nakumacwecwe ashukumayo, sinokusebenzisa amazwi kaHenry Mayhew:—“Indawo ekula macandelo inobume obungakumbi bokulunga kunentengiso. Isibane esizivelisayo segesi, okanye sikhanyiswa lilangatye elibomvu eliqhumayo lezibane zegrisi zamandulo; iye yaqengqeleka idiphu yakhe eshinyeneyo idyasi yephepha elimdaka, elivutha kude kunye nekhandlela elibomvu elinomlilo okhanyayo kwimingxuma engaphantsi kwesitovu se-chestnut esibhakiweyo, ngelixa abambalwa banekhandlela elikhanyayo ngesefa, kunye ne-sparkling ye-sparkling-grounds. ukuphaphazela emoyeni njengeeflegi zelangatye, kuthululele isikhukula sokukhanya, ukuba kumgama umoya ngokukhawuleza ngaphezu kwendawo uphazamisekile ngokungathi isitrato sivutha umlilo 
nge-2 Novemba 1756, uRichard Bathurst wahambisa ileta yakhe yokurhoxa kwiBhodi yeSibhedlele saseMiddlesex, ngaloo ndlela 
Madoda, Ukunyanzelwa yiMfuneko yokufumana iMicimbi yeJamica 

. ukuba ndibuye, ndicela ukuba ukususela ngolu suku niyithathele ingqalelo indawo yam eSibhedlele senu njengengenamntu Andinakwenza oku Madoda ngaphandle kokubuyisa umbulelo wam ongazenzisiyo ngoMahluko endinyulwe ngawo, uBubele endivumeleke ngabo ukungabikho kwam ngamaxesha athile, kunye neMibutho endiyifumeneyo ndiya kuhlala ndinqwenelela iProsperity eSibhedlele, kwaye abasayi kuphinda ndibange ngombulelo wakho. Madoda. Esona sicaka senu sinyanzelekileyo nesithobekileyo, uRichard Bathurst 
Isazi somlibo wokuzalwa uAnne M. Amandla ubhale uphononongo ngotshintshiselwano phakathi kwenkulungwane ye-18 yaseJamaica kunye neLondon ethengisayo kwincwadi yakhe kunye nebhlog ethi 'A Parcel of Ribbons', enika ingqiqo kwiSitrato saseBerners ngamaxesha obukoloniyali.



Xa uRobert Cooper Lee wabuyela eNgilani esuka eJamaica kunye nosapho lwakhe ekupheleni kuka-Agasti 1771, bahlala ixesha elifutshane kwiSitalato sase-Old Bond eLondon. Kodwa kwiiveki nje ezimbalwa uRobert wafumana indlu eBerners Street apho watyikitya isivumelwano sokuqeshisa iminyaka engamashumi amathathu. Namhlanje eBritani nabani na okwaziyo ukuthenga indlu ukwathenga indawo yasimahla kwaye ke ngoko ungumnini wendlu kunye nomhlaba emi kuwo. Ngenkulungwane ye-18 eLondon imeko enjalo yayingaqhelekanga. Nditsho nabantu abazizityebi bangatyikitya isivumelwano sokuqeshisa ngendlu ngayo nantoni na ukusuka kwiinyanga ezimbalwa (ukuya kwixesha lezentlalo laseLondon) ukuya kwixesha leminyaka. Iminyaka engamashumi amathathu yayiqhelekile kodwa inokuba nantoni na ukuya kwiminyaka engamashumi alithoba anesithoba. ILondon apho usapho lwakwa-Lee lwabuyela kuyo yande kakhulu kumashumi amabini eminyaka okoko uRobert emkile. Kwakukho iibhulorho ezimbini ezintsha ngaphaya kweThames – iBhulorho yaseWestminster eyayisakhiwa xa wayehamba yavulwa ngo-1750, iBhulorho iBlackfriars yavulwa ngo-1769. Ibhulorho yaseLondon ekugqibeleni yaphulukana nesiphithiphithi sayo sezindlu neevenkile zamaxesha aphakathi ngo-1757 yaza yafumana udonga olutsha olubukekayo lwaseItali. Ukongezelela kuphuhliso lweebhulorho ezintsha, iLondon yayisasazeka ngokukhawuleza ngaphandle, igubungela imimandla eyayingamabala nje kulutsha lukaRobert, yaye abemi banda besuka kwisiqingatha sesigidi ngowe-1750 ukuya kutsho kwisithathu kwikota yesigidi kwiminyaka engamashumi amabini kamva. Zakuba iindawo ezinefashoni ezifana neCovent Garden zehlile kwaye ngoku zazihlala amasela namahenyukazi. Abemi bazo bangaphambili bafudukela ngasentshona, yaye imimandla emikhulu esemantla nakumazantsi eSitrato iOxford yabona uphuhliso lwezitrato ezintle nezikwere, uninzi lwazo olusazigcinayo ubuncinane ezinye zezindlu zabo zaseGeorgia. ISitrato saseBerners sihamba ngee-engile ezichanekileyo ukuya kwisitalato iOxford, ngoko ngamanye amaxesha saziwa ngokuba yiOxford Road, kwaye ngelixa kamva safumana udumo njengendawo yamagcisa kunye nababhali, bekukho iqela leentsapho ezinonxibelelwano lwaseJamaican ezazihlala apho kwaye abahlali bayo babezizityebi ngokubanzi kwaye benxibelelene kakuhle. Ezi zindlu zazintsha - zintle, iiterras zaseGeorgia ezinokufikelela ngasemva kwizitali zazo ngeBerners Mews. Indlu kaLee ekwinani lamashumi amabini anesithandathu yachazwa njengenamagumbi aphezulu anomoya anomoya omninzi, amagumbi ezicaka kunye namagumbi amaninzi, igumbi lokuzoba elinomgangatho ophezulu kunye neqhekeza letshimini elihle kunye ne-stucco cornice, igumbi lokutyela elikhulu kunye nebhodi esecaleni, ithala leencwadi, iholo ephezulu yokungena, kunye neeofisi ezifanelekileyo ezihlonyelwe kakuhle, kwaye zibonelelwe ngamanzi; emele iinqwelo ezimbini, stabling amahashe amahlanu kunye eyomileyo arched cellaring. Imbali yophuhliso lwalo mmandla ibuyela kumbindi wenkulungwane yangaphambili xa, ngo-1654, uJosias Berners wathenga umhlaba kwirhamente yaseSt Marylebone nge-£970 kuSir Francis Williamson wase-Isleworth. Uphuhliso olukhulu lwenziwa kwisiqingatha sokuqala senkulungwane yeshumi elinesibhozo nguWilliam Berners, kwaye ke intsapho yanika igama layo kwisitrato.Usapho lakwaBerners ladityaniswa neJamaica izihlandlo ezithathu ngosapho lukaJarrett. Abazukulwana abathathu bakaWilliam Berners batshata noJarretts waseOrange Valley, eTrelawny – uMaria Berners watshata noHerbert Newton Jarrett (ongowesithathu kwelo gama), umntakwabo uWilliam watshata noRachel Allen Jarrett (owesibini kwelo gama) nomntakwabo uHenry Denny Berners watshata noSarah Jarrett. USarah noRachel babengoodade, uHerbert wayengumntakwabo omncinci kayise. Kodwa ukubuyela kwiSitrato saseBerners! Indlela eqhelekileyo yophuhliso kwinkulungwane yeshumi elinesibhozo yayikukuba umnini-mhlaba aqeshise ngomhlaba wophuhliso kubakhi abaqikelelwayo abaza kwakha iqela lezindlu ze baziqeshise kubaqeshi. Maxa wambi umakhi wayedla ngokugxumeka iqokobhe kuze kugqitywe uqweqwe lwangaphakathi ngomnye umntu, ngokufuthi phantsi kolwalathiso lwalowo uqeshe indlu. Kwakungekho mfuneko yokuhambelana kwinkangeleko yezindlu, nangona imfashini yemilinganiselo yeklasi ukuya kwinqanaba elithile yayikhuthaza. Ngokungafaniyo nanamhlanje akukho mvume yokucwangcisa ifunekayo kwaye bekukho imimiselo yokwakha embalwa ngokufanelekileyo ukulawula umgangatho wokwakha. Kwakukho imimiselo ephathelele umzekelo kwizinto zokwakha kunye nobubanzi bezitrato ezalandela ukusuka kuMlilo Omkhulu waseLondon ngowe-1666. Kungenxa yesi sizathu ukuba ezi zindlu zintle zaseGeorgia zazidla ngokwakhiwa ngezitena, umhlaba wezitena wembiwa ukusuka kwidiphozithi yodongwe enkulu kakhulu ejikeleze iLondon. Umzekelo idolophu encinci yaseWare eHertfordshire yayineendawo zezitena ezinkulu kunye nomzila olungileyo wokuthutha izitena eziya eLondon ngesikhephe esihla ngeLea navigation (ekupheleni kwayo namhlanje kumi iPaki yeOlimpiki). Phakathi kwabanini bomhlaba eMarylebone kwakukho iiDukes zaseChandos, zaseDevonshire nasePortland amagama abo akhunjulwayo namhlanje kwizitrato zayo kunye nezikwere. Unokufunda inkcazo yangoku yenkqubela phambili yale ndawo eyabhalwa ekupheleni kwenkulungwane ye-18 nguDaniel Lysons ogama lakhe lingumthombo wenkcazelo yaseLondon ngenkulungwane ye-18. Ubungakanani bokuhlaliswa kwendawo ngamalungu ePlantocracy bubonakaliswa ngamanani eerekhodi kwiirejista zerhamente yaseSt Marylebone, ngokubhaptizwa kwabo, imitshato kunye nokungcwatywa. Ethubeni kule nkulungwane aba bahlali bazizityebi bahamba ngokuthe ngcembe besiya emantla njengoko uphuhliso lwaluqhubeka phezu kweMarylebone Gardens endala, eyayikade iyindawo entle yokuhamba kodwa ngoku yoyiswa ziingeniso eziza kwenziwa kuphuhliso. Nditsho noRobert Cooper Lee waqhubeka. Nangona wasigcinayo isivumelwano sengqesho kwindlu yesitalato iBerners, wafudukela kwi-Bedford Square esanda kugqitywa, ekwahlala abantu baseJamaican ababesakuba ngabaxhamli abanjengoMarchant Tubb, kunye namalungu osapho lakwaHibbert. Nangona i-Bedford Square ... ihlala ingatshintshi kakhulu, indlu kaRobert Cooper Lee's Berners Street sele ihambile, kunye nekhulu le-18 leminyaka eLondon, yatshintshwa ngamagumbi ama-Victorian, athatyathwe ziibhombu ngexesha lemfazwe,yakhiwa kwakhona emva kwemfazwe kwaye yatshintshwa kwakhona yiglasi kunye neebhloko zentsimbi.

I-Berners Street Hoax 
Isitrato wanikwa udumo ngokuqhula okusebenzayo, okwaziwa ngokuba yi-Berners Street hoax, eyenziwa ngumbhali uTheodore Hook ngo-1810. [7] UHook wenze ubhejo kunye nomhlobo wakhe, uSamuel Beazley, ukuba unokuguqula nayiphi na indlu eLondon ibe yeyona dilesi ithethwa kakhulu ngeveki, awayizuza ngokuthumela amawaka eeleta egameni likaNksk Tottenham, owayehlala e-54 Berners Street, ecela ukuhanjiswa, iindwendwe, kunye noncedo. UHook wazimisa endlwini ejongene ngqo ne-54 Berners Street, apho yena nomhlobo wakhe bachitha imini yonke bebukele isiphithiphithi esasisenzeka. Indawo eku-54 Berners Street ngoku ikwiSanderson Hotel. 

UCharles Booth 
Ngo-Okthobha ka-1898, uCharles Booth wathatha uthotho lweehambo kunye noConstable wePolisa uRJ French weTottenham Court Road subdivision yecandelo lamapolisa e-D kwaye wabhala imigqaliselo kwiincwadana zakhe zoBomi kunye noMsebenzi waBantu baseLondon. Ngomhla we-21 ngo-Oktobha wahamba kunye ne-PC French ejikelezayo "kwiSithili se-3" kubandakanywa nommandla "oboshwe eMntla nge-Mortimer Street kunye ne-Goodge St. eMpuma nguCharlotte St. kunye ne-Rathbone Place, kuMzantsi nge-Oxford Street kunye ne-West yi-Regent St. ukuba yinxalenye yamarhamente ayo Yonke imiphefumlo kunye ne-All Saints." Ukumisa ukusuka kwikona yeSitalato saseGoodge kunye neCharlotte Street wahamba waya emantla eBerners Street ephawula kuphela "i-4 1/2 storeys, iziko lokusekwa komculo, ipiyano, isixhobo, abapapashi bomculo njl. njl. 


Ubugcisa 
uWilliam Chambers, umakhi wezakhiwo kunye nomhlobisi wangaphakathi, wakwazi ukuzakhela indlu "kwintekelelo yakhe", kwi-13, i-Berners Street, kunye nezindlu ezimbini ze-1 kunye ne-1 no-James. UThomas Rouse, zonke zaqala ngo-1764. Ngokutsho kombhali webhayoloji uJohn Harris, "Igadi yeChambers inqanyulwe kwi-mews ngesitali kunye negumbi elikhulu elimele ukuba yiofisi yakhe yokuzoba, evumela ukufikelela kwi-mews kubancedisi. Ngasemva kwendlu yakhe yayihonjiswe kwi-papier mâché 'kwi-fanciful', mhlawumbi i-Chinoiserie, isimbo."[9] Imifanekiso yezinye izinto zangaphakathi ze-Chambers zigcinwe kwithala leencwadi le-RIBA. 
UThomas Collins, umtyabeki wokuhombisa owayesebenzela, kwaye wayengumhlobo kunye neqabane likaSir William Chambers. 
UJohn Opie, imbali, i-historic kunye ne-portrait ye-7 Berners Street, i-8 igcisa lokufa lika- 
Henry Berners 18 Umzobi waseSwitzerland kunye nomzobi (13, Berners Street, ikhaya langaphambili likaWilliam Chambers) 1803

ISitrato saseBerners sinxulunyaniswa kakhulu nombhali uCharles Dickens. Umakazi omkhulu kaDickens, uNksk. Charles Charlton, wayenendlu yokulala e-16 Berners Street, kwaye uDickens wayesoloko ethathwa ngumama wakhe, waza wafumana umsebenzi ngenxa yoko ngo-1827. Omnye wabalali yayiligqwetha eliselula elalibizwa ngokuba ngu-Edward Blackmore, owachukumiseka ngulo mncinci waza wamqesha njengegqwetha e-Ellisn 1 Blackmore (umvuzo ophindwe kabini wowoyikwa kukaDickens, nowawusaziwayo, umsebenzi womzimveliso omnyama). 

KwakuseSitrato saseBerners apho, eseyinkwenkwana, uDickens wabona umfazi obhadulayo, apho umlinganiswa onguNkosazana Havisham ovela kuLindiso olukhulu wayesekelwe phezu kwakhe. UDickens wamchaza "njengesidalwa esidala esizidlayo, esibandayo kwaye esisesikweni" "esinxibe mhlophe ngokupheleleyo kunye nentsimbi emhlophe eyoyikisayo ejikeleze intloko kunye nobuso ngaphakathi kwebhonethi yakhe emhlophe." Wongeze ngelithi "waphambana ngezizathu zakhe yedwa - ngaphandle kwamathandabuzo ngenxa yokuba isityebi seQuaker sasingafuni ukumtshata. Yilokhwe yakhe yomtshakazi le. Uhlala enyuka apha… sibona kwinyathelo lakhe elithambileyo kunye neliso elilotywayo ukuba ujonge ukumkhokelela kubomi obubukhali." Oku kwakukwisincoko sakhe esithi "Apho Siyeke Ukukhula" esapapashwa kwi-Household Words ngomhla we-1 kaJanuwari 1853. 

Kamva ebomini, kwi-31 Berners Street, uDickens wafaka umthandi wakhe omncinci oyimfihlo, umdlali we-actress u-Ellen Lawless Ternan (obizwa ngokuba nguNelly), owayeneminyaka eyi-19 iminyaka engama-27 emncinci kuye, kunye nentombi yakhe endala. KwakungoSeptemba 1858 xa wangena ephelekwa ngunina uFrancis, owayengumdlali weqonga, kunye noodade ababini, uMaria, omnye umdlali weqonga, noFanny, imvumi. Emva kwenyanga nje uEllen noMaria bamxelela ukuba babengcungcuthekiswa lipolisa, uDickens awayerhanela ukuba lalinyotywe yindoda eyayinomdla ngokwesini kuwo omabini okanye omabini. Wakhalazela le “ndlela ingaqhelekanga, kwaye iyingozi nengafunekiyo kwipolisa” awayecinga ukuba kufuneka igxothwe. Kodwa ukoyika ukubhengezwa kuye kwamthintela ekusukeleni. Mhlawumbi yiloo nto ke bafuduka bonke ngoMatshi 1859 ukuya eAmpthill Square. U-Ellen wayenomkhwa wokugqoka iigeraniums ezibomvu kunye ne-heather emhlophe ezinweleni zakhe. Wacengwa ukuba ayeke ukusebenza nguDickens ngo-Agasti 1859, kwaye wafumana iintlawulo rhoqo kwiakhawunti yakhe yaseCoutts Bank. Ekufeni kwakhe eneminyaka engama-75 ubudala, wangcwatyelwa eSouthsea, kufutshane nalapho uDickens wazalelwa khona. 

U-Ellen Ternan, umlingisi kunye nenkosikazi kaCharles Dickens (31, Berners Street) 
USamuel Taylor Coleridge, imbongi (71, Berners Street) 
Abanye abahlali 
uRobert Cooper Lee (26, Berners Street) iminyaka engama-30 yokuqeshisa ukusuka ngo-1771, emva koko bafudukela eBedford Square[16] 
uJohn Slater, FRSA, umyili we-4. 1891
Ekupheleni kwenkulungwane yeshumi elinesithoba indawo ejikeleze iBerners Street yayingasenandawo yokuhlala ngokupheleleyo kwaye iziza zophuhliso zazidityaniswa ukuze kwakhiwe izakhiwo ezikhulu zorhwebo kunye nesiqingatha soshishino okanye iibhloko ezinkulu zeeflethi. Imizekelo yezo bloko zezindlu zibandakanya izindlu ezinkulu zesitalato zika-Edwardian Berners (34–36, Berners Street) kunye neNkundla yaseLancaster.

Iqela leBerners labasetyhini (9, Berners Street) c. 1871–1898.
u-Elizabeth Crawford uphawule kumsebenzi wakhe we-Women's Suffrage Movement:

Ngowe-1871 ikomiti yeBerners Club yayiquka uFrancis Power Cobbe noBarbara Bodichon. Iklabhu apho umrhumo wonyaka wawuyi-10s, yayivulwa ukusuka ngo-8 ekuseni ukuya ku-10.30 pm ngeentsuku zeveki kwaye ukusuka ngo-9 ukuya ku-10.30 pm ngeeCawe. Iklabhu yayinegumbi lokufunda, elibonelelwa ngamaphephandaba kunye namaphepha-ncwadi; igumbi lokuzoba loluntu kunye nencoko, kunye negumbi lokutyela. Iklabhu yayingakhethi cala, kwaye yayivulekele amalungu angaphandle kunye namaNgesi. Ikomiti yayifuna ukuba ilungu ngalinye elinokubakho linike ireferensi malunga nokuhlonipheka. IBerners Club yayingasekho ngo-1898. 

ICentral Committee yeNational Society for Women's Suffrage, yasekwa 1867 (9, Berners Street) Ladies Town and Country Club (yabhaliswa eBerners Street Mansions c. 1898–1900, unobhala L. Jackson) yaze yadweliswa kwi-73 kunye ne-75 Piars 4 
ukwenza

Mortimer4 ibekwe Berners Street phakathi 1820 kunye 1860, kuquka:[28] 
Thomas Dodd, umenzi wohadi. UThomas Dodd uvela kusapho lwabenzi bezixhobo-izaphetha zevayolin zikaDodd zazidumile ukusukela phakathi kwe1700. Uyise u-Edward wafa ngo-1810 eneminyaka ehloniphekileyo ye-95. U-Dodd wayengumthengisi wezixhobo ukusuka kwi-1809 ukuya ku-1823, xa wayefudukela eBerners Street waza waba nomdla kwiihadi. WayekwakwiSitrato saseBerwick ngo-1827 ngaphambi kokuba abuyele kwisitalato iBerners. UThomas wasweleka malunga no-1830, kwaye ishishini laqhubeka de kwangowe-1846 – mhlawumbi ngoonyana bakhe aba-2 (bona u-Edward Dodd, 3, Berners Street). Kukho i-patent ye-1822 yentamo elaminated. 
Haarnack, umenzi wohadi (53 Berners Street). Kwakukho izizukulwana ezininzi zeHaarnack eziqala phakathi koo-1920s. Ishishini lalikwisitalato iCharlotte kwaye kwakukho igumbi lokubonisa eFitzroy Square. Ngexesha elithile babekwa-53 Berners Street ezantsi kwendlela esuka eDodds. Owokuqala emgceni waba ngumkhandi oyintloko e-Erards ngo-1808. I-Haarnack yayingomnye wabenzi bokugqibela abaqhubeleka nokurhweba kwaye babeneshishini lokulungisa eliqhuba kakuhle. UMarie Goosens ukhankanya ukudibana nezizukulwana ezi-3 kwivenkile yabo kwincwadi yakhe ethi "Life on a Harpstring". 
I-Erat's Hap Saloon yayise-23 Berners Street ukusuka ngo-1820 ukuya ku-1858, kwaye iikonsathi zikawonke-wonke zaziqhutyelwa apho. Ngeminyaka yoo-1920 ukuya kutsho kweyee-1950 iRudall, iCarte & Co, umenzi wezixhobo zokhuni kunye nobhedu, yayise-23 Berners Street. 
Upapasho lomculo 
i-Novello & Co (1, Berners Street, 1867-1906) yinkampani yaseLondon eshicilela umculo oshicileleyo osebenza ngokukhethekileyo kumculo weklasiki, ngakumbi irepertoire yeekwayala. Yasekwa ngo-1811 nguVincent Novello.


 
iQela leNtengiso loMculo ngowona mpapashi mkhulu womculo oshicilelweyo waseYurophu, onekomkhulu eBerners Street, eLondon. Inamalungelo kumakhulu amawaka eengoma, ishicilela zombini iincwadi kunye nomculo weshiti, isebenza e-UK yeevenkile ezinkulu zomculo, kwaye ithengisa umculo wamaphepha, izixhobo kunye nezixhobo ngqo kwiMusicroom.com.
Umbutho wamaLungelo okwenziwa kuMculo (29–33 Berners Street), owawusakuba nguMbutho oSebenzayo oLungileyo, owasekwa ngo-1914, ngumbutho wase-UK wokuqokelelwa kwamalungelo okukopisha kunye nombutho wamalungelo okusebenza owenza ulawulo lwamalungelo adibeneyo emisebenzi yomculo. I-PRS yoMculo yasungulwa kwi-1997 njenge-MCPS-PRS Alliance, idibanisa imibutho emibini yokuqokelela: i-Mechanical-Copyright Protection Society (MCPS) kunye ne-Performing Right Society (PRS).
