Bourne kunye neHollingsworth 
Bourne & Hollingsworth yayiyivenkile yesebe kwikona yesitalato iOxford kunye neBerners Street. Isakhiwo sayo sakhiwa ekupheleni kwenkulungwane yeshumi elinesithoba, kwaye ivenkile yafudukela kwisakhiwo ekuqaleni kweminyaka yoo-1900, yahlala apho de yavalwa ngo-1983. I-Bourne & Hollingsworth iboniswa kwifilimu ye-Adelphi ka-1954 ethi The Crowded Day, elandela usuku olunye kubomi beqela labasebenzi bevenkile yesebe kwaye yadutyulwa ngokuyinxenye kwindawo ngaphakathi nangaphandle kwendawo. 
































IBhanki yaseNgilani yibhanki esembindini yase-United Kingdom kunye nemodeli apho uninzi lweebhanki ezingoovimba bale mihla zisekwe kuyo. Yasekwa ngo-1694 ukuba isebenze njengomgcini-bhanki kuRhulumente wamaNgesi kunye nomphathi wamatyala, kwaye isengomnye wabagcini bebhanki kurhulumente wase-United Kingdom, yibhanki enguvimba enkulu yesibini kwihlabathi.

Le bhanki yayiyeyabucala ngabaninimasheya ukususela kwisiseko sayo ngo-1694 de yaphunyezwa ngo-1946 yinkonzo yase-Attlee.[4] Ngo-1998 yaba ngumbutho karhulumente ozimeleyo, ophethwe ngokupheleleyo nguNondyebo egameni likarhulumente, [5] kunye nesigunyaziso sokuxhasa imigaqo-nkqubo yezoqoqosho yorhulumente welo xesha, [6] kodwa ukuzimela geqe ekugcineni uzinzo lwamaxabiso.[7] Ngenkulungwane yama-21 ibhanki ithathe uxanduva olongezelelekileyo lokugcina nokubeka iliso uzinzo lwezezimali e-UK, kwaye iya isanda ukusebenza njengomlawuli osemthethweni. 

Ikomkhulu lebhanki belikwisithili semali saseLondon, isiXeko saseLondon, ukusukela ngo-1694, nakwiSitalato i-Threadneedle ukusukela ngo-1734. Ngamanye amaxesha yaziwa ngokuba yi-"Old Lady of Threadneedle Street", igama elithathwe kwikhathuni ye-satirical nguJames Gillray ngo-1797. Indlela yokuhlangana ngaphandle yaziwa ngokuba yi-Bank Junction. 

Ibhanki, phakathi kwezinye izinto, ingumlondolozi koovimba begolide abasemthethweni baseUnited Kingdom (kunye nabo bamalunga nama-30 amanye amazwe).[10] Ukusukela ngo-Epreli ka-2016, ibhanki ibambe malunga ne-5,134 yeetoni (iitoni ezi-5,659) zegolide, ezixabisa i-£ 141 yebhiliyoni. Olu qikelelo lucebisa ukuba ivault inokubamba ukuya kutsho kwi-3% yeetoni zegolide ezili-171,300 zombiwa kwimbali yoluntu. 

Imisebenzi 
Ngokwe-strapline yayo, eyona njongo yebhanki 'kukukhuthaza okulungileyo kwabantu base-United Kingdom ngokugcina uzinzo lwemali kunye nezezimali'. Oku kuphunyezwa ngeendlela ezahlukeneyo: 

Uzinzo lwemali 
Amaxabiso azinzileyo kunye neendlela ezikhuselekileyo zentlawulo zezona nqobo ziphambili zokumisela uzinzo lwemali. 

Amaxabiso azinzileyo 
Amaxabiso azinzileyo agcinwa ngokuzama ukuqinisekisa ukuba ukonyuka kwamaxabiso kuyahlangabezana nommiselo kaRhulumente wokunyuka kwamaxabiso. Ibhanki ijolise ekuhlangabezaneni nale njongo ngokulungelelanisa isiseko senzala (eyaziwa ngokuba yizinga lebhanki), eligqitywe yiKomiti yoMgaqo-nkqubo weMali webhanki (MPC). (I-MPC iye yanikezela uxanduva lokulawula umgaqo-nkqubo wezemali; i-HM Treasury inamagunya agciniweyo okunika imiyalelo kwikomiti "ukuba ifunwa ngokwentando yoluntu kunye neemeko zoqoqosho ezigqithisileyo", kodwa iPalamente kufuneka ivume loo myalelo kwiintsuku ezingama-28.) 

Ukususela ngo-2024 i-inflation target yi-2%; ukuba le thagethi iphosiwe iRhuluneli kufuneka ibhale ileta evulekileyo kwiNgqonyela ye-Exchequer echaza imeko kunye nokucebisa izilungiso.[15] Ngaphandle kokumisela isiseko senzala, esona sixhobo sisetyenziswa yibhanki kulo mba kukuphunguka kobungakanani. 

Iifomu ezikhuselekileyo zentlawulo
Ibhanki ine-monopoly kwimiba yemali ebhankini eNgilani naseWales kwaye ilawula ukukhutshwa kweebhanki kwiibhanki zorhwebo eScotland naseMntla Ireland. (Scottish kunye Northern Irish banks bagcina ilungelo lokukhupha iimali zabo, kodwa kufuneka baxhaswe enye-nganye kunye iidiphozithi ebhankini, ngaphandle kwezigidi ezimbalwa zeeponti ezimele ixabiso amanqaku ababenawo kujikelezo 1845.) 

Ukongeza ibhanki yongamela ezinye iinkqubo zokuhlawula, esebenza njenge-arhente yokuhlalisa kunye neenkqubo zokuhlalisa i-ChaPS yexesha elililo. [18] Ngo-2024 ibhanki yayizinzile malunga ne-500 yeebhiliyoni zeerandi zeentlawulo phakathi kweebhanki suku ngalunye. 

Uzinzo lwezemali 
Ukugcina uzinzo lwemali kubandakanya ukukhusela abagcini-mali base-UK, abatyali-mali kunye nababoleki ngokuchasene nezoyikiso kwinkqubo yezemali xa iyonke.[8] Izoyikiso zibonwa yibhanki kunye nemisebenzi yobuntlola kwimarike, kwaye kujongwana nayo ngokwemali neminye imisebenzi (ekhaya nakwamanye amazwe). Uninzi lwezi zikhuselo zafakwa emva kwengxaki yezemali ka-2008: 

Ummiselo 
Ngo-2011 ibhanki ye-Prudential Regulation Authority yasekwa ukuze ilawule kwaye ibeke iliso kuzo zonke iibhanki ezinkulu, imibutho yokwakha, imibutho yamatyala, ii-inshurensi kunye neefemu zotyalo-mali e-UK ('ulawulo oluncinci').[19] Ibhanki ikwanendima esemthethweni yokulawula ngokunxulumene neziseko zophuhliso lwemalike yemali. 

Ulawulo lomngcipheko 
Kwangaxeshanye, iKomiti yeFinancial Policy yebhanki (FPC) yamiselwa ukuze ibone kwaye ibeke iliso kumngcipheko wenkqubo yezemali, kwaye ithathe amanyathelo afanelekileyo apho kuyimfuneko ('ulawulo oluphangaleleyo'). I-FPC ipapasha iziphumo zayo (kunye namanyathelo athathiweyo) kwiNgxelo yoZinzo lwezeMali kabini ngonyaka. 

Iinkonzo zebhanki 
Ibhanki ibonelela ngeenkonzo zebhanki kwi-wholesale kuRhulumente wase-UK (kunye nangaphezulu kwekhulu leebhanki ezingoovimba zaphesheya).[22] Ilawula i-Akhawunti ye-Exchange Equalization Account yase-UK egameni likaNondyebo we-HM kwaye igcina i-akhawunti yeNgxowa-mali eManyeneyo karhulumente.[23] Ikwalawula oovimba botshintshiselwano lwamazwe angaphandle kwaye ingumlondolozi wogcino lwegolide lwase-UK (kunye nabanye). 

Ibhanki ikwabonelela 'ngenkxaso yotywala kunye nezinye iinkonzo kwiibhanki nakwamanye amaziko emali'.[13] Iibhanki zorhwebo ngokwesiqhelo zigcina umlinganiselo wemali ebekelwe bucala kwidiphozithi kwiBhanki yaseNgilani. Ezi zovimba zebhanki zisetyenziswa ziibhanki ukuhlawula omnye nomnye;[25] (ngesi sizathu iBhanki yaseNgilani ngamanye amaxesha ibizwa ngokuba 'yibhanki yebhanki').[26] Kwiimeko ezingaqhelekanga, iBhanki isenokuthi ibe ngumbolekisi wemali yokugqibela ngokuthi ibolekwe ngetyala xa lingekho elinye iziko.

Njengomlawuli kunye nebhanki ephakathi, iBhanki yaseNgilani ayizange ibonelele ngeenkonzo zebhanki zabathengi iminyaka emininzi, kodwa isalawula ezinye iinkonzo ezijongene noluntu (ezifana nokutshintshiselana ngamanqaku ebhanki afakwe endaweni).[27] Kuze kube yi-2017, abasebenzi beBhanki babenelungelo lokuvula ii-akhawunti zangoku ngokuthe ngqo kwiBhanki yaseNgilani kwaye banikwa ikhowudi yohlobo olulodwa lwe-10-00-00. 

ISigqibo 
Phantsi kwemiqathango yoMthetho wokuBhankisha ka-2009, ibhanki yi-UK's Resolution Authority kuyo nayiphi na ibhanki okanye umbutho wesakhiwo obonwa 'mkhulu kakhulu ukuba ungasilela'; ngoko ke ixhotyisiwe ukuba isebenze kwimeko yokusilela kwebhanki 'ukukhusela iinkonzo zezemali ezibalulekileyo zase-UK kunye nokuzinza kwezemali'. 

Iinkonzo zembali kunye noxanduva 
Phakathi kuka-1715 no-1998, iBhanki yaseNgilani yayilawula i-Government Stocks (eyayiyimali eninzi yetyala lesizwe): ibhanki yayinoxanduva lokukhupha izitokhwe kubaninimasheya, ukuhlawula izabelo kunye nokugcina irejista yokudluliselwa; iphinde yathatha ulawulo lwemali ye-Exchequer noxanduva lokukhupha amatyala kaNondyebo kwibhanki ngo-2000. [30] I-Computershare ithathe indawo njengombhalisi kwiibhondi zikaRhulumente wase-UK (ii-gilt-edged securities okanye 'gilts') ukusuka ebhankini ekupheleni kuka-2004. Ibhanki, nangona kunjalo, iyaqhubeka isebenza njenge-arhente yokuhlawula i-Ofisi yoLawulo lweTyala kunye nomgcini wezibambiso zayo. 

Ukusukela ekusekweni kwayo ngo-1694, ibhanki ibonelele ngenkonzo yebhanki yokuthengisa kuRhulumente; nangona kunjalo ngo-2008 yagqiba ekubeni irhoxe ekunikezeni ezi nkonzo, ngoku zibonelelwa ngoluhlu lwamanye amaziko emali kwaye alawulwa yiNkonzo yeBhanki kaRhulumente. 

Kuze kube ngo-2016, ibhanki ibonelele ngeenkonzo zebhanki zobuqu njengelungelo kubasebenzi.[28] Ngaphambili, ibhanki ibigcine iiakhawunti zabucala kunye nezorhwebo kuzo zonke iintlobo zabathengi, kubandakanywa abantu, amashishini amancinci kunye nemibutho yoluntu; kodwa utshintsho lomgaqo-nkqubo olandela iMfazwe yeHlabathi yokuQala yabona ibhanki isanda ukurhoxa kolu hlobo lweshishini ukuze igxininise ngakumbi kwindima yayo yebhanki ephakathi. 


Imali ebhalwe ngesandla ebhalwe ngesandla yowe-1697, yasayinwa 'yeRhuluneli kunye neNkampani yeBhanki yaseNgilani' nguCashier wesi-2 uRobert Hedges 
Ngexesha leMfazwe yeMinyaka eliThoba, uMkhosi waManzi wasebukhosini woyiswa nguMkhosi waManzi waseFransi ngo-1690 kwidabi laseBeachy Head, nto leyo eyabangela unxunguphalo kurhulumente kaWilliam III waseNgilani. Urhulumente wamaNgesi wagqiba ekubeni akhe kwakhona uMkhosi Waselwandle wasebukhosini ube ngumkhosi owawukwazi ukucel’ umngeni amaFrentshi ngokulinganayo; nangona kunjalo, amandla abo okwenza oko athintelwa kukunqongophala kwemali karhulumente kunye netyala eliphantsi likarhulumente. Oku kungabikho kwetyala kwenza ukuba urhulumente wamaNgesi angakwazi ukuboleka i-£ 1.5m awayefuna ukuyisebenzisa ukwandisa iRoyal Navy.[32]


Ngo-1691, uWilliam Paterson wenze isindululo sokuseka ibhanki yesizwe njengendlela yokuxhasa imali yoluntu. [33] Njengoko kamva wabhalayo kwincwadana yakhe ethi, A Brief Account of the Intended Bank of England (1694): 

“...kwaphakanyiswa kwiminyaka ethile eyadlulayo ukuba iNgxowa-mali yeNgxowa-mali enokutshintshelwa kuwonke-wonke kufuneka isekwe yiPalamente, kwaye yenziwe ibe lula ukufumana iirisithi kunye neeNtlawulo kwiSixeko saseLondon neseWestminster; kunye nokuseka uMbutho waMadoda eMali afanele ukutshintshelwa ngurhulumente ngokutshintshiselana ngeMali yawo. Ingxowa-mali, kuyo yonke imfuno" 

Nangona iskimu sakhe singakhange sithathwe ngokukhawuleza, sibonelela ngesiseko seTshatha yokuqala yebhanki kunye nomthetho owenze ukuba ukusekwa kwayo kwenzeke 

Amanye amanani amabini abalulekileyo ekudalweni kwebhanki nguCharles Montagu, iLungu lePalamente yaseMaldon, owadlala indima ebalulekileyo ekuqhubeni izindululo ngePalamente (kwaye emva koko wamiselwa njengeNgqonyela ye-Exchequer); kunye noMichael Godfrey, owanceda ukucenga abaxhasi beSixeko kwiinzuzo zaso (kwaye emva koko wakhethwa ukuba abe nguSekela-Rhuluneli wokuqala webhanki) 

Kuye kwakhona ibango (ngu-WR Scott, phakathi kwabanye) [35] ukuba uWilliam Phips wadlala ngexesha elifanelekileyo, ukuba kwenzeka, indima: uhambo lwakhe oluyimpumelelo lokubuyisela amaxhoba kwi-galleon yaseSpain eyayitshonelwe (ibhanki yase-Nuestra i-Seestra inceda ibhanki yase-Nuestra i-Seestra i-Seestra i-design). isiseko: ukukhukulisa imakethi nge bullion kunye nokudala uchulumanco kumashishini adityanisiweyo 

Umthetho 

uCharles Montagu udlale indima ephambili ekuqulunqeni umthetho wokuseka iBhanki kunye nokulawula iNdlu yeMibutho. 
Isiphakamiso sikaPaterson sasifuna ukuba uRhulumente aseke ingxowa-mali apho inzala yayiza kuhlawulwa kubabhalisi. Kwaye kwagqitywa ekubeni oku kuya kubonelelwa ngengeniso esuka kwitoni, kunye neminye imisebenzi yokuthumela ngenqanawa erhafiswa rhoqo yi-HM Exchequer; ngoko ke iPalamente yamkele ukusekwa kwebhanki ngoMthetho weTonnage 1694[37] ('uMthetho wokunika ooKhulu babo iiRhafu ezininzi kunye neMithetho phezu koThutho lweeNqanawa kunye neZithuthi kunye noBeere Ale kunye nobunye uTywala ukuze kukhuselwe iMbuyekezo ethile kunye neNzuzo kulo Mthetho ukhankanyiweyo kuBantu abangamawaka aPhakamileyo njengoko baya kuthi bafikelele kwikhulu lamawaka aBantu abalishumi elinesibini. Ukuqhuba iMfazwe echasene neFransi') 

Ukungenisa umrhumo wemali-mboleko, ababhalisileyo babeza kubandakanywa negama leRhuluneli kunye neNkampani yeBhanki yaseNgilani. Iimali zoluntu zazikwimeko emaxongo kakhulu ngelo xesha[39] kangangokuba imiqathango yemali-mboleko (njengoko ibekiwe kuMthetho wePalamente) yayikukuba yayiza kunikwa iinkonzo ngesantya esisi-8% ngonyaka; kwakukho nentlawulo yenkonzo ye-£ 4,000 ngonyaka ehlawulwa ebhankini yokulawula imali mboleko.

UMthetho uthintele utyalo-mali lwababhalisi ukuya kubuninzi be-£10,000 nganye kwisihlandlo sokuqala, kunye ne-£1,200,000 iyonke (kwakucingelwa ukuba i-Exchequer iyakunyusa i-£300,000 eseleyo ngezinye iindlela zokuboleka) Ukutywinwa 

kokuhlanganiswa 

kweBhanki yaseNgilani Charter (1694), ngu-Lady Janel05 waseNgilani, ngu-Lady Janel05 
waseNgilani. inikwe ngomhla we-27 Julayi 1694, kwiinyanga ezintathu emva kokupasiswa koMthetho 

. Abantu abali-1,268 babhalisile. Ukugcinwa kwabo kwaziwa ngokuba yi-Bank Stock (i-Bank Stock yaqhubeka ibanjwe kubunini babucala de kwangowe-1946 xa iBhanki yaseNgilani yamiselwa phantsi kolawulo).[40] Uninzi lwababhalisi bokuqala 'yayingabo baphakathi kwabarhwebi baseLondon' (nangona abarhwebi namagcisa nabo barhuma). [41] Uninzi (ngaphezu kwesibini esithathwini) lunikele ngaphantsi kwe-£ 1,000. Njengomlinganiselo wemali iyonke ephakanyisiweyo, i-25% isuka 'kwi-esquires', i-21% ivela kubathengisi kunye ne-15% evela kwii-aristocrats. Ishumi elinesibini ekhulwini lababhalisi bokuqala yayingabafazi.[41] UKumkani uWilliam kunye noKumkanikazi uMary (ngokudibeneyo) batyale i-£ 10,000, eyona mali iphezulu evunyelweyo, njengoko kwenza iqaqobana labanye (kuquka noSir John Houblon) 

Utyalo-mali kumkhosi wenqanawa lwenzeka ngokufanelekileyo. Njengesiphumo, inzame enkulu yefektri efunekayo (kuquka ukusekwa kweentsimbi ukwenza iinzipho ezininzi kunye nenkqubela phambili[ingcaciso efunekayo] kwezolimo ukondla amandla aphindwe kane omkhosi wamanzi) yaqalisa ukuguqula uqoqosho. Oku kwanceda uBukumkani obutsha beGreat Britain - iNgilani neSkotlani zadityaniswa ngokusesikweni ngo-1707 - ukuba zibe namandla. Amandla eRoyal Navy enza iBritani ibe ligunya lehlabathi elilawulayo ekupheleni kwe-18th nasekuqaleni kwenkulungwane ye-19 

Ulawulo 
Irhuluneli yokuqala yebhanki yayinguJohn Houblon, kunye noSekela-Rhuluneli wokuqala uMichael Godfrey. (iminyaka engama-330 kamva, kwi-1994, ibhanki yayiza kukhupha i-£ 50 yephepha elibonisa i-Houblon ukuphawula i-tercentenary yayo 


) 
. baqeshwe kwisiXeko); Abalawuli bonyulwa minyaka le 'yiNkundla Jikelele' yabo bonke abaninimasheya ababhalisiweyo beBhanki (ababizwa ngokuba 'ngabaProprietors'). Isitywina esiqhelekileyo seNkundla yabaLawuli, esamkelwa nge-30 kaJulayi 1694, sibonise 'iBritannia ihleli kwaye ijonge kwiBhanki yemali'; IBritannia ibiluphawu lwebhanki ukusukela ngoko.

INkundla yonyula amagosa aphezulu amathathu awathi, ecaleni kweRhuluneli kunye noSekela-Rhuluneli, banoxanduva lokuqhuba kwayo imihla ngemihla ebhankini: Unobhala kunye neGqwetha, uMfaki-sicelo wokuQala kunye noMgcini-mali wokuQala. (Abangena ezihlangwini zabo, uNobhala, uMgcini-mali oyiNtloko kunye noMgcini-mali oyiNtloko, baqhubeka bekhokela amacandelo aphambili emisebenzi yebhanki kule minyaka ingama-250 ilandelayo: iCashier eyiNtloko kunye noMgcini-mali oyiNtloko babejongene ‘necala lemali’ kunye ‘necala lesitokhwe’ sebhanki, ngokulandelelanayo, ngelixa uNobhala elongamele ulawulo lwangaphakathi 

. abagcini-mnyango. 

Izakhiwo 
Ibhanki ekuqaleni yayingenaso isakhiwo sayo, yavula okokuqala ngomhla woku-1 ku-Agasti ka-1694 kwiHolo yeMercers kwi-Cheapside. Oku kwafunyaniswa ukuba kuncinci kakhulu kwaye ukusuka nge-31 kaDisemba 1694 ibhanki yasebenza ukusuka kwiHolo ye-Grocers (ekwakuseNkukhuni ngoko), apho yayiza kuhlala iminyaka ephantse ibe ngama-40.[47] (uHoublon wayesebenze njengoMphathi weNkampani yeeGrosari ngo-1690–1691.) 

Umsebenzi 
UMthetho wePalamente wawuyithintela ibhanki ekurhwebeni ngeempahla okanye urhwebo lwalo naluphi na uhlobo, nangona yayivunyelwe ukuba ithengise ngegolide nesilivere, kunye namatyala otshintshiselwano.[48] Kungekudala, ibhanki yayandisa inzuzo yayo ngokukhupha imali engamaphepha, ithatha idiphozithi kunye nokuboleka imali yokubambisa. 

Ngemihla yayo yokuqala ibhanki yenza ilahleko enkulu, hayi kancinci ngokwamkela iingqekembe ezichetyiweyo ngokutshintshiselana ngamaphepha ayo.[48] Ukusekwa kweBhanki yoMhlaba (nguJohn Asgill noNicholas Barbon) ngo-1695, kunye nokunqongophala kwemali okubangelwa yi-Great Recoinage ka-1696, zombini zasongela isikhundla sebhanki; Usuku loKwahlulwa 

kwenkulungwane ye-18 

eBhankini, ngo-1770. Iholo yePay ka-1732 yayisesinye sezakhiwo zokuqala zeBhanki eThreadneedle Street. (Ngaxa lithile abanini-zabelo kuye kwafuneka ukuba bazimase ngokwabo ukuze kuhlawulwe izabelo zikaRhulumente; lo mkhuba wapheliswa ngowe-1910). 
Ngomnyaka we-1700, iNkampani ye-Hollow Sword Blade yathengwa liqela loosomashishini abanqwenela ukuseka ibhanki yesiNgesi ekhuphisanayo (kwisenzo esiya kuthathwa namhlanje "njengoluhlu lwangasemva"). Ulawulo lokuqala lweBhanki yaseNgilani kugcino-mali lwebhanki yesiNgesi lwaluza kuphelelwa ngowe-1710. Noko ke, endaweni yoko lwahlaziywa, kwaye inkampani yeSword Blade ayizange ilufezekise usukelo lwayo.

Umbono kunye nobunyani betyala lesizwe buye kwenzeka ngeli xesha, kwaye oku kwakulawulwa kakhulu yibhanki. Ngokusebenzisa i-1715 Ways and Means Act, iPalamente yagunyazisa ibhanki ukuba ifumane imirhumo yomba karhulumente we-5% annuities, eyenzelwe ukunyusa i-£ 910,000; [50] oku kwaphawula ukuqala kwendima yebhanki ekulawuleni i-Stocks zikaRhulumente, ezaziyindlela yokuba abantu batyale imali kwityala likarhulumente (ngaphambili ukuboleka kukaRhulumente kwakulawulwa yi-Exchequer ngqo).[5] Ibhanki ibibophelelekile nguMthetho ukuba ihlawule izabelo zesiqingatha sonyaka kwaye igcine irekhodi yencwadi yazo zonke iimali ezidluliselweyo (njengoko ibisele iqhele ukwenza ngokubhekiselele kwi-Bank Stock yayo). 

Ibhanki ayizange ibe ne-monopoly ekubolekeni kurhulumente, nangona kunjalo: iNkampani yoLwandle lwaseMazantsi yasekwa ngo-1711, kwaye ngo-1720 nayo yaba noxanduva lwenxalenye yetyala lesizwe lase-UK, yaba ngumkhuphisana omkhulu kwiBhanki yaseNgilani. Ngelixa intlekele ye "South Sea Bubble" yavela kungekudala, inkampani yaqhubeka nokulawula inxalenye yetyala lesizwe lase-UK de kwangowe-1853. Inkampani yase-East India nayo yayingumbolekisi okhetha urhulumente. 

Ngo-1734 kwakukho abasebenzi abangamashumi alithoba anesithandathu ebhankini.[46] Umqulu webhanki wahlaziywa ngo-1742, kwaye kwakhona ngo-1764. Ngomthetho we-1742 ibhanki yaba kuphela kwenkampani edibeneyo yesitokhwe evunyelwe ukukhupha amanqaku ebhanki kwi-metropolis. 

I-Threadneedle Street 

i-Perspective View yeBhanki yaseNgilani (eyapapashwa ngo-1756): ibhanki ekuqaleni yayikwisiza esimxinwa ngasemva kwe-front kwi-Threadneedle Street. 
IBhanki yaseNgilani yafudukela kwindawo yayo yangoku, kwindawo yendlu kaSir John Houblon kunye negadi eThreadneedle Street (kufutshane necawa yaseSt Christopher le Stocks), ngo-1734 [52]. (Ifa lathengwa kwiminyaka elishumi ngaphambili; uHoublon wafa ngowe-1712, kodwa umhlolokazi wakhe wahlala endlwini de kwasekufeni kwakhe ngowe-1731, ekwathi emva koko kwadilizwa indlu kwaza kwaqaliswa ukusebenza ebhankini.)
 
Indawo entsha eyakhiweyo, eyilwe nguGeorge Sampson, yayikwisiza esimxinwa (esimalunga neemitha ezingama-80 (esimalunga neemitha ezingama-24 ukusuka kwisitrato esinobubanzi obuziimitha ezingama-24). Isakhiwo esingaphambili sasineeofisi zotshintshelo kumgangatho wokuqala, ngaphantsi kwayo kwakukho iarch yokungena eya kwintendelezo. Ujongene nomnyango 'yayisesona sakhiwo siphambili' sebhanki:[54] iHolo enkulu (79 ft × 40 ft (24 m × 12 m)) apho amanqaku ebhanki akhutshelwa khona kwayekutshintshiselwana, [55] nalapho iidiphozithi kunye nokutsalwa kungenziwa.[41] (Sampson's Great Hall, kamva eyaziwa ngokuba yiPay Hall, yahlala ikwisitu kwaye isetyenziswa de kwasakhiwa ngokutsha kukaHerbert Baker ekupheleni kweminyaka yoo-1920.) Kwicala elingasezantsi lonxantathu kwakukho iGumbi leNkundla kunye neGumbi leKomiti, kwicala elingasentla kwakukho iOfisi yoMbali-mali; macala omabini kwakukho iindlela zokuhamba, anamagumbi amagosa aphezulu, ngelixa imigangatho ephezulu ineeofisi kunye namagumbi.[53] Ngaphantsi kombhobho omacala amane kwakukho amagumbi angaphantsi ('aneeNdonga ezomeleleyo kunye neeGango zentsimbi, zokuGcina iMali'); ukungena kwintendelezo kwabonelelwa, ngendlela yepaseji ekhokelela 'kwiSango elikhulu' kwiNdlela yeBartholomew, kubaqeqeshi neenqwelwana 'ezifika rhoqo zithwele iGolide kunye neSilver Bullion'.[54] I-pediment engentla komnyango weHolo engundoqo yayihonjiswe ngomzobo oqingqiweyo we-alto relievo waseBritannia (owayevele kwitywina eliqhelekileyo lebhanki ukususela nge-30 kaJulayi 1694); [57] umkroli waba nguRobert Taylor, owathi waqeshwa njengoMyili wezakhiwo, ngokulandelelana ukuya kuSampson, ngo-1764. III,[58] inconywa kumbhalo okhaphayo wesiLatini njengomseki webhanki (i-conditor);[48] kwelinye icala, ifestile enkulu yaseVenice yayijonge kwiyadi yecawa yaseSt Christopher. 

Ukwandiswa
 
kweThreadneedle Street front in 1773, emva kokongezwa kwephiko likaTaylor empuma kodwa phambi kokudilizwa kweSt Christopher le Stocks (ekhohlo)
Kwisiqingatha sesibini senkulungwane ye-18 ibhanki ngokuthe ngcembe yafumana iziza zomhlaba ezingabamelwane ukuze ikwazi ukwandisa, kwaye emva kwe-1765 izakhiwo ezitsha zaqala ukongezwa ngumyili webhanki osanda kuqeshwa uRobert Taylor. Kumntla-ntshona weHolo yePay, ejongene nendlu yecawa yaseSt Christopher ukuya emazantsi, uTaylor wakha uluhlu lwamagumbi aBalawuli bebhanki esekelwe kwigumbi elitsha (elikhulu kakhulu) leNkundla kunye neGumbi leKomiti (Xa ibhanki yayisakhiwa ngokutsha ngeminyaka yee-1920-30s, la magumbi asuswa kwindawo yawo yokuqala ekumgangatho osezantsi kwaye aphinda akhiwa kumgangatho wokuqala wenkundla kwaye aqhubekeka kumgangatho wokuqala weNkundla; IKomiti yoMgaqo-nkqubo weMali ngokulandelelanayo.).[59][60] Empuma Pay Hall, Taylor wakha uluhlu lweeholo kunye neeofisi ezinikezelwe kulawulo lwesitokhwe kunye nezahlulo, eziye zaphinda zaphinda kabini ubukhulu bendawo yebhanki (eyandisa ukuya kuthi ga eBartholomew Lane).[41] La magumbi ayegxile kwiRotunda enkulu, ekwabizwa ngokuba yiBrokers' Exchange, apho kuthengwe ngeStokhwe sikaRhulumente; macala onke kwalungiselelwa iiOfisi zokuTshintshela ezine ezinobungakanani, nganye ihambelana nengxowa-mali eyahlukileyo (njengoko kuchaziwe kwiminyaka yoo-1820: 'Kwi-ofisi nganye phantsi koonobumba abaliqela bealfabhethi, kucwangciswe iincwadi apho amagama abo bonke abantu abanepropathi kwiimali abhaliswe kuzo, ngokunjalo neenkcukacha zomdla wabo').[48] Zonke ezi ofisi zazikhanyiswe phezulu, ukuthintela imfuneko yeefestile kwiindonga zangaphandle. 


Ibhanki ngo-1797: amaphiko empuma nasentshona nguSir Robert Taylor flank Sampson's centerpiece ka-1733. 
Ngo-1782 icawa yaseSt Christopher le Stocks yachithwa, ivumela ibhanki ukuba yandise ngasentshona ecaleni kweSitalato i-Threadneedle. Iphiko elitsha lasentshona lagqitywa kuyilo lukaTaylor ngo-1786 (umphambili walo uhambelana nephiko likaTaylor ngaphambili lasempuma): lalihlala kwi-Reduced Annuities Office, i-Check Office kunye ne-Dividend Warrant Office (phakathi kwezinye). Kwangoko emantla kukho indawo eyayisakuba yindlu yecawe yase-St Christopher le Stocks, eyayilondolozwe ngaphakathi kwezakhiwo njengegadi (eyaziwa ngokuba 'yiNkundla yoMyezo'). Emantla eNkundla yeBullion, uTaylor wakha iThala leeNcwadi elinemigangatho emine, ukugcina ingqokelela yebhanki eyandisiweyo yogcino-mpepha. 

I-Bank Picquet 
Ukudilizwa kwecawe kubangelwe zizidubedube zikaGordon zika-1780, nalapho kuthiwa abaqhankqalazi bakhwela kwicawe besiya kugibisela ngeembumbulu kwizakhiwo zebhanki. Ngexesha lodushe, ngoJuni 1780, iNkosi uSodolophu waseLondon wabongoza uNobhala kaRhulumente ukuba athumele umlindi womkhosi ukuze akhusele ibhanki kunye ne-Mansion House.[61] Ukusukela ngoko unogada wasebusuku ('Bank Picquet') wabonelelwa ngamajoni eHousehold Brigade (uqheliselo olwaqhubeka de kwangowe-1973). Ukugcina umlindi uTaylor wakha inqaba (ekufikelelwa kuyo kwisango elisecaleni kwiSitalato iPrinces) kumntla-ntshona wekona yesiza.

Ukwakhiwa ngokutsha kukaJohn Soane
I-Bank of England Site Act 1793 

I-Ofisi yoLwahlulo njengoko yakhiwa ngokutsha nguJohn Soane 
Sir Robert Taylor wasweleka ngo-1788 kwaye endaweni yakhe ibhanki yamisela uJohn Soane njengoMyili wezakhiwo kunye noMvavanyi (uya kuhlala kwisithuba kude kube ngo-1827). Ngaphantsi kolwalathiso lwakhe, ibhanki yandiswa ngakumbi kwaye yakhiwa kwakhona, kancinci kancinci kodwa kwisicwangciso esidibeneyo. Uphando lwezakhiwo, olwenziwa ekuqaleni kolawulo lwakhe, lwafumanisa iingxaki ezithile, ezathi zalungiswa ngokukhawuleza nguSoane: umzekelo ngo-1795 waphinda wakha iRotunda kunye neeOfisi zokuTshintshela ezimbini ezikufutshane (i-Ofisi ye-Bank Stock kunye ne-Four Per Cent Office), endaweni yophahla lwamaplanga ka-Taylor, olwaluvuza, kunye nomsebenzi wamatye oqinileyo. [62] Ngelo xesha uSoane wayenikwe umsebenzi wokuthenga iipropati eziya kumntla-mpuma, kunye namagunya okuthenga anyanzelekileyo anikwe yiBhanki yaseNgilani yeSiza Act 1793 (33 Geo. 3. c. 15), ukwenzela ukuba ibhanki ikwazi ukwandisa kwelo cala ukuya eLothbury. Phakathi kwe-1794 kunye ne-1800 wayila isethi edibeneyo yezakhiwo ngaphakathi kwesiza esitsha esinemilo engaqhelekanga: walungisa kwakhona iNkundla yaseBullion kwaye wanikezela indlela entsha yokungena yezithuthi ezivela emantla, ebizwa ngokuba yiNkundla yaseLothbury; ngasempuma wakha ibhloko entsha yeThala leeNcwadi waza wongeza iOfisi yoTshintsho yesihlanu (i-Ofisi yoTshintsho yeConsols) kumntla kwezinye ezine. 

I-Brokers 'Exchange kwiBhanki 

kaSoane's Rotunda, xa isasetyenziswa njengomgangatho wokurhweba (1804) 
Ngasekupheleni kwe-18 kunye nasekuqaleni kwenkulungwane ye-19, ngaphambi kokusekwa kweLondon Stock Exchange, iRotunda kwiBhanki yaseNgilani yayisetyenziswa njengendawo yokurhweba 'apho abarhwebi bempahla, abarhwebi bempahla, kunye nabanye abantu, badibana ngenjongo yokuthengisa imali yoluntu. Isebe elisuka eRotunda 'yayiiofisi ezabelwe ulawulo lwesitokhwe ngasinye' ezineencwadi ezidwelisa umdla womntu ngamnye obhalisiweyo kwingxowa-mali. Ukusetyenziswa kweRotunda ekurhwebeni kwayekwa ngo-1838, kodwa iqhubekile isetyenziselwa ukuthathwa kwemali kwiziqinisekiso zezabelo zengxowa-mali. 

Iingxabano kunye neengxaki zekhredithi 

Ikhathuni yeSatirical ephikisana nokuqaliswa kwemali yephepha, nguJames Gillray, 1797. "I-Old Lady yaseThreadneedle St" (ibhanki yomntu) ihlanjululwe nguWilliam Pitt Omncinci. 
Ingxaki yetyala ka-1772 ichazwe njengengxaki yokuqala yebhanki yanamhlanje ejongene neBhanki yaseNgilani. [65] IsiXeko saseLondon sisonke saba nesiphithiphithi xa uAlexander Fordyce kwathiwa akanamali. [66] NgoAgasti 1773, iBhanki yaseNgilani yancedisa i-EIC ngemali-mboleko. [67] Uxinzelelo koovimba beBhanki yaseNgilani aluzange lwehliswe kude kube sekupheleni konyaka. 

Ngexesha leMfazwe yaseMelika yokuzimela, ishishini lebhanki lalilungile kangangokuba uGeorge Washington wahlala engumnini-zabelo ngalo lonke ixesha.

Ngokuhlaziywa kwamalungelo ebhanki ngo-1781, yayiyibhanki yogcino-mali – igcina igolide eyaneleyo yokuhlawula amanqaku ayo de kube yi-26 kaFebruwari 1797 xa imfazwe yayicuthe kakhulu oovimba begolide kangangokuba – kulandela ukoyikeka okwabangelwa yiDabi leFishguard kwiintsuku ezingaphambili – urhulumente walela ibhanki ekuhlawuleni nge-bank17 Restriction Act. de 1821. 

Ngo 1798, ngexesha French Revolutionary Wars, a Corps of Bank Volunteers yasekwa (phakathi 450 kunye 500 amadoda) ukukhusela ibhanki xa kuhlaselwe. Yachithwa ngo-1802, kodwa yaphinda yenziwa kunyaka olandelayo ekuqaleni kweeMfazwe zeNapoleonic. Amajoni alo ayeqeqeshelwa ukuba xa kunokuthiwa ahlaselwe, asuse igolide nesilivere kumagumbi okuhlala ayise kwindawo esemagqagaleni, kunye noomatshini bokushicilela bemali engamaphepha kunye neengxelo ezithile ezibalulekileyo.[70] Kwabonelelwa indawo yokugcina izixhobo kwisiza esiseThreadneedle Street ukuze bafumane izixhobo zabo kunye nezixhobo zabo.[48] I-Corps yachithwa ekugqibeleni ngo-1814. Imbonakalo 

yenkulungwane ye-19 

yeBhanki yaseNgilani ithathwe kwi-engile yomntla-ntshona njengoko yakhiwe ngo-1805 (JM Gandy, 1825) 
Ekuqaleni kwenkulungwane ye-19 isicwangciso senziwe nguJohn Soane sokwandiswa kwezakhiwo zebhanki, ngeli xesha ukuya kumntla-ntshona weSitrato, ukuya kwiSitrato esitsha sasePrince, ukuya kwiSitrato kwindawo). Uninzi lommandla wolwandiso olutsha lwathatyathwa ngoomatshini bokushicilela abaqhutywa ngumphunga ukuze kushicilelwe imali engamaphepha (amanqaku aqhubeka eshicilelwa kwisiza de kwayiMfazwe Yehlabathi yokuqala, xa iSibhedlele saseSt Luke sangaphambili safunyanwa saza saguqulelwa ekubeni yimisebenzi yoshicilelo yebhanki).[71] USoane waqhubeka nomsebenzi de kwangowe-1833; kwiminyaka yokugqibela phambi kokuthatha umhlala-phantsi wakhe wagqiba ukwakha kwakhona iphiko likaTaylor lasempuma kwaye waphinda walungisa iifaçades zeSampson kunye neTaylor ezijongene nesitrato ukwenza yonke iperimeter yekhompleksi iphelele. 

Ngo-1811, 'iwotshi eyilwe ngobukrelekrele' ngabakwaThwaites & Co. yafakwa ngaphezulu kweHolo yePay:[72] kunye nokutshiza iiyure kunye nekota, yahambisa ixesha kude (ngeentonga zobhedu ezandisa ubude obuziimitha ezingama-700 (210 m) ukudayela ezibekwe kwiiofisi ezilishumi elinesithandathu ezahlukeneyo malunga nesiza.

 
IHolo yokuHlawula (apho amanqaku atshintshiselwana ngeengqekembe zemali, kwaye ngokuphambeneyo) eboniswe ngowe-1866.
'Uloyiko luka-1825' luqaqambise imingcipheko ekhoyo kwindlela ezintathu zokuthembeka ebhankini: kubanini-zabelo, kuRhulumente (kunye noluntu), kunye nabathengi bayo beebhanki zorhwebo. Ngo-1825–26 ibhanki yakwazi ukunqanda ingxaki yokungabikho kwemali xa uNathan Mayer Rothschild waphumelela ukuyibonelela ngegolide;[74] nangona kunjalo, emva kobunzima, iibhanki ezininzi zamazwe kunye nezamaphondo aziphumelelanga zibangele ukutshona kwezorhwebo okuninzi.[75] Ukugqithiswa kwe-Country Bankers Act 1826 kwavumela ibhanki ukuba ivule amasebe ephondo ukwenzela ukusasazwa okungcono kweebhanki zayo (ngelo xesha iibhanki zelizwe ezincinci, ezinye zazo zaziphantsi kakhulu, zakhupha amanqaku azo); ekupheleni konyaka olandelayo amasebe asibhozo eBhanki yaseNgilani aye asekwa kwilizwe jikelele. 


ISitokhwe seBhanki yeBhanki yaseNgilani, yakhutshwa nge-25 kaJanuwari 1876 
Umthetho weBhanki Charter 1844 ubophelele umba wamanqaku koovimba begolide waza wanika iBhanki yaseNgilani kuphela amalungelo mayela nomba wemali engamaphepha eNgilani. Iibhanki zabucala ebezinalo ngaphambili elo lungelo ziye zaligcina, ngaphandle kokuba ikomkhulu lazo lingaphandle kweLondon kwaye zifaka isibambiso kumanqaku eziwakhuphileyo; kodwa banikwa inkuthazo ukuba balincame eli lungelo. (Ibhanki yokugqibela yabucala eNgilani ukukhupha amanqaku ayo yayinguThomas Fox's Fox, Fowler and Company bank eWellington, eyakhula ngokukhawuleza de yadityaniswa ne-Lloyds Bank ngo-1927. Bahlala besenza ithenda esemthethweni kwada kwangowe-1964. (Kukho amanqaku alithoba ashiyekileyo ajikelezayo; enye igcinwe eTone Dale House, eWellington.)) 

Ibhanki yokugqibela 1 yasebenza njenge-panic yokuqala. 

Inkulungwane yama-20 

inqaku leBhanki elimhlophe leeponti ezintlanu lahlala lisetyenziswa de kwangowe-1957. 
Ukuza kuthi ga ngo-1931 iBritane yayikumgangatho wegolide, nto leyo ethetha ukuba ixabiso le-sterling lamiselwa ngexabiso legolide. Ngaloo nyaka, iBhanki yaseNgilani kwafuneka ithathe iBritani isuke kumgangatho wegolide ngenxa yemiphumo yoxinzelelo olukhulu olusasazeka eYurophu. 

Ngo-1913 kwazama ukuqhushumba ibhombu 
Jonga kwakhona: Ibhombu ye-Suffragette kunye nephulo lokutshisa 
 
Iziqhushumbisi ezimbini ze-suffragette eziboniswe kwi-City of London Police Museum ngo-2019.
Ibhombu yabanqolobi yazanywa ngaphandle kwesakhiwo seBhanki yaseNgilani ngomhla we-4 ku-Epreli 1913. Kwafunyanwa ibhombu eqhumayo kwaye ilungele ukudubula ecaleni kweentsimbi ezingaphandle kwesakhiwo.[78][79] Le bhombu yatyalwa njengenxalenye yephulo lokuqhunyiswa kwebhombu kunye nokutshiswa, apho iManyano yabaseTyhini yeNtlalo neyezoPolitiko (WSPU) yasungula uthotho lweziqhushumbisi ezinempembelelo yezopolitiko kunye nohlaselo lokutshiswa kwilizwe lonke njengenxalenye yephulo labo lokulwela amalungelo abasetyhini.[79][80] Ibhombu yapheliswa ngaphambi kokuba iqhushumbe, kwindawo eyayisesinye sezitrato zikawonke-wonke ngelo xesha kwikomkhulu, nto leyo ekusenokwenzeka ukuba yathintela abantu abaninzi abangxwelerhekileyo.[79] [81] Le bhombu yatyalwa kusuku emva kokuba inkokeli yeWSPU uEmmeline Pankhurst egwetywe iminyaka emithathu entolongweni ngokwenza uqhushumbo kwikhaya lezopolitiko uDavid Lloyd George.

Amathambo ale bhombu, eyakhiwe kwindawo yokusebenzela ubisi, ngoku aboniswe kwiMyuziyam yamaPolisa eSixeko saseLondon. 

Ukuhlengahlengiswa kunye nokwakhiwa ngokutsha 
Ngexesha lolawulo lwaseMontagu Norman, ukususela ngowe-1920 ukuya kutsho ngowe-1944, ibhanki yenza iinzame ezingabom zokushiya iibhanki zorhwebo ukuze ibe yibhanki enguvimba. Kamva iRhuluneli, uRobin Leigh-Pemberton, wayichaza 'njengexesha lokutshintsha ngokukhawuleza, apho saqala ukuhamba kude nezithethe zabefundisi beminyaka engama-200 [...] kunye nokwamkela ubungcali, umatshini kunye neendlela zolawulo lwanamhlanje'.[46] Iingcali zezoqoqosho kunye namanani-manani aqala ukuqeshwa ebhankini ngenani elandayo. Ngo-1931 'iKomiti yePikoko', eyamiselwa ukucebisa ngophuculo lombutho, yapapasha izindululo eziquka ukuqeshwa kwaBalawuli besigqeba abahlawulwayo (kunye namalungu eNkundla angengawo alawulayo). Ikwacebise uhlengahlengiso lweziseko zesebe lebhanki. 


Ibhanki eyakhiwe ngokutsha ka-Baker ime emva kodonga lomkhusane ka-Soane olugcinelwe inxalenye 
Umsebenzi webhanki uye wanda kakhulu ukususela ekupheleni kweMfazwe yeHlabathi yokuQala, kwaye isigqibo sathathwa sokwandisa. Phakathi kuka-1925 no-1939 ikomkhulu lebhanki eliseThreadneedle Street lakhiwa ngokutsha ngokupheleleyo nguHerbert Baker. (Oku kwakubandakanya ukudilizwa kwezakhiwo ezininzi zikaMhlekazi uJohn Soane, isenzo esichazwe ngumbhali-mbali wezokwakha uNikolaus Pevsner “njengolona lwaphulo-mthetho lwezakhiwo, kwiSixeko saseLondon, kwinkulungwane yamashumi amabini”.) Ukudilizwa kunye nokwakhiwa kwakhona kwenzeka ngezigaba, abasebenzi besuka kwenye indawo yesakhiwo ukuya kwenye (okanye, kwezinye iimeko, kwindawo yokuhlala yethutyana eFinsbury Circus). I-bullion kunye nezibambiso zahlala kwindawo yonke. Ngexesha lokwakhiwa ngokutsha iintsalela zabantu eziphathelele kwiyadi endala yecawe yaseSt Christopher le Stocks zaye zagrunjwa zaza zangcwatywa kwakhona kumangcwaba eNunhead. 


Umfanekiso oqingqiweyo ka-Ariel nguCharles Wheeler
Isakhiwo esakhiwe ngentsimbi sika-Baker simi kwimigangatho esixhenxe ukuphakama, kunye nemigangatho emithathu eyongezelelekileyo enabela ngaphantsi komgangatho ophantsi. Ihonjiswe ngemifanekiso eqingqiweyo kunye nomsebenzi wobhedu nguCharles Wheeler, udaka lukaJoseph Armitage kunye nemifanekiso eyenziwe nguBoris Anrep. [83] Ibhanki namhlanje sisakhiwo esidweliswe kwiBanga lokuqala. 

Ngowe-1939 kwamiselwa uLawulo loTshintsho eUnited Kingdom ekuqhambukeni kweMfazwe Yehlabathi yesiBini; ezi zilawulwa yibhanki.[46] Ngexesha le-WWII, ngaphezulu kwe-10% yexabiso lobuso lokujikeleza imali ye-Pound Sterling yayiye yaveliswa yiJamani.
 
Inani lemisebenzi yebhanki kunye nabasebenzi bafuduselwa eHampshire ngexesha lemfazwe, kubandakanywa nemisebenzi yokushicilela (eyafudukela e-Overton), iSebe le-Accountant's (eyayiya e-Hurstbourne Park) kunye nezinye iiofisi ezahlukeneyo. Abo bashiyeka eThreadneedle Street, kuquka nabaLawuli, bafudusa iiofisi zabo kumagumbi angaphantsi komhlaba. 

Ukwenziwa kwelizwe emva kwemfazwe 
Ngo-1946, kamsinya nje emva kokuphela kolawulo luka-Montagu Norman, ibhanki yafakwa phantsi kolawulo lukarhulumente waBasebenzi. Kwangaxeshanye inani laBalawuli lancitshiswa laya kutsho kwishumi elinesithandathu (abane kubo yayingaBalawuli abaLawuli abasisigxina). 

Ibhanki ilandele iinjongo ezininzi zezoqoqosho zaseKeynesian emva kwe-1945, ngokukodwa "imali elula" kunye nenzala ephantsi yokuxhasa imfuno edibeneyo. Izamile ukugcina izinga lotshintshiselwano olusisigxina kwaye yazama ukujongana nokunyuka kwamaxabiso kunye nobuthathaka be-sterling ngetyala kunye nolawulo lotshintshiselwano. 


IBhanki yaseNgilani iNew Change (ezantsi ekunene) njengoko ibonwa eSt Paul's 
Emva kwemfazwe, iSebe le-Accountant elikhulu kakhulu (elalilawula icala lesitokhwe sebhanki) labuyela eLondon lisuka eHampshire. Indawo yayo ye-ofisi echongiweyo e-Threadneedle Street, nangona kunjalo, okwangoku yathathwa yi-ofisi yoLawulo loTshintsho. Endaweni yoko isebe libonelelwe ngendawo yokuhlala yethutyana (ephinde yafumaneka eFinsbury Circus), kulindelwe ukwakhiwa kwesakhiwo esitsha, esiya kuhlala kwindawo yeehektare ezimbini ngoko nangoko ngasempuma kweSt Paul's Cathedral. 'I-Bank of England New Change' yayilwa nguVictor Heal yaza yavulwa ngo-1957 (ngelo xesha yayiyeyona projekthi yokwakhiwa kwakhona kwemfazwe yaseLondon emva kwemfazwe); [86] isakhiwo esitsha sasiqulathe izinto eziluncedo zabasebenzi abaliqela ecaleni kwendawo yokuhlala yeofisi kwaye, kwinqanaba lesitrato, iiyunithi zokuthengisa zaye zavunyelwa kwiintlobo ezahlukeneyo zamashishini. Ibhanki yayinesakhiwo esinesivumelwano sokuqeshisa seminyaka engama-200; kodwa ngokufika kweekhompyutha amanani abasebenzi ancitshiswa kakhulu ngeminyaka yoo-1980-90s; iinxalenye zesakhiwo zaye zavunyelwa kwezinye iifemu (ingakumbi ifemu yomthetho iAllen & Overy). Ibhanki yathengisa isakhiwo ngo-2000 kwaye ngo-2007 yachithwa; Utshintsho olutsha ngoku lumi kwindawo. 

Ibhanki "inqaku le-10 bob" yarhoxiswa ekujikelezweni kwi-1970 ekulungiseleleni uSuku lweDesimali ngo-1971.

  1 inyanga 
Jonga kwakhona: Igophe lesivuno esiguquliweyo
Ngo-1977 ibhanki yaseka icandelo eliphantsi elibizwa ngokuba yiBank of England Nominees Limited (BOEN), inkampani yabucala engasekhoyo, enezabelo ezibini kwikhulu le-£1. Ngokwememorandam yayo yombutho, iinjongo zayo yayizi: "Ukusebenza njengoMtyunjwa okanye i-arhente okanye igqwetha nokuba kuphela okanye ngokudibeneyo nabanye, kuye nawuphi na umntu okanye abantu, intsebenziswano, inkampani, iqumrhu, urhulumente, urhulumente, umbutho, umlawuli, iphondo, igunya, okanye iqumrhu likarhulumente, okanye naliphi na iqela okanye umbutho wabo". I-Bank of England Nominees Limited yanikwa ukukhululwa ngu-Edmund Dell, uNobhala weLizwe wezoRhwebo, kwiimfuno zokudiza phantsi kweCandelo lama-27(9) loMthetho weeNkampani 1976, kuba "kwakuthathwa njengokungathandekiyo ukuba iimfuno zokubhengeza kufuneka zisebenze kwiindidi ezithile zabanini-zabelo". IBhanki yaseNgilani ikwakhuselwe yiwonga layo lolawulo lwasebukhosini kunye noMthetho weeMfihlo ezisemthethweni. [87] I-BOEN yayiyisithuthi sikarhulumente kunye neentloko zelizwe ukuba zityale kwiinkampani zase-UK (ngokuxhomekeke kwimvume evela kuNobhala kaRhulumente), ngokubonelela ukuba bathathe "ukungaphembeleli imicimbi yenkampani".[88] Kwiminyaka yayo yamva, i-BOEN yayingasakhululwa kwiimfuno zokudiza umthetho wenkampani. [89] Nangona inkampani eleleyo,[90] ukulala akuthinteli inkampani esebenzayo njengomnini-sabelo otyunjiweyo.[91] I-BOEN yayinabanini-zabelo ababini: iBhanki yaseNgilani, kunye noNobhala weBhanki yaseNgilani. 

Imfuneko yokugcina iibhanki ukuba zibambe ubuncinane obumiselweyo beediphozithi zabo njengoovimba kwiBhanki yaseNgilani yapheliswa ngo-1981: bona imfuneko ye-Reserve § United Kingdom ngeenkcukacha ezithe vetshe. Utshintsho lwangoku olusuka kwi-Keynesian economics ukuya kwi-economics yaseChicago lwahlalutywa nguNicholas Kaldor kwiSibetho seMonetarism. 

Ukunikezelwa komgaqo-nkqubo wemali ebhankini kwaba liplanga eliphambili lomgaqo-nkqubo wezoqoqosho weLiberal Democrats kunyulo jikelele luka-1992.[94] Ilungu leLungu lePalamente uNicholas Budgen naye wayecebise oku njengomthetho oyilwayo welungu labucala ngo-1996, kodwa umthetho oyilwayo awuphumelelanga njengoko wawungenankxaso kurhulumente okanye iqela eliphikisayo. 

Urhulumente wase-UK washiya i-European Exchange Rate Mechanism ebiza kakhulu ukugcina i-European Rate Mechanism ngoSeptemba 1992, kwisenzo esabiza i-HM Treasury ngaphezu kwe-3 yezigidigidi zeedola. Oku kukhokelele kunxibelelwano phakathi kukarhulumente nebhanki. 


Imbali yokunyuka kwamaxabiso e-UK ukusukela ngo-1960 
Jonga kwakhona: 1976 sterling crisis 
Ngo-1993, ibhanki yavelisa iNgxelo yayo yokuqala yokunyuka kwamaxabiso kurhulumente, inika iinkcukacha ngeendlela zokunyuka kwamaxabiso kunye noxinzelelo. Le ngxelo eveliswa minyaka le ihlala yenye yeempapasho ezinkulu zebhanki.[84] Impumelelo yokujolisa kwixabiso lentengo eUnited Kingdom kubangelwe kujoliso lwebhanki ekuhleni.[95] IBhanki yaseNgilani ibe yinkokeli ekuveliseni iindlela ezintsha zokunxibelelana noluntu, ngakumbi ngeNgxelo yokunyuka kwamaxabiso,ezinye iibhanki ezingoovimba ezininzi ziye zaxelisa.

Ibhanki ibibhiyozela usuku lwayo lokuzalwa lwamakhulu amathathu ngo-1994. 

Ngo-1996, ibhanki yavelisa uphononongo lwayo lokuqala lweFinancial Stability Review. Olu papasho lonyaka lwaziwa njengeNgxelo yoZinzo lwezeMali ngo-2006. [84] Kwakhona ngaloo nyaka, ibhanki yaseka inkqubo yayo yexesha langempela lokuhlawulwa kwentlawulo (RTGS) yokuphucula ukuhlaliswa komngcipheko phakathi kweebhanki zase-UK. 

Ngomhla wesi-6 kuCanzibe ka-1997, kulandela unyulo lukawonke-wonke luka-1997 olwathi lwesa urhulumente wezabasebenzi okokuqala ngqa ukusukela ngo-1979, kwabhengezwa yiNgqonyela yeSebe lezeMali, uGordon Brown, ukuba ibhanki iya kunikwa ukuzimela geqe kumgaqo wolawulo-mali.[97] Phantsi kwemiqathango yoMthetho weBhanki yaseNgilani ka-1998 (owaqalisa ukusebenza ngomhla woku-1 kuJuni 1998) iKomiti yoMgaqo-nkqubo weMali webhanki (MPC) yanikwa uxanduva olulodwa lokumisela amazinga enzala ukuhlangabezana neSilathisi samaxabiso eRetail Prices (RPI) ekujoliswe kuwo yi-2.5%. [98] Ithagethi itshintshile ukuya kwi-2% ukususela ekubeni i-Consumer Price Index (CPI) ithathe indawo ye-Retail Prices Index njenge-inflation index kaNondyebo.[99] Ukuba ukunyuka kwamaxabiso kugqithise okanye kunciphisa ithagethi ngaphezu kwe-1% iRhuluneli kufuneka ibhale ileta kwi-Chancellor ye-Exchequer ichaza ukuba kutheni, kwaye iya kuyilungisa njani imeko. 

Iibhanki ezingoovimba ezizimeleyo ezamkela ummiselo wokunyuka kwamaxabiso ezinto zaziwa ngokuba ziibhanki zeFriedmanite central. Olu tshintsho kwipolitiki yezaBasebenzi lwachazwa nguSkidelsky kwincwadi ethi UkuBuyiswa koMphathi[101] njengempazamo nanjengokwamkelwa koqikelelo lolindelo olusengqiqweni njengoko lwalubhengezwe nguAlan Walters.[102] Okujoliswe kuko ekunyukeni kwamaxabiso kudityaniswe nokuzimela kwebhanki enguvimba kuphawulwe njengesicwangciso-qhinga “sokulamba isilo” esidala ukunqongophala kwemali kwicandelo likarhulumente. 

ngo-June 1998 uxanduva lolawulo nokubekwa kweliso kwimizi-mveliso yeebhanki kunye ne-inshorensi lwaye lwasuswa ebhankini lwasiwa kwi-Financial Services Authority. Imemorandam yokuqonda ichaze imiqathango apho ibhanki, iSebe lezeMali, kunye neFSA iza kusebenza ngokubhekiselele kwinjongo efanayo yokwandisa uzinzo lwemali.[103] (Iminyaka elishumi kamva, nangona kunjalo, emva kobunzima bezemali ka-2008, umthetho omtsha webhanki udlulisele uxanduva lokulawula kunye nokulawulwa kweebhanki kunye ne-inshurensi kwi-Bank of England). 

Inkulungwane yama-21 ngo 

-2013: ukususela ngenkulungwane ye-18 abagcini-masango bebhanki banxibe 'iipinki' (i-livery enxulumene noSir John Houblon) [104] 
Ibhanki yagqiba ekubeni ithengise imisebenzi yayo yoshicilelo lwemali kwiDe La Rue ngoDisemba 2002, phantsi kwengcebiso yeClose Brothers Corporate Finance Ltd. 

UMervyn King waba yiRhuluneli yeBhanki yaseNgilani nge-30 Juni 2003.

Ngo-2009, isicelo esenziwe kwi-HM Treasury phantsi koMthetho weNkululeko yoLwazi safuna iinkcukacha malunga ne-3% ye-Bank of England stock ephethwe ngabanini-zabelo abangachazwanga amagama abo ibhanki ingenankululeko yokuchaza.[106] Kwileta yempendulo yomhla we-15 ngo-Oktobha 2009, i-HM Treasury yachaza ukuba "Ezinye ze-3% ye-Treasury stock eyayisetyenziselwa ukuhlawulela abanini bangaphambili be-stock yebhanki ayizange ikhululwe. Nangona kunjalo, inzala ihlawulwe kabini ngonyaka kwaye akunjalo ukuba oku kuye kwaqokelela kunye nokudibanisa. I-

. kwakhona: Inverted isivuno curve 
Ngo-2010, i-Chancellor engenayo ibhengeze injongo yayo yokudibanisa i-Financial Services Authority ibuyele ebhankini Ngo-2011 iKomiti ye-Financial Policy yethutyana (i-FPC) yenziwa (njengekomiti yesipili kwiKomiti yoMgaqo-nkqubo weMali) ukukhokela igunya elitsha lebhanki malunga nozinzo lwezemali, kunye ne-FPC eyongezelelweyo imisebenzi I-Prudential Regulation Authority (PRA), kunye namagunya amaninzi okulawula ababoneleli beziseko zemalike 

yemali Ummi woBukumkani kodwa sele enikwe ubumi ngokwesicelo sikarhulumente, ixesha lakhe landiswa ukuya ku-2019, emva koko kwakhona ukuya 
ku 

- 

2020 

. esebenza, ukususela ngoJanuwari 2009, i-Asset Purchase Facility (APF) ukuthenga "impahla ekumgangatho ophezulu exhaswa ngumba we-Treasury bills kunye nemisebenzi yolawulo lwemali ye-DMO" kwaye ngaloo ndlela iphucula ukuthengiswa kweemalike kwiimarike zetyala. i-MPC Kanye nokulawula iimali ze-QE, ezaziyi-£895 bn kwincopho, i-APF iyaqhubeka nokusebenza izibonelelo zayo zequmrhu Zombini zenziwa yinkampani encedisayo yeBhanki yaseNgilani, i-Bank of England Asset Purchase Facility Fund Limited (BEAPFF).

I-QE yayiyilwe ikakhulu njengesixhobo somgaqo-nkqubo wemali. Inkqubo yayifuna ukuba iBhanki yaseNgilani ithenge iibhondi zikarhulumente kwimarike yesibini, ixhaswa ngemali ngokudala imali entsha yebhanki enguvimba. Oku kuya kuba nesiphumo sokunyusa amaxabiso ee-asethi zeebhondi ezithengiweyo, ngokwenjenjalo kuthotywa izivuno kunye nokunciphisa inzala yexesha elide. Injongo yalo mgaqo-nkqubo ekuqaleni ibikukunciphisa imiqobo yokuhlawula amatyala kwinkqubo ye-sterling reserves kodwa yaguquka yaba ngumgaqo-nkqubo obanzi wokubonelela ngovuselelo lwezoqoqosho. 

I-QE yenziwe ngezigaba ezintandathu phakathi kwe-2009 kunye ne-2020. Kwincopho yayo kwi-2020, iphothifoliyo iphelele i-£ 895 yezigidigidi, equka i-£ 875 yeebhiliyoni zebhondi zikaRhulumente wase-UK kunye ne-£ 20 yeebhiliyoni ze-high-grade bonds zorhwebo. 

NgoFebruwari 2022, iBhanki yaseNgilani yabhengeza injongo yayo yokuqalisa ukuvala ipotfoliyo yeQE.[113] Ekuqaleni oku bekuya kuphunyezwa ngokungatshintshwa kwezabelo zeebhondi ezivuthwayo, kwaye kamva bekuya kukhawuleziswa ngokuthengiswa kwebhondi esebenzayo. 

Ngo-Agasti ka-2022, iBhanki yaseNgilani yaphinda yaphinda injongo yayo yokukhawulezisa i-QE-wind-down ngokuthengiswa kwebhondi esebenzayo. Lo mgaqo-nkqubo waqinisekiswa kutshintshiselwano lweeleta phakathi kweBhanki yaseNgilani kunye neChancellor yase-UK ye-Exchequer ngoSeptemba 2022. [114] Phakathi kukaFebruwari 2022 kunye noSeptemba 2022, iyonke i-£ 37.1bn yeebhondi zikarhulumente zikhulile, zinciphisa isitokhwe esibalaseleyo ukusuka kwi-£ 875.0bn ekupheleni kwe-2021 ukuya kwi-837.9bn. Ukongezelela, isamba se-£ 1.1bn yeebhondi zenkampani zikhulile, ukunciphisa isitokhwe kwi-£ 20.0bn ukuya kwi-£ 18.9bn, kunye nokuthengiswa kwempahla eseleyo ecetywayo ukuqala ngo-27 Septemba. 

Imiba yemali yebhanki 
Inqaku eliphambili: I-Bank of England ikhupha amanqaku 

Inqaku le-£1 lomhla ka-1797 (yaye yaphawulwa njengehlawulwe ngo-1928) 
Ibhanki iye yakhupha imali engamaphepha ukususela ngo-1694. Amanqaku ayebhalwe ngesandla ekuqaleni; nangona zashicilelwa ngokuyinxenye ukususela ngowe-1725 ukuya phambili, oonomali kwakusafuneka batyobele inqaku ngalinye baze babhatalwe komnye umntu. Amanqaku aprintwa ngokupheleleyo ukususela ngo-1855. Ukuza kuthi ga ngo-1928 onke amanqaku ayeyi-"White Notes", eprintwe ngombala omnyama kunye ne-reverse engenanto. Ngeenkulungwane ze-18 kunye ne-19, iiNqaku eziMhlophe zikhutshwe kwi-£ 1 kunye ne-£ 2 yeenkonzo. Ngexesha le-20th inkulungwane, amaNqaku aMhlophe akhutshwe kwiinkonzo phakathi kwe-5 kunye ne-£ 1000. Kude kwaphunyezwa uMthetho woMgangatho weGolide wowe-1925 ibhanki yayibophelelekile ukuba ihlawule ngokwemfuno ixabiso lenowuthi kwingqekembe yegolide kumphathi wayo. 

Ngo-1724 ibhanki yangena kwikhontrakthi kunye noHenry Portal waseWhitchurch, eHamphire ukubonelela ngephepha elikumgangatho ophezulu wokushicilela imali engamaphepha.[115] Ushicilelo ngokwalo lwenziwa ziifemu zabucala zoshicilelo; iipleyiti zobhedu zazigcinwa kwivault, kwaye zikhatshwa ngexesha labo kumshicileli ngunobhala webhanki (owayeya kubhala inani leekopi ezenziweyo); xa sele yomile ziya kusiwa ebhankini. Umsebenzi wokushicilela wangeniswa kwizakhiwo zebhanki (nangona wawuphantsi kwesivumelwano sabucala) ngowe-1791; ngowe-1808 yaziswa ngokupheleleyo endlwini.


Ibhanki ye-One Guinea, eyakhutshwa yiGloucester Old Bank ngo-1813 
De kwaphakathi kwinkulungwane ye-19, iibhanki zorhwebo zazivunyelwe ukuba zikhuphe imali yazo, kwaye amanqaku akhutshwe ziinkampani zebhanki zephondo ayedla ngokujikeleza.[116] Umthetho weBhanki Charter Act 1844 uqale inkqubo yokuthintela umba wamanqaku ebhankini; Iibhanki ezintsha azizange zivunyelwe ukuba zikhuphe imali yazo, kwaye iibhanki ezikhupha amanqaku azizange zivunyelwe ukuba zandise umba wazo. Njengoko iinkampani zebhanki zephondo zadityaniswa zenza iibhanki ezinkulu, zaphulukana nelungelo lazo lokukhupha amanqaku, yaye imali yabucala yeNgesi yabhanga ekugqibeleni yanyamalala, yashiya ibhanki inolawulo olupheleleyo lwemiba yamanqaku eNgilani naseWales. Ibhanki yokugqibela yabucala ukukhupha imali yayo eNgilani naseWales yayinguFox, Fowler kunye neNkampani ngo-1921. [117] Nangona kunjalo, imida yoMthetho we-1844 ichaphazele kuphela iibhanki eNgilani naseWales, kwaye namhlanje iibhanki ezintathu zorhwebo eScotland kunye nezintathu zaseNorthern Ireland ziyaqhubeka nokukhupha iibhanki zazo, ezilawulwa yibhanki. 


Inqaku le-Treasury leeshilling ezilishumi (eyaqala ngo-1914), latyikitywa nguJohn Bradbury 
Ekuqaleni kweMfazwe Yehlabathi yokuqala, uMthetho weMali kunye neBhanki yamanqaku ka-1914 wapasiswa, owanika amagunya exeshana kuNondyebo we-HM wokukhupha imali yebhanki kumaxabiso e-£1 kunye ne-10/- (iisheleni ezilishumi). Amanqaku kaNondyebo ayenesimo esipheleleyo sethenda esisemthethweni kwaye ayengatshintshwa abe yigolide ngebhanki; bathathe indawo yengqekembe yegolide ejikelezayo ukuthintela ukubaleka kwi-sterling kunye nokwenza ukuba kuthengwe izinto ezikrwada zokuvelisa izixhobo. La manqaku abonisa umfanekiso kaKumkani uGeorge V (amanqaku eBhanki yaseNgilani ayizange iqalise ukubonisa umfanekiso wenkosi de kube yi-1960). Amagama kwinqaku ngalinye ayesithi: 

UNITED KINGDOM OF GREAT BRITAIN AND IRELAND – Currency notes are Legal Tender of Legal payment of any amount – Ikhutshwe ngabaKomishinala beNkosi beOfisi kaNondyebo phantsi koGunyaziso loMthetho wePalamente 

Amanqaku kaNondyebo akhutshwa de kwangowe-1928 xa i-Curency and Bank8 Notes powering Act 192 bank8s Act 192 IBhanki yaseNgilani yakhupha amanqaku eesheleni ezilishumi kunye neponti enye okokuqala ngomhla wama-22 kuNovemba 1928. 


Inqaku elithi 'Operation Bernhard' £ 50, elenziwe ngamabanjwa kwinkampu yoxinaniso yaseSachsenhausen 
Ngexesha leMfazwe yesibini yeHlabathi, i-Operation yaseJamani uBernhard yazama ukukhohlisa amahlelo phakathi kwe-£ 5 kunye ne-£ 50, ukuvelisa i-500,000 yemali kwi-parachu yenyanga nganye kwi-3 ye-parachu yase-UK. umzamo wokudodobalisa uqoqosho lwaseBritane, kodwa kwafunyanwa kuluncedo ngakumbi ukusebenzisa amanqaku ukuhlawula iiarhente zaseJamani ezisebenza kulo lonke elaseYurophu. Nangona uninzi lwawela kwizandla zama-Allied ekupheleni kwemfazwe, ubuqhetseba buhlala bubonakala iminyaka emva koko, nto leyo eyakhokelela ekubeni amahlelo ebhanki angaphezulu kwe-£5 asuswe ekujikelezweni. 

Ngo-2006, ngaphezulu kwe-£53 yezigidi zeemali zemali zebhanki zabiwa kwindawo yokugcina imali eTonbridge, eKent.

Ngowe-1917 ibhanki yayifudusele umsebenzi wayo wokushicilela kwiSt Luke’s Printing Works, eyayisakuba sisibhedlele; ngo-1958 yafudukela eDebden. Iimali zebhanki zala maxesha ziprintwa ngesivumelwano neDe La Rue Currency eLoughton, Essex. 

Iiofisi zesebe 

IBhanki yaseNgilani, eKing Street, eLeeds: esinye sezakhiwo ezitsha zesebe ezinogonyamelo ezavulwa ekuqaleni kweminyaka yee-1970. 
Kwiminyaka emininzi yenkulungwane yeshumi elinesithoba elinesithoba ibhanki yayinamasebe amaninzi eLondon nakwezinye izixeko zaseNgilani. 

Amasebe okuqala avulwa ngo-1826 (ngenkuthazo ebonelelwe ngokupasiswa koMthetho weeBhanki zeLizwe, owathi okokuqala wavumela ukusekwa kweebhanki ezidibeneyo ngaphandle kweLondon).[75] Ibhanki ijonge ukuba uthungelwano olutsha lwamasebe luza 'kwandisa ukusasazwa kweeNkcazo zeBhanki, lunike ibhanki ulawulo olupheleleyo ngakumbi kulo lonke ujikelezo lwamaphepha, nokukhusela ibhanki kukhuphiswano lweeNkampani zebhanki ezinkulu'.[121] Isebe ngalinye lalisonganyelwa yi-Agent (umntu 'onolwazi lwezorhwebo, onamava asekuhlaleni').[75] Ngowe-1829 kwakukho amasebe alishumi elinanye asebenza (alishumi eNgilani nelinye eWales). Amanye amasebe angenangeniso kangako ayenexesha elifutshane, kodwa amanye aqhubeka esebenza kwaya kutsho ngoo-1990. 

Ngowe-1997 amasebe amahlanu okugqibela aseleyo avalwa; Ii-Agent, nangona kunjalo, zagcinwa, kunye nesakhiwo see-Arhente zeNgingqi ezenziwe (kuyo yonke i-UK), ezinye zazo bezisekelwe kwizakhiwo zesebe zangaphambili.

Birmingham 1827 1997 Yavulwa eUnion Street (kwindlu yangaphambili yebhanki yaseGibbins, Smith & Goode); yafuduka ngo-1838 ukuya kwisakhiwo esasisakuba seBhanki yaseBirmingham eBennetts Hill, yaze yangena kwindawo eyayisakuba yiStaffordshire Joint Stock Bank indawo e-1 Temple Row ngo-1890. Ngo-1970 yafudukela kwisakhiwo esitsha (kumfanekiso) kwiNombolo 55.	 
Bristol 1827 1997 Yavulwa kwiBridge Street. Yasiwa kwindawo eyakhiwe ngenjongo eBroad Street (ngu-CR Cockerell) ngo-1847; kwaye ukusukela kwisakhiwo esitsha kwisitalato esiPhezulu ngo-1963.	 
Exeter 1827 1834 Yavulwa kwindlu e-18 Southernhay Place; ivalwe emva kweminyaka esixhenxe ngenxa yelahleko yorhwebo (ishishini latshintshelwa ePlymouth).	 
Gloucester 1826 1849 Yavulwa kwindawo eyayisakuba yibhanki yephondo (Turner, Turner & Morris) eNorthgate Street; xa ivaliwe ngenxa yelahleko yorhwebo ishishini lathathwa lisebe laseBristol.	 
Hull 1829 1939 Wavulwa e Salthouse Lane (kumfanekiso); yasiwa kwisakhiwo esitsha (nguPhilip Hardwick) eWhitefriargate ngo-1856. Yavalwa emva kokuba indawo leyo ibonwe njengekwimeko embi kwaye ibekwe ngendlela engafanelekanga.	  
Leeds 1827 1997 Ivulwe kwipropati erentwayo e-Boar Lane; yasiwa kwiSitalato i-Albion ngo-1835. Indawo esePark Row (esemfanekisweni), eyilwe nguPhilip Hardwick, yavulwa ngo-1847; isebe lafudukela kwisakhiwo esitsha eKing Street ngowe-1971.	
I-Leicester 1844 1872 Ivulwe kwi-10 Gallowtree Gate (indawo yangaphambili yendlu yebhanki engasebenzi iClarke, eMitchell & Co.); xa ivaliwe ngenxa yelahleko yorhwebo ishishini ladityaniswa kwelo lesebe laseBirmingham.	 
Liverpool 1827 1986 Ivulwe eHanover Street; yasiwa ngo-1849 kwindawo eyakhiwe ngenjongo ngu-CR Cockerell.

Umlawuli weNkundla 
ka-Andrew
INkundla yaBalawuli yibhodi emanyeneyo enoxanduva lokumisela isicwangciso sombutho kunye nohlahlo lwabiwo-mali kunye nokwenza izigqibo eziphambili malunga nezibonelelo kunye nokuqeshwa. Ibandakanya amalungu amahlanu alawulayo avela ebhankini (iRhuluneli kunye nooSekela-Rhuluneli abane, ngamnye kubo ojongene nommandla owahlukileyo womsebenzi webhanki), kunye namalungu angengawo alawulayo afikelela kwi-9, bonke abo baqeshwe yiCrown. I-Chancellor ikhetha uSihlalo weNkundla phakathi kwamalungu angengawo alawulayo. INkundla kufuneka idibane ubuncinane kasixhenxe ngonyaka. 

IRhuluneli isebenza isithuba seminyaka esibhozo, amaSekela-Rhuluneli iminyaka emihlanu, kunye namalungu angengawo alawulayo ukuya kutsho kwiminyaka emine.

yesiGqeba 
soLawulo 
nguNobhala ongekho kwiBhanki yaseNgilani. uxanduva lolawulo lweebhanki kunye nokuziphatha: 'Unoxanduva lokuqinisekisa ukuba umbutho uqhutywa kakuhle kwaye ucebisa iNkundla yethu yabaLawuli [...] Ukwayigosa lethu leengxabano kwaye uxhasa uRhulumente xa esenza ukuqeshwa kwiikomiti zethu zomgaqo-nkqubo kunye neNkundla yabaLawuli'. 
Ukususela ngo-2013, ibhanki inegosa eliyintloko lokusebenza (COO) kunye nenqanaba kunye nomvuzo weSekela-Rhuluneli. [126] Ukususela ngo-2024, i-COO yebhanki nguBen Stimson; unoxanduva lwemisebenzi yemihla ngemihla yebhanki, kuquka iMicimbi yaBasebenzi, iPropati, i-IT kunye noKhuseleko. [127] Ngo-Matshi 2025, iBhanki yaseNgilani yamisela uSarah John njengeGosa eliPhezulu eliSebenzayo. UJohn ebekhe wasebenza njengoMgcini-mali oyiNtloko weBhanki. 
Abanye abalawuli abangamashumi amabini basebenza kunye neeRhuluneli, besenza 'iqela elilawulayo elibanzi lolawulo'. Phakathi kwenani labo yi-economist eyintloko yebhanki (Ipilisi ye-Huw ukususela ngo-2021),  kunye nomphathi wemali.



Ngolawulo lwangoku, jonga eNgilani. Ngombuso ukusuka kwi-1707 ukuya kwi-1800, bona i-Kingdom of Great Britain. Ngombuso ukusuka kwi-1801 ukuya ku-1922, bona i-Kingdom of Great Britain ne-Ireland. Ngelizwe langoku elizimeleyo, bona i-United Kingdom.

IMAP ENTSHA YOBUKUMKANI base-ENGLAND, Emele iNkosana yase-WALES, kunye namanye amaPhondo, IZIXEKO, IIMPAWU ZEZIDLOKO, NEENDLELA ezisuka edolophini ukuya edolophini (1685)
