Timeline 
idolophu 
yaseNgilani 
I 
-Timeline 
idolophu yase-England Ilizwe elizimeleyo kwisiqithi saseGreat Britain ukusukela ngenkulungwane ye-10, xa lalidityaniswe kwizikumkani ezahlukeneyo ze-Anglo-Saxon, de kwaba nge-1 kaMeyi ngo-1707, xa yadibana neSkotlani ukuze yenze uBukumkani baseBritane, obabuya kuthi kamva bube yiUnited Kingdom. Ubukumkani baseNgilani babuphakathi kwawona mazwe anamandla eYurophu ngexesha lamaxesha aphakathi nasekuqaleni kwexesha langoku. 
Ukuqala ngonyaka wama-886 [4] uAlfred Omkhulu waphinda wayibamba iLondon esuka kwiiVikings zaseDanish kwaye emva kwesi siganeko wazichaza njengoKumkani wama-Anglo-Saxons, de wafa ngo-899. Ebudeni benkulungwane yokuqala yenkulungwane yeshumi, izikumkani ezahlukeneyo ze-Anglo-Saxon zadityaniswa yinzala ka-Alfred u-Edward the Elder (walawula) 924–939) ukwenza uBukumkani bamaNgesi. Ngo-927, u-Æthelstan woyisa ubukumkani bokugqibela beViking, eYork, emenza umlawuli wokuqala wase-Anglo-Saxon kulo lonke elaseNgilani. Kwi-1016, ubukumkani baba yinxalenye ye-North Sea Empire ye-Cnut the Great, imanyano yomntu phakathi kweNgilani, iDenmark neNorway. I-Norman Conquest ngo-1066 yakhokelela ekutshintshelweni kwekomkhulu lesiNgesi kunye nekomkhulu lasebukhosini ukusuka kwi-Anglo-Saxon enye eWinchester ukuya eWestminster, kwaye iSixeko saseLondon sazimisa ngokukhawuleza njengeziko lezorhwebo elikhulu laseNgilani kunye nelona liphambili. 
Iimbali zobukumkani baseNgilani ukusuka kuNorman Conquest ka-1066 ngokwesiqhelo ukwahlula amaxesha athiywe emva kobukhosi obulandelanayo obulandelanayo: uNorman/Angevin 1066–1216, iPlantagenet 1216–1485, iTudor 1485–1603 kunye neStuart 1603–1707 (iphazanyiswe nge-60gne-160 ephazanyiswe nge-16-160). Bonke ookumkani baseNgesi emva kwe-1066 ekugqibeleni behla bevela kumaNorman, kwaye ukwahlula kwePlantagenet kuqhelekileyo-ukuqala ngoHenry II (walawula ngo-1154-1189) ukususela ngelo xesha, ookumkani base-Angevin baba "ngesiNgesi ngakumbi kwindalo"; izindlu Lancaster kunye York zombini Plantagenet cadet amasebe, ubukhosi Tudor babanga inzala Edward III nge John Beaufort kunye noJames VI kunye nam weNdlu Stuart babanga umnombo ukusuka Henry VII nge Margaret Tudor.



Ukugqitywa kokoyiswa kweWales ngu-Edward I ngo-1284 kwabeka iWales phantsi kolawulo lwesithsaba samaNgesi. U-Edward III (walawula ngo-1327–1377) waguqula uBukumkani baseNgilani baba lelinye lawona magunya omkhosi anamandla eYurophu; kulawulo lwakhe kwabakho inguqu ebalulekileyo kumthetho nakurhulumente—ingakumbi inguqulelo yePalamente yamaNgesi. Ukusukela ngeminyaka yoo-1340s, amabango esiNgesi kwisihlalo sobukhosi saseFransi ayebanjwe ngokuhanahanisa, kodwa emva kweMfazwe Yeminyaka Elikhulu kunye nokuqhambuka kweeMfazwe zeRoses ngo-1455, amaNgesi ayengasenawo nasiphi na isikhundla sokulandela amabango awo aseFransi kwaye alahlekelwa ngumhlaba wawo wonke kwilizwekazi, ngaphandle kweCalais. Emva kweziphithiphithi zeeMfazwe zeRoses, ubukhosi bakwaTudor balawula ngexesha leMvuselelo yamaNgesi kwaye baphinda bandisa amandla obukhosi baseNgilani ngaphaya kweNgilani ngokufanelekileyo, bafezekisa umanyano olupheleleyo lwaseNgilani kunye neNqununu yaseWales phantsi kweMithetho eWales IZenzo 1535-1542. UHenry VIII wongamela uHlaziyo lwamaNgesi, kunye nentombi yakhe u-Elizabeth I (walawula ngo-1558-1603) i-Elizabethan Religious Settlement, ngeli xesha eseka iNgilani njengamandla amakhulu kwaye ebeka iziseko zoBukhosi baseBritane ngokusebenzisa ikoloniyali yaseMelika. 

Ukungena kukaJames VI kunye nam ngo-1603 kwaphumela kwiManyano yamaCrown, kunye nobukhosi bukaStuart obulawula izikumkani zaseNgilani, eSkotlani naseIreland. Phantsi kweStuarts, iNgilani yangena kwimfazwe yamakhaya, eyafikelela incopho yayo ngokubulawa kukaCharles I ngowe-1649. Ubukhosi babuya ngowe-1660, kodwa iMfazwe Yamakhaya yamisela umzekelo wokuba ukumkani waseNgesi akanakulawula ngaphandle kwemvume yePalamente. Le ngcamango yamiselwa ngokusemthethweni njengenxalenye yeMvukelo Ezukileyo yowe-1688. Ukususela ngeli xesha ubukumkani baseNgilani, kwakunye nelizwe elingene ezihlangwini zabo iUnited Kingdom, basebenza ngokusebenzayo njengobukhosi obungokomgaqo-siseko.[a] Ngomhla woku-1 kuCanzibe 1707, phantsi kwemiqathango yeMithetho yeManyano yowe-1707, iipalamente, yaye ngenxa yoko izikumkani, zombini iNgilani neSkotlani zapheliswa. Izinto zabo kunye nemihlaba yabo imanyaniswe 'ngonaphakade, eBukumkanini ngegama leBritane enkulu', benza uBukumkani baseBritane enkulu kunye nePalamente yaseBritane. [7][8] 

Igama 
Inqaku eliphambili: Igama laseNgilani 
Ama-Anglo-Saxons azibiza ngokuba yi-Engle okanye i-Angelcynn, ekuqaleni amagama ee-Angles. Bawubiza umhlaba wabo ngokuba yiEngla, gama elo elithetha "umhlaba wamaNgesi", nguÆthelweard Latinized Anglia, evela kwiAnglia vetus yantlandlolo, ilizwe ekucingelwa ukuba lihlala kwii-Angles (elibizwa ngokuba nguAngulus ngoBede).[9] Igama elithi Engla umhlaba waba yiNgilani ngehaplology ngexesha lesiNgesi esiphakathi (Engle-land, Engelond) [10][iphepha elifunekayo] Igama lesiLatini laliyi-Anglia okanye i-Anglorum terra, i-Old French kunye ne-Anglo-Norman enye i-Engleterre.[11]

Iwonga eliqhelekileyo lookumkani ukusuka e-Æthelstan de kube nguJohn yayinguRex Anglorum (“uKumkani wamaNgesi”). UCnut, waseDane, wayengowokuqala ukuzibiza ngokuba "nguKumkani waseNgilani". Ngexesha lamaNorman uRex Anglorum wahlala esemgangathweni, ngokusetyenziswa ngamaxesha athile uRex Anglie ("uKumkani waseNgilani"). Ukususela kulawulo lukaYohane ukubheka phambili zonke ezinye izihloko zaye zaphetshwa zixhasa uRex okanye uRegina Anglie. Ngo-1604 uJames I, owafumana isihlalo sobukhosi samaNgesi kunyaka ophelileyo, wamkela isihloko (ngoku esiqhele ukuguqulelwa ngesiNgesi endaweni yesiLatini) uKumkani waseBritane.[b] 


Ubukumkani baseNgilani baphuma ekudibaneni ngokuthe ngcembe kwezikumkani zamandulo zama-Anglo-Saxon ezaziwa ngokuba yi-Heptarchy: i-East Anglia, iMercia, iNorthumbria, i-Essexssex, i-Sussex, i-Essexssex yaseSussex. Uhlaselo lweViking lwenkulungwane ye-9 luphazamise amandla phakathi kwezikumkani zamaNgesi, kunye nobomi bomthonyama base-Anglo-Saxon ngokubanzi. Imihlaba yamaNgesi yadityaniswa ngenkulungwane ye-10 kulwahlulo olwagqitywa ngama-927.[5] 

Ngexesha le-Heptarchy, oyena kumkani unamandla phakathi kobukumkani base-Anglo-Saxon unokuvunywa njengoBretwalda, ukumkani ophakamileyo phezu kwabanye ookumkani. Ukuwohloka kweMercia kwavumela iWessex ukuba ibe namandla ngakumbi, yathabatha izikumkani zaseKent naseSussex ngowama-825. Ngo-827, i-Northumbria yangenisa ku-Egbert wase-Wessex e-Dore, ngokufutshane yenza u-Egbert abe ngukumkani wokuqala ukulawula phezu kweNgilane emanyeneyo.[13] 

Ngo-886, uAlfred Omkhulu wayithimba kwakhona iLondon, ekubonakala ukuba wayigqala njengeyona nguqulelo kulawulo lwakhe. I-Anglo-Saxon Chronicle ithi "bonke abantu abangamaNgesi (bonke i-Angelcyn) ababengathotyelwanga phantsi kwamaDanes bazithoba kuKumkani uAlfred."[14] uAsser wongezelela ukuba "uAlfred, ukumkani wama-Anglo-Saxon, wasibuyisela isixeko saseLondon ngokumangalisayo ... kwaye wasenza ukuba kuhlale kuso kwakhona." Ukwakha iindawo 

zokuhlala ecaleni komlambo iThames, kunye nokubeka isicwangciso esitsha sesitrato sesixeko. Isihloko esithi "uKumkani wamaNgesi" okanye uRex Anglorum ngesiLatini, saqala ukusetyenziswa ukuchaza i-Æthelstan komnye wemiqulu yakhe ngo-928. Isihloko esiqhelekileyo sookumkani ukusuka e-Æthelstan de kube nguYohane "uKumkani wamaNgesi". Kwiminyaka elandelayo i-Northumbria yatshintsha ngokuphindaphindiweyo izandla phakathi kookumkani baseNgesi kunye nabahlaseli baseNorway, kodwa ngokuqinisekileyo yaziswa phantsi kolawulo lwesiNgesi ngu-Eadred ngo-954, igqibezela ukuhlanganiswa kweNgilani. Kunyaka we-1018, uLothian, inxalenye yesiqingatha esisemantla eNorthumbria Bernicia yanikezelwa kuBukumkani baseScotland. [18] [19]

 
Ulawulo lwe-Cnut (1014–1035)
INgilani iye yahlala imanyene kwezopolitiko ukususela ngoko. Ngexesha lolawulo luka-Æthelred i-Unready (978-1016), iliza elitsha lohlaselo lwaseDanish laqulunqwa ngu-Sweyn I waseDenmark, elafikelela incopho emva kwekota yenkulungwane yemfazwe kwiDanish yoloyiso lwaseNgilani ngo-1013. Ngo-1015, unyana kaSweyn u-Cnut (owaziwa njengeCanute) waqalisa uhlaselo olutsha. Imfazwe eyalandelayo yaphela ngesivumelwano ngo-1016 phakathi kukaCanute no-Æthelred owangena ezihlangwini zika-Edmund Ironside, ukuba bahlule iNgilani phakathi kwabo, kodwa ukufa kuka-Edmund nge-30 kaNovemba waloo nyaka kwayishiya iNgilani imanyene phantsi kolawulo lwaseDenmark. Oku kwaqhubeka iminyaka eyi-26 kwaze kwaba sekufeni kukaHarthacnut ngoJuni 1042. Wayengunyana kaCanute noEmma waseNormandy (umhlolokazi ka-Æthelred the Unready) kwaye wayengenazo iindlalifa zakhe; walandelwa ngumntakwabo ngamzali mnye, unyana ka-Æthelred, u-Edward the Confessor. [20] 

Norman Conquest 
Inqaku eliphambili: Uloyiso lukaNorman 
Uxolo lwahlala de kwasweleka uEdward owayengenamntwana ngoJanuwari 1066. Usibali wakhe wathweswa isithsaba njengoKumkani uHarold, kodwa umzala wakhe uWilliam uMnqobi, uDuke waseNormandy, ngoko nangoko wabanga itrone yakhe. UWilliam waqalisa uhlaselo lwaseNgilani waza wahlala eSussex ngomhla wama-28 kuSeptemba 1066. UHarold nomkhosi wakhe babeseYork kulandela uloyiso lwabo nxamnye namaNorwegian kwidabi laseStamford Bridge (25 Septemba 1066) xa iindaba zafika kuye. Wagqiba kwelokuba aphume ngaphandle kokulibazisa kwaye ajongane nomkhosi waseNorman eSussex ngoko nangoko waya emazantsi, ngaphandle kokuba umkhosi ungaphumlanga ngokufanelekileyo emva komlo kunye namaNorway. Imikhosi kaHarold noWilliam yajongana kwiDabi laseHastings (ngo-Oktobha 14, 1066), apho umkhosi wamaNgesi, okanye uFyrd, woyiswayo, uHarold nabantakwabo ababini babulawa, waza uWilliam waba yintshatsheli. Emva koko uWilliam wakwazi ukuyoyisa iNgilani ngaphandle kwenkcaso encinane. Noko ke, akazange acebe ukungenisa uBukumkani kwiDuchy yaseNormandy. Njengerhuluneli nje, uWilliam wayenetyala lokuthembeka kuPhilip I waseFransi, ngoxa kuBukumkani obuzimeleyo baseNgilani wayenokulawula ngaphandle kokuphazanyiswa. Wathweswa isithsaba nge-25 kaDisemba 1066 eWestminster Abbey, eLondon. 

AmaXesha aPhakathi aPhakamileyo 
Inqaku eliphambili: eNgilani kumaXesha aPhakathi aPhakamileyo 
Ulwazi olongezelelekileyo: uBukhosi baseAngevin, ukuhlasela kukaNorman eWales, kunye nokoyiswa kweWales nguEdward I.
Ngo-1092, uWilliam II wakhokela uhlaselo lwaseStrathclyde, ubukumkani baseCeltic kwindawo ngoku esemazantsi-ntshona eSkotlani naseCumbria. Ngokwenza oko, wahlohla indawo ngoku eyi-Cumbria eNgilani. Ngo-1124, uHenry I wanikezela into ngoku esemazantsi mpuma eSkotlani (ebizwa ngokuba yiLothian) kuBukumkani baseSkotlani, ngenxa yokunyaniseka kukaKumkani waseSkotlani. Oku kuqhawulwa kokugqibela kumisele into eya kuba yimida yemveli yaseNgilani ethe yahlala ingatshintshi ukusukela ngoko (ngaphandle kweenguqu zamathuba kunye nezexeshana). Lo mmandla womhlaba wawukade uyinxalenye yobukumkani base-Anglian baseNorthumbria. ILothian yayiqulethe into eyathi kamva yaba likomkhulu laseScotland, i-Edinburgh. Eli lungiselelo kamva laqukunjelwa ngo-1237 yiSivumelwano saseYork. [22] 


UKumkani uJohn usayina uMagna Carta eRunnymede ngo-1215, ejikelezwe yibhanari yakhe. Illustration from Cassell's History of England, 1902. 
Uhlaselo lwama-Anglo-Norman eIreland lwenzeka ekupheleni kwenkulungwane ye-12, xa ama-Anglo-Normans ngokuthe ngcembe athimba aza afumana umhlaba omkhulu kuma-Irish, ekwathi ngoko iNgilani yabanga ulongamo phezu kwawo, konke okutyholwa ukuba kwavunywa nguPopu bull Laudabiliter.[23] Ngelo xesha, iGaelic Ireland yayibunjwe zizikumkani ezininzi, kunye noKumkani oPhezulu obanga ubukhosi ngaphezu kwabanye ookumkani.[24] 

I-Duchy yase-Aquitaine yangena kumanyano lobuqu kunye neNgilani ekungeneni kukaHenry II, owayetshate no-Eleanor, iDuchess yase-Aquitaine. Bahlala bemanyene de uJohn Lackland, unyana kaHenry II kunye nesizukulwana sesine kwisizukulwana sikaWilliam uMnqobi, walahlekelwa yimpahla yelizwekazi kuPhilip II waseFransi ngokukhawuleza emva kweMfazwe yaseBouvines ngo-1214. Intsalela embalwa yaseNormandy, kuquka neZiqithi zeChannel, yahlala kwifa likaYohane, kunye neninzi yeDuchy of Aquitaine. 

Ukoyiswa kweWales 
ukuya kuthi ga kuNombolo kaNorman waseNgilani, iWales yayisele izimele ubukhulu becala kwizikumkani zase-Anglo-Saxon, nangona abanye ookumkani baseWales babekhe bayivume iBretwalda. Noko ke, kungekudala emva koloyiso lukaNorman lwaseNgilani, ezinye iinkosi zamaNorman zaqalisa ukuhlasela iWales. Bayoyisa baza balawula iinxalenye zayo, bevuma ukongama kookumkani baseNorman baseNgilani kodwa ngokukhululeka okukhulu kwendawo. Kwiminyaka emininzi le "Marcher Lords" yoyisa ngakumbi nangakumbi eWales, ngokuchasene nokuxhathisa okukhulu okukhokelwa ziinkosana ezahlukeneyo zaseWelsh, nazo ezihlala zivuma ukongamela kookumkani baseNorman baseNgilani. [26] [iphepha elifunekayo] 

u-Edward I woyisa uLlywelyn ap Gruffudd, kwaye ngoko ngempumelelo woyisa iWales, ngo-1282 wadala iNkosana yakhe ye-1282 kwi-Wales. 1301. Uloyiso luka-Edward I lwalunoburhalarhume kwaye ingcinezelo eyalandelayo yayininzi, njengoko iinqaba ezimangalisayo zaseWales ezifana neConwy, iHarlech, kunye neCaernarfon zingqina.[27] 

AmaXesha Aphakathi kade  
Inqaku eliphambili: ENgilani kumaXesha aPhakathi asekupheleni
Ulwazi olongezelelekileyo: Iimfazwe zeRoses, iMfazwe yeMinyaka eyikhulu,kunye ne-Great Slump (kwinkulungwane ye-15)

I-miniature yenkulungwane yeshumi elinesihlanu ebonisa uloyiso lwesiNgesi phezu kweFransi kwi-Battle of Agincourt 
Edward III wayeyinkosi yokuqala yamaNgesi ukuba nebango kwitrone yaseFransi. Ukusukela kwakhe elo bango kwaphumela kwiMfazwe Yeminyaka Elikhulu (1337–1453), eyabandakanya ookumkani abahlanu baseNgilani beNdlu yePlantagenet nxamnye nookumkani abahlanu baseFransi beNdlu yaseCapetian yaseValois. Uhlaselo olukhulu lwaselwandle lwenziwa macala onke ngexesha lemfazwe, ngokufuthi lubandakanya abantu abazimeleyo abafana noJohn Hawley waseDartmouth okanye iCastilian Pero Niño. Nangona amaNgesi aphumelele uloyiso oluninzi, awazange akwazi ukoyisa ukongama kwamanani amaFrentshi kunye nokusetyenziswa kwawo ngobuchule kwezixhobo zerhuluwa. INgilani yoyiswa kwiDabi laseFormigny ngo-1450 kwaye ekugqibeleni kwidabi laseCastillon ngo-1453, ligcina idolophu enye kuphela eFransi, eCalais. 

Ngexesha leMfazwe yeMinyaka eliKhulu isazisi samaNgesi saqala ukukhula endaweni yeyantlukwano yangaphambili phakathi kweenkosi zaseNorman kunye nezifundo zabo ze-Anglo-Saxon. Oku kwaba sisiphumo sobutshaba obuzinzileyo kumaFrentshi asanda ngobuzwe, ookumkani kunye nezinye iinkokeli (ngokukodwa uJoan wase-Arc onothando) wasebenzisa ingqiqo ekhulayo yesazisi samaFrentshi ukunceda ukutsalela abantu kwinjongo yabo.[29] 

Ubukumkani babanexesha elincinane lokubuyela emva kokungena kwiiMfazwe zeRoses (1455-1487), uthotho lweemfazwe zamakhaya ngenxa yokuba nesihlalo sobukhosi phakathi kweNdlu yaseLancaster (omqondiso wayo we-heraldic yayiyi rose ebomvu) kunye neNdlu yaseYork (esimboli sayo yayiyi roses emhlophe), nganye ikhokelwa ngamasebe ahlukeneyo enzalo ka-Edward III. Ukuphela kwezi mfazwe kwafumana itrone ebanjwe yinzala yelungu elingekho mthethweni leNdlu yaseLancaster, etshate nentombi enkulu yeNdlu yaseYork: uHenry VII no-Elizabeth waseYork. 

Ixesha leTudor 
Amanqaku aphambili: Ixesha likaTudor, ixesha likaElizabethan, ixesha likaStuart, kunye noHlaziyo lwesiNgesi 
Bona kwakhona: Ukoyiswa kukaTudor kweIreland 
IWales igcine inkqubo eyahlukileyo yomthetho nolawulo, eyayisekwe nguEdward I ngasekupheleni kwenkulungwane ye-13. Ilizwe lahlulahlulwe phakathi kweeNkosi zikaMarcher, ezathi zanikezela ngokuthembeka kwisithsaba, kunye neNqununu yaseWales. Phantsi kobukhosi bukaTudor, uHenry VIII wathatha indawo yemithetho yaseWales wabeka eyaseNgilani (phantsi kweMithetho eWales IZenzo 1535–1542). IWales yadityaniswa eNgilani, kwaye ukusukela ngoku iye yamelwa ePalamente. [31] 

 
Umfanekiso kaElizabeth I owenzelwa isikhumbuzo sokoyiswa kweArmada yaseSpain (1588), eboniswe ngasemva. Amandla kaElizabeth ezizwe ngezizwe afuziselwa sisandla esiphumle emhlabeni.
Ebudeni beminyaka yee-1530, uHenry wabhukuqa amandla eCawa yamaKatolika phakathi kobukumkani, ethatha indawo kapopu njengentloko yeCawa yakhe yamaNgesi waza wathimba imihlaba yeCawa yamaKatolika, ngaloo ndlela eququzelela ukudalwa kokwahluka kobuKatolika obabuba nobuProtestanti ngakumbi ekuhambeni kwexesha. Oku kwaba nomphumo wokulungelelanisa iNgilani neSkotlani, eyathi ngokuthe ngcembe yamkela unqulo lobuProtestanti, ngoxa awona magunya abalulekileyo elizwekazi, iFransi neSpeyin, ahlala engamaKatolika.[32]

"I-Tudor conquest" (okanye i-reconquest) yase-Ireland 'yenzeke phantsi kolawulo lukaTudor. Ukulandela imvukelo engaphumelelanga ngokuchasene nesithsaba nguSilken Thomas, i Earl of Kildare, kwi-1530s, uHenry VIII wabhengezwa njengoKumkani wase-Ireland ngo-1542 ngommiselo wePalamente yase-Ireland, ngenjongo yokubuyisela igunya eliphakathi njengoko lalilahlekile kulo lonke ilizwe kwiinkulungwane ezimbini ezidlulileyo.[33] 

ICalais, indawo yokugqibela eseleyo yoBukumkani kwilizwekazi, yalahleka ngowe-1558, ebudeni bolawulo lukaPhilip noMary I. Ilandela labo, uElizabeth I, lamanyanisa iCawa yamaProtestanti yaseTshetshi eyayisanda. Kwakhona waqala ukwakha amandla omkhosi waselwandle, kwiziseko uHenry VIII awayezibeke phantsi. Ngo-1588, umkhosi wakhe omtsha waselwandle wawusomelele ngokwaneleyo ukoyisa i-Armada yaseSpain, eyayifuna ukuhlasela iNgilani ukuze imise inkxaso yamaNgesi kubavukeli bamaDatshi nokubeka ukumkani ongumKatolika etroneni endaweni yakhe.[34][35][36] 

Imbali yamandulo yanamhlanje 
Amanqaku aphambili: IBritane yamandulo kunye nexesha leStuart 
Indlu kaTudor yaphela ngokusweleka kuka-Elizabeth I ngomhla wama-24 Matshi 1603. UJames I wenyuka esihlalweni sobukhosi baseNgilani waza wayizisa kumanyano lobuqu kunye noBukumkani baseScotland. Ngaphandle koManyano lweziCwangciso, izikumkani zahlala zahlukene kwaye zizimeleyo: imeko yemicimbi eyathatha iminyaka engaphezu kwekhulu.[37] 

Imfazwe yamakhaya kunye ne-Interregnum 
Amanqaku aphambili: Imfazwe yamakhaya yesiNgesi, i-Interregnum yesiNgesi, i-English Commonwealth, kunye neNgesi uMkhuseli 

uCromwell eDunbar. U-Oliver Cromwell wadibanisa i-British Isles yonke ngenkani waza wenza i-Commonwealth yaseNgilani. 
Ookumkani bakwaStuart bawaqiqisa kakhulu amandla obukumkani bamaNgesi, baza bawiswa phantsi yiPalamente ngowe-1645 nangowe-1688. Kwisihlandlo sokuqala, ukungenisa kukaCharles I iindlela ezintsha zokurhafiswa ngokudelela iPalamente kwakhokelela kwiMfazwe Yamakhaya yamaNgesi (1641–1645), apho ukumkani woyiswayo, nasekubhangisweni kobukhosi buka-Oliver Cromwell. 1649–1660 [38] 

Emva kokuxoxwa kwetyala kunye nokubulawa kukaCharles I ngoJanuwari 1649, iPalamente yaseRump yadlulisela isenzo esibhengeza iNgilani ukuba ibe yi-Commonwealth ngomhla we-19 kuMeyi 1649. Ubukhosi kunye neNdlu yeeNkosi zapheliswa, kwaye ngoko iNdlu yoBukhosi yaba yindlu yowiso-mthetho ehlangeneyo kunye nequmrhu elitsha, iBhunga leSizwe laba sisigqeba solawulo. Nangona kunjalo uMkhosi wasala ungowona ziko kwiriphabliki entsha kwaye oyena jikelele ubalaseleyo yayinguOliver Cromwell. I-Commonwealth yalwa iimfazwe e-Ireland naseSkotlani ezathi zoyiswa zaza zabekwa phantsi kolawulo lomkhosi we-Commonwealth.[39]

Ngeli xesha, ubudlelwane kunye neRiphabhlikhi yaseDatshi behlile. Ngaphandle kwenkxaso yokuqala yesiNgesi ngexesha leMfazwe yaseDatshi yeNkululeko ngokuchasene namaSpanish, kwabakho ukruthakruthwano njengoko iRiphabhlikhi yaseDatshi yavela njengeyona mbangi yaseNgilani yorhwebo kunye nomkhosi waselwandle. Phakathi kwinkulungwane ye-17, yaba lelona lizwe liphambili kwezorhwebo. Ukuphendula amaNgesi, ekhwankqisiwe lukhuphiswano lwawo olunciphayo, asebenzisa imigaqo-nkqubo engqongqo yorhwebo ukuze athintele ulawulo lwamaDatshi. IMfazwe yokuQala yamaNgesi namaDatshi eyalandelayo, nangona kunjalo, ayiphumelelanga ukusombulula imiba yorhwebo. [40][41] 

Ngo-Aprili 1653 uCromwell kunye nezinye iiGrandees zeNew Model Army, bedidekile kunye namalungu ePalamente yaseRump abangazange baphumelele umthetho wokuchitha iRump kunye nokuvumela ipalamente entsha yommeli ukuba inyulwe, bamisa iseshoni yeRump kwaye babhengeza ukuba iRump ichithwe. 

Emva kovavanyo lweNdibano eMiselweyo (iPalamente yaseBarebone), iiGrandees eMkhosini, ngeBhunga leSizwe lamisela ilungiselelo elitsha lomgaqo-siseko phantsi komgaqo-siseko obhaliweyo obizwa ngokuba yi-Instrument of Government. Phantsi kweSixhobo soLawulo lukaRhulumente amandla alawulayo ayenoMkhuseli weNkosi (i-ofisi eza kubanjwa ubomi bonke balowo usesikhundleni) kwaye bekufuneka kubekho iiPalamente zeminyaka emithathu, apho intlanganiso nganye yayihlala iinyanga ezintlanu ubuncinci. Inqaku lama-23 leSixhobo sikaRhulumente lathi u-Oliver Cromwell wayeza kuba nguMkhuseli wokuqala weNkosi. Isixhobo sikaRhulumente sathatyathelw’ indawo ngumgaqo-siseko wesibini (Isibongozo esithobekileyo neNgcebiso) apho uMkhuseli weNkosi wayenokutyumba indlalifa yakhe. UCromwell wonyula unyana wakhe uRichard owaba nguMkhuseli weNkosi ekufeni kuka-Oliver nge-3 Septemba 1658. [43] 

Ukubuyiselwa kunye neNguqu ezukileyo 
Amanqaku aphambili: Ukubuyiselwa (eNgilani) kunye neNguquko ezukileyo 

UCharles wahamba ngesikhephe esuka elubhacweni eNetherlands ukuya ekubuyiselweni kwakhe eNgilani ngoMeyi 1660. Ukupeyintwa nguLieve Verschuier. 
URichard akazange aphumelele yaye akazange akwazi ukuqhubeka nolawulo lwakhe. Warhoxa kwisihloko sakhe waza wathabatha umhlala phantsi. IPalamente yaseRump iye yabizwa kwakhona kwaye kwabakho ixesha lesibini apho amandla olawulo ayelele kwiBhunga likarhulumente. Kodwa oku kubuyiselwa kolawulo lweCommonwealth, olufana nolo lwaphambi koMkhuseli, lwangqineka lungazinzanga, kwaye ummangali owayegxothiwe, uCharles II, wabuyiselwa etroneni ngo-1660.[44]

Ngo-1665 imiba yorhwebo engasonjululwanga namaDatshi yakhokelela kwiMfazwe yesiBini yamaNgesi namaDatshi, eyafikelela kuvuthondaba ngoHlaselo olubi kwiMedway yaze yanyanzela uCharles owayethotyiwe ukuba angene kwisivumelwano soxolo esingathandekiyo. Umnqophiso wasusa imiba emininzi yexesha elide, kwaye kwixesha elide lenze ukuba amazwe amabini ahlangane ngokuchasene nemigaqo-nkqubo yokwandisa elandelwa nguLouis XIV waseFransi. Noko ke, kwixeshana elingephi, umnqweno kaCharles wokuphindezela lo mqobo wakhokelela kwiMfazwe yesiThathu yamaNgesi namaDatshi ngowe-1672. Phezu kwako nje ukufumana inkxaso yamaFrentshi ngesi sihlandlo, impumelelo yomkhosi waselwandle wamaDatshi yenza ukuba iPalamente ingazimiselanga ukuxhasa imfazwe kaCharles ngakumbi, yaye waphinda wanyanzelwa ukuba enze uxolo.[45] 

Emva kokuBuyiselwa kobukhosi ngowe-1660, ilinge likaJames II lokuphinda abuyisele ubuRoma Katolika—kwinkulungwane emva kokucinezelwa kwabo ngamaTudors—lakhokelela kwiMvukelo Ezukileyo yowe-1688, awathi kuyo wagxothwa yinkosana yamaDatshi uWilliam waseOrange. UWilliam nenkosikazi yakhe uMary bathweswa isithsaba yiPalamente. [46] UWilliam wahlengahlengisa umgaqo-nkqubo wangaphandle waseNgilani ukuxhasa iRiphabliki yaseDatshi kwiimfazwe zayo ezichasene noLouis XIV waseFransi. [c] [47] 

Union kunye neSkotlani 
Kwimeko yaseSkotlani, umtsalane wawuyinxenye yemali kwaye inxalenye yokwenza nokususa izohlwayo zorhwebo zesiNgesi ezibekwe nge-Alien Act 1705. AmaNgesi ayenexhala ngakumbi ngokulandelelana kobukhosi. Ukufa kukaWilliam III ngo-1702 kwakhokelela ekubeni udadezala wakhe u-Anne abekwe ezitroneni zaseNgilani naseSkotlani, kodwa ekuphela komntwana wakhe owasindayo wasweleka ngo-1700, kwaye uMthetho weNgesi wokuHlaliswa kwawo ngo-1701 wawunike ulandelelwano kwisithsaba seNgesi kwiNdlu yamaProtestanti yaseHanover. Ukuqinisekisa ukulandelelana okufanayo eSkotlani kwaba yeyona nto iphambili yokucinga ngobuchule besiNgesi ukuya eSkotlani. Ngo-1704, iManyano yamaTrown yayisengxakini, kunye noMthetho waseScotland woKhuseleko uvumela iPalamente yaseSkotlani ukuba ikhethe ukumkani owahlukileyo, nto leyo eyayinokukhokelela kumgaqo-nkqubo wangaphandle ozimeleyo ngexesha lemfazwe enkulu yaseYurophu.[48] 

ISivumelwano soManyano kwavunyelwana nge-22 kaJulayi 1706, kwaye emva kweMithetho yeManyano ye-1707, eyadala uBukumkani baseBritani eNkulu, ukuzimela kwezikumkani zaseNgilani naseSkotlani kwafikelela esiphelweni ngomhla woku-1 kuMeyi 1707. IMithetho yoManyano yenza umanyano lwezithethe kunye nomanyano lwemali kwaye ibonelele ukuba nayiphi na "imithetho kunye nemithetho engqinelanayo nemithetho "yokuchasana nemithetho" okanye "imithetho kunye nemithetho" engqinelanayo nemithetho "yemithetho" kunye nemithetho "eyayichasana nemithetho". "Yeka uze ube lilize." [49]

IPalamente yamaNgesi neyaseSkotlani yadityaniswa yaba yiPalamente yaseGreat Britain, eseWestminster, eLondon. Ngeli xesha iNgilani yayeka ukubakho njengequmrhu elizimeleyo lezopolitiko, kwaye ukususela ngoko ayizange ibe norhulumente welizwe. Imithetho yaseNgilani ayizange ichaphazeleke, igunya elisemthethweni liqhubeka lilelo laseNgilani naseWales, ngoxa iSkotlani saqhubeka sinemithetho neenkundla zomthetho. Oku kwaqhubeka emva komanyano lwe-1801 phakathi kwezikumkani zaseBritane kunye ne-Ireland, zenza i-United Kingdom ye-Great Britain ne-Ireland. Ngo-1922 i-Irish Free State yazihlubula kwi-United Kingdom, yakhokelela ekubeni leya mva yabizwa ngokuba yi-United Kingdom ye-Great Britain kunye ne-Northern Ireland.[50] Amanqaku aphambili 

kaRhulumente 
: Urhulumente kurhulumente wamaxesha aphakathi eNgilani kunye norhulumente kaElizabeth 
Ulwazi oluthe vetshe: Imbali yobukhosi bamaNgesi 
Ulwahlulo lweNdawo 
Ulwazi oluthe vetshe: Imimandla eyimbali yaseNgilani, Uluhlu lweeNdawo zaseNgilani, iDomesday Book, County palatine, imbali yesithili yesiNgesi, kunye nesiNgesi feudal barony 
. Bayekile ukusetyenziswa kulawulo kuphela ngokudala iingingqi zolawulo ngo-1889. [51][52] 

Ngokungafaniyo nenxalenye ezilawulayo ezizilawulayo eziquka imimandla yasezidolophini, amabala eNgilani yamaxesha aphakathi ayekho ngokuyintloko njengendlela yokunyanzeliswa kwamandla karhulumente, okwenza ukuba ookumkani babe nolawulo lwemimandla yasekuhlaleni ngabameli babo abanyuliweyo - ekuqaleni oosherifu kwaye kamva iinkosi-lieutenants - kunye nabagwebi abaphantsi babo boxolo.[53] Amacandelo ekuqaleni ayesetyenziselwa ulawulo lobulungisa, ukuqokelelwa kwerhafu kunye nokulungelelaniswa komkhosi, kwaye kamva kurhulumente wasekhaya kunye nonyulo lokumelwa kwepalamente. Eyokugqibela enjalo, i-County Palatine yaseDurham, ayizange iphulukane nesi simo sikhethekileyo de kwayinkulungwane ye-19 

. Ngenxa yokwahluka kwemvelaphi yawo le mimandla yahluka kakhulu ngobukhulu. Imida yedolophu yayimi ngokufanelekileyo phakathi kweMithetho yenkulungwane ye-16 kwizenzo zaseWales kunye noMthetho woRhulumente waseKhaya ka-1888.[56] I-shire nganye yayinoxanduva lokuqokelela irhafu kurhulumente ophakathi; kukhuseleko lwasekuhlaleni; kunye nobulungisa, ngeenkundla ze-assize.[57][iphepha elifunekayo]

Amandla ee-feudal barons ukulawula ukugcinwa kwawo komhlaba aye enziwa buthathaka kakhulu ngo-1290 ngummiselo kaQuia Emptores. I-feudal baronies yaba mhlawumbi iphelelwe lixesha (kodwa ayipheli) ekuyekisweni kwe-feudal tenure ngexesha leMfazwe yombango, njengoko kungqinwe yi-Tenures Abolition Act 1660 epasiswe phantsi koBuyiselo ethathela kude inkonzo ye-knight kunye namanye amalungelo asemthethweni. I-tenure by knight-service yapheliswa yaze yayekiswa kwaye imihlaba ephantsi kolu lawulo lwengqesho, kuqukwa nee-feudal baronies, ukusukela ngoku yabanjwa yi-socage (okt, ukutshintshiselana ngerenti yemali). I-English Fitzwalter Case ngo-1670 yagweba ukuba i-barony yi-tenure iye yayekiswa iminyaka emininzi kwaye nawaphi na amabango kwi-peerage ngesiseko esinjalo, okuthetha ilungelo lokuhlala kwiNdlu yeeNkosi, kwakungafuneki kuvuselelwe, okanye naliphi na ilungelo lokulandelelana ngokusekelwe kubo. 

UMthetho waseRhuddlan ngowe-1284 walandela ukoyiswa kweWales nguEdward I waseNgilani. Yathatha imihlaba ebanjwe ziiNkosana zaseGwynedd phantsi kwesihloko esithi "iNkosana yaseWales" njengenxalenye esemthethweni yelizwe laseNgilani, yaza yaseka imimandla yaseshire kwimodeli yesiNgesi kwezo ndawo. IiNkosi zikaMarcher zazibotshelelwa ngokuqhubekayo kookumkani bamaNgesi ngezibonelelo zemihlaba nobukhosi eNgilani. IBhunga laseWales kunye neMarches, elawulwa ukusuka kwiNqaba yaseLudlow, yaqala yasekwa ngu-Edward IV waseNgilani ukulawula imihlaba ebanjwe phantsi koBunqununu baseWales ngo-1472. 

Kwangelo xesha linye iBhunga laseWales lasekwa ngo-1472, iBhunga laseMantla lasekwa kwiingingqi ezisemantla eNgilani. Emva kokuba ingasasetyenziswa, yaphinda yasekwa ngo-1537 yaza yabhangiswa ngo-1641. IBhunga laseNtshona elahlala ixesha elifutshane lalikhona kwiLizwe laseNtshona phakathi kuka-1537 no-1540.[60] 

Irhafu 
Ngexesha le-Anglo-Saxon, i-geld okanye irhafu yepropathi yayitsalwa kuqala ngokusabela kuhlaselo lwaseDenmark kodwa kamva yaba yirhafu eqhelekileyo. Uninzi lwengeniso yenkosi efunyenwe kwi-royal demesne kunye "nefama" yonyaka evela kwi-shire nganye (imali emiselweyo ehlawulwe ngoonothimba ngelungelo lokulawula kunye nokwenza inzuzo kwimihlaba yasebukhosini). Ookumkani nabo benza ingeniso evela kwizohlwayo zenkundla kunye nolawulo lorhwebo.[61] Abantu babetyala inkonzo kakumkani ngohlobo lwe-trinoda necessitas-inkonzo ye-fyrd, i-burh building, kunye nokwakhiwa kwebhulorho.[62] 

Emva koloyiso luka-1066, amaNorman aqhubeka eqokelela ijeld rhoqo. Baye bazisa imithombo emitsha yengeniso esekwe kwiingqikelelo zobufeudalism. Ukumkani wayenelungelo lokuqokelela uncedo xa unyana wakhe wamazibulo ekhaliphile, intombi yakhe enkulu itshatile, okanye xa ukumkani efuna ukuzihlawulela intlawulelo. Kwakhona indlalifa yerhamncwa kwakufuneka ihlawule ukumkani ngaphambi kokuba ithabathe ilifa layo. Ukumkani wayekwanelungelo kwinkonzo yasemkhosini yabakhonzi bakhe, kodwa amagosa ayenokuhlawula i-scuage endaweni yoko. [63] 

Ezomkhosi 
: uMkhosi wamaNgesi kunye neMbali yeRoyal Navy (ngaphambi kwe1707)
Ngexesha le-Anglo-Saxon, iNgilani yayingenamkhosi omileyo. Ukumkani kunye nezihandiba zagcina imikhosi yasekhaya yobuchwephesha (jonga i-housecarl), kwaye onke amadoda akhululekileyo ayebophelelekile ukuba enze inkonzo yasemkhosini kwi-fyrd. Ukongeza, abanini beencwadi babebophelelekile ukuba babonelele ngenani elithile lamadoda ngokusekelwe kwinani leekhumba abanazo.[64] 

Emva kweNorman Conquest, imikhosi yendlu kakumkani yahlala isembindini wawo nawuphi na umkhosi wasebukhosini. I-Anglo-Saxon fyrd nayo yahlala isetyenziswa. Kodwa abantu baseNormans baphinda bazisa enye into entsha kumkhosi wamaNgesi. Abaqeshwa bakakumkani (iingqwayingqwayi zakhe) babebophelelekile ukuba balungiselele umkhosi wasebukhosini okanye babe ngamajoni axhobileyo. Itotali yenani lamajoni atyalwayo lalibizwa ngokuba yi-servitium debitum (ngesiLatini: "inkonzo etyalwayo"), kwaye umbhali-mbali uRichard Huscroft uqikelela ukuba eli nani lalimalunga nama-5,000. Enyanisweni, i-servitium debitum yayinkulu kunokuba nayiphi na inkosi yayiza kuyidinga ngexesha lemfazwe. Eyona njongo yayo yayikukuhlola ukuba singakanani na isigebenga awayenaso ukumkani. I-scuage yayisetyenziselwa ukuhlawulela amajoni, awayeyinxalenye ebalulekileyo yawo nawuphi na umkhosi waseNorman.[65] 



"Urhulumente woBunene bakhe" kunye "noRhulumente woBunene" zibhekisa apha. Ukusetyenziswa kweli gama, jonga uRhulumente kaNgangamsha (igama). 
Eli nqaku limalunga negunya elilawulayo lase-UK. Kubantu abakulawulo lwangoku lwase-Bhritane, bona i-frontbench yoRhulumente wase-Bhritane. Ngenkqubo ebanzi yezopolitiko yase-UK, bona iPolitics yase-United Kingdom.

Amanye amazwe 
vte
URhulumente woNgangamsha wakhe, [a] ishunqulelwe kuRhulumente we-HM [b] okanye ngenye indlela uRhulumente wase-UK, ligunya elilawulayo laseUnited Kingdom of Great Britain kunye noMntla Ireland.[4][5] Urhulumente ukhokelwa yinkulumbuso (uKeir Starmer ukusukela nge-5 kaJulayi 2024) onyula bonke abanye abaphathiswa. Ilizwe belinorhulumente wezabaSebenzi ukusukela ngo-2024. Inkulumbuso kunye nabaphathiswa bakhe abakhulu bakwikomiti ephezulu yokwenza izigqibo, eyaziwa ngokuba yiKhabhinethi.[5] 

Abaphathiswa boBukhosi banoxanduva kwiNdlu abahlala kuyo; benza iinkcazo kuloo Ndlu kwaye bathathe imibuzo kumalungu aloo Ndlu. Kuninzi lwabaphathiswa abaphezulu le iqhele ukuba yiNdlu yeeMimandla eyonyuliweyo kuneNdlu yeeNkosi. Urhulumente uxhomekeke kwiPalamente ukuba yenze umthetho ophambili, [6] kwaye unyulo jikelele lubanjwa rhoqo emva kweminyaka emihlanu (ubuninzi) ukunyula iNdlu entsha yeMibutho, ngaphandle kokuba inkulumbuso icebisa ukumkani ukuba ayichithe iPalamente, apho unyulo lunokuthi lubanjwe ngokukhawuleza. Emva konyulo, inkosi ikhetha njengenkulumbuso inkokeli yeqela ekunokwenzeka ukuba iyalele intembeko yeNdlu yoWiso-mthetho, idla ngokuba nesininzi samaLungu ePalamente.[7] 

Phantsi komgaqo-siseko waseBhritane ongabhalwanga, igunya lesigqeba lilele kumlawuli, nangona eli gunya lisetyenziswa kuphela emva kokufumana ingcebiso yeBhunga labucala.[8] Inkulumbuso, iNdlu yeeNkosi, inkokeli yeqela eliphikisayo, kunye namapolisa kunye nomkhosi ophakamileyo womkhosi basebenza njengamalungu kunye nabacebisi bokumkani kwiBhunga lePrivy. Kwiimeko ezininzi ikhabhinethi isebenzisa amagunya ngokuthe ngqo njengeenkokeli zamasebe karhulumente, nangona ezinye izikhundla zeKhabhinethi zisisikhundla esikhulu okanye esingaphantsi (umzekelo iNgqonyela yeDuchy yaseLancaster okanye iLord Privy Seal). 

Urhulumente ngamanye amaxesha ubizwa ngegama elithi "Westminster" okanye "Whitehall", njengoko uninzi lweeofisi zakhe zilapho. Ezi zifaniso zisetyenziswa ngokukodwa ngamalungu kaRhulumente waseScotland, uRhulumente waseWelsh kunye neNorthern Ireland Executive ukuze bahlule urhulumente wabo kuRhulumente woBunene. 

Imbali 
Olunye ulwazi: Imbali yomgaqo-siseko we-United Kingdom kunye neMbali yobukhosi e-United Kingdom 
I-United Kingdom yi-monarchy yomgaqo-siseko apho ukumkani olawulayo (oko kukuthi, ukumkani okanye ukumkanikazi oyintloko yelizwe nangaliphi na ixesha) akenzi naziphi na izigqibo zezopolitiko ezivulekileyo. Zonke izigqibo zezopolitiko zithathwa ngurhulumente kunye nePalamente. Esi simo somgaqo-siseko sisiphumo sembali ende yokunyanzeliswa kunye nokunciphisa amandla ezopolitiko enkosi, eqala ngoMagna Carta ngo-1215.

Ukusukela ekuqaleni kolawulo luka-Edward VII ngo-1901, ngengqungquthela, inkulumbuso iye yaba lilungu elinyuliweyo lePalamente (MP) kwaye ke ngoko iphendule kwiNdlu yeeMibutho, nangona bekukho iiveki ezimbini ngo-1963 xa uAlec Douglas-Home wayelilungu lokuqala leNdlu yeeNkosi kwaye emva koko kungekho ndlu. Ingqungquthela efanayo iyasebenza kwisikhundla se-chancellor ye-exchequer. Ingqonyela yokugqibela ye-exchequer ukuba lilungu leNdlu yeeNkosi nguLord Denman, owasebenza inyanga enye ngo-1834.[9] Inqaku eliphambili: 

Ilungelo 
lasebukhosini 
e-United Kingdom 
Inkosi yaseBritane yintloko yelizwe kunye nomlawuli, kodwa hayi intloko karhulumente. Ngokwesiqhelo, ukumkani udla ngokuthabatha inxaxheba encinane ekulawuleni ilizwe kwaye akathathi cala kwimicimbi yezopolitiko. Nangona kunjalo, igunya likarhulumente eliphathiswe ulongamo, owaziwa ngokuba siSithsaba, lihlala lingumthombo wamandla olawulo asetyenziswa ngurhulumente. 

Ukongeza kwigunya elisemthethweni elicacileyo, i-Crown ikwanequmrhu lamagunya kwimiba ethile ngokudibeneyo eyaziwa ngokuba lilungelo lasebukhosini. La magunya asusela kwigunya lokukhupha okanye lokurhoxisa iincwadana zokundwendwela ukuya kwizibhengezo zemfazwe. Ngengqungquthela ekudala ikho, uninzi lwala magunya asuka kumlawuli anikezelwe kubaphathiswa abohlukeneyo okanye amanye amagosa oBukhosi, abanokuthi bawasebenzise ngaphandle kokufumana imvume yePalamente. 

Inkulumbuso ikwaba neendibano qho ngeveki nokumkani. Into ethethwayo kwezi ntlanganiso iyimfihlo ngokungqongqo; nangona kunjalo, ngokubanzi zibandakanya urhulumente kunye nemicimbi yezopolitiko apho ukumkani "anelungelo kunye nomsebenzi" wokuphawula. [10] Ezo zimvo azibopheleli nangona kunjalo kwaye uKumkani kufuneka ekugqibeleni athobele izigqibo zikarhulumente.[11] 

Amagunya anelungelo lobukhosi aquka, kodwa akaphelelanga koku kulandelayo: 

Amagunya asekhaya 

uKumkanikazi uElizabeth II efumana iNkulumbuso uTony Blair emva kokuphumelela isihlandlo sesithathu e-ofisini ngomhla wesi-6 kuMeyi ka-2005 
Amandla okumisela nokugxotha inkulumbuso. La mandla asetyenziswa yinkosi buqu. Noko ke, ixesha lokugqibela uKumkani wasebenzisa ingqiqo yakhe xa esebenzisa eli gunya ngowe-1834, kunye nengqungquthela yale mihla abamisela yona (kwaye kulindeleke ukuba banyule) oyena mntu ekunokwenzeka ukuba abe nako ukukhokela isininzi kwiNdlu yoWiso-mthetho.[12] 
Igunya lokumisela nokugxotha abanye abaphathiswa. Eli gunya lisetyenziswa yinkosi ngokwengcebiso yenkulumbuso. 
Igunya lokuvuma nokuwisa imithetho ngokunika imvume yasebukhosini kwimithetho eyilwayo epasiswe yiPalamente, efunekayo ukuze umthetho usebenze (ube ngumthetho). Oku kwenziwa yinkosi, ekwanamandla okwala ukuvunywa, nangona kungekho kumkani yale ukwamkelwa kumthetho oyilwayo owapasiswa yiPalamente ukusukela kuKumkanikazi u-Anne ngo-1708.
Amandla okunika kunye nokukhupha iikhomishini kumagosa agunyazisiweyo kuMkhosi. 
Imibuzo yeNkulumbuso, 2024 
Amandla okuyalela uMkhosi oxhobileyo. Eli gunya lisetyenziswa liBhunga lezoKhuselo egameni leKumkani. 
Igunya lokunyula amalungu kwiBhunga labucala.
Amandla okukhupha, ukunqumamisa, ukurhoxisa, ukukhumbula, ukubamba, ukurhoxisa, okanye ukurhoxisa iipaspoti zaseBritane kunye namandla ngokubanzi okubonelela okanye ukwala izibonelelo zepaspoti zaseBritane kubemi baseBritane nabemi baseBritane. Oku kwenziwa eUnited Kingdom (kodwa akunyanzelekanga ukuba kwiIsle of Man, Channel Islands okanye kwiBritish Overseas Territories) ngunobhala wekhaya. 
Igunya lokuxolela nakuphi na ukugwetyelwa (ilungelo lasebukhosini lenceba). 
Igunya lokunika, ukurhoxisa kunye nokubhangisa nawaphi na amawonga. 
Amandla okudala amaqumrhu (kubandakanywa newonga lokuba sisixeko, kunye nequmrhu laso) ngomqulu wamalungelo, kunye nokuguqula, ukubuyisela kunye nokurhoxisa imiqulu ekhoyo. 
Amagunya angaphandle 

, i-Ofisi ye-Commonwealth kunye noPhuhliso, i-Whitehall 
Amandla okwenza kunye nokuqinisekisa izivumelwano. 
Amandla okuvakalisa imfazwe nokugqiba uxolo nezinye iintlanga. 
Amandla okuhambisa uMkhosi oxhobileyo phesheya kolwandle. 
Amandla okuqonda amazwe. 
Amandla okuthenga ngetyala kwaye afumane oonozakuzaku. 
Nangona kungekho maxwebhu asemthethweni abeka amalungelo, urhulumente wapapasha olu luhlu lungasentla ngo-Okthobha ka-2003 ukwandisa ukungafihli, njengoko amanye amagunya asetyenziswa egameni lokumkani eyinxalenye yelungelo lobukhosi.[13] Nangona kunjalo, ubungakanani obupheleleyo bamagunya asebukhosini abuzange buchazwe ngokupheleleyo, njengoko uninzi lwawo luvela kwisithethe samandulo kunye nexesha lobukumkani obupheleleyo, okanye alungiswa ngomgaqo-siseko wamva. 

Abaphathiswa kunye namasebe 
Amanqaku aphambili: Uluhlu lwabaphathiswa bakarhulumente base-United Kingdom kunye namaSebe kaRhulumente wase-United Kingdom 
Ukusukela ngo-2019, kukho malunga ne-120 yabaphathiswa bakarhulumente[14] abaxhaswa ngabasebenzi bakarhulumente abangama-560,000[15] kunye nabanye abasebenzi abasebenza kumasebe angama-24 omphathiswa[16] kunye neearhente zabo ezilawulayo. Kukwakho namanye amasebe angama-20 angengawo amacandelo anoluhlu lwemisebenzi eyongezelelweyo. 

Ngokwethiyori, umphathiswa karhulumente akanyanzelekanga ukuba abe lilungu layo nayiphi na iNdlu yePalamente. Ngokwenyani, nangona kunjalo, ingqungquthela yeyokuba abaphathiswa kufuneka babe ngamalungu eNdlu yeeNkosi okanye eNdlu yeeNkosi ukuze baphendule kwiPalamente. Amaxesha ngamaxesha, iinkulumbuso zinyula abantu abangengabo amalungu epalamente njengabaphathiswa. Kwiminyaka yakutshanje aba befundisi baye bonyulwa kwiNdlu yeeNkosi.[17] 

Urhulumente ePalamente

Urhulumente ufunwa yingqungquthela kunye nezizathu ezibambekayo zokugcina ukuzithemba kweNdlu yeeMimandla. Ifuna inkxaso yeNdlu yoWiso-mthetho yokugcina unikezelo (ngokuvota ngohlahlo lwabiwo-mali lukarhulumente) kunye nokuwisa umthetho ophambili. Ngokwengqungquthela, ukuba urhulumente ulahlekelwa yintembeko yeNdlu yoWiso-mthetho kufuneka arhoxe okanye kubanjwe unyulo jikelele. Inkxaso yeenkosi, nangona iluncedo kurhulumente ekuphumezeni umthetho wakhe ngaphandle kokulibazisa, ayibalulekanga. Urhulumente akanyanzelekanga ukuba arhoxe nokuba ulahlekelwe kukuthenjwa ziinkosi kwaye woyiswe kwiivoti eziphambili kuloo Ndlu. I-House of Commons yindlu enoxanduva. 

Inkulumbuso iya kuphendula ngexesha leMibuzo yeNkulumbuso (PMQs) enika ithuba kumalungu ePalamente kuwo onke amaqela ukuba abuze i-PM ngawo nawuphi na umba. Kukwakho nemibuzo yesebe xa abaphathiswa bephendula imibuzo ephathelele kushwankathelo lwesebe labo. Ngokungafaniyo nee-PMQs, bobabini abaphathiswa bekhabhinethi besebe kunye nabaphathiswa abancinci kwisebe banokuphendula egameni likarhulumente, ngokuxhomekeke kumxholo wombuzo. 

Ngexesha leengxoxo malunga nomthetho ocetywayo ngurhulumente, abaphathiswa-abadla ngokuba noxanduva lwesebe lomthetho oyilwayo-baya kukhokela ingxoxo karhulumente kwaye baphendule kumaphuzu abekwe ngamaLungu ePalamente okanye iiNkosi. 

IiKomiti[18] zazo zombini iNdlu yoWiso-mthetho kunye neNdlu yeeNkosi zibambe urhulumente ukuba aphendule, aphicothe umsebenzi wakhe kwaye avavanye ngokweenkcukacha izindululo zomthetho. Abaphathiswa bavela phambi kweekomiti ukunika ubungqina kwaye baphendule imibuzo. 

Abaphathiswa bakarhulumente nabo kufuneka ngokwengqungquthela kunye neKhowudi yoMphathiswa, [19] xa iPalamente ihleli, ukuba benze iinkcazo ezinkulu malunga nomgaqo-nkqubo karhulumente okanye imiba ebaluleke kakhulu kwiPalamente. Oku kuvumela amalungu ePalamente okanye iiNkosi ukuba abuze urhulumente malunga nengxelo. Xa urhulumente endaweni yoko ekhetha ukwenza izibhengezo kuqala ngaphandle kwePalamente, kudla ngokuba ngumxholo wokugxekwa okubalulekileyo kumaLungu ePalamente kunye nosomlomo weNdlu yoWiso-mthetho.[20] 

Indawo 

Umnyango omkhulu we-10 Downing Street, indawo yokuhlala esemthethweni kunye ne-ofisi yeNkosi yokuQala ye-Ofisi kaNondyebo, ngokwesiko kule mihla ikwayinkulumbuso Inkulumbuso 
isekelwe e-10 Downing Street eWestminster, eLondon. Iintlanganiso zeKhabhinethi nazo zibanjelwa apha. Uninzi lwamasebe karhulumente anekomkhulu lawo elikufutshane eWhitehall. 

Imida yamandla karhulumente 
Jonga kwakhona: UMthetho wePalamente (e-UK) kunye naMagunya enkulumbuso yase-United Kingdom
Amagunya karhulumente aquka amandla olawulo jikelele kunye namagunya amiselwe ngokomthetho, uwiso-mthetho olunikezelweyo, kunye namagunya amaninzi okutyumba kunye nokuxhasa. Nangona kunjalo, amanye amagosa anamandla kunye namaqumrhu, (umz. iijaji ze-HM, oogunyaziwe bengingqi, kunye neekhomishini zesisa) zizimele ngokusemthethweni ngakumbi okanye ngaphantsi kurhulumente, kwaye amagunya karhulumente anqunyelwe ngokusemthethweni kulawo agcinwe nguBukhosi phantsi komthetho oqhelekileyo okanye anikwe kwaye anqunyelwe ngumthetho wePalamente. Zombini izithintelo ezibambekayo kunye neenkqubo zinyanzeliswa kwiinkundla ngokuphononongwa kwenkundla. 

Nangona kunjalo, oomantyi noosodolophu basengabanjwa baze bagwetywe ngenxa yorhwaphilizo, kwaye urhulumente unamagunya okufaka abakomishinala kurhulumente wengingqi ukuba abeke iliso kumsebenzi wawo, nokukhupha imiyalelo ekufuneka ithotyelwe ngumasipala ukuba ngaba umasipala akawuthobeli uxanduva lwakhe olusemthethweni.[21] 

Ngokwahlukileyo, njengakumazwe angamalungu e-European Union (EU), amagosa e-EU akanakutshutshiswa ngazo naziphi na izenzo ezenziwayo ekulandeleni imisebenzi yawo esemthethweni, kunye noonozakuzaku belizwe langaphandle (nangona ingengabo abasebenzi babo) kunye namalungu angaphandle ePalamente yaseYurophu[22] abakhuselekanga ekutshutshisweni kumazwe e-EU phantsi kwayo nayiphi na imeko. Ngenxa yoko, akufuneki ukuba amaqumrhu e-EU okanye oonozakuzaku bahlawule irhafu, kuba bekungenakwenzeka ukuba batshutshiswe ngokuphepha irhafu. Xa i-UK yayililungu le-EU, oku kwabangela ingxabano xa unozakuzaku wase-US e-UK wabanga ukuba intlawulo yokuxinana yaseLondon yayiyirhafu, kwaye ayikho intlawulo (nangona igama), kwaye ngoko ke akazange ayihlawule-ibango i-Greater London Authority yaphikisana. 

Ngokufanayo, inkosi ikhuselekile kutshutshiso lolwaphulo-mthetho kwaye inokumangalelwa kuphela ngemvume yayo (oku kwaziwa njengokungakhuseleki okuzimeleyo). Umlawuli, ngokomthetho, akafuneki ukuba ahlawule irhafu yengeniso, kodwa uKumkanikazi u-Elizabeth II ngokuzithandela wayihlawula ukusuka ngo-1993 de kube sekupheleni kolawulo lwakhe ngo-2022, kwaye wahlawula iirhafu zasekhaya ngokuzithandela. Nangona kunjalo, ubukhosi bukwafumene isibonelelo esikhulu kurhulumente, iSibonelelo seNkxaso eNgameleyo, kunye nelifa likaKumkanikazi uElizabeth II elivela kunina, uKumkanikazi u-Elizabeth uMama weKumkanikazi, wayekhululwe kwirhafu yelifa. 

Ukongeza kumagunya owiso-mthetho, uRhulumente obekekileyo unempembelelo enkulu kumagunya asekuhlaleni kunye namanye amaqumrhu amiswe nguye, ngamandla emali kunye nezibonelelo. Imisebenzi emininzi eyenziwa ngoogunyaziwe bengingqi, efana nokuhlawula izibonelelo zezindlu kunye nezibonelelo zerhafu yebhunga, ixhaswa ngemali okanye inxalenye enkulu yenkxaso-mali ngurhulumente omkhulu.

Akukho rhulumente oyintloko okanye oogunyaziwe basekhaya abavumelekanga ukuba bamangalele nabani na ngokunyelisa. Abantu bezopolitiko ngabanye bavumelekile ukuba bamangalele abantu ngokungcoliswa kwisikhundla somntu kwaye ngaphandle kokusebenzisa imali karhulumente, kodwa oku kunqabile (nangona uGeorge Galloway, owayelilungu le-backbench kwikota yenkulungwane, uye wamangalela okanye woyikisa ngokumangalela ngokungcolisa izihlandlo ezininzi). Nangona kunjalo, lityala lolwaphulo-mthetho ukwenza ingxelo yobuxoki malunga nawuphi na umgqatswa wonyulo ngexesha lonyulo, ukunciphisa inani leevoti abazifumanayo (njengoko kunye ne-libel, izimvo azibali). 

Isigama 

Intlanganiso yekhabhinethi kwiGumbi leKhabhinethi, 10 Downing Street 
Ngelixa urhulumente eliqela langoku labaphathiswa (i-Bhritane Government frontbench), urhulumente ngamanye amaxesha ubonwa ngokubanzi njengokubandakanya abantu okanye imibutho esebenzela abaphathiswa. Inkonzo karhulumente, ngelixa 'izimele kurhulumente', [23] ngamanye amaxesha ichazwa njengenxalenye karhulumente, [24][25][26][27] ngenxa yokusondelelana nokusebenza kwayo nabaphathiswa, ukubacebisa, ukuxhasa, kunye nokuphumeza izigqibo zabo zesigqeba. Abanye abantu abasebenzela abaphathiswa bade babe negama elithi 'uRhulumente' kwizihloko zabo, njengeGovernment Actuary kunye noMcebisi wezeNzululwazi oyiNtloko kaRhulumente, ngokunjalo nemibutho yenkonzo karhulumente efana neGovernment Statistical Service, iGovernment Legal Profession, neOfisi kaRhulumente yeSayensi. Iinkampani eziphantsi kukarhulumente nazo zinokubonwa njengenxalenye karhulumente, njengoTyalo-mali lukaRhulumente wase-UK [28] kunye ne-HS2 Ltd. [29] 

Ngokunjalo, oonobhala bePalamente babucala abangobaphathiswa kwaye abayonxalenye karhulumente. [30] Nangona kunjalo, zibotshelelwe ziinxalenye zekhowudi yomphathiswa, ziyinxalenye yevoti yomvuzo, kwaye zinokubonwa 'njengakwinqanaba lokuqala leleli yomphathiswa'.[31][32] Ngamanye amaxesha bachazwa njengenxalenye karhulumente.[33][34][35] 

Iimpawu 
Inqaku eliphambili: Idyasi yengalo yase-United Kingdom 

Iingalo ezincinci ezisetyenzisiweyo ukusukela ngo-2024 
Urhulumente wase-UK usebenzisa indlela eyenziwe lula yeengalo zasebukhosini njengelogo ebizwa ngokuba ziingalo ezincinci. Iqhele ukushiya ihelm kunye ne-mantling, inciphisa i-crest ibe sisithsaba sodwa, kwaye ayinayo indawo.[36] Nangona i-blazon yeengalo ayizange itshintshe ukususela ngo-1837, umboniso omtsha we-Royal Arms wenziwa kulawulo olutsha ngalunye.[36]

Ukusetyenziswa kweArms yasebukhosini ngamasebe kunye neearhente zikarhulumente kulawulwa yiOfisi yeKhabhinethi.[37] I-Royal Arms ibonakala kuyo yonke iMithetho yePalamente, kwiilogos zamasebe karhulumente, kuqweqwe lwazo zonke iincwadana zokundwendwela zase-UK (kunye neepaspoti ezikhutshwe kweminye imimandla yaseBritane kunye nokuxhomekeka), njenge-inescutcheon kwiiflegi zozakuzo zoonozakuzaku baseBritane, nakwi-The London Gazette. Ikwasetyenziswa nakwiiNgingqi zaseBritish Overseas, ezizezi kuzo zonke izenzo zeNdlu yeNdibano yase-Anguilla kunye nolawulo lwe-Akrotiri kunye neDhekelia, ii-Pitcairn Islands, kunye ne-South Georgia kunye ne-South Sandwich Islands. 

Amanye amasebe asebenzisa isimboli eyahlukileyo njengezizathu zembali yelogo, kuquka iOfisi yaseScotland, iOfisi yeKhaya, iSebe lezoKhuselo kunye neSebe lezoShishino noRhwebo. [37] 

Oorhulumente abaDlulisiweyo 
Inqaku eliphambili: Unikezelo lwelizwe e-United Kingdom 
Ulwazi oluthe vetshe: uRhulumente waseSkotlani, iSigqeba saseNorthern Ireland, kunye noRhulumente waseWelsh 
Ukusukela ngo-1999, imimandla ethile yorhulumente ophakathi iye yanikezelwa koorhulumente abaphendulayo eScotland, Wales naseNorthern Ireland. Aba abayonxalenye yoRhulumente woNgangamsha, kwaye baphendula ngokuthe ngqo kumaziko abo, negunya labo phantsi koBukhosi; ngokuchaseneyo, akukho rhulumente wesizwe ogqithiselweyo eNgilani, nangona amagunya athile karhulumente ophakathi anikezelwe kwiGunya eliKhulu laseLondon kunye namagunya adibeneyo. 

Urhulumente wasekhaya 
Amanqaku aphambili: Urhulumente wasekhaya eNgilani, eSkotlani, eWales, naseMntla Ireland 
Ukuya kuthi ga kwimigangatho emithathu yamagunya asekuhlaleni anyuliweyo (anje ngenqila, ibhunga lerhamente yamabhunga) akhoyo kuzo zonke iindawo zaseUnited Kingdom, kwezinye iindawo ezidityanisiweyo zaba ngamagunya amanyeneyo. Banamandla alinganiselweyo okunyusa irhafu. Amanye amagunya amaninzi kunye namaziko nawo anamagunya asemthethweni, aphantsi kolawulo lukarhulumente. 



UClement Attlee wamenywa nguKumkani uGeorge VI ukuba enze inkonzo yokuqala yase-Attlee e-United Kingdom nge-26 kaJulayi 1945, [1] wangena ezihlangwini zikaWinston Churchill njengenkulumbuso yase-United Kingdom. I-Labour Party yaphumelela uloyiso kunyulo jikelele luka-1945, yaza yaqhubela phambili ukumisela imigaqo-nkqubo yoko kwaziwa ngokuba yimvumelwano yasemva kwemfazwe, kuquka nokusekwa kwentlalo-ntle kunye nokubekwa phantsi kwe-20 ekhulwini loqoqosho luphela.[2] Ukubetha kukarhulumente eofisini kwaphawulwa ngamanyathelo okunciphisa emva kwemfazwe; ukutyunyuzwa kweentshukumo ezixhasa ukuzimela kunye nezobukomanisi eMalaya; ukunikezelwa kokuzimela kweIndiya, iPakistan, iCeylon, neBurma; ukuzibandakanya kwiMfazwe Yomlomo echasene nobuKomanisi baseSoviet; kunye nokudalwa kweNkonzo yeSizwe yezeMpilo yelizwe (NHS).

U-Attlee uye waphumelela isininzi esimxinwa kunyulo jikelele luka-1950, esenza inkonzo yesibini yase-Attlee. Kwiinyanga nje ezingamashumi amabini emva kolonyulo, u-Attlee wabiza unyulo olutsha lwe-25 ka-Okthobha ka-1951, kodwa woyiswa kancinane yi-Conservative Party, yathumela uMsebenzi kwisithuba seminyaka eli-13 ngokuchaseneyo. 

Iinkokeli 
Iqela lezabasebenzi langena kulawulo kulandela uloyiso lwalo olungalindelekanga kunyulo lukaJulayi 1945. Inkokeli yeqela uClement Attlee waba yinkulumbuso ethatha indawo kaWinston Churchill ngasekupheleni kukaJulayi. U-Ernest Bevin wayenguNobhala Wezangaphandle kwaze kwaba nje ngaphambi kokufa kwakhe ngo-Aprili 1951. UHugh Dalton waba nguChancellor we-Exchequer (nangona kwafuneka arhoxe kwi-1947), ngoxa uJames Chuter Ede wayenguNobhala weKhaya. 

Amanye amanani aphawulekayo kurhulumente aquka: u-Herbert Morrison, uSekela-Nkulumbuso kunye neNkokeli yeNdlu yoBukhosi, owathatha indawo kaBevin njengoNobhala Wezangaphandle ngoMatshi 1951; UMhlekazi u-Stafford Cripps ekuqaleni wayenguMongameli weBhodi yezoRhwebo kodwa wathatha indawo ka-Dalton njengeNgqonyela ye-Exchequer ngo-1947; UHugh Gaitskell wabamba izithuba ezincinci ezimbalwa ngaphambi kokuthatha indawo yeCripps njengeChancellor kwi-1950; U-Aneurin Bevan wayenguMphathiswa wezeMpilo; U-Arthur Greenwood wayeyi-Lord Privy Seal kunye ne-Paymaster General ngelixa u-Nkulumbuso wexesha elizayo u-Harold Wilson waba lilungu elincinci lekhabhinethi kwi-20th inkulungwane (eneminyaka eyi-31) xa wenziwa uMongameli weBhodi yezoRhwebo ngo-1947. Eyona nto iphawulekayo kumalungu ambalwa amabhinqa karhulumente ngu-Ellen Wilkinson, owayenguMphathiswa wezeMfundo de wafa kwi-Powaiesr47 

inqaku 
lokuqala. (1945-1979) 

Ikhathuni yangoku kwimagazini yasePoland satirical Szpilki igxeka inkonzo yase-Attlee 
"Yayiyixesha lobungqongqo", njengoko umlinganiselo wexesha lemfazwe wawuqhubekile nangona uloyiso lwe-Allied Forces, kwaye yade yandiswa ukuze iquke isonka. Iimeko zokuphila zazimbi; endaweni yokwanda, umsebenzi welizwe yayikukuthabathel’ indawo ubutyebi belizwe obatshatyalaliswayo okanye obabusetyenziswa ebudeni bemfazwe. UkuDodobala Okukhulu akuzange kubuye, kwaye kwadaleka umsebenzi opheleleyo. Amagqala abuyayo aphinda aphinda aphinda aphinda afakwa kuluntu lwasemva kwemfazwe.[5] Urhulumente wase-Attlee waqulunqa ilizwe malunga ne-20% yezoqoqosho, kubandakanywa amalahle, umzila kaloliwe, izithuthi zendlela, iBhanki yaseNgilani, i-aviation civil, umbane kunye negesi, kunye nentsimbi. Ibincinci imali yotyalo-mali ukwenza la mashishini aphucuke, kwaye ulawulo lwagcinwa ngurhulumente, kunokuba lugqithiselwe kumalungu emanyano. Urhulumente wase-Attlee wandise kakhulu urhulumente wentlalontle, kunye noMthetho weNkonzo yezeMpilo yeSizwe we-1946, owenzela izibhedlele kuzwelonke kwaye wanikezela ngokhathalelo lwezempilo lwasimahla jikelele. INational Insurance Act 1946 ibonelele ngezibonelelo zokugula nokungaphangeli kubantu abadala, kunye nemali yomhlalaphantsi.

Iskimu soNcedo lweSizwe esekwe phantsi koMthetho woNcedo weSizwe ka-1948 (11 & 12 Geo. 6. c. 29) lubonelele ngengqiqo yokongezwa kweveki ukuhlangabezana neemeko ezikhethekileyo ezifana nokutya kunye neendleko zokuhlamba impahla, ngexa ngokwengqiqo yeBhodi yoNcedo yeSizwe 'Izibonelelo zeemfuno ezikhethekileyo' (iintlawulo zesambuku eziye zavela kwiindidi ezikhethekileyo zeentlawulo ezifumanekayo. Ukongeza, "irenti yayijongwa njengento efunekayo: abaninimzi babeya kufumana irenti ngokupheleleyo, ngelixa abangengabo babeza kufumana 'isabelo esifanelekileyo' serenti ehlawulwe ngumninimzi, ngokuxhomekeke kwimida ephezulu nangaphantsi." izigulane kunye nokubonelela abafaki-zicelo kumakhaya abasemagunyeni. Isixa-mali seveki ngokubhekiselele kwiimfuno zerenti yavunyelwa, leyo kwimimiselo ekubhekiselwe kuyo "kwirenti yeveki, okanye inxalenye yayo, efanelekileyo ngeveki, ngaphandle kwamatyala asemva kwayo, kunye nomlinganiselo weveki wokuphumayo othwalwa ngumninimzi kubandakanywa, ngokukodwa, amaxabiso, isibonelelo esifanelekileyo malunga nayo nayiphi na inkcitho eyimfuneko ekulungisweni okanye kwi-inshorensi ehlawulwayo ngexesha lentlawulo ye-inshorensi, kunye nexabiso lemali ehlawulwayo kwi-inshorensi. Ityala lemali yendlu okanye isibambiso esihlawulelwayo esibizwa kwindlu ahlala kuyo umninimzi, okanye ngaphandle kwenzala kuyo."[7]

Ukungahoywa okwahlukeneyo kuye kwenziwa phantsi koMthetho woNcedo kaZwelonke ka-1948, kubandakanywa nasiphi na isibonelelo sokufa esihlawulwe kumntu phantsi kwemiqathango yecandelo lamashumi amabini anesibini loMthetho we-Inshorensi yeSizwe ka-1946, nasiphi na isibonelelo sokubeleka apho owasetyhini anelungelo lokusifumana phantsi kwecandelo leshumi elinesine loMthetho we-Inshurensi kaZwelonke ka-1946, ishumi leesheleni zokuqala kunye nentlawulo yesithandathu yokuqala yokufumana intlawulo yeshumi leminyaka yokugula okanye intlawulo yeshumi lokuqala kwiveki enye. amathandathu eveki "ayo nayiphi na intlawulo yempesheni okanye intlawulo yempesheni ngokuphathelele kwinkonzo yangaphambili okanye ingqesho apho umamkeli ethe warhoxa okanye warhoxa (nokuba uhlawulwa ngumqeshi wangaphambili okanye hayi), ingeyiyo intlawulo okanye iintlawulo- (i) ngenxa yomhlalaphantsi phantsi koMthetho wePension Act, ka-1936 okanye phantsi okanye ngenxa ye-Old Age, i-Old Penstory, i-Old Penstory, i-Old Penstory 1936 ukuya ku-1941, okanye phantsi kwawo nawuphi na umthetho ochithiweyo yiyo nayiphi na loo Mithetho, okanye (ii) ngenxa yepenshini yomhlalaphantsi phantsi koMthetho we-Inshorensi kaZwelonke, ka-1946,” nayiphi na intlawulo “emalunga nomvuzo omhlala phantsi okanye ipenshini exhomekeke kuyo icandelo leshumi elinesithandathu [9 & 10 Geo] 5. c. isibonelelo esincanyathiselwe kumhlalaphantsi onjalo," nayiphi na intlawulo "ngokubhekiselele kwipension yokukhubazeka enikezelwa phantsi kwe [2 & 3 Geo 6. c 82.] Personal Injuries (Emergency Provisions) Act, 1939, kubandakanywa, ukonyuka komhlalaphantsi onjalo ngokubhekiselele kwabo baxhomekeke kubo," nayiphi na intlawulo yeveki "ngembuyekezo yembuyiselo" ngayo nayiphi na intlawulo yembuyiselo yomsebenzi. inzuzo phantsi kwecandelo leshumi elinesibini leNational Insurance (Industrial Injuries) Act, 1946."[8] 

Izindlu zebhunga ezingakumbi zakhiwa, kwaye izicwangciso zenziwa ngoMthetho weeDolophu eziNtsha wowe-1946 (9 & 10 Geo. 6. c. 68) ukuze kukhuliswe amahlomela edolophu, nokunciphisa ingxinano kwizixeko ezikhulu ezifana neLondon neGlasgo. Ekubeni kwakukho imali encinci yocwangciso oluneenkcukacha, urhulumente wamkela i-Keynesianism, eyavumela ukucwangciswa ngengqiqo yolawulo olupheleleyo lwentsilelo yesizwe kunye nentsalela. [9] [10] [11] 

UMthetho wezoThutho ka-1947 waseka iKomishoni yezoThutho yaseBritani, eyathatha ulawulo koololiwe ukusuka kwiBig Four-Great Western Railway, eLondon, eMidland naseScottish Railway, eLondon nakwiNorth Eastern Railway kunye neSouthern Railway-ukwenza uloliwe waseBritani. [12] 

Kwimicimbi yangaphandle, urhulumente wayesebenza kwiZizwe eziManyeneyo kwaye wathethathethana nge-5 yeebhiliyoni zeedola mboleko evela eUnited States naseKhanada ngo-1946. Wajoyina ngomdla kwi-Marshall Plan ngo-1948. Yayingasenakukwazi ukuxhasa urhulumente waseGrike ngexesha leMfazwe yamaGrike kwaye yakhuthaza i-US ukuba ithathe indawo yayo nge-Truman Doctrine kwi-1947. Yathatha indima esebenzayo kwiMfazwe yase-United States ekujoyineni i-NATO. Yanika inkululeko eIndiya, ePakistan,eCeylon naseBurma kwaye bafudukela ukomeleza iBritish Commonwealth.[13] 
eCeylon naseBurma kwaye bafudukela ukomeleza iBritish Commonwealth.[13]
