Imigaqo-nkqubo yeNtlalo 
ye-Health 

Trafford General Hospital, eyaziwa ngokuba yindawo yokuzalwa yoMphathiswa 
wezeMpilo we-NHS Attlee, u-Aneurin Bevan, walwa kanzima ngokuchasene nokungavunyelwa ngokubanzi kokusekwa kwezonyango, kuquka neBritish Medical Association, ngokudala iNkonzo yezeMpilo yeSizwe kwi-1948. Le yayiyinkqubo yokunakekelwa kwezempilo exhaswa ngurhulumente, eyanikezela unyango kubo bonke, kungakhathaliseki ukuba yingeniso, ngaphandle kwentlawulo kwinqanaba lokusetyenziswa. Ibonisa imfuno evaliweyo ekudala ikho yeenkonzo zonyango, i-NHS yanyanga izigulana zamazinyo ezimalunga ne-8,500,000 kwaye yakhupha ngaphezu kwe-5,000,000 izibini zemibukiso kunyaka wayo wokuqala wokusebenza.[27] 

Abacebisi bangenelwa kule nkqubo intsha ngokuhlawulwa imivuzo ebonelela ngomgangatho owamkelekileyo wokuphila ngaphandle kwemfuneko yokuba babhenele kuqheliselo lwabucala.[28] I-NHS yeza uphuculo olukhulu kwimpilo yabantu abakumgangatho ophantsi, kunye nokufa ngenxa ye-diphtheria, inyumoniya, kunye nesifo sephepha kuncitshiswe kakhulu.[29] Nangona kwakusoloko kukho iingxabano malunga nombutho kunye nenkxaso-mali, amaqela ezopolitiko aseBritani aqhubeka evakalisa inkxaso yawo jikelele kwi-NHS ukuze ahlale ekhethwa. [30]

Kwinkalo yokhathalelo lwempilo, iimali zabelwa ukuphuculwa kunye nezikimu zolwandiso ezijolise ekuphuculeni impumelelo yolawulo. Uphuculo lwenziwa kwindawo yokuhlalisa abongikazi ukuze kufunyanwe abongikazi abaninzi kunye nokunciphisa ukunqongophala kwabasebenzi ababegcina iibhedi ezingama-60,000 zingasetyenziswa, kwaye kwenziwa iinzame zokunciphisa ukungalingani "phakathi kokugqithiswa komkhuhlane kunye nesifo sephepha (TB) iibhedi kunye nokunqongophala kweebhedi zokubeleka".[31] 

Ugonyo lwe-BCG lwaye lwaziswa ukuze kukhuselwe abafundi bezonyango, ababelethisi, abongikazi, kunye noqhagamshelwano lwezigulane ezinesifo sephepha, [32] iskimu somhlalaphantsi sasekwa kubasebenzi be-NHS esanda kusekwa, [33] I-National Health Service (Superannuation) Regulations 1947 yabeka inani lezibonelelo zabaxhamli kubandakanya isibonelelo sokuhlawula igosa, ipenshini yokulimala, intlawulo emfutshane kunye nenkonzo yokufa. i-gratuity, ipenshoni yomhlolokazi, kunye nentlawulo eyongezelelweyo kwimeko yeeklasi ezikhethekileyo zamagosa. Kwenziwa ilungiselelo lokwabiwa kwenxalenye yepenshini okanye isibonelelo somonzakalo kumntu oxhomekeke kuye.[34] 

Umthetho we-Radioactive Substances Act 1948 wamisela izibonelelo ngokubanzi zokulawula amachiza okusasazeka ngemitha.[35] Uhlaziyo oluninzi olungaphantsi luye lwaziswa, ezinye zazo zaba luncedo olukhulu kumacandelo athile oluntu lwaseBritane, njengabaswele ingqondo nabangaboniyo.[36] Phakathi kwe-1948 kunye ne-1951, urhulumente wase-Attlee wandisa inkcitho kwimpilo ukusuka kwi-£ 6,000,000,000 ukuya kwi-£ 11,000,000,000: ukwanda kwe-80%, kwaye ukusuka kwi-2.1% ukuya kwi-3.6% ye-GDP. [37] 

Intlalontle 
Urhulumente umisele ukuphumeza izicwangciso zeNgxelo ye-Beveridge ngexesha lemfazwe ekudalweni kwentlalontle 'eya kungcwatywa', kunye nokumisela inkqubo entsha ngokupheleleyo yokhuseleko loluntu. Phakathi kweyona mithetho ibalulekileyo ibinguMthetho we-Inshurensi yeSizwe wowe-1946, apho abantu abaphangelayo bahlawula i-inshurensi yesizwe. Ngembuyekezo, bona (kunye nabafazi babaxhasi abangamadoda) babefanele ukufumana inkamnkam, isibonelelo sokugula, inzuzo yokungaphangeli, kunye nenzuzo yokungcwaba.[38] Amalungiselelo awohlukeneyo aqukwa kuMthetho we-Inshorensi kaZwelonke ka-1946 kubandakanywa inzuzo yokungaphangeli nokugula, isibonelelo sokubeleka kunye nesibonelelo sokuzimasa, isibonelelo sokubeleka, isibonelelo somhlolokazi, ipenshoni yomhlolokazi kwiimeko ezizodwa, isibonelelo somgcini, ipenshini yomhlalaphantsi, kunye nesibonelelo sokusweleka.[39] UMthetho we-Inshurensi weSizwe wowe-1951, njengoko waphawulwa kolunye uhlolisiso, “waqalisa isibonelelo esihlawulwa kunye nezibonelelo zabahlolokazi kumntwana ngamnye oxhomekeke entsatsheni.”[40] 

Eminye imithetho eyahlukahlukeneyo elungiselelwe ingenelo yomntwana nenkxaso yabantu abangenawo omnye umthombo wengeniso.[38] Ngo-1949, ukungaphangeli, ukugula kunye neenzuzo zokubeleka zakhululwa kwirhafu.[41]

Isibonelelo sebhloko esaziswa ngo-1948 sanceda iinkonzo zentlalontle ezibonelelwa ngabasemagunyeni basekuhlaleni.[42] Iinkonzo zeNtlalo yoBuqu okanye iinkonzo zentlalontle zaphuhliswa ngo-1948 ukulungiselela umntu ngamnye kunye neentsapho ngokubanzi, ngakumbi amaqela akhethekileyo anje ngengqondo ephazamisekileyo, abantwana abasweleyo, abantu abadala, kunye nabakhubazekileyo.[43] 

Urhulumente wase-Attlee uye wenyusa imali yomhlalaphantsi kunye nezinye izibonelelo, kunye nemali yomhlalaphantsi ephakanyisiweyo ukuze ibe yingeniso yokuphila ngakumbi kunangaphambili. Imali yenkamnkam emfazweni nezibonelelo (zozo zombini iiMfazwe zehlabathi) zandiswa ngesenzo sowe-1946 [esiyintoni?] esanika indoda eyenzakeleyo isibonelelo somfazi nabantwana bayo ukuba itshatile emva kokuba yenzakele, ngaloo ndlela isusa isikhalazo esingaphezu kweminyaka engamashumi amabini imile.[44] Olunye uphuculo lwenziwa kwipenshoni yemfazwe ngexesha lika-Attlee njengenkulumbuso. Isibonelelo sokuBakho rhoqo saphindwa kathathu, iSibonelelo sokungaqeshwa saphindwa kathathu ukusuka kwi-10 ukuya kwi-30s ngeveki, kwaye isibonelelo esikhethekileyo sobunzima ukuya kuthi ga kwi-£ 1 ngeveki saziswa. Ukongeza, uHlahlo-lwabiwo-mali luka-1951 lwenze olunye uphuculo kwizibonelelo ezongezelelweyo zabaninzi abadla umhlala-phantsi emfazweni. Ukusukela ngo-1945 ukuya phambili, amabango amathathu kwane epenshoni aye aphumelela, ngeli lixa emva kweMfazwe yeHlabathi yokuQala yaba linye ibango lomhlalaphantsi kwisithathu elavunyelwayo.[45] Phantsi koMthetho weSuperannuation (iMiscellaneous Provisions) Act ka-1948, abasebenzi bequmrhu elimele oogunyaziwe bengingqi okanye amagosa olawulo lwengingqi banokumkelwa "ngemigaqo efanelekileyo kwingxowa-mali yempesheni kamasipala".[46] Ngo-1951, kwaqaliswa isibonelelo sobuntofo-ntofo esathi sahlawulwa ngokuzenzekelayo kwabo badla umhlala-phantsi emfazweni "abafumana isongezelelo sokungaqeshwa kunye nesibonelelo sokuzimasa esiqhubekayo".[47]
 
IiPersUkonzakala ngomhlane (Abahlali) Isicwangciso sika-1947 siquka iinzuzo ezahlukeneyo ezifana nowona mlinganiselo uphakamileyo wesibonelelo sokuzimasa esingaguqukiyo sama-40s ngeveki, kunye nesibonelelo sokukrala nokukrazuka kwempahla okubangelwa kukusetyenziswa kwamalungu kunye nezixhobo zombane. Ukongeza, izibonelelo ezihlawulwayo ngelixa umntu odla umhlala-phantsi ebefumana unyango lwezigulana "ngokuqhelekileyo azisaxhomekeke ekuxhuzulweni kwenkcitho yekhaya." Utshintsho olwahlukeneyo lwenziwa ngokubhekiselele kubantu abaqeshwe ngokufanelekileyo kunye namavolontiya okhuselo loluntu athe agcina ukwenzakala emfazweni. Oku kuquka isibonelelo semali yomfazi nabantwana kubantu abonzakeleyo abafumana isibonelelo somonzakalo okanye umhlala-phantsi wokukhubazeka, izilungiso kwizibonelelo zesibonelelo kumntu odla umhlala-phantsi obonwa njengongaphangeliyo ngenxa yokukhubazeka kwakhe komhlala-phantsi “ukuqinisekisa ukuba uyasifumana isibonelelo sokungaqeshwa kunye nazo naziphi na izibonelelo zenkonzo yezentlalo afanele ukunyuselwa ubuncinane ngeveki engama-20. isibonelelo esihlawulwa umfazi womntu ofumana isibonelelo sonyango, isibonelelo sokungaqeshwa okanye isibonelelo sokulimala phantsi kweemeko ezithile kwaye "ukuba akukho sibonelelo sihlawulwa kumfazi, isibonelelo sinokunikezelwa kumntu omdala oxhomekeke kuye," kunye nesibonelelo sentlalontle samadoda akhubazeke ngokuyinxenye "athi, nangona engaqeshwanga, athintelwe kukukhubazeka kwakhe umhlala-phantsi ngokuthatha isiphene sakhe sokuphinda abuyele emsebenzini." Kwakhona, “Apho indoda isifa ngenxa yokwenzakala okufanelekileyo okumfaneleyo umhlolokazi wayo unokunikwa umhlala-phantsi (kunye nezibonelelo zabantwana bayo) ngaphandle kokunikela ingqalelo kumhla womtshato.”[48] 

Inkqubo ebanzi ngakumbi yeengenelo zentlalontle yayisekwe ngurhulumente waseAttlee, owathi wenza okuninzi ekunciphiseni ukunqongophala okuqatha kwezentlalo. Impembelelo eyongezelelekileyo yemigaqo-nkqubo yezempilo kunye nentlalontle karhulumente ka-Attlee yayinjalo ukuba zonke izalathiso zempilo (ezifana neenkcukacha zonyango lwesikolo okanye amagosa amazinyo, okanye amagosa ezempilo ezempilo) abonise iimpawu zokuphucula, kunye nokuphuculwa okuqhubekayo kumazinga okuphila kwiintsana kunye nokwanda kwexesha lokuphila kwabantu abadala.[42] Impumelelo yomthetho wentlalontle kaRhulumente wase-Attlee ekunciphiseni intlupheko yayinjalo, kunyulo jikelele lwe-1950, ngokutsho kolunye uphando, "I-propaganda yezabasebenzi ingenza ibango elikhulu lokuba ukhuseleko loluntu luye lwaphelisa ubuhlwempu obuninzi bee-1930s".[27] 

Izindlu nocwangciso
UMthetho weeDolophu eziNtsha wowe-1946 (9 & 10 Geo. 6. c. 68) waseka amaqumrhu ophuhliso ukuze akhe iidolophu ezintsha, ngelixa uMthetho woCwangciso lweDolophu noweLizwe ka-1947 wayalela amabhunga ommandla ukuba alungise izicwangciso zophuhliso kwaye ukwabonelele namagunya okuthenga anyanzelekileyo.[49] Urhulumente wase-Attlee ukwandise amagunya amagunya asekuhlaleni ekufuneni izindlu nenxalenye yezindlu, waza wenza ukuba ukufunyanwa komhlaba kube nzima kakhulu kunangaphambili.[50] I-Housing (Skotlani) Act 1949 ibonelele ngezibonelelo ze-75% (87.5% kwi-Highlands kunye neZiqithi) malunga neendleko zohlaziyo ezihlawulwa nguNondyebo kumagunya asekuhlaleni.[51] 

Ngo-1949, amagunya asekuhlaleni axhotyiswa ukuba abonelele abantu abahluphekayo ngenxa yempilo enkenenkene ngezindlu zoluntu kwiirenti ezixhaswa ngemali. [52] 

Ukunceda ubunini bezindlu, umda wemali abantu ababenokuyiboleka kumagunya asekuhlaleni ukuze bathenge okanye bakhe indlu wanyuswa ukusuka kwi-£800 ukuya kwi-£1,500 ngowe-1945, ukuya kutsho kwii-£5,000 ngowe-1949.[53] Phantsi koMthetho woNcedo lweSizwe ka-1948 (11 & 12 Geo. 6. c. 29), abasemagunyeni basekuhlaleni babenomsebenzi “wokubonelela ngendawo yokuhlala yexeshana yonxunguphalo kwiintsapho ezingenamakhaya ngaphandle kwempazamo yazo”.[54] 

Inkqubo enkulu yokwakha izindlu yaqhutywa ngenjongo yokubonelela izigidi zabantu ngezindlu ezikumgangatho ophezulu.[27] Umthetho wolwakhiwo wezindlu wandisa izibonelelo zeSebe lezeMali kulwakhiwo lwezindlu zabasemagunyeni eNgilani naseWales. [49] Izindlu ezine kwezintlanu ezazakhiwe phantsi kwezaBasebenzi yayizizakhiwo zebhunga ezakhiwe ngendlela yesisa ngakumbi kunangaphambi kweMfazwe yesiBini yeHlabathi, kwaye uncediso-mali lwagcina phantsi irenti yebhunga. Lilonke, le migaqo-nkqubo ibonelele ngezindlu zecandelo likarhulumente ngeyona ndlela inkulu yakha yanyuswa ukuza kuthi ga ngelo xesha, ngelixa abarhola imivuzo ephantsi baxhamla ngokukodwa kolu phuhliso. Nangona uRhulumente wase-Attlee wasilela ukuhlangabezana nosukelo lwakhe, ngokuyintloko ngenxa yeengxaki zoqoqosho, phezu kwe-1,000,000 amakhaya amatsha akhiwa phakathi kwe-1945 kunye ne-1951 (impumelelo ebalulekileyo phantsi kweemeko) eyaqinisekisa ukuba izindlu ezifanelekileyo, ezifikelelekayo zazifumaneka kwiintsapho ezininzi ezinengeniso ephantsi okokuqala ngqa.[27] 

Amalungelo ophuhliso enziwe abe phantsi kolawulo lukarhulumente ngelixa urhulumente wayezama ukuthathela urhulumente yonke ingeniso yophuhliso. Amagunya ocwangciso aqingqekileyo amiselwa ukulawula ukusetyenziswa komhlaba, kwaye akhupha iincwadana zesikhokelo ezigxininisa ukubaluleka kokukhusela umhlaba wolimo. Isixokelelwano esinamandla seeofisi zengingqi zasekwa ngaphakathi komphathiswa wocwangciso ukuze zinike isikhokelo esiluqilima kwimigaqo-nkqubo yophuhliso lommandla.[55] IiNdawo zoPhuhliso oluBanzi (CDAs), ukutyunjwa phantsi koMthetho woCwangciso lweDolophu kunye neLizwe ka-1947, zavumela abasemagunyeni basekhaya ukuba bafumane ipropati kwiindawo ezichongiweyo besebenzisa amagunya okuthenga okunyanzelekileyo ukuze baphinde bacwangcise kwaye baphuhlise imimandla yasezidolophini ethwaxwa yintlupheko yasezidolophini okanye umonakalo wemfazwe.[56]
 
Abafazi nabantwana
Iqela lohlaziyo lwenziwe ukuphucula iimeko zabasetyhini nabantwana. Ngo-1946, izibonelelo zosapho jikelele zaziswa ukunika inkxaso yemali kwimizi yokukhulisa abantwana.[57][58] Ezi zibonelelo ziye zawiswa ngokusemthethweni kunyaka ongaphambili ngu-Churchill's Family Allowances Act ka-1945. I-Conservatives kamva yayiza kugxeka abasebenzi ngokuba "bengxamile kakhulu" ukwazisa izibonelelo zosapho.[50] 

UMthetho ka-1949 wabasetyhini abatshatileyo (uZithintelo phezu kolindelo) ukuze "ukulingana, ukunikezela ngokungasebenziyo naziphi na izithintelo kulindelo okanye ukwahlukaniswa okuyanyaniswa nolonwabo lwempahla ngumfazi", ngelixa uMthetho waBafazi abatshatileyo (iSondlo) we-1949 wawiswa ngenjongo yokuphucula ukwanela kunye nexesha lokuxhamla kwabasetyhini abatshatileyo.[59] 

Umthetho iCriminal Law (Amendment) Act 1950 uhlomele uMthetho woLungiso loMthetho wolwaPhulo-mthetho ka-1885 ukuze ungenise oonongogo phakathi komthetho kwaye ubakhusele ekuxhwilweni nasekuphathweni gadalala.[60] UMthetho woBulungisa boLwaphulo-mthetho ka-1948 wawunqanda ukuvalelwa kwabaselula waza wazisa uphuculo kwiinkqubo zamaziko ovavanyo kunye neziko lokuvalela, ngelixa ukuphunyezwa koMthetho wezoBulungisa woXolo ka-1949 kukhokelele kuhlaziyo olubanzi lweenkundla zikamantyi.[61] Urhulumente wase-Attlee ukwabhangisile isivalo somtshato kwiNkonzo kaRhulumente, ngaloo ndlela evumela abafazi abatshatileyo ukuba basebenze kwelo ziko.[62] 

Ngo-1946, urhulumente waseka iZiko leSizwe laBasebenzi baseKhaya njengendlela yokubonelela ngeenkonzo zasekhaya ngokwentando yesininzi. [63] 

Ngasekupheleni kowe-1946, kwamiselwa imilinganiselo yoqeqesho ekuvunyelenwe ngayo, nto leyo eyalandelwa kukuvulwa kwekomkhulu loqeqesho nokuvulwa kwamaziko oqeqesho asithoba awongezelelekileyo eWales, eSkotlani, kwaza emva koko kulo lonke ilizwe laseBritani. UMthetho weSizwe weNkonzo yezeMpilo ka-1946 wabonisa ukuba uncedo lwasekhaya kufuneka lubonelelwe kumakhaya apho olo ncedo lufuneka khona “ngenxa yobukho bakhe nabani na ogulayo, oleleyo, umama okhulelweyo, okhubazekileyo ngokwengqondo, ubudala okanye umntwana ongadlulanga kwiminyaka enyanzelekileyo yokuya esikolweni”. 'Uncedo lwasekhaya' ke ngoko luquke ilungiselelo loncedo lwasekhaya kwabongikazi kunye noomama abakhulelweyo kunye noomama abanabantwana abangaphantsi kweminyaka emihlanu ubudala, kwaye ngo-1952 malunga nama-20,000 abasetyhini bebezibandakanye kule nkonzo.[64]
 
Amalungelo abasebenzi
Amanyathelo awohlukeneyo enziwa ukuphucula iimeko emsebenzini. Ilungelo lekhefu lokugula landiswa kakhulu, kwaye izikimu zentlawulo yokugula zaziswa kulawulo lwasekuhlaleni, abasebenzi abaziingcali kunye nabasebenzi bobuchwephesha ngo-1946 nakwiindidi ezahlukeneyo zabasebenzi bezandla ngo-1948.[65] Imbuyekezo yabasebenzi nayo yaphuculwa kakhulu.[66] Kwaziswa uMthetho we-Inshurensi yeSizwe (uLwaphulo-mthetho lwamashishini) ka-1946 oquka izibonelelo ezahlukeneyo ezifana nenzuzo yokwenzakala, inzuzo yokukhubazeka, ukonyuka komhlalaphantsi wokukhubazeka kwiimeko zokungaqeshwa, ubunzima obukhethekileyo, ukuhamba rhoqo, kwaye ngexesha lokuvunywa konyango esibhedlele, kunye nokonyuka kwenzuzo yokulimala kunye nomhlalaphantsi wokukhubazeka ngokubhekiselele kubantwana kunye nabantu abadala abaxhomekeke kubo.[67] Ngaphantsi kwe-Inshurensi yeSizwe (i-Industrial Injuries) (iZifo ezimiselweyo) ye-1948, abaxhamli ekufumaneni ipenshini yokukhubazeka kwi-byssinosis babenelungelo kwiimeko ezithile zokunyuswa komhlalaphantsi ngokuphathelele ubunzima obukhethekileyo, ngelixa inzuzo yokukhubazeka ngokubhekiselele kwi-pneumoconiosis yandiswa] kwiimeko ezininzi. [68] 

I-Fair Wages Resolution ka-1946 yayifuna nayiphi na ikontraka esebenza kwiprojekthi yoluntu ukuba ubuncinane ifanise imilinganiselo yentlawulo kunye nezinye iimeko zengqesho ezibekwe kwisivumelwano esifanelekileyo esidibeneyo.[69][70][71] Ngo-1946, iRhafu yokuThenga yasuswa ngokupheleleyo kwizinto zokufakwa ekhitshini nakwizitya, ngelixa izinga lancitshiswa kwizinto ezahlukeneyo zegadi.[63] UMthetho weNgqesho noQeqesho wowe-1948 wawuquka amalungiselelo afana namalungiselelo okuqeqeshelwa ingqesho kunye neentlawulo ezibhekiselele kwiindleko zokususa nokuhlalisa abasebenzi[72] 

UMthetho weeNkonzo zoMlilo 1947 wazisa inkqubo entsha yomhlalaphantsi kubacimi bomlilo,[73] ngelixa uMthetho woMbane we-1947 wazisa izibonelelo ezingcono zomhlalaphantsi kubasebenzi kwelo shishini.[74] UMthetho weMbuyekezo yaBasebenzi (iSongezo) ka-1948 kwaye wazisa izibonelelo kubasebenzi abanezifo ezithile ezinxulumene neasbestos ezenzeke phambi ko-1948.[75] UMthetho wokuThunyelwa kweeNqanawa ngo-1948 kunye noMthetho wokuThunyelwa kweeNqanawa kuRhwebo (iNgqungquthela yoKhuseleko) ka-1949 zapasiswa ukuphucula iimeko zabahambi ngolwandle. Umthetho iShops Act 1950 udibanise umthetho wangaphambili owawubonelela ukuba kungabikho mntu unokuqeshwa evenkileni ixesha elingaphezu kweeyure ezintandathu ngaphandle kokuba aphumle kangangemizuzu engama-20 ubuncinane. Lo mthetho wawufuna ikhefu lesidlo sasemini ubuncinane lemizuzu engama-45 kuye nabani na osebenza phakathi kwe-11:30am kunye ne-2:30pm, kunye nekhefu leti lesiqingatha seyure kuye nabani na osebenza phakathi kwe-4pm kunye ne-7pm.[76] Urhulumente ukwaqinise iSigqibo seMivuzo eLungileyo, kunye nesolotya elifuna ukuba bonke abaqeshi bafumane iikhontrakthi zikarhulumente ukuze baqonde amalungelo abasebenzi babo okujoyina imibutho yabasebenzi.[77]

Umthetho weTrades Disputes Act 1927 wabhangiswa, kwaza kwasungulwa iDock Labour Scheme ngo-1947 ukuze kupheliswe inkqubo eqhelekileyo yokuqesha abasebenzi emadokisini.[78] Esi sikimu sanika abadokhi ababhalisiweyo ilungelo elisemthethweni lomsebenzi omncinane kunye neemeko ezifanelekileyo. NgeBhodi yeSizwe yaBasebenzi beDock (apho imibutho yabasebenzi nabaqeshi babenokumelwa ngokulinganayo) iimanyano zafumana ulawulo ekugayweni nasekugxothweni. Iidokhi ezibhalisiweyo eziyekiweyo ngabaqeshi ngaphakathi kweNgxowa-mali zazinelungelo lokuba zithathwe ngomnye, okanye lembuyekezo yesisa.[79] Onke amadokhi ayebhaliswe phantsi kweSikimu seMisebenzi yeDock, ebanika ilungelo elisemthethweni lobuncinci bomsebenzi, iiholide kunye nomvuzo wokugula.[80] 

Imivuzo yamalungu asebupoliseni yonyuswe kakhulu.[81] Ukwaziswa koMnqophiso wabasebenzi basezimayini ngo-1946 kwamisela iveki yokusebenza yeentsuku ezintlanu kubasebenzi-mgodini kunye nolwakhiwo lwemivuzo yosuku olusemgangathweni, [42] kwaye ngo-1948 i-Colliery Workers Supplementary Scheme yamkelwa, ibonelela ngezibonelelo ezongezelelweyo kubasebenzi bamalahle abakhubazekileyo kunye nabo baxhomekeke kubo.[82][83] Izibonelelo ezahlukeneyo zabonelelwa phantsi kwesikimu, kubandakanywa inzuzo yokulimala eyongezelelweyo, ipenshini yokukhubazeka ngokubhekiselele kwingozi yengozi okanye isifo se-colliery, izibonelelo zokufa, kunye nezibonelelo ezongezelelweyo.[84] 

Ngo-1948, kwasekwa iskimu somhlalaphantsi ukuze kubonelelwe ngezibonelelo zomhlalaphantsi kubasebenzi be-NHS entsha, kunye nabo baxhomekeke kubo.[85] Phantsi kweMimiselo yoShishino lwamalahle kuZwelonke (Superannuation) ka-1950, inkqubo yomhlalaphantsi yabasebenzi-mgodini yasekwa.[86] Uphuculo lwenziwa kwimivuzo yabasebenzi basezifama, [45] kunye neBhodi yeMivuzo yezoLimo ngo-1948 ayigcinanga nje ngokukhusela amanqanaba emivuzo, kodwa yaqinisekisa nokuba abasebenzi babonelelwa ngendawo yokuhlala.[87]

Iqela lemigaqo ejolise ekukhuseleni impilo nokhuseleko lwabantu emsebenzini yaziswa ngexesha lika-Attlee ese-ofisini. Imimiselo yakhutshwa ngoFebruwari 1946 eyayisebenza kwiifektri ezibandakanyekayo "kukwenza iibrikethi okanye iibhloko zepetroli ezibandakanya amalahle, uthuli lwamalahle, icoke okanye udaka olunodaka njengento ebophelelayo," kwaye ephathelele "uthuli kunye nokuphuma komoya, izixhobo zokuhlambela kunye nendawo yokuhlala yempahla, ukhuseleko lwamehlo kunye nolusu lwezonyango kunye novavanyo [8]. IMigodi yamalahle (iVentilation) Jikelele yeMithetho yomhla we-17 kuMeyi 1947 "iphumeza iingcebiso zeKhomishoni yaseRoyal yoKhuseleko kwiMigodi yamalahle malunga nezihloko ezibini eziphambili: iindlela zokujonga amaxesha ngamaxesha umgangatho oqhelekileyo wokungena komoya kunye neendlela zokunciphisa ukuvuza komoya. Izibonelelo zibekwe ngokumalunga nokumiselwa komxholo we-firedamp kunye neendlela apho ezi zigqibo zenziwe kwiRadio8). I-30 Juni 1948, "elawula ukungeniswa, ukuveliswa, ukuthengiswa, ukugcinwa kunye nokusetyenziswa kwezinto ezine-radioactive, iquka izibonelelo ezixhobisa uMphathiswa ofanelekileyo ukuba akhuphe imimiselo yokuthintela ukwenzakala kwimpilo ebangelwa yimisebe ye-ionizing kunye nokukhusela ukulahlwa okukhuselekileyo kweemveliso zenkunkuma ye-radioactive." kunye ne-flash point engaphantsi kwe-32 ° C. (90 ° F.) ekusetyenzisweni ukucoca okomileyo ngaphandle kokubona."[91] I-Blasting (I-Castings kunye namanye amaNqaku) iMimiselo eKhethekileyo ka-1949, "iyakuthintela ukuqhushumba kwesanti kunye nokujongana nendawo ebiyelweyo yokuqhushumba, ukucocwa kwe-abrasive esetyenzisiweyo, iplanti yokungenisa umoya, ukuhlolwa, ukucocwa kwezixhobo eziselula kunye nokugcinwa kwezixhobo zokusebenza, ukucocwa kwezixhobo kunye nokugcinwa kwezixhobo zokusebenza. abantu, kunye nokuxelwa kweziphene kwisixhobo sokuqhunyiswa kweSandblasting akuvumelekanga kwiCandelo lesi-5, elithi: "Akukho sihlabathi okanye enye into equkethe i-silica yamahhala iya kwaziswa njenge-abrasive kuyo nayiphi na into yokuqhushumba." Ngowe-1948 "kubandakanya ukuphakanyiswa nokuthwala imithwalo ngabasetyhini kunye nabantu abatsha, umoya, ubushushu kunye nokufuma, intlalontle, ukwakhiwa kunye nokusetyenziswa koomatshini kunye nokuthengiswa kunye nokuqeshwa koomatshini".[90]

I-Magnesium (UkuSila ii-Casings kunye namanye amaNqaku) (IiMimiselo eKhethekileyo) Umyalelo kaDisemba 1946 wawuqulathe amanyathelo akhethekileyo "ngokuhlonela ukugcinwa kwezityalo kunye nezixhobo; izilumkiso malunga nokubangela iintlantsi; ukukhutshwa kunye nokususwa kothuli; ukusebenza ngokuzenzekelayo kwezixhobo zombane; iimpahla ezikhuselayo; kunye nokuthintela ukutshaya, izibane ezivulekileyo kunye nemililo". Kwabo basebenzi babandakanyeka kwiinkqubo zokukhanyisa, iFactories (Luminising) Special Regulations (1947) yathintela ukuqeshwa kwabo bangaphantsi kweminyaka eyi-18 kwaye yayalela "uvavanyo lokuqala lwezonyango kufuneka lwenziwe ngaphambi komhla wesixhenxe wengqesho; iimviwo ezilandelayo kufuneka zenziwe kanye ngenyanga" i-silica kufuneka isetyenziswe kuyo nayiphi na inkqubo yokuqhushumba ", ngelixa i-Foundries (i-Parting Materials) i-Special Regulations (1950) yalela ukusetyenziswa komgubo othile wokuqhawula "okuthi kubangele umngcipheko omkhulu we-silicosis".[93] 

I-Regulations yeSakhiwo (uKhuseleko, iMpilo kunye neNtlalontle) ka-1948 yayifuna ukuba kuthathwe amanyathelo okunciphisa ukuvezwa kuthuli olunokuba yingozi okanye umsi,[94] ngelixa iPottery (iMpilo) iMimiselo eYodwa (1947) yayingavumeli ukusetyenziswa "ngaphandle kokwenziwa kweethayile ezikhazimlisiweyo" kuzo zonke "kodwa iinkqubo ezithile ezicwangcisiweyo okanye eziphantsi komhlaba zinika i-lead okanye i-lead ephantsi. okanye iquartz akufuneki iqeshwe." [93] I-Pottery (iMpilo kunye neNtlalontle) iMimiselo eKhethekileyo ka-1950 yenza ilungiselelo lempilo kunye nokhuseleko lwabasebenzi abaqeshwe kwimizi-mveliso "apho kuqhutyelwa khona ukwenziwa okanye ukuhombisa izinto zomdongwe okanye abenzi abathile okanye iinkqubo".[95] 

Umthetho 
Uhlaziyo lomthetho olwahlukeneyo luye lwenziwa ngurhulumente ka-Attlee. UMthetho woBulungisa boLwaphulo-mthetho ka-1948 wawubonelela ngeendlela ezintsha zokujongana nabaphuli-mthetho, waphelisa umsebenzi onzima, ubukhoboka bezohlwayo, izahlulo zentolongo kunye nokubethwa. [96] UMthetho woHlaziyo loMthetho ka-1948 wenza ukuba abasebenzi bamangalele abaqeshi babo kumatyala apho baye bafumana ukwenzakala ngenxa yokungakhathali komnye umsebenzi.[97] UMthetho woNcedo lwezoMthetho kunye neeNgcebiso ka-1949 wazisa inkqubo yoncedo lukarhulumente ukunceda abo bangenakho ukufikelela kwiinkonzo zomthetho.[98] I<em>The Witnesses Allowances Regulations 1948 yayimisela intlawulo yesibonelelo samangqina, isibonelelo sasebusuku, nesibonelelo sobungqina obuchwephesha kwiimeko ezithile.[99] 

Imvumelwano yasemva kwemfazwe 
Inqaku eliphambili: Imvumelwano yasemva kwemfazwe
Uninzi lweembali-mlando zithetha ukuba imigaqo-nkqubo yasekhaya ephambili (ngaphandle kwelizwe lensimbi) ibonise isivumelwano esibanzi se-bipartisan. Imvumelwano yasemva kwemfazwe ngumzekelo wembali wesivumelwano sezopolitiko ukususela ngo-1945 ukuya ekupheleni kweminyaka yoo-1970. Ngo-1979 iNkulumbuso entsha uMargaret Thatcher wayikhaba waza wayirhoxisa. [100] Amabango engcamango kukho ukuvumelana okubanzi okubandakanya inkxaso yephakheji ehambelanayo yemigaqo-nkqubo eyaphuhliswa ngo-1930s, eyathenjiswa ngexesha leMfazwe yesiBini yeHlabathi, kwaye yenziwa phantsi kwe-Attlee. Imigaqo-nkqubo ijongene noqoqosho oluxubeneyo, iKeynesianism, kunye nentlalontle ebanzi yelizwe.[101] Kwiminyaka yakutshanje ubunyaniso bale nkcazelo buye baxoxisana ngababhali-mbali. 

Imodeli yababhali-mbali yemvumelwano yasemva kwemfazwe yaphuhliswa ngokupheleleyo nguPaul Addison.[102] Ingxoxo esisiseko yeyokuba ngeminyaka yoo-1930, iinkcuba-buchopho zeLiberal Party ezazikhokelwa nguJohn Maynard Keynes kunye noWilliam Beveridge zavelisa uthotho lwezicwangciso eziye zaba nomtsalane ngakumbi njengoko urhulumente wexesha lemfazwe wathembisa ngeBritani engcono kakhulu emva kwemfazwe waza wabona imfuneko yokubandakanya onke amacandelo oluntu. Urhulumente womanyano ebudeni bemfazwe, owayekhokelwa nguChurchill noAttlee, watyikitya ungcelele lwamaphepha amhlophe awayethembisa iBritani ngentlalo-ntle ephucuke kakhulu. Emva kwemfazwe, izithembiso zaziquka iNkonzo Yezempilo yeSizwe, nokwandiswa kwemfundo, izindlu, kunye neqela leenkqubo zentlalo-ntle. Ayizange ibandakanye ukulawulwa kwesinyithi kunye nentsimbi, eyavunywa kuphela yi-Labour Party. 

Imodeli ithi ukususela kwi-1945 kwada kwafika u-Thatcher kwi-1979, kwakukho isivumelwano esibanzi selizwe lonke malunga nomgaqo-nkqubo wentlalontle kunye noqoqosho, ngokukodwa malunga nombuso wentlalontle, iinkonzo zempilo zikazwelonke, ukuguqulwa kwezemfundo, uqoqosho oluxubekileyo, umgaqo karhulumente, imigaqo-nkqubo ye-macroeconomic yaseKeynesian, kunye nengqesho epheleleyo. Ngaphandle komba wokubekwa phantsi kolawulo kwamanye amashishini, le migaqo-nkqubo yamkelwa ngokubanzi ngamaqela amathathu amakhulu, kunye namashishini, uluntu lwezezimali kunye nemibutho yabasebenzi. Ukuza kuthi ga ngeminyaka yee-1980, ababhali-mbali babevumelana ngokubanzi ngobukho nokubaluleka kwemvumelwano. Abanye ababhali-mbali abafana noRalph Miliband bavakalise ukuphoxeka kukuba imvumelwano yayiyipakethe ethozamileyo okanye egcinayo eyavala uluntu olunentlalontle ngokupheleleyo.[103] Umbhali-mbali uAngus Calder wakhalaza ngokukrakra ukuba uhlaziyo lwasemva kwemfazwe lwalungumvuzo onganelanga wamadini ngexesha lemfazwe, kunye nokungcatsha okuphoxayo kwethemba labantu loluntu olunobulungisa ngakumbi emva kwemfazwe.[104] Kwiminyaka yakutshanje, kuye kwakho ingxoxo yezembali malunga nokuba isivumelwano esinjalo sakha saba khona.[105]
 
Ikamva
NgoFebruwari 1950 unyulo jikelele iLabour Party yagcina isininzi sayo ngezihlalo ezi-5 nje. Oku bekunganelanga ukulawula nangona kunjalo, ngenxa yokwahlukana kweBevanite okubangela ukungavisisani kwiqela. Olunye unyulo jikelele lwabizwa ngo-1951 ukuzama ukwandisa uninzi lwabo. Noko ke, ngonyulo luka-Oktobha 1951 ngokubanzi iConservatives yabuyela kulawulo phantsi kukaWinston Churchill. Abasebenzi babeza kuhlala bengekho kwiofisi iminyaka elishumi elinesithathu ezayo, kude kube ngo-1964, xa uHarold Wilson waba yinkulumbuso. 


Uzinzo lwezemali kukungabikho kweziqendu zenkqubo ngokubanzi apho kwenzeka ingxaki yezemali kwaye ibonakaliswa njengoqoqosho olunoguquguquko oluphantsi. Kukwabandakanya ukomelela koxinzelelo lwenkqubo yezemali ukukwazi ukumelana namaxesha alungileyo namabi. Uzinzo lwemali yinjongo yoorhulumente abaninzi kunye neebhanki ezingoovimba. Injongo ayikokuthintela ingxaki okanye ukumisa izigqibo ezimbi zemali. Kukho ukubamba uqoqosho kunye nokugcina inkqubo isebenza kakuhle ngelixa iziganeko ezinje zisenzeka. [1] 

Isiseko sozinzo lwemali kukuyilwa kwenkqubo ekwaziyo ukufunxa zonke iziganeko ezilungileyo nezimbi ezenzekayo kuqoqosho nangaliphi na ixesha. Ayinanto yakwenza nokuthintela abantu okanye amashishini ukuba angaphumeleli, aphulukane nemali, okanye aphumelele. Inceda nje ekudalweni kweemeko zenkqubo eqhubelekayo yokusebenza ngokufanelekileyo ebusweni bezo zehlo.[2] 

Uqoqosho luhlala lutshintsha kwaye lukhula, kwaye luzele ngamashishini aqala, akhula, kwaye angaphumeleli: imisebenzi yesiqhelo yomjikelo weshishini. Iimarike zezemali kunye namaziko emali agqalwa njengezinzile xa ekwazi ukubonelela amakhaya, uluntu, kunye namashishini ngemithombo, iinkonzo, kunye neemveliso ezizifunayo ukuze atyale imali, akhule kwaye athathe inxaxheba kuqoqosho olusebenza kakuhle. Amaziko emali aquka iibhanki, ukonga kunye nemali-mboleko, kunye nezinye iimveliso zemali kunye nababoneleli beenkonzo.[2] Inkqubo yezemali ehlangabezana neemfuno zeentsapho eziqhelekileyo kunye namashishini ukuboleka imali yokuthenga indlu okanye imoto, ukugcina umhlala-phantsi, okanye ukuhlawula ikholeji ithathwa njengozinzo lwemali. Ngendlela efanayo, amashishini kufuneka athathe imali-mboleko ukuze andise, akhe imizi-mveliso, afune abasebenzi abatsha, kwaye enze intlawulo.

Ukukwazi ukwaba izibonelelo ngokufanelekileyo, ukuvavanya nokulawula imingcipheko yezemali, ukugcina amanqanaba engqesho kufutshane nezinga lendalo loqoqosho, kunye nokuphelisa ukunyakaza kwexabiso elihambelanayo lee-asethi zokwenyani okanye zemali eziya kuchaphazela uzinzo lwemali okanye amanqanaba engqesho zonke ziimpawu zenkqubo ezinzileyo yezemali. Ukungalingani kwezemali okuvela ngokwemvelo okanye ngenxa yeziganeko ezibalulekileyo ezimbi nezingalindelekanga ziyachithwa xa inkqubo yezemali ikuluhlu lozinzo. Xa le nkqubo izinzile, iyakuthi ibambe izothuso ngokusebenzisa iindlela zokuzilungisa, ithintele iziganeko ezimbi ekuphazamiseni uqoqosho lokwenyani okanye ezinye iinkqubo zemali. Ngenxa yokuba uninzi lwentengiselwano yehlabathi lokwenene lwenzeka ngenkqubo yezemali, uzinzo lwezemali luyimfuneko ngokupheleleyo ekwandeni koqoqosho.[1][3] 

Imilinganiselo yokuqina 
Imilinganiselo yozinzo lwenqanaba elizinzileyo 
I-Altman's z-score isetyenziswa kakhulu kuphando lobungqina njengomlinganiselo wozinzo lwenqanaba lefem yonxulumano oluphezulu nokuba nokwenzeka kokusilela. Lo mlinganiselo uthelekisa izithinteli (iintengo ezinkulu kunye nembuyekezo) kunye nomngcipheko (ukuguquguquka kwembuyekezo) kwaye wenze kakuhle ekuqikeleleni ukutshona kwezimali kwiminyaka emibini. Ngaphandle kophuhliso lwezinye iimodeli zokuqikelela uzinzo lwezemali imodeli ka-Altman iseyeyona isetyenziswa kakhulu. [4][5] 

Enye imodeli esetyenziselwa ukulinganisa uzinzo kwinqanaba leziko yimodeli ye-Merton (ekwabizwa ngokuba yimodeli yexabiso le-asethi). Ivavanya ukukwazi kwefemu ukuhlangabezana nezibophelelo zayo zezemali kwaye ilinganisela ukuba kunokwenzeka ukusilela ukusilela. Kulo mzekelo, i-equity yeziko ithathwa njengenketho yokufowuna kwii-asethi ezigcinwe kuyo, kuthathelwa ingqalelo ukuguquguquka kwezo asethi. I-Put-call parity isetyenziselwa ukuxabisa ixabiso lendlela echaziweyo "yokubeka", emele umngcipheko wekhredithi yefemu. Ekugqibeleni, imodeli ilinganisa ixabiso lee-asethi zefem (zilinganiswe ukuguquguquka) ngexesha apho abanini bamatyala basebenzisa "inketho yokubeka" ngokulindela imbuyekezo. Ngokucacileyo, imodeli ichaza ukusilela njengaxa ixabiso lamatyala efemu lidlula elo lee-asethi zayo libala ukuba nokwenzeka kokusilela kwetyala. Kwiimpinda ezahlukeneyo zemodeli, inqanaba le-asethi/lityala linokusetwa kumanqanaba ahlukeneyo ethreshold. 

Kuphando olulandelayo, imodeli kaMerton iye yalungiswa ukuze ibambe uluhlu olubanzi lwemisebenzi yezemali kusetyenziswa idatha yokutshintsha ngetyala. Umzekelo, iMoody's iyisebenzisa kwimodeli ye-KMV zombini ukubala ukuba nokwenzeka kokusilela kwetyala kwaye njengenxalenye yenkqubo yolawulo lomngcipheko wetyala. Umgama ukuya kuSilelo (DD) ngomnye umlinganiselo osekwe kwimarike womngcipheko wokusilela weshishini osekelwe kwimodeli kaMerton. Ilinganisa zombini umngcipheko we-solvency kunye nomngcipheko wokuhlawula amatyala kwinqanaba eliqinileyo. 

Amanyathelo ozinzo olucwangcisiweyo 
Ngelishwa, akukabikho inye, imodeli esemgangathweni yokuhlola uzinzo lwenkqubo yezemali kunye nokuvavanya imigaqo-nkqubo.

Ukulinganisa uzinzo lwenkqubo, inani lezifundo lizama ukudibanisa imilinganiselo yozinzo lwe-firm-level (i-z-score kunye nomgama ukuya kwi-default) kwi-system-wide evaluation yozinzo, mhlawumbi ngokuthatha i-avareji elula okanye ukulinganisa umlinganiselo ngamnye ngobungakanani obunxulumene neziko. Nangona kunjalo, la manyathelo adibeneyo ayasilela ukunika ingxelo ngeengozi ezihambelanayo phakathi kwamaziko emali. Ngamanye amazwi, imodeli iyasilela ukuthathela ingqalelo unxibelelwano phakathi kwamaziko, kwaye ukusilela kweziko elinye kunokukhokelela ekosuleleni. 

Ukuba nokwenzeka kokuQala ukuya kuMiselweyo, okanye ukuba nokwenzeka kokuqwalasela ukusilela kokunye phakathi kwenani lamaziko, kucetywe njengomlinganiselo womngcipheko wenkqubo kwiqela lamaziko amakhulu emali. Lo mlinganiso ujonga umngcipheko wokungathathi hlangothi okunokwenzeka ukusuka kwi-credit swap swap spreads. Ngokungafaniyo nemilinganiselo yomgama-ukuya-okumiselweyo, ukuba nokwenzeka kuqaphela ukuthungelana phakathi kokusilela kwamaziko ahlukeneyo. Nangona kunjalo, amaphononongo ajolise kumathuba okusilela adla ngokungayihoyi isiphumo esibangelwa kukusilela kweziko elikhulu. 

Olunye uvavanyo lozinzo lwenkqubo yezemali yiSystemic Expected Shortfall (SES), elinganisa igalelo kumngcipheko wenkqubo ngamaziko ngamanye. I-SES iqwalasela inqanaba lomntu ngamnye kwaye ilinganisa izinto zangaphandle ezenziwe kwicandelo leebhanki xa la maziko esilela. Lo mzekelo ufanelekile ngakumbi ekuchongeni ukuba ngawaphi amaziko afanelekileyo ngokwenkqubo kwaye anokuba nefuthe elikhulu kuqoqosho xa lusilela. Enye intsilelo yendlela ye-SES kukuba kunzima ukumisela ukuba amaziko abalulekileyo ngokwenkqubo anokusilela nini.[6] 

Ukomeleza amandla okuxela kwangaphambili, umlinganiselo we-SES obuyela emva wandiswa waza walungiswa kuphando lwamva. Imodeli eyandisiweyo ibizwa ngokuba yi-SRISK, evavanya ukunqongophala kwenkunzi elindelekileyo kwifemu kwimeko yobunzima. Ukubala le SRISK, umntu kufuneka aqale amisele iLong-Run Marginal Shortfall (LRMES), elinganisa ubudlelwane phakathi kwembuyekezo ye-equity yefemu kunye nembuyekezo yemarike (eqikelelwa kusetyenziswa i-asymmetric volatility, correlation, kunye ne-copula). Emva koko, imodeli iqikelela ukuhla kwexabiso le-equity ye-firm ukuba i-aggregate market ifumana ama-40% okanye ukuwa okukhulu kwisithuba seenyanga ezintandathu ukumisela ukuba yimalini eyinkunzi efunekayo ukuze kuphunyezwe i-8% ye-capital to asset value ratio. Ngamanye amazwi, i-SRSK inika ulwazi kwipesenti yefemu yokusilela kwenkunzi yecandelo lezemali. I-SRISK ephezulu % ibonisa abona bantu baphulukene kakhulu xa kukho ingxaki. Enye intsingiselo yesalathisi se-SES kukuba ifem ithathwa "njengengozi ngokwenkqubo" ukuba ijongene nokunqongophala okukhulu kwenkunzi xa icandelo lezemali libuthathaka.[7]

Enye igeyiji yozinzo lwemali kukusasazwa kwelahleko yenkqubo, ezama ukuvala ezinye zezikhewu zale milinganiselo ikhankanywe ngasentla. Lo mlinganiselo ubandakanya imiba emithathu engundoqo: ukuba nokwenzeka kweziko ngalinye lokusilela, ubungakanani belahleko enikwe ukusilela, kunye nokosulela okubangelwa kukusilela kumaziko anxibelelanayo.[8] 


Ulawulo lwezemali luluhlu olubanzi lwemigaqo-nkqubo esebenza kwicandelo lezemali kwiindawo ezininzi zolawulo, ezithethelela iimpawu ezimbini eziphambili zezemali: umngcipheko wenkqubo, othetha ukuba ukusilela kweefemu zemali kubandakanya ukuqwalaselwa komdla woluntu; kunye ne-asymmetry yolwazi, ethethelela ukunqanda inkululeko yekhontrakthi kwiindawo ezikhethiweyo zeenkonzo zemali, ngakumbi ezo zibandakanya abaxhasi bokuthengisa kunye/okanye iingxaki zeearhente eziyintloko. Inxalenye ebalulekileyo yolawulo lwezemali kulawulo lweefemu ezichongiweyo zezemali kunye neemarike ngabasemagunyeni abakhethekileyo abafana neekomishoni zokhuseleko kunye nabaphathi beebhanki. 

Kwezinye iindawo, imiba ethile yolawulo lwemali inikezelwe kwimibutho ezilawulayo. Ulawulo lwezemali lwenza enye yeendidi ezintathu ezisemthethweni eziqulathe umxholo womthetho wezezimali, ezinye ezimbini zizenzo zemarike kunye nomthetho wetyala.[1] 

Imbali 
[icon]	 
Eli candelo lifuna ukwandiswa. Unokunceda ngokongeza kuyo. (Novemba 2023) 
Ngexesha langoku, amaDatshi ayengoovulindlela kulawulo lwezemali.[2] Ukuvalwa kokuqala okurekhodiweyo (umgaqo) ekuthengiseni okufutshane kwenziwa ngabasemagunyeni baseDatshi ekuqaleni kwe-1610. 

Iinjongo zolawulo 
Iinjongo zabalawuli bezemali zidla ngokuba: [3] 

ukuzithemba kweemarike - ukugcina ukuzithemba kwinkqubo yezemali 
uzinzo lwemali - igalelo ekukhuseleni nasekuphuculeni uzinzo lwenkqubo yezemali 
ukhuseleko lwabathengi - ukufumana iqondo elifanelekileyo lokukhusela abathengi. 
ukunciphisa ulwaphulo-mthetho lwezemali 
lawula intatho-nxaxheba yamazwe angaphandle 
Ulwakhiwo lokongamela 
IMithetho ixhobisa imibutho, urhulumente okanye ongekho phantsi kolawulo lukarhulumente, ukubeka iliso kwimisebenzi nokunyanzelisa amanyathelo.[4] Kukho iindlela ezahlukeneyo zokuseta kunye nendibaniselwano endaweni yolwakhiwo lolawulo lwemali kwihlabathi jikelele.[5][6] 

Ukulawulwa kweemarike zeSecurities 
Inqaku eliphambili: Ikhomishini yezokhuseleko 
Izenzo zokutshintshiselana ziqinisekisa ukuba ukurhweba kumgangatho wokutshintshiselana kwenziwa ngendlela efanelekileyo. Eyona ibalaseleyo inkqubo yokubeka amaxabiso, ukwenziwa kunye nokuhlaliswa korhwebo, esweni urhwebo oluthe ngqo nolusebenzayo.[7][8]

Abalawuli bezemali baqinisekisa ukuba iinkampani ezidwelisiweyo kunye nabathathi-nxaxheba beemarike bathobela imimiselo eyahlukeneyo phantsi kwezenzo zokurhweba. Izenzo zorhwebo zifuna ukuba iinkampani ezidwelisiweyo zipapashe iingxelo zemali rhoqo, izaziso ze-ad hoc okanye ukusebenzelana kwabalawuli. Nangona abathathi-nxaxheba kwimarike kufuneka bapapashe izaziso eziphambili zabaninizabelo. Injongo yokubeka iliso kuthotyelo lweenkampani ezidwelisiweyo kunye neemfuno zabo zokudiza kukuqinisekisa ukuba abatyali-mali bayafikelela kulwazi oluyimfuneko nolwaneleyo ukwenza uhlolo olunolwazi lweenkampani ezidwelisiweyo kunye nezibambiso zabo.[9][10][11][12] 

Ukongamela ulawulo lwe-asethi okanye izenzo zotyalo-mali ziqinisekisa ukusebenza ngokungenamvisiswano kwezo zithuthi.[13] 

Ukongamela iibhanki kunye nabanikezeli beenkonzo zemali 
Inqaku eliphambili: Ummiselo webhanki 
Imithetho yebhanki imisela imigaqo yeebhanki ekufuneka iyiqwalasele xa zisasekwa naxa ziqhuba ishishini. Le migaqo yenzelwe ukuthintela uphuhliso olungamkelekanga olunokuthi luphazamise ukusebenza kakuhle kwenkqubo yebhanki. Ngaloo ndlela kuqinisekiswa inkqubo yebhanki eyomeleleyo nesebenzayo.[14][15]

IsiXeko saseLondon (esidla ngokusaziwa njengeSixeko okanye iSquare Mile), sisixeko, idolophu enemisitho kunye nesithili sikarhulumente wasekhaya eNgilani. Yasekwa ngamaRoma malunga nowama-47 AD njengeLondinium, yenza iziko eliyimbali lemetropolis ebanzi yaseLondon. Singqongwe yidolophu yale mihla ye-Greater London, ehlala yahlukile kuyo, iSixeko siyindawo eyodwa yabasemagunyeni elawulwa siSixeko saseLondon Corporation, esikhokelwa yiNkosi uSodolophu waseLondon; nangona iyinxalenye yommandla olawulwa liGunya laseLondon eliKhulu. 

Ebizwa ngokuba yiSquare Mile, isiXeko saseLondon sinendawo eyi-1.12 sq mi (716.80 iihektare; 2.90 km2), sisenza esona sixeko sincinci eUnited Kingdom. Yayinabemi be-8,583 kubalo lwabantu luka-2021, [1] [2] nangona kunjalo abantu abangaphezu kwe-500,000 baqeshwe kule ndawo ukususela ngo-2019 [3] [4] 

Kunye neCanary Wharf kunye neWest End, isiXeko saseLondon senza isithili seshishini esisembindini saseLondon, lelinye lamaziko ezezimali aphambili ehlabathi. IBhanki yaseNgilani kunye neLondon Stock Exchange zombini zizinze kwisiXeko. Ishishini le-inshorensi likwanobukho obuphambili kulo mmandla, kwaye ubukho beNdawo yokulala yeNkundla kumda ongasentshona weSixeko kwenze ukuba libe liziko lomsebenzi wezomthetho. 

IsiXeko sangoku saseLondon senza uninzi lweLondon ukusuka ekuhlalweni kwayo ngamaRoma ngenkulungwane yoku-1 yeXesha Eliqhelekileyo ukuya kumaXesha Aphakathi. Iqulethe iziza ezininzi zembali, kubandakanya iSt Paul's Cathedral, iRoyal Exchange, iMansion House, iGuildhall, iOld Bailey, iMarike yaseSmithfield, iSikhumbuzo soMlilo omkhulu waseLondon, kunye neentsalela zoDonga lwaseLondon yakudala. 

Imbali 
Inqaku eliphambili: Imbali yeLondon 
Origins 
Inqaku eliphambili: Londinium 

Isigcina-ntloko saseWaterloo, c. 150–50 BC, yafunyanwa kuMlambo iThames
 
Isiqwenga esasindayo soDonga lwaseLondon, olwakhiwa malunga noAD 200, kufutshane neTower Hill.
Imikhosi yaseRoma yaseka indawo yokuhlala eyaziwa ngokuba yi "Londinium" kwindawo yangoku yeSixeko saseLondon malunga ne-AD 43. Ibhulorho yayo phezu koMlambo iThames yajika isixeko saba yindlela kunye nezibuko elikhulu, elisebenza njengeziko elikhulu lezorhwebo eBritani yaseRoma de yalahlwa ngexesha le-5 leminyaka. Umembi wezinto zakudala uLeslie Wallace uphawula ukuba, ngenxa yokuba ukugrumba okubanzi kwezinto zakudala akuzange kuveze naziphi na iimpawu zobukho obubalulekileyo bangaphambi kwexesha lamaRoma, "iingxoxo zesiseko saseRoma eLondon zixhaphakile kwaye azikho mpikiswano."[5] 

Ekuphakameni kwaso, isixeko saseRoma sasinabemi abamalunga ne-45,000-60,000 yabemi. ILondinium yayisisixeko esineemvelaphi ezahlukeneyo, esinabemi abavela phesheya koBukhosi baseRoma, kuquka abantu bomthonyama baseBritannia, kwilizwekazi laseYurophu, kuMbindi Mpuma, nakuMntla Afrika.[6] AmaRoma akha uDonga lwaseLondon ngexesha elithile phakathi kwe-AD 190 kunye no-225. Imida yesixeko saseRoma yayifana naleyo yeSixeko saseLondon namhlanje, nangona iSixeko sinabela entshona kuneLudgate yaseLondinium, kwaye iThames yayingacuthwanga kwaye ibe banzi ngakumbi kunokuba kunjalo namhlanje, kunye nonxweme lwaseLondinium kumantla kancinane onxweme lwesixeko. AmaRoma akha ibhulorho enqumla umlambo, ekuqaleni kuka AD 50, kufutshane neLondon Bridge yanamhlanje. 

Ukuwohloka 
Ngexesha lokwakhiwa koDonga lwaseLondon, ubutyebi beso sixeko babudodobala, yaye sasijamelene neengxaki zobhubhani nomlilo. Ubukhosi baseRoma bangena kwixesha elide lokungazinzi kunye nokuncipha, kuquka ne-Carausian Revolt eBritani. Ngenkulungwane yesi-3 neyesine, isixeko sasihlaselwa ngabahlaseli basePicts, baseScots, nabaseSaxon. Ukuwohloka kwaqhubeka, kwi-Londinium kunye ne-Empire, kwaye ngo-AD 410 amaRoma arhoxa ngokupheleleyo eBritani. Uninzi lwezakhiwo zikawonke-wonke zaseRoma eLondinium ngeli xesha zazisele ziwohlokile kwaye zingasasetyenziswa, kwaye ngokuthe ngcembe emva kokurhoxa ngokusemthethweni isixeko saphantse saphantse ukuba (ukuba akunjalo, ngamanye amaxesha, ngokupheleleyo) singahlali mntu. Iziko lorhwebo kunye nabemi bafuduka besuka kwiLondinium ebiyelwe ngodonga baya eLundenwic ("imarike yaseLondon"), indawo yokuhlala ngasentshona, malunga nendawo yanamhlanje yaseStrand/Aldwych/ 

Covent 
Garden 
. I-Wessex, nangona ukusuka kwinkulungwane yesi-8 yayihlala iphantsi kwesoyikiso sokuhlaselwa ngamaqela ahlukeneyo kubandakanya iiVikings. 


I-Plaque kufuphi ne-Southwark Bridge iphawula imisebenzi malunga nexesha likaKumkani uAlfred
UBede ubhala ukuba ngo-AD 604 uSt Augustine wangcwalisa uMellitus njengobhishophu wokuqala kubukumkani base-Anglo-Saxon baseMpuma Saxons kunye nokumkani wabo, uSæberht. Umalume kaSæberht kunye nomphathi omkhulu, u-Æthelberht, ukumkani waseKent, wakha icawa enikezelwe kwiSt Paul eLondon, njengendawo yokuhlala kabhishophu omtsha.[7] Kucingelwa ukuba, nangona kungangqinwanga, ukuba le cathedral yokuqala yase-Anglo-Saxon yayimi kwindawo enye neyasemva kwexesha eliphakathi kunye necathedrals ekhoyo 
Isiganeko esibalulekileyo ngexesha leMvukelo yaBalimi, 1381: inkokeli yabo uWat Tyler uhlatywe nguWilliam Walworth, iNkosi uSodolophu. 
Bona kwakhona: Norman kunye Medieval London

U-Alfred the Great, uKumkani waseWessex wathatha kwaye waqala ukuhlaliswa kwakhona kwendawo yakudala ebiyelwe ngodonga lwaseRoma, ngo-886, kwaye wonyula umkhwenyana wakhe u-Earl Æthelred waseMercia phezu kwayo njengenxalenye yokuphinda bathathe indawo yeViking eNgilani. Indawo yokuhlala ehlaziyiweyo ye-Anglo-Saxon yaziwa njenge ("London Fort", isithili). Umbhali-mbali uAsser wathi “uAlfred, ukumkani wama-Anglo-Saxon, wasibuyisela isixeko saseLondon ngokumangalisayo ... waza wasenza sahlala kwakhona.”[8] “Ukubuyiselwa” kuka-Alfred kwakuquka ukuhlaliswa ngokutsha nokuhlaziya isixeko saseRoma esasiphantse sashiywa sibiyelwe, ukwakha iindawo zokuzilolonga ecaleni komlambo iThames, kunye nokubekwa kwesicwangciso esitsha sesitrato sesixeko.[9] 

Ukuthatha kuka-Alfred iLondon kunye nokwakhiwa kwakhona kwesixeko saseRoma esidala kwaba lutshintsho kwimbali, kungekuphela nje njengokumiselwa ngokusisigxina kweSixeko saseLondon, kodwa kwakhona njengenxalenye yomzuzu wokumanyanisa ekuqaleni kweNgilani, kunye ne-Wessex yaba bubukumkani bamaNgesi obuphambili kunye nokugxothwa (ukusa kwinqanaba elithile) kokuhlala kunye nokuhlaselwa kweeViking. Ngelixa iLondon, kwaye ngenene iNgilani, zathi emva koko ziphantsi kohlaselo olungakumbi lweViking kunye neDanish kunye nokuhlala, ukusekwa kweSixeko saseLondon kunye noBukumkani baseNgilani kwaphumelela.[10] 

Ngenkulungwane ye-10, iAthelstan yavumela ukuba kusekwe iiminti ezisibhozo, xa kuthelekiswa nezintandathu kwikomkhulu layo, iWinchester, nto leyo ebonisa ubutyebi beso sixeko. Ibhulorho yaseLondon, eyayiwele kwintshabalalo emva kokufuduswa kwamaRoma kunye nokulahlwa kweLondinium, yaphinda yakhiwa ziiSaxons, kodwa yatshatyalaliswa ngamaxesha athile luhlaselo lweViking kunye nezaqhwithi. 

Njengoko ugqaliselo lwezorhwebo kunye nabemi lwabuyiselwa ngaphakathi kwiindonga zakudala zaseRoma, indawo yokuhlala endala yaseSaxon yaseLundenwic yashiywa kakhulu kwaye yafumana igama lika-Ealdwic ("indawo yokuhlala yakudala"). Eli gama lisaphila nanamhlanje njenge-Aldwych ("indawo yentengiso endala"), igama lesitrato kunye nommandla weSixeko saseWestminster phakathi kweWestminster kunye neSixeko saseLondon. 

Era Medieval 

Imephu yaseLondon malunga ne-1300 

Ukulandela iDabi laseHastings, uWilliam uMnqobi wahamba waya eLondon, waya kufikelela eSouthwark, kodwa akazange akwazi ukuwela iLondon Bridge okanye woyise abantu baseLondon. Ekugqibeleni wawuwela uMlambo iThames eWallingford, ewuphanga umhlaba njengoko wayehamba. Endaweni yokuqhubeka nemfazwe, uEdgar wase-Ætheling, uEdwin waseMercia kunye noMorcar waseNorthumbria banikezela eBerkhamsted. UWilliam wanika abemi baseLondon umqulu ngo-1075; isixeko sasingomnye wemizekelo embalwa yokuba amaNgesi agcine igunya elithile. Esi sixeko sasingagutyungelwa yiDomesday Book. 

UWilliam wakha iinqaba ezintathu ezijikeleze isixeko, ukugcina abantu baseLondon boyisiwe: 

iTower of London, esesona siseko siphambili. 
IBaynard's Castle, engasekhoyo kodwa yanika igama layo kwiwadi yesixeko. 
Inqaba yaseMontfichet okanye iNqaba kwiNduli yaseLudgate, eyadilizwa yaze yathengiswa ngenkulungwane ye-13. 
Malunga no-1132 isiXeko sanikwa ilungelo lokumisela oonothimba baso endaweni yokuba noonothimba abanyulwe ngukumkani. Oonothimba abanyuliweyo baseLondon basebenze njengoonothimba kwidolophu yaseMiddlesex. Oku kuthetha ukuba iSixeko kunye neMiddlesex zithathwa njengenye kwezolawulo zokujongana nolwaphulo-mthetho kunye nokugcina uxolo (kungekhona ukuba idolophu ibixhomekeke kwisixeko). Oonothimba baseLondon baqhubekile nokusebenzela iMiddlesex de idolophu yaphinda yanikwa oonothimba bayo kwakhona kulandela uMthetho woRhulumente waseKhaya ka-1888.[11][12] Ngo-1141 lonke iqela labemi lalijongwa njengoluntu olunye. Le 'commune' yayiyimvelaphi yeSixeko saseLondon Corporation kwaye abemi bafumana ilungelo lokumisela, ngemvume yokumkani, usodolophu ngo-1189-kunye nokunyula ngokuthe ngqo usodolophu ukusuka ku-1215. 

Ukususela kumaxesha aphakathi, isixeko siye saqulunqwa ngamawadi amandulo angama-25, ngalinye likhokelwa yi-alderman, ehlala ehlala i-Wardmotes ngonyaka. I-Folkmoot, yesiXeko siphela eyayibanjelwe kumnqamlezo ongaphandle we-St Paul's Cathedral, nayo yayikhe yabanjwa. Uninzi lwee-ofisi zamaxesha aphakathi kunye nezithethe ziyaqhubeka ukuza kuthi ga ngoku, zibonisa ubume obukhethekileyo beSixeko kunye neQumrhu laso. 

Ngowe-1381, iMvukelo yaBalimi yachaphazela iLondon. Aba bavukeli basithimba iSixeko kunye neNqaba yaseLondon, kodwa imvukelo yaphela emva kokuba inkokeli yaso, uWat Tyler, ebulewe kungquzulwano olwaluquka iNkosi uSodolophu uWilliam Walworth. Ngo-1450, imikhosi yabavukeli yaphinda yasithimba isiXeko ngexesha leMvukelo kaJack Cade ngaphambi kokuba igxothwe ngabemi baseLondon kulandela umlo owawuphalaza igazi eLondon Bridge. Ngo-1550, ummandla osemazantsi eLondon Bridge eSouthwark waba phantsi kolawulo lwesiXeko ngokusekwa kwewadi yeBridge Without. 


Imephu ye "Woodcut" yaseLondon, eyaqala ngeminyaka yoo-1560s 

imephu ebonisa ubungakanani boMlilo omkhulu waseLondon, otshabalalise phantse i80% yesiXeko.

Umlilo oMkhulu we-1666 njengoko uboniswe kumzobo wenkulungwane ye-17: ubonisa iBhulorho yase-Old London ngasekhohlo, iicawa, izindlu, kunye neNqaba yaseLondon ngasekunene, njengoko ibonwa kwisikhephe esikufuphi neTower Wharf. 
Esi sixeko satsha kanobom kangangezihlandlo eziliqela, esona sibi sasingowe-1123 nakuMlilo Omkhulu waseLondon ngowe-1666. Yomibini le mililo yayibizwa ngokuba nguMlilo Omkhulu. Emva komlilo we-1666, inani lezicwangciso zazotywa ukuze kulungiswe isixeko kunye nepateni yesitrato saso ukuba sibe sisixeko esinesitayile sovuselelo esineebhloko ezicwangcisiweyo zasezidolophini, izikwere kunye neebhowudi. Ezi zicwangciso phantse azizange zithathwe ngokupheleleyo, kwaye ipateni yesitrato samaxesha aphakathi yaphinda yavela phantse ngokupheleleyo. 

Ekuqaleni kwexesha langoku 
Inkulungwane ye-19 neye-20 
Ngee-1630s iCrown yafuna ukuba iNkampani yesiXeko saseLondon yandise ulawulo lwayo kwimimandla ejikelezileyo. Kuloo nto maxa wambi ibizwa ngokuba “kukukwala okukhulu”, iQumrhu lathi hayi kuKumkani, nto leyo ngokuyinxenye ichaza ubume bayo obukhethekileyo borhulumente ukuza kuthi ga ngoku.[13]

Ngasekupheleni kwenkulungwane ye-16, iLondon iye yaba liziko eliphambili leebhanki, urhwebo lwamazwe ngamazwe kunye norhwebo. I-Royal Exchange yasekwa ngo-1565 nguMhlekazi Thomas Gresham njengeziko lorhwebo kubarhwebi baseLondon, kwaye yazuza ukuxhaswa kweRoyal ngo-1571. Nangona ingasasetyenziswanga injongo yayo yasekuqaleni, indawo yayo kwikona yeCornhill kunye neThreadneedle Street iyaqhubeka ibe liziko lejografi yedolophu engundoqo yebhanki yebhanki kunye neendawo zebhanki eNgilani ezichaseneyo kwi-Reserve Banking kunye nenkonzo yezemali, kunye ne-Royal 13 yenkonzo yemali, kunye ne-Royal Banking kunye neenkonzo zezezimali. Kwangoko kumazantsi eCornhill, isitalato iLombard yayiyindawo ukusuka kwi1691 yeLloyd's Coffee House, eyaba yimarike yeinshurensi ekhokelayo kwihlabathi. Icandelo le-inshorensi yaseLondon liyaqhubeka ukusekwe kule ndawo, ngakumbi kwisitalato iLime. 

Ngo-1708, umsebenzi wobugcisa kaChristopher Wren, iSt Paul's Cathedral, wagqitywa ngomhla wokuzalwa kwakhe. Inkonzo yokuqala yayibanjwe nge-2 kaDisemba 1697, ngaphezu kweminyaka eyi-10 ngaphambili. Yathatha indawo yeSt Paul's yantlandlolo, eyayitshatyalaliswe ngokupheleleyo kuMlilo Omkhulu waseLondon, kwaye igqalwa njengeyona cawa ibalaseleyo yaseBritani nomzekelo omhle woyilo lweBaroque. 

Ukukhula kweLondon 
Inkulungwane ye-18 yayilixesha lokukhula ngokukhawuleza kweLondon, nto leyo ebonisa ukwanda kwabemi belizwe, ukuvuseleleka kwangaphambili kweNguqu yezoShishino, kunye nendima yaseLondon embindini woBukhosi baseBritane obuguqukayo. Indawo yasedolophini yandiswa ngaphaya kwemida yeSixeko saseLondon, ngakumbi ngeli xesha ukuya eWest End naseWestminster. 

Ulwando lwaqhubeka lwaza lwakhawuleza ngakumbi ekuqaleni kwenkulungwane ye-19, iLondon ikhula macala onke. Ukuya eMpuma iZibuko laseLondon likhule ngokukhawuleza kule nkulungwane, ngolwakhiwo lweedokhi ezininzi, ezifunekayo njengoko umlambo iThames kwisiXeko wawungenako ukumelana nomthamo worhwebo. Ukufika koololiwe kunye neTube kwakuthetha ukuba iLondon inokwandisa indawo enkulu. Embindini wenkulungwane ye-19, iLondon ibisakhula ngokukhawuleza kubemi kunye nommandla, isiXeko sasisele siyinxalenye encinci ye-metropolis ebanzi.

Umzamo wenziwa ngo-1894 kunye neKomishoni yaseRoyal kuManyano lweSixeko kunye neNqila yaseLondon ukuphelisa umahluko phakathi kwesixeko kunye neNqila engqongileyo yaseLondon, kodwa utshintsho kurhulumente eWestminster luthetha ukuba ukhetho aluzange luthathwe. Isixeko njengopolitiko olwahlukileyo sasinda ngaphandle kwesikhundla saso ngaphakathi kwindibano yaseLondon kunye nohlengahlengiso oluninzi kurhulumente wasekhaya. Ukuxhasa esi simo, isixeko sasiyindawo yepalamente ekhethekileyo esonyula amalungu amane kwiNdlu yeMibutho engekaguquguquki, athi agcinwa emva koMthetho woHlaziyo we-1832; zicuthwe zibe zimbini phantsi koMthetho woKwabiwa ngokutsha kweZitulo ka-1885; kwaye yayeka ukuba licandelo lovoto elahlukileyo phantsi koMmeli woMthetho waBantu ka-1948. Ukusukela ngoko isixeko siliqaqobana (ngokwenani labemi kunye nommandla) kwiziXeko zaseLondon naseWestminster. 


I-St Paul's Cathedral (ekumfanekiso we-1896) ibilawula isibhakabhaka kwiSixeko kangangeenkulungwane - isakhiwo saso sangoku nguChristopher Wren sagqityezelwa ngo-1706, emva kokuba umanduleli wayo wamaxesha aphakathi atshise uninzi lweSixeko kuMlilo Omkhulu we-1666 
. amahlomela-dolophu amakhulu, nezakhiwo ezininzi zokuhlala zadilizwa ukuze kuvuleleke iiofisi. Njengemimandla emininzi yaseLondon nakwezinye izixeko zaseBritane, isiXeko saba lixhoba lokuqhushumba kwebhombu emoyeni ngexesha leMfazwe yesibini yeHlabathi, ngakumbi kwiBlitz. Ngelixa iSt Paul's Cathedral yasindayo kuhlaselo, iindawo ezinkulu zale ndawo azizange kwaye uhlaselo olukhulu lwasekupheleni kukaDisemba 1940 lwakhokelela kumlilo obizwa ngokuba nguMlilo oMkhulu weSibini waseLondon. 

Kwakukho inkqubo enkulu yokwakha kwakhona kumashumi eminyaka emva kwemfazwe, kwezinye iindawo (ezifana neBarbican) iguqule ngokumangalisayo imbonakalo yedolophu. Kodwa ukutshatyalaliswa kwelaphu elidala lembali kuvumele ukwakhiwa kophuhliso lwangoku kunye nolukhudlwana, ngexa kwezo ndawo zingachatshazelwanga kakhulu ngumonakalo weziqhushumbisi iSixeko silugcina luphawu lwaso oludala lwezakhiwo ezincinci. Ipateni yesitrato, esele ikwixesha eliphakathi, yatshintshwa kancinane kwiindawo, nangona kukho indlela yamva nje yokubuyisela umva ezinye zeenguqu zasemva kwemfazwe ezenziweyo, njengasePaternoster Square. 

IsiXeko siye safumana uhlaselo lwabanqolobi oluquka ukuqhushumbiswa kweBishopsgate ngo-1993 (IRA) kunye nokudubula kweLondon ngomhla we-7 kaJulayi 2005 (kwiSilamsi). Ukuphendula kwibhomu ye-1993, inkqubo yeendlela zokuthintela, iindawo zokuhlola kunye neekhamera zokujonga ezibizwa ngokuba yi "ring of steel" igcinwe ukulawula iindawo zokungena kwisixeko.

Ngoo-1970 kwabona ukwakhiwa kwezakhiwo zeofisi ezinde eziquka i-600-foot (183 m), i-47-storey ye-NatWest Tower, i-skyscraper yokuqala e-UK. Ngoo-2010, uphuhliso lwendawo yee-ofisi lwaluqina kwiSixeko, ngakumbi kumbindi, emantla nasempuma iindawo, ezinezakhiwo eziphakamileyo ezibandakanya i-30 St. Mary Ax (“the Gherkin”’), iSakhiwo seLeadenhall (“iCheesegrater”), i-20 Fenchurch Street (“i-Walkie-Talkie”), i-2 ye-Broadgate Tower kunye ne-Broadgate Tower. 

Elona candelo leendawo zokuhlala kwisiXeko namhlanje yiBarbican Estate, eyakhiwa phakathi ko-1965 no-1976. IMyuziyam yaseLondon yayisekwe khona de kwaba ngoMatshi ka-2023 (ngenxa yokuvulwa kwakhona eWest Smithfield ngo-2026), [14] ngelixa ezinye iinkonzo ezibonelelwa ngumbutho zisagcinwa kwiBarbican Estate. 

Ulawulo 

Guildhall liziko lomsitho kunye nolawulo lwesixeko. 

I-Mansion House yindawo yokuhlala esemthethweni yeNkosi uSodolophu. 

UJohn Stuttard, iNkosi uSodolophu weSixeko saseLondon ngo-2006–2007, ngexesha loMboniso weNkosi uSodolophu ka-2006 
Jonga 
kwakhona: Iqumrhu leSixeko saseLondon kunye neMbali yorhulumente wasekhaya eNgilani Ngokwembali inkqubo yayo yolawulo ibingeyonto ingaqhelekanga, kodwa ayizange ihlengahlengiswe nguMthetho we-Municipal Corporations Act 1835 kwaye yatshintshwa kancinane luhlaziyo lwamva, ukuze ibe kuphela korhulumente wasekhaya e-UK apho unyulo lungaqhutywa ngevoti enye yakhe wonke ummi omdala. 

Ilawulwa sisiXeko saseLondon Corporation, ekhokelwa yiNkosi uSodolophu waseLondon (akufunekanga ibhidaniswe noSodolophu owahlukileyo waseLondon, i-ofisi eyakhiwe kuphela ngonyaka wama-2000), enoxanduva lwemisebenzi eliqela kwaye enomdla kumhlaba ongaphaya kwemida yesixeko. Ngokungafaniyo nabanye abasemagunyeni basekhaya abangamaNgesi, iqumrhu linamaqumrhu amabini ebhunga: iNkundla ye-Aldermen (ngoku ubukhulu becala) kunye neNkundla yeBhunga eliqhelekileyo. INkundla ye-Aldermen imele iiwadi, kunye newadi nganye (kungakhathaliseki ubukhulu) ibuyisela i-alderman enye. Umphathi oyintloko weQumrhu une-ofisi yakudala kaMabhalane weDolophu yaseLondon. 

Esi sixeko sisixeko esinemibhiyozo yedolophu eneKomishoni yoBukhosi ekhokelwa yiNkosi uSodolophu endaweni yeNkosi-uLieutenant kwaye inoNothimba ababini endaweni kaNothimba oPhezulu (jonga uluhlu loonothimba baseLondon), ii-ofisi zenkundla ezichongwe ziinkampani zelivery, inkqubo yezopolitiko yakudala esekwe kumelo kunye nokhuseleko lwezorhwebo (imibutho). Amalungu aphezulu eenkampani zokuthengisa iinyama aziwa ngokuba ngabagadi bezilwanyana kwaye abumba iHolo iCommon, ekhetha usodolophu wenkosi, oonothimba kunye namanye amagosa athile. 

IiWadi 
Inqaku eliphambili: IiWadi zeSixeko saseLondon
Isixeko sineewadi ezingama-25. Bangamaxhoba kwinkqubo karhulumente wamaxesha aphakathi eyavumela indawo yendawo kakhulu ukuba ibekho njengeyunithi ezilawulayo ngaphakathi kwesixeko esibanzi.[15] Zinokuchazwa njengezahlulo zonyulo/zezopolitiko; amaziko emisitho, ejografi nawolawulo; amacandelwana esixeko. Iwadi nganye ine-Alderman, eyathi kwade kwaphakathi kwiminyaka yoo-1960[16] yabamba i-ofisi ubomi babo bonke kodwa ukusukela oko yazibeka kunyulo kwakhona ubuncinci rhoqo emva kweminyaka emi-6, kwaye kuphela kwe-Aldermen enyulwe ngokuthe ngqo e-United Kingdom. Iiwadi ziyaqhubeka ukuba neBeadle, indawo yakudala ngoku engumbhiyozo ubukhulu becala umsebenzi wayo oseleyo ikukuqhuba kweWardmote yonyaka yabanyuli, abameli kunye namagosa.[17] KwiWardmote i-Alderman yewadi yonyula ubuncinane uSekela-Sekela lonyaka ozayo, kwaye ii-Wardmotes nazo ziyabanjwa ngexesha lonyulo. Iwadi nganye ineQela leWadi, elifana nombutho wabahlali.[18] 

Iiwadi zindala kwaye inani lazo litshintshile izihlandlo ezithathu ukususela kwixesha lakudala: 

ngo-1394 iFarringdon yahlulwa yaba yiFarringdon Ngaphakathi kunye neFarringdon Ngaphandle 
ngo-1550 iwadi yeBridge Ngaphandle, emazantsi omlambo, yadalwa, iwadi yeBridge yaba yiBridge Ngaphakathi;[19] 
ngo-1978 ezi wadi zeBridge zadityaniswa njengewadi yeBridge. 

Imephu yeewadi njengoko zazinjalo ekupheleni kwenkulungwane ye-19 

Imephu yeewadi ukusukela ngo-2003 
Ukulandela utshintsho lwemida ngo-1994, kunye nohlaziyo lwamva lwevoti yoshishino esixekweni, bekukho umda omkhulu kunye nohlaziyo lokumelwa konyulo lweewadi ngo-2003, kwaye zaphinda zaphononongwa kwakhona ngo-2010 ngotshintsho olukhulu ukuya kutsho kwi-2010. Uphononongo lwenziwe ngamagosa aphezulu equmrhu kunye neejaji eziphezulu ze-Old Bailey;[21] iiwadi zihlaziywa yile nkqubo ukuphepha ukungahambi kakuhle. Inkqubo yokuphonononga iyingqayizivele e-United Kingdom njengoko ingaqhutywa yiKomishoni yoNyulo okanye ikhomishini yemida yorhulumente wendawo yonke iminyaka eyi-8 ukuya kwe-12, okuyiyo imeko yazo zonke ezinye iiwadi e-Great Britain. Iicawe ezikhethekileyo, iiholo zeenkampani zelivery kunye nezinye izakhiwo zembali kunye nezakhiwo ezinxulumene newadi, efana neSt Paul's Cathedral eneCastle Baynard, kunye neLondon Bridge eneBridge; utshintsho lwemida ngo-2003 lwasusa ezinye zezi zidibanisi zembali.

Iwadi nganye yonyula i-alderman kwiNkundla ye-Aldermen, kunye nabantu abaqhelekileyo (iSixeko esilingana noceba) kwiNkundla yeBhunga leSigqeba sombutho. Ngabavoti kuphela abangamaFreemen besiXeko saseLondon abafanelekileyo ukuba bame. Inani labantu abaqhelekileyo iwadi ibathumela kwiBhunga eliPhezulu liyahluka ukusuka kwisibini ukuya kwishumi, ngokuxhomekeke kwinani labavoti kwiwadi nganye. Ukususela kuphononongo lwe-2003 kuye kwavunyelwana ukuba iiwadi ezine zokuhlala ezingaphezulu: iPortsoken, iQueenhithe, i-Aldersgate kunye neCripplegate kunye zonyula i-20 yabantu abaqhelekileyo be-100, ngelixa intsalela yezoshishino ikhetha abantu abaqhelekileyo abangama-80. Utshintsho lwemida luka-2003 no-2013 lunyuse ugxininiso lweendawo zokuhlala kwiiwadi ezine ezikhankanyiweyo. 

Idatha yoBalo lwabantu ibonelela ngeewadi ezisibhozo kuneewadi zokwenyani ezingama-25, zonke ezinobungakanani obahlukeneyo kunye nabemi. Ngokuxhomekeke ekuthiyweni ngokutsha kunye nenkcazo nangaliphi na ixesha, ezi 'wadi' zobalo ziphawuleka ekubeni ezine kwezisibhozo zithatha i-67% 'yesikwere seekhilomitha' kwaye zibambe i-86% yabemi, kwaye ezi ngokwenene zazifana kwaye zithiywe ngegama leewadi ezine zesiXeko saseLondon:

Ulonyulo 
Isixeko sinenkqubo yonyulo eyodwa. Uninzi lwabavoti bayo ngabameli bamashishini kunye neminye imibutho ehlala kwizakhiwo ezisesixekweni. Iiwadi zayo zamandulo zinamanani angalinganiyo kakhulu abavoti. Kunyulo, omabini amashishini azinze esixekweni kunye nabahlali besiXeko bayavota. 

ISixeko saseLondon Corporation asizange sitshintshwe nguMthetho wamaShishini kaMasipala we-1835, kuba sasinemvume yonyulo ebanzi kunaso nasiphi na esinye idolophu okanye isixeko; eneneni, iye yandisa oku ngakumbi ngomthetho wayo olinganayo ovumela umntu ukuba abe ngumntu okhululekileyo ngaphandle kokuba ngumgcini wenyama. Ngo-1801, esi sixeko sasinabemi abamalunga ne-130,000, kodwa ukonyuka kophuhliso lwesixeko njengendawo esembindini yeshishini kukhokelele ekuweleni ngaphantsi kwe-5,000 emva kweMfazwe yesibini yeHlabathi. Ngo-2009, ivoti yoshishino yayimalunga nama-24,000, idlula kakhulu abavoti beendawo zokuhlala. [23] Njengoko iSixeko saseLondon Corporation singachatshazelwanga ngomnye umthetho kamasipala kwisithuba sexesha ukusukela ngoko, inkqubo yaso yonyulo iye yanda ngendlela engaqhelekanga. Ngokukodwa kunyulo lwesixeko okanye lwenqila, unyulo lwaso luhlala luzimele geqe.

Ishishini okanye "ivoti engeyiyo yokuhlala" yapheliswa kolunye unyulo lwebhunga lasekhaya lase-UK nguMmeli woMthetho waBantu ka-1969, kodwa wagcinwa kwisiXeko saseLondon. Esona sizathu siphambili esinikwe ngoorhulumente be-UK abalandelelanayo ukugcina le ndlela yokunika amashishini ukumelwa, kukuba isixeko "indawo yokwenza ishishini".[24] Malunga nama-330,000 abantu abangengabo abahlali babandakanya abemi bemini kwaye basebenzisa uninzi lweenkonzo zabo, bebodlula kakhulu abahlali, ababalelwa kuma-7,000 (2011). Ngokwahlukileyo koko, abachasi bokugcinwa kwevoti yeshishini baphikisa ukuba yimbangela yokungahambi kakuhle kweziko.[25] 

UMthetho weSixeko saseLondon (uNyulo lweWadi) ka-2002 (c. vi), umthetho wasekhaya wePalamente, [26] wayihlaziya inkqubo yokuvota kwaye yandisa kakhulu inkululeko yoshishino, ivumela amashishini amaninzi ukuba amelwe. Ngaphantsi kwenkqubo entsha, inani labavoti abangengabo abemi liphindwe kabini ukusuka kwi-16,000 ukuya kwi-32,000. Iifemu ebezifudula zihluthelwa amalungelo (kunye neminye imibutho) zinelungelo lokutyumba abavoti, ukongeza kwabo sele bemelwe, kwaye onke amaqumrhu anjalo ngoku kufuneka akhethe abavoti bawo ngendlela yokumelwa. Amaqumrhu aqeshe abantu abangaphantsi kwe-10 angatyumba umvoti omnye; abo baqesha abantu abali-10 ukuya kuma-50 umvoti omnye kubasebenzi aba-5; abo baqeshe abantu abangaphezu kwama-50 abavoti abali-10 kunye nomvoti owongezelelweyo omnye kubasebenzi abangama-50 ngaphaya kwabasebenzi bokuqala abangama-50. Lo Mthetho uphinde watshintsha eminye imiba yesenzo sangaphambili esinxulumene nonyulo esixekweni, ukusuka ngo-1957. Inqaku 

leTempile 
eliPhambili: ITempile, iLondon 
Inner Temple kunye neTempile ePhakathi (engabamelwane omnye komnye) kwiwadi esentshona yeFarringdon kunye nedolophu yaseFarringdon. ii-enclaves ezizimeleyo. Zimbini kwiinkululeko ezimbalwa eziseleyo, igama elidala lecandelo lejografi elinamalungelo akhethekileyo. Ziindawo ezongezelelekileyo, [27] ngokwembali azilawulwa sisiXeko saseLondon Corporation[28] (kwaye namhlanje zithathwa njengamagunya asekuhlaleni ngeenjongo ezininzi[29]) kwaye ngokulinganayo ngaphandle kolawulo lwecawa lukaBhishophu waseLondon. 

Eminye imisebenzi 

IMarike yaseLeadenhall yimarike eyimbali phakathi kwesitalato iGracechurch kunye neLime Street. 
Ngaphakathi esixekweni, iQumrhu lingabanini kwaye liqhuba zombini iMarike yeSmithfield kunye neLeadenhall Market. Inomhlaba ongaphaya kwemida yawo, kubandakanya neendawo ezivulekileyo (iipaki, amahlathi kunye neendawo eziqhelekileyo) ngaphakathi nakufutshane neGreater London, kubandakanya uninzi lwehlathi le-Epping kunye neHampstead Heath. I-Corporation ingumnini weMarike ye-Old Spitalfields kunye ne-Billingsgate Fish Market, kwi-London Borough yase-Tower Hamlets. Ingumnikazi kwaye inceda ngemali i-Old Bailey, iNkundla yoLwaphulo-mthetho ePhakathi yaseNgilani naseWales, njengesipho kwisizwe, sele iqalile njengeSeshini yesiXeko kunye ne-Middlesex. Obekekileyo Umbutho wase-Ireland, iqumrhu elidityaniswe ngokusondeleyo nequmrhu, ukwaneendawo ezininzi zoluntu kuMntla Ireland.

Isixeko sinamapolisa aso azimeleyo, isiXeko saseLondon samaPolisa—iBhunga eliqhelekileyo (iqumrhu eliyintloko lequmrhu) ligunya lamapolisa.[30] Iqumrhu likwaqhuba i-Hampstead Heath Constabulary, i-Epping Forest Keepers kunye neendawo zentengiso zeSixeko saseLondon (amalungu azo angasangqinwayo njengamagosa kodwa agcina isihloko esiyimbali). Uninzi lweLondon enkulu lubanjwe yiNkonzo yamaPolisa eMetropolitan, esekelwe eNew Scotland Yard. 

Esi sixeko sinesibhedlele esinye, iSibhedlele iSt Bartholomew, nesaziwa njenge'Barts'. Yasekwa ngo-1123, ibekwe eSmithfield, kwaye ifumana uhlaziyo ekudala ilindelwe emva kwamathandabuzo malunga nokuqhubeka nokusetyenziswa kwayo ngeminyaka yoo-1990. 

Isixeko sesesithathu ngobukhulu umxhasi wezobugcisa wase-UK. Yongamela iZiko leBarbican kwaye ibonelela ngeenkampani ezininzi ezibalulekileyo zobugcisa. 

UGunyaziwe wezeMpilo weZibuko laseLondon, oluluxanduva lwequmrhu, unoxanduva lwayo yonke imisebenzi yezempilo yezibuko kwindawo ejikelezayo yomlambo iThames, kubandakanywa iZibuko laseLondon kunye namazibuko anxulumeneyo, kunye neSikhululo seenqwelomoya saseLondon City.[31] Iqumrhu longamela iBridge House Estates, egcina iBlackfriars Bridge, iMillennium Bridge, iSouthwark Bridge, iLondon Bridge kunye neTower Bridge. Iflegi yesiXeko ibhabha phezu kweTower Bridge, nangona kungekho ndawo ikhoyo esixekweni.[32] 

Umda weSixeko 

saseLondon umda ophawulayo xa usondela kwiBhulorho yaseLondon 
Ubungakanani besixeko babuthintelwe ludonga olukhuselayo olubizwa ngokuba ludonga lwaseLondon, olwakhiwa ngamaRoma ngasekupheleni kwenkulungwane yesi-2 ukukhusela isixeko sabo esinezibuko. Nangona kunjalo imida yeSixeko saseLondon ayisadibani nodonga lwesixeko esidala, njengoko iSixeko sandise ulawulo lwaso kancinci ngokuhamba kwexesha. Ngexesha lamaxesha aphakathi, ulawulo lwesi sixeko lwanda ngasentshona, lunqumla umda oyimbali osentshona wendawo yokuhlala yantlandlolo—uMlambo iFleet—ngakwiFleet Street ukuya kwiBar yeTempile. Isixeko sikwathathe nezinye "iibhari zesiXeko" ezazimi ngaphaya nje kwendawo endala ebiyelwe ngodonga, njengaseHolborn, eAldersgate, eWest Smithfield, eBishopsgate naseAldgate. La yayingamasango abalulekileyo esixeko yaye ulawulo lwawo lwalubalulekile ekulondolozeni amalungelo akhethekileyo esixeko kurhwebo oluthile. 


Umfanekiso we-Dragon kwisikhumbuzo seBar yeTempile, ephawula umda phakathi kweSixeko saseLondon kunye neSixeko sase-Westminster 
Uninzi lwedonga luye lwanyamalala, kodwa amacandelo amaninzi ahlala ebonakala. Inxalenye ekufutshane neMyuziyam yaseLondon yatyhilwa emva kokutshatyalaliswa kohlaselo lomoya ngomhla wama-29 kuDisemba 1940 kwindawo ephakamileyo yeBlitz. Amanye amacandelo abonakalayo aseSt Alphage, kwaye kukho amacandelo amabini kufutshane neNqaba yaseLondon. I-River Fleet yenziwa ngumjelo emva koMlilo oMkhulu ka-1666 kwaye emva koko ngezigaba yaqalwa ngezitena kwaye ukusukela ngenkulungwane ye-18 "yemilambo okanye imisinga" elahlekileyo yaseLondon, namhlanje iphantsi komhlaba njengemvula yemvula.

Umda wesixeko awuzange utshintshwe de kwatshintshwa umda ongephi ngomhla woku-1 kuTshazimpuzi ka-1994, xa wawusanda kancinci ukuya entshona, emantla nasempuma, uthatha iipasela ezincinci zomhlaba ukusuka kwiLondon Boroughs yaseWestminster, eCamden, eIslington, eHackney naseTower Hamlets. Eyona njongo iphambili yolu tshintsho yayikukucoca imida apho yayishiywe lixesha ngenxa yeenguqu kubume bendawo yasezidolophini. Kule nkqubo isixeko sikwaphulukene nemihlaba emincinci, nangona bekukho inzuzo epheleleyo (iSixeko sikhule ukusuka kwi-1.05 ukuya kwi-1.12 yeemayile zesikwere). Okuphawuleka kakhulu, utshintsho wabeka (emva koko kutshanje kuphuhliswa) Broadgate estate ngokupheleleyo esixekweni.[33] 

ISouthwark, kumazantsi esixeko kwelinye icala leThames, yayingaphakathi kweSixeko phakathi kowe-1550 nowe-1899 njengeWadi yeBhulorho Ngaphandle, imeko enxulumene neGuildable Manor. Uxanduva lolawulo lwesi sixeko apho lwathi shwaka ngexesha laphakathi kweVictorian njengoko imiba eyahlukeneyo yolawulo lwemetropolitan yayinatyiselwa kwimimandla ekufutshane. Namhlanje iyinxalenye yeLondon Borough yaseSouthwark. INqaba yaseLondon ibisoloko ingaphandle kwesixeko kwaye iza phantsi kweLondon Borough yeTower Hamlets. 

Izixhobo, isaci kunye neflegi 
Amanqaku aphambili: ICoat of Arms yeSixeko saseLondon kunye neFlegi yeSixeko saseLondon 

iXeko laseLondon zixhonywe kwingubo yesali, njengoko kubonwa ngaphandle kweRoyal Courts of Justice ngexesha loMboniso weLord Mayor's Show, 2011 
IQumrhu leSixeko saseLondon linempumelelo epheleleyo yokuthwala izixhobo ezibandakanya ikhaka elixhonywe phezu kwesikhuseli, isikhuseli, isikhuseli esixhonywe phezu kwayo. abaxhasi macala omabini kunye nemotto eboniswe kumqulu phantsi kweengalo. [34][35][36] 

Idyasi yengalo "yabhalwa kwakudala" kwiKholeji yeSizwe. Iingalo ziquka ikhaka lesilivere elinomnqamlezo obomvu kunye nekrele elibomvu elime nkqo kwikota yokuqala. Badibanisa imifuziselo abangcwele umxhasi eNgilani naseLondon: uMnqamlezo St George kunye nesimboli yokufela ukholo Saint Paul. [35][36] Ikrele lidla ngokucingelwa ukuba likhumbula ukubulawa kwenkokeli yovukelo lwabaLimi uWat Tyler nguSodolophu waseLondon uWilliam Walworth. Nangona kunjalo iingalo zazisetyenziswa kwiinyanga ezithile phambi kokufa kukaTyler, kwaye isithethe sokuba ikrele likaWalworth liyaboniswa linokuba lisusela ekupheleni kwenkulungwane ye-17. [35][37][38][39] 

Imotto yesiLatini yesixeko ithi "Domine dirige nos", eguqulela ngokuthi "Nkosi, siqondise". Kucingelwa ukuba yamkelwa ngenkulungwane ye-17, njengoko ingxelo yokuqala yayo ikwi-1633.[36][38] 

Ibhanile yeengalo (uyilo olukwikhaka) ibhabha njengeflegi.
 
IJografi
IsiXeko saseLondon sesona sixeko sincinci semibhiyozo yaseNgilani ngendawo kunye nabemi, kwaye eyesine enabantu abaninzi. Kwizithili ezingama-326 zamaNgesi, yeyesibini ukuba mncinci ngokwabemi, emva kweIsles of Scilly, kwaye yeyona incinci ngokwengingqi. Ikwasesona sixeko sincinci samaNgesi ngabemi (kwaye eBritane, zizixeko ezibini kuphela eWales zincinci), kwaye esona sincinci e-UK ngokwendawo. 

Umphakamo weSixeko usukela kumphakamo wolwandle kwiThames ukuya kwi-21.6 yeemitha (71 ft) ekudibaneni kweNdlela yeHolborn kunye neChancery Lane.[40] Iinduli ezimbini ezincinci kodwa eziphawulekayo zingaphakathi kombindi wembali, iLudgate Hill ngasentshona kunye neCornhill ngasempuma. Phakathi kwabo kwagijima iWalbrook, enye yemilambo emininzi "elahlekileyo" okanye imisinga yaseLondon (enye yiFleet). Imida 

yeMida 

yangoku yeSixeko saseLondon, ebonisa iidolophu ezingqonge iLondon kunye nomda wangaphambi ko-1994 (apho utshintshiwe) ngombala obomvu. Indawo egqunywe yiTempile yaNgaphakathi kunye nephakathi iphawulwe ngombala oluhlaza. 
Ukuqala ngasentshona, apho iSixeko sinqumla iWestminster, umda unqumla i-Victoria Embankment ukusuka kumlambo iThames, udlulele kwintshona yeTempile ePhakathi, emva koko ujike umgama omfutshane ecaleni kweStrand kwaye kufutshane neTemple Bar emva koko unyuke iChancery Lane, apho umda weCamden. Ijikela ngasempuma ngakwiHolborn ukuya eHolborn Circus emva koko iye emantla-mpuma kwisitalato iCharterhouse. Njengoko inqumla iFarringdon Road iba ngumda we-Islingt . Iyaqhubeka eAldersgate, iya emantla, kwaye ijikela empuma kwizitrato ezingemva nje emva kokuba iAldersgate ibe yiGoswell Road, ukusukela ngo-1994 ibandakanya yonke iGolden Lane Estate yequmrhu. Apha, eBaltic Street West, yeyona ndawo isemantla. Umda ubandakanya yonke iBarbican Estate kwaye uqhubeleka ngasempuma ecaleni kwesitalato iRopemaker kunye nokuqhubekeka kwayo kwelinye icala leMoorgate, iba yiNdawo eseMazantsi. Iya emantla, ifikelela kumda kunye neHackney, emva koko impuma, emantla, empuma kwizitrato ezingasemva, kunye neSitrato soNqulo senza umda osemantla, ukuze ibandakanye i-Broadgate estate. Umda ke ujikela emazantsi eNorton Folgate kwaye ube ngumda kunye neTower Hamlets. Iqhubekeka emazantsi ukuya kutsho eBishopsgate, kwaye ithatha izitalato ezingasemva ukuya kwiSitalato iMiddlesex (iPetticoat Lane) apho iqhubekeka emazantsi-mpuma nasezantsi. Emva koko ijikela ngasemzantsi-ntshona, inqumla iMinories ukuze ingaquki iNqaba yaseLondon, ize ifike kumlambo iThames. 

Umda ke unyuka unyuka embindini wejelo elisezantsi lomlambo weThames, ngaphandle kokuba iBhulorho iBlackfriars (kubandakanya umlambo ongaphantsi kunye nomhlaba ekupheleni kwayo esemazantsi) iyinxalenye yesiXeko ngokupheleleyo, isenza isiXeko kunye neBorough yaseRichmond phezu kweThames kuphela kwezithili zaseLondon ezinqumla emantla nakumazantsi omlambo. Ubude kunye nommandla osemazantsi weBhulorho yaseLondon yinxalenye yesixeko ngeenjongo ezithile[41] (kwaye ke yinxalenye yewadi yeBhulorho).[42]

Imida iphawulwe ngeebhodi ezimnyama ezinophawu lwesixeko, kunye namanqaku omda wedragoni kumasango amakhulu, anjengeHolborn kunye nesiphelo esisemazantsi seLondon Bridge. Ilitye lesikhumbuzo elibaluleke ngakumbi liphawula umda weTemple Bar eFleet Street. 

Kwezinye iindawo, isithili sezemali sinabela kancinane ngaphaya kwemida, ngakumbi ukuya emantla nasempuma, ukuya kwidolophu yaseLondon iTower Hamlets, iHackney ne-Islington, kwaye ngokungekho sikweni ezi ndawo zithathwa njengenxalenye ye "Square Mile". Ukusukela ngeminyaka yoo-1990s umphetho ongasempuma, ukuya kutsho eHackney kunye neTower Hamlets, iye yakhula ibeyingqwalasela yophuhliso lweeofisi ezinkulu ngenxa yokufumaneka kweziza ezinkulu xa kuthelekiswa nangaphakathi kwesixeko. 

Iigadi kunye nobugcisa boluntu 
Bona kwakhona: Uluhlu lobugcisa boluntu kwisiXeko saseLondon 

Finsbury Circus, eyona ndawo inkulu evulekileyo yoluntu, ibonwa ukusuka kwiTower 42 
Esi sixeko asinazo iipaki ezinobungakanani ngaphakathi komda walo, kodwa sinothungelwano lwenani elikhulu leegadi kunye neendawo ezincinci ezivulekileyo, uninzi lwazo lugcinwe ngumbutho. Ezi zisuka kwiigadi ezisesikweni ezifana neseFinsbury Circus, equlathe i-bowling eluhlaza kunye ne-bandstand, ukuya kwiiyadi zecawa ezifana neSitalato i-St Olave Hart, ukuya emanzini kunye nomsebenzi wobugcisa kwiiyadi kunye neendlela ezihamba ngeenyawo.[43]

Kukho inani leegadi zabucala kunye neendawo ezivulekileyo, rhoqo ngaphakathi kweeyadi zophuhliso olukhulu lwentengiso. Emibini kwezona zinkulu zezo zeTempile yaNgaphakathi kunye neThe Middle Temple Inns yeNkundla, kumzantsi-ntshona othe qelele. 

IThames kunye nokuhamba kwayo ngasemlanjeni kuya kuxatyiswa ngakumbi njengendawo evulekileyo kwaye kwiminyaka yakutshanje kuye kwenziwa iinzame zokwandisa amandla okuba abahambi ngeenyawo bafikelele kwaye bahambe ecaleni komlambo. 

Imozulu 
Esona sikhululo semozulu sikufutshane ngokwembali ibiliZiko leMozulu laseLondon eKingsway/Holborn, nangona uqwalaselo lwaphela ngo-2010. Ngoku iSt. James Park ibonelela ngofundo olukufutshane olusemthethweni.

Isixeko sinemozulu yolwandlekazi (Köppen "Cfb") eguqulwe sisiqithi sobushushu basezidolophini kumbindi weLondon. Oku kudla ngokubangela ukuba ixesha lasebusuku libe lincinci kuneendawo ezingaphandle. Umzekelo, u-Agasti uthetha ubuncinane[45] we-14.7 °C (58.5 °F) uthelekiseka nenani le-13.3 °C (55.9 °F) yeGreenwich[46] kunye neHeathrow[47] ngelixa i-11.6 °C (52.9 °F) e-Wisley[48] embindini weemayile ezininzi ze-Greenwich Belt. Onke amanani abhekiselele kwixesha loqwalaselo lika-1971–2000. 

Ngokunjalo, isikhululo semozulu sibambe irekhodi lelona qondo lobushushu lisezantsi lase-UK ngobusuku, i-24.0 °C (75.2 °F), irekhodishwe nge-4 Agasti 1990. [49] Ubuninzi bungama-37.6 °C (99.7 °F), lusekwe nge-10 ka-Agasti 2003.[50] Ubuncinane obugqibeleleyo[51] kwisikhululo semozulu yi-−8.2 °C nje (17.2 °F), xa kuthelekiswa nokufunda malunga -15.0 °C (5.0 °F) ukuya kwincam yeLondon. Ngokungaqhelekanga, obu bushushu babusebudeni bengqele eqhaqhazelisa amazinyo nekhephu (phakathi kuJanuwari 1987), kunokuba kube nengqele epholileyo ngobusuku—kubanjwa umoya obandayo ngenxa yommandla omkhulu wedolophu ongqonge eso sixeko. 

Isikhululo sibambe irekhodi lelona qondo lobushushu liphezulu laseBritani lenyanga, [52] 24.5 °C (76.1 °F) (lithetha ubuninzi be-29.2 °C (84.6 °F), lithetha ubuncinane be-19.7 °C (67.5 °F) ngo-Julayi ka-2006). Nangona kunjalo, ngokomlinganiselo wobushushu emini, iCambridge NIAB[53] kunye neBotanical Gardens[54] enomlinganiselo ophakamileyo wama-29.1 °C (84.4 °F), kunye neHeathrow[55] ene-29.0 °C (84.2 °F) zonke zigqithile koku.
