Uncwadi lwabantwana luye lwabunjwa yimithombo yonqulo, njengezithethe zamaPuritan, okanye ngeembono zentanda-bulumko nezenzululwazi ngeempembelelo zikaCharles Darwin noJohn Locke.[48] Ngasekupheleni kwenkulungwane yeshumi elinesithoba kunye nasekuqaleni kwenkulungwane yamashumi amabini zaziwa njenge "Golden Age of Children's Literature" kuba iincwadi ezininzi zabantwana zakudala zapapashwa ngoko. 

Iphepha elisuka kwincwadi yamanqaku esetyenziswa njengedayari ebhalwe ngesandla 
Engapapashwanga 
Jonga kwakhona: Uluhlu lweencwadi ezingapapashwanga 
Iincwadi ezininzi zisetyenziselwa kuphela ukurekhoda izimvo zobuqu, amanqaku, nee-akhawunti, ezinjengeencwadana zamanqaku, iincwadi zelogi, iincwadi eziqhelekileyo, kunye needayari. Ezi ncwadi azifane zipapashwe kwaye zidla ngokutshatyalaliswa okanye zihlale ziyimfihlo. 

Iincwadi zeedilesi, iincwadi zefowuni, kunye nekhalenda/iincwadi zokuqeshwa ziqhele ukusetyenziselwa ukurekhoda amadinga, iintlanganiso kunye nolwazi loqhagamshelwano lomntu. Amashishini ngokwembali ayesebenzisa iincwadi ze-accounting ezifana neejenali kunye neeledgers ukurekhoda idatha yezemali kwindlela ebizwa ngokuba yi-bookkeeping (ngoku edla ngokubanjelwa kwiikhomputha kunokuba ibhalwe ngesandla). 

Ukuqokelelwa kunye nokuhlelwa 

Eli candelo lifuna izicatshulwa ezongezelelweyo zokuqinisekisa. Nceda uncede ukuphucula eli nqaku ngokongeza izicatshulwa kwimithombo ethembekileyo kweli candelo. Izixhobo ezingasetyenziswanga zinokucelwa umngeni kwaye zisuswe. (Agasti 2024) (Funda indlela kwaye nini ukususa lo myalezo) 
Amathala eencwadi omntu kunye nawoluntu, oovimba kunye nezinye iindlela zokuqokelela iincwadi ziye zakhokelela ekudalweni kwemibutho emininzi eyahlukeneyo kunye nezicwangciso zokuhlela. Kwinkulungwane ye-19 neye-20, amathala eencwadi kunye neengcali zamathala eencwadi alungelelanise ukuqokelela iincwadi kunye neenkqubo zokuhlela ukuphendula kushishino olukhulayo. Eyona nkqubo isetyenziswa kakhulu yi-ISBN, ebonelele ngeempawu ezizodwa zeencwadi ukusukela ngo-1970. 

Amathala eencwadi 
Inqaku eliphambili: Ithala leencwadi

IThala leencwadi likaCelsus elise-Efese, eTurkey, lakhiwa ngo-135 AD, kwaye lalinokugcina imisongo emalunga ne-12,000. 
Ithala leencwadi yingqokelela yeencwadi, mhlawumbi nezinye izixhobo namajelo eendaba, anokufikelelwa ukuze asetyenziswe ngamalungu alo kunye namalungu amaziko amanyeneyo. Amathala eencwadi abonelela ngezinto eziphathekayo (iikopi ezingamaphepha) okanye zedijithali (iikopi ezithambileyo), kwaye inokuba yindawo ebonakalayo, indawo ebonakalayo, okanye zombini. Ingqokelela yethala leencwadi idla ngokubandakanya imathiriyeli eshicilelweyo enokubolekwa, kwaye ngokuqhelekileyo ikwabandakanya icandelo lereferensi yopapasho olunokusetyenziswa kuphela ngaphakathi kwizakhiwo. Izixhobo ezinjengokukhutshwa kweefilim, iinkqubo zikamabonakude, ezinye iividiyo ezirekhodiweyo, unomathotholo, umculo kunye noshicilelo lweaudio zinokufumaneka kwiifomathi ezininzi. Ezi ziquka iiDVD, iiBlu-rays, iiCD, iikhasethi, okanye ezinye iifomathi ezisebenzayo ezifana ne-microform. Basenokunikezela ngokufikelela kulwazi, umculo okanye omnye umxholo ogcinwe koovimba beenkcukacha zebhayibhilografi. 

Amathala eencwadi anokwahluka kakhulu ngobukhulu yaye anokulungiswa aze agcinwe liqumrhu likarhulumente elinjengorhulumente, iziko (elifana nesikolo okanye imyuziyam), iqumrhu, okanye umntu wabucala. Ukongeza ekuboneleleni ngemathiriyeli, amathala eencwadi akwabonelela ngeenkonzo zoonolayibrari abaqeqeshelwe ukufumana, ukukhetha, ukujikeleza nokulungelelanisa ulwazi ngelixa betolika iimfuno zolwazi kunye nokukhangela kunye nokuhlalutya izixa ezikhulu zolwazi ngezixhobo ezahlukeneyo. 

Izakhiwo zamathala eencwadi zidla ngokuba neendawo ezolileyo zokufundela, kwaneendawo eziqhelekileyo zokufundisisa neqela kunye nentsebenziswano, yaye zisenokubonelela ngeendawo zikawonke-wonke zokufikelela kwimithombo yazo ye-elektroniki, njengeekhompyutha nokufikelela kwi-Intanethi. 

Abathengi bethala leencwadi kunye neenkonzo ngokubanzi ezibonelelwayo ziyohluka ngokuxhomekeke kuhlobo lwayo: abasebenzisi bethala leencwadi loluntu banezidingo ezahlukileyo kwezo zethala leencwadi elikhethekileyo okanye ithala lemfundo, umzekelo. Amathala eencwadi asenokuba ziindawo zokuhlala, apho iinkqubo zenziwa zifumaneke kwaye abantu bazibandakanye kwimfundo yobomi bonke. Amathala eencwadi anamhlanje andisa iinkonzo zawo ngaphaya kweendonga ezibonakalayo zesakhiwo ngokubonelela ngemathiriyeli enokufikeleleka ngeendlela zombane, kuquka nasekhaya nge-Intanethi. 

Ukuchongwa kunye nokuhlelwa kwe 

-ISBN ngebhakhowudi
Ngo-2011, iManyano yaMazwe ngaMazwe yeMibutho yaMathala eeNcwadi kunye namaZiko (IFLA) yenza iNgcaciso yoMgangatho weBhayibhilografi yaMazwe ngaMazwe (ISBD) ukuze ilungelelanise iinkcazo kwiincwadi zeencwadi nakwiikhathalogu zamathala eencwadi. Incwadi nganye icaciswa yiNombolo yeNcwadi eMigangatho yaMazwe ngaMazwe, okanye i-ISBN, eyenzelwe ukuba yodwa kulo lonke uhlelo lwencwadi nganye eveliswa ngabapapashi abathatha inxaxheba, kwihlabathi jikelele. Ilawulwa yi-ISBN Society. I-ISBN ineenxalenye ezine: inxalenye yokuqala yikhowudi yelizwe, eyesibini ikhowudi yomshicileli, kunye neyesithathu ikhowudi yesihloko. Inxalenye yokugqibela yidijithi yokutshekisha, kwaye inokuthatha amaxabiso ukusuka ku-0–9 no-X (10). Iinombolo ze-EAN Barcodes zeencwadi zithathwe kwi-ISBN ngokufaka isimaphambili 978, kwi-Bookland, kunye nokubala idijithi yokutshekisha entsha. 

Abapapashi borhwebo kumazwe ahambele phambili kwezoshishino badla ngokunika ii-ISBNs ezincwadini zabo, ngoko ke abathengi banokucinga ukuba i-ISBN yinxalenye yenkqubo yamazwe ngamazwe iyonke, ngaphandle kwemikhethe. Nangona kunjalo, abapapashi bakarhulumente abaninzi, kumazwe amashishini kunye nasakhulayo, abathabathi nxaxheba ngokupheleleyo kwinkqubo ye-ISBN, kwaye bapapashe iincwadi ezingenazo ii-ISBN. Ingqokelela enkulu okanye yoluntu ifuna ikhathalogu. Iikhowudi ezibizwa ngokuba zii-"call numbers" zinxulumanisa iincwadi nekhathalogu, kwaye zimisele iindawo ezikuzo ezishelufini. Iinombolo zokufowuna zisekelwe kwinkqubo yokuhlelwa kweThala leeNcwadi. Inombolo yomnxeba ibekwe kumqolo wencwadi, ngokuqhelekileyo umgama omfutshane ngaphambi kwezantsi, nangaphakathi. Imigangatho yeziko okanye yesizwe, efana ne-ANSI/NISO Z39.41 – 1997, iseka indlela echanekileyo yokubeka ulwazi (njengesihloko, okanye igama lombhali) kwiincwadi ezijikelezayo, nakwizinto ezifana neencwadi “ezinoshelufa”, ezifana nezikhongozeli zeeDVD, iiteyiphu zevidiyo nesoftware. 


Iincwadi ezikwiishelufu zamathala eencwadi kunye neenombolo zokufowuna ezibonakala kwii- 
spines Enye inkqubo eyaziwa ngokubanzi yinkqubo yoHlelo lweThala leeNcwadi leCongress. Zombini ezi nkqubo zityekele kwizifundo ezazimelwe kakuhle kumathala eencwadi ase-US xa zaye zaphuhliswa, kwaye ngenxa yoko zineengxaki zokusingatha izifundo ezitsha, ezifana ne-computing, okanye izifundo ezinxulumene nezinye iinkcubeko.[49] Ulwazi malunga neencwadi kunye nababhali lunokugcinwa koovimba beenkcukacha ezifana noovimba beenkcukacha zeencwadi ezinomdla ngokubanzi kwi-intanethi. I-Metadata, ethetha "idatha malunga nedatha" lulwazi malunga nencwadi. Imethadatha malunga nencwadi inokubandakanya isihloko sayo, i-ISBN okanye enye inombolo yokuhlelwa (jonga ngasentla), amagama abaxhasi (umbhali, umhleli, umzobi) kunye nomshicileli, umhla kunye nobukhulu bayo, ulwimi lombhalo, umxholo wayo, njl.

Iinkqubo zokuhlela 
iBliss bibliographic classification (BC) 
Chinese Library Classification (CLC) 
Colon Classification 
Dewey Decimal Classification (DDC) 
iSkimu soHlelo olutsha lwamaThala eeNcwadi aseTshayina 
.
IThala leeNcwadi loHlelo lweNkongolo yeNkongolo (LCC) 
UHlelo lweDesimali oluqhelekileyo (UDC) 
ULondolozo 

Igcisa lolondolozo livavanya umsebenzi wobugcisa phantsi kwemakroskopu kwiMyuziyam yezoBugcisa yase-Indianapolis 
Ukugcinwa nokubuyiselwa kweencwadi, imibhalo-ngqangi, amaxwebhu, kunye ne-ephemera inikezelwe ekwandiseni ubomi bezinto zembali kunye nexabiso lobuqu elenziwe ngokuyintloko, ngesikhumba, ngesikhumba. Xa isetyenziswa kwilifa lenkcubeko, imisebenzi yolondolozo idla ngokuqhutywa ngumgcini. Eyona njongo iphambili yolondolozo kukwandisa ubomi bento kunye nokugcina ingqibelelo yayo ngokugcina zonke izongezo zibuyela umva. Ulondolozo lweencwadi kunye nephepha lubandakanya ubuchule bokudibanisa iincwadi, ukubuyisela, ukukhemikhali kwephepha, kunye nobunye ubugcisa bezinto eziphathekayo kuquka ugcino kunye nobuchule bokugcinwa koovimba.[50] 

Ugcino lwencwadi kunye nephepha lufuna ukuthintela kwaye, kwezinye iimeko, ukubuyisela umva umonakalo ngenxa yokuphatha, ubugwenxa bendalo, kunye nokusingqongileyo.[51][52] Abalondolozi bamisela iindlela ezifanelekileyo zokugcina iincwadi kunye namaxwebhu, kuquka iibhokisi kunye neshelufu ukuthintela umonakalo ongakumbi kunye nokukhuthaza ukugcinwa kwexesha elide.[53] Iindlela ezikhethwe ngononophelo kunye nobuchule bolondolozo olusebenzayo zinokubuyisela umva umonakalo kwaye zithintele umonakalo ongakumbi kwiibhetshi okanye unyango lwento enye esekelwe kwixabiso lencwadi okanye uxwebhu.[54] 

Ngokwembali, iindlela zokubuyisela iincwadi bezingekho ngokusesikweni kwaye ziqhutywa ziindima ezahlukeneyo kunye nemvelaphi yoqeqesho. Kule mihla, ukugcinwa kwamaxwebhu ephepha kunye neencwadi kaninzi kwenziwa ngumlondolozi oyingcali.[52][55] Abagcini bephepha okanye iincwadi ezininzi bangamalungu equmrhu leengcali, njengeAmerican Institute for Conservation (AIC) okanye iGuild of Bookworkers (zombini eUnited States), iArives and Records Association (eUnited Kingdom naseIreland), okanye iZiko loLondolozo (ICON) (eUnited Kingdom).[56] 

Imiba yezentlalo nenkcubeko 
Ulwamkelo 
Inqaku eliphambili: Ukugxekwa koncwadi 
Impembelelo yeencwadi inokuhluka, kwaye irekhodi yolwamkelo iza kwiifomathi ezininzi: ukuqala ngokwamkelwa koluntu okokuqala kumaphephandaba anamhlanje, inkcubeko yepop kunye nembalelwano, kwaye emva koko kuphuhliswe ngeendlela ezahlukeneyo zokugxekwa koncwadi ngabagxeki beengcali kunye nezemfundo. Kwishishini lokushicilela "uphononongo lwencwadi" yinxalenye ebalulekileyo yokwandisa ulwazi kunye nokwamkelwa kwencwadi: ekwaziyo ukwenza okanye ukwaphula uluvo loluntu malunga nencwadi entsha [icatshulwa] 

Uphononongo lwencwadi 
Eli candelo liyisicatshulwa kuphononongo lweNcwadi.[ hlela ] 
Uphononongo lwencwadi luhlobo lokugxekwa koncwadi apho incwadi ichazwa nje (uphononongo lwesishwankathelo) okanye ihlalutywe ngokusekelwe kumxholo, isimbo, kunye nesitayela, [5].

Uphononongo lwencwadi lunokuba ngumthombo ophambili, isicatshulwa soluvo, isishwankathelo sophononongo, okanye imbono yesifundiswa.[58] Iincwadi zinokujongwa kwakhona ukuze zishicilelwe kumaphepha-ndaba, amaphephancwadi namaphephandaba, njengomsebenzi wesikolo, okanye kwiiwebhusayithi zeencwadi kwi-Intanethi. Ubude bophononongo lwencwadi bunokwahluka ukusuka kumhlathi omnye ukuya kwisincoko esikhulu. Uhlolisiso olunjalo lunokuyihlolisisa le ncwadi ngokusekelwe kukhetho lobuqu. Ababuyekezi banokusebenzisa ithuba lophononongo lwencwadi kwisincoko esandisiweyo esinokuthi sisondelelene okanye sinxibelelene ngokusondeleyo nomxholo wencwadi, okanye ukwazisa izimvo zabo ngesihloko somsebenzi oyintsomi okanye ongeyonyani. 

Ezinye iijenali zinikezelwe kuphononongo lweencwadi, kwaye uphononongo lufakwe kwi-indexed database njenge-Book Review Index kunye noPhononongo lweKirkus; kodwa uphononongo lweencwadi ezininzi ngakumbi lunokufunyanwa kuluhlu lwedatha lwephephandaba kunye nolwezifundiswa olunjengoBugcisa noBuntu Citation Index, iSocial Sciences Citation Index, kunye noovimba beenkcukacha ezithe ngqo. 
Ukuhlolwa kweencwadi kunye nokuvalwa kweencwadi 
Ukuhlolwa kweencwadi sisenzo segunya elithile lithatha amanyathelo okucinezela iingcamango nolwazi olusencwadini.[59] Ulawulo "lulawulo lwentetho ekhululekileyo kunye nezinye iindlela zegunya elimiliselweyo".[60] Abahloli babona ngokuqhelekileyo njengomzali ochaphazelekayo, amalungu oluntu asabela kwisicatshulwa ngaphandle kokufunda, okanye imibutho yendawo okanye yesizwe.[61] Iincwadi ziye zahlolwa ngoozwilakhe abangoozwilakhe ukuze bavale umlomo abantu abaphikisayo, njengePeople's Republic of China, iJamani yamaNazi kunye neSoviet Union. Iincwadi zihlala zivavanyelwa ukufaneleka kweminyaka, ulwimi olukhubekisayo, umxholo wesondo, phakathi kwezinye izizathu.[62] Ngokufanayo, iinkolo zinokukhupha uluhlu lweencwadi ezivaliweyo, ezinjengomzekelo wembali we-Index yeCawa yamaKatolika, i-Librorum Prohibitorum kunye nokuvalwa kweencwadi ezifana nekaSalman Rushdie ethi The Satanic Verses ngu-Ayatollah Khomeini,[63] ezingasoloko ziphethe amandla asemthethweni. I-Censorship inokwenziwa kwinqanaba likazwelonke okanye le-subnational ngokunjalo, kwaye inokuthwala izohlwayo ezisemthethweni. Kwiimeko ezininzi, ababhali bezi ncwadi banokujamelana nezigwebo eziqatha, ukugxothwa kweli lizwe, okanye nokubulawa.[64][65] 

Ukutshiswa kwencwadi 
Eli candelo licatshulwe ekutshisweni kweNcwadi.[ hlela ] 

Ikopi yeNdlu yaMahlamvu iyatshiswa 
Ukutshiswa kwencwadi kukutshabalalisa ngabom ngomlilo weencwadi okanye ezinye izinto ezibhaliweyo, ezidla ngokuqhutywa kumxholo woluntu. Ukutshiswa kweencwadi kubonisa inkalo yokuvalwa kwaye ngokuqhelekileyo kuvela kwinkcaso yenkcubeko, yenkolo, okanye yezopolitiko kwizinto ekuthethwa ngazo.[66] Ukutshiswa kweencwadi kusenokuba sisenzo sokudelela okuqulethwe yincwadi okanye umbhali, okunenjongo yokutsalela ingqalelo yoluntu ngokubanzi kule nkcaso, okanye ukufihla inkcazelo equlethwe kwisicatshulwa ukuba ibhengezwe esidlangalaleni, njengeedayari okanye iileja. Ukutshisa kunye nezinye iindlela zokutshatyalaliswa kunye zaziwa ngokuba yi-biblioclasm okanye i-libricide.

Kwezinye iimeko, imisebenzi etshatyalalisiwe ayinakuphinda ibuyiselwe kwaye ukutshiswa kwayo kwenza ilahleko enkulu kwilifa lenkcubeko. Imizekelo ibandakanya ukutshiswa kweencwadi kunye nokungcwatywa kwabaphengululi phantsi kobukhosi baseTshayina baseQin (213-210 BCE), ukutshatyalaliswa kweNdlu yoBulumko ngexesha lokungqingwa kweMongol yaseBaghdad (1258), ukutshatyalaliswa kweekhowudi ze-Aztec ngu-Itzcoatl (1430s), ukutshiswa kwee-Maya codices 5 kunye ne-Landang 6 Diego kwi-Landang 6 de Diego (6) Jaffna Public Library e Sri Lanka (1981).[68] 

Kwezinye iimeko, ezinjengokutshiswa kweencwadi zamaNazi, imibhalo yeencwadi ezitshatyalalisiweyo iyasinda, kodwa ukutshiswa kweencwadi kuba ngumfuziselo wolawulo olungqwabalala nolucinezelayo olufuna ukuvalela okanye ukuvala inkalo ethile yenkcubeko ekhoyo.



"Imibhalo" kunye "Bhala" ziqondise kwakhona apha. Kwicandelo leBhayibhile yesiHebhere, bona iiKetuvim. Ngolunye usetyenziso, jonga Bhala (disambiguation). 

Ilitye laseRosetta (196 BC) libhala ngemibhalo emithathu eyahlukeneyo. IiHieroglyphs (phezulu) kunye neDemotic (ephakathi) zirekhoda umbhalo ofanayo ngolwimi lwaseYiputa, ngelixa isicatshulwa esilinganayo kwisiGrike sisebenzisa ialfabhethi yesiGrike (ezantsi). Ezi mbalelwano zazingundoqo ekuqondweni kwe-hieroglyphs yaseYiputa ekuqaleni kwenkulungwane ye-19. 
Ukubhala sisenzo sokudala umelo oluzingileyo lolwimi. Inkqubo yokubhala iquka iisimboli ezithile ezibizwa ngokuba yiscript, kunye nemithetho ebethelela ngayo ulwimi oluthile oluthethwayo. Lonke ulwimi olubhaliweyo luvela kulwimi oluthethwayo oluhambelanayo; lo gama ukusetyenziswa kolwimi kuxhaphakile kuluntu lonke, uninzi lweelwimi ezithethwayo azibhalwanga.[1] 

Ukubhala ngumsebenzi wokuqonda kunye noluntu olubandakanya iinkqubo ze-neuropsychological and physical. Isiphumo salo msebenzi, okukwabizwa ngokuba kukubhala (okanye isicatshulwa) luludwe lweesimboli ezibhalwe ngokwasemzimbeni, ezidluliselwe ngoomatshini, okanye ezimelwe ngokwamanani. Ukufunda yinkqubo ehambelanayo yokutolika isicatshulwa esibhaliweyo, kunye netoliki ekubhekiselwa kuyo njengomfundi.[2] 

Ngokubanzi, iisistim zokubhala azenzi iilwimi kuzo kwaye ngokwazo, kodwa ziyindlela yokukhowuda ulwimi ukuze lufundwe ngabanye ngexesha nakwindawo.[3][4] Ngelixa ingezizo zonke iilwimi ezisebenzisa inkqubo yokubhala, ezo zisebenzisayo zinokuncedisana kwaye zandise amandla olwimi oluthethwayo ngokudala iindlela ezomeleleyo zolwimi ezinokuthi zigqithiswe kwindawo yonke (umz. imbalelwano ebhaliweyo) kwaye zigcinwe ngokuhamba kwexesha (umz. amathala eencwadi).[5] Ukubhala kusenokuchaphazela ulwazi olufunyanwa ngabantu, njengoko kuvumela abantu ukuba bakhuphe iingcinga zabo ngeendlela ekulula ukucinga ngazo, ukucacisa, ukuphinda kuqwalaselwe, kunye nokuzihlaziya.[6][7][8] 

Izixhobo, izixhobo, kunye nenkuthazo yokubhala 
Nawuphi na umzekelo wokubhala ubandakanya intsebenziswano entsonkothileyo phakathi kwezixhobo ezikhoyo, iinjongo, amasiko enkcubeko, iindlela zokuqonda, iintlobo, ulwazi olufihlakeleyo kunye nolwazi olucacileyo, kunye nemiqobo kunye nokunciphisa iinkqubo ezisetyenziswayo.[9] Izixhobo zokubhala ezisetyenziselwa ukwenza imibhalo ebonakalayo ziquka iminwe, izitayile, iibhrashi ze-inki, iipensile, iipeni, kunye neendlela ezininzi zokubhala; iindawo zokubhala ekunokwenzelwa kuzo imibhalo ziquka amacwecwe amatye, amacwecwe odongwe, iziliphu zoqalo, ipapyrus, amacwecwe ewax, ivellum, isikhumba, iphepha, icwecwe lobhedu nesileyiti.[10] 

Umatshini wokuchwetheza, kunye nomqhubekekisi wamagama wedijithali, uvumela ababhali ngabanye ukuba bavelise isicatshulwa esibonakalayo esingaguqukiyo ngoomatshini besebenzisa ikhibhodi.[11]

Ukuqhubela phambili ekusetyenzweni kolwimi lwendalo kunye nokuveliswa kolwimi lwendalo kubangele isoftware ekwaziyo ukuvelisa iindlela ezithile zokubhala ngendlela emiselweyo (umz. uqikelelo lwemozulu kunye nengxelo yezemidlalo) ngaphandle kokubandakanyeka ngokuthe ngqo kwabantu[12] emva koqwalaselo lokuqala okanye, ngokuqhelekileyo, ukuba isetyenziselwe ukuxhasa iinkqubo zokubhala ezifana nokuvelisa uyilo lokuqala, ukuvelisa ingxelo ngoncedo lwerubrikhi, ukukopisha3, ukukopisha-3, ukuguqulela, nokuncedisa[12]. 

Iimpembelelo kunye neenjongo 

I-Bronze tympanum ebonisa umntu wokuBhala - uThomas Jefferson Building, eWashington, DC 
Ngokwembali, ukubhala kuye kwavela ukulungisa iimfuno zoluntu olukhula kubunzima bezoqoqosho nentlalontle. Zakuba ziphuhlisiwe, izicelo ezinokubakho zibandakanya ukulandelela imveliso kunye nobunye ubutyebi, imbali yokurekhoda, ukugcinwa kwenkcubeko, ukudibanisa ulwazi ngekharityhulam kunye noluhlu lweetekisi ekucingelwa ukuba ziqulethe ulwazi olusisiseko (umz. ICanon of Medicine) okanye ixabiso lobugcisa (umzkl i-canon yoncwadi). Uncedo kulawulo lwaluquka iikhowudi zomthetho, iingxelo zokubalwa kwabantu, izivumelwano, amaxwebhu obunini, irhafu, izivumelwano zorhwebo nezivumelwano. Njengoko uCharles Bazerman echaza, "ukumakishwa kwemiqondiso ematyeni, udongwe, ephepheni, kwaye ngoku iinkumbulo zedijithali-nganye iphathekayo kwaye ihamba ngokukhawuleza kuneyangaphambili-ibonelele ngeendlela zokulungelelaniswa kunye nokwandisa isenzo kunye nememori kumaqela amakhulu abantu ngexesha kunye nendawo." uphando lwezenzululwazi kunye nolawulo lolwazi, zonke ezo bezixhomekeke ubukhulu becala kwiindlela eziphathwayo nezifumaneka ngokulula zolwimi olubhaliweyo. Imbali yokubhala ibanzi ngokuhambelana nokusetyenziswa kokubhala kunye nokucaciswa kweenkqubo zokwenziwa komsebenzi ezithi zibangele nokujikelezisa ukubhala.[15] 

Iimpembelelo zomntu ngamnye zokubhala ziquka ukukwazi ukusebenza ngaphaya kwemida yenkumbulo kabani[16] (umz. uluhlu lwezinto eziza kwenziwa, iiresiphi, izikhumbuzo, iincwadi zokubhalela, iimephu, izalathiso zemisebenzi entsokothileyo okanye izithethe), ukusasazwa kwezimvo kunye nolungelelwaniso (umz. izincoko, iimonographs, ibroadsides, izicwangciso, izibongozo, ezinye iimanifestos kunye nentlalontle), uthungelwano, [17] imbalelwano yoshishino malunga nempahla kunye neenkonzo, kunye nokubhala ubomi (umzekelo, idayari okanye ijenali).[18]

Ukusasazeka kweenkqubo zonxibelelwano lwedijithali ezifana ne-imeyile kunye namajelo eendaba ezentlalo zenze ukuba ukubhala kube yinto ebaluleke ngakumbi yobomi bemihla ngemihla, apho ezi nkqubo zixubana nobuchwepheshe obudala obufana nephepha, iipensile, iibhodi ezimhlophe, abashicileli kunye nabakhupheli. Izixa ezikhulu zokubhalwa kwemihla ngemihla ziphawulwa kwiindawo ezininzi zokusebenza kumazwe ahambele phambili kwezoqoqosho.[20] Kwimisebenzi emininzi (umzekelo, umthetho, ucwangciso-mali, uyilo lwesoftware, izibonelelo zabasebenzi), amaxwebhu abhaliweyo ayingowona mbandela uphambili kuphela ohanjiswayo kodwa ikwayindlela yomsebenzi ngokwawo.[21] Nakwimisebenzi engahambelani nokubhala, ulawulo lweerekhodi lunabasebenzi abaninzi ababhalayo ngamanye amaxesha.[22] 

Usetyenziso lwangoku 
Ezinye iiprofessional zidla ngokunxulunyaniswa nokubhala, njengababhali boncwadi, iintatheli, nababhali bobugcisa, kodwa ukubhala kuxhaphakile kwiindlela zale mihla zomsebenzi, ukuthatha inxaxheba koluntu, ulawulo lwendlu, kunye nemisebenzi yolonwabo.[23] 

Ishishini nezemali 
Jonga kwakhona: Ukubhala kobuNgcali kunye nonxibelelwano lobuNgcali 
Ukubhala kugxuphuleka kurhwebo lwemihla ngemihla. Umzekelo, emva kwemini, umthengisi unokufumana umbuzo obhaliweyo malunga nokufumaneka komgca wemveliso, emva koko anxibelelane nababoneleli kunye nabenzi bezinto ezenziwe ngee-odolo zomsebenzi kunye nezivumelwano zokuthenga, banxibelelane nge-imeyile ukuze baqinisekise ukufumaneka kokuthumela ngenqanawa kunye nenkampani yedrayage, bhala i-invoyisi, kwaye ucele ubungqina berisithi ngohlobo lwesiginitsha ebhaliweyo. Ngomlinganiselo omkhulu, iinkqubo zale mihla zezimali, iibhanki nezoshishino zixhomekeke kumaxwebhu abhaliweyo—kuquka imimiselo, imigaqo-nkqubo nemigaqo; ukuyilwa kweengxelo kunye namanye amaxwebhu okubeka iliso ukuze kwenziwe, kuvavanywe, kunye nokubonelela ngokuphendula ngezigqibo nemisebenzi; ukwenziwa nokugcinwa kweerekhodi; unxibelelwano olubhaliweyo lwangaphakathi kumasebe ukulungelelanisa umsebenzi; unxibelelwano olubhaliweyo oluquka iimveliso zomsebenzi ezinikezelwa kwamanye amasebe kunye nabathengi; kunye nonxibelelwano lwangaphandle kubaxumi kunye noluntu.[24] [iphepha elifunekayo] [25] [iphepha elifunekayo] Imibutho yoshishino neyemali nayo ixhomekeke kumaxwebhu amaninzi asemthethweni abhaliweyo, afana nezivumelwano, iingxelo eziya kumaziko karhulumente, iirekhodi zerhafu, kunye neengxelo zokubala. Amaziko emali kunye neemarike ezibamba, ezithumelayo, ezirhwebayo, ze-inshurensi, okanye ezilawula ukugcinwa kwabathengi okanye amanye amaziko axhomekeke ngokukodwa kwiirekhodi ezibhaliweyo (nangona ngoku zihlala zikwimo yedijithali) ukugcina ingqibelelo yeendima zabo.[27][iphepha elifunekayo]
 
kuLawulo nomthetho.
Iinkqubo ezininzi zanamhlanje zoorhulumente zilungelelaniswe zize zingcwaliswe ngemigaqo-siseko ebhaliweyo kumanqanaba kazwelonke yaye maxa wambi karhulumente okanye eminye intlangano. Imithetho nemigaqo ebhaliweyo idla ngokukhokela amasebe, amasebe, namanye amaqumrhu karhulumente, asoloko evelisa iingxelo namanye amaxwebhu njengemveliso aze aphendule ngezenzo zawo. Ukongeza kwizindlu zowiso-mthetho eziqulunqa kwaye zipasise imithetho, le mithetho ilawulwa lisebe lesigqeba, elinokuthi linike eminye imimiselo ebhaliweyo echaza imithetho kunye nendlela eqhutywa ngayo.[28] Oorhulumente kumanqanaba ahlukeneyo nabo bagcina iirekhodi ezibhaliweyo kubemi malunga nezazisi, iziganeko zobomi ezifana nokuzalwa, ukufa, imitshato, kunye noqhawulo-mtshato, ukunikezelwa kweelayisensi zemisebenzi elawulwayo, iintlawulo zolwaphulo-mthetho, ulwaphulo-mthetho lwendlela, kunye nezinye izohlwayo ezincinci nezinkulu, kunye noxanduva lwerhafu kunye neentlawulo.[29] 

Inzululwazi kunye nophando lwezifundo 
Uphando olwenziwe kwiinkalo zemfundo ludla ngokupapashwa njengamanqaku kwiijenali okanye kwiimonographs zobude bencwadi. Iingxoxo, iimvavanyo, idatha yokujonga, kunye nobunye ubungqina obuhlanganisiweyo ngexesha lophando bumelwe ngokubhaliweyo, kwaye busebenza njengesiseko somsebenzi kamva. Ukuqokelelwa kwedatha kunye nokuqulunqwa kwemibhalo-ngqangi kunokuxhaswa ngezibonelelo, ezihlala zifuna izindululo ezimisela ixabiso lalo msebenzi kunye nesidingo senkxaso-mali.[30] Idatha kunye neenkqubo ngokuqhelekileyo ziqokelelwa kwiincwadi zamanqaku zaselebhu okanye ezinye iifayile zokuqala. [31] [iphepha elifunekayo] Imibhalo engaphambili yempapasho enokubakho inokuthi inikezelwe kwiinkomfa zezemfundo okanye zoluleko okanye kwiiseva zewebhu ezifikeleleke esidlangalaleni ukufumana ingxelo yoontanga kunye nokwakha umdla kumsebenzi. Ngaphambi kokupapashwa ngokusemthethweni, la maxwebhu ngokuqhelekileyo afundwa kwaye avavanywe ngokuphononongwa koontanga kwiingcali ezifanelekileyo, ezigqiba ukuba umsebenzi unexabiso elaneleyo kunye nomgangatho oza kupapashwa.[32] 

Upapasho aluqinisekisi amabango okanye iziphumo zomsebenzi njengenyaniso egunyazisiweyo, kuphela nje ukuba zifanele ukuhoywa zezinye iingcali. Njengoko umsebenzi uvela kumanqaku ophononongo, iincwadi zezandla, iincwadi zezifundo, okanye ezinye iiaggregations, kunye nabanye bewucaphula ekuqhubeleni phambili uphando lwabo, ngaba ulungelelaniswa njengolwazi oluthembekileyo oluhlala luhleli.[33] 

Ubuntatheli
Iindaba kunye neengxelo zeendaba zingundoqo ekubandakanyekeni kwabemi kunye nolwazi lwamacandelo amaninzi omsebenzi abantu abanokuba nomdla malunga nobume boluntu lwabo, kubandakanywa izenzo kunye nokunyaniseka koorhulumente babo kunye namagosa karhulumente, iimeko zezoqoqosho, iintlekele zendalo kunye neempendulo kubo, iziganeko ze-geopolitical ngamazwe, kuquka iingxabano, kodwa kunye nezemidlalo, ukuzonwabisa, iincwadi kunye nezinye izinto zokuzonwabisa. Ngelixa iindaba kunye namaphephandaba ziye zanda ngokukhawuleza ukusuka kwinkulungwane yeshumi elinesibhozo ukuya kweyamashumi amabini, uqoqosho oluguqukayo kunye nokukwazi ukuvelisa nokusasaza iindaba kuzise imingeni enzima nekhawulezayo kubuntatheli kunye nombutho osisiphumo solwazi lommi kunye nokuzibandakanya. 

Imfundo namaziko emfundo 
Imfundo esesikweni yimeko yezentlalo enxulunyaniswa kakhulu nokufunda kokubhala, kwaye abafundi basenokuqhuba le mibutho kwakudala bephumile esikolweni.[37] Ecaleni kokubhala okufundiweyo ngabafundi (kwiintlobo zeencwadi zezifundo, iincwadi ezimiselweyo, nezinye izinto zokufundisa kwakunye neencwadi abazikhethele ngokwabo) abafundi babhala kakhulu ngaphakathi ezikolweni kuwo onke amanqanaba, kwiimviwo zezifundo, kwizincoko, ekubhaleni amanqaku, ekwenzeni umsebenzi wesikolo wasekhaya, nakwiimvavanyo ezakhayo nezishwankathelayo. Okunye koku kujoliswe ngokuthe ngqo ekufundweni kokubhala, kodwa okuninzi kugxilwe ngakumbi ekufundeni isifundo.[38][39] 

Iinkqubo zokubhala 
Iisistim zokubhala zingahlelwa ngokubanzi ngokweeyunithi zolwimi ezimelwe ngokubanzi ziisimboli zalo:[40][41] 

Iifonografi zimele izandi zentetho – ezinoonobumba kunye nezilabhari zisebenzisa iisimboli kwiifowuni kunye namalungu ngokulandelelana kwawo. 
Iilogografi zimela iiyunithi zentsingiselo yolwimi (amagama okanye iimofim), nangona zisanxulunyaniswa ngabafundi nendlela yokubiza amagama kulwimi oluthethwayo oluhambelanayo. 
Iilogographies 

Uthelekiso lwendaleko ukusuka kwiipictograms ukuya kwiimilo zabalinganiswa abangabonakaliyo, kwi-cuneiform yaseMesopotamiya, i-hieroglyphs yaseYiputa kunye noonobumba baseTshayina 
. Iilogogram ezininzi zinezakhiwo zangaphakathi, ezinamacandelwana anokumela zombini ifonografi kunye ne-ideographic (umzekelo, ii-radicals zamaTshayina, i-hieroglyphic determinatives) imiba yemofim.[42] 

Eyona nkqubo iphambili yelogographic esetyenziswayo ngoonobumba baseTshayina, abasetyenziselwa ukubhala iilwimi zesiTshayina kunye nesiJapan, kwaye ngokwembali abanye abavela kwimimandla ephenjelelwa yinkcubeko yamaTshayina, njengesiKorea nesiVietnam. Ezinye iinkqubo zelogographic zibandakanya umbhalo otsobhileyo nowamaMaya.[43] 

Ii-syllabaries
Isilabhari yiseti yeesimboli ezibhaliweyo ezimele amalungu,[40] ngokwesiqhelo iconsonanti elandelwa sisikhamiso, okanye isikhamiso sodwa. Kwezinye izikripti amalungu antsokothileyo ngakumbi (umz. i-consonant-vowel-consonant okanye i-consonant-consonant-vowels) anokuba neeglyphs ezikhethekileyo. Iisilabhi ezifanayo ngefonetiki azibhalwanga ngokufanayo.[40] 

Iisilabhari zezona zilungele iilwimi ezinokwakheka kwamalungu alula, njengesiJapani. Ezinye izikripthi zesilabhiki ziquka Umgca B kunye neCherokee syllabary.[44] 

Iialfabhethi 
Ialfabhethi yisethi yeempawu ezibhaliweyo ezimele iiconsonants kunye nezikhamiso.[40] IiAlfabhethi 

zeAbjads 
ezinamagama kuphela eekhonsoni zibizwa ngokuba zii-abjads okanye iiconsonantari; nangona kunyanzelekile, ii-abjads zinokusebenzisa amanqaku okuchaza amagama ukucacisa ukuba zeziphi na izikhamiso ezilandela ikhonsonanti nganye. Iialfabhethi zakuqala yayizii-abjad, eziphenjelelwa ziisimboli ezimele oonobumba abathile abasuka kwi-hieroglyphs yaseYiputa. Uninzi lwee-abjads ngokunjalo luyinzalelwane yakuMbindi Mpuma, lubonisa ukuguquguquka okulinganiselweyo kwezikhamiso kwimopholoji yeelwimi zamaSemite ezithethwa kulo mmandla.[40] 

U-Abugidas 
Kuninzi lweealfabhethi zase-Indiya kunye ne-Asia-mpuma ye-Asia, izikhamiso zibonakaliswa ngokusebenzisa iimpawu ze-diacritics okanye ukuguqulwa kwemilo ye-consonant. Ezi zibizwa ngokuba zii-abugidas okanye ii-alphasyllabaries.[40] Igama elithi abugida lithatyathwe kumagama oonobumba bokuqala bombhalo weGeʽez, enye i<em>abugida edumileyo eyasetyenziswa ekubhaleni iilwimi ezininzi e-Ethiopia nase-Eritrea.[45] 

Imbali kunye nemvelaphi 
Inqaku eliphambili: Imbali yokubhala 
Ukubhala kuqala kwavela kwi-Early Bronze Age ukuhlangabezana neemfuno zezoqoqosho ezikhulayo zesixeko saseSumeria, esikumazantsi eMesopotamiya. Ngeli xesha, ubunzima borhwebo kunye nolawulo lugqithise amandla ememori, kunye ne-cuneiform yaseSumeri esebenza njengendlela ethembekileyo yokurekhoda iintengiselwano, ukugcina ii-akhawunti zemali, kunye nokugcina iirekhodi zembali, phakathi kwemisebenzi efanayo. [46] 

I-Cuneiform, esetyenziselwa ukubhala ulwimi lwaseSumeri, yalandelwa ngokukhawuleza yi-hieroglyphs yaseYiputa, kunye nokuvela kwiinkqubo zokubhala phakathi kwe-3400 kunye ne-3100 BC, kunye nemibhalo yokuqala ehambelanayo ukusuka c. 2600 BC.[47] I-Indus script (c. 2600 - c. 2000 BC), efunyenwe kwiintlobo ezahlukeneyo zezinto zobugcisa eziveliswe yi-Indus Valley Civilization kwi-Indian subcontinent, ihlala ingachazwanga, kwaye ingaba isebenze njengokubhalwa kwenyani akuvunyelwanga ngayo.[48] Nangona imvelaphi yayo ayibonakali ngokucacileyo, ithuba lokusasazwa kwenkcubeko yaseMesopotamiya ukuba liqalise ingcamango yokubhala kubantu base-Indus licacile.[49] Imvulophu 

yeMesopotamia 

yeGlobular eneqela leethokheni zeakhawunti, ixesha lase-Uruk, lisuka eSusa - Louvre Museum
Ngeminyaka yoo-1970, i-archaeologist uDenise Schmandt-Besserat ubonise ithiyori yokuseka ikhonkco phakathi kwe-cuneiform kunye "neempawu" zodongwe ezingahlelwanga ngaphambili, eyona midala ifunyenwe kwingingqi yaseZagros eIran. Malunga ne-8000 BC, abantu baseMesopotamiya baqala ukusebenzisa iithokheni zodongwe ukubala iimpahla zabo zezolimo nezemveliso. Kamva baqalisa ukubeka ezi mpawu ngaphakathi kwezingxobo zodongwe ezinkulu nezingenamgongxo (i-bulla, okanye iimvulophu zeglobula) ezazithi emva koko zitywinwe. Ubuninzi beempawu kwisikhongozeli ngasinye bubonakaliswe ngokuchukumisa, kumphezulu wesikhongozeli, umfanekiso omnye kumzekelo ngamnye wophawu ngaphakathi. Ngokulandelayo basasaza amathokheni, bexhomekeke kuphela kwiisimboli zeempawu, ezotywe kwindawo yodongwe. Ukuphepha ukwenza umfanekiso kumzekelo ngamnye wento efanayo (umzekelo: 100 imifanekiso yomnqwazi ukumela 100 iminqwazi), babala izinto ngokusebenzisa amanqaku amancinci ezahlukeneyo.[50] 

Cuneiform (elisuka kwisiLatin cunius, lit. 'wedge') kwavela c. I-3200 BC kumxholo wale teknoloji yokugcina iiakhawunti. Ekupheleni kwe 4th millennium BC,[51] abantu baseMesopotamiya babesebenzisa usiba olumilise unxantathu olucinezelwe kudongwe oluthambileyo ukurekhoda amanani. Le nkqubo yongezwa ngokuthe ngcembe kusetyenziswa usiba olubukhali ukubonisa oko kubalwa ngeefoto zemifanekiso. Izimbo zokubhala ezingqukuva nezibukhali zathatyathelwa indawo ngezitayile ezimile okwe wedge, ekuqaleni iilogograms ezirekhodwayo kuphela – ezineezakhi zefonetiki ezaziswa ngenkulungwane yama-29 BC ukumela amalungu eSumeri, okubangele inkqubo yokubhala ngenjongo ngokubanzi. [52][53] 

Ukusukela kwinkulungwane yama-26 BC, oonobumba abatsobhileyo baguqulelwa ukuba babhale ulwimi lwase-Akkadian lwamaSemite aseMpuma (iAsiriya neBhabhiloni) eyayisasazeke kuwo wonke amazantsi eMesopotamiya – emva koko yaya kwezinye ezifana namaElam, Hattian, Hurrian kunye namaHeti. Izibhalo ezifanayo ngenkangeleko yale nkqubo yokubhala ziquka ezo zeUgarit nesiPersi Sakudala. Ngokwamkelwa kolwimi lwesiAramiki njengelingua franca yoBukhosi baseNeo-Asiriya (911–609 BC), isiAramaic esiDala satshintshwa saguqulelwa kwisiMesopotamian cuneiform. Imibhalo yamva nje ebhalwe ngoonobumba abatsobhileyo yesiAkkadian efunyenwe ukuza kuthi ga ngoku isuka kwinkulungwane yoku-1 yeXesha Eliqhelekileyo. [54] 

EYiphutha
 
IPalethi yeNarmer, ebonisa iiserpopards ezimbini ezoyikekayo ezimele umanyano lweYiputa ePhezulu nesezantsi, c. Ngowama-3100 BC
Iihieroglyphs zakudala ezaziwayo (ukusuka kwisiGrike, lit. 'umbhalo ongcwele') zielebhile zodongwe zomlawuli we-Predynastic "Scorpion I", yabhalwa c. ngenkulungwane yama-33 BC kwaye wachacha e-Abydos (i-Umm el-Qa'ab yanamhlanje) – okanye ngenye indlela iNarmer Palette, yango c. 3100 BC.[55] Umbhalo wehieroglyphic wawuyilogographic, kunye nezihlomelo zefonetiki eziquka ialfabhethi esebenzayo. Esona sivakalisi sidala sicatshuliweyo singqinwa kwitywina elivela kwingcwaba likaSete-Peribsen eAbydos, eliqala kuLawulo lwesiBini (28th okanye 27th century BC). Malunga ne-800 hieroglyphs yasetyenziswa ngexesha elidala, eliphakathi, nelitsha loBukumkani (2686-1077 BC); ngexesha Greco-Roman (30 BC - 642 AD), ngaphezu 5,000 ezahlukeneyo glyphs zingqinwe.[56] 
Iinkqubo zeAegean

Ukubhala kwakubalulekile ekugcineni ubukhosi baseYiputa, kwaye ukufunda nokubhala kwinkqubo enzima yokubhalwa kwemibhalo kwakugxininiswe phakathi kwababhali abafundileyo abafundileyo ababekhonza itempile, uFaro, kunye namagunya omkhosi.[57] 

I-Mesoamerica 
Yemibhalo emininzi yangaphambi kwe-Columbian e-Mesoamerica, eyona nto ibonakala ngathi iphuhliswe kakhulu, kwaye ekuphela kwayo ekufuneka iqondwe, siscript sesiMaya. Umbhalo wokuqala owachongwa njengeMaya usukela kwinkulungwane yesi-3 BC.[58] Ubhalo lwesiMaya lusetyenziswa malunga nama-800 eesimboli ezahlukeneyo – ubukhulu becala iilogograms, ezincediswa yiseti yeesilabhogramu ezisetyenziswa kwizihlomelo, ukungavisisani phakathi kofundo olwahlukileyo lwelogogram, okanye ukutshintshwa kweelogo ezithile ngokupheleleyo.[59] 

ETshayina 
Ulwazi Oluthe vetshe: I-Oracle bone script kunye nemibhalo yobhedu yaseTshayina 
Imizekelo yokuqala ekhoyo yokubhala eTshayina - imibhalo kumathambo e-oracle, ngokuqhelekileyo iiplastrons ze-tortoise kunye ne-ox scapulae ezazisetyenziselwa ukuvumisa - umhla ukusuka c. 1200 BC, ngexesha Late Shang. Inani elincinane lemibhalo yobhedu eyabhalwa kwangelo xesha linye nayo iye yasinda.[60] 

Imibhalo ye-Elamite 
Umbhalo weProto-Elamite, osetyenziswayo c. 3200 - c. 2900 BC, ingqinwa kumacwecwe odongwe afunyanwa kwiindawo ezahlukeneyo kwi-Iran yale mihla, uninzi lwembiwa eSusa, isixeko sakudala esisempuma yeTigris.[61] Umbhalo kucingelwa ukuba ngokuyinxenye logographic, ukuba ziphuhliswe ukusuka cuneiform ekuqaleni, kwaye baye basebenzisa ngaphezu 1,000 imiqondiso - nangona imibhalo yayo "ibe, kwaye iya kuhlala, ingxaki kakhulu kwingxoxo yokubhala ngenxa yokuba bamele ixesha elingacacanga kakhulu lokufunda nokubhala".[62] 

Umbhalo woonobumba abatsobhileyo wamaElam, owasetyenziswa c. 2500 - 331 BC, yatshintshwa ukusuka kwi-cuneiform njengoko yayisetyenziselwa ukubhala isiAkkadian. Kuyo nayiphi na indawo ngeli xesha, i-Elamite cuneiform isetyenziswe malunga neesimboli ezili-130 - kunye netotali engama-206 esetyenzisiweyo kubomi bayo bonke, ngaphantsi kakhulu kunezinye iincwadi ezibhalwe ngoonobumba abatsobhileyo.[40] 

Ngaphambi kokuveliswa kwealfabhethi yesiGrike ngexesha le-Iron Age, i-hieroglyphs yaseCretan ingqinwa kwi-artefacts evela eKrete ngexesha lokuqala ukuya embindini we-2 leminyaka ye-BC. I-Linear B, inkqubo yokubhala yamaGrike aseMycenaean, yasetyenziswa eKnossos eKrete kunye nakwilizwe lamaGrike c. 1450−1200 BC.[63] Umgca A, osaza kuqondwa, wawusetyenziswa kwiZiqithi zeAegean nakwilizwekazi c. 1800–1450 BC.[64] 

Uphuhliso lwealfabhethi 
Inqaku eliphambili: Imbali yealfabhethi
Ialfabhethi yaziwa kuphela ukuba yaqanjwa kanye kwimbali yoluntu, luluntu lwabasebenzi basemgodini baseKanan kwiSinayi Peninsula c. 1800 BC ukubhala iilwimi zamaSemite West, [65] "kwimeko yokutshintshiselana ngenkcubeko phakathi kwabantu abathetha Semitic ukusuka Levant kunye noluntu eYiputa".[66] Le fomu yokuqala engqiniweyo yaziwa ngokuba yiProto-Sinaitic script, kwaye ilungelelanise iikhonsepthi kunye nobuncinci ezinye zeeleta ezibhaliweyo ezivela kwi-hieroglyphic yaseYiputa; yamkela ngokupheleleyo amaxabiso esandi saseNtshona Semitic kwiileta zayo, ngokuchaseneyo nokulungelelanisa esele ikho yaseYiputa.[67] Umhla ochanekileyo wemvelaphi yayo, kunye nemvelaphi yomzobo yeeleta ezininzi (ukuba zikhona) zihlala zingacacanga, kwaye umbhalo uhlala ungachazwanga.[68] Malunga nemibhalo engama-30 ekrwada ifunyenwe kwindawo yemigodi yase-Egypt enentaba eyaziwa ngokuba yiSerabit el-Khadem, eneempawu ezimele izandi zoonobumba omnye kunamagama apheleleyo okanye iikhonsepthi - isiseko senkqubo yealfabhethi. Kwada kwaba phakathi kwenkulungwane ye-12 neye-9 BC apho ukusetyenziswa kwealfabhethi kwanda kakhulu.[65] 

Ialfabhethi yamaFenike (c. 1050 BC) yinzala ethe ngqo yeProto-Sinaitic. I-Proto-Sinaitic kunye neFenike yayizi-abjads ezazinoonobumba kuphela abamele izandi zoonobumba; IsiFenike ekugqibeleni yaguqulelwa kwialfabhethi yesiGrike (c. 800 BC), eyokuqala ukumela izandi zezikhamiso, nto leyo eyenze ngokuphinda isetyenziswe imiqondiso engasetyenziswayo yoonobumba baseFenike.[69] Ialfabhethi yeCumae, imo eyahlukileyo yealfabhethi yokuqala yesiGrike, yavelisa ialfabhethi yeEtruscan kunye nenzala yayo, efana nealfabhethi yesiLatini.[70] Eminye inzala yoonobumba besiGrike iquka isiCyrillic, esisetyenziselwa ukubhala iilwimi ezinjengesiBulgaria nesiRashiya.[71] Ialfabhethi yamaFenike yaphinda yaguqulelwa kwiscript sesiAramaic, apho iWest Asian Square yesiHebhere, isiArabhu, [72] kunye nemibhalo yaseBrahmic yaseMzantsi Asia yehla.[73] 

Imibhalo yezenkolo 
Kwimbali yokubhala, imibhalo yenkolo okanye ukubhala kuye kwadlala indima ekhethekileyo. Umzekelo, ukuhlanganiswa kwemibhalo yenkolo ibiyenye yemibhalo yokuqala edumileyo, okanye ekuphela kwemibhalo ebhaliweyo kwezinye iilwimi, kwaye kwezinye iimeko zisadume kakhulu kwihlabathi liphela 



. 

Eli nqaku linemiba emininzi. Nceda uncede ukuyiphucula okanye uxoxe ngale miba kwiphepha lentetho. (Funda ukuba ungayisusa njani kwaye nini le miyalezo) 
Eli nqaku lifuna ucaphulo olongezelelweyo lokuqinisekisa. (Okthobha 2017)
Ithoni yeli nqaku okanye isimbo sisenokungabonakalisi ithowuni yeencyclopedic esetyenziswe kwiWikipedia. (Okthobha 2022) 
Kwintetho engokwasemthethweni, umbhali ngumyili wencwadi yantlandlolo epapashiweyo, enoba loo ncwadi ibhalwe, inemifanekiso, ibonwa okanye irekhodiweyo.[1] Isenzo sokwenza umsebenzi onjalo ubizwa ngokuba ngumbhali, okuthetha ukuba umkroli, umzobi, okanye umqambi uthathwa njengombhali wemifanekiso eqingqiweyo, imizobo, okanye iingoma zomculo. Nangona lisetyenziswa ngokufanayo, igama elithi "umbhali" lidla ngokunxulunyaniswa ngokukodwa nombhali wencwadi, inqaku, umdlalo, okanye omnye umsebenzi obhaliweyo.[2] Kwiimeko ezibandakanya umsebenzi wokuqeshwa, umqeshi okanye iqela eligunyazisayo lithathwa ngokusemthethweni njengombhali womsebenzi, nokuba wawudalwe ngomnye umntu.[1] 

Ngokuqhelekileyo, umnini wokuqala welungelo lokushicilela ngumdali womsebenzi onelungelo lokushicilela, oko kukuthi, umbhali. Ukuba ngaphezulu komntu omnye udale umsebenzi, ngoko ububhali obuhlangeneyo buye kwenzeka. Umthetho welungelo lokushicilela uyahluka kwihlabathi jikelele. Ngokomzekelo, i-Ofisi ye-Copyright yaseUnited States ichaza ilungelo lokushicilela “njengohlobo lokhuseleko olunikezelwa yimithetho yaseUnited States (isihloko 17, iKhowudi yase-US) kubabhali ‘bemisebenzi yantlandlolo yobuqambi 

. Ingxabano ye-monkey selfie copyright ngo-2010s yayiyingxabano ephawulekayo yobubhali ebandakanya iifoto ezithathwe nguCelebes crested macaques usebenzisa izixhobo zomfoti wendalo. Umfoti waqinisekisa ububhali beefoto, nto leyo eyakhatywayo yi-Ofisi ye-Copyright yase-United States, isithi: "Ukuze ufaneleke njengomsebenzi 'wombhali' umsebenzi kufuneka wenziwe ngumntu."[5] Ukuphuhliswa kobukrelekrele bokwenziwa kwemveliso kuye kwakhokelela kwintetho emalunga nobubhali bamajelo eendaba eyivelisayo. 

Ukubaluleka okusemthethweni kobuqambi 
Ukubamba isihloko "sombhali" phezu kwayo nayiphi na "uncwadi, idrama, umculo, ubugcisa, [okanye] eminye imisebenzi yobungqondi" inika amalungelo kulo mntu, umnini welungelo lokushicilela, ngokukodwa ilungelo elikhethekileyo lokubandakanya okanye ukugunyazisa nayiphi na imveliso okanye ukuhanjiswa komsebenzi wabo.[3][4] Nawuphi na umntu okanye iziko elinqwenela ukusebenzisa ipropathi enomgangatho ophezulu wokuqonda egcinwe phantsi kwelungelo lokushicilela kufuneka lifumane imvume kumnini-copyright yokusebenzisa lo msebenzi, kwaye ngokufuthi liya kucelwa ukuba lihlawulele ukusetyenziswa kwezinto ezinelungelo lokushicilela.[4]

Amalungelo okukopisha kumsebenzi wobukrelekrele aphelelwa emva kwexesha elithile. Ingena kwindawo yoluntu, apho inokusetyenziswa ngaphandle komda.[4] Imithetho ye-copyright kwiindawo ezininzi zolawulo - ubukhulu becala ilandela ukukhokela kwe-United States, apho amashishini okuzonwabisa kunye nopapasho anamandla amakhulu okuphembelela - iye yalungiswa ngokuphindaphindiweyo ukususela ekusekweni kwayo, ukwandisa ubude beli xesha limiselweyo apho umsebenzi ulawulwa ngokukodwa ngumnini-copyright. Ngokobuchwephesha, umntu ungumnikazi womsebenzi wakhe ukususela kwixesha lokudalwa kwawo. Umba obalulekileyo wombhali uvela kunye nelungelo lokushicilela kuba, kwiindawo ezininzi, linokudluliselwa komnye umntu, xa umntu efile. Umntu ozuze ilifa lelungelo lokushicilela ayingombhali, kodwa unokufikelela kwizibonelelo zomthetho ezifanayo. 

Imithetho yepropathi enomgangatho ophezulu wokuqonda intsonkothile. Imisebenzi yeentsomi ibandakanya umthetho weempawu zorhwebo, amalungelo afanayo, amalungelo okusebenzisa ngokufanelekileyo agcinwe luluntu (kubandakanywa nelungelo lokuhlekisa okanye ukuhlekisa), kunye nezinye iingxaki ezininzi zokusebenzisana.[6] 

Ababhali bangabelana ngamalungelo ahlukeneyo abanawo kumaqela ahlukeneyo ngamaxesha ahlukeneyo, kunye neenjongo ezahlukeneyo okanye ukusetyenziswa, okufana nelungelo lokulungelelanisa iploti ibe yifilim, uthotho lukamabonakude, okanye umdlalo wevidiyo. Ukuba elinye iqela likhetha ukulungelelanisa umsebenzi, kusenokufuneka baguqule izakhi zeploti okanye amagama abalinganiswa ukuze baphephe ukophula uhlengahlengiso lwangaphambili. Umbhali usenokungabi namalungelo xa esebenza phantsi kwekhontrakthi ebeya kuba nayo, njengaxa esenza umsebenzi wokuqesha (umzekelo, uqeshelwe ukubhala isikhokelo sokhenketho lwesixeko ngurhulumente kamasipala ongumnini welungelo lokukhuphela umsebenzi ogqityiweyo), okanye xa ebhala imathiriyeli esebenzisa ubukrelekrele bepropathi enabanye (njengaxa ubhala inoveli okanye umdlalo weskrini osisavenge esitsha kurhwebo lwemidiya esele lusekiwe). 

EUnited States, iGatya lelungelo lokushicilela loMgaqo-siseko waseUnited States (iSiqendu I, iCandelo lesi-8, iGatya lesi-8) libonelela iNkongolo ngamandla "okukhusela amaXesha aqingqiweyo kuBabhali kunye nabaqambi beLungelo elikhethekileyo kwiZibhalo zabo kunye noFunyanisiweyo".[7] Ulwimi olumalunga nababhali luthatyathwe kwizindululo zikaCharles Pinckney, "ukukhusela ababhali amalungelo awodwa okwexeshana eliqingqiweyo", kunye noJames Madison, "ukukhusela ababhali boncwadi amalungelo abo okukhuphela ixesha eliqingqiweyo", okanye, ngenye indlela, "ukukhuthaza, ngeepremiyamu ezifanelekileyo kunye neMibonelelo, ukuqhubela phambili kolwazi oluluncedo kunye nezinto ezifunyenweyo".[8] Zozibini ezi zindululo zithunyelwe kwiKomiti yeeNkcukacha, eyathi yanika ingxelo ngesindululo esiqulathe ulwimi lokugqibela, esathi sabandakanywa kuMgaqo-siseko ngesivumelwano esimxhelo mnye sendibano.[8] 

Iimbono zefilosofi ngobume bombhali
UMthetho ka-Anne ngowe-1710 wamisela umzekelo osemthethweni owathi wabeka iziseko zelungelo lokushicilela, waseka ngakumbi umbhali njengomyili okuphela kwakhe woncwadi. Ngelixa lo mthetho wawuvuma ukuba amazwi ombhali ayipropathi yabo yeNgqondo, awuzange nangayiphi na indlela ukhusele iingcamango zaloo mbhali. Ngokomzekelo, omnye umbhali wayenokukhuphela iploti yomnye umbhali ngokuthe ngqo, logama nje amagama engakhutshelwanga ngokwelizwi nelizwi. Ngamanye amazwi, iSifanekiso sika-Anne sikhusele indlela yokuthetha yombhali kodwa kungekhona iingcamango emva kwamagama abo.[9] 


UJames Joyce wayengunoveli owaziwayo waseIreland, imbongi kunye nomgxeki woncwadi ngenkulungwane yama-20. 
Kwithiyori yoncwadi, abagxeki bafumana iingxaki kwigama elithi umbhali ngaphaya koko kubumba ubuqambi kwimeko yezomthetho. Emva koncwadi lwamvanje, abahlalutyi abanjengoRoland Barthes noMichel Foucault baye bahlola indima kunye nokufaneleka kombhali kwintsingiselo okanye ukutolikwa kwesicatshulwa soncwadi. 

UBarthes ucela umngeni kwingcamango yokuba isicatshulwa singabalelwa kuye nawuphi na umbhali omnye. Ubhala, kwisincoko sakhe esithi “Ukufa koMbhali” (1968), ukuba “lulwimi oluthethayo, hayi umbhali.”[10] Amagama nolwimi lwesicatshulwa ngokwaso simisela kwaye sibhentsise intsingiselo kaBarthes, ingenguye umntu onoxanduva olusemthethweni ngenkqubo yokuveliswa kwayo. Wonke umgca wesicatshulwa esibhaliweyo yimbonakaliso nje yeembekiselo ezivela kuyo nayiphi na intaphane yezithethe, okanye, njengoko uBarthes esitsho, "isicatshulwa sisicuku sesicatshulwa esithathwe kumaziko angenakubalwa enkcubeko"; asiyonto yoqobo.[10] Ngale nto, imbono yombhali iyasuswa kwisicatshulwa, kwaye imida eyayibekwe ngaphambili yingcamango yelizwi elinye eligunyazisiweyo, intsingiselo enye yokugqibela kunye neyomhlaba wonke, iyatshatyalaliswa. Ingcaciso kunye nentsingiselo yomsebenzi akufuneki ukuba ifunwe kulowo wawuvelisayo, "ngokungathi usoloko ekugqibeleni, ngokusebenzisa i-alkori ecacileyo okanye engaphantsi yentsomi, ilizwi lomntu omnye, umbhali 'ozithembayo' kuthi." Ukubhentsisa iintsingiselo kumsebenzi obhaliweyo ngaphandle kokubhenela kusaziwayo wombhali, izinto abazithandayo, iinkanuko zabo, ubugwenxa, kuBarthes, ukuvumela ulwimi ukuba luthethe, kunombhali.

UMichel Foucault uxoxa kwisincoko sakhe esithi "Yintoni umbhali?" (1969) ukuba bonke ababhali bangababhali, kodwa asingabo bonke ababhali abangababhali. Uthi “ileta yabucala inokuba nomsayini—ayinaye umbhali.”[11] Ukuba umfundi abele isihloko sombhali kuwo nawuphi na umsebenzi obhaliweyo kukunxulumanisa imigangatho ethile kwisicatshulwa esithi, kwiFoucault, sisebenza kunye nengcamango “yomsebenzi wombhali.”[11] Umsebenzi wombhali kaFoucault yingcamango yokuba umsebenzi wombhali uyinxalenye yomsebenzi obhaliweyo, kodwa uyinxalenye yomsebenzi obhaliweyo kuphela, kodwa uyinxalenye yesakhiwo esibhaliweyo kuphela, kodwa iyinxalenye yomsebenzi obhaliweyo. inkqubo yokutolika. Igama lombhali "libonisa ubume bentetho phakathi koluntu kunye nenkcubeko," kwaye ngaxa lithile lalisetyenziswa njengeankile yokutolika isicatshulwa, isenzo apho uBarthes anokuthi asingomzamo ofanelekileyo okanye osemthethweni. 

Ukwandisa indawo kaFoucault, uAlexander Nehamas ubhala ukuba uFoucault ucebisa "umbhali [...] nguye nabani na onokuqondwa ukuba uvelise isicatshulwa esithile njengoko sisitolika," kungekhona ukuba ngubani obhale isicatshulwa.[12] Ngulo mahluko phakathi kokuvelisa umsebenzi obhaliweyo kunye nokuvelisa ukutolikwa okanye intsingiselo kumsebenzi obhaliweyo ukuba bobabini uBarthes noFoucault banomdla kuyo. UFoucault ulumkisa ngeengozi zokugcina igama lombhali engqondweni ngexesha lokutolikwa, kuba kunokuchaphazela ixabiso kunye nentsingiselo umntu aphatha ngayo ukutolika. 

Abahlalutyi boncwadi uBarthes noFoucault bacebisa ukuba abafundi mabangathembeli okanye bajonge ingcamango yelizwi elinye elibalaseleyo xa betolika umsebenzi obhaliweyo, ngenxa yeengxaki ezifumaneka kwisihloko sombhali esithi "umbhali." Balumkisa ngeengozi ezinokubangelwa kukutolika xa benxulumanisa umbandela wamagama anentsingiselo ngokwemvelo kunye nobuntu belizwi elinye elinegunya. Endaweni yoko, abafundi kufuneka bavumele isicatshulwa ukuba sitolikwe ngokolwimi "njengombhali." 

Ubudlelwane nompapashi 
Ukuzipapasha 
Inqaku eliphambili: Ukuzipapasha 
Ukuzipapasha kuxa ababhali besebenza njengabapapashi beencwadi zabo kwaye bathathe uxanduva olupheleleyo kunye nolawulo lweendleko. Ezo ndleko ziquka ukuhlela, ukushicilela, nokusasaza eyabo imisebenzi. 

Upapasho lwemveli 
Ngopapasho olugunyazisiweyo, umshicileli wenza onke amalungiselelo opapasho kwaye umbhali uhlawula zonke iindleko.

Ababhali banokubuyekezwa ngepesenti yesamba sencwadi okanye ixabiso elithile, okanye ngokufumana imali emiselweyo ngekopi nganye ethengisiweyo. Ukuze kuncitshiswe ingozi, maxa wambi abavakalisi bayayirhoxisa loo ntlawulo de kuthengiswe inani elithile leekopi. EKhanada, le ndlela yavela ngeminyaka yee-1890 kodwa ayizange isasazeke de kwangoo-1920. Ababhali abasele bebekiwe banokunikwa iintlawulo zakwangaphambili xa kuthelekiswa ne royalty yexesha elizayo, nangona le nkqubo inqabile. Uninzi lwabashicileli abazimeleyo ngoku bahlawula imirhumo njengepesenti yeerisithi ezishiyekileyo nangona iirisithi ezibaliweyo zinokwahluka njani ngumvakalisi. Ngaphantsi kwezi zivumelwano, umbhali akanalo uxanduva lwazo naziphi na iindleko zokupapashwa; umthwalo wemali uthwalwa ngokupheleleyo ngumvakalisi, ogcina esona sabelo sikhulu sengeniso. Bona kwakhona Imbuyekezo.[13] 

Upapasho lwamampunge 
Inqaku eliphambili: Amampunge oshicilelo 
Amampunge abapapashi badla ngokubiza umrhumo othe tyaba ukulungiselela upapasho, banikeze iqonga lokuthengisa, baze bathathe ipesenti yentengiso yekopi nganye yencwadi.[14] Umbhali ufumana eseleyo imali eyenziweyo. [14] Uninzi lwezixhobo ezipapashwe ngale ndlela zezamaqela e-niche hayi abaphulaphuli abaninzi.[15] 

Upapasho lwamampunge, okanye upapasho lwenkxaso-mali,[15] lubekwe ibala kwihlabathi lobuchwephesha. Ngo-1983, uBill Henderson wachaza abapapashi abangamampunge njengabantu abaya "kupapasha nantoni na umbhali aya kuyihlawulela, idla ngokuba yilahleko kumbhali kunye nenzuzo entle kumshicileli." Ngenxa yoku, abapapashi bangamampunge akufuneki batyale imali ekwenzeni iincwadi zithengiswe njengoko kufuneka abanye abapapashi [15] Oku kukhokelela ekubeni iincwadi ezikumgangatho ophantsi zaziswe emarikeni. 

Ubudlelwane nomhleli 
Ubudlelwane phakathi kombhali kunye nomhleli, amaxesha amaninzi unxibelelwano lombhali kuphela kwinkampani epapashayo, luphawulwa njengendawo yoxinzelelo. Ukuze umbhali afikelele kubaphulaphuli bakhe, rhoqo ngokupapashwa, umsebenzi kufuneka utsale umdla womhleli. Ingcamango yombhali njengoyena kuphela umenzi wentsingiselo yotshintsho olufunekayo ukubandakanya iimpembelelo zomhleli kunye nomshicileli ukuba abandakanye abaphulaphuli ngokubhala njengesenzo sentlalo. 

Zintathu iindidi eziphambili zokuhlela: 

Ukuqinisekisa (ukukhangela igrama kunye nopelo, ukukhangela iimpazamo zokuchwetheza), 
Ibali (ekunokwenzeka ukuba yindawo yomsindo onzulu kubo bobabini umbhali kunye nomshicileli), kunye 
noYilo (ulungiselelo lohlobo olufunekayo ukulungiselela umsebenzi wokupapasha ngokuqhelekileyo kufuna utshintsho oluncinci lokubhaliweyo, ngoko ke umhleli woyilo uyaqeshwa ukuqinisekisa ukuba ezi zinto azikwenzi oko).
Isincoko sikaPierre Bourdieu "Intsimi yeMveliso yeNkcubeko" ibonisa ishishini lopapasho "njengesithuba sokuthatha indawo yoncwadi okanye yobugcisa," ekwabizwa ngokuba "yintsimi yemizabalazo," echazwa ngoxinzelelo kunye nentshukumo ekhoyo phakathi kwezikhundla ezahlukeneyo kulo mmandla.[17] U-Bourdieu ubanga ukuba "indawo yokuthatha indawo [...] ayisiyomveliso yenjongo yokufuna ukuhambelana okanye ukuvumelana kwenjongo," oku kuthetha ukuba ishishini elibonakaliswe ngokuthatha isikhundla asiyiyo yemvisiswano kunye nokungathathi hlangothi.[18] Ngokukodwa kumbhali, ukubhala kwabo kumsebenzi wabo kwenza umsebenzi wabo ube yinxalenye yesazisi sabo, kwaye kuninzi okusemngciphekweni buqu ngothethathethwano lwegunya malunga nobo bangobani. Noko ke, ngumhleli “onegunya lokumisela eyona nkcazelo ibalaseleyo yombhali yaye ngoko ke ukucanda imida yabantu abanelungelo lokuthabatha inxaxheba kumzabalazo wokuchaza umbhali”.[19] "Njengabatyali-mali benkcubeko," abapapashi baxhomekeke kwisikhundla somhleli ukuchonga utyalo-mali olulungileyo "kwinkunzi yenkcubeko" enokukhula ivelise inkunzi yezoqoqosho kuzo zonke izikhundla.[20] 

Ngokutsho kwezifundo zikaJames Curran, inkqubo yemilinganiselo ekwabelwana ngayo phakathi kwabahleli eBritani iye yavelisa uxinzelelo phakathi kwababhali ukuba babhale ukuze ilingane nolindelo lwabahleli, isuse ugxininiso kubafundi-abaphulaphuli kwaye ibeka uxinzelelo kubudlelwane phakathi kwababhali nabahleli kunye nokubhala njengesenzo soluntu. Nkqu nophononongo lwencwadi ngabahleli lubalulekile kunolwamkelo lwabafundi.[21] 

Imbuyekezo 
Ababhali baxhomekeke kwimirhumo yangaphambi kwexesha, iintlawulo zobukhosi, ukulungelelaniswa komsebenzi kumdlalo wesikrini, kunye neemali eziqokelelwa ngokunikela iintetho.[22] 

Ikhontrakthi esemgangathweni yombhali idla ngokubandakanya isibonelelo sentlawulo ngendlela ye-advanced and royalties. 

I-Advance: isixa-mali esihlawulwa phambi kokuba sipapashwe. Intlawulo yangaphambili kufuneka ihlawulwe phambi kokuba kuhlawulwe iiroyalties. Inokuhlawulwa ngezixa-mali ezimbini: eyokuqala intlawulo ngokusayinwa kwemvumelwano, ize eyesibini ihlawulwe ngokuziswa kombhalo-ngqangi ogqityiweyo okanye ngokupapashwa. 
Intlawulo yeRoyalty: imali ehlawulwe kubabhali ngekopi nganye yencwadi ethengisiweyo kwaye ngokwesithethe ijikeleze i-10-12%, kodwa ababhali abazipapashayo banokufumana malunga ne-40% - 60% yemali yentlawulo yencwadi nganye yentengiso.[22] Ikhontrakthi yombhali inokucacisa, umzekelo, ukuba baya kufumana i-10% yexabiso lentengiso yencwadi nganye ethengisiweyo. Ezinye iikhontrakthi zichaza isikali semali ehlawulwayo (umzekelo, apho iiroyalty ziqala kwi-10% kwiintengiso ezili-10,000 zokuqala, kodwa zinyuke ziye kumyinge wepesenti ephezulu kwimida yokuthengisa ephezulu).
Ngokwesiqhelo, incwadi yombhali kufuneka ifumane imali yangaphambili phambi kokuba kuhlawulwe naziphi na ezinye iiroyalty. Ngokomzekelo, ukuba umbhali uhlawulwe i-advanced advance ye-2000 yeedola, kwaye izinga labo lobukhosi li-10% yencwadi exabisa i-$ 20 - oko kukuthi, i-$ 2 ngencwadi - incwadi iya kufuna ukuthengisa iikopi ze-1000 ngaphambi kokuba nayiphi na intlawulo eyongezelelweyo iya kwenziwa. Abapapashi badla ngokuyibamba intlawulo yepesenti yemali ezuzwayo xa kuthelekiswa nembuyekezo. 

Kwamanye amazwe, ababhali nabo bafumana umvuzo kwisikimu sikarhulumente esifana ne-ELR (ilungelo lemfundo lemboleko) kunye ne-PLR (ilungelo lokuboleka imali kawonke-wonke) e-Australia. Phantsi kwezi nkqubo, ababhali bahlawulwa intlawulo ngenani leekopi zeencwadi zabo kumathala eencwadi emfundo kunye/okanye kawonke-wonke. 
 
Kwezi ntsuku, ababhali abaninzi bongeza ingeniso yabo ekuthengisweni kweencwadi ngothethathethwano loluntu,ukutyelelwa kwezikolo, iindawo zokuhlala, iigranti, nezithuba zokufundisa.

Ababhali beGhostwriters, ababhali bobugcisa, kunye nababhali beencwadi ngokuqhelekileyo bahlawulwa ngendlela eyahlukileyo: ngokuqhelekileyo intlawulo emiselweyo okanye ireyithi yegama ngalinye kunepesenti yokuthengisa. 

Kunyaka we-2016, ngokutsho kwe-US Bureau of Labor Statistics, phantse abantu abayi-130,000 basebenza kweli lizwe njengababhali, benza umyinge we-61,240 yeedola ngonyaka. 

Incwadi ye-ebook (ifutshane kwincwadi ye-elektroniki), ephinda ibhalwe njenge-e-book okanye i-eBook, yincwadi epapashiweyo eyenziwe yafumaneka ngohlobo lwe-elektroniki, equka umbhalo, imifanekiso, okanye zombini, efundeka kwiphaneli yephaneli ebonisa iikhompyutha okanye ezinye izixhobo zombane.[1] Nangona ngamanye amaxesha ichazwa "njengenguqulelo ye-elektroniki yencwadi eprintiweyo", [2] ezinye ii-e-books zikhona ngaphandle kokuprintwa okufanayo. Iincwadi ze-E-zinokufundwa kwizixhobo ezizinikeleyo zokufunda i-elektroniki, nakuso nasiphi na isixhobo sekhompyutha esinesikrini sokujonga esilawulekayo, kubandakanywa iikhompyutha zedesktop, iilaptops, iitafile kunye nee-smartphones. 

Kwi-2000s, kwakukho umkhwa wokuprinta kunye ne-e-book yokuthengisa ehamba kwi-Intanethi, [3] apho abafundi bathenga iincwadi zephepha zemveli kunye ne-e-ncwadi kwiiwebhusayithi usebenzisa iinkqubo ze-e-commerce. Ngeencwadi eziprintiweyo, abafundi baya bekhangela ngakumbi kwimifanekiso yamaqweqwe eencwadi kumshicileli okanye kwiiwebhusayithi zevenkile yeencwadi kunye nokukhetha kunye nokuodola izihloko kwi-Intanethi. Emva koko iincwadi zamaphepha zisiwa kumfundi ngeposi okanye ngayo nayiphi na enye inkonzo yokuhanjiswa. Ngee-books, abasebenzisi banokukhangela ngezihloko kwi-intanethi, bakhethe kwaye baodole izihloko, emva koko i-e-book inokuthunyelwa kubo kwi-intanethi okanye umsebenzisi unokukhuphela i-e-book.[4] Ekuqaleni koo-2010, ii-e-books zaziqalisile ukugqitha kwi-hardcover ngamanani apapashiweyo e-US[5]
 
Izizathu eziphambili zokuba abantu bathenge i-e-books mhlawumbi ngenxa yamaxabiso aphantsi, ukunyuka kokukhululeka (njengoko banokuthenga ekhaya okanye ekuhambeni ngezixhobo eziphathwayo) kunye nokukhethwa okukhulu kwezihloko.[6] Ngee-books, "iibhukhimakhi ze-elektroniki zenza kube lula ukubhekisela, kwaye abafundi be-e-book banokuvumela umsebenzisi ukuba achaze amaphepha." "Nangona iincwadi ezingeyonyani nezingezontsomi ziza kwiifomathi ze-e-book, izinto zobugcisa zifaneleke ngokukodwa ukuhanjiswa kwe-e-book kuba zinokukhangelwa ngedijithali" kumagama angundoqo. Ukongeza, kwiincwadi zeprogram, imizekelo yekhowudi inokukhutshelwa.[7] E-US, inani le-e-ncwadi yokufunda liyenyuka. Ngo-2021, i-30% yabantu abadala baye bafunda i-e-book kunyaka odlulileyo, xa kuthelekiswa ne-17% kwi-2011. Ngo-2014, i-50% yabantu abadala baseMerika babe ne-e-reader okanye ithebhulethi, xa kuthelekiswa ne-30% ephethe izixhobo ezinjalo kwi-2013. [9] 

Ngaphandle kweencwadi ezipapashiweyo kunye neemagazini ezinokulingana kwedijithali, kukwakho neencwadi zokufunda zedijithali ezijoliswe ukuba zisebenze njengesicatshulwa seklasi kunye nokunceda kwimfundo esekelwe kubuchwepheshe. 

Ii-Teminology 
E-books zikwabizwa ngokuba zii-"ebooks", "e-books", "eBooks", "Ebooks", "e-Books", "e-journals", "e-editions", okanye "digital books". Isixhobo esenzelwe ngokukodwa ukufunda iincwadi ze-e-book kuthiwa yi-"e-reader", "ebook device", okanye "eReader". 

Imbali 
The Readies (1930) 
Abanye balanda ingqikelelo ye-e-reader, isixhobo esiya kwenza ukuba umsebenzisi abone iincwadi kwiscreen, kwimanifesto ka-1930 kaBob Brown, eyabhalwa emva kokubukela i-"talkie" yakhe yokuqala (ifilimu enesandi). Wayibiza ngokuba yiThe Readies, edlala ingcamango ye "talkie".[10] Kwincwadi yakhe, uBrown uthi iimuvi ziye zayigqitha le ncwadi ngokwenza "iintetho" kwaye, ngenxa yoko, ukufunda kufuneka kufumane indlela entsha: 

Umatshini olula wokufunda endinokuthi ndiwuphathe okanye ndiwujikeleze,ncamathela nakweyiphi iplagi yombane endala kwaye ndifunde iinoveli zamagama alikhulu lamawaka ngemizuzu eli-10 ukuba ndiyafuna, kwaye ndiyafuna.

Ingcamango kaBrown, nangona kunjalo, yayigxile kakhulu ekuguquleni ukubhalwa kwe-orthography kunye nesigama, kunokuba kuphakathi. Uthi: "Lixesha lokukhupha isithinteli" kwaye uqalise "inguqu enegazi yegama," ukwazisa amanani amakhulu eesimboli ze-portmanteau ukubuyisela amagama aqhelekileyo, kunye neziphumlisi ukulinganisa isenzo okanye intshukumo, ngoko ke akucaci ukuba oku kuyangena kwimbali ye "e-books" okanye hayi. Kamva abafundi be-elektroniki abazange balandele imodeli kwaphela efana nekaBrown. Nangona kunjalo, wachaza ngokuchanekileyo i-miniaturization kunye nokuphatheka kwe-e-readers. Kwinqaku, uJennifer Schuessler ubhala athi: "Umatshini, uBrown wathi, uya kuvumela abafundi ukuba bahlengahlengise ubungakanani bohlobo, baphephe ukusika amaphepha kunye nokugcina imithi, ngelixa bekhawuleza imini xa amagama anokuthi 'abhalwe ngokuthe ngqo kwi-ether epholileyo. U-Schuessler uyinxulumanisa no-DJ ojikeleza amasuntswana eengoma ezindala ukwenza isingqi okanye ingoma entsha ngokupheleleyo, ngokuchaseneyo ne-remix yengoma eqhelekileyo.[11] 

Umqambi 
we-e-book yokuqala akuvunyelwana ngayo ngokubanzi. Abanye abaviwa abaphawulekayo baquka oku kulandelayo: 

URoberto Busa (1946-1970) 
I-e-book yokuqala ingaba yi-Index Thomisticus, i-index ye-elektroniki echazwe kakhulu kwimisebenzi kaThomas Aquinas, elungiselelwe nguRoberto Busa, SJ eqala ngo-1946 kwaye yagqitywa kwi-1970s [12]. Nangona ekuqaleni yayigcinwe kwikhompyutha enye, inguqulelo yeCD-ROM esasazwayo yavela ngowe-1989. Noko ke, lo msebenzi uyashiywa ngamanye amaxesha. Mhlawumbi oku kungenxa yokuba umbhalo ofakwe ekhompyutheni wawuyindlela yokufunda izicatshulwa ezibhaliweyo kunye nokuphuhlisa iikhonkodensi zolwimi, kunokuba ibe luhlelo olupapashiweyo ngokwalo.[13] Ngo-2005, i-Index yapapashwa kwi-intanethi.[14] 

U-Ángela Ruiz Robles (1949) 
Ngo-1949, u-Ángela Ruiz Robles, utitshala waseFerrol, eSpain, wafumana ilungelo elilodwa lomenzi kwi-Enciclopedia Mecánica, okanye i-Mechanical Encyclopedia, isixhobo somatshini esasisebenza emoyeni oxinanisiweyo apho okubhaliweyo kunye nemizobo yayiqulethwe kwii-spools ezithi abasebenzisi baziphonse ezijikelezayo. Umbono wakhe yayikukwenza isixhobo esiza kunciphisa inani leencwadi ezithwalwa ngabafundi bakhe xa besiya esikolweni. Esona sixhobo sokugqibela sasicetywe ukuba siquke izinto ezirekhodiweyo, iglasi yokukhulisa, isixhobo sokubala, nesibane sombane ukuze sifundwe ebusuku.[15] Isixhobo sakhe asizange sibekwe kwimveliso kodwa iprototype iboniswa kwiMyuziyam yeSizwe yeSayensi neTekhnoloji eA Coruña. [16] 

UDouglas Engelbart kunye noAndries van Dam (1960s)
Ngaphandle koko, abanye ababhali-mlando bacinga ukuba iincwadi ze-elektroniki ziqale ekuqaleni kwe-1960s, kunye neprojekthi ye-NLS ekhokelwa nguDouglas Engelbart kwi-Stanford Research Institute (SRI), kunye ne-Hypertext Editing System kunye neeprojekthi ze-FRESS ezikhokelwa ngu-Andries van Dam kwiYunivesithi yaseBrown [17] [18] [19] Amaxwebhu e-FRESS aqhutywa kwi-IBM izakhelo eziphambili kwaye ajolise kulwakhiwo kunokuba ajolise kumgca. Zaye zafomathwa ngokuguquguqukayo kubasebenzisi abahlukeneyo, i-hardware yokubonisa, ubungakanani befestile, njalo njalo, kunye nokuba neetafile ezizenzekelayo zemixholo, izalathisi, njalo njalo. Zonke ezi nkqubo zikwabonelele ngonxibelelwano olubanzi, imizobo, kunye nobunye ubuchule. UVan Dam kucingelwa ukuba wayila igama elithi "incwadi ye-elektroniki", [20][21] kwaye yasekwa ngokwaneleyo ukuba isetyenziswe kwisihloko senqaku ngo-1985. 

I-FRESS yayisetyenziselwa ukufunda izicatshulwa eziphambili ezibanzi kwi-intanethi, kunye nochazo kunye neengxoxo ze-intanethi kwiikhosi ezininzi, kuquka i-English Poetry kunye ne-Biochemistry. Ifakhalthi kaBrown isebenzise kakhulu iFRESS. Umzekelo isithandi sobulumko uRoderick Chisholm wasisebenzisa ukuvelisa uninzi lweencwadi zakhe. Ngaloo ndlela kwiNtshayelelo kuMntu kunye neNjongo (1979) ubhala athi: "Le ncwadi yayingayi kugqitywa ngaphandle kwe-epoch-making File Retrieval and Editing System ..." [23] Umsebenzi weYunivesithi yaseBrown kwiinkqubo zeencwadi ze-elektroniki waqhubeka iminyaka emininzi, kubandakanywa iiprojekthi ezixhaswa ngemali yi-US Navy yokulungiswa kwe-electronic-manual; eyakha iDynaText, inkqubo yokuqala esekwe kwiSGML ye-e-reader; kunye nomsebenzi obanzi weQela leTekhnoloji yeScholar kumgangatho we-Open eBook. 

UMichael S. Hart (1971) 

uMichael S. Hart (ngasekhohlo) kunye noGregory Newby (ekunene) weProjekthi Gutenberg, kwiNkomfa ye-Hackers kwiPlanethi yoMhlaba (HOPE), ngo-2006 
Nangona imbali yangaphambili ebanzi, iimpapasho ezininzi zibika uMichael S. Hart njengomqambi we-e-book.[26][27][28] Kwi-1971, abaqhubi be-Xerox Sigma V mainframe kwiYunivesithi yase-Illinois banike iHart ixesha elide lekhompyutheni. Efuna ukusetyenziswa ngokufanelekileyo kwesi sixhobo, wenza uxwebhu lwakhe lokuqala lwe-elektroniki ngokuchwetheza iSibhengezo seNkululeko saseUnited States kwikhompyutha ngombhalo ocacileyo. UHart ucwangcise ukwenza amaxwebhu esebenzisa umbhalo ocacileyo ukuze kube lula kangangoko ukukhuphela nokujonga kwizixhobo. Emva kokuba uHart elungelelanise iSibhengezo seNkululeko sase-US kuxwebhu lwe-elektroniki ngo-1971, iProjekthi Gutenberg yasungulwa ukwenza iikopi ze-elektroniki zemibhalo emininzi, ngakumbi iincwadi.[29]
 
Ukuphunyezwa kwehardware kwangoko
Izixhobo ze-hardware ezinikezelweyo zokufunda i-ebook zaqala ukuvela kwi-70s kunye ne-80s, ngaphezu kwesakhelo esiphambili kunye nezisombululo zelaptop, kunye nokuqokelelwa kwedatha nganye. Olunye ukuphunyezwa kwe-e-book kwasekuqaleni yayiyi-desktop yeprototype yekhompyuter ecetywayo, iDynabook, ngeminyaka yoo-1970 e-PARC: ikhompyuter yenjongo eqhelekileyo ephathwayo ekwaziyo ukubonisa iincwadi zokufunda.[30] Ngo-1980, iSebe lezoKhuselo lase-US laqala uphuhliso lwengqikelelo yesixhobo sokuhanjiswa kwe-elektroniki esiphathwayo solwazi logcino lobugcisa olubizwa ngokuba yiprojekthi iPEAM, i-Portable Electronic Aid for Maintenance. Iinkcukacha ezineenkcukacha zagqitywa ngo-FY 1981/82, kwaye uphuhliso lweprototype lwaqala nge-Texas Instruments kwangaloo nyaka. Iiprototypes ezine zaveliswa kwaye zanikezelwa ukuvavanywa kwi-1986, kwaye iimvavanyo zagqitywa ngo-1987. Ingxelo yokugqibela yesishwankathelo yaveliswa kwi-1989 yi-US Army Research Institute ye-Behavioral and Social Sciences, ebhalwe nguRobert Wisher kunye no-J. Peter Kincaid. Isicelo selungelo elilodwa lomenzi wechiza kwisixhobo sePEAM, [32] esinesihloko esithi "Izixhobo zokuzisa imiyalelo yohlobo lwenkqubo", sangeniswa yiTexas Instruments ngoDisemba 4, 1985, edwelisa uJohn K. Harkins noStephen H. Morriss njengabaqambi. 


Incwadi yokuqala ye-elektroniki ephathekayo, iSebe lezoKhuseleko lase-US "Uncedo lwe-elektroniki lobuqu kwi-Maintainance" 
Kwi-1992, u-Sony uqalise i-Data Discman, umfundi wencwadi ye-elektroniki onokufunda iincwadi ze-e-books ezigcinwe kwiiCD. Olunye upapasho lwe-elektroniki olwalunokudlalwa kwiDiscman yeDatha yayibizwa ngokuba yiThala leeNcwadi Lekamva.[33] Iincwadi ze-e-early zazibhalelwa iindawo ezikhethekileyo kunye nabaphulaphuli abambalwa, benzelwe ukufundwa kuphela ngamaqela amancinci kunye namaqela anomdla. Umda wemiba yesifundo sezi e-books ubandakanya iimanyuwali zobugcisa zehardware, ubuchule bokuvelisa, kunye nezinye izifundo. Kwiminyaka ye-1990, ukufumaneka ngokubanzi kwe-Intanethi kwenza ukuhanjiswa kweefayile ze-elektroniki kube lula kakhulu, kubandakanywa 

ne-e-books. Into ephawulekayo yayikukulandela umkhondo wephepha lokugqibela elifundiweyo ukuze xa ubuyela 'kwincwadi' ubuyiselwe apho ubuyeke ukufunda ngaphambili. Isihloko sesi sitaki sisenokuba sincede ekwenzeni igama elithi 'ebook' lidume. [34] 

Iifomathi ze-e-book 
Jonga kwakhona: Uthelekiso lweefomathi ze-e-book
 
Ibhinqa lifunda incwadi isebenzisa i-e-reader
Njengoko iifomathi ze-e-book zavela kwaye zanda, [ukucaphula] inkxaso efunyenweyo evela kwiinkampani ezinkulu zesoftware, njengeAdobe nefomathi yayo yePDF eyaziswa ngo-1993. [35] Ngokungafaniyo nezinye iifomathi ezininzi, amaxwebhu ePDF ahlala ebotshelelwe kubungakanani obuthile kunye noyilo, kunokuba ahlengahlengise ngokutshintshayo kwiphepha langoku, ifestile, okanye obunye ubungakanani. Izixhobo ezahlukeneyo ze-e-reader zilandele iifomathi ezahlukeneyo, uninzi lwazo lwamkela iincwadi ngefomathi enye okanye ezimbalwa, ngaloo ndlela zahlulahlula i-e-book market nangakumbi. Ngenxa yobubodwa kunye nomlinganiselo wokufunda we-e-books, imarike eyaphukileyo yabashicileli abazimeleyo kunye nababhali abakhethekileyo abazange bavumelane malunga nomgangatho wokupakisha kunye nokuthengisa iincwadi ze-e-books [icatshulwa] 

Ngelo xesha, abaphengululi baye baqulunqa i-Text Encoding Initiative, eyaphuhlisa izikhokelo zemvumelwano malunga neencwadi ze-encoding kunye nezinye izixhobo zokufunda kakuhle njengoko kuhlalutya umdla wokufunda. Iincwadi ezininzi kunye neminye imisebenzi iye yaphuhliswa kusetyenziswa indlela ye-TEI. Ekupheleni kweminyaka yoo-1990, kwasekwa iqumrhu lokuphuhlisa i-Open eBook ifomathi njengendlela yokuba ababhali nabapapashi babonelele ngomthombo omnye-uxwebhu olunokuthi luphathwe ngesoftware yokufunda iincwadi kunye namaqonga ehardware. Abaphengululi abaliqela abavela kwi-TEI babebandakanyeka ngokusondeleyo kuphuhliso lokuqala lwe-eBook evulekileyo, kuquka uAllen Renear, uElli Mylonas, noSteven DeRose, bonke baseBrown. Igxile ekuphatheni, Vula i-eBook njengoko kuchaziwe iiseti ezifunekayo ze-XHTML kunye neCSS; isethi yefomathi zemultimedia (ezinye zingasetyenziswa, kodwa kufuneka kwakhona kubekho ukubuyisela umva kwenye yeefomati ezifunekayo), kunye ne-XML schema ye "manifest", ukudwelisa amacandelo e-e-book enikeziweyo, ukuchonga uluhlu lweziqulatho, ubugcisa bokugubungela, njalo njalo. Iincwadi zikaGoogle ziguqule imisebenzi emininzi yoluntu kule fomati ivuliweyo.[36] 

Kwi-2010, iincwadi ze-e-books zaqhubeka zizuza kwiingcali zabo kunye neemarike eziphantsi komhlaba. Kwangaxeshanye, ababhali abaneencwadi ezingamkelwanga ngabapapashi banikela ngemisebenzi yabo kwi-intanethi ukuze ibonwe ngabanye. [37] Iikhathalogu zeencwadi ezingekho semthethweni (kwaye ngamanye amaxesha ezingagunyaziswanga) ziye zafumaneka kwiwebhu, kwaye iisayithi ezinikezelwe kwii-e-books zaqala ukusasaza ulwazi malunga ne-e-books eluntwini.[38] Phantse isibini kwisithathu se-US Consumer e-book publishing market ilawulwa yi "Big Five". Abapapashi be "Big Five" ngaba: Hachette, HarperCollins, Macmillan, Penguin Random House kunye noSimon & Schuster. [39] 

Amathala eencwadi
Amathala eencwadi ase-US aqala ukunikezela ngee-e-books zasimahla kuluntu ngo-1998 ngokusebenzisa iiwebhusayithi zabo kunye neenkonzo ezihambelanayo, [40] nangona iincwadi ze-e-books ubukhulu becala yayizizifundo, ubuchwephesha, okanye ubuchwephesha bendalo, kwaye zingenako ukukhutshelwa. Ngo-2003, amathala eencwadi aqala ukunikezela ngeencwadi ze-e-fiction ezikhutshelwayo simahla nezingezontsomi eluntwini, esungula imodeli yokuboleka i-e-ncwadi eyasebenza ngempumelelo kakhulu kumathala eencwadi oluntu. [41] Inani labahambisi beencwadi ze-e-ncwadi zethala leencwadi kunye nemifuziselo yokuboleka imali liqhubekile nokukhula kule minyaka imbalwa izayo. Ukususela ngo-2005 ukuya ku-2008, amathala eencwadi afumana ukukhula kwe-60% kwiiqoqo ze-e-book.[42] Ngo-2010, i-Public Library Funding and Technology Access Study yi-American Library Association [43] yafumanisa ukuba i-66% yamathala eencwadi oluntu e-US anikezela nge-e-books, [44] kunye nentshukumo enkulu kushishino lwamathala eencwadi yaqala ukuvavanya nzulu imiba enxulumene nokubolekwa kwe-e-book, ukuvuma "inqaku lokuphonononga" xa i-e-book iteknoloji iya kusekwa ngokubanzi. Isiqulatho esivela kumathala eencwadi oluntu sinokukhutshelwa kwi-e-readers kusetyenziswa isoftwe yesicelo efana ne-Overdrive kunye neHoopla.[46] 
 
ILayibrari yeSizwe yezoNyango yase-US iminyaka emininzi ibonelela nge-PubMed, i-bibliography ebanzi yoncwadi lwezonyango. Ekuqaleni kuka-2000, i-NLM yaseka indawo yokugcina i-PubMed Central, egcina iinguqulelo ezipheleleyo ze-e-book zamanqaku amaninzi ejenali yezonyango kunye neencwadi, ngokusebenzisana nabaphengululi kunye nabapapashi entsimini. I-Pubmed Central ikwabonelela ngogcino kunye nokufikelela kumanqaku angaphezu kwezigidi ezi-4.1, agcinwe kwifomathi eqhelekileyo yeXML eyaziwa ngokuba yiJournal Article Tag Suite (JATS).

Nangona ukwamkelwa ngokubanzi kweencwadi ze-e-books, abanye abapapashi kunye nababhali abazange bayivume ingcamango yokupapashwa kwe-elektroniki, bekhankanya imiba efunwa ngumsebenzisi, ukuphulwa kwelungelo lokushicilela kunye nemingeni kunye nezixhobo zobunikazi kunye neenkqubo. [47] Kuphando lwemali mboleko yamathala eencwadi (ILL), kwafunyaniswa ukuba ama-92% amathala eencwadi abamba ii-e-books kwingqokelela yawo kwaye ama-27% aloo mathala athethathethane ngamalungelo e-ILL kwezinye zeencwadi zawo ze-e-book. Olu phononongo lufumene imiqobo ebalulekileyo ekuqhubeni imali-mboleko yamathala eencwadi kwi-e-books.[48] I-Patron-driven acquisition (PDA) ikhona iminyaka eliqela kumathala eencwadi kawonke-wonke, ivumela abathengisi ukuba balungelelanise inkqubo yokufumana ngokunikezela ukutshatisa iprofayile yokhetho lwethala leencwadi kunye nezihloko ze-e-book yomthengisi. Ikhathalogu yethala leencwadi ke izaliswe ngeerekhodi zazo zonke ii-e-books ezihambelana neprofayile. Isigqibo sokuthenga itayitile sishiyelwa kubaxhasi, nangona ithala leencwadi linokubeka iimeko zokuthenga ezifana nexabiso eliphezulu kunye neekepusi zokuthenga ukuze imali enikezelweyo isetyenziswe ngokohlahlo lwabiwo-mali lwethala leencwadi.[49] Intlanganiso ka-2012 ye-Association of American University Presses yayiquka iphaneli kwi-PDA yeencwadi eziveliswe ngoomatshini bokushicilela baseyunivesithi, ngokusekelwe kwingxelo yokuqala kaJoseph Esposito, umcebisi wokushicilela wedijithali oye wafunda iimpembelelo zePDA kunye nesibonelelo esivela ku-Andrew W. Mellon Foundation.[50] 

Imingeni 
Nangona imfuno yeenkonzo ze-e-book kwiilayibrari ikhule kwiminyaka engamashumi amabini yokuqala yekhulu lama-21, ubunzima bugcina amathala eencwadi ekuboneleleni nge-e-books kubathengi. Abapapashi baya kuthengisa iincwadi ze-e-books kumathala eencwadi, kodwa kwiimeko ezininzi baya kunika amathala eencwadi kuphela ilayisenisi elinganiselweyo kwisihloko, oku kuthetha ukuba ithala leencwadi alinayo itekisi ye-elektroniki kodwa ivumelekile ukuyijikeleza nokuba yithuba elithile lexesha, okanye inani elithile lokuphuma, okanye zombini. Xa ithala leencwadi lithenga ilayisenisi ye-e-book, ixabiso liphinda kathathu into ebeliya kuba yiyo kumthengi wobuqu.[51] Iilayisensi ze-E-book zibiza kakhulu kunohlelo lwefomathi yephepha kuba abapapashi banexhala lokuba incwadi ye-e-ncwadi ethengiswayo inokufundwa kunye/okanye ijongwe liqela elikhulu labasebenzisi, ukuthengisa okunokuba yingozi. Nangona kunjalo, ezinye izifundo zifumene umphumo ochaseneyo ukuba yinyani (umzekelo, uHilton noWikey 2010).[52] 

Ugcino loovimba 
Uvimba we-Intanethi kunye neThala leeNcwadi eliVulelekileyo zibonelela ngaphezulu kwezigidi ezithandathu ezifikeleleka ngokupheleleyo kwii-e-books zoluntu. IProjekthi Gutenberg ineencwadi ze-e-books ezifumaneka simahla kwidomeyini yoluntu. 

Abafundi behardware abazinikeleyo kunye nesoftware ephathwayo 
Inqaku eliphambili: I-E-reader 
Jonga kwakhona: Ukuthelekiswa kwe-e-readers 

IBEBook e-reader
I-e-reader, ekwabizwa ngokuba yi-e-book reader okanye i-e-book device, sisixhobo sombane esiphathwayo esenzelwe ngokukodwa injongo yokufunda ii-e-books kunye neeperiodical digital. I-e-reader ifana nefom, kodwa iyancipha ngakumbi kwinjongo kunethebhulethi. Xa kuthelekiswa namacwecwe, uninzi lwe-e-readers lungcono kuneetafile zokufunda ngenxa yokuba ziphathwa ngakumbi, zifundeka ngcono ekukhanyeni kwelanga kwaye zinobomi obude bebhetri. [53] NgoJulayi 2010, umthengisi weencwadi kwi-intanethi i-Amazon.com ibike ukuthengiswa kwe-e-books ye-Kindle yayo yobunikazi, ingaphezulu kweentengiso zeencwadi ezinoqweqwe olunzima okokuqala ngqa kwikota yesibini ye-2010, isithi ithengise ii-e-books ze-140 kuzo zonke iincwadi ze-100 ezinoqweqwe olulukhuni, kubandakanywa ii-hardcovers apho kwakungekho uhlelo lwedijithali.[54] NgoJanuwari 2011, ukuthengiswa kwe-e-book e-Amazon yayigqithise intengiso yayo yamaphepha. [55] Kuyo yonke imarike yase-US, ukuthengiswa kwencwadi yephepha kusenkulu kakhulu kunoqweqwe olulukhuni okanye i-e-ncwadi. I-American Publishing Association iqikelelwa ukuba i-e-books imele i-8.5% yeentengiso phakathi no-2010, ukusuka kwi-3% ngonyaka ngaphambili. [56] Ekupheleni kwekota yokuqala ka-2012, ukuthengiswa kwe-e-book e-United States kwadlula ukuthengiswa kwencwadi enoqweqwe olulukhuni okokuqala.[5] 

Kuze kube sekupheleni kuka-2013, ukusetyenziswa kwe-e-reader kwakungavumelekanga kwiinqwelomoya ngexesha lokuhamba kunye nokuhla yi-FAA. [57] NgoNovemba 2013, i-FAA ivumele ukusetyenziswa kwe-e-readers kwiinqwelomoya ngamaxesha onke ukuba ikwiModi yeenqwelomoya, oku kuthetha ukuba zonke iirediyo zicinyiwe, kwaye iYurophu yalandela esi sikhokelo kwinyanga ezayo. Kwi-2014, i-New York Times iqikelele ukuba ngo-2018 iincwadi ze-e-ncwadi ziza kwenza ngaphezu kwe-50% yengeniso yokushicilela abathengi eUnited States nase-Great Britain. [59] 
Inkcazo

Izicelo 

Ukufundwa kwezicelo kwizixhobo ezahlukeneyo 
Abanye abathengisi beencwadi abaphambili kunye nabaphuhlisi abaninzi beqela lesithathu babonelela simahla (kwaye kwezinye iimeko zomntu wesithathu, intlawulo ehlawulwayo) usetyenziso lwesoftware ye-e-reader (ii-apps) zekhompyuter yeMac kunye nePC kunye ne-Android, iBlackberry, i-iPad, i-iPhone, iWindows Phone kunye nezixhobo zePalm OS ukuvumela ukufundwa kwe-e-ncwadi kunye namanye amaxwebhu ngokuzimeleyo kwizixhobo ezinikezelweyo ze-ebook. Imizekelo ziiapps zeAmazon Kindle,[60] Barnes & Noble Nook, iBooks, Kobo eReader kunye neSony Reader. 

Ukuhlelwa kwethala leencwadi yinkqubo esetyenziswa ngaphakathi kwithala leencwadi ukulungiselela imathiriyeli, kuquka iincwadi, isandi kunye noshicilelo lwevidiyo, izixhobo zombane, njl. Into nganye idla ngokunikwa inombolo yomnxeba, echaza indawo yento ngaphakathi kwesixokelelwano. Izinto eziphathekayo zinokucwangciswa ngezinto ezininzi ezahlukeneyo, ngokuqhelekileyo kwisakhiwo somthi esinoluhlu olusekelwe kwisifundo okanye ukusebenzisa inkqubo yokuhlelwa kwe-faceted, evumela ukunikezelwa kokuhlelwa kwezinto ezininzi kwinto, eyenza ukuba ukuhlelwa kulandelelwe ngeendlela ezininzi.[1] 

Ukuhlelwa kwethala leencwadi ngumba obalulekileyo nobalulekileyo kwithala leencwadi nakwinzululwazi yolwazi. Yahlukile kuhlelo lwenzululwazi kuba inenjongo yokubonelela ngolungelelwaniso oluluncedo lwamaxwebhu kunokuba intlangano yethiyori yolwazi.[2] Nangona inenjongo esebenzayo yokudala ucwangco lwamaxwebhu, iyazama ngokubanzi ukubambelela kulwazi olwamkelekileyo lwezenzululwazi.[3] Ukuhlelwa kwethala leencwadi kunceda ekwamkeleni lonke uncwadi olusandul' ukupapashwa ngokolandelelwano olusele lwenziwe ngokolandelelwano lwesibini.[4] 

Ukuhlelwa kwethala leencwadi kunokuchazwa njengokucwangciswa kweencwadi ezishelfini, okanye ukuchazwa kwazo, ngendlela eluncedo kakhulu kwabo bafundayo ngeenjongo zokuhlanganisa izinto ezifanayo. Ukuhlelwa kwethala leencwadi kwenzelwa ukuphumeza ezi njongo zine: ukulungelelaniswa kwemimandla yolwazi ngendlela ecwangcisiweyo, ukuhlanganisa izinto ezinxulumene noko ngolandelelwano oluluncedo kakhulu, ukubonelela ngofikelelo ngocwangco eshelufini, nokubonelela ngendawo yento ekwishelufu.[5] 

Ukuhlelwa kwethala leencwadi kwahlukile ekusetyenzisweni kwezihloko zezifundo kuba ukuhlelwa kolwazi kucwangciswa ngendlela ecwangcisiweyo, ngelixa izihloko zezifundo zibonelela ngokufikelela kwimathiriyeli yobukrelekrele ngokusebenzisa isigama esinokuthi silungelelaniswe okanye singacwangciswanga njengenkqubo yolwazi.[6] Iimpawu ezifunwa luhlelo lweencwadi ngenjongo yokufikelela ezi njongo zezi: ulandelelwano oluluncedo lwezifundo kuwo onke amanqanaba, ubhalo olufutshane olukhumbulekayo, kunye nentaphane yobuchule kunye nezixhobo zokudityaniswa kwamanani.[7] 

Imbali 
Ukuhlelwa kwethala leencwadi kwandulelwa luhlelo olusetyenziswa ngababhali beencwadi abanjengoConrad Gessner.
