Izikim zokuqala zokuhlela iilayibrari zaziququzelela iincwadi kwiindidi zezifundo ezibanzi. Esona sikimu samandulo esaziwayo sokuhlelwa kwethala leencwadi ziiPinakes nguCallimachus, isifundiswa kwiThala leencwadi laseAlexandria ngenkulungwane yesithathu ngaphambi kweXesha Eliqhelekileyo. Ebudeni bexesha loHlaziyo neloHlaziyo, “Amathala eencwadi ayelungelelaniswa ngokokuthanda okanye ulwazi lwabantu abaphetheyo.”[8] Oku kwayitshintsha indlela izinto ezahlukahlukeneyo ezazihlelwa ngayo. Ezinye ingqokelela zazihlelwa ngokolwimi yaye ezinye zazihlelwa ngendlela ezazishicilelwa ngayo. 

Emva kwenguqulelo yoshicilelo kwinkulungwane yeshumi elinesithandathu, ukwanda kwezinto ezishicilelweyo ezifumanekayo kwenza ukuba ukuhlelwa okubanzi ngolo hlobo kungasebenzeki, kwaye ukwahlulwa ngokwegranula kwezixhobo zamathala eencwadi kwafuneka kuphuhliswe kwinkulungwane yeshumi elinesithoba.[9]

Ngowe-1627 uGabriel Naudé wapapasha incwadi ethi Advice on Establishing a Library. Ngelo xesha, wayesebenza kwithala leencwadi labucala likaMongameli à mortier Henri de Mesmes II. IMesmes yayineencwadi ezishicilelweyo ezimalunga nama-8,000 kunye neminye imibhalo-ngqangi ebhaliweyo yesiGrike, isiLatini nesiFrentshi. Nangona yayilithala labucala, abaphengululi abaneembekiselo babenokuyifikelela. Injongo yeNgcebiso ngokuSekwa kweThala leencwadi yayikukuchonga imithetho yabaqokeleli beencwadi yabucala ukuba baququzelele ukuqokelela kwabo ngendlela enocwangco ukuze kwandiswe ukusebenziseka nobuhle bengqokelela. UNaudé wavelisa inkqubo yokuhlela esekelwe kwiindidi ezisixhenxe ezahlukeneyo: ezakwalizwi, amayeza, umthetho, imbali, intanda-bulumko, imathematika, nobuntu. Ezi klasi zisixhenxe kamva ziya kwandiswa zibe lishumi elinambini.[10] Ingcebiso ekuSekweni kweThala leencwadi yayimalunga nethala leencwadi labucala, kodwa ngaphakathi kwaloo ncwadi, uNaudé wakhuthaza imbono yamathala eencwadi oluntu avuleleke kubo bonke abantu kungakhathaliseki ukuba banako na ukuhlawula ukufikelela kwingqokelela. Elinye lamathala eencwadi adumileyo awathi uNaudé wawaphucula laliyiBibliothèque Mazarine yaseParis. UNaudé wachitha iminyaka elishumi apho njengononcwadi. Ngenxa yenkolelo kaNaudé enamandla yokufikelela ngokukhululekileyo kumathala eencwadi kubo bonke abantu, iBibliothèque Mazarine yaba lithala leencwadi lokuqala likawonke wonke eFransi malunga nowe-1644.[11] 

Nangona amathala eencwadi adala ucwangco phakathi kweengqokelela zawo ukususela ekuqaleni kwenkulungwane yesihlanu BC, [9] ukuhlelwa komthengisi weencwadi waseParis, ophuhliswe ngo-1842 nguJacques Charles Brunet, ngokubanzi ubonwa njengeyokuqala kuhlelo lwencwadi yanamhlanje. I-Brunet ibonelele ngeeklasi ezintlanu eziphambili: ezakwalizwi, i-jurisprudence, isayensi kunye nezobugcisa, ii-belles-lettres, kunye nembali.[12] Ukuhlelwa ngoku kunokubonwa njengomboneleli wokufikelela kwisifundo kulwazi kwindawo enxibeleleneyo.[13] 

Iindidi 
Zininzi iinkqubo ezisemgangathweni zokuhlelwa kwethala leencwadi ezisetyenziswayo, kwaye ezininzi ngakumbi ziye zacetywa ekuhambeni kweminyaka. Nakuba kunjalo, ngokubanzi, iisistim zokuhlela zinokwahlulwa zibe ziindidi ezintathu ngokuxhomekeke kwindlela ezisetyenziswa ngayo: 

Izikim ze-Universal 
Zigubungela zonke izifundo, umz. i-Dewey Decimal Classification (DDC), i-Universal Decimal Classification (UDC), kunye ne-Colon Classification (CC).  
Izikimu zokuhlela ezikhethekileyo
Ibandakanya izifundo ezithile okanye iintlobo zemathiriyeli, umz. Iconclass (ubugcisa), iCatalog yaseBritani yoHlelo loMculo, kunye nokuhlelwa kukaDickinson (umculo), okanye uHlelo lwe-NLM (amayeza). 
Izikim zesizwe 
Ezenzelwe amazwe athile ngokukodwa, umzekelo, inkqubo yokuhlelwa kwethala leencwadi laseSweden, i-SAB (Sveriges Allmänna Biblioteksförening). UHlelo lweThala leeNcwadi leCongress layilwa ngokujikeleza ingqokelela yeThala leencwadi lase-US leCongress kwaye linomkhethe waseMelika, waseYurophu, nowobuKrestu. Nangona kunjalo, isetyenziswa ngokubanzi kumathala eencwadi amakhulu ezemfundo kunye nophando. 
Ngokokusebenza, iinkqubo zokuhlela zihlala zichazwa ngolu hlobo: 

Ubalo
Izihloko zezihloko zidweliswe ngokwealfabhethi, amanani anikwe kwisihloko ngasinye ngokulandelelana kwealfabhethi. Imixholo 
yeHierarchical 
yahlulwe ngokoluhlu, ukusuka kwezona ziqhelekileyo ukuya kwezona zikhethekileyo. 
I-Faceted/analytico-synthetic 
Imixholo yahlulwe yangamacandelo ahlukeneyo oorthogonal. 
Zimbalwa iisistim ezibalayo ngokupheleleyo okanye iisistim ezimacala; iinkqubo ezininzi zingumxube kodwa zikhetha olunye uhlobo okanye olunye. Ezona nkqubo ziqhelekileyo zokuhlela, i-LCC kunye ne-DDC, zibala kakhulu, nangona zinoluhlu lwemigangatho kunye ne-faceted elements (ngakumbi kwi-DDC), ngakumbi kwinqanaba elibanzi kunye nelona jikelele. Inkqubo yokuqala yokwenyani yayiluhlelo lwekholoni yeSR Ranganathan.[14] 

Iimethodi okanye imixholo ye-sys Iintlobo 
zokuhlela zichaza ulwahlulo okanye ukuhlelwa ngokwemo okanye iimpawu okanye iimpawu zesikim sohlelo okanye izikimu. Indlela kunye nenkqubo inentsingiselo efanayo. Indlela okanye iindlela okanye inkqubo ithetha izikimu zokuhlela ezifana nokuhlelwa kweedesimali zikaDewey okanye uHlelo lweDecimal oluqhelekileyo. Iindidi zokuhlela zezokuchonga nokuqonda okanye imfundo okanye iinjongo zophando ngelixa indlela yokuhlela ithetha ezo zikim zokuhlela ezifana ne-DDC, i-UDC. 

Iinkqubo zokuhlela jikelele ngolwimi lwesiNgesi 

IMoys Classification Scheme njengoko isetyenziswa lithala leencwadi leNkundla ePhakamileyo yaseHong Kong 
Iinkqubo ezixhaphakileyo kumazwe athetha IsiNgesi zezi: 

Dewey Decimal Classification (DDC) 
Library of Congress Classification (LCC) 
Universal Decimal Classification (UDC)

Book Industry Standards and Communications (BISAC), iye yanda incwadi yoMsebenzi woNxibelelwano (BISAC), iye yaphuhliswa yincwadi yase-US. amathala eencwadi.[15] 
Ukuhlelwa kweencwadi zeBliss ezisetyenziswa kwamanye amathala eencwadi aseBritani 
Ukuhlelwa kweColon (CC) 
Uhlelo lweGarside olusetyenziswa kuninzi lwamathala eencwadi eYunivesithi yaseLondon [16]

) 
UHlelo lweThala leeNcwadi laseGladstone, layilwa nguWE Gladstone kwaye lisetyenziswa kuphela kwiThala leeNcwadi laseGladstone[17]
UHlelo lweHarvard-Yenching, inkqubo yesiNgesi yokuhlelwa kwezixhobo zolwimi lwesiTshayina 
Iinkqubo zokuhlela jikelele ezingezizo ezesiNgesi 
IsiJamani Regensburger Verbundklassifikation (RVK)

Iinkqubo zokuhlela jikelele ezixhomekeke kuhlanganiso (iinkqubo ezinamacandelo athile)

lweDesimali oluDityanisiweyo 
Iinkqubo zokuhlela ezitsha zikholisa ukusebenzisa umthetho-siseko wokudityaniswa (ukudibanisa iikhowudi ezisuka kwizintlu ezahlukeneyo ukumela iimpawu ezahlukeneyo zomsebenzi olawulwayo kwiDDC ngokudibeneyo. Ulwahlulo lweThala leeNcwadi 

lokuSebenza 
lunxulunyaniswa noluhlu lwethala leencwadi (elichazayo) phantsi kwerubrikhi yoluhlu nolwahlulo, ngamanye amaxesha zidityaniswe kunye njengeenkonzo zobugcisa. Ingcali yethala leencwadi elizibandakanya kwinkqubo yokuhlelwa nokuhlelwa kwemathiriyeli yethala leencwadi ibizwa ngokuba yikhathalogu okanye ithala leencwadi. Iisistim zokuhlela amathala eencwadi sesinye sezixhobo ezibini ezisetyenziselwa ukuququzelela ukufikelela kwisifundo. Enye iqulathe iilwimi zokwalatha ngokwealfabhethi ezifana ne-Thesauri kunye ne-Subject Headings systems. 

Ukwenziwa kokuhlelwa kwethala leencwadi luhlobo lomsebenzi wokuhlela ngokubanzi ngokubanzi. Umsebenzi unamanyathelo amabini. Okokuqala, umxholo okanye umxholo wemathiriyeli uyaqinisekiswa. Okulandelayo, inombolo yomnxeba (eyona nto ibalulekileyo idilesi yencwadi) esekelwe kwinkqubo yokuhlela esetyenziswa kwithala leencwadi elithile iya kwabelwa kumsebenzi kusetyenziswa ubhalo lwenkqubo. 

Ngokungafaniyo nesihloko sesifundo okanye i-thesauri apho amagama amaninzi anokwabelwa umsebenzi omnye, kwiinkqubo zokuhlelwa kwethala leencwadi, umsebenzi ngamnye unokubekwa kwiklasi enye kuphela. Oku kungenxa yeenjongo zokubeka iishelufu: Incwadi inokuba nendawo enye kuphela ebonakalayo. Nangona kunjalo, kwiikhathalogu ezihleliweyo umntu unokuba namangeniso aphambili kunye nawongezwayo. Uninzi lweenkqubo zokuhlela ezifana noHlelo lweDesimali lukaDewey (DDC) kunye neThala leeNcwadi loHlelo lweCongress nalo longeza inani lomsiki kumsebenzi ngamnye elongeza ikhowudi yongeniso oluphambili (indawo yofikelelo ephambili) yomsebenzi (umz. umbhali). 

Iinkqubo zokuhlela kumathala eencwadi zidlala iindima ezimbini ngokubanzi. Okokuqala, baququzelela ukufikelela kwisifundo ngokuvumela umsebenzisi ukuba afumanise ukuba yintoni esebenzayo okanye amaxwebhu ethala leencwadi ngombandela othile.[18] Okwesibini, babonelela ngendawo eyaziwayo ukuze kubekwe umthombo wolwazi (umz. apho ugcinwe khona).
 
Ukuza kuthi ga kwinkulungwane ye-19, uninzi lwamathala eencwadi ayevalile, ngoko ke ulwahlulo lwethala leencwadi lwasebenza kuphela ekulungiseleleni ikhathalogu yezifundo. Ngenkulungwane yama-20, amathala eencwadi avuleleke kuluntu ngokubanzi kwaye aqalisa ukubekel’ iishelufa imathiriyeli yethala leencwadi ngokwalo ngokohlelo oluthile lwethala leencwadi ukuze kube lula ukukhangelwa kwezifundo. 

Ezinye iisistim zokuhlela zifaneleke ngakumbi ukunceda ukufikelela kwisifundo, endaweni yendawo yeshelufu. Ngokomzekelo, i-Universal Decimal Classification, esebenzisa i-notation eyinkimbinkimbi yee-pluses kunye neekholoni, kunzima kakhulu ukuyisebenzisela injongo yokuhlelwa kweshelufu kodwa icacisa ngakumbi xa kuthelekiswa ne-DDC malunga nokubonisa ubudlelwane phakathi kwezifundo. Izikimu zokuhlela ezikwicala elifanayo kunzima kakhulu ukuzisebenzisa kulungiselelo lweshelufu, ngaphandle kokuba umsebenzisi unolwazi ngomyalelo wocaphulo.
 
Ngokuxhomekeke kubungakanani bengqokelela yethala leencwadi, amanye amathala eencwadi anokusebenzisa iinkqubo zokuhlela kuphela injongo enye okanye enye. Kwiimeko ezigqithisileyo, ithala leencwadi likawonke-wonke elinengqokelela encinci linokusebenzisa nje inkqubo yokuhlela kwindawo yezibonelelo kodwa lingasebenzisi inkqubo yokuhlela izifundo ezintsonkothileyo. Endaweni yoko zonke izixhobo zinokufakwa kwiindidi ezininzi ezibanzi (uhambo, ulwaphulo-mthetho, iimagazini njl.njl.). Oku kwaziwa ngokuba "uphawu kunye nepaki" indlela yokuhlela, ebizwa ngokusesikweni "ukuhlelwa komdla womfundi".[19] 

Ukuthelekisa iinkqubo zokwahlulwa kwethala leencwadi 
Ngenxa yomahluko kubhalo, kwimbali, ekusetyenzisweni kobalo, kuluhlu lwamanani nakwimigangatho, iinkqubo zokuhlela zinokwahluka ngolu hlobo lulandelayo: 

Uhlobo lobhalo: Ubhalo lunokuba msulwa (oluquka amanani kuphela, umzekelo) okanye luxutywe (olubandakanya oonobumba namanani, okanye oonobumba, amanani, kunye nezinye iisimboli). 
Uvakaliso: Eli liqondo apho ubhalo lunokuvakalisa unxulumano phakathi kweekhonsepthi okanye ulwakhiwo. 
Nokuba bayayixhasa na iminemonikhi: Umzekelo, inani lama-44 kwinqaku le-DDC lihlala lithetha ukuba lichaphazela umba othile weFransi. Ngokomzekelo, kwi-Dewey classification 598.0944 inkxalabo "Iintaka eFransi", i-09 ibonisa ulwahlulo lwejografi, kwaye i-44 imele iFransi. 
Ukwamkela iindwendwe: Iqondo lenkqubo ekwazi ngayo ukwamkela izifundo ezitsha. 
Ubufutshane: Ubude benqaku lokuvakalisa ingcamango efanayo. 
Isantya sohlaziyo kunye nenqanaba lenkxaso: Iinkqubo ezingcono zokuhlela zihlala zijongwa rhoqo. 
Ukungqinelana 
nokuSebenzisa ngokulula

nqaku limalunga nodidi lomxholo wemidiya. Ngolunye usetyenziso, jonga iFiction (disambiguation). 
"Intsomi" iphinda iqondise apha. Kwiqela laseJamani, bona iFictional (ibhendi). 

Umzekeliso ovela kwinoveli kaLewis Carroll ka-1865 ka-Alice's Adventures kwi-Wonderland 

Eli nqaku lifuna ucaphulo olongezelelweyo lokuqinisekisa. Nceda uncede ukuphucula eli nqaku ngokongeza izicatshulwa kwimithombo ethembekileyo. Izixhobo ezingasetyenziswanga zinokucelwa umngeni kwaye zisuswe. 
Fumana imithombo yolwazi: "Fiction" - iindaba · amaphephandaba · iincwadi · isifundiswa · JSTOR (Agasti 2025) (Funda ukuba uwususa njani kwaye nini lo myalezo)
Intsomi ngawo nawuphi na umsebenzi woyilo, ikakhulu nawuphi na umsebenzi ochazayo, obonisa abantu, iziganeko, okanye iindawo ezithelekelelayo okanye ngeendlela ezithelekelelwayo.[1][2][3] Ngaloo ndlela imifanekiso eyintsomi ayivisisani nesibakala, imbali, okanye into enokwenzeka. Ngokwengqiqo eqhelekileyo emxinwa, amabali angeyonyaniso abhekiselele kumabali abhaliweyo akwiprozi – amaxesha amaninzi ngokukodwa iinoveli, iinoveli, namabali amafutshane.[4][5] Ngokubanzi ngakumbi, nangona kunjalo, intsomi ibandakanya amabali entelekelelo achazwa kuyo nayiphi na indlela, kubandakanywa kungekuphela nje imibhalo kodwa kunye nemidlalo yethiyetha ephilayo, iifilimu, iinkqubo zikamabonwakude, iidrama zikanomathotholo, iicomics, imidlalo yokudlala indima, kunye nemidlalo yevidiyo. 

Inkcazelo kunye nethiyori

Ithiyori yeLacuna kunye nokugxeka 
iSociologyMagazineUkwakhekaUlwimiUlwimiUncwadiUlwazi
Ngokuqhelekileyo, intsomi yomsebenzi ichazwa esidlangalaleni, ngoko ke abaphulaphuli balindele ukuba umsebenzi wentsomi ujike uye kwiqondo elikhulu okanye elingaphantsi kwihlabathi lokwenyani, endaweni yokubonisa umzekelo kuphela imifanekiso echanekileyo okanye abalinganiswa abangabantu bokwenyani.[6] Ngenxa yokuba intsomi ngokuqhelekileyo iqondwa njengengabambeleliyo kwihlabathi lokwenene, imixholo kunye nomxholo wencwadi entsonkothileyo, enjengokungathi yaye ihlobene njani nemiba okanye iziganeko zehlabathi zokwenene, ziyakwazi ukutolikwa.[7] Ekubeni iintsomi zisekwe ixesha elide kummandla woncwadi (intsomi ebhaliweyo ebhaliweyo), uphononongo olubanzi lwendalo, umsebenzi, kunye nentsingiselo yefiction kuthiwa yithiyori yoncwadi, kwaye ukutolikwa okucutheneyo kweetekisi ezithile zobuxoki kubizwa ngokuba kukugxeka koncwadi (kunye neeseti ezinjengokugxekwa kwefilimu kunye nokugxekwa kwethiyetha nazo sele zisekwe ixesha elide). Ngaphandle koqhakamshelwano lwehlabathi lokwenyani, eminye imisebenzi yentsomi inokubonisa abalinganiswa kunye neziganeko ngaphakathi komxholo wabo, zahluke ngokupheleleyo kwindalo ebonakalayo ebonakalayo: indawo yonke eyintsomi ezimeleyo. Ubugcisa bokuyila bokwakha ihlabathi lentelekelelo elinjalo laziwa njengolwakhiwo lwehlabathi.

Umgxeki woncwadi uJames Wood uthi "intsomi zombini i-artifice kunye ne-verisimilitude", nto leyo ethetha ukuba ifuna zombini izinto zokuyila kunye nenqanaba elithile elamkelekileyo lokukholelwa kubaphulaphuli bayo, [8] ingcinga ehlala ifakwe kwingcamango yembongi uSamuel Taylor Coleridge yokunqumamisa kwabaphulaphuli ngokuzithandela ukungakholelwa. Iimpembelelo zokufumana intsomi, kunye nendlela abaphulaphuli abatshintshwa ngayo ngolwazi olutsha abalufumeneyo, lufundwe kwiinkulungwane. Kwakhona, amathuba angeyonyani angenasiphelo ngokwawo abonisa ukungenzeki kokwazi ngokupheleleyo ubunyani, ngokuxhokonxayo ukubonisa iingcamango zentanda-bulumko, njengokuba kungabikho migaqo yokulinganisa ulwakhiwo lwenyani.[9] 

Iintsomi neziyinyani 
Iincwadi ezingeyonyani 
xa zithelekiswa nezingeyonyani Ngokwahlukileyo kumabali angeyonyani, abaqulunqi bamabali angeyonyani bathwala uxanduva lokunikezela ngolwazi (kwaye ngamanye amaxesha noluvo) olusekelwe kuphela kwimbali nakwinyani eyinyani. Ngaphandle kwembono yemveli yokuba intsomi kunye neyokwenyani zizichasi, eminye imisebenzi (ngokukodwa kwixesha langoku) iyawusitha lo mda, ngakumbi imisebenzi ewela phantsi kweentlobo ezithile zokubalisa amabali-kubandakanywa intsomi yasemva kwemini, into eyenzeka ngokuzenzekela,[10] okanye intsomi yokuyila efana neenoveli ezingezizo ezenyani kunye nee-docudramas-kunye nobuqhetseba bobuqhetseba bobuxoki. intsomi.[11] 

Ngaphaya koko, kwanemisebenzi emininzi yeentsomi idla ngokuba neempawu, okanye isiseko, inyaniso yohlobo oluthile, okanye inyaniso ngokwembono ethile. Umahluko phakathi kwezi zimbini unokuchazwa ngcono ngokwembono yabaphulaphuli, kuye lowo umsebenzi ungeyonyani ukuba abantu bayo, iisetingi, kunye neploti zibonwa ngokupheleleyo njengembali okanye ngokwenyani, ngelixa umsebenzi uthathwa njengentsomi ukuba uyatenxa kwinto eyinyani kuyo nayiphi na kwezo ndawo. Umahluko uqhubeka ufihliwe kukuqonda kwefilosofi, kwelinye icala, ukuba inyaniso inokubonakaliswa ngeendlela ezicingelwayo kunye nokwakhiwa, ngelixa, kwelinye icala, imisebenzi yentelekelelo inokuzisa iimbono ezintsha ezibalulekileyo, okanye izigqibo malunga, inyaniso kunye nenyani. 

Zonke iindidi zeentsomi zimema abaphulaphuli bazo ukuba baphonononge izimvo zokwenyani, imiba, okanye okunokwenzeka besebenzisa isicwangciso sentelekelelo ngenye indlela okanye basebenzise into efana neyenyani, nangona besahluka kuyo.[qaphela 1][qaphela 2] 

Intelekelelo xa ithelekiswa nenyani eyiyonyani.
Uhlobo lweambrela yefiction eqikelelwayo luphawulwa ngenqanaba elincinci lokubambelela kubantu bokwenyani okanye ababambekayo, iziganeko, okanye iindawo, ngelixa uhlobo lweambrela yefiction yokwenyani luphawulwa ngomgangatho omkhulu. Umzekelo, intsomi eqikelelwayo isenokubonisa ummandla wendalo wentelekelelo ngokupheleleyo okanye leyo apho imithetho yendalo ingasebenzi ngokungqongqo (kaninzi, uhlobo olungaphantsi lwentelekelelo). Okanye, ibonisa amaxesha embali yokwenyani, ngaphandle kokuba aqukunjelwe ngendlela ethelekelelwayo ngokupheleleyo okanye elandelwa ziziganeko ezikhulu ezitsha ezithelekelelwayo ngokupheleleyo (uhlobo lwembali eyenye). Okanye, ibonisa itekhnoloji engenakwenzeka okanye itekhnoloji edelela ukuqonda okanye izakhono zangoku zenzululwazi (uhlobo lwentsomi yenzululwazi). 

Ngokuchaseneyo, intsomi eyinyani ibandakanya ibali elinesetingi esisisiseko (ixesha kunye nendawo esehlabathini), eneneni, iyinyani kwaye iziganeko zayo zinokuthi zenzeke ngokukholelekayo kumxholo wehlabathi lokwenyani. Enye indidi yentsomi eyinyani yintsomi yembali, egxile kwiziganeko ezinkulu zokwenyani kunye namaxesha exesha elidlulileyo.[14] Iinzame zokwenza amabali azive enyanisekile kwizinto eziyinyani okanye ukuchaza ngokucacileyo iinkcukacha, kunye nentshukumo yobugcisa yenkulungwane ye-19 eyaqala ukuyikhuthaza ngamandla le ndlela, ibizwa ngokuba yinyani yoncwadi, ebandakanya ezinye zeencwadi zobuxoki nezingeyonyani. Ukubaliswa 

kwamabali 
Ulwazi oluthe vetshe: Imbali yoncwadi
Ukubaliswa kwamabali kukho kuzo zonke iinkcubeko zabantu, kwaye inkcubeko nganye ibandakanya izinto ezahlukeneyo zenyaniso kunye nentsomi ekubaliseni amabali. Iintsomi zamandulo zazinxulunyaniswa ngokusondeleyo nembali kunye neentsomi. Iimbongi zamaGrike ezinjengoHomer, uHesiod, noAesop zavelisa amabali angeyonyani awayebaliswa kuqala ngokubaliswa kwamabali omlomo aze emva koko abhalwe. Iprose fiction yaphuhliswa kwiGrisi yaMandulo, iphenjelelwa zizithethe zaseAsia naseYiphutha. Umsebenzi oyintsomi ocacileyo awuzange uqatshelwe njengowahlukileyo kumabali embali okanye asentsomini kude kube lixesha lobukhosi. Ingxelo yePlasmatic, ilandela abalinganiswa neziganeko eziyilwe ngokupheleleyo, yaphuhliswa ngedrama yakudala kunye neComedy eNtsha.[15] Olunye ulwakhiwo oluqhelekileyo phakathi kweentsomi zamandulo luthotho lweziganeko ezingaqhelekanga nezimangalisayo njengoko ababhali bokuqala bevavanya imida yokubhala iintsomi. Iintsomi zaseMilesi zazingumzekelo wokuqala wokubhalwa kweentsomi kwiGrisi yaMandulo nase-Itali. Njengoko ukubhalwa kwentsomi kuphuhliswa kwiGrisi yaMandulo, abalinganiswa abanokuthenjwa kunye neemeko ezibambekayo ziye zagxininiswa ukuze zinxibelelane ngcono nabaphulaphuli, kuquka izinto ezifana nezothando, ubusela, kunye nemisitho yenkolo. Uthando lobugorha lwaphuhliswa kwiYurophu yamaxesha aphakathi, lubandakanya izinto ezinxulumene nentelekelelo, kubandakanywa izinto ezingaphezu kwendalo kunye nobugorha. [16] 

Ulwakhiwo lwenoveli yangoku lwaphuhliswa nguMiguel de Cervantes kunye noDon Quixote ekuqaleni kwenkulungwane ye-17. Le noveli yaba yeyona nto iphambili kwiintsomi kwinkulungwane ye-18 neye-19. Babehlala benxulunyaniswa neengcamango zokuKhanya ezifana ne-empiricism kunye ne-agnosticism. Ubunyani buphuhliswe njengesimbo soncwadi ngeli xesha.[18] Iindlela ezintsha zosasazo ezininzi zaphuhliswa ngasekupheleni kwe-19th kunye nasekuqaleni kwenkulungwane yama-20, kubandakanywa neemagazini ezingeyonyani kunye nefilimu yokuqala. [19] Iintsomi ezisebenzisanayo zaphuhliswa ngasekupheleni kwenkulungwane yama-20 ngemidlalo yevidiyo. [20] 

Iingongoma 
Ulwazi oluthe vetshe: Inkcazo § Izinto ezisisiseko 
Imiba ethile esisiseko ichaza yonke imisebenzi yokubalisa, kuquka yonke imisebenzi yebali eliyintsomi. Oko kukuthi, onke amabali abandakanya izakhi zomlinganiswa, impixano, imo yokubalisa, isakhiwo, isimo kunye nomxholo. Abalinganiswa ngabantu abangaphakathi kumsebenzi webali, ungquzulwano luxinezeleko okanye ingxaki eqhuba iingcinga nezenzo zabalinganiswa, iindlela zokubalisa ziindlela ibali elidluliselwa ngazo ibali, amabali ayindlela elandelelanayo yeziganeko ebalini, iisetingi ziindawo ebali kuzo ngexesha kunye nendawo, kwaye imixholo yimiyalezo okanye utoliko olunzulu malunga nebali ekuyekwa ukuba abaphulaphuli balo baxoxe kwaye bacamngce ngalo. 

Iifomathi 
Ulwazi oluthe vetshe: Uluhlu lweendidi ezingeyonyani 

icandelo le-Fiction kwivenkile yeencwadi
Ngokwesithethe, intsomi ibandakanya iinoveli, amabali amafutshane, iintsomi, iintsomi, iintsomi, iintsomi, imibongo eyimbali nebalisayo, imidlalo (kuquka iiopera, umculo, iidrama, imidlalo yoonopopi neentlobo ngeentlobo zemidaniso yethiyetha). Nangona kunjalo, iintsomi zisenokuquka iincwadi ezihlekisayo, kunye neekhathuni ezininzi ezinoopopayi, iintshukumo zokumisa, i-anime, i-manga, iifilim, imidlalo yevidiyo, iinkqubo zikanomathotholo, iinkqubo zikamabonwakude (amabali ahlekisayo kunye nemidlalo yeqonga), njl. njl. 

I-Intanethi ibe nempembelelo enkulu ekudalweni nasekuhanjisweni kwebali elingeyonyani, ibuza ukuba ngabanakho ukukopisha njengesixhobo sokuqinisekisa ukuba iintlawulo zihlawulwa kubanini-copyright.[21] Kwakhona, amathala eencwadi edijithali afana neProjekthi Gutenberg enza ukuba imibhalo yesizinda soluntu ifumaneke lula. Ukudityaniswa kweekhompyutha zasekhaya ezingabizi mali ininzi, i-Intanethi, nobuchule babasebenzisi bayo bukhokelele kwiindlela ezintsha zamabali, njengemidlalo yekhompyutha esetyenziswayo okanye amahlaya enziwe ngekhompyutha. Iiforamu ezingenakubalwa zeentsomi zabalandeli zinokufumaneka kwi-intanethi, apho abalandeli abathembekileyo beendawo ezithile eziyintsomi benza kwaye basasaze amabali aphuma. I-intanethi iphinda isetyenziswe ekuphuhliseni i-blog fiction, apho ibali lihanjiswa ngeblogi mhlawumbi njenge-flash fiction okanye i-serial blog, kunye ne-fiction yokubambisana, apho ibali libhalwa ngokulandelelana ngababhali abahlukeneyo, okanye isicatshulwa sonke sinokuhlaziywa nabani na usebenzisa i-wiki. 

Ukubhalwa kwamabali angeyonyani  
Inqaku 
eliphambili: Intsomi yoncwadi
Inkcazo yebali loncwadi iyaphikiswana. Isenokubhekisa kuwo nawuphi na umsebenzi wentsomi kwifomu ebhaliweyo. Nangona kunjalo, kukho ezinye iinkcazo ezahlukeneyo, kubandakanywa nomsebenzi obhaliweyo wentsomi othi: 

awungeni kakuhle kuhlobo olumiselweyo (ngokuchaseneyo nento ebizwa ngokuba yintsomi), xa isetyenziswa njengeleyibhile yokuthengisa kurhwebo lwencwadi 
iqhutywa ngabalinganiswa kunokuba iqhutywa licebo 
ivavanya 
imeko yomntu 
esebenzisa ulwimi ngendlela yovavanyo okanye yombongo 
ithathwa njengobunzulu njengomsebenzi wobugcisa[22] imibhalo egqalwa ngokukhethekileyo njengohlobo lobugcisa.[23] Ngelixa iintsomi zoncwadi ngamanye amaxesha zigqalwa njengezona ziphakamileyo kunoncwadi oluyintsomi, ezi zimbini azihlukani, kwaye amanani oncwadi aphambili aqeshe iindidi zeentsomi zesayensi, iintsomi zolwaphulo-mthetho, ezothando, njl.njl., ukwenza imisebenzi yoncwadi. Ngaphaya koko, uphononongo lohlobo olungeyonyani luphuhliswe phakathi kwezemfundo kumashumi eminyaka akutshanje.[24]

Eli gama ngamanye amaxesha lisetyenziswa njengokulinganisa intsomi yoncwadi noncwadi. Ukuchaneka koku kuyaxoxwa. U-Neal Stephenson ucebise ukuba, ngelixa nayiphi na inkcazo iya kuba lula, kukho namhlanje umahluko wenkcubeko ngokubanzi phakathi koncwadi kunye nohlobo lweentsomi. Kwelinye icala ababhali boncwadi kule mihla basoloko bexhaswa ngabaxhasi, ngokuqeshwa eyunivesithi okanye kwiziko elifanayo, kunye nokuqhubekeka kwezikhundla ezilolo hlobo kumiselwa kungekuko ukuthengiswa kweencwadi kodwa ngokunconywa okugxekayo ngabanye ababhali boncwadi abasele bekho nabagxeki. Kwelinye icala, ucebisa ukuba, ababhali beentsomi bathanda ukuzixhasa ngokuthengisa iincwadi. [25] Nangona kunjalo, kudliwano-ndlebe, uJohn Updike wakhala ngelithi "udidi 'lweentsomi zoncwadi' luye lwavela mva nje ukuze luthuthumbise abantu abafana nam abasanda kubhala iincwadi, kwaye ukuba nabani na ufuna ukuzifunda, zoyikeka ngakumbi. ... Ndingumbhali wohlobo oluthile. Ndibhala intsomi yoncwadi, efana ne-chick6 lit [2] ". Ngokunjalo, kwi-Charlie Rose Show, waxoxa ngelithi eli gama, xa lisetyenziswa kumsebenzi wakhe, limthintele kakhulu kunye nolindelo lwakhe lwento enokuza kukubhala kwakhe, ngoko akayithandi ncam. Wacebisa ukuba yonke imisebenzi yakhe yeyoncwadi, kuba nje “ibhalwe ngamazwi”.[27]

Iintsomi zoncwadi zidla ngokubandakanya amagqabantshintshi ezentlalo, ukugxekwa kwezopolitiko, okanye ukucinga ngemeko yomntu.[28] Ngokubanzi, igxile "kwi-introspective, izifundo ezinzulu zabalinganiswa" zabalinganiswa "abanomdla, abantsokothileyo nabaphuhlisiweyo". [28] Oku kuchasene nohlobo lwentsomi apho iploti yeyona nto ixhalabisayo.[29] Ngokwesiqhelo kwintsomi yoncwadi kugxininiswa "kwibali langaphakathi" labalinganiswa abaqhuba iploti, kunye neentshukumisa ezineenkcukacha zokufumana "ukubandakanyeka ngokweemvakalelo" kumfundi.[ucaphulo olufunekayo] Isimbo soncwadi oluyintsomi sihlala sichazwa njenge "ebhalwe ngobuchule, iilyrical, kunye ... ngokwemaleko".[30] Ithoni yentsomi yoncwadi inokuba mnyama kunohlobo lwentsomi,[31] ngelixa isantya soncwadi sinokucotha kunentsomi edumileyo.[31] Njengoko uTerrence Rafferty ephawula, "iintsomi zoncwadi, ngokwendalo yazo, zizivumela ukuba zikhanye, zihlale kubuhle abalahlekileyo nokuba kusemngciphekweni wokuphulukana nendlela yazo".[32] 

Uhlobo lwentsomi 
Inqaku eliphambili: Intsomi yodidi 
Ngokusekelwe kwindlela echazwa ngayo intsomi yoncwadi, intsomi yoncwadi isenokuba yiseti (intsomi ebhaliweyo elungelelanisa uhlobo oluthile), okanye isichasi sayo: ileyibhile yokuvavanya intsomi ebhaliweyo equka inkcubeko edumileyo, njengobugcisa okanye ngokwengqondo engaphantsi kwenkcubeko ephezulu. Noxa kunjalo, intsomi idla ngokuqhekeka ibe ziindidi ezahlukeneyo: iindidi zeentsomi, ngalinye lahlulwe ngethoni ethile edibanisayo okanye isimbo; iseti yeendlela zokubalisa, ii-archetypes, okanye ezinye iitropes; umxholo wemidiya; okanye enye inqobo echaziweyo edumileyo. 

Intsomi yenzululwazi iqikelela okanye icingela ubugcisa obungeyiyo yokwenyani ngexesha lokudalwa komsebenzi: Inoveli kaJules Verne ethi Ukusuka Emhlabeni ukuya eNyangeni yapapashwa ngo-1865, kodwa ngo-1969 kuphela apho oosomajukujuku uNeil Armstrong kunye noBuzz Aldrin baba ngabantu bokuqala ukuhlala eNyangeni. 

Intsomi yembali ibeka abalinganiswa bentelekelelo kwiziganeko zokwenyani zembali. Kwinoveli yembali ye-1814 iWaverley, umlinganiswa oyintsomi kaSir Walter Scott u-Edward Waverley udibana nomntu osuka kwimbali, uBonnie Prince Charlie, kwaye uthatha inxaxheba kwidabi lasePrestonpans. Eminye imisebenzi yentsomi icingelwa kancinane okanye icingelwe ngokutsha ngokusekelwe kwibali elithile lantlandlolo eliyinyani, okanye ibhayografi eyakhiwe ngokutsha.[33] Ngokufuthi, kwanaxa ibali eliyintsomi lisekelwe kwisibakala, kusenokubakho ukongezelelwa nokuthatyathwe kwebali lokwenyani ukuze libe nomdla ngakumbi. Umzekelo nguTim O'Brien's The Things They Carried, uthotho lwamabali amafutshane ngo-1990 malunga neMfazwe yaseVietnam. 


Umfanekiso oqingqiweyo kaHarry Potter eLeicester Square, eLondon 
Imisebenzi yeFictional ebandakanya ngokucacileyo amandla angaphezu kwawemvelo, imilingo, okanye izinto ezingenakwenzeka ngokwenzululwazi zihlala zihlelwa phantsi kohlobo lwentelekelelo, kubandakanywa inoveli kaLewis Carroll ka-1865 kaAlice's Adventures eWonderland, kaJRR Tolkien's The Lord of the Rings, kunye nochungechunge lweJK Rowling kaHarry Potter.Abadali bentelekelelo ngamanye amaxesha bazisa izidalwa ezithelekelelwayo kunye nezidalwa ezinjengeedragons neefairies.[3]

Iindidi ngokubala kwamagama 
Iintlobo zebali elingeyonyani elibhaliweyo kwiprozi zahlulwa ngobude obunxulumeneyo kwaye zibandakanya: [34] [35] 

Ibali elifutshane: umda phakathi kwebali elifutshane elifutshane kunye ne-novella ayicacanga, [36] nangona ibali elifutshane liquka amagama angaphantsi kwe-7,500 i 
-Novella: ngokuqhelekileyo, i-17,500 ukuya kwi-40,00 yamagama ngobude; imizekelo ibandakanya i-Strange Case ka-Robert Louis Stevenson kaGqr Jekyll kunye noMnu Hyde (1886) okanye i-Heart of Darkness kaJoseph Conrad (1899) [37]

Inkqubo yokubhalwa kwe-fiction 
Inqaku eliphambili: Ukubhala okungeyonyani 
Ukubhala okungeyonyani yinkqubo apho umbhali okanye umdali avelisa umsebenzi ongeyonyani. Ezinye izinto zenkqubo yokubhala zinokucwangciswa kwangaphambili, ngelixa ezinye zinokuthi zenzeke ngokuzenzekelayo. Ababhali beentsomi basebenzisa iindlela ezahlukeneyo zokubhala kwaye banamagama ababhali abahlukileyo xa bebhala amabali aqwetyiweyo.[38] 

Ukuqikelelwa njengengqikelelo 
 
Kwifilimu ehlekisayo ka-1940 ethi The Great Dictator, umdlali weNgesi kunye nomlingisi ohlekisayo uCharlie Chaplin wabonisa i-eccentric despot Adenoid Hynkel, ecacileyo kubabukeli ngelo xesha njengenguqulelo eyintsomi ka-Adolf Hitler kunye neziganeko zokwenyani ezenzeka ngexesha leMfazwe yesibini yeHlabathi. 
Ukusetyenziswa kweziganeko zokwenyani okanye abantu bokwenyani njengempembelelo ethe ngqo yeziganeko zentelekelelo okanye abantu bentelekelelo kwaziwa ngokuba yintsomi. Imeko echaseneyo, apho ihlabathi elibonakalayo okanye ukuguquka kokwenyani kweziganeko kubonakala kuphenjelelwa yintsomi yexesha elidlulileyo, ngokuqhelekileyo kuchazwa ngebinzana elithi "ubomi bokuxelisa ubugcisa". Eli binzana lamva lidume ngokunxulunyaniswa nombhali we-Anglo-Irish fiction u-Oscar Wilde.[39]

Ukuguqulwa kweziganeko zokwenyani zibe yifomathi eyintsomi, oku kubandakanya ukumelwa okumangalisayo kweziganeko zokwenyani okanye abantu, kwaziwa njengokuyinyani, okanye, ngokumxinwa ngakumbi kwintsebenzo yembonakalo isebenza njengakwithiyetha nakwifilimu, ukulinganisa. Ngokutsho kwempapasho yezemfundo i-Oxford Reference, umsebenzi owenziwe ngale ndlela uya kuba "nengxelo esekelwe ngokuyinxenye okanye ngokupheleleyo kwinyani kodwa ibhalwe ngokungathi yintsomi" kangangokuba "[f] iidrama kunye nemidlalo yosasazo yolu hlobo ihlala ineleyibhile 'esekelwe kwibali lokwenyani'. Kuphando lwengqondo, ukuvavanya le nkqubo yinxalenye yezifundo zosasazo.[40] 

Imizekelo yefictionalization ebalaseleyo kubugcisa bokudala ibandakanya ezo zikwimeko eqhelekileyo yeMfazwe yeHlabathi yesiBini kwinkcubeko edumileyo kwaye ngokukodwa iinkokeli zamaNazi zaseJamani ezinjengoAdolf Hitler kwinkcubeko edumileyo kunye noReinhard Heydrich kwinkcubeko edumileyo. Umzekelo, umlingisi waseMelika kunye nomhlekisi uCharlie Chaplin ubonise i-eccentric despot Adenoid Hynkel kwifilimu ye-1940 ye-satirical ethi The Great Dictator. Umntu ongaguquguqukiyo, ongakrelekrele wenza iziganeko zokwenyani ukusuka kwiMfazwe yesibini yeHlabathi eyayiqhubeka ngelo xesha ngendlela eyabonisa abantu bobuFasi njengabangenangqondo kwaye balusizi. Uninzi lwabanye abantu abakhohlakeleyo baphefumlelwa ngokuthe ngqo kubantu bokwenyani ngelixa beneempawu ezingeyonyani, inkangeleko, imvelaphi, amagama, njalo njalo.


I-non-fiction (okanye infiction) nalo naluphi na uxwebhu okanye umxholo weendaba ozama, ngokholo oluhle, ukuhambisa ulwazi malunga nehlabathi lokwenene kuphela, kunokuba lusekelwe kwintelekelelo.[1] Iincwadi ezingezizo ezenyani ngokuqhelekileyo zijolise ekuboniseni izihloko ngokungakhethi cala ngokusekelwe kwimbali, inzululwazi, kunye nolwazi lobungqina. Nangona kunjalo, uluhlu oluthile olungeyonyani lungena kumhlaba oxhomekeke ngakumbi, kubandakanywa izimvo ezibambe ngokunyanisekileyo kwizihloko zehlabathi lokwenyani.[2] 

Ihlala ibhekisa ngokuthe ngqo ekubhalweni kweprozi, [3] intsomi yenye yeendlela ezimbini ezisisiseko ebalini nasekubaliseni amabali, ngokuchaseneyo nebali eliyintsomi, elizaliswe kakhulu ngabalinganiswa kunye neziganeko zentelekelelo.[1][4] Ababhali abangeyonyani banokubonisa izizathu kunye neziphumo zeziganeko, banokuthelekisa, bathelekise, bahlele, bahlele kwaye bashwankathele ulwazi, babeke iinyani ngokulandelelana okanye ngokulandelelana kweziganeko, bacinge kwaye bafikelele kwizigqibo malunga nezibakala, njl. Basenokusebenzisa iimpawu zembonakalo yegraphic, yesakhiwo neprintiweyo njengemifanekiso, iigrafu okanye iitshati, iidayagram, iiflowutshati, isishwankathelo, iiglosari, iibhari ezisecaleni, amaxesha, isiqulatho, imixholo, imixholwana, amagama abhalwe ngqindilili okanye akekelelweyo, imibhalo esemazantsi, iimephu, izalathisi, iilebhile, ii-captions, njl. njl. ukunceda abafundi bafumane ulwazi.[5] 

Ngelixa amabango athile kumsebenzi ongeyonyani anobungqina obunganyanisekanga, umbhali onyanisekileyo unenjongo yokuba nenyani ngexesha lokubhala. I-akhawunti engeyonyani ngumsebenzi wokumela isihloko ngokuchanekileyo, kwaye ihlala yahlukile kulo nakuphi na ukuqinisekiswa okuchaziweyo. 

Ukwahlula
Ubuninzi beendlela zokubalisa ezisetyenzisiweyo kwintsomi zicingelwa ukuba azifanelekanga ukuba zisetyenziswe kwizinto ezingezontsomi. Zisekho ngokukodwa kwimisebenzi emidala, kodwa zihlala zithulisiwe ukuze zingasitheli ulwazi olungaphakathi komsebenzi. Ubulula, ukucaca, kunye nokuthe ngqo zezinye zezona ngqwalasela zibalulekileyo xa kusenziwa into engeyonyani. Abaphulaphuli babalulekile kuwo nawuphi na umzamo wobugcisa okanye ochazayo, kodwa mhlawumbi kubaluleke kakhulu kwizinto ezingeyonyani. Kwibali eliyintsomi, umbhali ukholelwa ukuba abafundi baya kwenza iinzame zokulandela nokutolika ukuqhubela phambili komxholo ngokungangqalanga okanye owenziwe ngokungathanga ngqo, ngelixa ukuveliswa kweengxelo ezingeyonyani kunento yokwenza ngakumbi nokubonelela ngokuthe ngqo kolwazi. Ukuqonda usetyenziso olunokubakho ngabafundi kulo msebenzi kunye nolwazi lwabo olukhoyo lwesifundo zombini zisisiseko kwiincwadi ezingeyonyani ezisebenzayo. Phezu kwako nje ibango lenyaniso yenyaniso engeyonyani, ngokufuthi yimfuneko ukweyisela umfundi ukuba avumelane neengcamango yaye ngoko ke ingxoxo elungeleleneyo, eyondeleleneyo nesekelwe kwinkcazelo ebalulekileyo ibalulekile. Nangona kunjalo, imida phakathi kweentsomi nezingeyonyani isoloko imfiliba kwaye kuxoxwa ngayo, ngakumbi kwicandelo lebhayografi;[6] njengoko uVirginia Woolf watshoyo: “ukuba sicinga ngenyani njengento yokuqina okufana negraniti kunye nobuntu njengento engabambekiyo efana nomnyama kwaye ibonakalisa ukuba injongo yebhayografi kukudibanisa ezi zimbini zibe yingxaki enye, siya kuyidibanisa yonke loo mfuneko Andinakuzibuza enoba ababhali bobomi babantu, ubukhulu becala basilela kusini na ukuyicombulula.”[7] 

Ukuquka inkcazelo umbhali ayaziyo ukuba ayiyonyaniso kwiincwadi ezinjalo kudla ngokugqalwa njengokunganyaniseki. Sekunjalo, iindidi ezithile zeencwadi ezibhaliweyo zisenokuba yintsomi okanye ayiyonyani, njengeencwadi zokuzichaza, iileta, amanqaku eemagazini, kunye namanye amazwi omfanekiso. Nangona ubukhulu becala inye okanye enye, ukudityaniswa kwazo zombini kuyenzeka. Ezinye iintsomi zinokuquka izinto ezingezontsomi; I-semi-fiction yintsomi ephumeza inkitha yezinto ezingeyonyani,[8] (ezifana nenkcazo eyintsomi esekelwe kwibali lokwenyani). Ezinye izinto ezingeyonyani zinokubandakanya izinto ezicingelwayo ezingangqinwanga, ukuxhuzulwa, okanye ukucinga ngenjongo yokugudisa ibali, kodwa ukubandakanywa kobuxoki obusekuhleni kuya kuyijongela phantsi njengomsebenzi ongeyonyani. Amashishini apapashayo nawokuthengisa iincwadi ngamanye amaxesha asebenzisa igama elithi "ubugcisa obungeyonyani" ukwahlula imisebenzi enoncwadi okanye ingqondo egobileyo, ngokuchaseneyo nobuninzi bezifundo ezingezizo ezenyani. 

Umzobo bubugcisa obubonakalayo obusebenzisa isixhobo sokumakisha iphepha okanye omnye umphezulu one-dimensional, okanye umboniso wedijithali onjalo. Ngokwemveli, izixhobo ezisetyenziselwa ukwenza umzobo ziquka iipensile, iikhrayoni, kunye neepeni zeinki, ngamanye amaxesha zidibene. Izixhobo zanamhlanje ezingakumbi ziquka izitayile zekhompyuter ezineetafile zemizobo kunye neepadi zeemidlalo kwisoftware yokuzoba yeVR.

Isixhobo sokudweba sikhupha into encinci phezu komhlaba, sishiya uphawu olubonakalayo. Eyona nkxaso ixhaphakileyo yokuzoba liphepha, nangona kuye kwasetyenziswa ezinye izinto ezifana nekhadibhodi, ivellum, umthi, iplastiki, ufele, iseyile kunye nebhodi. Imizobo yethutyana inokwenziwa ebhodini okanye ebhodini emhlophe. Umzobo ibiyeyona ndlela ithandwayo nesisiseko yokubonakalisa uluntu kwimbali yoluntu. Yeyona ndlela ilula nesebenzayo yokunxibelelana ngezimvo.[1] Ukufumaneka okubanzi kwezixhobo zokuzoba kwenza umzobo ube yenye yezona zinto ziqhelekileyo zobugcisa. 

Ukongeza kwiifom zayo zobugcisa, umzobo usetyenziswa rhoqo kwimifanekiso yorhwebo, i-animation, i-architecture, ubunjineli kunye nomzobo wobugcisa. Umzobo okhawulezayo, okhululekileyo, ngokuqhelekileyo awujoliswanga njengomsebenzi ogqityiweyo, ngamanye amaxesha ubizwa ngokuba ngumzobo. Umzobi oqhelisela okanye osebenza ngomzobo wobugcisa usenokubizwa ngokuba ngumyili, umzobi, okanye umzobi.[2] 

Isishwankathelo 

uMadame Palmyre kunye neNja Yakhe, ngo-1897. 
Umzobo kaHenri de Toulouse-Lautrec yenye yezona ndlela zindala zokubonakaliswa komntu ngaphakathi kobugcisa obubonakalayo. Ngokuqhelekileyo ixhalabele ngokumakishwa kwemigca kunye nemimandla yethoni kwiphepha / ezinye izinto, apho ukubonakaliswa okuchanekileyo kwehlabathi elibonakalayo kubonakaliswe kumphezulu wendiza.[3] Imizobo yesiNtu yayiyimonochrome, okanye ubuncinci inombala omncinci, [4] ngelixa imizobo yale mihla yepensile enombala inokusondela okanye iwele umda phakathi komzobo nokupeyinta. Kwisigama saseNtshona, umzobo wahlukile kwipeyinti, nangona amajelo eendaba afanayo ehlala esetyenziswa kuyo yomibini imisebenzi. Imidiya eyomileyo, edla ngokunxulunyaniswa nomzobo, njengetshokhwe, ingasetyenziswa kwimizobo ye-pastel. Umzobo unokwenziwa ngolwelo oluphakathi, olugalelwe ngeebrashi okanye ngeepeni. Ukusebenzisa ibrashi yokuzoba kuxhaphake kakhulu kwaye nantsi ngakumbi inkqubo yokusebenzisa imigca kunye nokuqandusela, ebonakalisa into ethile njengomzobo. Iinkxaso ezifanayo nazo zinokusebenza zombini: ukupeyinta ngokubanzi kubandakanya ukusetyenziswa kwepeyinti elulwelo kwiseyile elungisiweyo okanye iiphaneli, kodwa ngamanye amaxesha umzobo ongaphantsi uzotywa kuqala kwaloo nkxaso inye. 

Umzobo ukholisa ukuphonononga, kugxininiswa kakhulu kuqwalaselo, ukusombulula iingxaki kunye nokwakheka. Umzobo uphinda usetyenziswe rhoqo ekulungiseleleni umzobo, uphazamisa ngakumbi ukuhlukana kwabo. Imizobo eyenzelwe ezi njongo ibizwa ngokuba yimizobo. 

Kukho iindidi ezininzi zokuzoba, ezibandakanya: 

umzobo womzobo 
wokuzoba 
i-doodling 
sketch 
freehand. 
Zininzi iindlela zokuzoba, ezinje: 

umzobo weline 
stippling 
shading 
entopic graphomania (indlela ye-surrealist apho amachaphaza enziwa kwiindawo zokungcola kwiphepha elingenanto lephepha, kwaye imigca yenziwa phakathi kwamachaphaza)
ukukhuphela (ukuzoba kwiphepha eligqamileyo, elifana nephepha lokukhuphela, ujikeleze ulwandlalo lweemilo esele zikhoyo ezibonakala ephepheni). 
Kwimimandla engaphandle kobugcisa, imizobo yobugcisa okanye izicwangciso zezakhiwo, oomatshini, iisekethe kunye nezinye izinto zidla ngokubizwa ngokuba "yimizobo" nangona zitshintshelwe kwenye indawo ngokuprinta. 

Imbali 
Kunxibelelwano 
Umzobo yenye yezona ndlela zindala zokuchazwa komntu, kunye nobungqina bobukho bayo ngaphambi konxibelelwano olubhaliweyo.[5] Kukholelwa ukuba umzobo wawusetyenziswa njengendlela ekhethekileyo yonxibelelwano phambi kokuyilwa kolwimi olubhaliweyo, [5] [6] yaboniswa yimveliso yemizobo yomqolomba kunye namatye malunga neminyaka engama-30,000 eyadlulayo (Ubugcisa bePaleolithic ePhezulu).[7] Le mizobo, eyaziwa ngokuba pictograms, izinto ezinemifanekiso kunye neengqikelelo abstract.[8] Imizobo kunye nemizobo eveliswe ngamaxesha e-Neolithic ekugqibeleni yenziwe isimbo kwaye yenziwa lula kwiinkqubo zesimboli (ukubhalwa kweproto) kwaye ekugqibeleni kwiinkqubo zokubhala zakwangoko. 

Kwimibhalo-ngqangi 
Ngaphambi kokuba kuxhaphake ukufumaneka kwephepha eYurophu, iimonki kwiimonki zaseYurophu zasebenzisa imizobo, mhlawumbi njengemizobo engaphantsi kwemibhalo-ngqangi ekhanyisiweyo kwivellum okanye yesikhumba, okanye njengomfanekiso wokugqibela. Ukuzoba sele kusetyenziswe kakhulu kwinkalo yenzululwazi, njengendlela yokufumanisa, ukuqonda kunye nengcaciso. 

Kwinzululwazi 
Inqaku eliphambili: Umzobo wobugcisa 

Galileo Galilei, iZigaba zeNyanga, 1609 okanye 1610, i-inki emdaka kunye nokuhlamba ephepheni. 208 × 142 mm. IThala leeNcwadi leSizwe elikumbindi (iFlorence), Gal. 48, abantu. 28r 
Ukuzoba imizobo yoqwalaselo yinxalenye ebalulekileyo yophando lwenzululwazi. 

Ngo-1609, isazi ngeenkwenkwezi uGalileo Galilei wachaza amanqanaba aguqukayo eVenus kunye namabala elanga ngemizobo yakhe yeteleskopu [9] Ngo-1924, ingcali yokwakheka komhlaba uAlfred Wegener wasebenzisa imizobo ukubonisa imvelaphi yamazwekazi.[9] 

Njengentetha yobugcisa 
Ukuzoba yenye yezona ndlela zilula zokubona iingcinga kunye nokubonakalisa ubuchule bomntu; ke ngoko ibibalasele kwihlabathi lobugcisa. Kuyo yonke imbali, umzobo wawuthathwa njengesiseko sokwenza umsebenzi wobugcisa.[10] Ekuqaleni, abazobi babesebenzisa baze baphinde basebenzise amacwecwe eplanga ukwenza imizobo yawo.[11] Emva kokufumaneka ngokubanzi kwephepha ngenkulungwane ye-14, ukusetyenziswa komzobo kubugcisa kwanda. Ngeli xesha, umzobo wawuqhele ukusetyenziswa njengesixhobo sokucinga kunye nophando, usebenza njengendawo yokufunda ngelixa amagcisa ayelungiselela umsebenzi wawo wokugqibela.[12][13] IRenaissance yeza nobugocigoci obukhulu kubuchule bokuzoba, ivumela amagcisa ukuba amele izinto ngokwenyani kunangaphambili, [14] kunye nokutyhila umdla kwijometri nakwifilosofi.[15]

Ukuveliswa kohlobo lokuqala olufumaneka ngokubanzi lokufota kwakhokelela ekutshintsheni kwemigangatho yobugcisa.[16] Ukufota kubonelele ngenye indlela ekuzobeni njengendlela yokumela ngokuchanekileyo iziganeko ezibonwayo, kwaye ukuziqhelanisa nokuzoba kwemveli kwanikwa ugxininiso oluncinane njengesakhono esiyimfuneko kumagcisa, ingakumbi kuluntu lwaseNtshona.[9] 

Amagcisa aqaphelekayo nabayili Umzobo 
wabaluleka njengohlobo lobugcisa ngasekupheleni kwenkulungwane ye-15, kunye namagcisa kunye nabakroli abanobuchule abafana no-Albrecht Dürer noMartin Schongauer (c. 1448–1491), umzobi wokuqala waseMantla owaziwa ngegama. USchongauer wavela e-Alsace, kwaye wazalelwa kusapho lwabakhandi begolide. UAlbrecht Dürer, inkosi yesizukulwana esilandelayo, wayekwangunyana womkhandi wegolide. [17] [18] 

IMizobo ye-Old Master ihlala ibonisa imbali yelizwe apho yaveliswa khona, kunye neempawu ezisisiseko zesizwe ngelo xesha. Ngenkulungwane ye-17 eHolland, ilizwe lamaProtestanti, phantse kwakungekho mizobo yonqulo, yaye, kungekho Kumkani okanye inkundla, inkoliso yobugcisa yayithengwa ngasese. Imizobo yembonakalo-mhlaba okanye imiboniso yohlobo yayisoloko ijongwa kungeyiyo imizobo kodwa njengemisebenzi yobugcisa egqityezelwe kakhulu. Imizobo yaseItali, nangona kunjalo, ibonisa impembelelo yobuKatolika kunye neCawa, eyadlala indima enkulu ekuxhaseni ubugcisa. Kuhlala kuyinyaniso okufanayo kwimizobo yesiFrentshi, nangona ngenkulungwane ye-17 imfundiso ye-French Classicism [19] yayithetha ukuba imizobo yayingaphantsi kweBaroque kunezinye ezikhululekileyo zaseItali, ezibonisa intshukumo enkulu.[20] 

Kwinkulungwane yama-20 iModernism yakhuthaza "imvelaphi yentelekelelo"[21] kwaye indlela yamagcisa athile ekuzobeni iye yaphelelwa yinto yokoqobo, engaqondakaliyo. Amagcisa adumileyo kwihlabathi afana noPablo Picasso, uAndy Warhol kunye noJean-Michel Basquiat bancede umngeni ubume bemeko, ngokuzoba kumbindi wokwenza kwabo, kwaye ngokufuthi ukutolika kwakhona ubuchule bemveli. [22] 

Imizobo ye-Basquiat yaveliswa ngeendlela ezininzi ezahlukeneyo, i-inki eninzi, ipensile, i-tip-tip okanye i-marker, kunye ne-oyile-stick, kwaye wazoba kuyo nayiphi na indawo efika esandleni, njengeengcango, iimpahla, iifriji, iindonga kunye nezigcina-ntloko ze-baseball.[23] 

Iinkulungwane ziye zavelisa i-canon yamagcisa aphawulekayo kunye nabayili bedrafti, ngamnye ngolwimi lwakhe olwahlukileyo lokuzoba, kubandakanywa: 

14th, 15th kunye ne-16th: uLeonardo da Vinci[24] • Albrecht Dürer • Hans Holbein the Younger • Michelangelo • Pisanello • Raphael 
17th: Claude Guestinos Gynhec • Rembrandt • Peter Paul Rubens • Pieter Saenredam 
18th: François Boucher • Jean-Honoré Fragonard • Giovanni Battista Tiepolo • Antoine Watteau
19th: Aubrey Beardsley • Paul Cézanne • Jacques-Louis David • Honoré Daumier • Edgar Degas • Théodore Géricault • Francisco Goya • Jean-Auguste-Dominique Ingres • Pierre-Paul Prud’hon • Odilon Redon • John Ruskin • Georges Seuratuse Henri Goyat 2 
Max Govanni Goya Beckmann • Jean Dubuffet • MC Escher • Arshile Gorky • George Grosz • Paul Klee • Oskar Kokoschka • Käthe Kollwitz • Alfred Kubin • André Masson • Alphonse Mucha • Jules Pascin • Pablo Picasso • Egon Schiele • Jean-Michel Basquiat • Jean-Michel Basquiat • UJean-Michel Basquiat • UJean-Michel Basquiat • UJean-Michel Basquiat • 
U -Andy Warhol 
ngombala okanye ophakathi kumphezulu womzobo. Uninzi lwemidiya yokuzoba inokuba yomile (umz. igraphite, ilahle, ipastel, Conté, silverpoint), okanye isebenzisa isinyibilikisi solwelo okanye isithwala (umakishayo, ipeni ne-inki). Iipensile ze-Watercolor zingasetyenziselwa ezomileyo njengeepensile eziqhelekileyo, emva koko zifakwe ngebrashi emanzi ukufumana iziphumo ezahlukeneyo zepeyinti. Kunqabile kakhulu, amagcisa azobe nge-inki engabonakaliyo (ehlala ihlanjululwe). Umzobo wentsimbi udla ngokusebenzisa isilivere okanye ilothe.[25] Okunqabe kakhulu ukusetyenziswa yigolide, iplatinam, ubhedu, ubhedu, ubhedu, kunye netinpoint. 

Iphepha liza kwiindidi ezahlukeneyo zobukhulu kunye neempawu, ukusuka kwibakala lephephandaba ukuya kumgangatho ophezulu kunye nephepha elixabisa kakhulu elithengiswa njengamaphepha ngamanye.[26] Amaphepha ayahluka ngokokwakheka, umbala, iasidi, namandla xa emanzi. Iphepha eligudileyo lilungile ekunikezeni iinkcukacha ezintle, kodwa iphepha elithi "toothy" ngakumbi ligcina imathiriyeli yokuzoba ngcono. Ngaloo ndlela imathiriyeli erhabaxa iluncedo ekuveliseni umahluko onzulu. 

Ushicilelo lweendaba kunye nephepha lokuchwetheza zinokuba luncedo xa uziqhelanisa kunye nemizobo erhabaxa. Iphepha lokulanda lisetyenziselwa ukulinga umzobo ogqityiweyo, kunye nokudlulisa uyilo ukusuka kwelinye iphepha ukuya kwelinye. Iphepha leCartridge luhlobo olusisiseko lwephepha lomzobo elithengiswa kwiipads. Ibhodi yeBristol kunye neebhodi ezinzima ezingenayo iasidi, ezihlala zinemiphetho egudileyo, zisetyenziselwa ukuzoba iinkcukacha ezintle kwaye azigqwethi xa kufakwe imidiya emanzi (inki, ukuhlamba). I-Vellum igudile kakhulu kwaye ifanelekile kwiinkcukacha ezintle kakhulu. Iphepha le-watercolor epholileyo linokuthanda umzobo we-inki ngenxa yobume bayo. 

Iphepha elingena-asidi, elikumgangatho ogciniweyo ligcina umbala walo kunye nobume bexesha elide kunephepha elisekelwe kwiplanga elifana nephepha leendaba, elijika libe tyheli kwaye libe brittle kwamsinyane. 

Izixhobo ezisisiseko yibhodi yokudweba okanye itafile, i-pencil sharpener kunye ne-eraser, kunye nomzobo we-inki, iphepha lokusula. Ezinye izixhobo ezisetyenziswayo yikhampasi yesangqa, irula, kunye neseti yesikwere. I-Fixative isetyenziselwa ukuthintela amanqaku epensile kunye nekhrayoni ekungcoleni. Iteyiphu yokuyila isetyenziselwa ukukhusela iphepha kumphezulu womzobo, kunye nokugquma indawo ukuyigcina ingenawo amanqaku ngempazamo, njengokutshizwa okanye izinto ezitshiziweyo kunye nokuhlamba. I-easel okanye i-slented table isetyenziselwa ukugcina umzobo kwindawo efanelekileyo, ngokuqhelekileyo i-horizontal ngaphezu kwendawo esetyenziselwa ukupeyinta. 

Ubuchwephesha

UAntoine Watteau, ubuchule beekhrayoni basetrois 
Phantse bonke abaqulunqi bedrafti basebenzisa izandla neminwe ukuze baqabe kumajelo eendaba, ngaphandle kwabantu abathile abakhubazekileyo abazoba ngomlomo okanye ngeenyawo zabo.[27] 

Ngaphambi kokusebenza kumfanekiso, igcisa lijonga indlela amajelo osasazo asebenza ngayo. Basenokuzama izixhobo zomzobo ezahlukeneyo kumaphepha okuqhelanisa ukumisela ixabiso kunye nokwakheka, kunye nendlela yokusebenzisa isixhobo ukuvelisa iziphumo ezahlukeneyo. 


U-Raphael, ufundela oko kwaba yi-Alba Madonna, kunye neminye imizobo 
Ukukhethwa komzobi wokudweba kuchaphazela ukubonakala komfanekiso. Imizobo yosiba yosiba neye-inki idla ngokuqandusela - amaqela emigca ehambelanayo.[28] Ukuqandusela kusebenzisa ukuqandusela kumacala amabini okanye ngaphezulu ahlukeneyo ukwenza ithowuni emnyama. Ukuqanduselwa okwaphukileyo, okanye imigca enekhefu phakathi, yenza iithowuni ezikhaphukhaphu - kunye nokulawula ukuxinana kwezikhefu kuphumeza ukuhlelwa kwethoni. I-Stippling isebenzisa amachaphaza ukuvelisa ithoni, ukuthungwa kunye nomthunzi. Ukuthungwa okwahlukeneyo kunokuphunyezwa ngokuxhomekeke kwindlela esetyenziswayo ukwakha ithoni.[29] 

Imizobo kwimidiya eyomileyo isoloko isebenzisa iindlela ezifanayo, nangona iipensile kunye neentonga zokudweba zinokufikelela ukuhluka okuqhubekayo kwithoni. Ngokuqhelekileyo umzobo uzaliswa ngokusekwe kwisandla esithandwa ngumzobi. Igcisa elisekunene lizoba ukusuka ekhohlo ukuya ekunene ukunqanda ukudyobha umfanekiso. Iirabha zinokususa imigca engafunekiyo, zikhanyise iithowuni, kwaye zicoce namanqaku alahlekileyo. Kumzobo womzobo okanye umzobo, imigca ezotyiweyo ihlala ilandela i-contour yesihloko, idala ubunzulu ngokujonga njengezithunzi eziphoswe kwisibane esikwindawo yegcisa. 

Ngamanye amaxesha igcisa lishiya icandelo lomfanekiso lingachukunyiswanga ngelixa ligcwalisa intsalela. Ubume bendawo yokugcinwa bunokupeyintwa nge-mask fluid okanye ukunqunyulwa kwifrisket kwaye kusetyenziswe kwindawo yokudweba, ukukhusela ubuso kumanqaku alahlekileyo kude kube yilapho imaski isusiwe. 

Enye indlela yokugcina icandelo lomfanekiso kukusebenzisa i-spray-on fixative kumphezulu. Oku kubamba izinto ezikhululekileyo ziqine ngakumbi ephepheni kwaye zithintele ukuba zingaqabi. Nangona kunjalo isipreyi sokulungisa siqhele ukusebenzisa imichiza enokwenzakalisa inkqubo yokuphefumla, ngoko ke kufuneka isetyenziswe kwindawo enomoya owaneleyo njengangaphandle. 

Obunye ubuchule kukuzoba umzobo apho umzobo ugqunywe ngegraphite okanye ilahle uze ucinywe ukwenza umfanekiso.[30] 

Ithoni 

Umfanekiso wepensile nguHenry Macbeth-Raeburn, ngokuqandusela kunye nomthunzi (1909) 
Ukufihla bubuchule bokutshintsha amaxabiso ethoni kwiphepha ukumela umthunzi wezinto kunye nokubekwa kwezithunzi. Ingqwalasela ecacileyo ekukhanyeni okubonakalisiweyo, izithunzi kunye neendawo eziphambili zingabangela uguqulelo oluyinyani lomfanekiso.

Ukudibanisa kusebenzisa isixhobo ukuthambisa okanye ukusasaza imivimbo yokuqala yokuzoba. Ukudibanisa kwenziwa ngokulula ngesixhobo esingazilungisi ngokukhawuleza, esifana negraphite, itshokhwe, okanye ilahle, nangona i-inki esandul’ ukugalelwa ingaxutywa, imanzi okanye yome, ngenxa yeziphumo ezithile. Ngomthunzi kunye nokudibanisa, umzobi unokusebenzisa isiphunzi sokudibanisa, izicubu, i-eraser edibeneyo, i-fingertip, okanye nayiphi na indibaniselwano yazo. Isiqwenga se-chamois siluncedo ekudaleni ukuthungwa okugudileyo, kunye nokususa izinto zokukhanyisa ithoni. Ithoni eqhubekayo inokufezekiswa ngegraphite kumphezulu ogudileyo ngaphandle kokuxubana, kodwa ubuchule bunobunzima, bubandakanya imivimbo emincinci esetyhula okanye e-oval enenqaku elithile elibuthuntu. 

Iindlela zokuthungatha ezikwazisa ukuthungwa kumzobo ziquka ukuqandusela kunye nokumisa. Uninzi lwezinye iindlela zivelisa ukuthungwa. Ukongeza kukhetho lwephepha, izinto zokudweba kunye nobuchule buchaphazela ukuthungwa. Ubume bunokwenziwa ukuba bubonakale buyinto eyinyani ngakumbi xa izotywe ecaleni kwendlela eyahlukileyo; i-texture erhabaxa ibonakala ngakumbi xa ibekwe ecaleni kwendawo exutywe kakuhle. Umphumo ofanayo unokufumaneka ngokuzoba amathoni ahlukeneyo ngokusondeleyo. Ungqameko olukhanyayo ecaleni kwemvelaphi emnyama lugqamile kwiliso, kwaye phantse lubonakala ludada ngaphezulu komphezulu. 

Isalathiso kunye nomgangatho wokukhanya kudlala indima ebalulekileyo kwi-shading, echaphazela ubunzulu kunye nobukhulu bomzobo. Ukuqonda indlela ukukhanya okuhlangana ngayo neendawo ezahlukeneyo kunceda amagcisa enze ingqiqo yokwenyani, nokuba anikezela ngemathiriyeli egudileyo, ebonakalisayo okanye erhabaxa, i-matte textures. Ukujonga iimeko zokukhanya kwelizwe lokwenyani kunye nokuziqhelanisa nobomi kunokuphucula isakhono segcisa lokuzoba izithunzi eziqinisekisayo kunye neempawu ezibalaseleyo. 

Ukongeza, iindlela eziphambili zokuthungatha, ezinje nge-cross-hatching kunye ne-scrubling, zivumela ulawulo olukhulu kutshintsho lwetoni kunye neenkcukacha zomhlaba. Ukuqandusela okunqamlezileyo kubandakanya ukwahlula imigca enqamlezayo ukwakha ubunzulu kunye nethoni, ngelixa ukukrazula kusebenzisa imivumbo esetyhula okanye ekroliweyo ukwenza i-shading ethambileyo, ephilayo. Ezi ndlela, xa zidityaniswe ngokucokisekileyo ukudibanisa kunye nesicelo sokuthungwa, zibonelela abaculi ngezixhobo zezixhobo eziguquguqukayo zokuphumeza uluhlu lwemiphumo, ukusuka kwii-gradients ezithambileyo ukuya kwi-bold, i-contrast-contrast compositions. 

Imo kunye nobungakanani 

Ubungakanani bomzimba womntu 
Ukulinganisa imilinganiselo yesifundo ngelixa ubhloka kumzobo linyathelo elibalulekileyo ekuveliseni uguqulelo oluyinyani lwesifundo. Izixhobo ezifana nekhampasi zinokusetyenziswa ukulinganisa iiengile zamacala ahlukeneyo. Ezi engile zinokuphinda ziveliswe kumphezulu womzobo kwaye emva koko zihlolwe kwakhona ukuze kuqinisekiswe ukuba zichanekile. Olunye uhlobo lomlinganiselo kukuthelekisa ubungakanani obunxulumeneyo bamacandelo ahlukeneyo esifundo enye kwenye. Umnwe obekwe kwindawo ecaleni kwesixhobo somzobo unokusetyenziselwa ukuthelekisa loo mlinganiso kunye namanye amalungu omfanekiso. Irula inokusetyenziswa kokubini njengesixhobo sokulinganisa kunye nesixhobo sokubala imilinganiselo.


Ukwahluka ngokobungakanani nobudala 
Xa uzama ukuzoba imilo entsonkothileyo efana nomzobo womntu, kuyanceda ekuqaleni ukumela ifom kunye nesethi yemithamo yamandulo. Phantse naluphi na uhlobo lunokumelwa yindibaniselwano ethile yetyhubhu, ingqukuva, isilinda, kunye necone. Nje ukuba le miqulu yesiseko idityaniswe ibe ngumfanekiso, ngoko umzobo unokucokiswa ube yifomu echaneke ngakumbi necolisiweyo. Imigca yemithamo yamandulo iyasuswa kwaye ithatyathelwe indawo yokufana kokugqibela. Ukuzoba ulwakhiwo olusisiseko sisakhono esisisiseko sobugcisa bokumela, kwaye sifundiswa kwiincwadi ezininzi nakwizikolo. Usetyenziso lwayo oluchanekileyo lusombulula ukungaqiniseki okuninzi malunga neenkcukacha ezincinci, kwaye lwenza umfanekiso wokugqibela ubonakale uhambelana.[31] 

Ubugcisa obucokiseke ngakumbi bomzobo buxhomekeke kwigcisa elinokuqonda okunzulu kwe-anatomy kunye nobungakanani bomntu. Umculi oqeqeshiweyo uqhelana nesakhiwo samathambo, indawo edibeneyo, ukufakwa kwemisipha, ukunyakaza kwe-tendon, kunye nendlela amacandelo ahlukeneyo asebenza ngayo ngexesha lokuhamba. Oku kuvumela igcisa ukuba linikezele ngeemizo zendalo ezingabonakali ziqinile. Igcisa likwaqhelene nendlela imilinganiselo eyahluka ngayo ngokuxhomekeke kwiminyaka yomxholo, ngakumbi xa izoba umfanekiso. 

Umbono 
Inqaku eliphambili: Umbono 

Umzobo wembono eneengongoma ezimbini Umzobo wokujonga 
umgca yindlela yokuzoba izinto kumphezulu osicaba ukuze imilinganiselo icuthe ngomgama. Iseti nganye ehambelanayo, imiphetho ethe tye yayo nayiphi na into, nokuba sisakhiwo okanye itafile, ilandela imigca ethi ekugqibeleni idibane kwindawo yokunyamalala. Ngokuqhelekileyo le ndawo yokudibanisa ikwindawo ethile ecaleni kwe-horizon, njengoko izakhiwo zakhiwe kwinqanaba kunye nomphezulu osicaba. Xa izakhiwo ezininzi zilungelelaniswe enye kwenye, njengezakhiwo ecaleni kwendlela, imiphezulu ethe tye kunye nomzantsi wezakhiwo idla ngokudibana kwindawo yokunyamalala. 

Xa izotywe imiphambili namacala esakhiwo, ngoko ke imigca engqameneyo eyenza icala idibana kwindawo yesibini elundini (enokuthi isuke kwiphepha lomzobo.) Le yimbono yeengongoma ezimbini.[32] Ukuguqula imigca ethe nkqo ukuya kwindawo yesithathu ngaphezulu okanye ngaphantsi kwe-horizon emva koko ivelise imbono yeengongoma ezintathu. 


Igcisa lizoba umfanekiso ngokwembono yeworm's-eye
Ubunzulu bunokubonakaliswa ngeendlela ezininzi zobuchule ukongeza kwindlela yembono engentla. Izinto ezinobukhulu obufanayo kufuneka zibonakale zincinci kakhulu xa zisuka kumjongi. Ngaloo ndlela ivili langemva lenqwelo libonakala lincinci kunevili langaphambili. Ubunzulu bunokuzotywa ngokusetyenziswa kokuthungwa. Njengoko ubume bento busiya busiya buqina ngakumbi kwaye buxakekile, buthatha umlinganiswa owahluke ngokupheleleyo kunokuba bekufutshane. Ubunzulu bunokubonakaliswa ngokunciphisa umahluko kwizinto ezikude kakhulu, kunye nokwenza imibala yabo ihluthe. Oku kuvelisa kwakhona umphumo wenkungu ye-atmospheric, kwaye kubangela ukuba iliso ligxile ikakhulu kwizinto ezizotywe ngaphambili. 

Ukuqulunqa 

Umzobo wophononongo onamagqabantshintshi amhlophe nguWilliam-Adolphe Bouguereau 
Ukubunjwa komfanekiso yinto ebalulekileyo ekuveliseni umsebenzi onomdla wobuchule bobugcisa. Igcisa licwangcisa ukubekwa kwento kubugcisa ukunxibelelana ngezimvo kunye neemvakalelo kunye nombukeli. Ukuqulunqwa kunokumisela ugxininiso lobugcisa, kwaye kubangele yonke into ehambelanayo ekhangayo kwaye ivuselele. 

Ukukhanya komxholo kukwayinto ephambili ekudaleni isiqwenga sobugcisa, kwaye ukuhlangana kokukhanya nesithunzi yindlela exabisekileyo kwibhokisi yesixhobo somzobi. Ukubekwa kwemithombo yokukhanya kunokwenza umahluko omkhulu kuhlobo lomyalezo oziswayo. Imithombo yokukhanya emininzi inokuhlamba nayiphi na imibimbi ebusweni bomntu, umzekelo, kwaye inike inkangeleko yobutsha. Ngokwahlukileyo, umthombo omnye wokukhanya, njengokukhanya kwemini enzima, unokusebenza ukugqamisa naluphi na uhlobo okanye iimpawu ezinomdla. 

Xa uzoba into okanye umzobo, umzobi onobuchule unikela ingqalelo kuyo yomibini indawo engaphakathi kwe-silhouette kunye nento elele ngaphandle. Umphandle ubizwa ngokuba yindawo engafanelekanga, kwaye inokubaluleka kakhulu kumboniso njengomfanekiso. Izinto ezibekwe ngasemva komzobo kufuneka zivele zibekwe ngokufanelekileyo naphi na apho zinokujongwa khona. 

Uphononongo yidrafti yomzobo owenziwe ukulungiselela umfanekiso wokugqibela ocwangcisiweyo. Izifundo zingasetyenziselwa ukumisela ukubonakala kwamacandelo athile omfanekiso ogqityiweyo, okanye ukuzama indlela engcono yokufezekisa injongo yokugqibela. Nangona kunjalo isifundo esenziwe kakuhle sinokuba yinto yobugcisa ngokufanelekileyo, kwaye iiyure ezininzi zomsebenzi ocokisekileyo unokuhamba ukugqiba isifundo. 

Inkqubo 

Ibhinqa eliselula lizoba iBarberini Faun eMunich 
Abantu babonisa umahluko kubuchule babo bokuvelisa imizobo echanekileyo ebonwayo,[33] xa umzobo ochanekileyo obonwayo "uqondwa njengento ethile ngexesha elithile nakwindawo ethile, enikezelwa ngokongezwa okuncinci kweenkcukacha ezibonakalayo ezingenakubonwa kwinto emeleyo okanye ngokucinywa okuncinci kweenkcukacha ezibonakalayo."[34]

Izifundo zophando zijolise ekuchazeni izizathu zokuba kutheni abanye abantu bezoba ngcono kunabanye. Olunye uphononongo lubeke izakhono ezine ezingundoqo kwinkqubo yokuzoba: izakhono zemoto ezifunekayo ekwenziweni kwamanqaku, imbono yedrowa yomzobo wabo, ingqiqo yezinto ezizotywayo, kunye nokukwazi ukwenza izigqibo ezifanelekileyo zokumela.[34] Ukulandela le ngcamango, uphando oluninzi luye lwafuna ukugqiba ukuba yeyiphi na le nkqubo ibaluleke kakhulu ekuchaphazela ukuchaneka kwemizobo. 


Inkqubo yokuzoba kwiSifundo seSifundo seTorso eyindoda nguJean-Auguste-Dominique Ingres (1801, iMyuziyam yeSizwe, iWarsaw) 
Ulawulo 
lweMoto Ulawulo lwemoto luyinxalenye ebalulekileyo yomzimba 'kwiSigaba soMveliso' senkqubo yokuzoba.[35] Kuye kwacetyiswa ukuba ulawulo lwemoto ludlala indima kwisakhono sokuzoba, nangona iziphumo zalo azibalulekanga.[34] 

Ukuqonda 
Kuye kwacetyiswa ukuba ukukwazi komntu ukubona into ayizobayo lelona nqanaba libalulekileyo kwinkqubo yokuzoba.[34] Esi siphakamiso sixhaswa kukufunyaniswa kobudlelwane obuqinileyo phakathi kokuqonda kunye nokukwazi ukuzoba.[36] 

Obu bungqina busebenza njengesiseko sencwadi kaBetty Edwards yokuzoba, uMzobo kwicala lasekunene leBrain. [37] U-Edward wayejonge ukufundisa abafundi bakhe indlela yokuzoba, ngokusekelwe kuphuhliso lwezakhono zokuqonda zomfundi. 

Ngapha koko, igcisa elinempembelelo kunye nomgxeki wobugcisa uJohn Ruskin wagxininisa ukubaluleka kwembono kwinkqubo yokuzoba kwincwadi yakhe ethi The Elements of Drawing. [38] Wathi, "Kuba phantse ndiqinisekile, ukuba xa sibona ngokucokisekileyo ngokwaneleyo, kuncinci kakhulu kunzima ukuzoba oko sikubonayo." 

Inkumbulo ebonwayo 
Oku kukwabonakaliswe ukuphembelela isakhono somntu sokwenza imizobo echanekileyo ngokubonayo. Inkumbulo yexesha elifutshane idlala indima ebalulekileyo ekuzoba njengoko ukujonga komntu kukutshintsha phakathi kwento ayizobayo kunye nomzobo ngokwawo.[39] 

Ukwenziwa kwezigqibo 
Ezinye izifundo ezithelekisa amagcisa namagcisa angengawo amagcisa afumanise ukuba amagcisa achitha ixesha elininzi ecinga ngobuchule ngelixa ezoba. Ngokukodwa, amagcisa achitha ixesha elingakumbi kwimisebenzi 'ye-metacognitive' enjengokuthathela ingqalelo izicwangciso ezahlukeneyo zengqikelelo malunga nendlela abanokuqhubela phambili ngayo ngomzobo. 

Ifoto (ekwaziwa ngokuba yifoto, okanye ekubhekiselwa kuyo ngokubanzi njengomfanekiso okanye umfanekiso) ngumfanekiso owenziwe kukukhanya okuwela kumphezulu othatha ifoto, ngokuqhelekileyo ifilimu yezithombe okanye i-electronic sensor sensor. Inkqubo kunye nesenzo sokwenza imifanekiso enjalo ibizwa ngokuba yifoto. 

Uninzi lweefoto ngoku zenziwe kusetyenziswa i-smartphone okanye ikhamera, esebenzisa i-lens ukujolisa amaza okukhanya abonakalayo kwindawo ekuveliswe kuyo into enokubonwa liliso lomntu. 

I-Etymology
Igama elithi ifoto layilwa ngo-1839 nguMhlekazi uJohn Herschel kwaye lisekelwe kwigama lesiGrike elithi φῶς (phos), elithetha "ukukhanya," kunye no-γραφή (graphê), elithetha "ukuzoba, ukubhala," kunye elithetha "ukuzoba 
ngokukhanya 

. 
" inkqubo eyenziwe nguNicéphore Niépce. Iifoto zokuqala zomboniso wehlabathi lokwenyani, ezenziwe kusetyenziswa ikhamera obscura, zalandelwa kwiminyaka embalwa kamva eLe Gras, eFransi, ngowe-1826, kodwa inkqubo kaNiépce yayingenabuntununtunu ngokwaneleyo ukuba ibe nokwenzeka kweso sicelo: ukutyhilwa kwekhamera okuhlala iiyure okanye iintsuku kwakufuneka.[2] Kwi-1829, u-Niépce wangena kwintsebenziswano kunye noLouis Daguerre, kwaye bobabini basebenzisana ukuze basebenze inkqubo efanayo, kodwa enovelwano ngakumbi, kunye nolunye oluphuculweyo. 
Ukujonga kwiWindow eLe Gras, ngo-1826 nguJoseph Nicéphore Niépce 
Emva kokusweleka kukaNiépce nge-5 kaJulayi 1833 [3], uDaguerre wagxila kwiindlela ezizezinye ezisekelwe kwisilivere. Uveze icwecwe lobhedu elicwecwe ngesilivere kumphunga we-iodine, esenza umaleko we-iodide yesilivere ebuthathaka ukukhanya; wayityhila kwikhamera imizuzu embalwa; iphuhlise isiphumo somfanekiso ofihlakeleyo ongabonakaliyo ukuba ubonakale ngomphunga wemekyuri; emva koko wahlamba ipleyiti kwisisombululo setyuwa eshushu ukususa iodide yesilivere eseleyo, ukwenza iziphumo zikhanyiswe ngokukhawuleza. Wayibiza ngegama lakhe le nkqubo yokuqala yokwenza iifoto ngekhamera, i<em>daguerreotype. Ubukho bayo babhengezwa kwihlabathi nge-7 kaJanuwari 1839, kodwa iinkcukacha zokusebenza azizange zenziwe esidlangalaleni de kube yi-19 Agasti ngaloo nyaka. Abanye abavelisi bakhawuleza benza uphuculo olukhulu oluye lwanciphisa inani elifunekayo lexesha lokuvezwa ukusuka kwimizuzu embalwa ukuya kwimizuzwana nje embalwa, okwenza ukuba ukufota kusebenze ngokwenene kwaye kudume ngokubanzi ngeli xesha.



I-daguerreotype yayineziphene, ngokukodwa ubuthathaka bomfanekiso onjengesipili kunye neemeko ezithile zokujonga ezifunekayo ukuze ubone umfanekiso ngokufanelekileyo. Nganye yayinobuhle obungafaniyo, obucacileyo obunokuphindaphindwa kuphela ngokuyikopa ngekhamera. Abaqambi bamisela iinkqubo eziphuculweyo eziya kuba luncedo ngakumbi. Ekupheleni kweminyaka yee-1850, i-daguerreotype yayithatyathelw' indawo yi-ambrotype kunye ne-tintype ebonakala lula, eyathi yasebenzisa inkqubo ye-collodion eyayisandul' ukuqaliswa. Glass plate collodion negatives ezisetyenziselwa ukwenza ushicilelo kwiphepha albumen ngokukhawuleza yaba yindlela ekhethwayo yokufota kwaye wabamba eso sikhundla iminyaka emininzi, nasemva kokuba kusungulwe inkqubo gelatin elula ngakumbi ngo 1871. Ukulungiswa kwenkqubo gelatin ziye zahlala inkqubo yokufota ephambili emnyama-namhlophe ukuza kuthi ga namhlanje, ezahlukeneyo ngokuyintloko kubuntununtunu bezinto emulsion esetyenziswayo, nto leyo eguquguqukayo iglasi yenkxaso esetyenziswayo yiplastiki yeplastiki. iifilimu, kunye neendidi ezahlukeneyo zamaphepha oshicilelo lokugqibela. 


I-Market Square yase-Helsinki, ngeminyaka yee-1890 
ukufota ngemibala iphantse yandala njengomnyama-nomhlophe, kunye nemifuniselo yangaphambili equka ushicilelo lwe-Anthotype ka-John Herschel ngo-1842, umsebenzi wobuvulindlela kaLouis Ducos du Hauron ngeminyaka yee-1860s, kunye nenkqubo ye-Lippmann eyatyhilwa ngo-1891, kodwa iminyaka emininzi yahlala incinci i-curioratory coloratory. Kwaqala ukuba yinyani yorhwebo olubanzi kunye nokuqaliswa kweeplati ze-Autochrome kwi-1907, kodwa iiplati zazibiza kakhulu kwaye azifanelekanga ukuthabatha i-snapshot-i-snapshot engavamile kunye neekhamera ezibanjwe ngesandla. Embindini we-1930s yabona ukuqaliswa kwe-Kodachrome kunye ne-Agfacolor Neu, iifilimu zokuqala zemibala ekulula ukuyisebenzisa zohlobo lwanamhlanje lwe-chromogenic. Ezi nkqubo zangaphambili zavelisa izinto ezibonisa elubala ukuze zisetyenziswe kwiiprojekti zesilayidi kunye nezixhobo zokubukela, kodwa ukuprintwa kombala kuye kwanda ukuduma emva kokwaziswa kwephepha loshicilelo lombala wechromogenic ngeminyaka yoo-1940. Iimfuno zeshishini lemifanekiso eshukumayo zenze inani leenkqubo ezikhethekileyo kunye neenkqubo, mhlawumbi eyona nto iyaziwa ngokuba yinkqubo yeTechnicolor enemicu emithathu ephelelwe lixesha. 

Iindidi zeefoto 

Ifoto ebonisa ixesha elide yeTelesikophu Enkulu Kakhulu[4] 
Iifoto ezingezizo ezedijithali zenziwe ngenkqubo yekhemikhali enamanyathelo amabini. Kwinkqubo yamanyathelo amabini, ifilimu ekhanyayo ibamba umfanekiso ongalunganga (imibala kunye nezibane / ubumnyama buguqulwa). Ukuvelisa umfanekiso olungileyo, i-negative idla ngokugqithiselwa ('printed') kwiphepha lokufota. Ukushicilela okungalunganga kwisitokhwe sefilim ekuhleni kusetyenziswa ukwenza iifilimu zemifanekiso eshukumayo.

Kungenjalo, ifilimu icutshungulwa ukuze iguqule umfanekiso ongalunganga, ivelise ukubonakala okucacileyo. Imifanekiso emihle enjalo idla ngokufakwa kwizakhelo, ezibizwa ngokuba zizilayidi. Phambi kwenkqubela phambili yamva nje yokufota kwedijithali, ii-transparencies zazisetyenziswa ngokubanzi ziingcali ngenxa yobukhali kunye nokuchaneka kokunikezelwa kombala. Uninzi lweefoto ezipapashwe kwiimagazini zithathwe kwifilimu ebonisa umbala. 

Ekuqaleni, zonke iifoto zaziyi-monochromatic okanye zipeyintwe ngesandla ngombala. Nangona iindlela zokuphuhlisa iifoto zemibala zazifumaneka kwangethuba ngo-1861, azizange zifumaneke ngokubanzi de kwaba ngoo-1940 okanye ngoo-1950, kwaye nangona kunjalo, de kwaba ngoo-1960, uninzi lweefoto zathathwa zimnyama namhlophe. Ukusukela ngoko, ukufota ngemibala kuye kwalawula ukufota okudumileyo, nangona kusasetyenziswa umbala omnyama nomhlophe, kuba kulula ukuyiphuhlisa kunombala. 

Imifanekiso yefomathi yepanoramic inokuthatyathwa ngeekhamera ezifana neHasselblad Xpan kwifilimu eqhelekileyo. Ukusukela ngeminyaka yee-1990s, iifoto zepanoramic bezifumaneka kwifilimu ekwiNdlela yeeFoto eziPhezulu (APS). I-APS yaphuhliswa ngabavelisi abaninzi beefilim ukuze babonelele ngefilim enefomathi ezahlukeneyo kunye nokhetho lwekhompyuter olufumanekayo, nangona iipanorama ze-APS zenziwe kusetyenziswa imaski kwiikhamera ezikwaziyo ukuxhobisa, kude kakhulu kunqweneleka kunekhamera yepanoramic yokwenyani, ephumeza isiphumo sayo ngefomathi yefilimu ebanzi. I-APS iye yangathandwa kakhulu kwaye iyekisiwe. 

Ukufika kwe-microcomputer kunye neefoto zedijithali kuye kwakhokelela ekunyukeni kweeprinta zedijithali. Olu shicilelo lwenziwa ngokugcinwa kwiifomati zegraphic ezifana neJPEG, TIFF, kunye neRAW. Iindidi zabashicileli abasetyenziswayo ziquka abashicileli be-inkjet, abashicileli bedayi-sublimation, abashicileli belaser, kunye nabashicileli be-thermal. Iiprinta ze-Inkjet ngamanye amaxesha zinikwa igama elidityanisiweyo "Giclée". 

IWebhu ibiyeyona ndlela idumileyo yokugcina nokwabelana ngeefoto ukusukela oko ifoto yokuqala yapapashwa kwiwebhu nguTim Berners-Lee ngo-1992 (umfanekiso weqela lendlu le-CERN iLes Horribles Cernettes). Namhlanje, iisayithi ezidumileyo ezifana neFlickr, PhotoBucket, kunye ne500px zisetyenziswa zizigidi zabantu ukwabelana ngemifanekiso yabo. 

Eyokuqala "selfie", okanye self-portrait, yathathwa Robert Cornelious emva 1839 [5]. "IiSelfies" ziye zaba zezona foto zixhaphakileyo, ngakumbi phakathi kwabasetyhini abancinci. Imidiya yoluntu iye yaba yinkqubela phambili yenkcubeko ngenxa yokufota. Abantu bayaphumelela kwii-selfies zabo badumileyo abadumileyo, abaninzi bafumana izigidi zokuthandwa kumajelo eendaba ezentlalo ngenxa ye-selfie enye elula. 
Iifolda zePhepha 

lokuGcina
Ugcino lweefoto olufanelekileyo lubandakanya ukubeka ifoto nganye kwisiqulathi seefayili somntu ngamnye esakhiwe nge-buffered, okanye iphepha elingenayo iasidi.[6] Iifolda zephepha ezithintelweyo zicetyiswa ngokukodwa kwiimeko apho ifoto ibifakwe ngaphambili kwizinto ezikumgangatho ophantsi okanye kusetyenziswa into encamathelayo eya kukhokelela ekudalweni kweasidi engakumbi.[7] Gcina iifoto ezinomlinganiselo we-intshi ezi-8x10 okanye ezincinci ngokuthe nkqo ecaleni komphetho omde wefoto kwifolda yephepha elikhuselweyo, ngaphakathi kwebhokisi enkulu yokugcina izinto, kwaye uleyibhelishe ifolda nganye ngolwazi olufanelekileyo ukuyichonga. Ubume obuqinileyo befolda bukhusela ifoto ekuthotyweni okanye ekuqhekekeni, ukuba nje ibhokisi ayipakishwanga kakhulu okanye igcwaliswe ngaphantsi. Iifoto ezinkulu zefolda okanye iifoto ezibhityileyo zipakishwe mcaba ngaphakathi kweebhokisi zoovimba kunye nezinye izinto ezinobungakanani obunokuthelekiswa.[8] 

Iindawo ezivaliweyo zepolyester
Iiplastiki ezizinzile kakhulu ezisetyenziselwa ukugcinwa kweefoto, i-polyester, ayivelisi nayiphi na imichiza eyingozi, kwaye ayinakho ukukwazi ukufunxa i-acids eveliswa yifoto ngokwayo. Imikhono yePolyester kunye ne-encapsulation iye yanconywa ngokukwazi kwabo ukukhusela ifoto kumswakama kunye nongcoliseko lokusingqongileyo, ukunciphisa ukusabela phakathi kwento kunye nomoya. Oku kuyinyani, nangona kunjalo i-polyester ibamba rhoqo ezi zinto ecaleni kwesixhobo esijolise ukuyikhusela. Oku kuyingozi ngakumbi kwindawo yokugcina efumana ukuguquguquka okukhulu kokufuma okanye ubushushu, okukhokelela kwi-ferrotyping, okanye ukuncamathela kwefoto kwiplastiki.[6] Iifoto ezinemikhono okanye ezifakwe kwi-polyester azikwazi ukugcinwa ngokuthe nkqo kwiibhokisi kuba ziya kutyibilika ecaleni komnye nomnye ngaphakathi kwebhokisi, ukugoba nokusonga, kwaye umgcini wogcino-zincwadi akanakubhala ngokuthe ngqo kwi-polyester ukuchonga ifoto. Ngoko ke, kuyimfuneko ukupakisha iifoto ezikhuselweyo zepolyester ngokuthe tye ngaphakathi kwebhokisi, okanye uzibophe kwi-binder ezintathu zeringi. Ukupakisha iifoto ngokuthe tye ngaphakathi kwebhokisi esicaba kuya kunciphisa kakhulu ukufikelela lula, kwaye izibophelelo zishiya amacala amathathu efoto evezwe kwiziphumo zokukhanya[9] kwaye aziyixhasi ifoto ngokulinganayo macala omabini, ekhokelela ekuweni kunye nokugoba ngaphakathi kwesibophelelo. Iplastiki esetyenziselwa ukuvaleka iye yaveliswa ukuba ingakhubeki kangangoko ukuthintela ukukrwela iifoto ngexesha lokufakwa kwimikhono. Ngelishwa, ubume obumtyibilizi bendawo ebiyelweyo buvelisa ukwakhiwa kombane ongatshintshiyo, otsala uthuli kunye namasuntswana e-lint. I-static inokutsalela uthuli ngaphakathi komkhono, ngokunjalo, apho inokukrwela ifoto.[6] Ngokunjalo, ezi zixhobo zinceda ekufakeni ifoto, ezibizwa ngokuba zii-slip agents, zinokuqhekeka kwaye zitshintshe ukusuka kwiplastiki ukuya kwifoto, apho zifaka khona njengefilimu eneoyile, zitsala umsonto kunye nothuli. Ngeli xesha, akukho luvavanyo lokuvavanya iziphumo zexesha elide zala macandelo kwiifoto. Ukongeza, imikhono yeplastiki inokuphuhlisa i-kinks okanye i-creases ebusweni, eya kukhupha i-emulsion ngexesha lokuphatha. 

Ukuphatha kunye nokunyamekela
Kungcono ukushiya iifoto zithe tyaba etafileni xa uzibukele. Musa ukuyichola ekoneni, okanye kumacala amabini kwaye uyibambe kwinqanaba lamehlo. Ngalo lonke ixesha ifoto igoba, nokuba kuncinci, oku kunokophula i-emulsion.[10] Ubume bokuvala ifoto kwiplastiki ikhuthaza abasebenzisi ukuba bayichole; abasebenzisi badla ngokuphatha iifoto zeplastiki ezivalelweyo ngobunono kuneefoto ezingavalwanga, kuba beva ukuba indawo ebiyelweyo yeplastiki yenza ukuba ifoto ingakwazi ukuphathwa kakubi. Logama nje ifoto ikwifolda yayo, akukho mfuneko yokuba uyichukumise; susa ngokulula incwadi esuka kwibhokisi, yibeke tyaba phezu kwetafile, kwaye uvule incwadi eneenkcukacha. Ukuba ngenxa yesizathu esithile abaphandi okanye abagcini bezinto zakudala kufuneka baphathe ifoto yokwenyani, mhlawumbi ukujonga i-verso yokubhala, banokusebenzisa iiglavu ukuba kukho umngcipheko ovela kwioyile okanye ukungcola ezandleni. 

Iintsomi kunye neenkolelo 
Bona kwakhona: I-Aniconism 
Ngenxa yokuba ii-daguerreotypes zanikezelwa kwindawo yesipili, abantu abaninzi bezomoya baye baba ngabasebenzi bolu hlobo lutsha lobugcisa. Iingcali zomoya zinokuthi umfanekiso womntu kwindawo yesipili wawufana nokujonga emphefumlweni womntu. Abakholelwa kwimimoya nabo babekholelwa ukuba iya kuyivula imiphefumlo yabo kwaye ivumele iidemon ukuba zingene. Phakathi kwamanye amaSilamsi, yi-makruh (engathandwa) ukwenza i-salah (unqulo) kwindawo ehonjiswe ngeefoto.[11] Ukufota kunye nokungahambi kakuhle kwegumbi elimnyama kunye nezinto ezenziweyo ngamanye amaxesha zikhokelela ababukeli ukuba bakholelwe ukuba imimoya okanye iidemon zifakwe kwiifoto. Abanye baye benza umsebenzi wabo ngokuthatha imifanekiso “yeziporho” okanye “imimoya”.[12] Kukho iimeko ezininzi apho abantu bakholelwa ukuba iifoto ziya kuzisa amashwa kumntu othatha umfanekiso okanye abantu abafakwe kwifoto. Ngokomzekelo, umfanekiso othatyathiweyo womfazi okhulelweyo uya kuzisa amashwa kusana olusesibelekweni kwaye iifoto ezithathwe ngabantu abafileyo ziya kuqinisekisa ukuba loo mntu akaphumeleli kubomi basemva kokufa.[13] 

Umthetho 
Inqaku eliPhambili: Ukufota kunye nomthetho 
Ukuveliswa okanye ukusasazwa kweentlobo ezithile zeefoto akuvumelekanga phantsi kwemithetho yanamhlanje, njengaleyo yezakhiwo zikarhulumente, [14] imimandla ehlelwe kakhulu,[15] ipropati yabucala, imisebenzi enelungelo lokushicilela,[16][17] amalungu angasese abantwana, [18] iphonografi yabantwana kunye nephonografi engaxhaphakiyo xa iyonke.[19] Le mithetho yahluka kakhulu phakathi kwamagunya.

Kwezinye iindawo zikawonke-wonke eziphantsi kukarhulumente, ezifana neenkundla zomthetho,[20] izakhiwo zikarhulumente, amathala eencwadi, amaziko oluntu [21][22] kunye nezinye iimyuziyam eHong Kong, ukufota akuvumelekanga ngaphandle kwemvume evela kurhulumente. Akukho mthethweni ukuxhobisa okanye ukuthatha iifoto kunye nokurekhoda kwindawo yokuzonwabisa yoluntu, njengemiboniso bhanyabhanya kunye nethiyetha zangaphakathi. [23][24] E-Hungary, ukususela ngo-15 Matshi 2014 xa i-Code Civil Code yayilindelwe ixesha elide yapapashwa, umthetho waphinda wachaza into eyayiyinto eqhelekileyo, oko kukuthi, umntu unelungelo lokwala ukufotwa. Nangona kunjalo, imvume echaziweyo ikhona: akukho mthethweni ukufota umntu ongachasi ngokusebenzayo. [25][26] 

EMzantsi Afrika ukufota abantu esidlangalaleni kusemthethweni.[27] Ukuvelisa kwakhona kunye nokuthengisa iifoto zabantu kusemthethweni ukulungiselela ukuhlelwa kunye nosetyenziso olulinganiselweyo olufanelekileyo lweenjongo zorhwebo. Akukho mthetho wetyala wokuchaza ukuba yeyiphi imida ekusetyenzisweni kwezorhwebo. EUnited Kingdom akukho mithetho ithintela ukufotwa kwempahla yabucala kwindawo kawonke-wonke.[28] Ukufota okuzingisileyo kunye nobundlongondlongo yomntu omnye kunokuba phantsi kwenkcazelo yomthetho yokuxhatshazwa.[29][30][31][32] Ilungelo lokuba neemfihlo libekho kumthetho wase-UK ngenxa yokudityaniswa kweNgqungquthela yaseYurophu yamaLungelo oLuntu kumthetho wasekhaya ngoMthetho wamaLungelo oLuntu ka-1998. Oku kunokukhokelela kwizithintelo zokupapashwa kokufota. 

Umculo weshiti yindlela ebhalwe ngesandla okanye eprintiweyo yokubhalwa komculo esebenzisa iisimboli zomculo ukubonisa iipitshi, izingqisho, okanye iichords zengoma okanye isixhobo somculo. Njengee-analogs zayo - iincwadi eziprintiweyo okanye iincwadana zesiNgesi, isiArabhu, okanye ezinye iilwimi - indlela yomculo wamaphepha idla ngokuba liphepha (okanye, kwiinkulungwane zangaphambili, ipapyrus okanye isikhumba). Nangona kunjalo, ukufikelela kumanqaku omculo ukususela ngeminyaka yee-1980s kubandakanye ukuboniswa kwamanqaku kwizikrini zekhompyuter kunye nophuhliso lweenkqubo zekhompyuter zamanqaku anokuthi aphawule ingoma okanye isiqwenga nge-elektroniki, kwaye, kwezinye iimeko, "udlale umva" umculo ophawulweyo usebenzisa i-synthesizer okanye izixhobo ezibonakalayo. 

Ukusetyenziswa kwephepha lamagama kujoliswe ekwahluleni iintlobo zomculo ezibhaliweyo okanye ezishicilelweyo kwiirekhodi zesandi (kwiirekhodi zevinyl, iikhasethi, iCD), unomathotholo okanye umabonwakude okanye iinkqubo ezirekhodiweyo ezirekhodiweyo, ezinokuthi zifake ifilimu okanye ividiyo yevidiyo yomdlalo kunye necandelo le-audio. Kusetyenziso lwemihla ngemihla, umculo wephepha (okanye umculo nje) unokubhekisa kushicilelo olushicilelweyo lomculo weshiti lokuthengisa ngokubambisana nokukhutshwa kwefilimu entsha, umboniso weTV, icwecwe elirekhodiweyo, okanye esinye isiganeko esisodwa okanye esithandwayo esibandakanya umculo. Umculo wokuqala oshicilelweyo owenziwe ngomatshini wokushicilela wenziwa ngowe-1473.

Umculo wamaphepha luhlobo olusisiseko apho umculo weklasikhi waseNtshona uqatshelwa khona ukuze ufundwe kwaye uqhutywe ziimvumi ezizimeleyo, ii-instrumentalists okanye ii-ensembles zomculo. Iindidi ezininzi zomculo waseNtshona wesintu nowaziwayo ziqhele ukufundwa ziimvumi neemvumi "ngendlebe", endaweni yokusebenzisa umculo wamaphepha (nangona kwiimeko ezininzi, umculo wesintu kunye nowepop nawo unokufumaneka kuhlobo lomculo wamaphepha). 

Igama elithi amanqaku ligama eliqhelekileyo (kunye nelinye eliqhelekileyo) kumculo wephepha, kwaye kukho iindidi ezininzi zamanqaku, njengoko kuxoxwe ngazo ngezantsi. Igama elithi amanqaku linokubhekisa kumculo wethiyetha, umculo weokhestra okanye iingoma ezibhalelwe umdlalo, umculo, iopera okanye i-ballet, okanye kumculo okanye iingoma ezibhalelwe inkqubo kamabonakude okanye ifilimu; okokugqibela kwezi, bona iFilimu amanqaku. 

Elements 

Iphepha lesihloko lohlelo lokuqala lwezwi likaHector Berlioz's Béatrice et Bénédict 
Isihloko kunye 
nomculo weTyala leTyala ukusuka kwinkulungwane yama-20 kunye neyama-21 ubonisa isihloko sengoma okanye ukuqamba kwiphepha lesihloko, uqweqwe, okanye phezulu kwiphepha lokuqala xa kungekho phepha lahlukileyo lesihloko.
