Ukuba ingoma okanye isiqwenga sivela kwimuvi, umculo weBroadway, okanye i-opera, isihloko somsebenzi oyintloko apho ingoma / isiqwenga sithatyathwe kuwo sinokuboniswa. 

Ukuba umbhali wengoma okanye umqambi uyaziwa, igama labo liboniswa kunye nesihloko. Iphepha lomculo lingabonisa igama lombhali weengoma, ukuba amazwi abhalwa ngumntu ongenguye omnye wabaqambi beengoma okanye abaqambi. Isenokubandakanya igama lomququzeleli, ukuba ingoma okanye isiqwenga silungiselelwe ukupapashwa. Akukho mbhali weengoma okanye igama lomqambi elinokuthi liboniswe kumculo wesintu wakudala, iingoma zemveli kwiindidi ezinjengeblues kunye nebluegrass, kunye neengoma zakudala kakhulu kunye nezomoya, kuba kulo mculo, ababhali bahlala bengaziwa; kwiimeko ezinjalo, igama elithi "imveli" lihlala libekwe apho igama lomqambi lidla ngokuya khona. 

Amaphepha ezihloko zeengoma anokuba nomfanekiso obonisa abalinganiswa, iisetingi, okanye iziganeko kumazwi engoma. Amaphepha ezihloko asuka kumculo wezixhobo angawushiya umzekeliso, ngaphandle kokuba umsebenzi lowo ngumculo weprogram othi, ngesihloko okanye amagama ecandelo lawo, unxulumane nesetingi, abalinganiswa, okanye ibali. 

Ubhalo lomculo 
Uhlobo lwenowuthi yomculo yahluka kakhulu ngohlobo okanye isimbo somculo. Kuninzi lomculo weklasiki, uncuthu lwengoma kunye neenxalenye ezikhaphayo (ukuba zikhona) ziphawulwa kwimigca yabasebenzi abasebenzisa iintloko zeenowuthi ezingqukuva. Kumculo weklasiki, abasebenzi bakholisa ukuqulatha: 


Iphepha elisuka kumanqaku e-autograph ye- 
Fugue 
No. encinci
isignesha yexesha, edla ngokuba namanani amabini alungelelaniswe ngokuthe nkqo kunye nenani elisezantsi elibonisa ixabiso lenowuthi elimele ukubetha enye kunye nenani eliphezulu elibonisa ukuba zingaphi iibhithi ezikwi-bar-umzekelo, utyikityo lwexesha le-2 
4 lubonisa ukuba kukho amanqaku amabini ekota (crotchets) ngebha. 
Uninzi lweengoma kunye neziqwenga zexesha leClassical (c. 1750) ukuya phambili zibonisa itempo yesiqwenga kusetyenziswa intetho-ehlala isiTaliyane-njenge-allegro (ukukhawuleza) okanye ingcwaba (ecothayo) kunye nokuguquguquka kwayo (isandi okanye ukuthamba). Amazwi, ukuba akhona, abhalwa kufutshane namanqaku omculo. Nangona kunjalo, umculo weBaroque era (c. 1600–1750) okanye amaxesha angaphambili awunakuphawulwa ngokwetempo okanye umqondiso oguqukayo. Iimvumi kunye neemvumi zelo xesha bekulindeleke ukuba zazi ukuba yeyiphi itempo kunye nesandi sokudlala okanye ukucula ingoma okanye isiqwenga esinikiweyo ngenxa yamava kunye nolwazi lwabo lomculo. Kwixesha langoku lomculo weklasikhi (inkulungwane yama-20 neye-21), kwaye kwezinye iimeko ngaphambili (njengexesha le-Romantic kwimimandla ethetha isiJamani), abaqambi babehlala besebenzisa ulwimi lwabo lweenkobe kwiimpawu zetempo, kunokuba basebenzise isiTaliyane (umzekelo, ngokukhawuleza okanye i-schnell) okanye ukongeza amanqaku e-metronome (umzekelo, inqaku lekota = i-100 beats ngomzuzu). 

Le migaqo yobhalo lomculo weklasikhi, kwaye ngakumbi ukusetyenziswa kwemiyalelo yetempo yesiNgesi, ikwasetyenziselwa iinguqulelo zomculo wamaphepha eengoma zomculo ezidumileyo zenkulungwane yama-20 neye-21. Iingoma zomculo ezidumileyo zihlala zibonisa zombini itempo kunye nohlobo: iiblues ezicothayo okanye i-uptempo rock. Iingoma zepop zihlala zinamagama eechord ngaphezulu kwabasebenzi esebenzisa amagama oonobumba (umz., C Maj, F Maj, G7, njl. njl.), ukuze umdlali wegitare we-acoustic okanye umdlali wepiyano aphucule ukukhatshwa kweechord. 

Kwezinye iintlobo zomculo, iindlela ezahlukeneyo zokuphawula umculo zinokusetyenziswa. Kwi-jazz, umzekelo, ngelixa uninzi lwabadlali abaqeqeshiweyo bekwazi ukufunda ubhalo lwe-"classical" -style, iingoma ezininzi ze-jazz ziphawulwa kusetyenziswa iitshati ze-chord, ezibonisa ukuqhubela phambili kweculo (umz., C, A7, D minor, G7, njl.njl.) kunye nohlobo lwayo. Amalungu ecandelo le-jazz rhythm (umdlali wepiyano, isiginkci sejazi kunye nebhesi) basebenzisa itshati yeechord ukukhokela iinxalenye ezikhaphayo eziphuculweyo, ngelixa izixhobo ezikhokelayo kwiqela le-jazz, njengomdlali wesaxophone okanye ixilongo, zisebenzisa utshintsho lwechord ukukhokela uphuculo lwabo bebodwa. Njengeengoma zomculo ezidumileyo, iingoma zejazz zihlala zibonisa zombini itempo kunye nohlobo: iiblues ezicothayo okanye ibop ekhawulezayo.

Iimvumi zeseshini yomculo welizwe eliqeqeshiweyo zidla ngokusebenzisa umculo obhalwe kwiNashville Number System, ebonisa ukuqhubela phambili kwechord kusetyenziswa amanani (oku kwenza ukuba ababhendi batshintshe isitshixo ngesaziso somzuzwana). Iitshati zechord zisebenzisa amagama oonobumba, amanani, okanye amanani esiRoma (umz., I–IV–V) zikwasetyenziswa ngokubanzi ekuphawuleni umculo ngeeblues, iR&B, umculo werock kunye neemvumi zentsimbi enzima. Ezinye iitshathi ze-chord aziboneleli naluphi na ulwazi lwesingqisho, kodwa ezinye zisebenzisa i-slashs ukubonisa ukubetha kwebar kunye ne-rhythm notation ukubonisa "i-hits" edibeneyo ukuba umbhali wengoma ufuna ukuba yonke ibhendi idlale kunye. Abadlali begitare abaninzi kunye nabadlali be-bass bombane bafunda iingoma kunye neengoma zeenowuthi besebenzisa i-tablature, ebonisa umzobo apho umculi kufuneka adlale iifrits kunye neentambo. "I-Tab" isetyenziswa kakhulu ngumculo we-rock kunye neegitala zentsimbi enzima kunye nabadlali be-bass. Iimvumi kwiintlobo ezininzi zomculo ezidumileyo zifunda ingoma zisebenzisa iphepha lamagama kuphela, zifunde ingoma kunye nesingqisho "ngendlebe" ekurekhodweni. 

Injongo kwaye usebenzise 

icwecwe lomculo wengoma ethi "Oregon, My Oregon" 
Umculo wePhepha ungasetyenziswa njengerekhodi, isikhokelo, okanye indlela yokwenza, ingoma okanye isiqwenga somculo. Umculo wamaphepha uvumela abadlali bezixhobo abakwaziyo ukufunda ubhalo lomculo (umdlali wepiyano, umdlali weokhestra, iqela lejazz, njl.njl.) okanye iimvumi zicule ingoma okanye isiqwenga. Abafundi bomculo basebenzisa amaphepha omculo ukufunda ngezimbo ezahlukeneyo kunye neentlobo zomculo. Injongo ekujoliswe kuyo yohlelo lomculo weshiti ichaphazela uyilo kunye noyilo lwawo. Ukuba iphepha lomculo lenzelwe iinjongo zokufunda, njengakwiklasi yembali yomculo, amanqaku kunye nabasebenzi banokwenziwa bancinci kwaye umhleli akafuneki ukuba abe nexhala malunga nokujika kwamaphepha. Kumanqaku okusebenza, nangona kunjalo, amanqaku kufuneka afundeke kwindawo yomculo kwaye umhleli kufuneka aphephe ukujika okugqithisileyo kwephepha kwaye aqinisekise ukuba naliphi na iphepha elijikayo libekwe emva kokuphumla okanye ukunqumamisa (ukuba kunokwenzeka). Kwakhona, amanqaku okanye inxalenye kwincwadi eshinyeneyo ayisayi kuhlala ivulekile, ngoko ke amanqaku okusebenza okanye inxalenye kufuneka ibe kwisibophelelo esincinane okanye isebenzise ifomathi yokubophelela eya kulala evulekileyo kwindawo yomculo. 

Kumculo weklasiki, ulwazi lomculo olugunyazisiweyo malunga neqhekeza lunokufunyanwa ngokufunda imizobo ebhaliweyo kunye neenguqulelo zokuqala zeengoma ezinokugcinwa ngumqambi, kunye nenqaku lokugqibela le-autograph kunye nokumakishwa komntu kubungqina kunye namanqaku ashicilelweyo.

Ukuqonda umculo wephepha kufuna uhlobo olukhethekileyo lokufunda nokubhala: isakhono sokufunda amanqaku omculo. Ukukwazi ukufunda okanye ukubhala umculo akuyomfuneko xa uqamba umculo. Kubekho iqela labaqambi kunye nabaqambi beengoma abakwaziyo ukuvelisa umculo ngaphandle kwesakhono sokufunda okanye ukubhala ngophawu lomculo, okoko nje kukho i-amanuensis yohlobo oluthile lokubhala phantsi iingoma abacinga ngazo. Imizekelo iquka umqambi oyimfama wenkulungwane ye-18 uJohn Stanley kunye nababhali beengoma benkulungwane yama-20 uLionel Bart, uIrving Berlin noPaul McCartney. Kananjalo, kwizitayile zomculo wesintu ezifana nomculo weblues kunye nomculo wesintu, baninzi ababhali beengoma abaninzi abangakwaziyo ukufunda umculo, endaweni yoko badlale kwaye bacule umculo “ngendlebe”. 

Ubuchule bokufunda ngokubona kukukwazi kwemvumi ukwenza umsebenzi ongaqhelekanga womculo xa ijonga iphepha lomculo okokuqala. Isakhono sokufunda sokubona silindeleke kwiimvumi ezivunyiweyo kunye nabangabasafundanga nzulu abadlala umculo weklasiki, ijezi kunye nezinye iindlela ezinxulumene noko. Obona buchule buphuculwe ngakumbi kukukwazi ukujonga ingoma entsha nokuva uninzi okanye zonke izandi (iingoma, iingoma, iingoma, njl.njl.) entloko ngaphandle kokudlala ingoma okanye ukuyiva idlalwa okanye iculwa. Abaqambi abanezakhono kunye nababhexeshi banalo buchule, kunye noBeethoven engumzekelo ophawulekayo wembali. 


Amanqaku omqhubi kunye ne-baton 
Iimvumi zeClassical ezidlala iiokhestra, umculo wegumbi, i-sonatas kunye nokucula imisebenzi yekwayala ngokuqhelekileyo inomculo wephepha phambi kwabo kwindawo yokuma yomculo xa kudlalwa (okanye kubanjwe phambi kwabo kwifolda yomculo, kwimeko yekwayara), ngaphandle komculo we-solo we-solo, iikonsathi, iingoma, i-opera, iingoma, njl njl. kulindeleke. Kwi-jazz, ephuculwe kakhulu, umculo weshiti (obizwa ngokuba yi-lead sheet kulo mxholo) usetyenziswa ukunika imiqondiso esisiseko yeengoma, utshintsho lwechord, kunye namalungiselelo. Nokuba iqela lomculo wejazz linecwecwe elikhokelayo, itshati yeechodi okanye umculo ocwangcisiweyo, izinto ezininzi zentsebenzo ziyaphuculwa. 

Umculo obhalwe ngesandla okanye oshicilelweyo awubalulekanga kangako kwezinye izithethe zomculo. Nangona kunjalo, kwiindidi ezinjengomculo wesintu kunye nomculo wesintu, iimvumi kunye nezixhobo zomculo ngokuqhelekileyo bafunda iingoma "ngendlebe" okanye ekubeni nengoma okanye ingoma abayifundiswa ngomnye umntu. Nangona umculo omninzi odumileyo upapashwa ngendlela ethile, kuyinto eqhelekileyo ukuba abantu bafunde ingoma beyiva. Oku kunjalo nakwiintlobo ezininzi zomculo wesintu waseNtshona, apho iingoma kunye nemidaniso idluliswa ngomlomo - kunye nesithethe - isithethe. Umculo wezinye iinkcubeko, owomthonyama kunye noweklasikhi, uhlala usasazwa ngomlomo, nangona ezinye iinkcubeko ezingezizo ezaseNtshona zavelisa iindlela zazo zomculo kunye nomculo weshiti ngokunjalo.

Nangona umculo wephepha uhlala ucingelwa njengeqonga lomculo omtsha kunye nokunceda ekuqulunqeni (oko kukuthi, umqambi "ubhala" umculo phantsi), unokusebenza njengerekhodi elibonakalayo lomculo osele ukhona. Abaphengululi kunye nabanye baye benza ushicilelo ukuze banike umculo waseNtshona kunye nongewona waseNtshona ngendlela efundekayo yokufunda, ukuhlalutya kunye nokusebenza kwakhona kokuyila. Oku akwenziwanga kuphela ngomculo wesintu okanye wesintu (umzekelo, imiqulu kaBartók yomculo wesintu waseMagyar nowaseRomania), kodwa nangesandi esirekhodiweyo sophuculo lweemvumi (umzekelo, ipiyano yejazz) kunye nemidlalo enokuthi isekelwe ngokuyinxenye kuphela kumanqaku. Umzekelo opheleleyo wale yokugqibela kumaxesha amva nje yingqokelela ethi The Beatles: Complete Scores (London: Wise Publications, 1993), efuna ukuguqulela kwizibonda kwaye icwecwe zonke iingoma njengoko zirekhodwe ziiBeatles ngezixhobo nangelizwi. 

Iintlobo 
Umculo wephepha langoku unokuza kwiifomathi ezahlukeneyo. Ukuba iculo liqulunqwe ngesixhobo esinye okanye ilizwi elinye (njengecwecwe lesixhobo somculo esithetha umntu omnye okanye i-cappella solo voice), wonke loo msebenzi unokubhalwa okanye uprintwe njengomculo omnye. Ukuba isixhobo somculo senzelwe ukwenziwa ngabantu abangaphezu komnye, umdlali ngamnye uya kuba necwecwe lomculo elahlukileyo, elibizwa ngokuba yinxalenye, anokuwudlala. Oku kunjalo ngakumbi kupapasho lweencwadi ezifuna abadlali abangaphezu kwabane, nangona ngokungaguquguqukiyo amanqaku apheleleyo apapashwa ngokunjalo. Iinxalenye eziculwa kumsebenzi wezwi azidli ngokukhutshwa ngokwahlukeneyo kwindlela yanamhlanje, nangona oku bekunjalo ngokwembali, ngakumbi ngaphambi kokuba ukushicilelwa komculo kufumaneke ngokubanzi. 

Umculo wephepha unokukhutshwa njengeziqwenga zomntu okanye imisebenzi (umzekelo, ingoma ethandwayo okanye i-Beethoven sonata), kwiiqoqo (umzekelo usebenza ngumqambi omnye okanye abaninzi), njengeziqwenga ezenziwe ngumculi onikwe, njl 

. Ngokwesiqhelo, amanqaku aqulathe ubhalo lomculo kunye nesixhobo ngasinye okanye indawo yelizwi kulungelelwaniso oluthe nkqo (okuthetha ukuba iziganeko ezifanayo kubhalo lwenxalenye nganye zicwangciswe ngokuhambelanayo). Igama elithi amanqaku likwasetyenziswe ukubhekisa kumculo wephepha obhalelwe umdlali omnye kuphela. Umahluko phakathi kwamanqaku kunye nenxalenye usebenza xa kukho ngaphezu kwenxalenye enye efunekayo ekusebenzeni. 

Amanqaku aza kwiifomathi ezahlukeneyo. 


Iphepha lokuqala lamanqaku apheleleyo eMax Reger's Der 100. Indumiso yekwayala, iokhestra kunye neorgan 
Amanqaku apheleleyo, ukwahluka, kunye nocondensations
Amanqaku apheleleyo yincwadi enkulu ebonisa umculo wazo zonke izixhobo okanye amazwi abhalwe ngendlela emiselweyo. Inkulu ngokwaneleyo ukuba umbhexeshi akwazi ukufunda ngoxa esalathisa iiokhestra okanye uqheliselo lweopera. Ukongeza kusetyenziso lwabo olubonakalayo kubaqhubi abakhokela iindibano, amanqaku apheleleyo akwasetyenziswa ziingcali zomculo, iithiyori zomculo, abaqambi kunye nabafundi bomculo abafunda umsebenzi othile. 

Amanqaku amancinci afana namanqaku apheleleyo kodwa ancitshiswe kakhulu ngobukhulu. Incinci kakhulu ukuba ingasetyenziswa kumqhubi wesifundo, kodwa iluncedo ekufundeni isiqwenga somculo, nokuba leleensemble enkulu okanye umntu ocula yedwa. Amanqaku amancinci angaqulatha amagqabaza ayintshayelelo. 

Amanqaku ophononongo ngamanye amaxesha anobukhulu obufanayo, kwaye kaninzi awahluki, amanqaku amancinci, ngaphandle kwegama. Amanye amanqaku ophononongo abukhulu be-octavo kwaye ke akwindawo ethile phakathi kobukhulu obupheleleyo kunye nobukhulu bamanqaku amancinci. Amanqaku okufunda, ngakumbi xa eyinxalenye ye-anthology yokufunda, angabandakanya amagqabantshintshi angaphezulu malunga nomculo kunye nokumakishwa kweenjongo zokufunda. 

Inqaku lepiyano (okanye ukuncitshiswa kwepiyano) lukhutshelwe ngokuthe ngqo okanye olungaphantsi lwepiyano yesiqwenga esilungiselelwe iindawo ezininzi ezenziwayo, ngakumbi imisebenzi yeokhestra; oku kunokubandakanya amacandelo asebenzayo phakathi kwemisebenzi emikhulu yezwi (jonga amanqaku elizwi ngokukhawuleza ngezantsi). Amalungiselelo anjalo enzelwe nokuba ipiyano solo (izandla ezibini) okanye ipiyano duet (piyano enye okanye ezimbini, izandla ezine). Izibonda ezincinci ezongezelelweyo ngamanye amaxesha zongezwa kwiindawo ezithile kumanqaku epiyano kwizandla ezibini ukwenza iprezenteyishini igqibeke ngakumbi, nangona kudla ngokungenzeki okanye kungenzeki ukuqukwa xa udlala. 

Njengakwinqaku lezwi (ngezantsi), kuthatha ubuchule obuninzi ukunciphisa inqaku leokhestra ukuya kwiifom ezincinci ngolo hlobo ngenxa yokuba ukuncipha kufuneka kungadlali kuphela kwikhibhodi kodwa ngokucokisekileyo ngokwaneleyo ekuboniseni kwayo ii-harmonies ezicetywayo, ukuthungwa, imifanekiso, njl. 

Ngelixa amanqaku epiyano awafane asenzelwa ukusebenza ngaphandle kokufunda kunye nolonwabo (imibhalo kaFranz Liszt yekhonsathi yeesymphonies zikaBeethoven ibe liqela elinye lezinto eziphawuleka kakhulu), ii-ballet zifumana inzuzo ebonakalayo kumanqaku epiyano kuba ngepiyano enye okanye ezimbini zivumela i-ballet ukuba yenze iziqhelaniso ezininzi ngexabiso eliphantsi kakhulu, ngaphambi kokuba ihlaziywe okanye ihlaziywe. Amanqaku epiyano nawo angasetyenziselwa ukuqeqesha abaqhubi abaqalayo, abanokuqhuba umdlali wepiyano odlala ukucuthwa kwepiyano yesimfoni; oku kubiza kancinci kunokuqhuba iokhestra epheleleyo. Amanqaku epiyano eeopera azibandakanyi izibonda ezahlukeneyo zamalungu elizwi, kodwa anokongeza isicatshulwa esiculwayo kunye nezalathiso zeqonga ngaphezulu komculo.

Inxalenye kutsalwa kumanqaku apheleleyo esixhobo esithile. Isetyenziswa ngabadlali beokhestra ekusebenzeni, apho amanqaku apheleleyo anokuba nzima kakhulu. Nangona kunjalo, ekusebenzeni, inokuba luxwebhu olukhulu ukuba umsebenzi umde, kwaye isixhobo esithile sidlala ixesha elide. 


Isicatshulwa samanqaku epiyano-izwi le-opera kaCésar Cui uWilliam Ratcliff. Dlalaⓘ 
Amanqaku elizwi 
Amanqaku elizwi (okanye, ngokufanelekileyo, ipiyano-inqaku lelizwi) kukucuthwa kwamanqaku apheleleyo omsebenzi wezwi (umzekelo, iopera, umculo, ioratorio, icantata, njl. njl.) ukubonisa amalungu elizwi (eyedwa kunye nekwayala) kwizibonda zabo kunye namalungu eokhestra kunciphiso lwepiyano (idla ngokuba ngamalungu elizwi eliphantsi kwezandla zozibini); amacandelo eokhestra kuphela amanqaku nawo ayancitshiswa kwipiyano. Ukuba inxalenye yomsebenzi yi-cappella, ukucuthwa kwepiyano kwamalungu ezwi kudla ngokudityaniswa ukuze kuncedwe ukuphindaphinda (oku kudla ngokuba yimeko yomculo we-cappella wecawa). 

Amanqaku epiyano-izwi asebenza njengendlela efanelekileyo yokuba iimvumi ezicula yedwa kunye neekwayala zifunde umculo kwaye baziqhelise ngokwahlukileyo kwiokhestra. Amanqaku omculo ngokuqhelekileyo awabandakanyi incoko yababini ethethiweyo, ngaphandle kweengcebiso. Amanqaku epiyano-izwi asetyenziswa ukubonelela ngepiyano ekhatshwayo xa kudlalwa iioperas, umculo kunye neeoratorios ngamaqela abantu abafundayo kunye namaqela amancinci amancinci. Oku kunokwenziwa ngumdlali wepiyano omnye okanye ngabadlali bepiyano ababini. Ngomculo wexesha lika-2000s, abadlali bekhibhodi banokudlala ii-synthesizer endaweni yepiyano. 

Amanqaku ekwayala anxulumeneyo kodwa angaxhaphakanga kakhulu aqulathe iinxalenye zekwayala ezikhatshwayo. 

Amanqaku ombutho athelekisekayo akhona ngokunjalo, ngokwesiqhelo ngokunxulumana nomculo wecawa wamazwi kunye neokhestra, njengamalungiselelo (ngezandla zamva) kaMesiya kaHandel. Kufana nomculo wepiyano kuba iquka izibonda zamalungu elizwi yaye inciphisa iiokhestra ezidlalwa ngumntu omnye. Ngokungafaniyo nenqaku lelizwi, amanqaku omzimba ngamanye amaxesha ajongwa ngumququzeleli ukuba athathe indawo yeokhestra xa kukho imfuneko. 

Ingqokelela yeengoma kumculo onikiweyo idla ngokuprintwa phantsi kweleyibhile yokukhetha amazwi. Oku kwahlukile kumanqaku ezwi avela kumboniso omnye kuba awubonisi umculo opheleleyo, kwaye ukukhapha ipiyano ngokuqhelekileyo kwenziwa lula kwaye kubandakanya umgca womculo. 

Ezinye iintlobo
Amanqaku amafutshane kukuncitshiswa komsebenzi wezixhobo ezininzi ukuya kwizibonda nje ezimbalwa. Endaweni yokuqamba ngokuthe ngqo ngamanqaku apheleleyo, abaqambi abaninzi basebenzela uhlobo oluthile lwamanqaku amafutshane ngelixa beqamba kwaye kamva bandise iokhestra epheleleyo. Ngokomzekelo, i-opera inokubhalwa kuqala ngamanqaku amafutshane, ize emva koko ibe ngamanqaku apheleleyo, emva koko ithotywe ibe kumazwi okuqhelisela. Amanqaku amafutshane asoloko engapapashwa; zisenokuba zixhaphake kakhulu kwezinye ii-ensembles (umz., ibhendi) kunezinye. Ngenxa yobume bawo bokuqala, amanqaku amafutshane ayindawo ephambili yereferensi yabaqambi abanqwenela ukugqibezela umsebenzi ongekagqitywa womnye (umzekelo, iiMovements 2 ukuya ku-5 ze-10th Symphony kaGustav Mahler okanye isenzo sesithathu seopera ka-Alban Berg ethi Lulu). 

Inqaku elivuliweyo linqaku lesiqwenga sepolyphonic esibonisa ilizwi ngalinye kubasebenzi abahlukeneyo. Kwiziqwenga zebhodi yeRenaissance okanye yeBaroque, amanqaku avuliweyo ezibonda ezine ayekhe asetyenziswe endaweni yendibano yangoku yabasebenzi omnye ngesandla. Ngamanye amaxesha ikwathetha into enye namanqaku apheleleyo (anokuba nangaphezulu kwenxalenye enye ngomsebenzi ngamnye). 

Kumanqaku akufutshane, onke amalungu elizwi amelwe kwiintonga ezimbini eziphambili (itreble nebass stick). 

Amanqaku asuka kwixesha leBaroque (c.1600–1750) aqheleke kakhulu ekwimo yomgca we-bass kwi-bass clef kunye neengoma ezidlalwa sisixhobo okanye ziculwa kwisibonda esingaphezulu (okanye izibonda) kwi-treble clef. Umgca we-bass udla ngokuba namanani abhalwe ngaphezulu kweenowuthsi ze-bass ezibonisa ukuba zeziphi izithuba ezingentla kwe-bass (umz., iichords) ekufuneka zidlalwe, indlela ebizwa ngokuba yi-figured bass. Amanani abonisa ukuba zeziphi izithuba umdlali we-harpsichord, umbhobho okanye umdlali welute ekufuneka adlale ngaphezu kwenowuthi yebhess nganye. 


Iphepha elikhokelayo lengoma ethi "Trifle in Pyjamas" libonisa kuphela iisimboli zomculo kunye neechord. Ukudlala le ngoma, iimvumi zecandelo lesingqisho leqela le-jazz zingaphucula amazwi echord kunye ne-bassline zisebenzisa iisimboli zechord. Izixhobo zomculo ezikhokelayo, ezinjengesax okanye ixilongo, zinokuphucula izihombiso ukuze zenze umculo ube nomdla ngakumbi, zize ke ziphucule inxalenye eyedwa. 
Umculo othandwayo 
Icwecwe elikhokelayo lichaza kuphela ingoma, amazwi kunye nemvisiswano, kusetyenziswa isitafu esinye esineesimboli zechord ezibekwe ngasentla kunye namazwi angezantsi. Iqhele ukusetyenziswa kumculo odumileyo kunye nejazz ukubamba izinto ezibalulekileyo zengoma ngaphandle kokuchaza iinkcukacha zendlela ingoma ekufuneka icwangciswe ngayo okanye yenziwe. 

Itshathi yeechord (okanye ngokulula, itshathi) iqulethe ulwazi oluncinci okanye alunalwazi kwaphela kodwa inika ulwazi olusisiseko lwe-harmonic. Ezinye iitshathi zechord zikwabonisa isingqisho esifanele ukudlalwa, ngakumbi ukuba kukho uchungechunge olulungelelanisiweyo lwe "hits" umcwangcisi ofuna ukuba lonke icandelo lesingqisho lenze. Kungenjalo, iitshati zechord zinokusishiya singenanto isingqisho okanye zibonise izikhewu kwisingqi ngasinye.

Olu lolona hlobo luqhelekileyo lomculo obhaliweyo osetyenziswa ziimvumi zeseshoni ezivunyiweyo ezidlala ijazz okanye ezinye iintlobo zomculo odumileyo kwaye lenzelwe icandelo lesingqisho (elihlala liqulathe ipiyano, isiginkci, ibhesi kunye namagubu) ukuze kuphuculwe ukukhatshwa kwazo kunye nazo naziphi na iimvumi eziphuculayo (umzekelo, abadlali besaxophone okanye abadlali bexilongo) ukuze basebenzise ireferensi yabo njengenqaku lereferensi. 

Incwadi yomgunyathi yingqokelela yeengoma zejazz kunye neengoma ezinezinto ezisisiseko zomculo onikiweyo. Zimbini iindidi zeencwadi zomgunyathi: (1) ingqokelela yamaphepha elothe, aquka amazwi omculo, iichords, namazwi (ukuba akhona), kunye (2) nengqokelela yeengoma neengoma ezineechowu kuphela. Iincwadi zomgunyathi eziqulathe iichords kuphela zisetyenziswa ngabadlali becandelo lesingqisho (ngokukodwa iimvumi ezidlala iichord ezifana neziginkci zombane kunye nabadlali bepiyano kunye nomdlali we-bassist) ukunceda ukukhokela ekuphuculeni iindawo ezikhapha ingoma. Iincwadi zomgunyathi ezineechords kuphela zinokusetyenziswa zizixhobo ezikhokelayo (umz., i-saxophone okanye ixilongo) njengesikhokelo sokuphucula indlela abadlala ngayo bebodwa. Ekubeni iculo lingaqukwanga kwiincwadi zomgunyathi ezixutyiweyo kuphela, abadlali besixhobo esikhokelayo kulindeleke ukuba bangawazi lo mculo. 


C isikali esikhulu kubhalo oluqhelekileyo (ngasentla) nakwitheyibhuli yekatala (ngezantsi) 
Ithebhulature (okanye ithebhu) luhlobo olukhethekileyo lwamanqaku omculo - ubukhulu becala kwisixhobo somculo esiyedwa - ebonisa indawo ekudlalwa kuyo iipitshi kwisixhobo esinikiweyo kunokuba zeziphi ii-pitches eziveliswayo, kunye nesingqisho esibonisiwe ngokunjalo. I-Tablature isetyenziswa kakhulu kwikatala kunye neengoma ze-bass zombane kunye neziqwenga kwiindidi zomculo ezidumileyo ezinjengomculo werock kunye nomculo onesingqi esinamandla. Olu hlobo lobhalo lwaqala ukusetyenziswa ekupheleni kwamaXesha Aphakathi, kwaye luye lwasetyenziswa kwibhodi yezitshixo (umzekelo, ilungu lombhobho) kunye nezixhobo zomtya ezixakiweyo (ilute, isiginci).[2] 

Amaphepha eengoma 
Amaphepha eengoma ngamagama ashicilelweyo ngaphandle kophawu lomculo. Izifundo zezifundo zomculo waseMelika zibiza la maphepha eengoma zengoma. [3]: 25 Ngaphezu kwesiqingatha sokuqala senkulungwane yama-20, amazwi eengoma ashicilelwe kwaye athengiswa ngabanye, kwiingqokelela kumaphepha alingana nephephandaba, adityaniswe abe ziincwadana, nakwiimagazini.[3]: 53–54 Amaphepha eengoma ayequka iifoto zabasasazi abadumileyo abanxulunyaniswa nengoma kunye nomculo we-58 kunye nomculo. 

Amaphepha eengoma aqatshelwa njengokhuphiswano lomculo wephepha yi-American Society of Composers, Authors and Publishers (ASCAP) ngo-1930, xa ummeli wathi, "Amawaka ngoku afunda iingoma ezidumileyo kwirediyo, abapapashi bathi. Ngamazwi afumanekayo kwiisenti ezintlanu okanye ezilishumi kunye noxinzelelo olwaziwayo, impembelelo yokuthenga umculo weshiti iyapheliswa." Ngelixa umculo weshiti wengoma unokubiza amashumi amathathu okanye amashumi amathathu anesihlanu eesenti, iphepha lengoma elidla ngokuthengiswa nge-nickel okanye i-dime. Imibutho yeekwayala ibiya kuthengela iimvumi ikopi enye yomculo wepiyano ize emva koko ithenge amaphepha eengoma amaninzi eemvumi  

. I-song-sheet bootlegging yabonwa njengengxaki encinci eChicago ekuqaleni kweminyaka yoo-1890, kodwa yaba ngumba obalulekileyo ukusuka ngo-1929 ukuya koo-1930. ukunyanzeliswa, kunye nokuvela kweemagazini zephepha lengoma esemthethweni, i-song-sheet bootlegging yaphela kwiminyaka yoo-1940  

. uphononongo, kunye nenkcazo ngobomi babantu abadumileyo.[3]: 69  

Imbali 
Izandulela zomculo 
Ubhalo lomculo lwaphuhliswa phambi kokuba kusetyenziswe isikhumba okanye iphepha ukubhala. Olona phawu lokuqala lomculo lunokufumaneka kwicwecwe elibhalwe ngoonobumba abatsobhileyo eladalwa eNippur, eSumer (eIraq yanamhlanje), malunga no 2000 BC. Eli cwecwe limela imiyalelo engaqeshwanga yokuculwa komculo, nto leyo ebonisa ukuba wawuyilwe ngokuhambelana kwesithathu kusetyenziswa isikali sediatonic.[4] 

Icwecwe elisusela malunga no-1250 BC libonisa indlela ephuhliswe ngakumbi yobhalo.[5] Nangona indlela yokutolikwa kwenkqubo yokubhala isaphikisana, kucacile ukuba ubhalo lubonisa amagama eentambo zohadi, okuthethwa ngazo kwamanye amacwecwe.[6] Nangona ziingceba, ezi cwecwe zimele ezona ngoma zamandulo eziphawulweyo ezifumaneka naphi na emhlabeni.[6] 


Ilitye loqobo eDelphi eliqulathe elesibini kwiingoma ezimbini zeDelphic kuApollo. Inqaku lomculo ngumgca weempawu zamaxesha athile ngaphezulu komgca oyintloko, ongaphazamisekiyo wombhalo wesiGrike.
Ingoma yamandulo yamaGrike yayisetyenziswa ukususela ubuncinane kwinkulungwane ye-6 BC ukuya malunga nenkulungwane yesi-4 ye-AD; Iingoma ezininzi ezipheleleyo kunye namaqhekeza eengoma kusetyenziswa olubhalo kusinda. Ubhalo luqulathe iisimboli ezibekwe ngaphezulu kwamalungu okubhaliweyo. Umzekelo wokuqulunqwa okupheleleyo yi-Seikilos epitaph, eye yahluka ngokungafaniyo phakathi kwe-2 yenkulungwane ye-BC ukuya kwi-1 yenkulungwane ye-AD. 

Kumculo wamandulo wesiGrike, amaculo amathathu kaMesomedes aseKrete afumaneka kwimibhalo-ngqangi. Omnye weyona mizekelo midala yaziwayo yobhalo lomculo sisiqwenga sepapyrus sexesha le-Hellenic play i-Orestes (408 BC), equlethe ubhalo lomculo we-choral ode. Inqaku lamandulo lamaGrike libonakala lingasasebenzi ngexesha lokuwohloka koBukhosi baseRoma. 

Ukubhalwa kwemibhalo-ngqangi yaseNtshona 
Ngaphambi kwenkulungwane ye-15, umculo waseNtshona wawubhalwa ngesandla kwaye ugcinwe kwimibhalo-ngqangi, ngokuqhelekileyo ubotshelelwe kwimiqulu emikhulu. Eyona mizekelo yaziwa kakhulu yobhalo lomculo wamaXesha Aphakathi yimibhalo-ngqangi yamandulo yengoma yemonophonic. Ubhalo lwengoma lubonise amanqaku omculo wengoma, kodwa ngaphandle kokubonisa isingqisho. Kwimeko ye-polyphony yamaXesha Aphakathi, njenge-motet, iinxalenye zabhalwa ngamacandelo ahlukeneyo ajongene namaphepha. Le nkqubo yancediswa kukufika kwe-mensural notation, ekwabonisa isingqisho kwaye yafaniswa nesenzo sexesha eliphakathi lokuqamba iinxalenye zepolyphony ngokulandelelana, kunokuba ngaxeshanye (njengakumaxesha amva). Imibhalo-ngqangi ebonisa iinxalenye kunye kwifomathi yamanqaku yayinqabile kwaye ilinganiselwe kakhulu kwi-organum, ngakumbi eso sesikolo saseNotre Dame. Ngexesha lamaXesha Aphakathi, ukuba u-Abbess wayefuna ukuba nekopi yokwakheka okukhoyo, okufana nokwakheka kuka-Abbess kwenye idolophu, kuya kufuneka aqeshe umkhupheli ukuba enze umsebenzi ngesandla, nto leyo eya kuba yinkqubo ende kwaye inokukhokelela kwiimpazamo zokukhuphela. 

Nasemva kokufika koshicilelo lomculo phakathi kwiminyaka yoo-1400, umculo omninzi waqhubeka ukho kuphela kwimibhalo-ngqangi ebhalwe ngesandla yabaqambi ukuya kutsho kwinkulungwane ye-18. 

Ushicilelo 
Jonga kwakhona: Imbali yopapasho lomculo kunye noMkroli woMculo 
wenkulungwane ye-15
Kwakukho ubunzima obuninzi ekuguquleleni iteknoloji entsha yokushicilela kumculo. Kwincwadi yokuqala eprintiweyo ukubandakanya umculo, i-Mainz Psalter (1457), ingoma yomculo (yombini imigca yabasebenzi kunye namanqaku) yongezwa ngesandla. Oku kuyafana negumbi elishiywe kwenye incunabula yee-capitals. Le ndumiso yashicilelwa eMainz, eJamani, nguJohann Fust noPeter Schöffer, yaye ngoku enye ihlala kwiNqaba yaseWindsor yaye enye kwiThala leeNcwadi laseBritani. Kamva, kwashicilelwa imigca yabasebenzi, kodwa ababhali bongeza ngesandla kumculo oseleyo. Obona bunzima kakhulu ekusebenziseni uhlobo olushenxisekayo ukuprinta umculo kukuba zonke izinto kufuneka zingqamene - intloko yenowuthi mayilungelelaniswe ngokufanelekileyo nabasebenzi. Kumculo wezwi, isicatshulwa kufuneka sihambelane namanqaku afanelekileyo (nangona ngeli xesha, nakwimibhalo-ngqangi, oku kwakungeyona nto iphambili). 

Umkroli womculo bubugcisa bokuzoba ubhalo lomculo kumgangatho ophezulu ngenjongo yokuvelisa ngoomatshini. Umculo wokuqala oshicilelwe ngumatshini wavela malunga ne-1473, malunga neminyaka engama-20 emva kokuba uGutenberg wazisa umatshini wokushicilela. Ngomnyaka we-1501, u-Ottaviano Petrucci wapapasha i-Harmonice Musices Odhecaton A, equlethe iinqununu ze-96 zomculo oshicilelweyo. Indlela kaPetrucci yokushicilela yavelisa umculo ococekileyo, ofundekayo, omnandi, kodwa yayiyinkqubo ende nenzima eyayifuna iindlela ezintathu ezahlukeneyo kumatshini wokushicilela. Kamva uPetrucci wavelisa inkqubo eyayifuna abantu ababini kuphela abadlulayo kumaphephandaba. Kodwa bekusatsalwa irhafu kuba ipasi nganye ibifuna ulungelelwaniso oluchanekileyo ukuze isiphumo sifundeke (okt, ukuze iintloko zeenowuthi zidweliswe ngokuchanekileyo kunye nemigca yabasebenzi). Lo ibingumculo wokuqala oshicilelwe kakuhle wepolyphonic. I-Petrucci iphinde yashicilela i-tablet yokuqala kunye nohlobo olususwayo. Ukushicilela ngomfanekiso omnye, apho imigca yabasebenzi namanqaku ayenokuprintwa kwipasi enye, yaqala ukuvela eLondon malunga nowe-1520. UPierre Attaingnant wasebenzisa obu bugcisa ngowe-1528, yaye akuzange kutshintshe kangako kangangeminyaka engama-200. 


I-Frontispiece ukuya kwi-Petrucci's Odhecaton okanye i-Harmonice Musices Odhecaton 
Ifomathi eqhelekileyo yokukhupha iinxalenye ezininzi, umculo wepolyphonic ngexesha le-Renaissance yayiyi-partbooks. Kule fomathi, inxalenye yelizwi nganye yengqokelela yee-madrigals ezinamacala amahlanu, umzekelo, iya kuprintwa ngokwahlukeneyo kwincwadi yayo, kangangokuba zonke iipartbooks ezintlanu ziya kufuneka ukwenza umculo. Kwaee-partbooks ezifanayo zinokusetyenziswa ziimvumi okanye ii- instrumentalers. Amanqaku omculo onamacandelo amaninzi ayengafane ashicilelwe kwiRenaissance, nangona ukusetyenziswa kwefomathi yamanqaku njengendlela yokuqamba iinxalenye ngaxeshanye (kunokuba zilandelelane, njengakumaXesha Aphakathi asekupheleni) kubalelwa kuJosquin des Prez, umqambi womculo we-renaissance ephezulu.

Umphumo womculo oshicilelweyo wawufana nomphumo wemibhalo eshicilelweyo, kuba loo nkcazelo yayisasazwa ngokukhawuleza, ngokunempumelelo ngakumbi, ngexabiso eliphantsi, nakubantu abaninzi kunokuba bekunjalo ngokukhutshelwa ngokubulaleka kwemibhalo-ngqangi ekhutshelwe ngesandla. Waba nomphumo owongezelelekileyo wokukhuthaza iimvumi ezingaphangeliyo ezinexabiso elaneleyo, ezikwaziyo ukuthenga umculo weshiti, ukuba zicule. Oku ngeendlela ezininzi kuchaphazele imboni yomculo iphela. Abaqambi ngoku banokubhala umculo omninzi kubadlali abasafundayo, besazi ukuba unokusasazwa kwaye uthengiselwe abakumgangatho ophakathi. 

Oku kwakuthetha ukuba abaqambi kwakungeyomfuneko ukuba baxhomekeke kuphela kuncedo lwezinhanha. Abadlali abaqeqeshiweyo banokuba nomculo omninzi abanawo kwaye banokufikelela kumculo osuka kumazwe ahlukeneyo. Yandisa inani labangaqeqeshwayo, ivumela abadlali abaqeqeshiweyo ukuba bafumane imali ngokubafundisa. Sekunjalo, kwiminyaka yokuqala, iindleko zomculo oshicilelweyo zazinciphisa ukusasazwa kwawo. Enye into eyayisikel’ umda impembelelo yomculo oshicilelweyo yayikukuba kwiindawo ezininzi, ilungelo lokushicilela umculo lalinikwa ukumkani, yaye kuphela abo babenolawulo olukhethekileyo ababevunyelwa ukuba benjenjalo, nto leyo eyayibanika igunya lokushicilela. Oku kwakudla ngokuba liwonga (kunye nenzuzo yezoqoqosho) eyayinikwa iimvumi zenkundla ezithandwayo okanye abaqambi. 

Kwinkulungwane ye-16 

Umzekelo womculo wephepha lenkulungwane ye-16 kunye nobhalo lomculo. Isicatshulwa kumbhalo-ngqangi "Muziek voor 4 korige diatonische cister".[7] 
Mechanical plate ekrolwa yaphuhliswa ekupheleni kwenkulungwane yeshumi elinesithandathu.[8] Nangona umkrolo wepleyiti wawusetyenzisiwe ukususela ekuqaleni kwenkulungwane yeshumi elinesihlanu ekudaleni ubugcisa obubonakalayo kunye neemephu, ayizange isetyenziswe kumculo de kwangowe-1581. Ngale ndlela, umfanekiso wesipili wephepha elipheleleyo lomculo wakrolwa kwipleyiti yentsimbi. Emva koko i-inki yayiqatywa kwimisele, yaye umculo owawushicilelwe wawukhutshelwa ephepheni. Iipleyiti zesinyithi zinokugcinwa kwaye zisetyenziswe kwakhona, nto leyo eyenza le ndlela ibe yindlela ekhangayo kubakroli bomculo. Ubhedu yayiyintsimbi yokuqala ekhethwayo kwiipleyiti zokuqala, kodwa ngenkulungwane yeshumi elinesibhozo, i-pewter yaba yinto eqhelekileyo ngenxa yokonakala kwayo kunye neendleko eziphantsi.[9] 

Umkrolo wepleyiti wawuyindlela ekhethwayo yoshicilelo lomculo de kwasekupheleni kwenkulungwane yeshumi elinesithoba, apho ukwehla kwawo kwakhawuleziswa kuphuhliso lobuchwephesha bokufota.[8] Noko ke, obu buchule buye bukho ukuza kuthi ga namhlanje yaye lusasetyenziswa ngamathuba athile ngabavakalisi abakhethekileyo abafana noG. Henle Verlag waseJamani.[10]

Njengoko ukuqanjwa komculo kwanda ngokuntsonkotha, ngokunjalo neteknoloji efunekayo ukuvelisa amanqaku omculo achanekileyo. Ngokungafaniyo noshicilelo loncwadi, ubukhulu becala olunamagama ashicilelweyo, umzobo womculo udlulisela iindidi ezahlukeneyo zenkcazelo ngaxeshanye. Ukuze kucace kwiimvumi, kunyanzelekile ukuba ubuchule bokukrola buvumele ukuchaneka ngokupheleleyo. Amanqaku eechords, amanqaku aguqukayo, kunye nolunye ubhalo luhambelana nokuchaneka okuthe nkqo. Ukuba okubhaliweyo kuqukiwe, ilungu ngalinye lihambelana ngokuthe nkqo nomculo walo owabelweyo. Ngokuthe tye, ulwahlulo lweebhithi luphawulwa kungekuphela nje ngeeflegi kunye nemiqadi, kodwa nangokwesithuba esiphakathi kwazo kwiphepha.[8] Ukwenziwa kweekopi ezichanekileyo ngolo hlobo kubangele iingxaki ezininzi kubazobi bomculo bokuqala, kwaye kukhokelele kuphuhliso lweetekhnoloji ezininzi zokukrola umculo. IZakhiwo 

zenkulungwane ye-19 

zeSixeko saseNew York iTin Pan Alley epapasha isithili ngo-1910. [11] 
Ngenkulungwane ye-19, ishishini lomculo lalilawulwa ngabapapashi bomculo weshiti. Embindini wenkulungwane, ulawulo lweengoma zomculo lwalungekho ngqongqo, yaye abapapashi babedla ngokuprinta iinguqulelo zabo zeengoma ezazithandwa ngelo xesha. Abanye abaqambi, abanjengoJN Pattison, baye baphikisa ngokupapasha owabo umculo. UPattison usebenze kwipiyano kunye negumbi lokuthengisa amalungu e-Union Square kumbindi wedolophu yaseManhattan. Emva kowe-1885, upapasho lomculo waseNew York lwalulawulwa liqela lababhali beengoma kunye nabaqambi abaziwa ngokuba yiTin Pan Alley. Ngemithetho eyomeleleyo yokukhuselwa kwelungelo lokushicilela ngasekupheleni kwenkulungwane, abaqambi beengoma, abaqambi, abaculi beengoma, kunye nabapapashi baqala ukusebenza kunye ukuze bafumane inzuzo efanayo yezemali. Abavakalisi besiXeko saseNew York banikela ingqalelo kumculo welizwi. Ezona zindlu zinkulu zomculo zizinzile kwisiXeko saseNew York, kodwa abapapashi abancinci basekhaya - bahlala benxibelelana nabashicileli bentengiso okanye iivenkile zomculo - baqhubeka bechuma kwilizwe lonke. Inani elingaqhelekanga labaphambukeli baseMpuma Yurophu baba ngabapapashi bomculo kunye nababhali beengoma kwiTin Pan Alley-oyena udumileyo nguIrving Berlin. Ababhali beengoma abathe baba ngabavelisi abazinzileyo beengoma eziphumeleleyo baqeshwa ukuba babe ngabasebenzi bezindlu zomculo.

EUnited States, ishishini lomculo weshiti liye lakhula ngokuhambelana ne-blackface minstrelsy, kunye nomculo we-parlor. Ngasekupheleni kwenkulungwane ye-19 yabona ugqabhuko-dubulo olukhulu lomculo we-parlor, ubunini, kunye nobuchule bokudlala ipiyano iba yi-rigueur yosapho olukumgangatho ophakathi. Ngasekupheleni kwenkulungwane ye-19, ukuba usapho olukumgangatho ophakathi lufuna ukuva ingoma okanye ingoma entsha edumileyo, lwaluthenga lo mculo luze lucule ingoma okanye ingoma ngendlela engaqhelekanga ekhayeni labo. Kodwa ekuqaleni kwenkulungwane yama-20 igramafoni nomculo orekhodiweyo zabaluleka kakhulu. Oku, kudityaniswa nokwanda kokuthandwa kosasazo lukanomathotholo ukususela ngeminyaka yee-1920 ukuya phambili, kwanciphisa ukubaluleka kwabapapashi bamashidi omculo. Ishishini lokurekhoda ekugqibeleni lithathe indawo yabapapashi bomculo njengawona mandla makhulu kushishino lomculo. 

Inkulungwane yama-20 nasekuqaleni kwenkulungwane yama-21 
ngasekupheleni kwenkulungwane yama-20 ukuya kuthi ga kwinkulungwane yama-21, umdla omkhulu uye waphuhla ekuboniseni umculo wephepha ngendlela efundeka ngekhompyutha (jonga isoftware yophawu lomculo), kunye neefayile ezikhutshelwayo. I-OCR yoMculo, isoftware "yokufunda" i-scanner sheet yomculo ukwenzela ukuba iziphumo zibe nokuguquguquka, iye yafumaneka ukususela ngo-1991. 

Ngo-1998, umculo we-virtual sheet wavela ngakumbi kwinto eyayiza kubizwa ngokuba ngumculo we-digital sheet, owathi okokuqala wavumela abapapashi ukuba benze i-copyright yomculo we-copyright ifumaneke ukuthengwa kwi-intanethi. Ngokungafaniyo nabalingane babo beekopi ezinzima, ezi fayile zivumela ukuguqulwa okufana nokutshintshwa kwesixhobo, ukuguqulwa kunye ne-MIDI (I-Musical Instrument Digital Interface) yokudlala. Ukuthandwa kwale nkqubo yokuhanjiswa kweenkonzo ngoko nangoko phakathi kweemvumi kubangele ukukhula koshishino olutsha ukusukela ekupheleni kweminyaka yoo-1990. 

Inkqubo yasekuqaleni yokubhalwa kwekhompyuter ekhoyo kwiikhompyuter zasekhaya yayiyiSeti yoKwakha uMculo, eyaphuhliswa ngo-1984 yaza yakhutshelwa amaqonga ahlukeneyo. Ukwazisa iikhonsepthi ezininzi ezazingaziwa kumsebenzisi wasekhaya welo xesha, kwavumela ukuguqulwa kwamanqaku kunye neesimboli ngesixhobo sokukhomba esifana nempuku; Umsebenzisi uya "kubamba" inqaku okanye isimboli kwiphalethi kwaye "ayibeke" kubasebenzi kwindawo echanekileyo. Inkqubo ivumele ukudlalwa kwakhona komculo ovelisiweyo ngamakhadi esandi ahlukeneyo asekuqaleni, kwaye inokushicilela amanqaku omculo kumshicileli wemifanekiso. 

Iimveliso ezininzi zesoftware yesixhobo sokusebenza sedijithali sanamhlanje kunye nababhali bamanqaku kwiikhompyuter zobuqu ngokubanzi zixhasa ukuveliswa komculo weshiti ukusuka kwiifayile zeMIDI, nokuba ngumculi odlala amanqaku kwikhibhodi ene-MIDI okanye omnye umlawuli weMIDI, okanye ngokungena ngesandla usebenzisa imawusi okanye esinye isixhobo sekhompyuter.

Ngo-1999, inkqubo kunye nendlela yokulungelelanisa ukuboniswa komculo phakathi kwabadlali beokhestra yayinelungelo elilodwa lomenzi nguHarry Connick Jr. [12] Sisixhobo esinescreen sekhompyuter esisetyenziselwa ukubonisa iimvumi zomculo weokhestra endaweni yephepha elisetyenziswa ngokuqhelekileyo. UConnick usebenzisa le nkqubo xa ekhenketha neqela lakhe elikhulu, umzekelo. [13] Ngokunyuka kweenethiwekhi ezingenazintambo kunye nee-iPads, iinkqubo ezifanayo ziye zaphuhliswa. Kwilizwe lomculo weklasikhi, amanye amaqela e-quartet yomtya asebenzisa iinxalenye ezisekwe kwikhompyuter. Kukho iingenelo ezininzi kwiindawo ezisekwe kwikhompyuter. Kuba amanqaku akwiscreen sekhompyuter, umsebenzisi unokulungelelanisa umahluko, ukuqaqamba kunye nobukhulu bamanqaku ukwenza ukufunda kube lula. Ukongeza, ezinye iisistim ziyakwenza "ukujika kwephepha" zisebenzisa i-pedal yeenyawo, okuthetha ukuba umenzi akaphoswanga kudlala umculo ngexesha lokujika kwephepha, njengoko kusenzeka rhoqo ngamacandelo ephepha. 

Owona mdla ukhethekileyo kuluntu ngokubanzi yiProjekthi yeMutopia, inzame yokuyila ithala leencwadi lomculo wedomeyini yoluntu, ethelekiswa nethala leencwadi likaProject Gutenberg leencwadi zoluntu. IProjekthi yeThala leeNcwadi yaManqaku oMculo yaMazwe ngaMazwe (IMSLP) ikwazama ukuyila ithala leencwadi lenyani eliqulethe onke amanqaku omculo wedomeyini yoluntu, kunye namanqaku avela kubaqambi abazimisele ukwabelana ngomculo wabo nehlabathi ngaphandle kwentlawulo. 

Ezinye iinkqubo zekhompyuter zamanqaku anophawu oluluncedo kakhulu kubaqambi kunye nabacwangcisi: ukukwazi "ukudlala kwakhona" umculo ophawulweyo usebenzisa izandi ze-synthesizer okanye izixhobo ezibonakalayo. Phambi kokuba iinkqubo zekhompyutha zibekho, iindleko eziphezulu zokuqesha iokhestra yesimfoni epheleleyo yayithetha ukuba abaqambi abaninzi nabaququzeleli babenokuyiva kuphela imisebenzi yabo yeokhestra ngokuyilungiselela ipiyano, iorgan okanye i-string quartet. Ngelixa iprogram ye-scorewiter idlala kwakhona ingenazo iinuances zeokhestra yobuchwephesha bokurekhodwa, isadlulisela ithoni yemibala kunye nesixhobo sokudlala. 

Ukungeniswa kwenowuthsi yabasebenzi baseNtshona kwezinye iinkcubeko 
Ngaphandle kweenkcubeko zaseNtshona zanamhlanje kukho iintlobo ngeentlobo zeenkqubo zokubhalwa komculo, nganye ilungelelaniswe kwiimfuno ezithile zeenkcubeko zomculo ekuthethwa ngawo. Ezinye izithethe zamandulo ezivele zavela kakhulu, ezinje ngekhyal kunye neefomu zedhrupad zaseMantla eIndiya, azisebenzisi nto zibhalileyo kwaphela okanye ziindlela ezizizo kuphela njengoncedo lwemnemonic. Iinkqubo zokubhala zaseNtshona azikufanelanga ukuchaza umculo wezinye iindidi, ezifana neentlobo zenkundla yegagaku yaseJapan, idhrupad yaseIndiya, okanye umculo obethwayo we-Ewe egubu[catshulwa]. Ukungeniswa kwabasebenzi baseNtshona kwezi nkcubeko kuchazwe ngumculi wezomculo u-Alain Daniélou [14] kunye noReebee Garofalo[15] njengenkqubo ye-impiriyalizim yenkcubeko.

Iphazili ngumdlalo, ingxaki, okanye into yokudlala evavanya ubukrelekrele okanye ulwazi lomntu. Kwiphazili, umsombululi ulindeleke ukuba adibanise amaqhekeza (okanye awahlukanise) ngendlela enengqiqo, ukuze kufumaneke isisombululo sephazili. Kukho iindidi ngeendidi zeephazili, ezifana neepuzzle zamagama, iipuzzle zokukhangela amagama, iipuzzle zamanani, iipuzzle ezizalanayo, kunye neelogic. Uphononongo lwezifundo zeepuzzle lubizwa ngokuba yi-enigmatology. 

Iipuzzle zihlala ziyilwe ukuba zibe luhlobo lokuzonwabisa kodwa zinokuvela kwiingxaki ezinzulu zemathematika okanye ezinengqondo. Kwiimeko ezinjalo, isisombululo sabo sinokuba negalelo elikhulu kuphando lwemathematika.[1] 

I-Etymology 
I-Oxford English Dictionary ithi igama elithi iphazili (njengesenzi) lisusela kwinkulungwane ye-16. Ukusetyenziswa kwayo kokuqala okubhalwe kwi-OED yayikwincwadi enesihloko esithi, Uhambo lukaRobert Dudley...ukuya kwi-West Indies, ngo-1594–95, ebaliswa nguKapteni Wyatt, eyedwa, kunye no-Abram Kendall, inkosi (eyapapashwa malunga nowe-1595). Eli gama kamva laye lasetyenziswa njengesibizo, okokuqala njengesibizo esingavakaliyo esithetha 'imeko okanye imeko yokubhideka', kuze kamva kuphuhliswe intsingiselo 'yengxaki edidayo'. Isicatshulwa sokuqala esicacileyo se-OED ngengqiqo 'yento yokudlala evavanya ubuchule bomdlali' ivela kwinoveli kaSir Walter Scott ka-1814 ethi Waverley, ebhekisela kwinto yokudlala eyaziwa ngokuba yi "reel ebhotileni".[2] 

I-etymology yephazili yesenzi ichazwa yi-OED “njengengaziwayo”; Uqikelelo olungangqinwanga malunga nemvelaphi yalo lubandakanya isenzi sesiNgesi esiDala esithi puslian esithetha 'khetha', kunye nokuvela kwisenzi sokuma.[3]

ithebhulethi i-puzzle ye-chemistry

Iiphazili zeMechanical okanye iipuzzle ze-dexterity ezifana neRubik's Cube kunye neSoma cube zinokuvuselela iithoyi zabantwana okanye imisebenzi yokuzonwabisa yabantu abadala.

Ukusombulula i 
-Minesweeper 
Eli candelo linokuba liqulathe uphando loqobo. Nceda uyiphucule ngokuqinisekisa amabango enziweyo kunye nokongeza izicatshulwa ezingaphakathi. Iingxelo ezibandakanya kuphela uphando lwangaphambili kufuneka zisuswe. (NgoNovemba 2018) (Funda indlela kwaye nini ukususa lo myalezo) 
Izisombululo zeepuzzle zihlala zifuna ukuqatshelwa kweepateni kunye nokubambelela kuhlobo oluthile lomyalelo. Abantu abanenqanaba eliphezulu lokuqiqa ngengqondo efanelekileyo banokuba ngcono ekusombululeni iipuzzle ezinjalo xa kuthelekiswa nabanye. Kodwa iipuzzle ezisekelwe kumbuzo kunye nokufumanisa zinokusonjululwa ngokulula ngabo banezakhono ezilungileyo zokuxhuzula. Ukuqiqa okuthobayo kuyaphucuka ngokuziqhelanisa. Iiphazili zemathematika zihlala zibandakanya i-BODMAS. I-BODMAS sisishunqulelo esimele i-Bracket, ye, iCandelo, ukuphindaphinda, ukudibanisa kunye nokuThatha. Kwimimandla ethile, i-PEMDAS (Ii-Parentheses, i-Exponents, Ukuphindaphinda, ulwahlulo, ukudibanisa kunye nokuThatha) sisithetha-ntonye se-BODMAS. Icacisa ulandelelwano lwemisebenzi ukusombulula intetho. Ezinye iiphazili zemathematika zifuna ukuhlangana ukusuka phezulu ukuya ezantsi ukunqanda ukungaqondakali kolandelelwano lwemisebenzi. Luluvo olulula oluxhomekeke, njengoko i-sudoku isenza, kwimfuno yokuba amanani avele kube kanye kuphela ukusuka phezulu ukuya ezantsi njengokuza kunye.[4] 
Abenzi bephazili 
ngabantu abenza iiphazili. Ngokumalunga nomsebenzi jikelele, umntu ophazili-phazili ngumntu oqamba kunye/okanye osombulula iipuzzle.
