Imbali yeepuzzle




Iphazili edityanisiweyo-amakhonkco alithoba, isixhobo sephazili ephucukileyo efuna ubalo lwemathematika ukusombulula, yasungulwa eTshayina ngexesha laMazwe alwayo (475-221 BCE).[5] Iiphazili zeJigsaw zayilwa malunga no-1760, xa uJohn Spilsbury, umzobi waseBritani nomzobi weemaphu, wahlohla imephu kwiphepha lomthi, awathi walisarha lijikeleze ulwandlalo lwelizwe ngalinye kwimephu. Emva koko wasebenzisa iziqwenga ezifunyenweyo njengoncedo ekufundiseni ijografi.[6] 

Emva kokuba idumile phakathi koluntu, olu hlobo loncedo lokufundisa lwahlala lusetyenziswa kakhulu kwiipuzzle de kwaba malunga no-1820.[7] 

Eyona iphazili inkulu (iziqwenga ezingama-40,320) yenziwe yinkampani yemidlalo yaseJamani iRavensburger. Eyona iphazili incinci kweyakhe yenziwa yadalwa eLaserZentrum Hannover. Ziimilimitha ezintlanu kuphela, ubukhulu bekhozo esantini. 

Iiphazili ezabhalwa kuqala ngamaqashiso. EYurophu, iintsomi zamaGrike zavelisa amaqhina afana neqhina leSphinx. Amaqashiso amaninzi aveliswa ngexesha lamaXesha Aphakathi, ngokunjalo.[9] 

Ekuqaleni kwenkulungwane yama-20, amaphephancwadi namaphephandaba afumanisa ukuba anokwandisa ulwazi lwawo ngokupapasha ukhuphiswano lwepuzzle, eqala ngamagama anqamlezayo nakwisudoku yanamhlanje.

Oonodoli bephepha yimizobo esikwe ephepheni okanye kwikhadi elibhityileyo elinempahla eyahlukileyo, nayo eyenziwe ngephepha, edla ngokubanjelwa koonodoli ngeethebhu zokusonga iphepha.[1] Zisenokuba ngumfanekiso womntu, wesilwanyana okanye wento engaphiliyo.[2] 

Oonodoli abangamaphepha baye basetyenziselwa intengiso, ukuvela kumaphephancwadi namaphephandaba, yaye bagubungela imixholo eyahlukahlukeneyo namaxesha. Ukutyhubela iminyaka, ziye zasetyenziselwa ukuqinisa iinkolelo zenkcubeko malunga nenkangeleko yabafazi abafanelekileyo.[3] 

Amanye amanani eplastiki asicaba ayafana noonodoli bephepha, njengamanani eeColorforms kunye noonodoli beFlatsy, kodwa oku kukulinganisa kwaye akujongwa njengophawu lobugcisa bonodoli wephepha.[4] Umfanekiso wephephancwadi 

weHistory 

1919 womdlali weqonga uNorma Talmadge kunye nezinye izinxibo zakhe zefilimu zikwimo kanodoli 
wephepha Oonodoli bephepha bebekho oko bekukho iphepha, mhlawumbi amakhulu okanye amawaka eminyaka ngoqikelelo oluthile. Ubuso okanye ezinye izinto zisetyenziswe kwiphepha kwaye zisetyenziswe ngexesha lezithethe zonqulo kunye nemikhosi kwiinkcubeko zaseAsia kwiinkulungwane ezininzi ezidlulileyo. Abantu baseBalinese benza iphepha kunye nesikhumba kwiipopu ukususela ngaphambi kweXesha lobuKristu. Ezinye iinkcubeko kwihlabathi jikelele ziye zaba nokwakheka kwephepha okanye ubugcisa bephepha, kubandakanywa ePoland, apho babebizwa ngokuba yiWycinanki. [ucatshulo olufunekayo] Ezi ntlobo zangaphambili zezibalo zephepha zahlukile koonodoli bephepha abaqhelekileyo bale mihla, njengoko kungekho mpahla yenziweyo ukuba isetyenziswe noonodoli. 

Unodoli wokuqala wephepha owenziweyo yayingu "Little Fanny", eveliswe ngu-S&J Fuller, eLondon, ngo-1810 [2]. EYurophu, ngakumbi eFransi, oonodoli bokuqala bephepha babedumile ukususela kwinkulungwane ye-18. Elona khadi lidala elaziwayo likanodoli wephepha lisingathwa yiGermanisches Nationalmuseum kwaye laprintwa malunga no-1650 kuMazantsi eJamani, libonisa amanani amabini amabhinqa anenani leelokhwe, iziqwenga zentloko, iinwele kunye nezincedisi. Eli phepha ladityaniswa laza labizwa ngokuba zii-pantin, okuthetha ukudanisa okanye ukutsiba unopopi kajack. Zazenzelwe ukonwabisa abantu abadala zize zisasazeke kulo lonke uluntu oluphakamileyo. Zazizotywa okanye zapeyintwa njengabantu abanefashoni ngonodoli ngamnye. Ezi zazifana kakhulu noonodoli bephepha baseNtshona. Iiseti ezinqabileyo ezipeyintwe ngesandla zamanani ephepha aqala ngasekupheleni kweminyaka yoo-1780 zinokufunyanwa kwezinye iimyuziyam.[6] 

"Imbali kunye ne-Adventures ye-Little Henry", ngu-J. Belcher yayiyithoyizi yokuqala yaseMelika equka oonodoli bamaphepha. Le ncwadi, eyapapashwa ngowe-1812, yabangela ukuba abantwana babonise imifanekiso eyahlukahlukeneyo ngoonodoli bephepha ababequkiwe.[3]

Oyena mvelisi mkhulu waseMelika woonodoli bephepha, uMcLoughlin Brothers, wasekwa ekuqaleni kuka-1800 kwaye wathengiswa kuMilton Bradley ngeminyaka yoo-1920. Ngeli xesha oonodoli bephepha baye baduma e-US kwaye bakhula ngokuthandwa kumashumi eminyaka alandelayo. Ukunyuka kwemveliso kanodoli wephepha phakathi kwenkulungwane ye-19 ukuya embindini wenkulungwane yama-20 kwakungenxa yenkqubela phambili yezobuchwepheshe eyenza ushicilelo lungabizi kakhulu.[3] 


Unodoli wephepha oneempahla 
Iinkampani zokupapasha iincwadi ezalandela ekuveliseni oonodoli bephepha okanye abasikiweyo babeyiLowe, Whitman, Saalfield kunye neMerrill phakathi kwabanye. Iinkwenkwezi ze-movie kunye nabadumileyo baba ingqwalasela kwiintsuku zokuqala zoonodoli bamaphepha e-USA. Oonodoli bephepha basaveliswa kwaye uWhitman noGolden Co. basapapasha oonodoli bephepha. 

Ngaphandle kwabadlali bemiboniso bhanya-bhanya, abafazi bezolonwabo babedla ngokuba ngabo baboniswe kwifomu yoonodoli bephepha. Njengoko abafazi abaninzi baqalisa ukungena emsebenzini kwinkulungwane yamashumi amabini, abavelisi boonodoli bephepha baqalisa ukuvelisa oonodoli abamele amabhinqa emisebenzi. Umbutho wamalungelo amabhinqa phakathi kwinkulungwane yama-20 wawunembopheleleko yokuphembelela olu tshintsho. Abatshakazi babengomnye umntu oqhelekileyo odla ngokumelwa ngoonodoli bephepha. 

"Incwadi yokuthetha" iphinda iqondise apha. Ngecwecwe, bona iNcwadi yokuThetha. Ngolunye usetyenziso, jonga iNcwadi yokuThetha (disambiguation). 
I-audiobook (okanye incwadi yokuthetha) kukurekhodwa kwencwadi okanye omnye umsebenzi ofundwa ngokuvakalayo. Ukufundwa kombhalo opheleleyo kuchazwa “njengokungafinyezwanga”, ngelixa ukufundwa kweenguqulelo ezimfutshane kusishwankathelo. 

Irediyo ethethwayo ibifumaneka ezikolweni nakwiilayibrari zikawonke-wonke kwaye kancinci kwiivenkile zomculo ukusukela ngeminyaka yoo-1930. Iialbham ezininzi zamazwi athethwayo zenziwa ngaphambi kwexesha lekhasethi, iicompact disc, kunye neaudio enokukhutshelwa, edla ngokuba yimibongo nemidlalo kuneencwadi. Kwakungekho de kwangoo-1980 apho i-medium yaqala ukutsala abathengisi beencwadi, emva koko abathengisi beencwadi baqala ukubonisa ii-audiobooks kwiishelufa zeencwadi endaweni yokubonisa okwahlukileyo. 

I-Etymology 
Igama elithi “incwadi yokuthetha” labakho ngeminyaka yee-1930 ngeenkqubo zikarhulumente ezilungiselelwe abafundi abangaboniyo, ngoxa igama elithi “audiobook” laqalisa ukusetyenziswa ebudeni beminyaka yee-1970 xa iikhasethi ezirekhodiweyo zaqalisa ukuthabathel’ indawo iirekhodi zegramafoni.[1] Ngo-1994, iAudio Publishers Association yaseka igama elithi "audiobook" njengomgangatho woshishino.[1] 

I-History 

Caption ifundeka ngolu hlobo: "Igramafoni ekhaya ifunda inoveli." Ukusuka kwiDaily Graphic (eNew York), 2 April 1878. Ngaphantsi konyaka emva kokuveliswa kwegramafoni, lo mzobo wanikela umbono wekamva. Noko ke, iinoveli zaziza kuhlala zingasebenzi kwiigramafoni de kwaba ngoo-1930.
Ushicilelo lwamagama athethwayo lwaqala ukwenzeka xa kwaveliswa igramafoni nguThomas Edison ngowe-1877 [1]. "Iincwadi zefonografi" yayiyenye yeendlela zokuqala ezabonwa nguEdison ezaziza "kuthetha nabantu abaziimfama ngaphandle komzamo wabo."[1] Amagama okuqala athethwa kwigramafoni yayilicengcelezo lika-Edison elithi "UMariya WayeneMvana Encinane", umzekelo wokuqala wendinyana erekhodiweyo.[1] Ngo-1878, umboniso kwiRoyal Institution eBritani wawuquka "Hey Diddle Diddle, iCat kunye neFiddle" kunye nomgca wemibongo kaTennyson ngaloo ndlela ukuseka kwasekuqaleni kobuchwephesha unxulumano noncwadi oluthethiweyo.[1] 

EUnited States 
Ukuqala ngo-1970 
Uninzi lwamagama amafutshane, arekhodiweyo athethwayo athengiswa kwi-cylinder ngasekupheleni kwe-19th nasekuqaleni kwenkulungwane yama-20;[2] nangona kunjalo, iisilinda ezingqukuva zazilinganiselwe malunga nemizuzu emi-4 inye isenza ukuba iincwadi zingasebenzi;[1] izicwecwe ezisicaba zonyuka zaya kutsho kwimizuzu eli-12 kodwa nako kwakungenzeki ukwenza imisebenzi emide.[1] “Omnye umphulaphuli wangaphambili wakhalaza esithi uya kufuna ikiriva ukuze aqhubele phambili iincwadi ezithetha ezirekhodiweyo kwiidiski ezinomthamo ongephi wogcino.”[1] Ngeminyaka yee-1930 iirekhodi ezisondeleleneyo zanda zaya kutsho kwimizuzu engama-20 zenza ukuba ibali elide libe nokwenzeka.[1] 

Ngo-1931, i-American Foundation for the Blind (AFB) kunye neThala leeNcwadi leNgqungquthela yeNgqungquthela yeProjekthi yabantu abadala abangaboniyo baseka "iNkqubo yeeNcwadi zokuThetha" (Iincwadi zeemfama), eyayijoliswe ukubonelela ngemathiriyeli yokufunda kumagqala onzakeleyo ngexesha leMfazwe Yehlabathi I kunye nabanye abantu abadala abangaboni kakuhle.[1] Ukurekhoda kokuqala kovavanyo ngo-1932 kwakuquka isahluko esivela kuHelen Keller's Midstream kunye no-Edgar Allan Poe "I-Raven" [1]. Umbutho ufumene imvume yenkongolo ukuze ukhululwe kwilungelo lokushicilela kunye nokuhanjiswa kweposi simahla kweencwadi zokuthetha.[1] Iikhasethi zokuqala ezirekhodiweyo zowe-1934 ezaziquka iinxalenye zeBhayibhile; isiBhengezo seNkululeko kunye namanye amaxwebhu okuthand’ izwe; imidlalo kunye neengoma zikaShakespeare; kunye nentsomi kaGladys Hasty Carroll, EM Delafield, Cora Jarrett, Rudyard Kipling, John Masefield, kunye noPG Wodehouse.[1] Ukugcina iindleko kunye nokwakha ngokukhawuleza uluhlu lwee-audiobooks, iBritane ne-United States zabelana ngokurekhodwa kwiikhathalogu zabo. Ngokujonga kwiikhathalogu ezindala, umbhali-mbali uMatthew Rubery "mhlawumbi" uchonge incwadi yokuqala ye-audio eveliswe eBritani njengeka-Agatha Christie's The Murder of Roger Ackroyd, efundwe ngu-Anthony McDonald ngo-1934.

Ukurekhodwa kweBlind & Dyslexic (i-RFBD, eyathi kamva yabizwa ngokuba yi-Learning Ally) yasekwa ngo-1948 ngu-Anne T. Macdonald, ilungu leThala leeNcwadi loLuntu laseNew York eliNcedisayo laBasetyhini, ekuphenduleni ukuthontelana kwemibuzo evela kumajoni awayephulukene nokubona ekulweni ngexesha leMfazwe Yehlabathi II. I-GI Bill of Rights esandula kupasiswa iqinisekise imfundo yasekholejini kuwo onke amagqala, kodwa imibhalo ibingafikeleleki ikakhulu kumagqala asandul’ ukumfamekiswa, angazange ayifunde iBraille kwaye enofikelelo oluncinane kubafundi abaphilayo. UMacdonald uhlanganise amakhosikazi aseNcedisi phantsi kwesaci esithi “Imfundo lilungelo, hayi inyhweba”. Amalungu oMncedisi aguqula igumbi elinophahla lweThala leeNcwadi loLuntu laseNew York laba sisitudiyo, erekhoda iincwadi kusetyenziswa iidiski zegramafoni zeVinyl eziziintshi ezintandathu zeVinyl SoundScriber ezazidlala malunga nemizuzu eli-12 yemathiriyeli kwicala ngalinye. Ngowe-1952, uMacdonald waseka izitudiyo zokurekhoda kwizixeko ezisixhenxe ezongezelelekileyo kulo lonke elaseUnited States. 

ICaedmon Records yayinguvulindlela kwishishini le-audiobook. Yayiyinkampani yokuqala ezinikele ekuthengiseni ushicilelo oluthethwayo kuluntu kwaye ibizwe ngokuba "yimbewu" yoshishino lwee-audiobook. [4] ICaedmon yasekwa eNew York ngo-1952 ngabaphumelele ekholejini uBarbara Holdridge noMarianne Roney. [4] Ukukhululwa kwabo kokuqala kwaba yingqokelela yemibongo kaDylan Thomas njengoko ifundwe ngumbhali.[4] I-LP's B-side iqulethe iKrisimesi yoMntwana eWales, eyaye yongezwa njengengcamango yamva. Ibali lalifihlakele kwaye uTomas ngokwakhe akazange akwazi ukukhumbula isihloko salo xa ebuzwa ukuba asebenzise ntoni ukuze azalise i-B-side-kodwa le rekhodi yaqhubeka yaba yenye yemisebenzi yakhe ethandwa kakhulu, kwaye yasungula iCaedmon kwinkampani ephumelelayo. Ushicilelo lwantlandlolo luka-1952 yayilukhetho lweRegistry yeSizwe yokuRekhoda ngo-2008 eUnited States, ichaza ukuba "inikwe imbeko ngokusungula ishishini le-audiobook eUnited States".[5] UCaedmon wasebenzisa iirekhodi zeLP, ezaqanjwa ngo-1948, nto leyo eyenza ukuba urekhodo olude lufikeleleke ngakumbi kwaye lusebenziseke, nangona kunjalo uninzi lwemisebenzi yabo yayiyimibongo, imidlalo kunye neminye imisebenzi emifutshane, hayi iincwadi ezingafinyezwanga ngenxa yokusikelwa umda kweLP malunga nexesha lokudlala lemizuzu engama-45 (amacala adibeneyo). 

Ithala leencwadi eliMamelayo[6] nayo yayiyinkampani enguvulindlela, yaba yenye yeyokuqala ukuhambisa iincwadi ezirekhodiweyo zabantwana ezikolweni, kumathala eencwadi nakwezinye iimarike ezikhethekileyo, kubandakanywa nezibhedlele zeVA.[7] Yasekwa ngu-Anthony Ditlow kunye nenkosikazi yakhe ngo-1955 kwi-Red Bank yabo, kwikhaya laseNew Jersey; UDitlow wayengaboni kakuhle.[7] Enye inkampani yokuqala eyayingoovulindlela yayiyiSpoken Arts eyasekwa ngowe-1956 ngu-Arthur Luce Klein nomfazi wakhe, bavelisa iirekhodisho ezingaphezu kwama-700 yaye babedume kakhulu ngemibongo nemidlalo erekhodiweyo eyayisetyenziswa ezikolweni nakwiilayibrari.[8] NjengoCaedemon, iThala leencwadi eliMamelayo kunye noBugcisa obuThethiweyo baxhamla kubuchwephesha obutsha bee-LPs, kodwa bandise inkxaso-mali karhulumente yezikolo namathala eencwadi ukususela ngeminyaka yoo-1950 no-60. [7]
 
1970 ukuya 1996
Nangona ushicilelo oluthethwayo lwaludumile kwi-33+1⁄3 yefomathi yerekhodi yevinyl yezikolo kunye namathala eencwadi ukuya ekuqaleni koo-1970, ukuqala kwentengiso yale mihla yokuthengisa iincwadi ezirekhodiweyo kunokulandwa ekwamkelweni ngokubanzi kweekhasethi ngeekhasethi ngeminyaka yoo-1970. [9] Iikhasethi zekhasethi zayilwa ngowe-1962 yaye amathala eencwadi ambalwa, anjengeThala leencwadi leCongress, aqalisa ukusasaza iincwadi ezikwikhasethi ngowe-1969.[9] Nangona kunjalo, ngeminyaka yoo-1970s, inani lezinto ezintsha zobuchwephesha zavumela ukuba ikhasethi isetyenziswe ngokubanzi kumathala eencwadi kwaye yavelisa ukuyilwa korhwebo olutsha lwee-audiobook market.[9] Ezi nguqulelo zibandakanya ukwaziswa kwabadlali abaphathwayo abancinci nabancinci njengeWalkman, kunye nokusetyenziswa ngokubanzi kweedekhi zeekhasethi ezimotweni, ingakumbi imifuziselo yaseJapan ethe yakhukulisa imarike ngexesha leentlekele ezininzi zamandla kule minyaka ilishumi.[9] 

Ekuqaleni koo-1970, ushicilelo lomyalelo lwaluphakathi kweemveliso zokuqala zorhwebo ezithengiswa kwikhasethi.[9] Kwakukho iinkampani ezisi-8 ezihambisa izinto kwiikhasethi ezinezihloko ezifana noLawulo nokuthengisa iiNkampani (iikhasethi ezili-12, iidola ezingama-300) kunye neSemina yesiGqeba kwiSound kuthotho lweekhasethi zemizuzu engama-60.[9] Kumathala eencwadi, uninzi lweencwadi ezikwiikhasethi bezisenzelwa abantu abaziimfama nabakhubazekileyo, nangona kunjalo ezinye iinkampani ezintsha zabona ithuba lokwenza iincwadi ezimanyelwayo ukwenzela abaphulaphuli ababanzi, njengeVoice Over Books ezivelise abathengisi abashwankathelweyo abanabadlali abaziingcali.[9] Oovulindlela bokuqala baquka imbasa yegolide yeOlimpiki uDuvall Hecht owathi ngo-1975 waseka iCarlifonia-based Books on Tape njengendawo ethe ngqo kwinkonzo yokurenta ngeposi yomthengi kwiincwadi ezirekhodiweyo ezingafinyezwanga kunye nokwandisa iinkonzo zabo zokuthengisa iimveliso zabo kumathala eencwadi kunye neencwadi ezirekhodiweyo ezifumana ukuthandwa ngabakhweli kunye nabahambi.[9] Ngo-1978, uHenry Trentman, umthengisi ohambahambayo owamamela iiteyipu ezithengiswayo ngelixa eqhuba imigama emide, wayenombono wokwenza ushicilelo olungafinyezwanga olusemgangathweni olufundwa ngabadlali abaqeqeshiweyo.[10] Inkampani yakhe, i-Maryland-based Recorded Books, ilandele imodeli yeeNcwadi kwiTape kodwa enomgangatho ophezulu wokurekhodwa kwesitudiyo kunye nabadlali. [10] Iincwadi ezirekhodiweyo kunye neChivers Audio Books zaba zezokuqala ukuphuhlisa amaqela emveliso adibeneyo kunye nokusebenza nabadlali abaqeqeshiweyo.[11]

Ngo-1984, bekukho iinkampani ezilishumi elinanye zokupapasha iincwadi ezirekhodiweyo, eziquka iCaedmon, iMetacom, iNewman Communications, iiRecord Books, iBrilliance kunye neeNcwadi kwiTape.[9] Iinkampani zazincinci, eyona inkulu yayinekhathalogu yezihloko ezingama-200.[9] Ezinye izihloko ezifinyeziweyo zazithengiswa kwiivenkile zeencwadi, njengeWaldenbooks, kodwa zazinamanani entengiso angahoywanga, ezininzi zazithengiswa ngokurhuma nge-odolo yeposi okanye ngamathala eencwadi.[9] Nangona kunjalo, ngo-1984, iBrilliance Audio yenza ubuchule bokurekhoda ngokuphindwe kabini kwikhasethi enye ngaloo ndlela ivumela ushicilelo olungafinyezwanga olufikelelekayo.[9] Ubuchule bubandakanya ukurekhoda kwitshaneli nganye yezimbini zengoma nganye yestiriyo.[9] Oku kwavulela amathuba amatsha emarikeni yaye ngoSeptemba 1985, abapapashi Beveki nganye bachonga abapapashi beencwadi ezirekhodiweyo abangamashumi amabini ananye.[9] Ezi ziquka abavakalisi abatsha abakhulu abafana noHarper noRow, iRandom House, kunye noNxibelelwano lweWarner.[9] 

I-1986 ichongiwe njengendawo yokuguqula ishishini, xa ikhulile ukusuka kumdla wokulinga. [9] Iziganeko ezininzi zenzekile: iAudio Publishers Association, umbutho worhwebo ongenzi nzuzo, wasekwa ngabapapashi abathe bajoyina ukukhuthaza ulwazi lwelizwi elithethwayo kunye nokubonelela ngezibalo zoshishino.[9] Ixesha-Ubomi baqala ukunika amalungu iincwadi ezirekhodiweyo. [9] Iklabhu ye-Book-of-the-Nyanga yaqala ukubonelela ngeencwadi zomsindo kumalungu ayo, njengoko kwenza i-Literary Guild. Ezinye iiklabhu ezinje ngeKlabhu yeeNcwadi zeMbali, iKlabhu ethi Get Rich, iNostalgia Book Club, iklabhu yeSifundo yabantwana zonke zaqala ukunika iincwadi ezimanyelwayo.[9] Abapapashi baqalisa ukukhupha izihloko zonqulo nezikhuthazayo kwiivenkile ezithengisa iincwadi zamaKristu. NgoMeyi 1987, iPublishers Weekly yaqalisa uluhlu oluqhelekileyo lokugubungela ishishini.[9] Ekupheleni kuka-1987, imarike ye-audiobook yayiqikelelwa ukuba yimalike ye-200 yezigidi zeedola, kunye neencwadi ezirekhodiweyo kwikhasethi zazithengiswa kwi-75% yeevenkile zeencwadi zengingqi kunye nezizimeleyo ezihlolwe ngabapapashi beVeki. NgoAgasti 1988 kwakukho abavakalisi beencwadi ezirekhodiweyo ezingamashumi amane, malunga nokuphindaphinda kane kunowe-1984.[9] 

Phakathi kwiminyaka yee-1990, ishishini lokupapasha ngokuvakalayo lakhula laya kutsho kwi-1.5 yebhiliyoni yeedola ngonyaka ngokwexabiso lokuthengisa.[12] Kwi-1996, i-Audio Publishers Association yaseka i-Audie Awards kwii-audiobooks, ezilingana ne-Oscar yeshishini le-audiobook. Abatyunjwa babhengezwa minyaka le ngoFebruwari. Abaphumeleleyo babhengezwa kwisidlo segala ngoMeyi, ngokuqhelekileyo ngokubambisana neBookExpo America. [13]
 
1996 ukuza kuthi ga ngoku
Ngokusasazwa kwe-Intanethi kubathengi ngeminyaka yoo-1990, isantya sokukhuphela ngokukhawuleza ngetekhnoloji ye-broadband, iifomati ezintsha zeaudio ezicinezelweyo kunye nabadlali beendaba abaphathwayo, ukuthandwa kweencwadi ezirekhodiweyo kunyuke kakhulu ngasekupheleni kweminyaka yoo-1990 kunye no-2000. Ngo-1997, eziviwayo nguvulindlela oyena mdlali wokuqala we-digital media market mass-market, ogama lingu "The Audible Player", [14] yathengiswa nge-200 yeedola, yabanjwa iiyure ezi-2 zomsindo kwaye yachazwa ngokuba "incinci kwaye ikhaphukhaphu kune-Walkman", isidlali sekhasethi esasetyenziswa ngelo xesha. [15] Iincwadi zeaudio zeDijithali yayilinyathelo elitsha elibalulekileyo njengoko zazivumela abaphulaphuli inkululeko kumajelo eendaba aphathekayo afana neekhasethi kunye neeCMP3sas ezazifuna ukuthuthwa ngeposi, zivumela ukhuphelo olukhawulezileyo lokukhuphela kwiilayibrari ezikwi-intanethi ezinobukhulu obungenamda, kunye nokuphatheka kusetyenziswa izixhobo ezincinci nezikhaphukhaphu. I-Audible.com yaba yeyokuqala ukuseka iwebhusayithi, kwi-1998, apho ii-audiobooks zedijithali zingathengwa khona. 

Enye into entsha yayiyindalo ye-LibriVox kwi-2005 ngumlobi waseMontreal u-Hugh McGuire owabuza umbuzo kwiblogi yakhe: "Ngaba umnatha unokubamba iqela lamavolontiya ekuncedeni ukuzisa iincwadi kwindawo yoluntu ebomini nge-podcasting?" Ngaloo ndlela kwaqala ukuyilwa kweencwadi zomsindo zedomeyini yoluntu ngababali abavolontiya. Ekupheleni kuka-2021, iLibriVox yayinekhathalogu yemisebenzi engaphezu kwe-16,870.[16] 

Utshintsho ukusuka kwivinyl, ukuya kwikhasethi, ukuya kwiCD, ukuya kwiMP3CD, ukuya kukhuphelo lwedijithali kuye kwabhalwa nguMbutho wabapapashi beAudio kuphando lonyaka (utshintsho lwangaphambili ukusuka kwirekhodi ukuya kwikhasethi luchazwe kwicandelo leminyaka yee-1970). Unyaka wokugqibela wokuba iikhasethi zimele ngaphezu kwe-50% yeentengiso zeemarike zizonke yayingu-2002. [17] Iikhasethi zaye zatshintshwa ziiCDs njengeyona ndlela iphambili ngo-2003–2004. IiCDs zafikelela kwincopho ye-78% yentengiso ngo-2008, [18] emva koko yaqala ukuhla ngokuthanda ukhuphelo lwedijithali. Uphando luka-2012 lufumene iiCDs zibalwa "malunga nesiqingatha" sayo yonke intengiso ethetha ukuba yayingaseyona nto iphambili (i-APA ayizange ichaze amanani okukhuphela idijithali ngo-2012, kodwa ngo-2011 ii-CDs zibalelwa kwi-53% kunye nokukhuphela kwedijithali yi-41%).[19][20] I-APA iqikelela ukuba ukuthengiswa kwe-audiobook kwi-2015 kwifomathi yedijithali kunyuke nge-34% ngaphezu kwe-2014. 

Ukuvela kwakhona kokubaliswa kwamabali okuvakalayo kubalelwa ngokubanzi kwinkqubela phambili yetekhnoloji ephathwayo efana nee-smartphones, iitafile, kunye neenkqubo zokuzonwabisa zemultimedia ezimotweni, ezaziwa ngokuba ngamaqonga eemoto aqhagamshelweyo.[22][23] Ushicilelo lwedrama yomsindo nayo ngoku ipodcast kwi-intanethi. [24] 

Ngo-2014, uBob kunye noDebra Deyan beDeyan Audio bavula i-Deyan Institute of Vocal Artistry and Technology, ikhampasi yokuqala yehlabathi kunye nesikolo sokufundisa ubugcisa kunye nobuchwepheshe bokuveliswa kwee-audiobook.[25]

Ngo-2018, malunga ne-50,000 yee-audiobooks zarekhodwa e-United States ngokukhula kwentengiso yeepesenti ezingama-20 unyaka nonyaka.[26] Intengiso ye-audiobook yase-US ngo-2019 iphelele kwi-1.2 yeebhiliyoni zeedola, inyuke nge-16% ukusuka kunyaka ophelileyo. Ukongeza kunyuso lwentengiso, uphando lwesizwe lwe-Edison Research lwabaphulaphuli beaudiobook yaseMelika abaneminyaka eyi-18 ukuya phezulu bafumanisa ukuba umndilili yenani leencwadi ezimanyelwayo ngonyaka lenyuke ukusuka kwi-6.8 ngo-2019 ukuya kwi-8.1 ngo-2020. 

EJamani 
Indaleko kunye nokusetyenziswa kweaudiobooks eJamani (Hörbuch, "incwadi yokuphulaphula") ihambelana ngokusondeleyo ne-US. Umzekelo okhethekileyo wokusetyenziswa kwayo yiWest German Audio Book Library for the Blind, eyasekwa ngo-1955. Abadlali abavela kwithiyetha kamasipala eMünster barekhoda iincwadi zokuqala ezirekhodiweyo zabo bangaboni kakuhle kwisitudiyo esiphuculiweyo esifakwe iibhokisi zamaqanda. Ngenxa yokuba ii-tram zadlula, ezi mveliso zokuqala zenzeka ebusuku. Kamva, imibhalo yarekhodwa zizithethi eziqeqeshiweyo kwizitudiyo zobuchule zaza zasasazwa kubasebenzisi ngeposi. Kude kube ngoo-1970 ushicilelo lwalukwiteyiphu reels, emva koko iikhasethi. Ukusukela ngo-2004, iminikelo irekhodwe kumgangatho weDAISY Digital Talking Book MP3, ebonelela ngeempawu ezongezelelweyo kubasebenzisi abangaboni kakuhle ukuba bamamele kwaye bajonge izinto ezibhaliweyo ngokuvayo.[28] Iincwadi zeAudio 

zaseIndiya 
eIndiya zaqala ukuvela emva kwexesha elithile kunakwilizwe liphela. Kuphela ngo-2010 apho ii-Audiobooks zafumana ukuthandwa okuqhelekileyo kwimarike yaseIndiya. Oku kuqala kungenxa yokungabikho kwemigudu yangaphambili ecwangcisiweyo ngakwicala labapapashi nababhali. Iinzame zentengiso kunye nokufumaneka kwee-Audiobooks zenze i-Indiya njengenye yezona marike ze-Audiobooks ezikhula ngokukhawuleza kwihlabathi.[cating] 

Indlela yokuphila yabemi base-Indiya basezidolophini kunye nelona xesha liphezulu lokuhamba mihla le kwihlabathi liye lanceda ekwenzeni ii-Audiobooks zidume kulo mmandla. Iincwadi zoShishino kunye nokuziNcedisa zinomtsalane kakhulu kwaye ziye zaziwa kakhulu kunezo zintsomi/ezingezontsomi.[cating] Oku kungenxa yokuba ii-Audiobooks zibonwa ikakhulu njengendlela yokuziphucula kunye nemfundo, endaweni yokuzonwabisa. 

Iincwadi ezirekhodiweyo zikhutshwa ngeelwimi ezahlukeneyo zaseIndiya. NgesiMalayalam, inoveli yokuqala yomsindo, enesihloko Ibhodi ye-Ouija, yakhululwa yiKathacafe ngo-2018. [29] 

EMzantsi Korea 
Kwicandelo lokushicilela laseKorea, ekubeni ishishini le-audiobook laqala ngo-2000, liye lanyamalala ngenxa yokungaphumeleli kwayo ukufumana iziphumo ezinentsingiselo. 

Phantse iminyaka engama-20 kamva, umdla kwiselula unyukile ngo-2019, kodwa kusekho imisebenzi ekufuneka isonjululwe. 

Okokuqala, i-Audiobook yayingenayo inkxaso eninzi yomgaqo-nkqubo enxulumene noshishino, kwaye okwesibini, i-Audiobook yemveliso yeziseko zophuhliso yayingonelanga. Okwesithathu, uphando kunye nophuhliso lwetekhnoloji, olufana nezemfundo, aluzange lusebenze ukuze luqhubeke lukhula njengoshishino lwe-Audiobook.[30]
 
Imveliso
Ukuvelisa i-audiobook iquka umbalisi ohleli kwindawo yokurekhoda efunda isicatshulwa, ngelixa injineli yesitudiyo kunye nomlawuli werekhodi kunye nokuqondisa ukusebenza. [31] Ukuba kukho impazamo ushicilelo luyayekwa aze umbalisi alufunde kwakhona.[31] Ngenkqubela phambili yakutsha kubuchwepheshe bokurekhoda, iincwadi ezininzi ezirekhodiweyo ngoku zirekhodwa kwizitudiyo zasekhaya ngababalisi abasebenza ngokuzimeleyo.[32] Ii-audiobooks eziveliswe ngamaziko amakhulu opapasho zivavanywa kunye nenkqubo yokuhlela emva kokuba ingxelo irekhodwe. 

Ababalisi badla ngokuhlawulwa ngesiseko seyure erekhodiweyo egqityiweyo, oku kuthetha ukuba kuthathe iiyure ezingama-20 ukuvelisa incwadi yeeyure ezi-5, umbalisi uhlawulwa iiyure ezi-5, ngaloo ndlela enika inkuthazo yokungenzi iimpazamo.[31] Kuxhomekeke kubalisa bahlawulwa US$150 ngeyure egqityiweyo ukuya US $400 (ukusukela 2011).[31] Uninzi lwababalisi bakwasebenza njengabavelisi kwaye bahambisa iincwadi ezirekhodiweyo eziveliswe ngokupheleleyo, ezilungisiweyo, zafundiswa, kwaye zavavanywa. Basenokubiza i-$75–$125 eyongezelelweyo ngeyure egqityiweyo ukongeza kumrhumo wabo wokubalisa ukulungelelanisa nokuhlawula iinkonzo zasemva kwemveliso. Iindleko ezipheleleyo zokuvelisa i-audiobook inokwahluka kakhulu, njengoko iincwadi ezinde zifuna ixesha elininzi lesitudiyo kunye nababalisi abaziwayo ngakumbi beza kwiprimiyamu. Ngokutsho kommeli kwi-Audible, iindleko zokurekhoda i-audiobook ziye zawa malunga ne-US $ 25,000 ekupheleni kwe-1990 ukuya malunga ne-US $ 2,000-US $ 3,000 ngo-2014. [33] 

Iifomathi 
Jonga kwakhona: Uluhlu lwexesha lweefomathi ezimanyelwayo 

Ingqokelela yeencwadi ezimanyelwayo kwithala leencwadi. Umxube wekhasethi kunye neefomathi ze-CD-ROM. 
Ii-audiobooks zisasazwa kuyo nayiphi na ifomati yomsindo ekhoyo, kodwa ngokuyintloko ezi ziirekhodi, iikhasethi, ii-CD, ii-MP3 CD, iifomati zedijithali ezikhutshelwayo (umzekelo, iMP3 (.mp3), iWindows Media Audio (.wma), i-Advanced Audio Coding (.aac)), kunye nemeko eqinileyo elayishwe kwangaphambili izixhobo zedijithali apho umxholo womsindo ulayishwe kwangaphambili kwaye uthengiswa kunye nesixhobo sehardware. 

Ngomnyaka we-1955, umqambi waseJamani wazisa inkqubo ye-Cassette ye-Sound Book esekelwe kwifomathi ye-Tefifon apho endaweni ye-tape magnetic isandi sarekhodwa kwi-loop eqhubekayo yeribhoni ye-vinylite ye-grooved efana ne-tape ye-8-track endala. Nangona i-Tefifon yasekuqaleni eyayisekelwe kuyo iqhutywe kwi-19 CPS kwaye ikwazi ukubamba ubuninzi beeyure ze-4, enye iNcwadi yeSandi yayinokubamba iiyure ezisibhozo zokurekhoda njengoko ibaleka kwisiqingatha sesantya okanye i-9.5 CPS. Nangona kunjalo, kanye njengeTefifon, ifomathi ayizange isasazeke ekusetyenzisweni.[34] 

Inani elincinane leencwadi zirekhodelwa kusasazo lukanomathotholo, ludla ngokwenziwa ngokufutshane kwaye ngamanye amaxesha zenziwe iisiriyeli. Ii-audiobooks zinokuza njengeenguqulelo ezidlalwe ngokupheleleyo zencwadi eprintiweyo, ngamanye amaxesha zibiza umboniso opheleleyo, umculo, kunye nesandi. Ngokufanelekileyo iidrama ezimanyelwayo, ezi audiobooks zaziwa njengee-audiobooks ezigcweleyo. Izikhululo zikanomathotholo ze-BBC iRadio 3, iRadio 4, kunye neRadio 4 Eyongezelelweyo ziye zasasaza imveliso efana noWilliam Gibson inoveli ethi Neuromancer. [35]

Imveliso yokuqala yomsindo ngumsebenzi welizwi elithethiweyo eliyimveliso yoqobo kodwa engasekelwanga kwincwadi. Imizekelo ibandakanya uJoe Hill, unyana kaStephen King, owakhupha iVinyl First audiobook ebizwa ngokuba yi-Dark Carousel ngo-2018. Ifike kwi-vinyl ye-2-LP iseti, okanye njengeMP3 ekhuphekayo, kodwa akukho mbhalo oshicilelweyo. [36] Omnye umzekelo ubandakanya i-Spin, i-Audiobook Musical (2018), inguqulelo yomculo kaRumpelstiltskin ebaliswa nguJim Dale, kunye neqela leenkwenkwezi zomculo zeBroadway. [37] 

Sebenzisa 

iAudiobook esetyenziselwa ukusasaza ulwazi kumafama aseKenya. 
Iincwadi ezirekhodiweyo zisetyenziselwe ukufundisa abantwana ukufunda nokwandisa ukuqonda kokufunda. Zikwaluncedo nakwiimfama. IThala leeNcwadi leSizwe leNgqungquthela e-US kunye neThala leeNcwadi le-CNIB eKhanada libonelela ngeentlawulo zeenkonzo zethala leencwadi ze-audiobook kubantu abangaboni kakuhle; iincwadi eziceliweyo zithunyelwa ngeposi (ngaphandle kweendleko) kubathengi. Yasekwa ngo-1996, i-Assistive Media ka-Ann Arbor, eMichigan yaba ngumbutho wokuqala ukuvelisa nokuhambisa urekhodo oluthethwayo lweentatheli ezibhaliweyo kunye nemisebenzi yoncwadi nge-Intanethi ukunceda abantu abangaboniyo. 

Malunga neepesenti ezingama-40 zokusetyenziswa kweencwadi ezimanyelwayo kwenzeka kumathala eencwadi oluntu, kwaye intsalela isetyenziswa ikakhulu kwiivenkile ezithengisa iincwadi. Iinkqubo zokukhuphela ithala leencwadi ngoku zikhula ngokukhawuleza (ngaphezu kwama-5,000 amathala eencwadi oluntu anikezela ngeencwadi ezirekhodiweyo simahla). Amathala eencwadi akwayindawo edumileyo yokujonga iincwadi ezirekhodiweyo ngendlela yeCD.[38] Ngokutsho kweSibonelelo seSizwe soFundo lwezoBugcisa, "Ukufunda kuMngcipheko: Uvavanyo loLwazi lokuFunda eMelika" (2004), ukuphulaphula iincwadi ezirekhodiweyo kwandisa ulwazi lokufunda nokubhala ngokubanzi.[39] 

Iinkqubo zokumamela 
Jonga kwakhona: Ialbham yamagama athethwayo 
Ngenxa yokuma kwayo, umntu unokumamela i-audiobook ngelixa esenza eminye imisebenzi, enjengokuhlamba impahla, ukwenza umthambo, ukuhlakula, kunye nemisebenzi efana nale. Olona setyenziso luqhelekileyo lweencwadi ezirekhodiweyo ngabantu abadala kuxa behamba ngemoto okanye ngelixa behamba ngezithuthi zikawonke-wonke, njengenye indlela yonomathotholo okanye umculo. 

Uphando lwakutsha nje olukhutshwe yiAudio Publishers Association lufumanise ukuba uninzi lwabasebenzisi beaudiobook bamamela emotweni, kwaye ngaphezulu kwesibini esithathwini sabathengi be-audiobook bachaza iincwadi zeaudio njengendlela yokuphumla kunye nendlela elungileyo yokwenza izinto ezininzi. Esinye isizathu esichaziweyo sokukhetha ii-audiobooks kunezinye iifomati kukuba ukusebenza kwesandi kwenza ezinye iincwadi zibe nomdla ngakumbi. [40] 

Iindlela eziqhelekileyo zokuphulaphula zibandakanya: 

Ukudlala kwakhona: Kuxhomekeke kumlinganiselo womntu wengqwalasela kunye nomdla, kudla ngokuba yimfuneko ukumamela amacandelo e-audiobook ngaphezu kwesihlandlo esinye ukuvumela umbandela ukuba uqondwe kwaye ugcinwe ngokwanelisayo. Ukuphindaphinda kunokwenziwa ngokukhawuleza okanye emva kwexesha elongeziweyo.
Ukufunda: Abantu banokumamela i-audiobook (idla ngokungafinyezwanga) ngelixa belandela kwincwadi yokwenyani. Oku kubanceda bafunde amagama abasenokungawafundi kakuhle ukuba bebenokufunda incwadi kuphela. Oku kunokuba yindlela ephumelelayo yokufunda ulwimi olutsha.
I-Multitasking: Uninzi lwabaphulaphuli beaudiobook bakhetha ifomathi kuba ivumela ukwenza izinto ezininzi ngexesha elinye okanye imisebenzi yesiqhelo efana nemithambo, ukwenza ubugcisa, okanye ukupheka. 
Ukuzonwabisa: Ii-audiobooks ziye zaba yindlela ethandwayo yokuzonwabisa yohambo kwiintsapho okanye kubakhweli. [41] 
Imibutho yesisa kunye nengenzi nzuzo 

Umzekelo we studio yomsindo yokufunda ngobuchule. Isitudiyo sijikelezwe ngeepaneli ze-baffle zesandi ukunciphisa isandi esisuka kwisithethi, sivumela imakrofoni ukuba ithathe isandi esicacileyo. 
Yasekwa ngo-1948, iLearning Ally ikhonza ngaphezu kwama-300,000 K–12, abafundi beekholeji kunye nabaphumelele izidanga, amagqala kunye nabafundi abakhubazekileyo ubomi babo bonke, okt abangakwaziyo ukufunda ushicilelo oluqhelekileyo ngenxa yokungaboni, ukungaboni kakuhle, idyslexia, okanye ezinye iziphene zokufunda. Ukufunda ingqokelela ka-Ally engaphezulu kwe-80,000 yeencwadi ezibaliswa ngabantu kunye nezihloko zoncwadi zinokukhutshelwa kwii-smartphones eziqhelekileyo kunye neetafile, kwaye yeyona inkulu yohlobo lwayo emhlabeni. 

Yasekwa ngo-2002, i-Bookshare lithala leencwadi elikwi-intanethi lee-audiobook ezifundwa ngekhompyutha kwiifomathi ezifikelelekayo kubantu abakhubazekileyo bokushicilela. 

Yasekwa ngo-2005, iLibriVox ikwalithala leencwadi elikwi-intanethi leencwadi ezikhutshelwayo kunye nombutho wasimahla ongenzi nzuzo ophuhliswe nguHugh McGuire. Ineencwadi ezirekhodiweyo zoluntu ngeelwimi ezininzi.[42] 

Ithala leencwadi leCaliber Audio licandelo lesisa lase-UK elibonelela ngenkonzo engahlawulelwayo yeencwadi ezirekhodiweyo ezingafinyezwanga kubantu abanengxaki yokubona, i-dyslexia okanye ezinye iziphene, abangakwaziyo ukufunda ushicilelo. Banethala leencwadi elinezihloko ezingaphezu kwama-8,550 zamabali angeyonyani nezingezontsomi ezinokubolekwa ngeposi kwiiCD zeMP3 kunye neememori stickers okanye ngokusasaza.[43] 

Iincwadi zokuMamela yi-UK audiobook yesisa ebonelela ngokusasazwa kwe-intanethi, ukukhuphela kunye nenkonzo yeposi kuye nabani na okhubazekileyo okanye ogulayo nto leyo eyenza kube nzima ukubamba incwadi, ukutyhila amaphepha ayo, okanye ukufunda ngendlela eqhelekileyo, oku kuquka abantu abanengxaki yokubona, ngokomzimba, yokufunda okanye yengqondo. Baneencwadi ezirekhodiweyo zokuzonwabisa kunye nokufunda kunye nethala leencwadi elinezihloko ezingaphezu kwama-7,500 ezirekhodwe kwizitudiyo zabo zedijithali okanye zifumaneke kurhwebo. 

IRoyal National Institute of the Blind People (RNIB) lisisa lase-UK elibonelela ngenkonzo yethala leencwadi leeNcwadi zokuthetha. Ii-audiobooks zibonelelwa ngefomathi ye-DAISY kwaye zisiwa endlwini yomfundi ngeposi njenge-CD okanye i-USB memory stick. Kukho ngaphezu kwe-30,000 yeencwadi zeaudio ezikhoyo onokuziboleka, ezisimahla ukuba ziprintwe amalungu ethala leencwadi elikhubazekileyo. I-RNIB ibonelela ngenkxaso-mali yenkonzo yeeNcwadi zokuthetha malunga ne-4 yezigidi zeerandi ngonyaka.

Umntu onesiphene sokushicilela “ngumntu ongakwaziyo ukufunda ngokukuko ushicilelo ngenxa yembonakalo, yomzimba, yengqondo, yophuhliso, yengqondo, okanye yokukhubazeka ekufundeni.”[1] Isiphene sokushicilela sithintela umntu ekufumaneni ulwazi kwizinto ezishicilelweyo ngendlela eqhelekileyo, kwaye kufuna ukuba basebenzise ezinye iindlela zokufikelela olo lwazi. Iziphene zoshicilelo ziquka ukungaboni kakuhle, iziphene zokufunda, okanye iziphene ngokwasemzimbeni ezithintela ubuchule bokuyila incwadi.[2] Eli gama layilwa nguGeorge Kerscher, uvulindlela kwiincwadi zokuthetha zedijithali. [3] IDAISY isetyenziswa ngamathala eencwadi njengendlela yokwenza iincwadi ezintsonkothileyo zifumaneke ngokuvakalayo.[4] 

Inkomfa eyayiququzelelwe yiWorld Intellectual Property Organisation (WIPO) eMarrakesh, eMorocco, ngoJuni ka-2013 yamkela isivumelwano esikhethekileyo esibizwa ngokuba "IsiVumelwano sokuLungiselela ukuFikelela kwiMisebenzi ePapashiweyo ngabantu abangaboniyo kunye nabantu abaKhubazekileyo ngokuShicilela" (ngokufutshane iSivumelwano se-VIP saseMarrakesh).[5][6] 

ISivumelwano saseMarrakesh simele utshintsho olubalulekileyo kwindlela abenzi bomthetho abalinganisa ngayo amabango abanini-copyright ngokuchasene nomdla wabantu abakhubazekileyo ngokukodwa, kunye nenqaku elinokubakho kwipolitiki ye-copyright jikelele ngokubanzi. 

Amanyathelo 
I-Accessible Books Consortium (ABC), eyasungulwa ngo-2014, yathathwa njenge "inyathelo elinye elinokwenzeka, phakathi kwezinye, ukuphumeza ngokubonakalayo iinjongo zeSivumelwano saseMarrakesh".[7] I-ABC ijolise ekwandiseni inani leencwadi kwihlabathi jikelele kwiifomathi ezifikelelekayo-ezifana ne-braille, i-audio kunye noshicilelo olukhulu-kunye nokuzenza zifumaneke kubantu abangaboniyo, abangaboni kakuhle okanye abashicilelwe ngenye indlela. 

Upapasho olufikelelekayo yindlela yokupapasha noyilo lweencwadi apho iincwadi nezinye izicatshulwa zenziwa zifumaneke ngeendlela ezizezinye ezenzelwe ukunceda okanye endaweni yenkqubo yokufunda. Ibaluleke kakhulu kubantu abangaboniyo, abangaboniyo okanye abashicilelweyo. 

Iifomathi ezizezinye eziye zaphuhliswa ukunceda abantu abohlukeneyo ukuba bafunde ziquka iindidi zeefonti ezinkulu, iifonti ezikhethekileyo zohlobo oluthile lokukhubazeka kokufunda, i-braille, i-e-books, kunye ne-audiobooks ezenzekelayo kunye ne-DAISY yedijithali ethetha iincwadi. 

Upapasho olufikelelekayo lwenziwe lula ngophuhliso lwetekhnoloji efana nokuprintwa ngokwemfuno (POD), abafundi be-e-book, ifomathi yedatha ecwangcisiweyo ye-XML, ifomathi ye-EPUB3 kunye ne-Intanethi. 

Injongo 
Injongo yopapasho olufikelelekayo kukwenza ukufunda kube lula kwabo banobunzima bokwenza oko. Eli qela liquka abantu abaziimfama okanye abangaboni kakuhle, abaneziphene zokufunda, nabantu abafunda ulwimi lwesibini. Ushicilelo olufikelelekayo lukwanenjongo yokuvumela abantu ukuba bafunde nayiphi na ifomathi ebavumela ukuba bafunde ngokukhawuleza okanye ibavumele ukuba bayifunxe inkcazelo ngendlela engcono.

Kwinkulungwane yamashumi amabini ananye, injongo yopapasho olufikelelekayo kukwenza ukuba yonke incwadi ifumaneke ngazo zonke iindlela ukuze wonke umfundi akwazi ukufunda ngokulula nangobuchule. 

Izikhokelo kunye nobuchule bokupapasha kwiifomathi ezifikelelekayo zenziwe zifumaneke yimibutho eliqela kunye nababhali, kubandakanywa: 

EDITEUR: "UkuFikelela ukuPapasha - Izikhokelo zokuSebenza eziPhuculo".[1] 
UMat Garrish: "I-EPUB efumanekayo 3" (isahluko esifumaneka ngokukhululekileyo kwi-EPUB 3 Iindlela eziGqwesileyo zikaMatt Garrish noMarkus Gylling, O'Reilly, 2013) [2] 
"Izikhokelo zeMedia yeDijithali eFikelelekayo" yiZiko leSizwe leMedia yokuFikelela (NCAM).[3] 
"Ukwenza iifayile zePDF zifikeleleke: izikhokelo zenqanaba lokudala i-DTP" yi-AcceDe PDF.[4] 
"Yenza uxwebhu lwePDF lufikeleleke kwi-Adobe InDesign kunye ne-Acrobat Pro"[5] 
"Yenza uxwebhu lwePDF lufumaneke kwiMicrosoft Word"[6] 
Imbali 
Ngaphambi kwenkulungwane yama-21, ishishini lopapasho laligxile ekuvelisweni kweencwadi ezishicilelweyo. Ithiyori ephambili yopapasho, eyayigxininisa uqoqosho lwesikali, yayithande ukwenza uhlobo olunye lwencwadi ekhoyo. Ngale ndlela zinokuveliswa ngobuninzi kwaye zenziwe zifumaneke kuluntu ngokubanzi. Le modeli ayizange ivumele nayiphi na enye ifomathi ukuba ifumaneke ngokubanzi, nangona kunjalo. 

Kubekho intaphane yophuhliso lweteknoloji eyandisa ukufikeleleka kweencwadi. Eyokuqala kwezi yaba kuphuhliso lwenkqubo yokubhala yebraille nguLouis Braille ngo-1821. [7] Kwabakho ke uphuhliso lweencwadi ezirekhodiweyo ezasuka kwiNkongolo yase-United States ngo-1931 [8] kwaye zaduma ngokuqhubekayo ekurekhodeni nasekusetyenzisweni kwabadlali belizwi. 

Ngo-1980, iThorndike Press yabakho njengompapashi kwakhona weencwadi ezinkulu zoshicilelo.[9][10] UThorndike uthenge amalungelo oshicilelo olukhulu lweencwadi kubapapashi emva koko waphinda wazipapasha ngefomathi enkulu nefikelelekayo kubantu abanengxaki yokufunda. 

Uphuhliso lwakutsha nje 
Abafundi abatsha abaphathwayo, abafana neemveliso zeVictor Reader[11] kunye nePlextalk Pocket[12] baphatha iincwadi ezithetha ngeendlela ezahlukeneyo eziquka iDAISY Digital Talking Book, MP3, umbhalo kuphela, kunye nezinye ezininzi. 

Ubuchwephesha obutsha, obufana nokwaziswa kwiSony Reader[13] ka-2004 kunye neAmazon's Kindle[14] ngo-2007, inike isakhono sokuguqula ubungakanani befonti ngokuzenzekelayo. 
 
ReadHowYouWant yenye inkokeli ekuphuhliseni obu bugcisa.[15] Isebenza ngentsebenziswano nabapapashi ukwenza iincwadi zifumaneke ngazo zonke iindlela kwihlabathi liphela.[16] Oku kuquka iifonti eziyilwe ngokukodwa ze-dyslexia, ukuwohloka kwe-macular kunye neengxaki zokulandelela umgca.
Ushicilelo olukhulu (kwakhona luluhlobo olukhulu okanye ifonti enkulu) lubhekisa kufomatho lwencwadi okanye olunye uxwebhu lokubhaliweyo apho ubungakanani befonti bukhulu kakhulu kunesiqhelo ukuze kuhlaliswe abantu abangaboni kakuhle. Rhoqo i-medium nayo inyuswa ngobukhulu ukuze ivumelane nesicatshulwa esikhulu. Amathala eencwadi aneemfuno ezikhethekileyo kunye namathala eencwadi amaninzi kawonke-wonke aya kuba neencwadi ezinombhalo omkhulu, kunye neenguqulelo ezibhalwe ngeBraille.

Ubungakanani befonti yoshicilelo olukhulu luqhelekile ukuba bubuncinci ngamanqaku ali-18 ubukhulu, bulingana no-24px kubungakanani befonti yewebhu yeCSS. Ubungakanani obahlukeneyo benziwa ukuba bulungele iimfuno ezahlukeneyo zokubonwayo, kunye nomgaqo oqhelekileyo wobhontsi ukuba ubuncinci buphindwe kabini ubuncinci besayizi ye-acuity.[1] 


Iincwadi ezinkulu zoshicilelo 
Imigangatho yokupapasha 
I-American National Association for Visually Handicapped (NAVH) ibonelela ngeSitywina se-NAVH sokuVunywa kubapapashi bezorhwebo e-US, kwiincwadi ezihlangabezana nemigangatho yazo enkulu yoshicilelo.[2] (I-Lighthouse International yafumana i-NAVH ngo-2010.) [3] 

Imigangatho[4] ibiza: 

Imida ephezulu kubukhulu, ubukhulu, kunye nobunzima 
Ubuncinane bomlinganiselo kwimida 
yohlobo lwesayizi ubuncinane ye-14 inqaku, ngokukhethekileyo i-18 inqaku[5] I 
-Sans serif okanye ifonti eguquliweyo ye-serif ecetyiswayo 
Unobumba owaneleyo kunye nesithuba segama 
esicetyiswayo kwi-Flexible book evulekileyo kwi-Flexible book evumela ukuba i-Flexible ivuleleke 

kwi 
-American Print. Imfama ichaza ubungakanani befonti ngolu hlobo: 

12 pt = iprinta rhoqo 
14–16 pt = "yandisiwe" print (engagqalwanga ngoshicilelo olukhulu) 
18 pt kunye nenkulu = iprinta enkulu 
18 pt kunye nenkulu kunye nolunye utshintsho lokufomatha = ushicilelo olwandisiweyo 
Ukongeza ekwandiseni ubungakanani bohlobo, ukwakheka kwephepha kunye neempawu zefonti kunokuba nefuthe elihle ekufundeni. Iifonti eziyilelwe ukufundeka zenza kube lula ukwahlula umlinganiswa omnye komnye. Ezinye iimpawu eziphambili zefonti ezinjalo zezi:[6] 

Unobumba ophezulu "I" kunye nenani lesiRoma "I", inani "1", kunye nonobumba omncinci "l" kufuneka abonakale ahlukile kwenye. 
Ifonti kufuneka ibe nomzimba obanzi kunye nesithuba phakathi konobumba ngamnye. 
Oonobumba abane "bubble" ngaphakathi kubo (eyaziwa ngokuba yikhawuntara, njengo-o, d, g, e), kufuneka babe nesithuba esaneleyo ngaphakathi kwekhawuntara. 
Iziphumlisi kufuneka zibe ngqukuva, zibe nkulu, kwaye zibonakale kakhulu. 
Imivumbo yefonti kufuneka yomelele kwaye ingabi nazikhewu. 

Imizekelo yeefonti ezifundeka lula yi-Antique Olive, iTahoma, iTiresias, kunye neVerdana. IiNkampani 

zeRatios 
ezibonelela ngoshicilelo olukhulu lokufomatha zisebenzisa iifomati ezahlukeneyo (ekwabizwa ngokuba yiratio) ukuxhasa ubungakanani befonti enkulu.[7] Phakathi kwezi reshiyo, sifumana: 
phakathi kwabapapashi beencwadi zokuqala ezishicilelweyo ezinkulu, iNkampani yokuPapasha Uhlobo olucacileyo yapapasha ingqokelela yeencwadi ezikuhlobo lwamanqaku angama-36, c. 1910.[8] Inkampani esekwe eOhio ikhethekileyo ngoshicilelo olukhulu, epapasha iincwadi kwi-36pt kunye ne-24pt.
 
Umlinganiselo 1: 1, umxholo wandiswa kwiphepha elilodwa (1) lomzobo kunye nobukhulu obuqhelekileyo betypological ngamanqaku ali-18.
I-Retiyo 1:2, umxholo wandiswa kwiphepha le-landscape ezimbini (2) kunye nobukhulu obuqhelekileyo be-typological ngamanqaku ali-18. 
Imilinganiselo yesiko, umxholo wandiswa kumaphepha amaninzi e-landscape kunye nobukhulu obuqhelekileyo be-typological ngamanqaku angama-28. 
Imbali 
yoShicilelo olukhulu 
ngo-1914 uRobert Irwin wavelisa uthotho lweencwadi zesikhokelo kumanqaku angama-36, ezilungiselelwe abantwana abangaboni kakuhle kwizikolo zaseCleveland, eOhio. Olu hlobo lubonakalise ukuba lukhulu kakhulu kwaye lwayekwa ngokukhawuleza kumanqaku angama-24 adumileyo. Uphando olwaxhaswa ngu-Irwin ngo-1919 lubonise uhlobo lwamanqaku angama-24 ukuba lolona lufundekayo kobukhulu obuvavanyiweyo. Uphando olongezelelweyo ngabanye kwi-1952 kunye ne-1959 baxhasa i-18 iphuzu okanye uhlobo lwe-24 yenqaku.[10] 
E-UK ngo-1964, uFrederick Thorpe waqalisa ukupapasha izihloko zoshicilelo eziqhelekileyo ezinohlobo oluphantse luphindwe kabini kunolo lwantlandlolo. Iincwadi zanikwa iibhatyi zothuli ezicacileyo, ezinekhowudi ezinemibala ebonisa iindidi ezinjengeemfihlelo (ezimnyama), iintsomi eziqhelekileyo (ezibomvu), ezothando (ezibhlowu), ezeNtshona (orenji), njl. 
Ngo-1969, inkampani kaThorpe, i-Ulverscroft, yaqala ukuvelisa iincwadi ngodidi lwamanqaku ali-16 kunye nezibophelelo ezinobungakanani obuqhelekileyo, abathi inkampani inyuse ukwamkelwa koshicilelo olukhulu kumathala eencwadi oluntu. Uhlobo lwamanqaku e-16 luncinci kunobuncinci obucetyisiweyo liBhunga leemfama laseMelika, [11] elicebisa inqaku le-20, kunye nenqaku le-18 njengobuncinci obucetyisiweyo.[12] 
Ngo-2008 i-W3.org yakhupha imigangatho yokufikeleleka kwewebhu yeWCAG 2.0, echaza isicatshulwa esikhulu njenge-18pt, eyi-24px kwi-CSS.[13] Ngaphaya koko, umgangatho uxela ukuba abasebenzisi mabakwazi ukwandisa ubungakanani befonti ngama-200% ngaphandle kokwaphula umxholo.[14] 
Namhlanje ushicilelo olukhulu lweencwadi zangoku zipapashwa ngaxeshanye kunye noshicilelo oluqhelekileyo ngabapapashi babo kwaye badla ngokubonisa iibhatyi ezinemibala egcweleyo efanayo kunye noyilo lwebhatyi. Amathala eencwadi kawonke-wonke asoloko enamacandelo amakhulu oshicilelo, kwaye iivenkile ezininzi zeencwadi ziphethe ushicilelo olukhulu. 
"Ushicilelo lukaGoogle" phinda apha; ungabhidaniswa neLifu likaGoogle Shicilela. 
Eli nqaku limalunga nenjini yokukhangela incwadi kaGoogle. Ngenkonzo ye-e-book kaGoogle, jonga iGoogle Play Books. Ngencwadi yabantwana, bona Incwadi kaGoogle. 
Iincwadi zikaGoogle 
zeScreenshot 
Uhlobo lwesayithi yeDijithali yethala leencwadi 
uMnini Google 
URL books.google.com 
Yaziswa ngo-Oktobha 2004; Iminyaka engama-20 eyadlulayo (njengoShicilelo lukaGoogle) 
Imo yangoku iyasebenza







 
Iincwadi zikaGoogle (ezaziwa ngokuba yiGoogle Book Search, Google Print, kunye nekhowudi-igama leProjekthi Ocean) [1] yinkonzo evela kuGoogle ekhangela isicatshulwa esipheleleyo seencwadi kunye neemagazini uGoogle azihlolile, ziguqulelwe kumbhalo usebenzisa ukuqondwa komlinganiswa obonakalayo (OCR), kwaye zigcinwe kuvimba wedatha yedijithali.[2] Iincwadi zibonelelwa mhlawumbi ngabapapashi kunye nababhali ngeNkqubo yoMlingane weeNcwadi zikaGoogle, okanye ngamahlakani ethala likaGoogle ngeProjekthi yeThala leeNcwadi.[3] Ukongeza, uGoogle ubambisene nenani labapapashi bemagazini ukwenza idijithali kugcino lwazo. [4][5]

INkqubo yoMpapashi yaziwa okokuqala njengePrinta kaGoogle xa yayiziswa kuMbono weNcwadi waseFrankfurt ngo-Okthobha ka-2004. IProjekthi yeThala leeNcwadi zikaGoogle, ehlola imisebenzi ekuqokelelweni kwamahlakani ethala leencwadi kwaye yongeze kuluhlu lwezixhobo zedijithali, yabhengezwa ngoDisemba ka-2004 

. ukwenziwa kwedemokhrasi yolwazi.[8] Nangona kunjalo, iphinde yagxekwa ngokuphulwa kwelungelo lokushicilela, [8] [9] kunye nokunqongophala kokuhlela ukulungisa iimpazamo ezininzi ezifakwe kwiitekisi eziskeniweyo yinkqubo ye-OCR. 

Ukusukela ngo-Okthobha ka-2019, uGoogle ubhiyozele iminyaka eli-15 yeeNcwadi zikaGoogle kwaye wabonelela ngenani leencwadi eziskeniweyo njengezihloko ezingaphezu kwezigidi ezingama-40.[10] UGoogle uqikelele ngo-2010 ukuba kukho malunga nezigidi ezili-130 zezihloko ezahlukeneyo emhlabeni, [11] kwaye wathi ufuna ukuziskena zonke. [11] Nangona kunjalo, inkqubo yokuskena kumathala eencwadi emfundo yaseMelika iye yacotha ukusukela ngeminyaka yoo-2000. [12][13] Iinzame zokuskena zeNcwadi yeGoogle zixhomekeke kwisimangalo, kubandakanywa i-Authors Guild v. Google, isimangalo se-class-action e-United States, sagqiba ngokuthanda kukaGoogle (jonga ngezantsi). Eli yayilityala elikhulu elathi lasondela ekutshintshweni kwemithetho yokukhutshelwa kwemisebenzi yeenkedama eUnited States. [14] Uphononongo luka-2023 ngabaphengululi abavela kwiYunivesithi yaseCalifornia, eBerkeley, nakwizikolo zoshishino zeYunivesithi yaseNortheastern yafumanisa ukuba iincwadi zeGoogle Books zikhokelele ekwenyukeni kweentengiso kwiinguqulelo eziphathekayo zeencwadi.[15] 

Iinkcukacha 
Iziphumo ezisuka kwiiNcwadi zikaGoogle zibonakala kuPhendlo lukaGoogle jikelele nakwiwebhusayithi yokukhangela kwiincwadi zikaGoogle (books.google.com). 

Ukuphendula imibuzo yokukhangela, iiNcwadi zikaGoogle zivumela abasebenzisi ukujonga amaphepha apheleleyo kwiincwadi apho amagama ophando avela khona ukuba incwadi ayinalungelo lokushicilela okanye ukuba umnini welungelo lokushicilela unike imvume. Ukuba uGoogle ukholelwa ukuba le ncwadi isephantsi kwelungelo lokushicilela, umsebenzisi ubona "iziqwengana" zombhalo malunga namagama okukhangela abuzwayo. Yonke imizekelo yamagama ophendlo kumbhalo wencwadi ibonakala ngokuqaqamba okutyheli. 

Amanqanaba amane ofikelelo asetyenziswa kwiiNcwadi zikaGoogle ngala:[16] 

Umbono ogcweleyo: Iincwadi ezikwidomeyini yoluntu ziyafumaneka ukuze "zibonwe ngokupheleleyo" kwaye zinokukhutshelwa simahla. Iincwadi eziprintiweyo ezifunyenwe ngeNkqubo yeNtsebenziswano nazo ziyafumaneka ukuze zibonwe ngokupheleleyo ukuba umshicileli unike imvume, nangona oku kunqabile.
I-Preview: Kwiincwadi ezishicilelweyo apho imvume inikwe khona, inani lamaphepha anokubonwa lilinganiselwe "kwi-preview" ebekwe ngeendlela ezahlukeneyo zokufikelela kunye nemilinganiselo yokhuseleko, ezinye zisekelwe ekulandeleni umsebenzisi. Ngesiqhelo, umpapashi unokuseta ipesenti yencwadi ekhoyo ukuze ibonwe kwangaphambili.[17] Abasebenzisi bathintelwe ekukhupheni, ukukhuphela okanye ukuprinta umboniso weencwadi. I-watermark efundwayo ethi "Copyrighted material" ibonakala emazantsi ephepha. Zonke iincwadi ezifunyenwe ngeNkqubo yeNtsebenziswano ziyafumaneka ukuze zijongwe. 
Imbono yesiqwengana: "Imbono yesiqwengana" - imigca emibini ukuya kwemithathu yombhalo ojikeleze igama lokukhangela elibuzwayo - iboniswa kwiimeko apho uGoogle akanayo imvume yomnini welungelo lokukhuphela ukubonisa umboniso. Oku kungenxa yokuba uGoogle akakwazi ukuchonga umnini okanye umnikazi wale mvume. Ukuba igama lokukhangela livela kaninzi encwadini, uGoogle akabonisi iziqwengana ezingaphezu kwesithathu, ngaloo ndlela ethintela umsebenzisi ukuba abukele incwadi eninzi. Kwakhona, uGoogle akabonisi naziphi na iziqwengana zeencwadi ezithile zereferensi, ezinje ngezichazi-magama, apho ukuboniswa kweziqwengana zinokwenzakalisa imarike yomsebenzi. UGoogle ugcina ukuba akukho mvume ifunwayo phantsi komthetho welungelo lokubonisa imbono yesiqwengana.[18] 
Akukho mboniso: uGoogle ukwabonisa iziphumo zophendlo lweencwadi ezingafakwanga ekhompyutheni. Njengoko ezi ncwadi zingakhange ziskenwe, isicatshulwa sabo asikhangeli kwaye kuphela imethadatha efana nesihloko, umbhali, umshicileli, inani lamaphepha, i-ISBN, ulwazi lwesihloko kunye ne-copyright, kwaye kwezinye iimeko, uluhlu lweziqulatho kunye nesishwankathelo sencwadi siyafumaneka. Enyanisweni, oku kuyafana nekhathalogu yekhadi lethala leencwadi elikwi-intanethi.[3] 
Ekuphenduleni ukugxekwa kwamaqela afana ne-American Association of Publishers kunye ne-Authors Guild, i-Google ibhengeze umgaqo-nkqubo wokuphuma ngo-Agasti 2005, apho abanini-copyright banokunika uluhlu lwezihloko abangafuni ukuskenwa, kwaye isicelo siya kuhlonishwa. Inkampani ikwathe ayizukuskena naziphi na iincwadi ezikwi-copyright phakathi kuka-Agasti nomhla woku-1 kuNovemba ka-2005, ukunika abanini ithuba lokugqiba ukuba zeziphi na iincwadi abanokuzikhuphela ngaphandle kweProjekthi. Ngaloo ndlela, abanikazi be-copyright banokukhetha okuthathu ngokubhekiselele kuwo nawuphi na umsebenzi: [18] 

Inokuthatha inxaxheba kwiNkqubo yoBambiswano ukwenza incwadi ifumaneke ukuze ibonwe kuqala okanye ibonwe ngokupheleleyo, apho iya kubelana ngengeniso evela kumboniso wamaphepha omsebenzi ekuphenduleni imibuzo yabasebenzisi.  
Inokuvumela uGoogle ukuba askene incwadi phantsi kweProjekthi yeThala leeNcwadi kwaye abonise iziqwengana ekuphenduleni imibuzo yabasebenzisi.
Inokuphuma kwiProjekthi yeThala leeNcwadi, apho uGoogle engayi kuskena incwadi. Ukuba incwadi sele iskeniwe, uGoogle uya kusetha ngokutsha inqanaba lofikelelo njenge 'Akukho mboniso'. 
Uninzi lwemisebenzi eskeniweyo ayisekho kushicilelo okanye kurhwebo.[19]

Ukongeza ekuthengeni iincwadi kumathala eencwadi, uGoogle ukwafumana iincwadi kumahlakani akhe abapapashi, esebenzisa "iNkqubo yeNtsebenziswano" - eyilelwe ukunceda abapapashi kunye nababhali ukuba bakhuthaze iincwadi zabo. Abapapashi kunye nababhali bangenise nokuba ikopi yedijithali yencwadi yabo kwiEPUB okanye kwifomathi yePDF, okanye ikopi eprintiweyo kuGoogle, eyenziwe ifumaneke kwiiNcwadi zikaGoogle ukuze zijongwe. Umpapashi unokulawula ipesenteji yencwadi ekhoyo ukuze ijongwe, ubuncinci bungama-20%. Basenokukhetha ukwenza incwadi ibonakale ngokupheleleyo, kwaye bavumele abasebenzisi ukuba bakhuphele ikopi yePDF. Iincwadi zinokwenziwa zifumaneke ukuba zithengiswe kuDlalo lukaGoogle.[3] Ngokungafaniyo neProjekthi yeThala leeNcwadi, oku akuphakamisi naziphi na iinkxalabo zamalungelo obunini njengoko kuqhutywa ngokwesivumelwano nompapashi. Umpapashi unokukhetha ukurhoxa kwisivumelwano nangaliphi na ixesha.[18] 

Kwiincwadi ezininzi, iiNcwadi zikaGoogle zibonisa amanani ephepha lokuqala. Nangona kunjalo, uTim Parks, ebhala kuThe New York Review of Books ngo-2014, waphawula ukuba uGoogle wayekile ukubonelela ngeenombolo zephepha kupapasho oluninzi lwamva nje (mhlawumbi ezo zifunyenwe ngeNkqubo yeNtsebenziswano) "kusenokwenzeka ukuba ibambisene nabapapashi, ukuze banyanzelise abo bafuna ukulungiselela imibhalo esemazantsi ukuthenga ushicilelo lwephepha 

. 
" Umseki kaGoogle uLarry Page wayesoloko enomdla wokudibanisa iincwadi. Xa yena noMarissa Mayer baqalisa ukuzama ukuskena incwadi ngo-2002, kwathatha imizuzu engama-40 ukuba bafake kwidijithali incwadi enamaphepha angama-300. Kodwa kamsinya nje emva kokuba obu bugcisa buphuhlisiwe ukusa kwinqanaba lokuba abaqhubi baskene ukuya kutsho kumaphepha angama-6000 ngeyure.[14] 

UGoogle useke amaziko atyunjiweyo okuskena apho iincwadi zithuthwa ngeelori. Izikhululo ziyakwazi ukusebenzisa idijithali ngesantya samaphepha ali-1,000 ngeyure. Iincwadi zibekwe kwi-cradle eyakhiwe ngokwesiqhelo elungelelanisa umqolo wencwadi endaweni ngelixa izibane ezininzi kunye nezixhobo zokukhanya ziskena amaphepha amabini avulekileyo. Iphepha ngalinye liya kuba neekhamera ezimbini ezijoliswe kuyo ukubamba umfanekiso, ngelixa i-LIDAR yokufumana uluhlu igqume igridi ye-laser ene-dimensional ezintathu kumphezulu wencwadi ukubamba ukugoba kwephepha. Umntu wayedla ngokutyhila amaphepha ngesandla, esebenzisa inyawo ukuze afote. Ngaphandle kwesidingo sokuthoba amaphepha okanye ukuwalungelelanisa ngokugqibeleleyo, inkqubo kaGoogle ayifikelelanga nje ekusebenzeni okumangalisayo kunye nesantya kodwa incede nokukhusela ingqokelela eethe-ethe ekubeni ingaphathwa kakhulu. Emva koko, imifanekiso ekrwada idlule kumanqanaba amathathu okuqhubela phambili: okokuqala, i-de-warping algorithms isebenzise idatha ye-LIDAR ukulungisa ukugoba kwamaphepha. Emva koko, i-software ye-optical character recognition (OCR) iguqule imifanekiso ekrwada ibe yinto ebhaliweyo, kwaye, ekugqibeleni, omnye umjikelo we-algorithms ekhutshwe amanani ephepha, imibhalo esemazantsi, imizobo kunye nemizobo.[14]

Uninzi lweencwadi ziskenwa kusetyenziswa ikhamera ye Elphel 323 [21][22] ngesantya samaphepha ali-1,000 ngeyure.[23] Ilungelo elilodwa lomenzi wechiza elanikwa uGoogle ngo-2009 latyhila ukuba uGoogle uze nenkqubo entsha yokuskena iincwadi esebenzisa iikhamera ezimbini kunye nesibane se-infrared ukulungisa ngokuzenzekelayo ukugoba kwamaphepha encwadi. Ngokwakha imodeli ye-3D yephepha ngalinye kwaye emva koko "yi-de-warping", uGoogle uyakwazi ukubonisa amaphepha ajongeka mcaba ngaphandle kokwenza amaphepha abe sicaba, nto leyo efuna ukusetyenziswa kweendlela ezitshabalalisayo ezifana nokungabophi okanye iipleyiti zeglasi ukuze zicandwe ngabanye iphepha ngalinye, nto leyo engasebenziyo ukuskena isikali esikhulu.[24][25] 

UGoogle wagqiba kwelokuba ashiye ulwazi lombala ethanda isisombululo esingcono sendawo, njengoko uninzi lweencwadi ezingaphandle kwelungelo lokushicilela ngelo xesha zazingenayo imibala. Umfanekiso wephepha ngalinye udluliselwe kwi-algorithms eyahlula isicatshulwa kunye nemimandla yemifanekiso. Iingingqi zombhalo ziye zacutshungulwa kusetyenziswa i-OCR ukuvumela uphendlo olupheleleyo. UGoogle uchithe izixhobo ezininzi ekuza nezona ndlela zocinezelo, ejolise kumgangatho ophezulu womfanekiso ngelixa egcina ubungakanani beefayile buncinci ukwenza ukuba abasebenzisi be-intanethi bafikelele kwi-bandwidth ephantsi. [26] 
 
Ukusebenza kwewebhusayithi
Kumsebenzi ngamnye, iiNcwadi zikaGoogle zizenzela ngokuzenzekelayo iphepha lokujonga. Eli phepha libonisa ulwazi olukhutshwe kwincwadi-iinkcukacha zayo zokupapasha, imephu yamagama aphindaphindiweyo, itafile yeziqulatho-kunye nezinto eziziisekondari, ezifana nezishwankathelo, ukuphononongwa kwabafundi (okungafundekiyo kwi-mobile version yewebhusayithi), kunye nezixhumanisi kwezinye izicatshulwa ezifanelekileyo. Umtyeleli kwiphepha, umzekelo, unokubona uluhlu lweencwadi ezabelana ngohlobo olufanayo kunye nomxholo, okanye unokubona uluhlu lwezifundo zangoku kwincwadi. Lo mxholo, ngaphezu koko, unikezela ngamathuba okunxibelelana kubasebenzisi abangene kwiakhawunti yabo kaGoogle. Bangathumela ngaphandle idata yebhayibhulografi kunye nokucaphula kwiifomathi eziqhelekileyo, babhale uphononongo lwabo, bayongeze kwithala labo leencwadi ukuze liphawulwe, lilungelelaniswe, kwaye kwabelwane ngalo nabanye abantu.[27][28] Ke, iiNcwadi zikaGoogle ziqokelela ezi zinto zitolika ngakumbi kuluhlu lwemithombo, kubandakanya abasebenzisi, iisayithi zomntu wesithathu ezifana neGoodreads, kwaye rhoqo ngumbhali kunye nomshicileli wencwadi. [29] 

Ngapha koko, ukukhuthaza ababhali ukuba balayishe ezabo iincwadi, uGoogle wongeze imisebenzi emininzi kwiwebhusayithi. Ababhali banokuvumela iindwendwe ukuba zikhuphele i-ebook yazo simahla, okanye banokuseta ixabiso labo lokuthenga. Bangatshintsha ixabiso emva naphambili, benikezela ngezaphulelo nanini na xa kufanelekile. Kwakhona, ukuba umbhali wencwadi ukhetha ukongeza i-ISBN, i-LCCN okanye inombolo yerekhodi ye-OCLC, inkonzo iya kuhlaziya i-url yencwadi ukuyifaka. Emva koko, umbhali unokuseta iphepha elithile njenge-anchor yekhonkco. Olu khetho lwenza ukuba incwadi yabo ifumaneke lula. 
Inqaku eliphambili 

loMjongi weNgram : Umbukeli weNgram kaGoogle
Umjongi weNgram yinkonzo eqhagamshelwe kwiiNcwadi zikaGoogle ezibonisa ukuphindaphindwa kokusetyenziswa kwamagama kwingqokelela yeencwadi zabo. Le nkonzo ibalulekile kubabhali-mbali kunye neengcali zolwimi njengoko inokubonelela ngenkangeleko yangaphakathi kwinkcubeko yabantu ngokusetyenziswa kwamagama ngamaxesha onke.[30] Le nkqubo iye yawa phantsi kokugxekwa ngenxa yeempazamo kwimetadata esetyenziswe kwinkqubo.[31] 

Imiba yesiqulatho kunye nokugxekwa 
Le projekthi ifumene ukugxekwa ukuba injongo yayo echaziweyo yokugcina imisebenzi yeenkedama kunye nengaphandle koshicilelo isemngciphekweni ngenxa yedatha eskeniweyo eneempazamo kwaye ezo ngxaki azisonjululwa.[32][33] 

Iimpazamo zokuskena 

Isandla siskenwe kwincwadi kaGoogle 
Inkqubo yokuskena ixhomekeke kwiimpazamo. Umzekelo, amanye amaphepha asenokungafundeki, ajonge phantsi, okanye alandelelane ngendlela engeyiyo. Abaphengululi baye bachaza amaphepha ashwabeneyo, oobhontsi abagqumayo neminwe, nemifanekiso eqatyiweyo okanye engacacanga.[34] Kulo mbandela, isibhengezo esivela kuGoogle ekupheleni kweencwadi eziskeniweyo sithi: 

I-digitization kwinqanaba elisisiseko lisekelwe kwimifanekiso yephepha leencwadi eziphathekayo. Ukwenza le ncwadi ifumaneke njengefayile efomathiweyo ye-ePub sithathe loo mifanekiso yamaphepha saze sakhupha umbhalo sisebenzisa itekhnoloji ye-Optical Character Recognition (okanye i-OCR ngokufutshane). Ukukhutshwa kwesicatshulwa kwimifanekiso yamaphepha ngumsebenzi onzima wobunjineli. I-smudges kumaphepha eencwadi eziphathekayo, iifonti ezintle, iifonti ezindala, amaphepha akrazukileyo, njl njl. I-OCR engafezekanga kuphela ngumngeni wokuqala kwinjongo yokugqibela yokuhamba ukusuka kwingqokelela yemifanekiso yephepha ukuya kwiincwadi ezisekelwe kwisicatshulwa. Ii-algorithms zethu zekhompyuter kufuneka zigqibe ngokuzenzekelayo ubume bencwadi (zithini iiheader kunye neefooter, apho imifanekiso ibekwe khona, nokuba umbhalo uyindinyana okanye iprozi, njalo njalo). Ukufumana eli lungelo kusenza sikwazi ukuyinikela incwadi ngendlela elandela indlela eyayibhalwe ngayo ekuqaleni. Ngaphandle kwemizamo yethu yokubona iimpazamo zopelo, iimpawu zenkunkuma, imifanekiso engaphandle, okanye amaphepha angekhoyo kule ncwadi. Ngokusekelwe kuqikelelo lwethu, ezi mpazamo akufuneki zikuthintele ekonwabeni umxholo wencwadi. Imiceli mngeni yobugcisa bokwakha ngokuzenzekelayo incwadi egqibeleleyo iyoyikisa, kodwa siyaqhubeka sisenza uphuculo kwi-OCR yethu kunye nobuchwephesha bokukhupha ubume bencwadi.[35] 

Ngo-2009, uGoogle wathi bazakuqala ukusebenzisa i-reCAPTCHA ukunceda ukulungisa iimpazamo ezifunyenwe kwiiskena zeNcwadi kaGoogle. Le ndlela yayiza kuphucula kuphela amagama askeniweyo ekunzima ukuwaqonda ngenxa yenkqubo yokuskena kwaye ayikwazi ukusombulula iimpazamo ezifana namaphepha ajikiweyo okanye amagama avaliweyo.[36] 

Iimpazamo zokuskena zikhuthaze imisebenzi yobugcisa njengengqokelela epapashiweyo yamaphepha angaqhelekanga kunye neblogi yeTumblr.[37] 

Iimpazamo kwimetadata
Abaphengululi baye baxela rhoqo iimpazamo ezixhaphakileyo kulwazi lwemetadata kwiiNcwadi zikaGoogle - kubandakanywa ababhali abachazwa kakubi kunye nemihla enempazamo yokupapashwa. UGeoffrey Nunberg, isazi seelwimi esiphanda ngotshintsho ekusetyenzisweni kwamagama ngokuhamba kwexesha uye waqaphela ukuba ukhangelo lweencwadi ezipapashwe ngaphambi kowe-1950 kunye negama elithi “intanethi” luvelise iziphumo ezingalindelekanga ezingama-527. UWoody Allen ukhankanywa kwiincwadi ezingama-325 ezipapashwa ngokucacileyo ngaphambi kokuba azalwe. UGoogle uphendule uNunberg ngokutyhola uninzi lweempazamo kwiikontraka zangaphandle. [31] 

Ezinye iimpazamo zemetadata ezixeliweyo ziquka imihla yokupapashwa phambi kokuzalwa kombhali (umz. I-182 isebenza nguCharles Dickens phambi kokuzalwa kwakhe ngo-1812); ukuhlelwa kwezifundo ezingachanekanga (uhlelo lukaMoby Dick olufunyenwe phantsi kwee-"computers", i-biography of Mae West classified under "religion"), ukuhlelwa kwezifundo ezingachanekanga (10 editions of Whitman's Leaves of Grass zonke zihlelwa njengazo zombini "fiction" kunye "no"nonfiction"), izihloko ezipelwe ngokungachanekanga, ababhali, nabapapashi (i-White metall efakwe kwidatha engachanekanga, okanye kwi-White metall efakwe kwidatha engachanekanga) incwadi eyahluke ngokupheleleyo (imetadata yomsebenzi wezibalo we-1818 ikhokelela kwinoveli yothando ka-1963).[38][39] 

Uphononongo lombhali, isihloko, umshicileli, kunye neempawu zemethadatha zonyaka wopapasho kwiirekhodi ezingama-400 ezikhethwe ngokungacwangciswanga kwiiNcwadi zikaGoogle zenziwa. Iziphumo zibonisa i-36% yeencwadi zesampula kwiprojekthi yokwenza idijithali iqulethe iimpazamo zemethadatha. Eli zinga lemposiso liphezulu kunokuba umntu angalindela ukulifumana kwikhathalogu yethala leencwadi eqhelekileyo ye-intanethi.[40] 

Ireyithi yempazamo epheleleyo ye-36.75% efunyenwe kolu phononongo icebisa ukuba imethadatha yeeNcwadi zikaGoogle inezinga eliphezulu lempazamo. Ngelixa iimpazamo "ezinkulu" kunye "nezincinci" zingumahluko ozimeleyo osekelwe kwingqikelelo engaqinisekanga ye "findability", iimpazamo ezifunyenwe kwizinto ezine zemetadata eziphononongwe kolu phononongo kufuneka zonke zithathelwe ingqalelo enkulu.[40] 

Iimpazamo zemethadatha ezisekelwe kwimihla eskeniweyo engachanekanga yenze uphando kusetyenziswa isiseko sedatha yeProjekthi yeeNcwadi zikaGoogle. Ngokwenqaku lika-2009 ngumfundi uGeoffrey Nunberg uGoogle wayezazi ezi mpazamo kwaye esebenzela ukuzilungisa. [41] 

Imiba yolwimi 
Abanye abezopolitiko kunye neengqondi zaseYurophu ziye zagxeka iinzame zikaGoogle kwizizathu ze-imperialism zolwimi. Baxoxa ngelithi ngenxa yokuba uninzi lweencwadi ezicetywayo ukuba ziskenwe zingesiNgesi, oko kuya kubangela ukumelwa okungafaniyo kweelwimi zendalo kwihlabathi ledijithali. IsiJamani, isiRashiya, isiFrentshi kunye neSpanish, umzekelo, ziilwimi ezidumileyo kwizifundo. Ugxininiso olungalinganiyo lwe-Intanethi kwisiNgesi, nangona kunjalo, lunokubumba ukufikelela kwizifundo zembali, kwaye, ekugqibeleni, ukukhula kunye nesikhokelo sokufunda kwixesha elizayo. Phakathi kwaba bagxeki nguJean-Noël Jeanneney, owayesakuba ngumongameli weBibliothèque nationale de France.[42] [43] 

Iincwadi zikaGoogle ngokuchasene noMfundi kaGoogle
Ngelixa iiNcwadi zikaGoogle zenze amanani amakhulu emicimbi yomva wejenali, iskena sayo asibandakanyi imetadata efunekayo ukuchonga amanqaku athile kwimiba ethile. Oku kukhokelele abaqulunqi beGoogle Scholar ukuba baqale eyabo inkqubo yokwenza ekhompyutheni kwaye bamkele amanqaku ejenali amadala (ngokuvumelana nabapapashi bawo).[44] 

Amaqabane eThala leeNcwadi 
Iprojekthi yeThala leeNcwadi zikaGoogle ijolise ekuskeneni nasekukhangeleni ukuqokelelwa kwamathala eencwadi amaninzi ophando. [45] Kunye nolwazi lwebhayibhilografi, iziqwengana zombhalo wencwadi zihlala zibonwa. Ukuba incwadi ingaphandle kwelungelo lokushicilela kwaye ikwindawo kawonke-wonke, le ncwadi ifumaneka ngokupheleleyo ukuba ifundwe okanye ikhutshelwe.[16] 

Iincwadi ze-copyright eziskeniweyo ngeProjekthi yeThala leeNcwadi zenziwe zifumaneke kwiiNcwadi zikaGoogle ukuze zijongwe. Ngokumalunga nomgangatho wokuskena, uGoogle uyavuma ukuba "azisoloko zikumgangatho ophakamileyo ngokwaneleyo" ukuba zithengiswe kuDlalo lukaGoogle. Kwakhona, ngenxa yemiqobo ecingelwayo yobugcisa, uGoogle akathathi ndawo iskeni ngeenguqulelo ezikumgangatho ophezulu ezinokuthi zibonelelwe ngabapapashi. [46] 

Le projekthi ngumxholo we-Authors Guild v. Google lawsuit, efakwe ngo-2005 kwaye yagweba ngokuxhasa uGoogle ngo-2013, kwaye kwakhona, kwisibheno, ngo-2015. 

Abanini be-copyright bangabanga amalungelo encwadi eskeniweyo kwaye bayenze ifumaneke ukuze ibonwe kwangaphambili okanye imbono epheleleyo (ngo "ngokuyidlulisela" kwi-akhawunti yabo yeNkqubo yoMlingane), okanye bacele uGoogle ukunqanda isicatshulwa sencwadi [4]. 

Inani lamaziko athatha inxaxheba kwiProjekthi yeThala leeNcwadi likhulile ukususela oko yasekwayo.[47] 

Amaqabane okuqala 

Eli candelo kufuneka lihlaziywe. Nceda uncede ukuhlaziya eli nqaku ukubonisa iziganeko zamva nje okanye ulwazi olutsha olukhoyo. (NgoNovemba 2024) 

Isaziso malunga neprojekthi kwiThala leeNcwadi leYunivesithi yaseMichigan 
IYunivesithi yaseHarvard, iThala leeNcwadi leYunivesithi yaseHarvard[48]
Ithala leencwadi leYunivesithi yaseHarvard kunye noGoogle baqhube ulingo kunyaka wonke ka-2005. Le projekthi iqhubekile, ngenjongo yokwandisa ukufikelela kwi-intanethi kwiindawo ezigcinwe kwiThala leeNcwadi leYunivesithi yaseHarvard, equka ngaphezu kwe-15.8 yezigidi zemiqulu. Ngelixa ufikelelo ngokwasemzimbeni kwimathiriyeli yethala leencwadi laseHarvard luthintelwe ngokubanzi kubafundi bangoku baseHarvard, ubuhlakani, kunye nabaphandi, okanye kubafundi abanokuthi beze eCambridge, Massachusetts, iprojekthi yeHarvard-Google iyilelwe ukuvumela omabini amalungu oluntu lwaseHarvard kunye nabasebenzisi kuyo yonke indawo ukuba bafumane imisebenzi kwingqokelela yeHarvard. IYunivesithi yaseMichigan, kwiThala 
leencwadi 
leYunivesithi yaseMichigan 
IThala leeNcwadi loLuntu laseNew York[51] 
Kule nkqubo yokulinga, i-NYPL isebenza noGoogle ukunika ingqokelela yeencwadi zayo zoluntu, eziya kuskenwa ngokupheleleyo kwaye zenziwe zifumaneke simahla eluntwini kwi-intanethi. Abasebenzisi baya kuba nakho ukukhangela kunye nokukhangela itekisi epheleleyo yale misebenzi. Xa inkqubo yokuskena igqityiwe, iincwadi zinokufikelelwa kwiwebhusayithi yeThala leeNcwadi loLuntu laseNew York nakwinjini yokukhangela kaGoogle.[51]

IYunivesithi yaseComplutense yaseMadrid[56][60] 
iYunivesithi yaseCornell, iThala leeNcwadi leYunivesithi yaseCornell [61] 
iYunivesithi yaseGhent, iThala leeNcwadi leYunivesithi yaseGhent/iBoekentoren[56][62] 
IYunivesithi yaseKeio, amaZiko eMedia eKeio (amaThala eeNcwadi)[63]
