yeYunivesithi yase-California, iYunivesithi yase-California yase-California. of Lausanne [56] [67] 
University of Mysore, Mysore University Library 
Ubambiswano yayiyeyokwenza digitizing 800,000 imibhalo, kuquka nemibhalo-ngqangi ebhalwe kumagqabi esundu ukususela kwinkulungwane yesibhozo. [68][69] 
IYunivesithi yaseTexas eAustin, kwiDyunivesithi yaseTexas kumathala eencwadi[70] 
Intsebenziswano ibiyeyokwenza ingqokelela yedijithali kwithala leencwadi laseLatin America – malunga nesiqingatha sesigidi semiqulu.[50] 
IYunivesithi yaseVirginia, iThala leeNcwadi leYunivesithi yaseVirginia[71] 
iYunivesithi yaseWisconsin-Madison, iDyunivesithi yaseWisconsin kumathala eencwadi[72] 
Ukusukela ngoMatshi ka-2012, malunga nama-600,000 imiqulu sele iskeniwe.[50] 
Imbali

Ngo-2002: Iqela lamalungu eqela likaGoogle lisungula ngokusemthethweni "iprojekthi 'yeencwadi' eziyimfihlo." [73] Abaseki bakaGoogle uSergey Brin kunye noLarry Page beza nombono wokuba kamva baba ziincwadi zikaGoogle ngelixa besathweswe izidanga eStanford ngo-1996. isalathiso umxholo weencwadi kwaye uhlalutye unxibelelwano phakathi kwazo, ukugqiba nayiphi na incwadi ebaluleke kakhulu kunye nokuba luncedo ngokulandelela inani kunye nomgangatho wezicatshulwa ezivela kwezinye iincwadi." iiprojekthi ezifana ne-JSTOR kunye nokwenza iMelika. Kwincoko kunye noMongameli weDyunivesithi uMary Sue Coleman ngelo xesha, xa iPhepha lafumanisa ukuba uqikelelo lwangoku lweyunivesithi lokuskena yonke imiqulu yethala leencwadi yiminyaka eyi-1,000, uPage waxelela uColeman ukuba "ukholelwa ukuba uGoogle unokunceda ukwenza ukuba kwenzeke kwisithandathu. 

" "ezinye iimpawu ezingalindelekanga."[73] 

Disemba 2004: UGoogle usayine ukongezwa kwenyathelo lakhe lokuShicilela likaGoogle elaziwa ngokuba yiProjekthi yeThala leeNcwadi likaGoogle [47] UGoogle ubhengeze ubambiswano kunye neyunivesithi ephezulu kunye namathala eencwadi oluntu, kubandakanywa neYunivesithi yaseMichigan, iHarvard (iThala leeNcwadi leYunivesithi yaseHarvard), iStanford (iThala leencwadi eliGreen), iOxford (iThala leencwadi laseBodleian), kunye neThala leeNcwadi loLuntu laseNew York. Ngokwamaphepha eendaba kunye noosomathala baseyunivesithi, uGoogle ucwangcise ukwenza idijithali kwaye enze ukuba kufumaneke ngenkonzo yakhe yeeNcwadi zikaGoogle malunga nezigidi ezili-15 zemiqulu kwisithuba seshumi leminyaka. Isibhengezo kungekudala savusa impikiswano, njengoko abashicileli kunye nemibutho yababhali bacela umngeni kwizicwangciso zikaGoogle zokusebenzisa idijithali, hayi nje iincwadi ezikwidomeyini yoluntu, kodwa nezihloko ezisephantsi kwelungelo lokushicilela. 

Septemba–Okthobha 2005: Izimangalo ezimbini ezichasene noGoogle zityhola inkampani engakhange ihloniphe amalungelo okushicilela kwaye ayiphumelelanga ukubabuyekeza ngokufanelekileyo ababhali nabapapashi. Enye yisuti yenyathelo leklasi egameni lababhali (Authors Guild v. Google, Septemba 20, 2005) kwaye elinye lityala loluntu eliziswe ngabapapashi abakhulu abahlanu kunye noMbutho wabapapashi baseMelika. (McGraw Hill v. Google, Okthobha 19, 2005)[9][74][75][76][77][78] 

Novemba 2005: UGoogle walitshintsha igama lalenkonzo ukusuka kuGoogle Print ukuya kuGoogle Book Search.[79] Inkqubo yayo eyenza abapapashi kunye nababhali ukuba babandakanye iincwadi zabo kwinkonzo yaqanjwa ngokuba yiNkqubo yeZahluleli zeeNcwadi zikaGoogle,[80] kunye nentsebenziswano namathala eencwadi yaba yiProjekthi yeThala leeNcwadi likaGoogle.

Ngo-2006: UGoogle wongeze iqhosha elithi "khuphela i-pdf" kuzo zonke iincwadi zayo ezingaphandle kwe-copyright, zesizinda soluntu. Yongeze ujongano olutsha lokukhangela iincwadi kunye namaphepha amatsha "Malunga nale Ncwadi". [73] 

EyeThupha ka-2006: IYunivesithi yaseCalifornia System yabhengeza ukuba iza kujoyina iprojekthi yokufakwa kwedijithali kwiiNcwadi. Oku kuquka inxalenye yezigidi ezingama-34 zemiqulu phakathi kwamathala eencwadi amalunga ne-100 alawulwa yiNkqubo.[81] 

Septemba 2006: IYunivesithi yaseComplutense yaseMadrid yaba lithala leencwadi lokuqala lolwimi lwesiSpanish ukujoyina iProjekthi yeThala leeNcwadi zikaGoogle.[82] 

Ngo-Okthobha 2006: IYunivesithi yaseWisconsin-Madison yabhengeza ukuba iza kujoyina iProjekthi yokuKhangela yedijithali kunye ne-Wisconsin Historical Society Library. Xa edityanisiwe, amathala eencwadi anezigidi ezisisi-7.2 ezigciniweyo.[83] 

NgoNovemba 2006: IYunivesithi yaseVirginia yajoyina iprojekthi. Amathala eencwadi ayo aqulethe imiqulu engaphezu kwezigidi ezihlanu kunye nemibhalo-ngqangi engaphezu kwezigidi ezili-17, iincwadi ezinqabileyo noovimba.[84] 

NgoJanuwari 2007: IYunivesithi yaseTexas e-Austin yabhengeza ukuba iya kujoyina iprojekthi yokuKhangela kwidijithali. Ubuncinci imiqulu esisigidi iya kufakwa ekhompyutheni kwiindawo zethala leencwadi ezili-13. 

Matshi 2007: Ithala leencwadi laseBavaria libhengeze ubambiswano noGoogle ukuskena ngaphezulu kwesigidi sedomeyini yoluntu kunye nemisebenzi ephumayo yoshicilelo yesiJamani kunye nesiNgesi, isiFrentshi, isiTaliyane, isiLatini, neSpanish.[85] 

UCanzibe 2007: Incwadi yobambiswano lweprojekthi eyenziwe ngedijithali yabhengezwa ngokudibeneyo nguGoogle kunye neCantonal kunye neThala leeNcwadi leYunivesithi yaseLausanne.[86] 

UCanzibe 2007: Ithala leencwadi laseBoekentoren leDyunivesithi yaseGhent libhengeze ukuba liza kuthatha inxaxheba noGoogle ekwenzeni iinguqulelo zedijithali zeencwadi zenkulungwane ye-19 kwiilwimi zesiFrentshi nesiDatshi ezifumaneka kwi-intanethi.[87] 

NgoMeyi 2007: IYunivesithi yaseMysore yazisa ukuba uGoogle uza kufakwa kwidijithali ngaphezu kwe-800,000 yeencwadi kunye nemibhalo-ngqangi-kuquka malunga ne-100,000 yemibhalo-ngqangi ebhalwe ngesiSanskrit okanye isiKannada kuwo omabini amaphepha kunye namagqabi esundu.[68] 

NgoJuni 2007: IKomiti yeNtsebenziswano yamaZiko (eye yaphinda yabizwa ngokuba yiBig Ten Academic Alliance ngo-2016) yabhengeza ukuba amathala eencwadi ayo alishumi elinesibini aza kuthatha inxaxheba ekuhloleni iincwadi ezizizigidi ezili-10 kule minyaka mithandathu izayo.[58] 

NgoJulayi 2007: IYunivesithi yaseKeio yaba lihlakani lokuqala lethala leencwadi likaGoogle eJapan ngesibhengezo sokuba baza kudidiyela ubuncinane iincwadi ezingama-120,000 zoluntu.[88] 

EyeThupha ngo-2007: UGoogle wabhengeza ukuba uza kufakwa kwidijithali ukuya kuthi ga kwi-500,000 zombini izinto ezinamalungelo okukopisha kunye nesizinda sikawonke-wonke kwiThala leeNcwadi leYunivesithi yaseCornell. UGoogle uza kubonelela ngekopi yedijithali yayo yonke imisebenzi eskeniweyo ukuze ibandakanywe kwinkqubo yethala leencwadi yeyunivesithi. [89] 

NgoSeptemba 2007: UGoogle wongeze into evumela abasebenzisi ukuba babelane ngeziqwengana zeencwadi ezikwidomeyini yoluntu. Iziqwengana zinokuvela kanye njengoko zivela kwiskena sencwadi, okanye njengesicatshulwa esicacileyo.[90]

NgoSeptemba 2007: UGoogle uqalise inqaku elitsha elibizwa ngokuba yi "Thala leeNcwadi lam" elivumela abasebenzisi ukuba benze amathala eencwadi alungele wena, ukhetho lweencwadi abanokuthi baleyibhelishe, bazihlole, balinganise, okanye baziphendle ngokubhalwe ngokupheleleyo.[91] 

Disemba 2007: IYunivesithi yase-Columbia yongezwa njengeqabane ekwenziweni kwedijithali imisebenzi yoluntu.[92] 

Meyi 2008: I-Microsoft yacutheka kwaye yaceba ukuphelisa iprojekthi yayo yokuskena, eyayifikelele kwiincwadi ezingama-750,000 kunye namanqaku ejenali angama-80 ezigidi. [93] 

Ngo-Okthobha 2008: Kwafikelelwa isivumelwano phakathi kweshishini lokupapasha kunye neGoogle emva kweminyaka emibini yothethathethwano. UGoogle uvumile ukubabuyekeza ababhali nabapapashi ngokutshintshiselana nelungelo lokwenza izigidi zeencwadi zifumaneke kuluntu.[9][94] 

Okthobha 2008: IHathiTrust "iNdawo yeDijithali eKwabelwana ngayo" (kamva eyaziwa ngokuba yiHathiTrust Digital Library) iqaliswe ngokudibeneyo yiKomiti yeNtsebenziswano yamaZiko kunye namathala eencwadi ali-11 eyunivesithi kwiYunivesithi yaseCalifornia, onke lawo ibingamathala eencwadi kaGoogle, ukuze kugcinwe kwaye kubonelele ngofikelelo lwemfundo kwiincwadi ezisuka kwingqokelela ye95 kaGoogle. 

NgoNovemba 2008: UGoogle ufikelele kumanqaku eencwadi azizigidi ezisi-7 kwizinto eziskenwe nguGoogle kunye namaqabane abo okupapasha. Isigidi esi-1 sasikwimowudi yokujonga kwangaphambili kwaye isigidi esi-1 sasijongeka ngokupheleleyo kwaye sikhuphela imisebenzi yesizinda soluntu. Malunga nezigidi ezihlanu bezingasashicilelwa.[19][96][97] 

NgoDisemba 2008: UGoogle ubhengeze ukufakwa kweemagazini kwiincwadi zikaGoogle. Izihloko ziquka iNew York Magazine, i-Ebony, kunye ne-Popular Mechanics[98][99] 

February 2009: UGoogle uphehlelele inguqulelo yeselula ye-Google Book Search, evumela i-iPhone kunye nabasebenzisi befowuni ye-Android ukuba bafunde ngaphezu kwe-1.5 yesigidi sendawo yoluntu esebenza e-US (kunye ngaphezu kwe-500,000 ngaphandle kwe-US) usebenzisa i-browser yeselula. Endaweni yemifanekiso yephepha, umbhalo ocacileyo wencwadi uyaboniswa.[100] 

NgoMeyi 2009: Kwindibano yonyaka ye-BookExpo eNew York, uGoogle wachaza injongo yakhe yokwazisa inkqubo eya kwenza abapapashi bathengise iinguqulelo zedijithali zezona ncwadi zabo zintsha ngokuthe ngqo kubathengi ngoGoogle.[101] 

NgoDisemba 2009: Inkundla yaseFransi yavala ukuskenwa kweencwadi ezishicilelwe eFransi, isithi oku kukwaphula imithetho yamalungelo okushicilela. Yayiyilahleko yokuqala enkulu esemthethweni yeprojekthi yokuskena.[102] 

Ngo-Epreli 2010: Abaculi ababonakalayo abazange bafakwe kwisimangalo sangaphambili kunye nokuhlaliswa, ngamaqela ummangali kwelinye ityala, kwaye bathi banenjongo yokuzisa ngaphezu kweeNcwadi zeGoogle phantsi kokuhlolwa. "Isenzo seklasi entsha," ifundeka le ngxelo, "idlula iProjekthi yeThala leencwadi likaGoogle, kwaye ibandakanya ukunyhashwa okucwangcisiweyo nokuxhaphakileyo kukaGoogle kwamalungelo abafoti, abazobi kunye namanye amagcisa abonakalayo." [103]

UCanzibe ngo-2010: Kwaxelwa ukuba uGoogle uza kuphehlelela ivenkile yedijithali ebizwa ngokuba luHlelo lukaGoogle.[104] Iza kukhuphisana neAmazon, Barnes & Noble, Apple kunye nabanye abathengisi beencwadi ze-elektroniki kunye nevenkile ye-e-book. Ngokungafaniyo nabanye, uHlelo lukaGoogle luya kuba kwi-intanethi ngokupheleleyo kwaye aluyi kufuna isixhobo esithile (njenge-kindle, Nook, okanye iPad). 

EyeSilimela 2010: UGoogle uphumelele iincwadi ezili-12 lezigidi eziskeniweyo.[11] 

EyeThupha ngo-2010: Kwabhengezwa ukuba uGoogle ujonge ukuskena zonke iincwadi ezikhoyo eziyi-129,864,880 ezaziwayo kwisithuba seminyaka elishumi, ezifikelela ngaphezu kwe-4 yeebhiliyoni zamaphepha edijithali kunye ne-2 yetriliyoni yamagama ewonke.[11] 

Disemba 2010: Ii-eBooks zikaGoogle (uhlelo lukaGoogle) lwaphehlelelwa eUS.[105] 

EyoMnga ngo-2010: uGoogle uphehlelele iNgram Viewer, eqokelela kunye neegrafu zedatha ekusetyenzisweni kwamagama kuyo yonke ingqokelela yencwadi. [30] 

EyoKwindla 2011: Ijaji yomanyano yala isivumelwano ekwafikelelwa kuso phakathi kweshishini lokupapasha kunye noGoogle.[106] 

EyoKwindla 2012: uGoogle upase izigidi ezingama-20 zeencwadi eziskeniweyo.[107][108] 

Matshi 2012: UGoogle ufikelele kwisigqibo nabapapashi.[109] 

NgoJanuwari 2013: Ingxelo kaGoogle kunye neWorld Brain yaboniswa kwiSundance Film Festival. [110] 

NgoNovemba 2013: Ukulawula kwiGuild Yababhali v. Google, iJaji yeSithili sase-US uDenny Chin uxhasa uGoogle, ecaphula ukusetyenziswa ngokufanelekileyo.[111] Ababhali bathi baza kubhena.[112] 

Okthobha 2015: Inkundla yezibheno ixhasa uGoogle, ibhengeza ukuba uGoogle akawophulanga mthetho welungelo lokushicilela.[113] Ngokutsho kweNew York Times, uGoogle uskene iincwadi ezingaphezu kwezigidi ezingama-25. [12] 

Epreli 2016: INkundla ePhakamileyo yase-US yalile ukumamela isibheno se-Authors Guild, nto leyo ethetha ukuba isigqibo senkundla esezantsi simile, kwaye uGoogle uza kuvunyelwa ukuba askene iincwadi zethala leencwadi kwaye abonise iziqwengana kwiziphumo zophando ngaphandle kokwaphula umthetho.[114] 

Ubume 
beGoogle buyimfihlo kakhulu malunga nezicwangciso zayo kwikamva leprojekthi yeeNcwadi zikaGoogle. Imisebenzi yokuskena ibicotha ukusukela ubuncinci ngo-2012, njengoko kungqinwe ngoononcwadi kumaziko amaninzi angamahlakani kaGoogle. KwiDyunivesithi yaseWisconsin, isantya sehlisiwe saya kutsho ngaphantsi kwesiqingatha sento ebiyiyo ngo-2006. Nangona kunjalo, oosomathala bathe ukuba ukuhla kwesantya kusenokuba sisiphumo sendalo sokuvuthwa kweprojekthi – ekuqaleni izixa zeencwadi zathatyathwa ngokupheleleyo ukuze zijongwe ngeli xesha ngoku kuphela izihloko ebezingekaskenwa ezifuna ukuqwalaselwa.[50] Iphepha lexesha le-Google Books lexesha alizange lichaze nto emva ko-2007 nakwi-2017, kwaye ibhlog yeeNcwadi zikaGoogle zadityaniswa kwibhlog yoPhendlo lukaGoogle ngo-2012. [115]

Nangona iphumelele ishumi leminyaka kwi-2017, iAtlantiki ithe iGoogle "yonke kodwa ivale umsebenzi wayo wokuskena." [14] Ngo-Epreli 2017, iWired yabika ukuba bambalwa abasebenzi bakaGoogle abasebenza kule projekthi, kwaye iincwadi ezintsha zisaskenwa, kodwa ngesantya esisezantsi kakhulu. Yaphawula ukuba idabi lezomthetho leminyaka elishumi lenze ukuba uGoogle aphulukane namabhongo ayo. [115] 

Imiba yezomthetho 
Ulwazi oluthe vetshe: I-Authors Guild, Inc. v. Google, Inc. 
Ngokusebenzisa le projekthi, iincwadi zethala leencwadi bezifakwa ekhompyutheni noko ngokungakhethiyo nokuba ithini na imeko yelungelo lokushicilela, nto leyo ekhokelele kumatyala amaninzi ngokuchasene noGoogle. Ekupheleni kuka-2008, uGoogle ubesele efake kwidijithali iincwadi ezingaphezulu kwezigidi ezisixhenxe, apho malunga nesigidi esinye kuphela esisebenza kwindawo yoluntu. Kwabanye, esinye isigidi sasibhalwe phantsi kwamalungelo okushicilela yaye sasishicilelwe, yaye izigidi ezihlanu zazinamalungelo okukhuphela kodwa zingashicilelwa. Kwi-2005, iqela lababhali kunye nabapapashi bazisa inkundla enkulu ye-class-action echasene ne-Google ngokuphulwa kwemisebenzi ye-copyright. UGoogle waxoxa ngelithi igcina "imisebenzi yeenkedama" - iincwadi ezisephantsi kwelungelo lokushicilela, kodwa abanini bamalungelo abo okukhuphela bebengekafumaneki.[116] 

Umbutho Wababhali kunye noMbutho wabapapashi baseMelika ngokwahlukeneyo bamangalela uGoogle ngo-2005 ngeprojekthi yakhe yencwadi, becaphula "ukophulwa okukhulu kwelungelo lokushicilela."[117] UGoogle waphikisa ngelithi iprojekthi yakhe imele ukusetyenziswa ngokufanelekileyo kwaye lixesha ledijithali elilingana nekhathalogu yekhadi elinalo lonke igama kupapasho oluphawulweyo.[9] Amatyala adityaniswa, kwaza ekugqibeleni kwacetywa ukulungiswa. Ukuhlaliswa kwafumana ukugxekwa okubalulekileyo kwizizathu ezininzi ezahlukeneyo, kubandakanywa ukungathembeki, ubumfihlo, kunye nokunganeli kweeklasi ezicetywayo zababhali kunye nabapapashi. Ekugqibeleni kwaliwa, [118] kwaye abapapashi bazinza noGoogle kungekudala emva koko. I-Authors Guild yaqhubeka netyala layo, kwaye ngo-2011 iklasi yabo ecetywayo yaqinisekiswa. I-Google yabhenela eso sigqibo, kunye nenani le-amici eliqinisekisa ukungonelanga kweklasi, kwaye iSekethe yesiBini yakhatywa isiqinisekiso seklasi ngoJulayi 2013, ibuyisela ityala kwiNkundla yeSithili ukuze iqwalaselwe ukhuseleko lokusetyenziswa ngokufanelekileyo kweGoogle. [119] 

Kwi-2015 Authors Guild yafaka esinye isibheno esichasene neGoogle ukuba siqwalaselwe yiNkundla yeSibheno yeSekethe ye-2 yase-US eNew York. UGoogle uphumelele ityala ngamxhelo mnye ngokusekelwe kwingxoxo yokuba bebengababonisi abantu izibhalo ezipheleleyo kodwa endaweni yoko iziqwengana, kwaye abavumeli abantu ukuba bayifunde ngokungekho mthethweni incwadi. [120] Kwingxelo, iinkundla zathi azizange zophule imithetho yelungelo lokushicilela, njengoko zikhuselwe phantsi kwegatya lokusetyenziswa ngokufanelekileyo.[121]

I-Authors Guild yazama kwakhona kwi-2016 ukubhena isigqibo kwaye ngeli xesha bathatha ityala labo ukuba liqwalaselwe yiNkundla ePhakamileyo. Ityala lakhatywa, lishiya isigqibo seSekethe yesiBini kwimeko, nto leyo ethetha ukuba i-Google ayizange iphule imithetho ye-copyright.[122] Eli tyala likwamisela umzekelo kwamanye amatyala afanayo ngokubhekiselele kwimithetho yokusetyenziswa ngokufanelekileyo, njengoko icacisa ngakumbi umthetho kwaye iwandisa. Ingcaciso enjalo ichaphazela ezinye iiprojekthi zokuskena ezifana noGoogle.[120] 

Amanye amatyala alandela ukhokelo lweAuthors Guild. Ngo-2006 isimangalo saseJamani, esasifakwe ngaphambili, sarhoxiswa. [123] NgoJuni ka-2006, uHervé de la Martinière,[124] umshicileli ongumFrentshi owaziwa ngokuba yiLa Martinière kunye ne-Éditions du Seuil,[125] ubhengeze injongo yakhe yokumangalela uGoogle France.[126] Ngo-2009, iNkundla yaseParis yanikezela nge-300,000 EUR (malunga ne-430,000 USD) yomonakalo kunye nenzala kwaye yayalela uGoogle ukuba ahlawule i-10,000 EUR ngosuku de isuse iincwadi zabapapashi kuvimba wayo wedatha.[125][127] Inkundla ibhale, "uGoogle wophule imithetho yelungelo lokushicilela ngokuvelisa ngokupheleleyo nokwenza ukuba kufikeleleke" iincwadi zikaSeuil ezingabaniniyo ngaphandle kwemvume yakhe[125] nokuba uGoogle "wenze izenzo zokophulwa kwelungelo lokushicilela, eziyingozi kubashicileli".[124] UGoogle uthe izakubhena. [125] I-Syndicat National de l'Edition, ethe yajoyina isimangalo, yathi uGoogle uskene malunga ne-100,000 yemisebenzi yesiFrentshi phantsi kwelungelo lokushicilela.[125] 

NgoDisemba ka-2009, umbhali waseTshayina uMian Mian wafaka isimangalo se-8,900 yeedola ngokuchasene noGoogle ngokuskena inoveli yakhe, Abathandi be-Acid. Esi sisimangalo sokuqala esinje ukuba sifakwe ngokuchasene noGoogle eTshayina. [128] Kwakhona, ngoNovemba ngaloo nyaka, i-China Written Works Copyright Society (CWWCS) yatyhola uGoogle ngokuskena iincwadi ezingama-18,000 ngababhali abangama-570 baseTshayina ngaphandle kwesigunyaziso. UGoogle wavuma nge-20 kaNov ukunika uluhlu lweencwadi zaseTshayina eziskeniweyo, kodwa inkampani yala ukuvuma ukuba "yaphule" imithetho yelungelo lokukhuphela [129] [umthombo ongathembekanga?] 

NgoMatshi ka-2007, uThomas Rubin, umcebisi jikelele welungelo lokushicilela, uphawu lwentengiso, kunye neemfihlo zorhwebo kwaMicrosoft, watyhola uGoogle ngokwaphula umthetho welungelo lokushicilela ngenkonzo yabo yokukhangela incwadi. URubin ugxeke ngokukodwa umgaqo-nkqubo kaGoogle wokukhuphela ngokukhululekileyo nawuphi na umsebenzi ade aziswe ngumnini-copyright ukuba ayeke.[130] 

Ilayisenisi kaGoogle yemisebenzi kawonke-wonke ikwayindawo exhalabisayo ngenxa yokusetyenziswa kobuchule bedijithali bokujonga amanzi ngeencwadi. Eminye imisebenzi epapashiweyo ekwidomeyini yoluntu, njengayo yonke imisebenzi eyenziwe ngurhulumente wase-US Federal, isaphathwa njengeminye imisebenzi phantsi kwelungelo lokushicilela, kwaye ke itshixiwe emva ko-1922. [131] 

Ukusukela noko ngo-2014, uGoogle uye wavumela ababhali kunye nabapapashi ukuba basuse umboniso wencwadi kwiincwadi zikaGoogle xa beceliwe.[132]
 
Iiprojekthi ezifanayo
IProjekthi iGutenberg ngumzamo wokuvolontiya wokufaka kwidijithali kunye nokugcina imisebenzi yenkcubeko, "ukukhuthaza ukuyilwa nokusasazwa kwee-eBooks". Yasekwa ngo-1971 nguMichael S. Hart kwaye lelona thala leencwadi lakudala ledijithali. Ukususela ngo-Oktobha 3, 2015, iProjekthi Gutenberg ifikelele kwizinto ze-50,000 kwingqokelela yayo. 
Uvimba wogcino-mpepha kwi-Intanethi yinto engenzi nzuzo eyenza iincwadi ezingaphezu kwe-1000 ngosuku zifakwe kwidijithali, kunye neencwadi zezibuko ezivela kwiiNcwadi zikaGoogle kunye neminye imithombo. Ukusukela ngoMeyi ka-2011, ibambe ngaphezulu kwe-2.8 yezigidi zeencwadi zoluntu, ezingaphezu kwesigidi esimalunga nesigidi seencwadi zoluntu kwiincwadi zikaGoogle.[133] Vula iThala leencwadi, iprojekthi engudade ye-Internet Archive, iboleka ama-80,000 eskeniweyo kwaye athengwe iincwadi zentengiso kwiindwendwe zamathala eencwadi ali-150.[134] 
I-HathiTrust igcina iThala leencwadi le-HathiTrust Digital ukususela nge-13 ka-Okthobha ka-2008, [135] egcina kwaye ibonelele ngokufikelela kwimathiriyeli eskenwe nguGoogle, ezinye zeencwadi zikaVimba we-Intanethi, kwaye ezinye ziskenwe ekuhlaleni ngamaziko angamahlakani. Ukusukela ngoMeyi ka-2010, ibandakanya malunga nezigidi ezi-6 zemiqulu, ngaphezulu kwe-1 yezigidi eziyindawo yoluntu (ubuncinci e-US). 
I-ACLS Humanities E-Book, ingqokelela ye-intanethi yeencwadi ezingaphezu kwe-5,400 zomgangatho ophezulu kubuntu kunye nesayensi yezentlalo ezinxulumeneyo, ezifikelelekayo ngokubhaliselwa kweziko. 
I-Microsoft ixhase ngezimali ukuskena iincwadi ezingama-300,000 ukwenza iiNcwadi zoPhando olubukhoma ngasekupheleni kuka-2006. Yaqhuba de kwangoMeyi 2008, xa iprojekthi yayekwayo[136] neencwadi zenziwa zifumaneke simahla kwi-Internet Archive.[137] 
IThala leeNcwadi leSizwe leDijithali yaseIndiya (NDLI) yiprojekthi ephantsi koMphathiswa woPhuhliso lwaBasebenzi, eIndiya. Injongo kukudibanisa amathala eencwadi edijithali elizwe nawezizwe ngezizwe kwiwebhu-portal enye. I-NDLI ibonelela ngokufikelela simahla kwiincwadi ezininzi zesiNgesi kunye neelwimi zaseIndiya. 
Europeana iqhagamshela malunga nezigidi ezili-10 zezinto zedijithali ukususela ngo-2010, kuquka ividiyo, iifoto, imizobo, iaudio, iimephu, imibhalo-ngqangi, iincwadi eziprintiweyo, kunye namaphephandaba asuka kwiminyaka eyi-2,000 edlulileyo yembali yaseYurophu ukusuka kwi-1,000 yogcino kwi-European Union.[138][139] 
I-Gallica evela kwiThala leeNcwadi leSizwe lesiFrentshi lidibanisa malunga ne-4,000,000 yeencwadi ezifakwe kwidijithali, amaphephandaba, imibhalo yesandla, iimephu kunye nemidwebo, njl. Eyilwe kwi-1997, ilayibrari yedijithali iyaqhubeka nokwandisa malunga ne-5000 yamaxwebhu amatsha ngenyanga. Ukusukela ekupheleni kuka-2008, uninzi lwamaxwebhu amatsha askeniweyo afumaneka kumfanekiso kunye neefomathi zombhalo. Uninzi lwala maxwebhu abhalwe ngesiFrentshi.

Upapasho yinkqubo yokwenza ulwazi, uncwadi, umculo, isoftware, kunye neminye imixholo, ebonakalayo okanye yedijithali, ifumaneke kuluntu ukuba ithengiswe okanye simahla.[1] Ngokuqhelekileyo, igama elithi ukupapasha libhekisela ekudalweni nasekuhanjisweni kweencwadi ezishicilelweyo, njengeencwadi, iincwadi ezihlekisayo, amaphephandaba kunye namaphephancwadi eluntwini. Ngokufika kweenkqubo zolwazi lwedijithali, ububanzi buye banda ukubandakanya ukupapashwa kwedijithali ezifana ne-e-books, iimagazini zedijithali, iiwebhusayithi, imidiya yoluntu, umculo, kunye nopapasho lomdlalo wevidiyo. 

Ishishini lopapasho lorhwebo lisusela kwiindibano ezinkulu zezizwe ngezizwe ezifana neNews Corp, Pearson, Penguin Random House, kunye neThomson Reuters[2] ukuya kwiibrendi eziphambili kunye namawakawaka abapapashi abancinci abazimeleyo. Inezahlulo ezahlukeneyo ezinjengorhwebo/upapasho lokuthengisa lweentsomi nezingeyonyani, upapasho olufundisayo, nopapasho lwezemfundo nolwenzululwazi.[3] Upapasho lukwaqhutywa ngoorhulumente, imibutho yoluntu, kunye neenkampani zabucala kwiimfuno zolawulo okanye zokuthotyelwa, ishishini, uphando, ubhengezo, okanye iinjongo zomdla woluntu.[4] Oku kunokubandakanya iingxelo zonyaka, iingxelo zophando, uphando lwemarike, iinkcazo zomgaqo-nkqubo, kunye neengxelo zobugcisa. Ukuzipapasha kuye kwaba yinto eqhelekileyo. 

Upapasho luye lwavela kuhlobo oluncinane, lwakudala olulinganiselwe ngumthetho okanye inkolo ukuya kwishishini langoku, elikhulu elisasaza zonke iintlobo zolwazi.[5] 

"Umpapashi" unokubhekisa kwinkampani epapashayo, umbutho, okanye umntu okhokela inkampani yopapasho, ushicilelo, iphepha-ndaba, okanye iphephandaba. 

Amanqanaba opapasho 
Inkqubo yopapasho egubungela uninzi lwemagazini, ijenali, kunye nabapapashi bencwadi ibandakanya: (Amanqanaba awohlukeneyo ayasebenza kwiindidi ezahlukeneyo zabapapashi)[6] 

Ukugunyazisa 
ukuBhala 
iKopi yokuhlela uYilo 
uKubhala 
isiHlomelo 
ULungiselelo 
Imijikelo yoLungiso Izalathiso 
Izilungiso 
zokugqibela 
Upapasho 
lwewebhu 
Prepress 
Ushicilelo 
Isithuba 
sokushicilela 
ukusasaza 
iindaba 
zopapasho
Amaphephandaba okanye iiwebhsayithi zeendaba lupapasho lweengxelo zangoku, amanqaku, kunye neempawu ezibhalwe ziintatheli. Bakhululekile, ngamanye amaxesha nge-premium edition, okanye bahlawulelwe, nokuba ngabodwa okanye ngokubhalisa. Zizaliswe ngeefoto okanye ezinye imidiya kwaye zihlala zixhaswa ngeentengiso. Ngokuqhelekileyo, bagubungela iindaba zasekhaya, zelizwe, kunye nezamazwe ngamazwe okanye babonise ishishini elithile. Eminye imibutho ibiza iifizi zeprimiyamu ukuba inobuchule kunye nolwazi olukhethekileyo. Ushishino lweendaba lwenzelwe ukunceda uluntu, lubambe abantu kunye namashishini ukuba baphendule, kunye nokukhuthaza inkululeko yolwazi kunye nokuthetha.[7] Abahleli balawula ithoni yelizwi lopapasho lwabo; umzekelo, amanqaku angalunganga xa ethelekisa akhuthazayo anokuchaphazela imbono yomfundi.[8] 

Upapasho lwejenali 
Ijenali yimpapasho yezemfundo okanye yobugcisa efumaneka ngedijithali kunye (okanye) nefomathi yoshicilelo, equlathe amanqaku abhalwe ngabaphandi, oonjingalwazi, kunye nabantu abanobuchule obuchwepheshile. Ezi mpapasho zingqale kwintsimi ethile yaye ngokufuthi zityhalela phambili imida emiselwe kwezi nkalo. Ngokuqhelekileyo baneenkqubo zokuphononongwa koontanga phambi kokupapasha ukuvavanya ukunyaniseka kunye nomgangatho womxholo.[9] 

Ukupapasha iimagazini 
Imagazini liphephancwadi elipapashwa rhoqo ngamathuba athile. Ibonisa uyilo loyilo, ukufota, kunye nemifanekiso egubungela umxholo okanye umdla othile. Iimagazini zifumaneka ngokuprintwa okanye ngefomathi yedijithali kwaye zingathengwa kwii-apps okanye iiwebhusayithi ezinjenge-Readly okanye zifikeleleke simahla kwii-apps okanye iiwebhusayithi ezifana ne-Issuu. 

Upapasho lweencwadi 
Ishishini lokupapasha iincwadi kwihlabathi liphela lineencwadi ezihlelwe njengeentsomi okanye ezingezizo ezenyani kunye noshicilelo, i-e-book, okanye i-audiobook. Imarike yeencwadi inkulu, inabantu abamalunga ne-1.5 yebhiliyoni abathetha isiNgesi.[10] Iinkonzo zoguqulo zikwafumaneka ukwenza ezi zibhalo zifikeleleke ngezinye iilwimi. Ukupapasha ngokwakho kwenza ukuba upapasho lufikeleleke ngokubanzi ngoshicilelo oluncinci oluqhutywa yidijithali okanye amaqonga okuzipapasha kwi-intanethi. Itekhnoloji yesikrini se-E-reader iyaqhubeka nokuphucuka ngochaso olwandisiweyo kunye nesisombululo sibenza bakhululeke ngakumbi ukufunda. Incwadi nganye ine-ISBN ebhalisiweyo ukuyichonga. Izalathisi 

zokupapasha uvimba 
weefayili ziqulathe idata enokuphendwa ephawulweyo malunga namashishini, iimveliso kunye neenkonzo. Zaziprintwa kwixesha elidlulileyo kodwa ngoku zifumaneka kakhulu kwi-intanethi. Izalathiso ziyafumaneka njengoluhlu olunokuphendwa, kwimephu, njenge-portal yecandelo elithile, njengendawo yophononongo (ingcali okanye umthengi), okanye njengendawo yokuthelekisa. Nangona amanye amashishini esenokungazithathi njengabapapashi, indlela idatha eboniswa ngayo ipapashwa. 

Ukupapashwa kweencwadi zokufunda
Incwadi yesikhokelo yincwadi efundisayo, okanye i-e-book, enenkcazelo ngombandela othile yaye isetyenziswa ngabantu abafunda eso sifundo.[11] Isidingo sokupapashwa kweencwadi siyaqhubeka ngenxa yemfuno yemfundo yehlabathi.[12][13] Iincwadi zezifundo ezivela kubapapashi abakhulu zidityaniswa kunye namaqonga okufunda kwi-intanethi ngolwazi lweengcali kunye nokufikelela kwilayibrari yeencwadi enomxholo wedijithali.[14] Umshicileli weyunivesithi ngumpapashi wezemfundo oqhutywa yiyunivesithi. IOxford University Press yeyona inkulu ehlabathini kwaye igxile kuphando, imfundo, kunye nokufundisa ulwimi lwesiNgesi kumazwe ngamazwe.[15] 

Ikhathalogu yopapasho 
Ikhathalogu lulawulo olubonakalayo okanye uluhlu loluhlu olukhulu lweemveliso ezikuvumela ukuba ukhangele kwaye uthenge kwinkampani ethile.[16] Kushicilelo, oku kuqhelekile kwifomathi yencwadi ethambileyo okanye uvimba weefayili. Iikhathalogu ezincinci ezibonakalayo ziyakwaziwa ngokuba ziincwadana. Nge-Intanethi, ziye zavela kugcino-lwazi olunokuphendwa lweemveliso ezaziwa phantsi kwegama elithi e-commerce. Iikhathalogu ezisebenzisanayo kunye neencwadana ezifana ne-IKEA[17] kunye ne-Avon[18] zivumela abathengi ukuba bakhangele uluhlu olupheleleyo ukuba abagqibanga ngokuthenga kwabo. Iwebhu ephendulayo kunye noyilo losetyenziso luya kuvumela ukudityaniswa okuthe kratya phakathi kwemiboniso yekhathalogu esebenzayo kunye nogcino-lwazi lwemveliso enokuphendwa. 

Ukupapashwa kweWebhu 
Kuze kube kutshanje, iincwadi zenyama bezingowona mthombo uphambili wolwazi lokurekhoda. Ukufikeleleka kunye nokufikelela kwihlabathi jikelele, lo mxholo unokuphinda usetyenziswe kwiwebhu. Ngokomzekelo, iThala leencwadi laseBritani, ligcina izinto ezingaphezu kwe-170 lezigidi kunye nezongezelelo ezitsha ezizizigidi ezi-3 nyaka ngamnye.[19] Ngemvume, umxholo unokupapashwa kwi-intanethi nge-e-books, iincwadi zeaudio, iiwebhusayithi ezisekelwe kwi-CMS, amaqonga okufunda kwi-intanethi, iividiyo, okanye ii-apps eziphathwayo. Kwi-Intanethi, ababhali kunye nabahleli bekopi baziwa njengababhali bomxholo kunye nabahleli bomxholo, nangona iindima zabo zihluka kubalingane babo abasekwe ngokuprinta. Intengiso 

yeNtengiso 
inokubonelela ngengeniso okanye ingeniso exhaswa ngemali kubapapashi. Ukuba intengiso inembuyekezo kutyalo-mali (ROI), umshicileli unokunyusa ingeniso ngokukhawuleza ngokunyusa inkcitho. I-ROI yokuya kuthi ga kwi-£10 nge-£1 nganye etyaliwe inokwenzeka, njengoko kubonwa kwimikhankaso yeKrisimesi kaJohn Lewis & Partners. [20][21] Ngokunjalo, naluphi na ugcino lweendleko olwenzakalisa umthengi/amava omthengi lunokuchaphazela uphawu kwixesha elide. Intengiso ye-Multichannel inokubiza ngakumbi ekudaleni amava antywilayo angenakuphinda aphindwe ngetshaneli enye. Umzekelo, xa ucinga ngokuchitha imali yokuthengisa, ivenkile enomda omncinci (okanye akukho nanye) xa kuthelekiswa newebhusayithi inexabiso eliphantsi kakhulu kuba isebenza njengebhodi yebhilibhodi enkulu enikezela ngamava okukhangela okuvumela abathengi ukuba benze izigqibo zokuthenga. Ibenza bazive benophawu, ibekho eluntwini, kwaye idale nemisebenzi. Kwakhona, ukusebenzisa i-media media publishing ukukhangisa kune-ROI enhle ukuba i-trending, umxholo ophezulu wekhwalithi wenziwa obonisa ngokufanelekileyo kwi-brand.

Upapasho oludityanisiweyo 
Inqaku eliphambili: 
Ifilim, umabonakude, unomathotholo, kunye neentengiso zipapasha ulwazi kubaphulaphuli babo. Imidlalo yekhompyuter, ukusasaza usetyenziso, kunye nemidiya yoluntu ipapasha umxholo ngeendlela ezahlukeneyo ezinokugcina abaphulaphuli bebandakanyeka ngakumbi. Ukuthengisa iimveliso ezongezelelweyo ngokusondeleyo kwifilimu enkulu, njenge-Star Wars, ngumzekelo wokushicilela. Ezi mveliso zibandakanya kodwa azikhawulelwanga kwiincwadi ezijikelezayo, iinoveli zegraphic, iialbham zengoma, imidlalo yekhompyuter, iimodeli kunye nezinto zokudlala, izithuba zemidiya yoluntu, kunye nopapasho lokwazisa. Imizekelo yopapasho oludityanisiweyo olusekwe kwiincwadi nguHarry Potter kunye noJames Bond franchise. 

Bona kwakhona: Upapasho lwamaxesha ngamathuba 
Upapasho lwencwadi amacandelwana 

Bona kwakhona: Imbali yeencwadi 
"Inkampani yoshicilelo lweencwadi" iqondisa kwakhona apha. Ngompapashi ogama linguNkampani yokuPapasha iNcwadi, bona iFama (Tennessee). 
Ubume bopapasho buhlala buguquka. Ngoku kukho iindidi ezine eziphambili zabapapashi kupapasho lweencwadi:[22] 

Abapapashi abaphambili 
Ezi nkampani ngokwesiko zivelisa iincwadi ezikhutshelweyo ngoshicilelo olukhulu. Baye baseka uthungelwano olusasaza ezo ncwadi kwiivenkile zezitena kunye nodaka kunye namathala eencwadi. 

Xa umshicileli oqhelekileyo esamkela incwadi ukuze ipapashwe, bafuna ukuba umbhali asayine isivumelwano esinikezela ngamalungelo athile kumpapashi. Ukutshintshana, umshicileli uya kuhoya yonke imiba yokupapasha incwadi ngexabiso lompapashi. Bathembele ngokupheleleyo kwiintengiso zencwadi ukubuyisela ezo ndleko kwaye benze inzuzo. Umbhali ufumana umrhumo kwintengiso nganye (kwaye maxa wambi intlawulo yangaphambili xa incwadi yamkelwa[23]). Ngenxa yomngcipheko wemali, abapapashi abaqhelekileyo bakhetha ngokugqithiseleyo into abaza kuyipapasha, kwaye bayayigatya imibhalo-ngqangi emininzi engeniswe kubo.[24] 

Ngo-2013, iPenguin (ephethwe nguPearson) kunye neRandom House (ephethwe nguBertelsmann) yadityaniswa, yanciphisa ishishini lokushicilela eliqhelekileyo ukuya kwiqaqobana labapapashi abakhulu njengoko liqhelanise nemidiya yedijithali.[25] Ukudityaniswa kwadala esona sipapashi sencwadi sabathengi sikhulu kwihlabathi jikelele, kunye nesabelo semarike yehlabathi esingaphezulu kwama-25 ekhulwini. [26] Ukusukela ngo-2022, malunga ne-80% yemarike yorhwebo yase-United States yeencwadi yayilawulwa yi-"Big Five" yezindlu zopapasho: iPenguin Random House, iHachette, iHarperCollins, iSimon & Schuster, kunye neMacmillan. [27]

NgoNovemba ka-2020, i-ViacomCBS yavuma ukuthengisa uSimon & Schuster, umshicileli wencwadi wesithathu ngobukhulu e-United States, kwiPenguin Random House kwisivumelwano, ukuba sasidlulile, ngesenzile eyona nkampani inkulu yopapasho emhlabeni. Ngomhla wesi-2 kuNovemba ka-2021, iSebe lezoBulungisa lase-United States lafaka isimangalo (i-US v. Bertelsmann SE & CO. KGaA, et al.) ukuthintela ukudityaniswa ngezizathu zokungathembeki, [28] kwaye nge-31 ka-Okthobha ka-2022, iNkundla yeSithili ye-DC yagweba iSebe lezoBulungisa, yafaka isithintelo esisisigxina kwisigwebo esisisigxina.[29] 

Nangona iinkampani zamaphephandaba namaphephancwadi zisenazo ngokufuthi oomatshini bokushicilela nokudibanisa iincwadi, abapapashi beencwadi abafane babe nayo.[catation] Ngokufanayo, urhwebo ludla ngokuthengisa iimveliso ezigqityiweyo ngokusebenzisa umsasazi ogcina aze asasaze izinto zompapashi ngexabiso lepesenti okanye azithengise ngexabiso lentengiso okanye ngokubuyisela. 

Abanye abapapashi abakhulu banezahlulo ezipheleleyo ezinikezelwe kwi-franchise enye, umz., i-Ballantine Del Rey LucasBooks inamalungelo akhethekileyo kwi-Star Wars e-United States; I-Random House UK (Bertelsmann) / Century LucasBooks inamalungelo afanayo e-United Kingdom. Ishishini lemidlalo yevidiyo lizipapasha ngokwalo ngeBL Publishing/Black Library (Warhammer) kunye neeWizards of the Coast (Dragonlance, Realms Forgotten, njl.). I-BBC inecandelo layo lopapasho elenza kakuhle kakhulu ngothotho olude olufana noGqirha Ngubani. Le misebenzi yemultimedia zithengiswe ngamandla, kwaye iintengiso zihlala zigqwesa umndilili oshicilelweyo wokuma wedwa, nto leyo eyenza ukuba ibeyingqwalasela yomdla wenkampani.[30] 

Ukufika kwe-Intanethi kunikeze enye indlela yokuhambisa iincwadi kwaye uninzi lwabapapashi abaqhelekileyo banikezela ngeencwadi zabo ngefomathi ye-ebook. Ukulungiselela incwadi yokupapashwa kwe-e-book kuyafana nokupapashwa, kunye neenguqu ezincinci kuphela kwinkqubo yokunika ingxelo kwiindlela ezahlukeneyo zokupapasha; Ukupapashwa kwe-E-ncwadi kwakhona kuphelisa ezinye iindleko ezifana nesaphulelo esinikwa abathengisi (ngokuqhelekileyo malunga neepesenti ezingama-45).[31] 

Abashicileli abancinci 
Abapapashi abancinci, abakwabizwa ngokuba ngabashicileli abazimeleyo okanye abakwi-indie,[32] basebenza ngemodeli yemveli (oko kukuthi umbhali unikezela ngamalungelo athile ngokutshintshiselana nompapashi othwele zonke iindleko zokupapasha), kodwa imiqathango yabo echanekileyo inokwahluka kakhulu.[33] Amaxesha amaninzi, abahlawuli kwangaphambili kwi-royalties. 

Ukupapashwa kweHybrid 
Umshicileli oxubileyo wabelana ngeendleko zokupapashwa (kwaye ngoko ke imingcipheko) kunye nombhali. Ngenxa yolu mngcipheko wemali, bayayikhetha into abayipapashayo. Ikhontrakthi iyahluka ngokokuthethwano phakathi kombhali kunye nenkampani, kodwa iya kuhlala ibandakanya ukunikezelwa kwamalungelo athile kumpapashi.[34] Upapasho oluxutyiweyo lungumthombo wengxoxo-mpikiswano kushishino lopapasho, ngenxa yokutyekela koshicilelo olungamampunge lokuzenza imixube. 

Amampunge okushicilela
Ushicilelo lwamampunge luya kupapasha nayiphi na incwadi. Ngembuyekezo, umbhali kufuneka ahlawule zonke iindleko zokupapashwa, anikezele amalungelo athile kumshicileli, kwaye ahlawule intlawulo kwiintengiso. Oomatshini bokushicilela abangamampunge badla ngokubandakanyeka kuqheliselo lwenkohliso okanye banikela iinkonzo ezinexabiso eliphezulu, nezikumgangatho ophantsi kunye noncedo olulinganiselweyo olufumanekayo kumbhali. E-US, ezi zenzo zikhankanywe yi-Bureau Business Bureau njengeengxelo ezingathandekiyo ngabathengi. [35] Ngenxa yodumo olubi lopapasho olungamampunge, uninzi lokushicilela olungamampunge luzibiza ngokuba ngabapapashi abaxubeneyo. Umbutho wabaBhali (SoA) kunye neGuild yababhali baseGreat Britain (WGGB) baye bacela uhlaziyo lwecandelo lopapasho elihlawulweyo. Le mibutho, emele ababhali abangama-14,800, ipapashe ngokudibeneyo ingxelo yokubhentsisa imikhwa emibi exhaphakileyo phakathi kweenkampani ezihlawulisa ababhali ukuba bapapashe umsebenzi wabo ngelixa behlutha amalungelo abo. 

Ukuzipapasha ngokwakhe 
Xa umbhali ezipapasha ngokwakhe incwadi, ugcina onke amalungelo kwaye athathe uxanduva kuwo onke amanqanaba okulungiselela, ukupapasha kunye nokusasaza incwadi. Umbhali unokuqesha iingcali ngentlawulo-ngenkonzo ngokwesiseko njengoko kufuneka, (umzekelo umhleli, umyili wekhava, umhloli-zingqinisiso) okanye abandakanye inkampani ukuze ibonelele ngephakheji ehlanganisiweyo.[36] 

Uphuhliso lwakutsha nje 
Upapasho olufikelelekayo lusebenzisa ukufakwa kwedijithali kweencwadi ukuzimakisha kwi-XML kunye nokuvelisa iifomati ezininzi zokuthengisa kubathengi, ngokuqhelekileyo kujoliswe kwabo bafumana ubunzima bokufunda. Iifomathi zibandakanya ubungakanani obukhulu boshicilelo, iifomati ezikhethekileyo zoshicilelo ze-dyslexia, [37] iingxaki zokulandelela iliso, kunye nokuncipha kwe-macular, kunye neBreyile, iDAISY, iincwadi ezimanyelwayo, kunye ne-e-books.[38] 

Ushicilelo oluluhlaza luthetha ukulungelelanisa inkqubo yopapasho ukunciphisa impembelelo yokusingqongileyo. Omnye umzekelo yingcamango yoshicilelo olufunekayo, usebenzisa iteknoloji yedijithali okanye yokuprinta-kwimfuno. Oku kucutha imfuno yokuthumela iincwadi kuba zenziwa kufutshane nomthengi ngexesha elililo. [39] 

Olunye uphuhliso kukukhula kopapasho lwe-intanethi, apho kungekho zincwadi zenyama zaveliswayo. Umbhali wenza i-e-book aze ayifake kwiwebhusayithi, apho nabani na anokuyikhuphela kwaye ayifunde. 

Inani elandayo lababhali basebenzisa intengiso ye-niche kwi-intanethi ukuthengisa iincwadi ezininzi ngokuzibandakanya nabafundi babo kwi-Intanethi.[40] 

Ukubekwa emgangathweni 
Jonga kulwahlulo lwe-ISO lwe-ICS 01.140.40 kunye ne-35.240.30 ngolwazi oluthe vetshe.[41][42] 

Imiba yomthetho 
Privishing 
Inqaku eliphambili: Ushicilelo
Upapasho kukusasazwa kweekopi okanye umxholo eluntwini.[43][44] I-Convention yaseBerne ifuna ukuba oku kunokwenziwa kuphela ngemvume yomnini-copyright, leyo ekuqaleni isoloko ingumbhali.[43] Kwi-Universal Copyright Convention, “upapasho” luchazwa kwiSiqendu VI “njengokuveliswa kwakhona ngendlela ebambekayo nokusasazwa ngokubanzi kuluntu lweekopi zomsebenzi ekunokufundwa kuwo okanye kubonwe ngenye indlela ngokubonwayo.”[44]

Ukupapasha (ushicilelo lwabucala, kodwa akufanele lubhidaniswe nokuzipapasha) ligama lanamhlanje lokupapasha incwadi kodwa ushicilele iikopi ezimbalwa kakhulu okanye ngokunqongophala kwentengiso, intengiso, okanye inkxaso yokuthengisa kangangokuba ngokunempumelelo ingafikeleli kuluntu.[45] Le ncwadi, ngelixa ipapashwe ngegama, iphantse ibe yinto engenakwenzeka ukuba ifumaneke ngeendlela eziqhelekileyo ezifana neevenkile zeencwadi, zihlala zingenako uku-odolwa ngokukodwa, kwaye inokungabikho kwenkxaso okuphawulekayo kumshicileli wayo, kubandakanywa nokwala ukuphinda ukuprinta isihloko. Incwadi efihliweyo inokuthiwa "ibulewe." Ngokuxhomekeke kwinkuthazo, ukuthengisa kusenokubandakanya ukophulwa kwemvumelwano, ukujongwa, [46] okanye ukuziqhelanisa neshishini elilungileyo (umz., ukungashicileli iincwadi ezininzi kunokuba umpapashi ekholelwa ukuba ziya kuthengiswa ngexesha elide elifanelekileyo). Umshicileli 

weMbali 

osebenza ekuqaleni kweGutenberg letterpress ukusuka kwinkulungwane ye-15 (umzobo ka-1877) 
Upapasho lwenzeka ngokuyilwa kokubhala kwaye lwaba luncedo ngakumbi ekusungulweni koshicilelo. Ngaphambi kokushicilela, iincwadi ezisasazwayo zazikhutshelwa ngesandla ngababhali. Ngenxa yoshicilelo, upapasho luye lwaqhubela phambili kunye nophuhliso lweencwadi. 

Umyili wamaTshayina u-Bi Sheng wenza uhlobo lwengqayi yodongwe enokushenxiswa c. 1045, kodwa akukho mizekelo yaziwayo eseleyo yomsebenzi wakhe. Umsebenzi waseburhulumenteni waseKorea uCh'oe Yun-ŭi, owayehlala ngexesha leGoryeo Dynasty, wayila intsimbi yokuqala eshukumayo ngo-1234–1250 AD. [47] 

EYurophu 
uJohannes Gutenberg wavelisa uhlobo olushukumayo eYurophu malunga ne-1450, kunye nezinto ezintsha zokuyila uhlobo olusekwe kwimatrix kunye nokungunda ngesandla. Ukuveliswa koomatshini bokushicilela ngokuthe ngcembe kwabangela ukuba iincwadi zingabizi mali ininzi ukuvelisa yaye zafumaneka ngokubanzi. 

Iincwadi zamandulo ezishicilelweyo, amaphepha angatshatanga, kunye nemifanekiso eyadalwa ngaphambi kowe-1501 eYurophu zaziwa ngokuba zii-incunables okanye incunabula. "Indoda eyazalwa ngo-1453, unyaka wokuwa kweConstantinople, yayinokukhangela emva ukususela kunyaka wayo wamashumi amahlanu kubomi bakhe apho kwakushicilelwe iincwadi ezimalunga nezigidi ezisibhozo, mhlawumbi ngaphezu kwabo bonke ababhali baseYurophu abaye bavelisa ukususela oko uConstantine waseka isixeko sakhe ngo-AD 

330. 

" yenkulungwane yeshumi elinesibhozo yorhwebo lweencwadi zaseJamani njengexesha leSturm und Drang, isiJamani “yesaqhwithi noxinzelelo.”[49] 

Abavangeli basemazweni bazisa oomatshini bokushicilela eAfrika engezantsi kweSahara phakathi kwenkulungwane ye-18. [50] 

Ngokwembali, upapasho luye lwaphathwa ngabapapashi, nangona abanye ababhali bazipapasha ngokwabo.[51] 

EUnited States 
Ulwazi olongezelelekileyo: Iincwadi eUnited States kunye neMbali yeNcwadi eMelika
Ishishini lokushicilela lase-US laqala ngomatshini wokushicilela eMassachusetts ngo-1638, laseka iNew England njengendawo yokuqala. IFiladelphia nayo yaba yinto ebalulekileyo, kunye noWilliam Bradford waseka indawo yokuqala yokusila kunye noBenjamin Franklin evula owakhe umatshini. Embindini wenkulungwane ye-19, isiXeko saseNew York saba liziko leshishini, eliphawulwe ngokunyuka kwezindlu ezinkulu zopapasho ezifana noHarper, Wiley, Putnam, kunye noScribner, abaxhamla kwimithetho yelungelo lokushicilela kunye neendlela ezintsha zokusasaza. Ekuqaleni, babethembele kakhulu kwimisebenzi yaseBritani erhwaphiliziweyo de kwasekwa imithetho yezizwe ngezizwe yamalungelo okukopi ngo-1891. [52] Embindini wenkulungwane ye-19 kwakhona kwabona izinto ezintsha ezifana nephepha "iinoveli zedime" zenza ukuba uncwadi lufikeleleke ngakumbi. [53] Ixesha lasemva kweMfazwe Yehlabathi I yayiyeyona nto iphambili yokupapasha kwaseMelika ngababhali abatsha kunye nabapapashi abafana noSimon & Schuster kunye neRandom House evelayo. Uxinzelelo olukhulu lwabangela ukudodobala, kodwa ishishini laphinda labuyela emva kwemfazwe. Ukusukela ngeminyaka yee-1960s, bekukho umkhwa wokudityaniswa kunye nokudityaniswa, ukukhawulezisa ngokunyuka kwabathengisi be-intanethi kunye ne-ebooks, nangona isiXeko saseNew York sihlala siyindawo enkulu yopapasho yehlabathi, ikhaya labapapashi be-"Big Five" (kubandakanya iHarperCollins, iPenguin Random House, kunye noSimon & Schuster, abashicileli bemfundo yaseMcmilw, iMcmilw Isikolo, kunye noWiley, kunye nabapapashi abaninzi abazimeleyo. [54] Ukuqala ngeCornell University Press ngo-1869 kunye neJohns Hopkins University Press ngo-1878, iiyunivesithi ezininzi zaseka izindlu zokupapasha ukupapasha iincwadi zezifundo kunye neejenali zolu hlobo eziveliswe ngabafundi babo kunye nabafundi abaphumeleleyo. Noko ke, kwinkulungwane yama-21, kukho iingxaki zemali. ziye zanciphisa imveliso yazo. [55] 

Uphononongo olusekelwe e-US ngo-2016 oluye lwaphanda abavakalisi abangama-34 lwafumanisa ukuba abafazi abathe tye, abanamandla, abamhlophe bamele kakhulu ishishini lokushicilela e-US.[56] I-Salon ichaze le meko “njengokunqongophala kweyantlukwano emva kweziganeko kwincwadi yehlabathi.” [57] Uphando ngo-2020 olwenziwa liqela elifanayo lafumanisa ukuba akukho tshintsho lubalulekileyo lwamanani kukungabikho kweyantlukwano ukusukela kuphando luka-2016.[58] Ukunqongophala kweyantlukwano kwishishini lokushicilela laseMelika ibe ngumba iminyaka. Ngaphakathi kolu shishino, eyona mali incinci yeyantlukwano ibikwizikhundla eziphezulu zokuhlela.[59] 

Ixesha le-Intanethi 
Ukusekwa kwe-World Wide Web ngo-1989 ngokukhawuleza kwaqhubela iwebhusayithi ibe yeyona ndlela iphambili yopapasho. I-Wikis kunye neeblogi zaphuhliswa ngokukhawuleza, zilandelwa ziincwadi ze-intanethi, amaphephandaba akwi-intanethi kunye neemagazini ze-intanethi. Oku kukwaququzelela ukuhlangana kwethekhnoloji yomxholo wentengiso kunye nokuzipapasha kunye nokudibanisa ukupapashwa kunye nokuveliswa kwimveliso ye-intanethi ngokuphuhliswa komxholo we-multimedia.

Ushicilelo yinkqubo yokuvelisa kwakhona ngobuninzi umbhalo kunye nemifanekiso kusetyenziswa i-master form okanye itemplate. Iimveliso zokuqala ezingezizo zamaphepha ezibandakanya ukuprinta ziquka izitywina zesilinda kunye nezinto ezifana neCyrus Cylinder kunye neCylinders kaNabonidus. Indlela yokuqala eyaziwayo yoshicilelo yavela kwimixube ye-inki eyenziwe kwiphepha okanye ilaphu elivela kwimibhalo ekwiicwecwe zamatye, ezazisetyenziswa ngenkulungwane yesithandathu.[1][a] Ukushicilela ngokucinezela umfanekiso oyinki ephepheni (usebenzisa ushicilelo lweplanga) lwavela emva kwaloo nkulungwane.[3] Uphuhliso lwakamva kubugcisa bokushicilela luquka uhlobo olushukumayo olwaqanjwa ngu-Bi Sheng malunga ne-1040[4][5] kunye nomatshini wokushicilela owayilwa nguJohannes Gutenberg ngenkulungwane ye-15. Ubugcisa bokushicilela badlala indima ephambili kuphuhliso lweRenaissance kunye neNguqulelo yeNzululwazi kwaye babeka isiseko sezinto eziphathekayo kuqoqosho lwale mihla olusekelwe kulwazi kunye nokusasazwa kwemfundo kubantu abaninzi.[6] 

Imbali 
Inqaku eliphambili: Imbali yoshicilelo 
lwe-Woodblock yoshicilelo 
Inqaku eliphambili: Ukuprintwa kwe-Woodblock 
Ukuprintwa kwe-Woodblock yindlela yokushicilela umbhalo, imifanekiso okanye iipateni ezazisetyenziswa ngokubanzi kwi-East Asia. Yavela eTshayina mandulo njengendlela yokushicilela kwilaphu kwaye kamva kwiphepha.[3] 

EMpuma Asia 

I frontispiece entsonkothileyo Diamond Sutra evela Tang ubukhosi China, AD 868 (British Library), yafunyanwa kuMqolomba Library of Mogao emiqolombeni e Dunhuang, kodwa mhlawumbi ishicilelwe e Sichuan.[7] 
Inqaku eliphambili: Imbali yoshicilelo eMpuma yeAsia 
Imizekelo yokuqala yokukhuhla inki-inkiyi kunye neebhloko zokushicilela zamatye ezinokuthi zivele phakathi kwenkulungwane yesithandathu eTshayina. Uhlobo loshicilelo olubizwa ngokuba lushicilelo lweplanga lomatshini ephepheni lwaqala ngenkulungwane yesi-7 kubukhosi baseTang, [3] [1] kwaye emva koko lwasasazeka kulo lonke elaseMpuma Asia. INara yaseJapan yashicilela iHyakumantō Darani en masse malunga ne-770, kwaye yasasazwa kwiitempile kulo lonke elaseJapan. EKorea, umzekelo wokuprintwa kweenkuni ukusuka kwinkulungwane yesibhozo wafunyanwa kwi-1966. Ikopi ye-Buddhist Dharani Sutra ebizwa ngokuba yi-Pure Light Dharani Sutra (isiKorea: 무구정광대다라니경; Hanja: 無垢淨光大陀 Mugugwa jeng : 無垢淨光大陀 Mugugwa jeg : darani-gyeong), yafunyanwa eGyeongju, kwi-pagoda yobukhosi baseSilla eyalungiswa ngo-751, [8] yayingenamhla kodwa kufuneka idalwe ngaphambi kokwakhiwa kwakhona kwe-Shakyamuni Pagoda ye-Bulguk Temple, kwiPhondo laseKyongju ngo-751. Kuqikelelwa ukuba uxwebhu lwenziwe emva kwe-704. [8] 

Ngenkulungwane yesithoba, ushicilelo ephepheni lwaluthathiwe, kwaye incwadi yokuqala eyasindayo ngokupheleleyo yiDayimane Sutra (iThala leeNcwadi laseBritani) ka-868, elafunyanwa eDunhuang [14]. Ngenkulungwane yeshumi, kwashicilelwa imibhalo engama-400 000 yezinye iisutra nemifanekiso, kwaza kwashicilelwa iincwadi zamandulo zikaConfucius. Umshicileli onobuchule unokuprinta ukuya kutsho kumaphepha angama-2,000 anamaphepha amabini ngosuku.[15]

Ushicilelo lwanwenwela kwangethuba eKorea naseJapan, ekwasebenzisa iilogogram zesiTshayina, kodwa obu buchule bukwasetyenziswa eTurpan naseVietnam kusetyenziswa iqela leminye imibhalo. Obu buchule ke bunwenwela ePersi naseRashiya.[16] Le ndlela yobugcisa yathunyelwa eYurophu malunga ne-1400 kwaye yayisetyenziswa ephepheni kwiiprinta ezindala kunye namakhadi 



okudlala 
. Kukho ubungqina obubonisa ukuba ezi bloko zokuprinta zenziwe ngezinto ezingezizo iinkuni, mhlawumbi itoti, ilothe, okanye udongwe. Ubuchule obusetyenziswayo abuqinisekanga. Block yoshicilelo kamva waphuma ukusetyenziswa ngexesha Renaissance Timurid.[18] Indlela yoshicilelo eYiphutha yamkelwa ngokuphinda kuveliswe imibhalo kwimicu yamaphepha kwaye inikezelwe ngeekopi ezahlukeneyo ukuhlangabezana nemfuno.[19][20] 

EYurophu 

Iplanga yokuqala eyaziwayo, i-1423, i-Buxheim, enemibala 
yeBlock yokuprinta yafika eYurophu njengendlela yokushicilela kwilaphu, apho yayixhaphake ngo-1300. Xa iphepha lalifumaneka lula, malunga ne-1400, ubuchule batshintshelwa ngokukhawuleza kwimifanekiso yonqulo emincinci yonqulo kunye namakhadi okudlala ashicilelwe ephepheni. Olu shicilelo lwaveliswa ngamanani amakhulu kakhulu ukusuka malunga no-1425 ukuya phambili.978-0-495-09705-1 

Malunga nenkulungwane yeshumi elinesihlanu, iincwadi zebhloko, iincwadi ezenziwe ngamaplanga ezinesicatshulwa kunye nemifanekiso, edla ngokukrolwa kwibhloko enye, zavela njengenye indlela engabizi kakhulu kwimibhalo-ngqangi kunye neencwadi eziprintwe ngohlobo olushukumayo. Yonke le yayiyimisebenzi emifutshane, enemifanekiso emininzi, eyeyona ithengiswa kakhulu ngelo xesha, ephindwa kwiinguqulelo ezininzi ezahlukeneyo zeencwadi ezineebhloko: iArs moriendi neBiblia pauperum yayizezona zixhaphakileyo. Kusekho ukuphikisana phakathi kwabaphengululi malunga nokuba intshayelelo yabo yandulelayo okanye, ngokombono woninzi, ilandele ukwaziswa kohlobo olushenxisekayo, noluhlu oluqikelelwayo lwemihla luphakathi ko-1440 no-1460.[21] 

Ukuprintwa kohlobo olushenxisekayo I- 

Copperplate ye-1215–1216 5000 yemali yephepha lemali eneentlobo ezilishumi zobhedu ezishenxisekayo 

iJikji, "Iimfundiso eziKhethiweyo zeZageli zamaBhuda kunye neeNgcali zoNyana" zaseKorea, eyona ncwadi yamandulo eyaziwayo yashicilelwa ngohlobo lwentsimbi eshukumayo, i- 
1377 
. i-typography esebenzisa iziqwenga ezihambayo zohlobo lwentsimbi, ezenziwe ngokuphosa kwimatriki ezibethelwa ziiletterpunches. Uhlobo olushukumayo luvunyelwe kwiinkqubo ezibhetyebhetye kakhulu kunokhuphelo lwesandla okanye ibhloko yoshicilelo.

Malunga ne-1040, inkqubo yokuqala eyaziwayo yohlobo olushukumayo yadalwa e-China ngu-Bi Sheng ngeporcelain. [5] UBi Sheng wasebenzisa uhlobo lodongwe, olwaphuka lula, kodwa uWang Zhen ngo-1298 wayeqingqe uhlobo oluhlala ixesha elide emthini. Kwakhona wavelisa inkqubo entsonkothileyo yokudibanisa iitafile ezijikelezayo nokunxulumanisa amanani noonobumba ababhaliweyo besiTshayina nto leyo eyenza ukuseta nokushicilela kube nempumelelo ngakumbi. Sekunjalo, eyona ndlela iphambili eyayisetyenziswa apho yahlala ishicilela i-woodblock (ixylography), “eyangqineka inexabiso eliphantsi yaye inempumelelo ngakumbi ekushicileleni isiTshayina, esinamawakawaka oonobumba baso”.[22] 

Umatshini wokushicilela wobhedu waqala eTshayina ekuqaleni kwenkulungwane ye-12. Yayisetyenziswa kushicilelo olukhulu lwemali yephepha eyayikhutshwe yindlu yobukhosi beNgoma yaseMntla. Uhlobo olushukumayo lwasasazeka lwaya eKorea ngexesha lolawulo lweGoryeo. 

Malunga ne-1230, amaKorea enza uhlobo lwentsimbi lokushicilela olushukumayo kusetyenziswa ubhedu. IJikji, eyapapashwa ngowe-1377, yeyona ncwadi yamandulo eyaziwa ngesinyithi. Kwasetyenziswa uhlobo lokuphosa, lutshintshwe kwindlela yokuphosa iingqekembe. Lo mlinganiswa wawusikwa kumthi we<em>beech, owathi emva koko wacinezelwa kudongwe oluthambileyo ukwenza isikhunta, yaye ubhedu lwagalelwa kumbumba, yaye ekugqibeleni olo hlobo lwakhazimliswa.[23] Uhlobo lwentsimbi yaseMpuma lwasasazwa eYurophu phakathi kwenkulungwane ye-14 kunye nasekuqaleni kwe-15. Uhlobo lwaseKorea lohlobo lwesinyithi olushukumayo lwachazwa ngumphengululi ongumFrentshi uHenri-Jean Martin njenge "ifana kakhulu nekaGutenberg".[29] Ababhali-mbali abagunyazisiweyo uFrances Gies noJoseph Gies babanga ukuba "Ukubaluleka kwe-Asia yokuveliswa kohlobo olushukumayo ngoku kumiselwe ngokuqinileyo, kwaye ubuchule baseTshayina-Korean, okanye ingxelo yayo yaya ngasentshona iphantse yaqingqwa."[30] 


Ityala leziqwenga zohlobo lwesinyithi kunye nomcimbi wohlobo kwintonga yokuqamba Inqaku 
lokushicilela 
Inqaku eliphambili: Ushicilelo lokushicilela 

, uyilo lokushicilela, uyilo lwe-Strany. IMyuziyam yasePlantin-Moretus 
Malunga nowe-1450, uJohannes Gutenberg wasungula inkqubo yokuqala yokushicilela eYurophu. Uphucule izinto ezintsha kuhlobo lokuphosa olusekwe kwi-matrix kunye nokungunda kwesandla, ukuziqhelanisa ne-screw-press, ukusetyenziswa kwe-inki esekwe kwi-oyile, kunye nokudalwa kwephepha elithambileyo nelifunxa ngakumbi.[31] UGutenberg waba ngowokuqala ukwenza iziqwenga zakhe zohlobo oluphuma kwialloyi yelothe, itoti, iantimony, ubhedu kunye nebismuth – amalungu afanayo asasetyenziswayo namhlanje.[32] UJohannes Gutenberg waqala umsebenzi kumatshini wakhe wokushicilela malunga no-1436, ngokubambisana no-Andreas Dritzehen - lowo wayemyalele ngaphambili ukusika i-gem - kunye no-Andreas Heilmann, umnini wephepha lokusila. [33] [iphepha elifunekayo]

Xa kuthelekiswa noshicilelo lweplanga, ukusetwa kwamaphepha ohlobo olushenxisekayo nokushicilela ngomatshini kwakukhawuleza yaye kuhlala ixesha elide. Kwakhona, iziqwenga zohlobo lwentsimbi zaziqinile kwaye noonobumba bafana ngakumbi, okukhokelela kuchwethezo kunye neefonti. Umgangatho ophezulu kunye nexabiso eliphantsi ngokwentelekiso yeBhayibhile kaGutenberg (1455) yamisela ukongama kohlobo lokubhala olunokushenxiswa kwiilwimi zaseNtshona. Umatshini wokushicilela wanda ngokukhawuleza kulo lonke elaseYurophu, wakhokelela kwiRenaissance, kwaye kamva kulo lonke ihlabathi. [34] 


Igumbi lokubeka iphepha – c. Ngowe-1920 
iphephancwadi i<em>Time Life labiza iinguqulelo ezintsha zikaGutenberg kushicilelo loonobumba olushenxisekayo lolona luyilwe lubalulekileyo lwewaka lesibini leminyaka.[35] 

Umatshini wokushicilela weRotary 
Inqaku eliphambili: Umatshini wokushicilela weRotary 
Umatshini wokushicilela werotary oqhutywa ngumphunga, owasungulwa ngo-1843 eUnited States nguRichard M. Hoe, [36] ekugqibeleni wavumela izigidi zeekopi zephepha ngosuku nje olunye. Ukuveliswa kwemisebenzi eprintiweyo ngobuninzi emva kokutshintshwa kwephepha eliqengqelekayo, njengoko ukutya okuqhubekayo kwavumela ukuba oomatshini basebenze ngesantya esiphezulu. Uyilo lwantlandlolo lukaHoe lwalusebenza ukuya kuthi ga kwi-2,000 revolutions ngeyure apho uguqulo ngalunye ludiphozithe imifanekiso yamaphepha ama-4, nto leyo enika umshicileli i-output yamaphepha angama-8,000 ngeyure.[37] Ngowe-1891, iNew York World nePhiladelphia Item zazisebenza ngoomatshini bokushicilela abangama-90,000 bevelisa amaphepha anamaphepha ama-4 ngeyure okanye angama-48,000 anamaphepha asi-8.[38] 

Umatshini wokushicilela ojikelezayo usebenzisa izinto ezibonwayo ezijikelwe kwicylinder ukuprinta kwimiqulu emide eqhubekayo yephepha okanye ezinye iisubstrates. Ukuprintwa kwegubu elijikelezayo kamva kwaphuculwa kakhulu nguWilliam Bullock. Kukho iintlobo ezininzi zetekhnoloji yoshicilelo olujikelezayo olusasetyenziswa nanamhla: i-sheetfed offset, irotogravure, kunye noshicilelo lwe-flexographic.[39] 

Umthamo woshicilelo 
Itheyibhile idwelisa elona nani liphezulu lamaphepha olunokushicilela uyilo loshicilelo ngeyure.

Inqaku eliphambili: Ushicilelo lwe-Woodblock 
Ushicilelo lweWoodblock bubuchule bokushicilela umbhalo, imifanekiso okanye iipateni ezazisetyenziswa ngokubanzi kulo lonke elaseMpuma Asia. Yavela eTshayina mandulo njengendlela yokushicilela kwilaphu kwaye kamva kwiphepha.[3] 
EMpuma Asia 
I frontispiece entsonkothileyo Diamond Sutra evela Tang ubukhosi China, AD 868 (British Library), yafunyanwa kuMqolomba Library of Mogao Imiqolomba e Dunhuang, kodwa mhlawumbi ishicilelwe e Sichuan.[45]


 
Inqaku eliphambili: Imbali yoshicilelo eMpuma Asia
Imizekelo yokuqala yokukhuhla kwe-inki kunye neebhloko ezinokubakho zokuprinta zivela phakathi kwenkulungwane yesithandathu e-China. Uhlobo loshicilelo olubizwa ngokuba lushicilelo lweplanga lomatshini ephepheni lwaqala ngenkulungwane yesi-7 kubukhosi baseTang, [3] [1] kwaye emva koko lwasasazeka kulo lonke elaseMpuma Asia. INara yaseJapan yashicilela iHyakumantō Darani en masse malunga ne-770, kwaye yasasazwa kwiitempile kulo lonke elaseJapan. EKorea, umzekelo wokuprintwa kweenkuni ukusuka kwinkulungwane yesibhozo wafunyanwa kwi-1966. Ikopi ye-Buddhist Dharani Sutra ebizwa ngokuba yi-Pure Light Dharani Sutra (isiKorea: 무구정광대다라니경; Hanja: 無垢淨光大陀 Mugugwa jeng : 無垢淨光大陀 Mugugwa jeg : darani-gyeong), yafunyanwa eGyeongju, kwi-pagoda yobukhosi baseSilla eyalungiswa ngo-751, [8] yayingenamhla kodwa imele ukuba idalwe ngaphambi kokwakhiwa kwakhona kwe-Shakyamuni Pagoda yeTempile yaseBulguk, kwiPhondo laseKyongju ngo-751 [9][46][47][48][49] Kuqikelelwa ukuba uxwebhu lwenziwe emva kwe-704. [8] 

Ngenkulungwane yesithoba, ushicilelo ephepheni lwaluthathiwe, kwaye incwadi yokuqala eyasindayo ngokupheleleyo yiDayimane Sutra (iThala leencwadi laseBritani) ka-868, elafunyanwa eDunhuang. Ngenkulungwane yeshumi, kwashicilelwa imibhalo engama-400 000 yezinye iisutra nemifanekiso, kwaza kwashicilelwa iincwadi zamandulo zikaConfucius. Umshicileli onobuchule unokuprinta ukuya kutsho kumaphepha angama-2,000 anamaphepha amabini ngosuku.[15] 

Ushicilelo lwanwenwela kwangethuba eKorea naseJapan, ekwasebenzisa iilogogram zesiTshayina, kodwa obu buchule bukwasetyenziswa eTurpan naseVietnam kusetyenziswa iqela leminye imibhalo. Obu buchule ke bunwenwela ePersi naseRashiya.[16] Le ndlela yobugcisa yathunyelwa eYurophu malunga ne-1400 kwaye yayisetyenziswa ephepheni kwiiprinta zakudala kunye namakhadi 



okudlala 
. Kukho ubungqina obubonisa ukuba ezi bloko zokuprinta zenziwe ngezinto ezingezizo iinkuni, mhlawumbi itoti, ilothe, okanye udongwe. Ubuchule obusetyenziswayo abuqinisekanga. Block yoshicilelo kamva waphuma ukusetyenziswa ngexesha Renaissance Timurid.[52] Indlela yoshicilelo eYiphutha yamkelwa ngokuphinda kuveliswe imibhalo kwimicu yamaphepha kwaye inikezelwe ngeekopi ezahlukeneyo ukuhlangabezana nemfuno.[53][20] 

EYurophu 

Iplanga yokuqala eyaziwayo, i-1423, i-Buxheim, enemibala 
yeBlock yokuprinta yafika eYurophu njengendlela yokushicilela kwilaphu, apho yayixhaphake ngo-1300. Xa iphepha lalifumaneka lula, malunga ne-1400, ubuchule batshintshelwa ngokukhawuleza kwimifanekiso yonqulo emincinci yonqulo kunye namakhadi okudlala ashicilelwe ephepheni. Ezi printing zaveliswa ngamanani amakhulu kakhulu ukusuka malunga ne-1425 ukuya phambili.978-0-495-09705-1

Embindini wenkulungwane yeshumi elinesihlanu, iincwadi zebhloko, iincwadi ezenziwe ngomthi ezinemibhalo kunye nemifanekiso, zihlala zikrolwa kwibhloko enye, zavela njengenye indlela engabizi kakhulu kwimibhalo-ngqangi kunye neencwadi eziprintwe ngohlobo olushukumayo. Yonke le yayiyimisebenzi emifutshane, enemifanekiso emininzi, eyeyona ithengiswa kakhulu ngelo xesha, ephindwa kwiinguqulelo ezininzi ezahlukeneyo zeencwadi ezineebhloko: iArs moriendi neBiblia pauperum yayizezona zixhaphakileyo. Kusekho ingxwabangxwaba phakathi kwabaphengululi malunga nokuba intshayelelo yabo yandulela okanye, ngokwembono yesininzi, ilandele ukwaziswa kohlobo olushukumayo, noluhlu oluqikelelwayo lwemihla luphakathi ko-1440 no-1460.[54] 

Ukuprintwa kohlobo olushenxisekayo I- 

Copperplate ye-1215–1216 5000 yemali yephepha lemali eneentlobo ezilishumi zobhedu ezishenxisekayo 

iJikji, "Iimfundiso eziKhethiweyo zeZageli zamaBhuda kunye neeNgcali zoNyana" zaseKorea, eyona ncwadi yamandulo eyaziwayo yashicilelwa ngohlobo lwentsimbi eshukumayo, i- 
1377 
. i-typography esebenzisa iziqwenga ezihambayo zohlobo lwentsimbi, ezenziwe ngokuphosa kwimatriki ezibethelwa ziiletterpunches. Uhlobo olushukumayo luvunyelwe kwiinkqubo ezibhetyebhetye kakhulu kunokhuphelo lwesandla okanye ibhloko yoshicilelo. 

Malunga ne-1040, inkqubo yokuqala eyaziwayo yohlobo olushukumayo yadalwa e-China ngu-Bi Sheng ngeporcelain. [5] UBi Sheng wasebenzisa uhlobo lodongwe, olwaphuka lula, kodwa uWang Zhen ngo-1298 wayeqingqe uhlobo oluhlala ixesha elide emthini. Kwakhona wavelisa inkqubo entsonkothileyo yokudibanisa iitafile ezijikelezayo nokunxulumanisa amanani noonobumba ababhaliweyo besiTshayina nto leyo eyenza ukuseta nokushicilela kube nempumelelo ngakumbi. Sekunjalo, eyona ndlela iphambili eyayisetyenziswa apho yahlala ishicilela i-woodblock (ixylography), “eyangqineka inexabiso eliphantsi yaye iphumelela ngakumbi ekushicileleni isiTshayina, esinamawakawaka oonobumba baso”.[55] 

Umatshini wokushicilela wobhedu waqala eTshayina ekuqaleni kwenkulungwane ye-12. Yayisetyenziswa kushicilelo olukhulu lwemali yephepha eyayikhutshwe yindlu yobukhosi beNgoma yaseMntla. Uhlobo olushukumayo lwasasazeka lwaya eKorea ngexesha lolawulo lweGoryeo. 

Malunga ne-1230, amaKorea enza uhlobo lwentsimbi lokushicilela olushukumayo kusetyenziswa ubhedu. IJikji, eyapapashwa ngowe-1377, yeyona ncwadi yamandulo eyaziwa ngesinyithi. Kwasetyenziswa uhlobo lokuphosa, lutshintshwe kwindlela yokuphosa iingqekembe. Lo mlinganiswa wawusikwa kumthi we<em>beech, owathi ke wacinezelwa kudongwe oluthambileyo ukwenza i<em>mold, yaye ubhedu lwagalelwa kumbumba, yaye ekugqibeleni olo hlobo lwakhazimliswa.[56] Uhlobo lwentsimbi yaseMpuma lwasasazwa eYurophu phakathi kwenkulungwane ye-14 kunye nasekuqaleni kwe-15. Uhlobo lwaseKorea lohlobo lwesinyithi olushukumayo lwachazwa ngumphengululi ongumFrentshi uHenri-Jean Martin njenge "efana kakhulu nekaGutenberg".[62] Ababhali-mbali abagunyazisiweyo uFrances Gies noJoseph Gies babanga ukuba "I-Asian ephambili yokuveliswa kohlobo olushukumayo ngoku imiselwe ngokuqinileyo, kwaye ubuchule baseTshayina-Korean, okanye ingxelo yayo yaya ngasentshona iphantse yaqiniseka."[30]


Ityala lohlobo lwamaqhekeza esinyithi kunye nomcimbi wohlobo kwintonga yokuqulunqa 
Umatshini wokushicilela 
Inqaku eliphambili: Umatshini wokushicilela 

Ukuveliswa koshicilelo, okungaziwa, ukuyilwa nguStradanus, ingqokelela yeMyuziyam yasePlantin-Moretus 
Malunga ne-1450, uJohannes Gutenberg wazisa inkqubo yokuqala yokushicilela yohlobo olushukumayo eYurophu. Uphucule izinto ezintsha kuhlobo lokuphosa olusekwe kwi-matrix kunye nokungunda kwesandla, ukuziqhelanisa ne-screw-press, ukusetyenziswa kwe-inki esekwe kwi-oyile, kunye nokuyilwa kwephepha elithambileyo nelifunxa ngakumbi.[63] UGutenberg waba ngowokuqala ukwenza iziqwenga zakhe zohlobo kwialloyi yelothe, itoti, iantimony, ubhedu kunye nebismuth – ezona zixhobo zisasetyenziswayo namhlanje.[64] UJohannes Gutenberg waqala umsebenzi kumatshini wakhe woshicilelo malunga no-1436, ngokubambisana no-Andreas Dritzehen - lowo wayemyalele ngaphambili ukusika igugu - kunye no-Andreas Heilmann, umnini wephepha lokusila 

. Kwakhona, iziqwenga zohlobo lwentsimbi zaziqinile kwaye noonobumba bafana ngakumbi, okukhokelela kuchwethezo kunye neefonti. Umgangatho ophezulu kunye nexabiso eliphantsi ngokwentelekiso yeBhayibhile kaGutenberg (1455) yamisela ukongama kohlobo lokubhala olunokushenxiswa kwiilwimi zaseNtshona. Umatshini wokushicilela wanda ngokukhawuleza kulo lonke elaseYurophu, wakhokelela kwiRenaissance, kwaye kamva kulo lonke ihlabathi. [65] 


Igumbi lokubeka iphepha – c. Ngowe-1920 
iphephancwadi i<em>Time Life labiza iinguqulelo ezintsha zikaGutenberg kushicilelo loonobumba olushenxisekayo lolona luyilwe lubalulekileyo lwewaka lesibini leminyaka.[66] 

Umatshini wokushicilela weRotary 
Inqaku eliphambili: Umatshini wokushicilela weRotary 
Umatshini wokushicilela werotary oqhutywa ngumphunga, owasungulwa ngo-1843 eUnited States nguRichard M. Hoe, [36] ekugqibeleni wavumela izigidi zeekopi zephepha ngosuku nje olunye. Ukuveliswa kwemisebenzi eprintiweyo ngobuninzi emva kokutshintshwa kwephepha eliqengqelekayo, njengoko ukutya okuqhubekayo kwavumela ukuba oomatshini basebenze ngesantya esiphezulu. Uyilo lwantlandlolo lukaHoe lwalusebenza ukuya kuthi ga kwi-2,000 revolutions ngeyure apho revolution nganye idiphozithe imifanekiso yamaphepha ama-4, inika umshicileli i-output yamaphepha angama-8,000 ngeyure.[67] Ngowe-1891, iNew York World nePhiladelphia Item zazisebenza ngoomatshini bokushicilela abangama-90,000 bevelisa amaphepha anamaphepha ama-4 ngeyure okanye angama-48,000 anamaphepha asi-8.[68] 

Umatshini wokushicilela ojikelezayo usebenzisa izinto ezibonwayo ezijikelwe kwicylinder ukuprinta kwimiqulu emide eqhubekayo yephepha okanye ezinye iisubstrates. Ukuprintwa kwegubu elijikelezayo kamva kwaphuculwa kakhulu nguWilliam Bullock. Kukho iintlobo ezininzi zetekhnoloji yoshicilelo olujikelezayo olusasetyenziswa nanamhla: i-sheetfed offset, i-rotogravure, kunye noshicilelo lwe-flexographic.[69] 

Umthamo woshicilelo 
Itheyibhile idwelisa elona nani liphezulu lamaphepha olunokushicilela uyilo loshicilelo ngeyure.

all 
printing process iintlobo zemimandla ekuphumeni kokugqibela: 

Indawo yomfanekiso (iindawo zoshicilelo) 
Indawo engeyiyo yomfanekiso (iindawo ezingashicileliyo) 
Emva kokuba ulwazi lulungiselelwe ukuveliswa (inyathelo lokushicilela kwangaphambili), inkqubo yokushicilela nganye ineendlela ezicacileyo zokwahlula umfanekiso kwiindawo ezingezizo umfanekiso. 

Ukuprintwa okuqhelekileyo kuneentlobo ezine zenkqubo: 

I-Planographics, apho iindawo zokuprinta kunye nezingashicileliyo zikwindawo enye yendiza kwaye umehluko phakathi kwabo ugcinwa ngamachiza okanye ngeempawu ezibonakalayo, imizekelo yile: i-lithography ye-offset, i-collotype, kunye ne-screenless printing. 
I-Relief, apho iindawo zokushicilela ziphezu kwendawo yendiza kunye neendawo ezingashicileli zingaphantsi komhlaba, imizekelo: i-flexography kunye ne-letterpress. 
I-Intaglio, apho iindawo ezingashicileliyo zikwindawo yendiza kunye nendawo yokushicilela ifakwe okanye ibhalwe ngaphantsi kwendawo, imizekelo: i-steel die engraving, i-gravure, i-etching, i-collagraph. 
I-Porous okanye i-Stencil, apho iindawo zokushicilela zikhona kwizikrini ze-mesh emihle apho i-inki ingangena khona, kunye neendawo ezingashicileliyo ziyi-stencil phezu kwesikrini ukuvala ukuhamba kwe-inki kwezo ndawo, imizekelo: ukuprintwa kwesikrini, i-stencil duplicator, i-risograph. 
Amanqaku okunqampuna 
Ukuprinta umfanekiso ngaphandle kwendawo engenanto ejikeleze umfanekiso, iindawo ezingashicileli kufuneka zinqunywe emva kokushicilela. Amanqaku okunqampuna angasetyenziswa ukubonisa umshicileli apho iphela khona indawo yoshicilelo, kunye nendawo engashicileliyo iqala.[71] Indawo yomfanekiso esikiweyo ibizwa ngokuba yi-bleed. 

I-Letterpress 

Miehle ishicilela ijenali yeLe Samedi. Montreal, 1939. 
Inqaku eliphambili: Letterpress printing 
Letterpress printing bubuchule bokushicilela boncedo. Umsebenzi uqamba aze atshixe uhlobo lomatshini wokushicilela, alufake i-inki, aze acinezele iphepha kuwo ukuze akhuphe i-inki kuhlobo olubangela ukuba kubonakale umfanekiso ephepheni. Kukho iphepha elahlukileyo lemisebenzi eyahlukeneyo umgangatho wephepha ubonisa i-inki eyahlukileyo yokusetyenziswa. 

I<em>Letterpress printing yayiyindlela eqhelekileyo yokushicilela umbhalo owaveliswa nguJohannes Gutenberg phakathi kwinkulungwane ye-15 yaye yahlala isetyenziswa ngokubanzi kwiincwadi nakwezinye izinto de kwakwisiqingatha sesibini senkulungwane yama-20, xa kwaveliswa ukushicilela ngeoffset. Kutshanje, i-letterpress printing ibone imvuselelo ngendlela yobugcisa. Inqaku eliphambili le- 

Offset 
: Umshicileli we-Offset 
Oomatshini bokushicilela be-910-toni kwi-Las Vegas Review-Journal yayingabona bakhulu emhlabeni xa bafakwa ngo-2000.
Ushicilelo lweOffset yinkqubo yoshicilelo esetyenziswa ngokubanzi kule mihla. Le teknoloji ichazwe kakuhle xa umfanekiso ochanekileyo (ochanekileyo) kwipleyiti yokushicilela inki kwaye idluliselwe (okanye "i-offset") ukusuka kwipleyiti ukuya kwingubo yerabha. Umfanekiso wengubo uba ngumfanekiso wesipili somfanekiso wepleyiti. Ugqithiso lwe-offset luhambisa umfanekiso kwi-substrate yokushicilela (ngokuqhelekileyo iphepha), ukwenza umfanekiso ufundeke ekunene kwakhona. Ushicilelo lwe-Offset lusebenzisa inkqubo ye-lithographic esekelwe ekugxothweni kweoli kunye namanzi. Inkqubo ye-offset isebenzisa isithwali semifanekiso esicaba (iplanographic) (ipleyiti) exhonywe kwisilinda sokushicilela. Umfanekiso oza kuprintwa ufumana i-inki kwii-inki rollers, ngelixa indawo engashicileliyo itsala ifilimu (i-acidic) yamanzi, igcina iindawo ezingezizo ze-inki-free. Uninzi lwabashicileli beoffset basebenzisa iisilinda ezintathu: Ipleyiti, ingubo, imbonakalo. Okwangoku, uninzi lweencwadi kunye namaphephandaba aprintwa kusetyenziswa i-offset lithography. 
Inqaku eliphambili 

leGravure : I-Rotogravure 
Gravure yoshicilelo yindlela yokushicilela ye-intaglio, apho umfanekiso oprintwayo wenziwe ngoxinzelelo oluncinci kumphezulu wepleyiti yokushicilela. Iiseli zizaliswe nge-inki, kwaye ukugqithisa kuchithwa kumphezulu nge-blade kagqirha. Emva koko irola enerabha egqunywe ngerabha icofa iphepha kumphezulu wepleyiti ize idibane ne-inki ekwiiseli. Iisilinda zokushicilela zivame ukwenziwa kwintsimbi yobhedu, ethi emva koko i-chromed, kwaye inokuveliswa ngokukrolwa kwedayimane; ukucima, okanye ukuchithwa kwe-laser. 
Ukuprintwa kweGravure kwaziwa ngokukwazi ukuvelisa imifanekiso ephezulu, echanekileyo kunye nokuveliswa kombala ngokuchanekileyo kunye nokusebenzisa izixhobo zokulawula i-viscosity ngexesha lokuvelisa. Ulawulo lwe-inki lokuphuma komphunga luchaphazela utshintsho kumbala womfanekiso oshicilelweyo. 
Ushicilelo lweGravure lusetyenziselwa ushicilelo olude, olukumgangatho ophezulu olunje ngeemagazini, iikhathalogu zokuodola ngeposi, ukupakishwa kunye nokushicilela kwilaphu kunye nephepha lodonga. Ikwasetyenziselwa ukuprinta izitampu zokuposa kunye nelaminates zeplastiki zokuhombisa, ezifana neendawo zokusebenza zasekhitshini. 
I-Flexography 
I-Flexography luhlobo loshicilelo lokukhululeka. Iipleyiti zoncedo ziqhele ukwenziwa kwiifotopolymers. Inkqubo isetyenziselwa ukupakishwa okuguquguqukayo, ibhodi yentsimbi, iilebhile, amaphephandaba kunye nokunye. Kule marike ikhuphisana noshicilelo gravure ngokubamba 80% kwimarike US, 50% eYurophu kodwa kuphela 20% Asia.[72] 
Obunye ubuchule bokuprinta 
Obunye ubuchule bokuprinta obubalulekileyo bubandakanya: 
Iprinta ye-Dayi-sublimation 
Ushicilelo lwe-Pad, oludumileyo ngokukwazi ukuprinta kwindawo entsonkothileyo enemigangatho emithathu 
Ushicilelo loncedo, olusetyenziswa ikakhulu kwiikhathalogu.




 
Inkjet, esetyenziswa ngokwesiqhelo ukuprinta inani elincinane leencwadi okanye ukupakishwa, kunye nokuprinta iintlobo ngeentlobo zemathiriyeli: ukusuka kumaphepha akumgangatho ophezulu alinganisa ushicilelo lwe-offset, ukuya kwiithayile zomgangatho. I-inkjet ikwasetyenziselwa ukufaka iidilesi zokuposa ukwalathisa amaqhekeza eimeyile
ILaser printing (toner printing) isetyenziswa ikakhulu eziofisini nakwitransactional printing (amatyala, amaxwebhu ebhanki). Ushicilelo lweLaser luqhele ukusetyenziswa ziinkampani zeposi ngokuthe ngqo ukwenza iileta zedatha eziguquguqukayo okanye amakhuphoni. 
Ukuprintwa kwesikrini kwiinkqubo ezahlukeneyo ukusuka kwii-T-shirts ukuya kwiithayile zomgangatho, kunye neendawo ezingalinganiyo 
i-Intaglio, esetyenziselwa ubukhulu becala amaxwebhu exabiso eliphezulu afana neemali. 
Ushicilelo lwe-Thermal, oludumileyo ngeminyaka yoo-1990 kushicilelo lwefeksi. Isetyenziswa namhlanje ukuprinta iilebhile ezifana neethegi zempahla yenqwelomoya kunye neeleyibhile zexabiso lomntu kwiikhawunta zedeli zevenkile enkulu. 
Impembelelo yomatshini wokushicilela wohlobo olususwayo lwesiJamani 

Imiba yobungakanani 

Imveliso yaseYurophu yeencwadi eziprintwa ngohlobo olususekayo ukusuka ku-c. 1450 ukuya ku-1800[73] 
Inqaku eliphambili: Imbali yoshicilelo 
Kuqikelelwa ukuba emva kokusungulwa komatshini wokushicilela kaGutenberg, imveliso yeencwadi yaseYurophu yenyuka ukusuka kwizigidi ezimbalwa ukuya malunga neekopi zeebhiliyoni kwisithuba esingaphantsi kweenkulungwane ezine.[73] 

Impembelelo yonqulo 
uSamuel Hartlib, owayegxothelwe eBritani yaye enomdla wohlaziyo lwezentlalo nenkcubeko, wabhala ngowe-1641 ukuba “ubugcisa bokushicilela buya kusasaza ulwazi kangangokuba abantu abaqhelekileyo, bewazi amalungelo nenkululeko yabo, abayi kulawulwa yingcinezelo”.[74][75] 


IReplica yoshicilelo lukaGutenberg kwiMyuziyam yoShicilelo yaMazwe ngaMazwe eCarson, eCalifornia 
Kwilizwe lamaSilamsi, ukushicilela, ngakumbi kwimibhalo yesiArabhu, kwachaswa ngamandla kulo lonke ixesha lokuqala lale mihla, ngokuyinxenye ngenxa yodumo oluphezulu lobugcisa bobugcisa becalligraphy yemveli. Noko ke, ukushicilela ngombhalo wesiHebhere okanye wesiArmenia ngokufuthi kwakuvunyelwa. Ngaloo ndlela, ushicilelo lokuqala lokushicilela ngoonobumba olushenxisekayo kuBukhosi baseOttoman lwalungowesiHebhere ngowe-1493, ekwathi emva koko imibhalo yonqulo nengezonqulo yashicilelwa ngesiHebhere.[76] Ngokonozakuzaku wase-Istanbul phakathi kwinkulungwane yeshumi elinesithandathu, yayisisono kubantu baseTurkey, ngakumbi amaSilamsi aseTurkey, ukushicilela iincwadi zonqulo. Ngowe-1515, uSultan Selim I wakhupha umyalelo wokuba umsebenzi wokushicilela wawufanele ufe. Ekupheleni kwenkulungwane yeshumi elinesithandathu, uSultan Murad III wavuma ukuba kuthengiswe iincwadi ezingeyonxalenye yonqulo ezibhalwe ngoonobumba besiArabhu, ukanti uninzi lwazo lwaluvela eItali. U-Ibrahim Muteferrika waseka umatshini wokuqala wokushicilela ngesiArabhu kwi-Ottoman Empire, ngokuchasene nenkcaso evela kwii-calligraphers kunye neenxalenye ze-Ulama. Yasebenza de kwangowe-1742, ivelisa imisebenzi elishumi elinesixhenxe iyonke, eyayinxulumene nemicimbi engeyiyo eyenkolo, eluncedo. Ukushicilela akuzange kube yinto eqhelekileyo kwihlabathi lamaSilamsi de kwayinkulungwane ye-19.[77]

Abashicileli bolwimi lwesiHebhere bavalwa ukuba bangabikho kwimibutho yokushicilela kwamanye amazwe aseJamani; ngenxa yoko, ukushicilela ngesiHebhere kwanda eItali, ukususela ngowe-1470 eRoma, kwandula ke kwanwenwela nakwezinye izixeko eziquka iBari, iPisa, iLivorno neMantua. Abalawuli basekuhlaleni babenegunya lokunika okanye lokurhoxisa iimpepha-mvume zokupapasha iincwadi zesiHebhere,[78] kwaye uninzi lwezo zishicilelweyo ngeli xesha zinamagama athi 'con licenza de superiori' (ebonisa ukuba ushicilelo lwabo lunikwe imvume ngokusemthethweni) kumaphepha ezihloko zawo. 

Kwakucingwa ukuba ukuqaliswa kokushicilela ‘kwakuya komeleza unqulo kuze komeleze amandla ookumkani.’[79] Uninzi lweencwadi zazizezonqulo, icawa nesithsaba zilawula oko kuqulethweyo. Iziphumo zokushicilela izinto 'ezingalunganga' zazigqithise. UMeyrowitz[79] wasebenzisa umzekelo kaWilliam Carter owathi ngo-1584 washicilela incwadana exhasa ubuKatolika kwiNgilane eyayilawulwa ngamaProtestanti. Umphumo wesenzo sakhe wawujinga. 

Impembelelo yezentlalo 
Ushicilelo lunike uluhlu olubanzi lwabafundi ukufikelela kulwazi kwaye lwenza ukuba izizukulwana zamva zakhe zakhe ngokuthe ngqo kwiimpumelelo zobukrelekrele zangaphambili ngaphandle kweenguqu ezivela kwizithethe zomlomo. Shicilela, ngokutsho kuka-Acton kwintetho yakhe yowe-1895 kwiSifundo seMbali, wanika "isiqinisekiso sokuba umsebenzi weRenaissance uya kuhlala uhleli, ukuba oko kubhaliweyo kuya kufikeleleka kubo bonke, ukuba ukugqwesa kolwazi kunye neengcamango njengoko kwakucinezele amaXesha Aphakathi akusayi kuphinda kuphinde kuvele, ukuba akukho ngcamango iya kulahleka".[74] 


Ushicilelo lweencwadi ngenkulungwane ye-16 
Ushicilelo lwaba luncedo ekutshintsheni intlalo yokufunda. 

U-Elizabeth Eisenstein uchaza iziphumo ezimbini zexesha elide zokuqanjwa kokushicilela. Ubanga ukuba ushicilelo ludale ireferensi ezinzileyo nefanayo yolwazi kwaye ivumele uthelekiso lweembono ezingahambelaniyo.[80] 

U-Asa Briggs noPeter Burke bachonga iindidi ezintlanu zokufunda eziye zaphuhliswa ngokunxulumene nokuqaliswa koshicilelo: 

Ukufundwa okubalulekileyo: Ngenxa yokuba imibhalo ekugqibeleni yafikeleleka kuluntu ngokubanzi, ufundo olunzulu lwavela njengoko abantu babekwazi ukwenza ezabo izimvo kwiitekisi. 
Ukufunda okuyingozi: Ukufunda kwakujongwa njengosukelo oluyingozi kuba kwakugqalwa njengemvukelo nokunganxulumani, ingakumbi kwimeko yabasetyhini, kuba ukufunda kwakunokuvuselela iimvakalelo eziyingozi ezinjengothando, yaye ukuba abafazi babekwazi ukufunda, babekwazi ukufunda amanqaku othando. 
Ukufunda ngokuyilayo: Ushicilelo lwaluvumela abantu ukuba bafunde izicatshulwa kwaye bazitolike ngokuyilayo, amaxesha amaninzi ngeendlela ezahluke kakhulu kunezo zombhali. 
Ufundo olubanzi: Emva kokuba ushicilelo lwenze uluhlu olubanzi lwemibhalo lufumaneke, imikhwa yangaphambili yokufunda ngokucokisekileyo izicatshulwa ukususela ekuqaleni ukuya ekugqibeleni yaqalisa ukutshintsha, yaye abantu baqalisa ukufunda izicatshulwa ezikhethiweyo, nto leyo eyayivumela ufundo olubanzi ngakumbi kuluhlu olubanzi lwezihloko.
Ufundo lwabucala: Ukufunda kwakunxulunyaniswa nokunyuka komntu ngamnye ngenxa yokuba, ngaphambi kokuba kushicilelwe, ukufunda kwakudla ngokuba sisiganeko seqela apho umntu omnye wayefundela iqela. Ngokushicilelweyo, ukufunda nokufumaneka kwemibhalo kwanda, yaye ukufunda wedwa kwaba yinto eqhelekileyo. 
Ukuveliswa kokushicilela nako kwatshintsha indlela yokusebenza kwezixeko zaseYurophu. Abashicileli baye bavela njengeqela elitsha lamagcisa ekwakubalulekile kubo ukufunda nokubhala, ngelixa umsebenzi onzima kakhulu wombhali wehla ngokwendalo. Ukulungiswa kobungqina kwavela njengomsebenzi omtsha, ngelixa ukunyuka kwamanani abathengisi beencwadi kunye noosomathala ngokwemvelo kulandela ukuqhuma kwamanani eencwadi. 

Impembelelo yemfundo 
Umatshini wokushicilela kaGutenberg ube neempembelelo ezinzulu nakwiiyunivesithi. Iidyunivesiti zaphenjelelwa "kulwimi lwazo lokufunda, amathala eencwadi, ikharityhulamu, [kunye] nokufundisa"[81] 

Ulwimi lwezifundo 
Phambi kokusungulwa komatshini wokushicilela, uninzi lwemathiriyeli ebhaliweyo yayingesiLatini. Noko ke, emva kokuveliswa kokushicilela inani leencwadi ezishicilelweyo landiswa kunye neelwimi zomthonyama. IsiLatini asizange sithathelwe indawo ngokupheleleyo, kodwa sahlala silulwimi lwamazwe ngamazwe de kwayinkulungwane yeshumi elinesibhozo.[81] 

Amathala eencwadi aseYunivesithi 
Ngeli xesha, iiyunivesithi zaqalisa ukuseka amathala eencwadi ahamba kunye. "I-Cambridge yenza umfundisi onoxanduva lwethala leencwadi ngenkulungwane yeshumi elinesihlanu kodwa esi sikhundla sapheliswa ngo-1570 kwaye ngo-1577 iCambridge yaseka iofisi entsha yelayibrari yaseyunivesithi. Nangona, iYunivesithi yaseLeuven ayizange ibone imfuneko yelayibrari yaseyunivesithi esekelwe kwingcamango yokuba unjingalwazi wayeyilayibrari. Iilayibrari nazo zaqala ukufumana iincwadi ezininzi ezivela kwizipho kunye nokuthengwa kwe-5. indoda egama linguMerton eyagqiba ekubeni iincwadi kufuneka zigcinwe kwiishelufu ezithe tyaba kunokuba 
i 

- 
lecterns i-comic lupapasho oluqulathe ubugcisa be-comic ngendlela yeephaneli ezilandelelanayo ezimele izigcawu zomntu ngamnye.


 
yayiyi-comic yaseBhritane eyapapashwa ukusuka ngo-1890 ukuya kutsho ngo-1953 i-Hollywood. (1884), nto leyo ephawuleka ngokusetyenziswa kwayo iikhathuni ezilandelelanayo ukutyhileka ezibalisayo ezihlekisayo British zazikho ecaleni lurid ethandwayo "penny dreadfuls" (ezifana Spring-heeled Jack), amakhwenkwe' "amaphepha ibali" kunye imagazini ezihlekisayo Punch, leyo yaba yeyokuqala ukusebenzisa igama elithi "ikhathuni" ngendlela ehlekisayo umzobo walo mihla.

Incwadi yokuqala yala maxesha yaseMelika ehlekisayo, iFamous Funnies: A Carnival of Comics, yakhululwa e-US ngo-1933 kwaye yayilushicilelo lwamaphetshana ahlekisayo ephephandaba angaphambili, awayeseke uninzi lwezixhobo zokubalisa amabali ezisetyenziswa kumabali ahlekisayo.
