[1] Igama elithi incwadi ehlekisayo lisuka kwiincwadi ezihlekisayo zaseMelika eyayikhe yaba yingqokelela yamabali ahlekisayo ethowuni ehlekisayo; nangona kunjalo, olu qheliselo lwathatyathelw’ indawo ngamabali azo zonke iindidi, ngokuqhelekileyo awahlekisayo ngethoni. 

Eyona marike inkulu yeencwadi ezihlekisayo yiJapan. Ngo-1995, imakethi yemanga eJapan yayixabisa i-¥586.4 yeebhiliyoni (i-6-7 yeebhiliyoni zeedola), [2] ngeentengiso zonyaka ze-1.9 yeebhiliyoni zeencwadi zemanga (imiqulu ye-tankōbon kunye neemagazini ze-manga) e-Japan, ilingana ne-15 lemiba kumntu ngamnye.[3] Ngo-2020, imakethi yemanga eJapan ifikelele kwixabiso elitsha lerekhodi le-¥612.5 yebhiliyoni ngenxa yokukhula okukhawulezayo kweentengiso zemanga zedijithali kunye nokonyuka kwentengiso yoshicilelo.[4][5] Imarike yeencwadi ezihlekisayo e-United States naseKhanada yayixabisa i-1.09 yeebhiliyoni zeedola ngo-2016. [6] Ukusukela ngo-2017, oyena mpapashi mkhulu wencwadi ehlekisayo e-United States ngumsasazi wemanga iViz Media, ilandelwa yi-DC Comics kunye neMarvel Comics equka amaqhawe ahlekisayo afana noSuperman, uBatman, uWonder Woman, u-Spider-Man, i-Incredible Hulk, kunye ne-X-Men.[7] Iindidi zeencwadi ezihlekisayo ezithengiswa kakhulu e-US ukusukela ngo-2019 ziintsomi zabantwana kwi-41%, manga nge-28% kunye ne-superhero comics kwi-10% yemarike.[8] Enye imarike enkulu yeencwadi ezihlekisayo yiFransi, apho amahlaya aseFranco-Belgian kunye nemanga yaseJapan nganye imele i-40% yemarike, ilandelwa ngamahlaya aseMelika kwisabelo semarike se-10%. 

Ulwakhiwo 
Inqaku eliphambili: Iikhomikhi § Isigama 
Iincwadi ezihlekisayo zaseMelika 
Inqaku eliphambili: Incwadi yaseMelika ehlekisayo
 
Iphepha 76 lenoveli engumzobo eqhelanisiweyo kaTristram Shandy, ezotywe ngumzobi wekhathuni waseBritane uMartin Rowson.
Iincwadi ezihlekisayo zithembele kakhulu kwintlangano yazo kunye nenkcazo ebonakalayo. Ababhali banikezela ingqwalasela ebalulekileyo kwimiba efana noyilo lwephepha, ubungakanani, uqhelaniso, kunye nokumiswa kweephaneli. Ezi mpawu zibalulekile ekugqithiseni ngokukuko umxholo kunye nemiyalezo ekwincwadi yamahlaya. Amacandelo aphambili eencwadi ezihlekisayo abandakanya iiphaneli, amaqamza entetho (ekwabizwa ngokuba ziibhaluni), imigca yesicatshulwa kunye nabalinganiswa. Iibhaluni zentetho zithatha uhlobo lwezikhongozeli zeconvex ezibamba incoko yababini kwaye ziqhagamshelwe kumlinganiswa kusetyenziswa into yomsila. Umsila uquka imvelaphi, indlela, incam, kunye nendawo eyalathayo. Ukwenziwa kweencwadi ezihlekisayo kubandakanya amanyathelo abalulekileyo aliqela: ukubhala, ukuzoba, kunye nemibala. Izixhobo ezahlukeneyo zetekhnoloji kunye neendlela zisetyenziselwa ukwenza iincwadi ezihlekisayo, ezibandakanya iikhonsepthi ezinjengezalathiso, izembe, idatha kunye neemetriki. Ukulandela ezi zikhokelo zokufomatha, inkqubo iqhubeka ngokubhala, ukuzoba, kunye nemibala.[10] EUnited States, igama elithi "incwadi ehlekisayo", lisetyenziswa ngokubanzi kumaphepha ahlekisayo kunye namaphepha orhwebo ngelixa "inoveli yegraphic" ligama elisetyenziselwa iincwadi ezizimeleyo. [11][12] 

Ii-Comics njengendlela yoshicilelo zikhona e-United States ukususela kushicilelo lwe-Adventures kaMnu Obadiah Oldbuck ngo-1842 kwi-hardcover, [13] eyenza ukuba ibe yincwadi yokuqala eyaziwayo yaseMelika eyincwadi ehlekisayo. Iincwadi zeProto-comics zaqala ukuvela kwasekuqaleni kwenkulungwane yama-20, kunye necomic yokuqala enobungakanani obuqhelekileyo obuhlekisayo ibiyiFunnies kwiParade. IFunnies on Parades yaba yincwadi yokuqala eyaseka ubungakanani, ubude bexesha, kunye nemo yencwadi yanamhlanje yamabali ahlekisayo. Ukulandela oku kwaba, iDell Publishing enamaphepha angama-36 eFamous Funnies: A Carnival of Comics njengeyona ncwadi yeendaba yokuqala eyinyani yaseMelika; UGoulart, umzekelo, uyibiza “njengelitye lembombo lelinye lawona masebe anengeniso yokupapasha iimagazini”.[14] Ngo-1905 iNkampani yakwaGW Dillingham yapapasha imicu engama-24 ekhethiweyo ngumzobi weekhathuni uGustave Verbeek kwincwadi ye-anthology ebizwa 'I-Incredible Upside-Downs yeNenekazi eliNcinci uLovekins kunye neNdoda Emdala Muffaroo'.[15] Ukwaziswa kukaJerry Siegel kunye noSuperman kaJoe Shuster ngo-1938 zajika iincwadi ezihlekisayo zaba lishishini eliphambili[16] kwaye zangenisa iGolden Age yeComic Books. I-Golden Age yavela kwi-archetype ye-superhero. Ngokutsho kombhali-mbali uMichael A. Amundson, abalinganiswa abanomtsalane abakuncwadi yamabali ahlekisayo banceda abafundi abaselula bathomalalisa ukoyika imfazwe yenyukliya baze bathomalalise ukuxhalaba ngemibuzo eyayibuzwa ngamandla eathom.[17]

Ababhali-mbali ngokubanzi bahlula umda wexesha lencwadi yaseMelika ehlekisayo ngokwexesha. I-Golden Age ye-Comic Books yaqala ngo-1938, ngokuqala kwe-Superman in Action Comics #1, epapashwe yi-Detective Comics (umanduleli we-DC Comics), ethathwa njengesiqalo sencwadi yanamhlanje yamahlaya njengoko yaziwa namhlanje.[18] ISilver Age of Comic Books ngokuqhelekileyo ijongwa njengeyomhla ukususela kuvuselelo lokuqala oluyimpumelelo lwefom ye-superhero eleleyo ngelo xesha, ngokuqala kweFlash in Showcase #4 (Oct. 1956).[19][20] ISilver Age yahlala ngasekupheleni kweminyaka yoo-1960 okanye ekuqaleni koo-1970s, ngelo xesha iMarvel Comics yaliguqula eliphakathi kunye namaqhawekazi endalo anjengoStan Lee kunye noJack Kirby's Fantastic Four kunye noLee kunye noSteve Ditko's Spider-Man. Umda phakathi kweSilver Age kunye neli xesha lilandelayo, iBronze Age yeComic Books, ayichazwanga kakuhle, kunye neBronze Age eqala kwasekuqaleni koo-1970 ukuya phakathi koo-1980. [21] IXesha lanamhlanje leeNcwadi ezihlekisayo ziqala phakathi kwiminyaka yee-1980 ukuza kuthi ga ngoku.[22] 
Inqaku eliphambili: Ikhomiksi ephantsi komhlaba

Isiganeko esibalulekileyo kuluhlu lwexesha lweencwadi ezihlekisayo zaseMelika senzeka xa ugqirha wengqondo uFredric Wertham wavakalisa ukugxeka kwakhe okuphakathi kwincwadi yakhe ethi Seduction of the Innocent (1954). Oku kugxeka kwakhokelela ekubandakanyekeni kweKomitana yeSenate yaseMelika kwi-Juvenile Delinquency, eyaqalisa uphando kwiincwadi ezihlekisayo. U-Wertham waxoxa ukuba iincwadi ezihlekisayo zinoxanduva lokunyuka kobunjubaqa babantwana kwaye zenze impembelelo enokubakho kwisini somntwana kunye nemilinganiselo yokuziphatha.[23] Ukusabela kwingqalelo evela kurhulumente nakumajelo eendaba, ishishini leencwadi ezihlekisayo zaseUnited States laseka iComics Magazine Association of America.[24] I-CMAA yafaka iGunya leKhowudi yeComics kwi-1954 kwaye yaqulunqa iKhowudi yeComics yokuzihlola ngaloo nyaka, eyayifuna zonke iincwadi zee-comic ukuba zihambe kwinkqubo yokuvunywa. Kwada kwaba ngowe-1970 apho iincwadi ezihlekisayo zazinokupapashwa ngaphandle kokudlula ekuhlolweni kweCMAA.[25] IKhowudi yenziwa yayekiswa ngokusesikweni ngoNovemba ka-2011. 

Iincwadi ezihlekisayo eziphantsi komhlaba 
Iicomics ezizezinye 
Inqaku eliphambili: Iicomics ezizezinye
Ngasekupheleni kweminyaka yee-1960s nakwiminyaka yokuqala yee-1970, kwavela ukwanda kokuyila kwinto eyaziwa ngokuba yi- underground comix. Ipapashiwe yaza yasasazwa ngokuzimeleyo kushishino lwamabali ahlekisayo olusekiweyo, uninzi lwaloo mabali ahlekisayo abonakalisa inkcubeko yolutsha kunye nenkcubeko yeziyobisi ngelo xesha. Ingxubevange engaphantsi komhlaba "ibonakaliswe kwaye yahlomla ngeyantlukwano yentlalo kunye neengxwabangxwaba zoluntu lwaseMelika". imifanekiso yabo engafihlisiyo yobunqunu, isini, inhlamba, kunye nezopolitiko azizange zithelekiseke ngaphandle kwezandulela zabo, iphonografi kwaye ifihlakele ngakumbi "iibhayibhile zaseTijuana". Iimidlalo ezihlekisayo ezingaphantsi komhlaba phantse azizange zithengiswe kwiindawo zokuthengisa iindaba, kodwa kwindawo ezifana neevenkile ezinkulu ezikwiivenkile ezinkulu nakwiivenkile ezirekhodishayo, nangeodolo yeposi. Amabali ahlekisayo angaphantsi komhlaba akhuthaze abadali ukuba bapapashe umsebenzi wabo ngokuzimeleyo ukuze babe namalungelo obunini apheleleyo kubalinganiswa babo.[26] 

UFrank Stack's The Adventures of Jesus, epapashwe phantsi kwegama elithi Foolbert Sturgeon, [27] [28] uye wabalelwa njenge-comix yokuqala engaphantsi komhlaba; 

Ukunyuka kweevenkile ezikhethekileyo zencwadi yamahlaya ngasekupheleni kweminyaka yoo-1970 kwadala kwaye kwahambelana nemarike ezinikeleyo "ezimeleyo" okanye "ezinye iicomics" e-US. Ezokuqala iicomics zibandakanya uthotho lwe-anthology Ukufikelela kwiNkwenkwezi, epapashwe ngumbhali wencwadi ehlekisayo uMike Friedrich ukusuka ngo-1974 ukuya ku-1979, kunye noHarvey Pekar's American Splendor, eyaqhubeka nokupapashwa okungaqhelekanga kwinkulungwane yama-21 nalapho uShari Springer Berman noRobert Pulcini baziqhelanisa nefilimu ka-2003. Ezinye ii-comics ezizimeleyo zaqhubeka kwisithethe samahlaya angaphantsi komhlaba. Ngelixa umxholo wabo uhlala ungacacanga, ezinye zifana nemveliso yabapapashi abaqhelekileyo kwifomathi kunye nohlobo kodwa zapapashwa ziinkampani ezincinci ezinamagcisa okanye ngamagcisa angatshatanga. Abambalwa (ngokukodwa i-RAW) bamele iinzame zokulinga ukuzisa ii-comics kufutshane nemo yobugcisa obuhle. 

Ngeminyaka yoo-1970 inkcubeko "yoshicilelo oluncinci" yakhula kwaye yahluka. Ngeminyaka yee-1980, abapapashi abaninzi abazimeleyo - njengePasifiki, i-Eclipse, eyokuQala, iComico, kunye neFantagraphics - babesele beqalile ukukhulula uluhlu olubanzi lweendlela kunye neefomathi-ukusuka kwi-color-superhero, umcuphi, kunye neencwadi ezihlekisayo zesayensi ukuya kumabali amnyama namhlophe-ifomathi yemagazini yeLatin America yokwenene yomlingo. 

Iqela labavakalisi abancinane ngeminyaka yee-1990, layitshintsha indlela nokusasazwa kweecomics zabo ukuze ifane ngokusondeleyo noshicilelo olungelulo olwamahlaya. Ifomu ye-"minicomics", inguqulelo engekho sikweni yokuzipapasha, yavela ngeminyaka yoo-1980 kwaye yaye yaduma ngakumbi phakathi kwamagcisa ngeminyaka yoo-1990, [29] nangona ifikelele kubaphulaphuli abambalwa kunoshicilelo oluncinci. 

Abapapashi abancinci bahlala bekhupha izihloko ezibandakanya iAvatar Press, Hyperwerks, Raytoons, kunye neTerminal Press,ikhuthazwa yinkqubela phambili enjalo kubugcisa bokushicilela njengoshicilelo-kwimfuno yedijithali.
 
Iinoveli zegraphic 

Amaziko oLawulo lweSifo kunye noThintelo apapashe le noveli yegraphic yokufundisa ngo-2018 ukufundisa ulutsha ukuba luyeke ukusasazeka kwezifo ezosulelayo. 
Inqaku eliphambili: inoveli yemizobo 
Ngo-1964, uRichard Kyle waqamba igama elithi "inoveli yegraphic".[30] 

Abanduleli befomu babekho ngeminyaka yoo-1920, ebone ukuvuselelwa kwesithethe samaxesha aphakathi enziwe ngamaplanga yiBelgian Frans Masereel, [31] American Lynd Ward kunye nabanye, kubandakanya uStan Lee. 

Ngomnyaka we-1947, iFawcett Publications yapapasha "iNoveli yeComics No. 1", njengeyokuqala kuluhlu olujoliswe kuyo ezi "noveli zamahlaya". Ibali elikushicilelo lokuqala lalingu "Anarcho, uDictator of Death", intsomi yezahluko ezihlanu ebhalwe ngu-Otto Binder yaza yatsalwa nguAl Carreno. Iyafundeka kwi-intanethi kwiMyuziyam yeDijithali ehlekisayo. [32] Eli phephancwadi alizange lifikelele nakwinkupho yesibini.
 
Ngo-1950, iSt. John Publications yavelisa "inoveli yomfanekiso" ye-digest-size, ejoliswe kubantu abadala, i-Rhymes with Lust, i-128-page digest ngumbhali ongaziwa "uDrake Waller" (uArnold Drake kunye noLeslie Waller), i-penciler Matt Baker kunye ne-inker Ray Osrinanvel "inqaku elipheleleyo" elibhalwe kwi-original-original. "It Rhymes with Inkanuko" iyafumaneka ukuze ufunde kwi-intanethi kwi Digital Comic Museum. [33] 

Ngo-1971, umbhali-igcisa uGil Kane kunye nabasebenzisana nabo basebenzisa ifomathi yephepha "kwinoveli yamahlaya" iBlackmark. UWill Eisner walenza laziwe igama elithi "inoveli eqingqiweyo" xa walisebenzisa kuqweqwe lohlelo olungemva lwencwadi yakhe ethi, Ikhontrakthi noThixo, kunye namanye amaBali eTenement ngo-1978 kwaye, emva koko, ukusetyenziswa kweli gama kwaqala ukwanda. 

Digital comics 
Bona kwakhona: Digital comic 
ubungakanani Market 
Ngo-2017, ubungakanani incwadi ehlekisayo kwimarike kuMntla Melika kwaba nje phezu $1 billion kunye neentengiso digital ukuba tyaba, iincwadi ezigcina incwadi ukuba 1% ukuhla, kunye neevenkile incwadi ehlekisayo ukuba 10% ukuhla phezu 2016 [34]. Imarike yeencwadi ezihlekisayo yehlabathi ibone ukukhula okubonakalayo kwe-12% ngo-2020, yafikelela kwixabiso le-8.49 yeebhiliyoni zeedola. Le ndlela intle iqhubekile ngo-2021, ixabiso lonyaka lemakethi linyuke laya kutsho kwi-9.21 yeebhiliyoni zeedola. Ukwanda kokuthandwa kweencwadi ezihlekisayo kunokubalelwa kumdla ophakamileyo wehlabathi, oqhutywa kakhulu ziinzame zentsebenziswano phakathi kweempawu ezahlukeneyo. Ezi ntsebenziswano zijoliswe ekuveliseni umxholo ohlekisayo onomdla kakhulu, onegalelo ekukhuleni okuqhubekayo kweshishini.[35] 

Ukuqokelela iincwadi ezihlekisayo 
Inqaku eliphambili: Ukuqokelelwa kwencwadi ehlekisayo 
Ngeminyaka yee-1970 kwavela iivenkile ezikhethekileyo zeencwadi ezihlekisayo. Ekuqaleni, iincwadi ezihlekisayo zazithengiswa ngabapapashi kubantwana kuba iincwadi ezihlekisayo zazibonwa njengolonwabo lwabantwana. Noko ke, ngokwanda kokuqondwa kwamabali ahlekisayo njengohlobo lobugcisa kunye nokukhula kobukho benkcubeko yepop yeendibano zencwadi ehlekisayo, ngoku zamkelwa ngabantu abadala abaninzi.[24]

Abaqokeleli beencwadi ezihlekisayo bahlala bebonisa uthando lobomi bonke bamabali angaphakathi komdlalo ohlekisayo, bahlala begxile kumaqhawe athile kwaye bazabalazela ukuqokelela ingqokelela epheleleyo yothotho oluthile. Ii-Comics zinikwe amanani alandelelanayo, kwaye umba wokuqala woluhlu lweencwadi ezihlekisayo ezihlala ixesha elide zithande ukuba zizo zombini ezinqabileyo kwaye zinqweneleka kakhulu phakathi kwabaqokeleli. Ukungeniswa komlinganiswa omtsha kungenzeka ngaphakathi kwesihloko esele sikhona. Umzekelo, ukubonakala kokuqala kwe-Spider-Man kwenzeka kwi-Amazing Fantasy #15. Abalinganiswa abatsha babesoloko beziswa ngolu hlobo, belinda abaphulaphuli abasele bemile ngaphambi kokuba baqalise izihloko zabo. Ngenxa yoko, iicomics ezibonisa inkangeleko yokuqala yomlinganiswa obalulekileyo ngamanye amaxesha kunokuba ngumceli mngeni ngakumbi ukuzifumana kunomcimbi wokuqala wochungechunge oluzimeleyo lwaloo mlinganiswa.

Ezinye iincwadi ezinqabileyo zamahlaya ziquka iikopi zeMotion Picture Funnies engakhutshwanga Weekly #1 ukusuka ngo-1939. Iikopi ezisibhozo, kunye nenye engenaqweqwe lweqweqwe, zavela kwilifa lompapashi ongasekhoyo ngo-1974. "Ikopi Yokuhlawula" yale ncwadi ithengiswe ngeedola ezingama-43,125 kwifandesi ye-2005 yeLifa leMveli.[36] 

Ii-comics ezixabisekileyo zaseMelika ziye zadibanisa ukunqaba kunye nomgangatho kunye nokubonakala kokuqala kwabalinganiswa abadumileyo kunye nokunyamezela. Iincwadi ezine zamahlaya zithengiswe ngaphezulu kwe-US$1 yezigidi ukusukela ngoDisemba ka-2010, kubandakanywa imizekelo emibini ye-Action Comics #1, inkangeleko yokuqala ye-Superman, [37][38] zombini zithengiswa ngasese ngomthengisi we-intanethi i-ComicConnect.com ngo-2010, kunye ne-Detective Comics #27, ukubonakala kokuqala kwe-Batman, ngefandesi kawonkewonke. 

Ukuhlaziya ixabiso elingentla elifunyenwe kwi-Action Comics #1, ukubonakala kokuqala kwe-Superman, intengiso ephezulu kwirekhodi yale ncwadi yi-$ 3.2 yezigidi, ikopi ye-9.0. [39] 

Iimpazamo, ushicilelo lwenkuthazo kumthengisi ohlekisayo, kunye nemiba enosasazo oluphantsi kakhulu ithande ukuba nexabiso elinqongopheleyo kwimarike yeencwadi ezihlekisayo. Ezona ncwadi zinqabileyo zale mihla ezihlekisayo ziquka ushicilelo lwantlandlolo lwe-League of Extraordinary Gentlemen #5, apho umphathi we-DC uPaul Levitz wayikhumbula kwaye wayikhupha ngenxa yenkangeleko yexesha le-Vintage lentengiso ye-"Marvel Douche", umpapashi awayijonga njengekhubekisayo; (Jonga iRecalled comics ukuze ufumane amahlaya amnandi, akhunjulweyo, kunye neempazamo.) 

Ngo-2000, inkampani ebizwa ngokuba yiComics Guaranty (CGC) yaqalisa uqheliselo lwe "slabbing" comics, nto leyo ebandakanya ukugqunywa kumatyala eplastiki ashinyeneyo kwaye iwanike ibakala lamanani. Le ndlela yaphefumlela ukuvela kweNkonzo yeSiqinisekiso seNcwadi yeComic. Ngenxa yokubaluleka kwemeko ekumiseleni ixabiso leecomics ezinqabileyo, ingcamango yokuhlelwa kwenkampani yinkampani engathathi hlangothi, engazibandakanyi ekuthengeni okanye ekuthengiseni iicomics, ibonakala ithembisa. Nangona kunjalo, kukho ingxoxo eqhubekayo malunga nokuba ixabiso eliphezulu lale nkonzo yokuhlela ifanelekile kwaye ingaba inceda abaqokeleli okanye ikakhulu ibonelela kubaxeli abafuna ingeniso ekhawulezileyo, ngokufana nokurhweba ngezitokhwe okanye ubugcisa obuhle. Ukuhlelwa kwe-Comic kudlale indima ekusekeni imigangatho yokuxabisa, apho izikhokelo zexabiso ze-intanethi ezifana ne-GoCollect kunye ne-GPAnalysis zisebenzise ukubonelela ngolwazi lwexabiso lemarike ngexesha lokwenyani. 

Abaqokeleli baphinda bafune amaphepha omzobo woqobo kwiincwadi ezihlekisayo, mhlawumbi ezona zinto zinqabile kwindawo yokuqokelela iincwadi ezihlekisayo. La maphepha abambe ukunqongophala okungenakuthelekiswa nanto ngenxa yento yokuba kukho iphepha elilodwa elikhethekileyo lomzobo wephepha ngalinye elishicilelweyo lapapashwa.

Ukuyilwa kwala maphepha obugcisa boqobo kubandakanya inzame yentsebenziswano: umbhali wenza ibali, igcisa lepensile liyila iipaneli ezilandelelanayo kwiphepha, igcisa le-inki lidlula kwipensile ngepeni kunye ne-inki, unobumba ubonelela ngencoko kunye nokubalisa ngokubhala ngesandla, kwaye ekugqibeleni, umbala wongeza umbala njengokucofa kokugqibela ngaphambi kokuba amaphepha athunyelwe kumshicileli. 

Xa umshicileli ebuyisela amaphepha oqobo lomsebenzi wobugcisa, abuyiselwa kumagcisa ngokwawo. La magcisa ngamanye amaxesha akhetha ukuthengisa la maphepha kwiindibano zencwadi yamahlaya, kwiigalari, nakwimiboniso yobugcisa egxile kubugcisa bencwadi ehlekisayo. Amaphepha oqobo avela kwi-DC kunye neMarvel, anembonakalo yokuqala yabalinganiswa abanjengoSuperman, Batman, Wonder Woman, Flash, Captain Marvel, Spider-Man, Incredible Hulk, Iron Man, Captain America kunye neMighty Thor zithathwa njengobutyebi obuxabisekileyo kwihlabathi lencwadi yamahlaya. 

Imbali yobuhlanga kwiincwadi zaseMelika ezihlekisayo 
Ngeli xesha, inkqubo eqhutywa ngurhulumente, iBhodi yeMfazwe yababhali, yabandakanyeka kakhulu kwinto eya kupapashwa kwiicomic. "Ibhodi yeMfazwe yababhali yasebenzisa iincwadi ezihlekisayo ukubumba iimbono ezidumileyo zobuhlanga kunye nobuhlanga..." [43] Babengasebenzisi nje iincwadi ezihlekisayo njengendlela yokugaya bonke abantu baseMelika, kodwa babezisebenzisa njengepropaganda "[ukwakha] ulungelelwaniso lwentiyo esekwe ngokobuhlanga kwiintshaba zaseMelika." Nangona kunjalo, "ezi ngxelo zokunyamezelana zazabalaza ukoyisa iitrope ezidumileyo neziqondwa ngokubanzi ezisetyenziswa kumashumi eminyaka kwinkcubeko enkulu yaseMelika..." [43] Nangona kunjalo, abazange bafeze le ajenda kuzo zonke ii-comics zabo.
 
Eli candelo linokufuna ukucocwa ukuhlangabezana nemigangatho yomgangatho weWikipedia. Ingxaki ethile yile: phinda ubhale ukwenza ukuxhomekeka kancinci kwiikowuti, ulungele isimbo seWP. Nceda uncede ukuphucula eli candelo ukuba unako. (Julayi 2019) (Funda ukuba ungawususa njani kwaye nini lo myalezo)
Uphindaphindo oluninzi lwantlandlolo lwabalinganiswa abamnyama kwiicomics "luye lwaba lutshintsho 'kumfanekiso omnye obambekayo weSambo'."[41] USambo wayenxulumene ngokusondeleyo ne-coon stereotype kodwa wayenomohluko othile ofihlakeleyo. Zombini ziyindlela ethoba isidima yokubonisa abalinganiswa abantsundu. "Igama ngokwalo, isifinyezo se-raccoon, lihlazo. NjengoSambo, i-coon yaboniswa njengevila, i-coon eyoyikisayo, engapheliyo, engabonakaliyo, i-buffoon." abalinganiswa. "Ukujonga nje kancinci ... kunokunika umbono wokuba iimeko ziye zaphucuka kubantu base-Afrika baseMelika kwiicomic."[41] Kwiimidlalo ezihlekisayo ezininzi eziveliswa ngeli xesha kwakukho utyhalo olukhulu lokunyamezelana phakathi kweentlanga. "La magorha acinga ngokulingana aqala ukwenza isenzo njengoko abantu base-Afrika baseMelika babecelwa ukuba bathathe inxaxheba kumzamo wemfazwe." [41]


Kuluhlu oluhlekisayo lukaCaptain Marvel Adventures, bekukho umlinganiswa ogama linguSteamboat oquka ingqokelela yeengcinga ezimbi kakhulu ezazixhaphakile ngelo xesha. IBhodi yeMfazwe yabaBhali ayizange icele naluphi na utshintsho kulo mlinganiswa ngaphandle kokuboniswa okuyingxaki. Ukususwa kweSteamboat kuluhlu lwenzeka kuphela ngenxa yenkxaso ethe gqolo yeqela lolutsha elimnyama elizinze kwisiXeko saseNew York. ngoko."[43] Emva koko, uSteamboat wanyamalala kwii-comics zonke kunye. Kwakukho i-comic eyenziwe malunga ne-99th Squadron, eyaziwa ngokuba yi-Tuskegee Airmen, iyunithi yomkhosi omnyama we-airmen. Endaweni yokwenza i-comic malunga nebali labo, i-comic yayimalunga ne-Hop Harrigan. Umqhubi wenqwelomoya omhlophe obamba amaNazi, wambonisa iividiyo zakhe ze-Nazi kunye namadoda akhe angama-99 emva koko atyhila iividiyo ze-Nazi. woyisiwe ngabantu base-Afrika baseMelika eyamcaphukisa njengoko ebabona njengohlanga olungaphantsi kwaye akakholelwa ukuba bangcono kakhulu kumadoda akhe." I-Tuskegee Airmen, kunye nemifanekiso yeenqwelomoya ezimnyama ibonakala kwiiphaneli ezintathu kuphela kumashumi amahlanu anesithathu ... "I-Spider-Man 'yayenza yacaca into yokuba amandla amnyama alwayo yayingelonyango lokungabikho kokusesikweni ngokobuhlanga."[41] "I-Falcon yayigxeka ngokuphandle ukuziphatha kwabantsundu isithi' mhlawumbi kubalulekile ukuba sizipholise izinto phantsi-ukuze sikwazi ukukhusela amalungelo esinawo ukuze sibe ngumlinganiswa omnyama [41] ngokuyinxenye utyholwa kwinto yokuba, ngeli xesha, "kwakunqabile ukuba kubekho igcisa okanye umbhali omnyama ovunyelweyo kwinkampani enkulu yamabali ahlekisayo."[41]

Abalinganiswa baseAsia kwiincwadi ezihlekisayo baye bafumana impatho efanayo njengoko benzayo abalinganiswa abamnyama. Babephantsi kwemizobo eyehlisa isidima sobuntu, ngamabali ahlala ebabonisa "njengabangenabuchule nabangenabuntu."[43] Kushicilelo lwango-1944 lwempapasho yase-United States Marines, kwakukho ibali elinesihloko esithi The Smell of the Monkeymen. Le ngxelo ichaza amajoni aseJapan njengama-simen akhohlakeleyo, kwaye yayibonisa izikhundla zabo ezifihliweyo zingcatshwa livumba lemizimba yabo elizothe.[43] Abalinganiswa baseTshayina bafumana impatho efanayo. "Ngexesha iUnited States ingena kwiWWII, iingcamango ezingalunganga zesiTshayina zaziyinxalenye yenkcubeko yobuninzi ...." [43] Nangona kunjalo, ixhala lokuba amaJapan angasebenzisa izinto ezichasene nesiTshayina njengepropaganda baqala "ukubonisa umfanekiso oncomekayo wamahlakani aseTshayina aseMelika..."[43] Kanye njengoko bezama ukubonisa ukumelwa okungcono kwabantu abaMnyama kwii-comics benza okufanayo kubantu baseAsia. Noko ke, “oonobumba bamaJapan nabakwiiPhilippines babengabonakali kakuhle. Omabini la maqela aneenja ezikrazukileyo, iimpahla ezikrazukileyo, nolusu oluqaqambileyo olutyheli.”[43] “Abapapashi babonisa amahlakani aseAsiya aseMerika ngemifanekiso ethob’ isidima nolwimi oluthotywayo kumashumi eminyaka angaphambili. Ngexesha leWWII, "[onke] iqhawe elikhulu elixabisa ispandex lizinikele ekupheliseni abahlaseli baseAsia."[41] Kwakukho "ugqatso oluqhubekayo lokugqithisela apho enye inkcubeko yaseAsia yanikezela nje intonga yentiyo komnye ngaphandle kotshintsho olubonakalayo kwindlela abalinganiswa abaza kuboniswa ngayo."[41 

] kuhle. Ngo-1975, uMarvel wasinika uHector Ayala (owaziwa ngokuba nguThe White Tiger)."[41] "Nangona walwela iminyaka eliqela ecaleni kwamagorha adumileyo anjengoSpider-Man kunye noDaredevil, wathatha iminyaka emithandathu kuphela phambi kokuba ukuthengiswa kwamabali ahlekisayo kuye kwaba kubi kangangokuba uMarvel wamenza ukuba athathe umhlala 

phantsi Ukumelwa komthonyama waseMelika kwiincwadi zamabali ahlekisayo "kunokushwankathelwa kwinkolelo ekhohlakeleyo ekhohlakeleyo"[41] "umxholo ophindaphindiweyo...wabongoza amaIndiya aseMelika ukuba alahle ubutshaba bawo bemveli ngakuMelika. Ngawo apeyintwe njengabanganyamezeliyo nabangabahloniphiyo ezona nkxalabo zibalaseleyo zaseMelika emhlophe".[41] 

Iicomic zaseMpuma Asia 
Imanga yaseJapan 
Inqaku eliphambili: IManga 
Manga (漫画) ziincwadi ezihlekisayo okanye iinoveli zegraphic ezisuka eJapan. Uninzi lwe-manga luhambelana nesitayile esaphuhliswa eJapan ngasekupheleni kwenkulungwane ye-19, nangona uhlobo lobugcisa lunembali ende kwimizobo yangaphambili yaseJapan. Igama elithi manga lisetyenziswa eJapan ukubhekisa kuzo zombini iicomics kunye nekhathuni ngokubanzi. Ngaphandle kweJapan,Eli gama lidla ngokusetyenziswa ukubhekisa kwiicomics ezipapashwe ekuqaleni kweli lizwe. 

Dōjinshi 
Inqaku eliphambili: Dōjinshi
I-Dōjinshi (同人誌, imagazini yabalandeli), iicomics zaseJapan ezenziwe ngabalandeli, zisebenza kwimakethi enkulu kakhulu eJapan kunentengiso yaseMelika "engaphantsi komhlaba"; eyona dōjinshi fair inkulu, Comiket, etsala 500,000 abatyeleli kabini ngonyaka.[44] Inqaku eliphambili 

lemanhwa yaseKorea 
: IManhwa 
Manhwa (만화) ziincwadi ezihlekisayo okanye iinoveli zegraphic ezisuka eKorea. Igama elithi manhwa lisetyenziswa eKorea ukubhekisa kuzo zombini iicomics kunye nekhathuni ngokubanzi. Ngaphandle kweKorea, eli gama lihlala libhekisa kwiicomics ezapapashwa eKorea. IManhwa iphenjelelwe kakhulu ziicomics zaseJapan zeManga nangona yohlukile kwimanga kunye nemanhua eneempawu zayo ezahlukileyo. 

IiWebtoons 
Inqaku eliphambili: 
IiWebtoons zeWebhu ziye zaduma eMzantsi Korea njengendlela entsha yokufunda iicomics. Enkosi ngokuyinxenye kwimithetho eyahlukeneyo yobalo, umbala kunye neziphumo ezibonwayo ezizodwa, kunye nokwenza ngcono ukufunda lula kwii-smartphones kunye neekhompyuter. I-manhwa eninzi yenze utshintsho ukusuka kwi-manhwa yoshicilelo lwemveli ukuya kwi-webtoons ye-intanethi enkosi kwintlawulo engcono kunye nenkululeko engaphezulu kune-manhwa yoshicilelo lwesintu. Ifomati yewebhutoon iye yanda nakwamanye amazwe angaphandle kweKorea njenge China, Japan, Southeast Asia, kunye namazwe aseNtshona. Abasasazi bewebhu abakhulu babandakanya iLezhin, iNaver, kunye neKakao. 

Chinese manhua 
Inqaku eliphambili: Manhua 
Vietnamese truyện tranh 
Inqaku eliphambili: Truyện tranh 
Iicomics zaseYurophu 
Inqaku eliphambili: Iicomic zaseYurophu 
Iicomics zaseFranco-Belgian 
Inqaku eliphambili: Bande dessinée 

René Goscinny (1926–1977), umbhali weAstérix iincwadi ezihlekisayo 
zaseBelgium zihlala zineencwadi ezihlekisayo zeBD ezihlala zibizwa ngokuba ziincwadi ezihlekisayo zaseFransi kunye neBd. (isishunqulelo se-bandes dessinées, esithetha ngokuthe ngqo "imicu ezotyiweyo")[45] ngesiFrentshi, kunye nemicu ngesiDatshi okanye isiFlemish. Iincwadi ezihlekisayo zaseBelgian ekuqaleni ezibhalwe ngesiDatshi zibonisa impembelelo yee-comics zeFrancophone "Franco-Belgian" kodwa zinendlela yazo eyahlukileyo. [icatshulwa] 

Iicomics zaseBritani 
Inqaku eliphambili: Iicomics zaseBritani 
 
Ikhava ukuya kwi-27 kaDisemba 1884 uhlelo lweHalf Holiday ka-Ally Sloper. U-Ally Sloper uthathwa njengomlinganiswa wokuqala ophinda-phinda kwiicomic.[46]
Nangona u-Ally Sloper's Half Holiday (1884) yayijoliswe kwimarike yabantu abadala, abapapashi bakhawuleza bajolise kubantwana abancinci kuluntu kunye noluntu oluye lwadala iingqondo zabantu abancinci kuluntu ngokubanzi, oluye lwadala iingqondo zabantu abancinci. yamabali ahlekisayo njengolutsha oluthile. I-Guardian ibhekisa ku-Ally Sloper "njengomnye wabalinganiswa bekhathuni bokuqala behlabathi", kwaye "njengodumo eBritane yaseVictoria njengoDennis the Menace yayiza kuba yinkulungwane kamva."[47] Iimidlalo ezihlekisayo zaseBritane ekuqaleni kwenkulungwane yama-20 ziye zavela kwimifanekiso eyoyikekayo yepenny yexesha le-Victori Ivampire) [48] Yaqala ukupapashwa ngeminyaka yoo-1830s, ezoyikeka zepenny "yayiyincasa yokuqala yaseBritani yenkcubeko eveliswe ngobuninzi kulutsha."[49]


Umfanekiso oqingqiweyo kaMinnie iMinx, umlinganiswa osuka eBeano, eDundee, eSkotlani. Yaziswa ngo-1938, i-Beano yaziwa ngoburharha bayo be-anarchic, kunye no-Dennis the Menace ebonakala kwikhava. 
Ezona ncwadi zimbini zidumileyo zaseBritane, iBeano kunye neDandy, zaqala ukupapashwa nguDC Thomson ngeminyaka yoo-1930s. Ngo-1950 ukusasazwa kweveki kuzo zombini kwafikelela kwizigidi ezi-2.[50][51] Echaza ukuthandwa okukhulu kwee-comics e-UK ngeli xesha, u-Anita O'Brien, umlawuli we-Cartoon Museum yaseLondon, uthi: "Xa ii-comics ezifana ne-Beano kunye ne-Dandy zayilwa emva phaya kwii-1930s - kwaye ngokwenene ukuya kwii-1950s kunye nee-60s - ezi midlalo zihlekisayo phantse yayikuphela kwendawo yokuzonwabisa eyayifumaneka ku-Dennis [500] abantwana. 1950s, apho intengiso yeBeano yanda. [52] Ubonisa kwiqweqwe le-Beano, kunye ne-BBC ebhekiselele kuye "njengenkwenkwe ekhohlakeleyo yehlabathi elihlekisayo." [52] 
 
Ngo-1954, iicomics zeTiger zazisa uRoy weRovers, umdlalo webhola ekhatywayo owaziwa kakhulu ochaza ubomi bukaRoy Race kunye neqela alidlalelayo, uMelchester Rovers. Ibinzana leendaba zesitokhwe "Izinto zokwenyani zeRoy Rovers" lihlala lisetyenziswa ngababhali bebhola, abahlalutyi kunye nabalandeli xa bechaza imiboniso yobuchule obukhulu, okanye iziphumo ezimangalisayo ezichasene nezinto ezingathandekiyo, ngokubhekiselele kumabali amangalisayo awayeluphawu lokuthengisa lomcu.[53] Ezinye iincwadi ezihlekisayo ezifana noKhozi, iValiant, iQhawe, iViz kunye no-2000 AD nazo zaphumelela. Ezinye iicomics, ezifana noJudge Dredd kunye nezinye izihloko ze-AD 2000, zipapashwe kwifom ye-tabloid. Iicomics ezingaphantsi komhlaba kunye nezihloko "zoshicilelo oluncinci" nazo ziye zavela e-UK, ngakumbi i-Oz kunye ne-Escape Magazine.

Umxholo wesenzo, esinye isihloko esijoliswe kubantwana kwaye sasungulwa phakathi kwiminyaka yee-1970, yaba ngumxholo wengxoxo kwiNdlu ye-Commons. Nangona kumlinganiselo omncinci kunophando olufanayo e-US, iinkxalabo ezinjalo zikhokelele ekumodareyithweni komxholo opapashwe ngaphakathi kwee-comics zaseBritani. Ukumodareyitha okunjalo akuzange kube ngokusesikweni ukusa kwinqanaba lokubhengezwa kwekhowudi, kwaye akuzange kuhlale ixesha elide. I-UK ikwaseke imakethi esempilweni ekushicilelweni kwakhona nasekupakishweni ngokutsha kwemathiriyeli, ngakumbi imathiriyeli evela e-US. Ukunqongophala kwezinto ezinokuthenjwa zeencwadi ezihlekisayo zaseMelika kukhokelele kwiindidi ezishicilelweyo ezimnyama namhlophe, kubandakanywa iicomics zikaMarvel's monster of the 1950s, Fawcett's Captain Marvel, kunye nabanye abalinganiswa abafana noSheena, uMandrake the Magician, kunye nePhantom. Iinkampani ezininzi zokuprinta ziphinde zathatha inxaxheba ekupakisheni kwakhona imathiriyeli yaseMelika kwimakethi yaseBritane, ngakumbi umrhwebi kunye nomthengisi uThorpe & Porter. IMarvel Comics yaseka iofisi yase-UK ngo-1972. I-DC Comics kunye ne-Dark Horse Comics nazo zavula iiofisi ngo-1990. Ukupakishwa ngokutsha kwezinto zaseYurophu akwenzekanga rhoqo, nangona uthotho lweThe Adventures of Tintin neAsterix luye lwaguqulelwa ngempumelelo lwaza lwapakishwa kwakhona kwiincwadi ezinoqweqwe oluthambileyo. Inani lee-comics zaseYurophu ezikhoyo e-UK linyukile kule minyaka ingamashumi amabini idlulileyo. Inkampani yaseBritane iCinebook, eyasungulwa ngo-2005, ikhuphe iinguqulelo eziguqulelwe ngesiNgesi zothotho lwaseYurophu.

Ngeminyaka yoo-1980, ukuvela kwakhona kwababhali namagcisa aseBritane kwazuza udumo kwiincwadi ezihlekisayo eziqhelekileyo, ezazibizwa ngokuba “luHlaselo lwaseBritani” kwimbali yencwadi ehlekisayo. [54] Aba babhali kunye namagcisa beza nemixholo yabo eqolileyo kunye nefilosofi efana nesiphithiphithi, impikiswano kunye nezopolitiko eziqhelekileyo kumajelo eendaba aseBritane. Ezi zinto beziza kuvula indlela yeencwadi ezihlekisayo eziqolileyo kunye "nezimnyama nezimbi" kwaye zitsibe ziqale iXesha lale mihla leeComics.[55] Ababhali baquka u-Alan Moore, odume nge-V yakhe yeVendetta, Ukusuka esihogweni, kwabalindi, kuMarvelman, kunye neLeague of Extraordinary Gentlemen;[56] uNeil Gaiman kunye neentsomi zikaSandman kunye neeNcwadi zeMilingo; UWarren Ellis, umdali weTransmetropolitan kunye nePlanethi; kunye nabanye abafana noMark Millar, umdali we-Wanted kunye ne-Kick-Ass. Uthotho lweencwadi ezihlekisayo uJohn Constantine, iHellblazer, ebekwe ikakhulu eBritani kwaye idlala nomlingo uJohn Constantine, yavula indlela kubabhali baseBritane abafana noJamie Delano. [57] 

Imvumi yeNgesi uPeter Gabriel yakhupha ngo-2000 Ibali le-OVO elakhutshwa kwincwadi yee-CD-booklet-comic book njengenxalenye yohlelo lweCD enesihloko esithi "OVO The Millennium Show". I 2000 Millennium Dome Show esekwe kuyo. [58] 
Inqaku eliphambili: Iicomics zaseSpain 
Kuye kwathiwa inkulungwane ye-13 iCantigas de Santa María inokuthathwa njenge "comic" yokuqala yaseSpain, nangona iincwadi ezihlekisayo (ezaziwa eSpeyin njengehistorietas okanye i-tebeos) zenza ukuqala kwazo malunga ne-1857. Emva kweMfazwe yaseSpain, urhulumente waseFranco wamisela ukunyanzeliswa okungqongqo kuwo onke amajelo eendaba: i-superhero comics yayingavumelekanga kwaye ngenxa yoko, amaqhawe ahlekisayo ayesekelwe kwiingcamango zembali (ngowe-1944 iqhawe lexesha eliphakathi u-El Guerrero del Antifaz ladalwa nguManuel Gago kunye nelinye iqhawe elidumileyo le-medieval, uCapitán Trueno, wadalwa ngu-Miguel 1956 ngu-Miguel-Ambro). Izindlu ezimbini zokupapasha-iBruguera yoHlelo kunye noHlelo lweValenciana-yayilawula imarike yamahlaya yaseSpain ngexesha layo legolide (1950-1970). Ii-comics ezidumileyo zibonise isitayile esibonwayo somdlalo we-slapstick (ephenjelelwe ngababhali baseFranco-Belgian abanjengoFranquin): UCarpanta kaEscobar kunye noZipi y Zape, uVázquez's Las hermanas Gilda kunye noAnacleto, i-Ibáñez's Mortadelo y y Superbel 13 Filemón . Emva kokuphela kwexesha lamaFrancoist, kwabakho umdla okhulayo kumabali ahlekisayo abantu abadala anamaphephancwadi anjengeTotem, El Jueves, 1984, noEl Víbora, kunye nemisebenzi efana neParacuellos nguCarlos Giménez.
 
NgeKrisimesi, abapapashi bapakisha kwakhona imathiriyeli yekhomikhi yonyaka, iprintwe kwaye ibotshwe njengeencwadi ezinoqweqwe olulukhuni ezinobukhulu obungu-A4; "I-Rupert" ibonelela ngomzekelo odumileyo we-comic yaseBrithani yonyaka.U-DC Thomson uphinde wapakisha imicu ye-Broons kunye ne-Oor Wullie kwiincwadi ezinobukhulu obuthambileyo obungu-A4 ngeli xesha leeholide.

Ngomhla we-19 kuMatshi ka-2012, inkonzo yeposi yaseBritane, iRoyal Mail, yakhupha iseti yezitampu ezibonisa abalinganiswa bencwadi ehlekisayo yaseBritani kunye nothotho. [59] Le ngqokelela ibonise iBeano, iDandy, Ukhozi, uKhozi, iRoy yeRovers, iBunty, iBuster, iValiant, iTwinkle kunye no2000 AD.[59] 

Amahlaya aseSpain 

amagcisa aseSpain ngokwesiko asebenza kwezinye iimarike efumana impumelelo enkulu, nokuba ngabaseMelika (umzekelo, abaphumelele iMbasa ye-Eisner uSergio Aragonés, uSalvador Larroca, uGabriel Hernández Walta, uMarcos Martín okanye uDavid Aja), amaBritane (umz., uCarlos Ezquerra, umyili weJaji Dredd-Belggi enye, okanye iFrancis Faruu uJulio Ribera [fr de es; 

Iicomic zaseTaliyane 
Inqaku eliphambili: Iicomic zaseTaliyane 

uHugo Pratt (1927-1995), umbhali woluhlu lweencwadi ezihlekisayo zaseCorto Malta 
E-Italiya, iicomics (ezaziwa ngesiTaliyane njengefumetti) zenza umdlalo wazo wokuqala njengezihlekisayo ekupheleni kwenkulungwane ye-19, kwaye kamva zaguqukela ekubeni ngamabali ohambo. Emva kweMfazwe Yehlabathi II, nangona kunjalo, amagcisa afana noHugo Pratt kunye noGuido Crepax baveze amahlaya aseTaliyane kubaphulaphuli bamazwe ngamazwe. Iincwadi ezihlekisayo ezidumileyo ezinjengeDiabolik okanye umgca weBonelli-okuthiwa uTex Willer okanye uDylan Dog-zihlala zithengiswa kakhulu. [60] 

Ii-comics eziphambili zidla ngokupapashwa rhoqo ngenyanga, kwifomathi yobungakanani be-black-and-white digest, malunga ne-100 ukuya kwi-132 amaphepha. Iingqokelela zezinto zakudala zabona balinganiswa abadumileyo, zihlala zinamaphepha angaphezu kwama-200, nazo ziqhelekile. Iicomics zombhali zipapashwa ngefomathi ye-BD yesiFrentshi, umzekelo nguPratt's Corto Maltese. 

Abazobi bamaTaliyane babonisa impembelelo yamabali ahlekisayo avela kwamanye amazwe, kuquka iFransi, iBelgium, iSpain, neArgentina. I-Italy nayo idume ngokuba ngomnye wabavelisi abaphambili beWalt Disney amabali ahlekisayo ngaphandle kwe-US; I-superhero alter ego kaDonald Duck, iPaperinik, eyaziwa ngesiNgesi njengeSuperduck, yenziwa eItali. 

IiKhomikhi kwamanye amazwe 
Jonga kwakhona: Uluhlu lweemidlalo ezihlekisayo ngokwelizwe 
Ukusasazwa kweshishini 
Ishishini leencwadi ezihlekisayo lisokole ngemiba yokusasaza kwimbali yalo, njengoko abathengisi abaninzi abaqhelekileyo bebethandabuza ukugcina izixa ezikhulu zezona zihlekisayo zibandakanyayo nezifunwayo. I-smartphone kunye nethebhulethi iye yajika yayindlela efanelekileyo yokusasazwa kwi-intanethi. [61] 

Ukuhanjiswa kwedijithali 
Ngomhla we-13 kuNovemba ka-2007, iMarvel Comics yaphehlelela iMarvel Digital Comics Unlimited, inkonzo yomrhumo evumela abafundi ukuba bafunde iicomics ezininzi kwimbali kaMarvel kwi-intanethi. Le nkonzo ikwabandakanya ukukhutshwa ngamaxesha amatsha amahlaya angafumanekiyo kwenye indawo. Ngokukhutshwa kwe-Aveng Spider-Man #1, uMarvel waba ngumpapashi wokuqala ukubonelela ngeekopi zedijithali zasimahla njengenxalenye yekopi eprintiweyo yencwadi ehlekisayo. [62]

Ngokukhula kokuthandwa kwee-smartphones kunye neetafile, uninzi lwabapapashi abakhulu sele beqalisile ukukhulula izihloko kwifomu yedijithali. Elona qonga lidumileyo yi-comiXology. Amanye amaqonga, anje ngeGraphicly, avaliwe. 
 
Iingqokelela ezihlekisayo kumathala eencwadi
Amathala eencwadi amaninzi aneengqokelela ezibanzi zeecomics ngendlela yeenoveli zegraphic. Oku kusebenza njengendlela efanelekileyo yokuba uluntu ngokubanzi luqhelane nomthombo.[63] 

IiRekhodi zeHlabathi zeGuinness 
Ngo-2015, igcisa lemanga laseJapan u-Eiichiro Oda wawongwa ngesihloko seeRekhodi zeHlabathi zeGuinness ngokuba "Ezona kopi zipapashiweyo kuthotho lweencwadi ezihlekisayo ezifanayo ngumbhali omnye". Ungcelele lwakhe lwe-manga ethi One Piece, alubhalayo aze alubonise, lushicilelwe kwimagazini yaseJapan i-Weekly Shōnen Jump ukusukela ngoDisemba ka-1997, kwaye ngo-2015, imiqulu engama-77 eqokelelweyo yayikhutshiwe. I-Guinness World Records yabika kwisibhengezo sabo ukuba imiqulu eqokelelweyo yochungechunge ithengise iiyunithi ezingama-320,866,000. I-One Piece ikwaphethe isihloko seeRekhodi zeHlabathi zeGuinness "Iikopi ezininzi ezipapashiweyo kuthotho lweemanga ezifanayo".[64] 

Nge-5 ka-Agasti ka-2018, isihloko seeRekhodi zeHlabathi ze-Guinness "yeyona ncwadi intle yakha yapapashwa" yanikezelwa kwi-Brazilian comic book Turma da Mônica — O Maior Gibi do Mundo!, epapashwe nguPanini Comics Brasil kunye noMauricio de Sousa Produções. Incwadi yamahlaya ilinganisa i-69.9 x 99.8 centimeters (2 iinyawo 3.5 intshi kunye ne-3 iinyawo 3.3 intshi). Incwadi ehlekisayo enamaphepha ali-18 yaprintwa iikopi ezili-120.[65] 

Ngopapasho lukaJulayi ka-2021 lomthamo wama-201 oqokelelweyo wothotho lweemanga zakhe iGolgo 13, igcisa lemanga laseJapan uTakao Saito wawongwa ngesihloko seGuinness World Records “ngobuninzi bemiqulu epapashwe ngothotho lwemanga enye.” 

Iphephandaba yimpapasho yamaxesha athile equlethe inkcazelo ebhaliweyo ngeziganeko zangoku yaye idla ngokuchwethezwa nge-inki emnyama enemvelaphi emhlophe okanye engwevu. Amaphephandaba anokugubungela iinkalo ezininzi ezahlukeneyo njengezopolitiko, ishishini, ezemidlalo, ubugcisa nenzululwazi. Zidla ngokuquka izixhobo ezifana nezimvo, uqikelelo lwemozulu, uphononongo lweenkonzo zasekuhlaleni, izidumbu, izaziso zokuzalwa, amagama anqamlezileyo, iipuzzle zesudoku, iikhathuni zokuhlela, iikhathuni, kunye neekholamu zeengcebiso. 

Uninzi lwamaphephandaba ngamashishini, kwaye ahlawula iindleko zawo ngomxube wengeniso yomrhumo, ukuthengiswa kweendaba, kunye nengeniso yentengiso. Imibutho yobuntatheli epapasha amaphephandaba ngokwayo idla ngokubizwa ngokuba ngamaphephandaba. Amaphephandaba ebesoloko epapashwa ngokushicilelwa (adla ngokufumaneka kwiphepha eliphantsi, elikwibakala elisezantsi elibizwa ngokuba yi-newsprint). Nangona kunjalo, namhlanje amaninzi amaphephandaba apapashwa kwiiwebhusayithi njengamaphephandaba e-intanethi, kwaye abanye baye bazishiya ngokupheleleyo iinguqulelo zabo zokushicilela.

Amaphephandaba aphuhliswa ngenkulungwane ye-17 njengamaphepha enkcazelo yabarhwebi. Ekuqaleni kwenkulungwane ye-19, izixeko ezininzi zaseYurophu, nakuMntla noMzantsi Merika, zapapasha amaphephandaba. Amanye amaphephandaba anenkululeko yokuhlela ephezulu, umgangatho wobuntatheli obuphezulu, nosasazo olukhulu ajongwa njengamaphephandaba arekhodiweyo. Ngokuthandwa kwe-Intanethi, amaphephandaba amaninzi ngoku adijithali, kunye neendaba zabo ezivezwa kwi-intanethi njengeyona ndlela iphambili esetyenziswa ngabafundi abaninzi, kunye noshicilelo olusesekondari (kwigcuntswana labathengi abakhetha ukuyihlawula) okanye, kwezinye iimeko, badla umhlala-phantsi. Ukwehla kwamaphephandaba ekuqaleni kwenkulungwane yama-21 ekuqaleni kwatolikwa kakhulu njengokhuphiswano nje loshicilelo-ngokuchasene nedijithali apho iibhithi zedijithali ziprintwa. Inyani iyahluka kwaye i-multivariate, njengoko amaphephandaba ngoku ahlala ekhona kwi-intanethi; nabani na ozimisele ukurhuma unokuzifunda ngokwedijithali kwi-intanethi. Izinto ezinje ngeentengiso ezihleliweyo azisenguye iziko elikhulu lengeniso (ngenxa yezinye iindlela zokuthenga kunye nokuthengisa kwi-intanethi) kunye nemibono yentengiso ngoku esasazwa kumajelo eendaba amaninzi ngamagalelo. 

Isishwankathelo 

Iphepha elingaphambili leNew York Times ngoSuku lweArmistice, 
amaphephandaba ka-1918 apapashwa mihla le okanye ngeveki. Iimagazini zeendaba nazo zeveki nganye, kodwa zinendlela yokuma yamaphephancwadi. Amaphephandaba anomdla ngokubanzi apapasha amanqaku eendaba kwaye abonise amanqaku ngeendaba zesizwe nezamazwe ngamazwe kunye neendaba zasekuhlaleni. Iindaba zibandakanya iziganeko zezopolitiko kunye nezopolitiko.", ishishini kunye nezezimali, ulwaphulo-mthetho, imozulu, kunye neentlekele zemvelo; impilo namayeza, isayensi, ikhompyutha kunye neteknoloji; ezemidlalo; kunye nokuzonwabisa, uluntu, ukutya nokupheka, iimpahla kunye nefashoni yasekhaya, kunye nobugcisa.
 
Ngokuqhelekileyo, eli phepha lahlulahlulwe langamacandelo eqela ngalinye lala maqela amakhulu (abhalwe A, B, C, njalo njalo, kunye ne-pagination ye-1B20 isimaphambili sephepha, i-1B20 iphepha, i-1B, isiqalo C1-C20, njalo njalo). Uninzi lwamaphepha emveli lukwabonisa iphepha lomhleli elibhalwe ngumhleli (okanye yibhodi yokuhlela yephepha) kunye nokuvakalisa uluvo kumcimbi woluntu, amanqaku oluvo abizwa ngokuba yi-"op-eds" abhalwe ngababhali beendwendwe (abakwicandelo elifanayo nelomhleli), kunye neekholamu ezivakalisa izimvo zobuqu zababhali bemihlathi abadla ngokuguqulela uhlalutyo lweendaba kuluhlu lwedatha oludla ngokuguqulela kuluhlu lwedatha. umfundi "into ethethwa yiyo yonke" kwaye ebacenga ukuba bavume.

Kuye kwapapashwa iindidi ngeendidi zenkcazelo kumaphephandaba. Ngaphandle kwezi ndaba zikhankanywe ngasentla, ulwazi kunye nezimvo, ziquka uqikelelo lwemozulu; ukugxekwa nophononongo lobugcisa (kubandakanywa uncwadi, ifilim, umabonakude, ithiyetha, ubugcisa obuhle, kunye nolwakhiwo) kunye neenkonzo zasekuhlaleni ezifana neendawo zokutyela; izidumbu, izaziso zokuzalwa kunye nezaziso zothweso-zidanga; iimpawu zokuzonwabisa ezifana namagama anqamlezileyo, ii-horoscopes, iikhathuni zokuhlela, iikhathuni zegag, kunye nemigca ehlekisayo; ikholamu iingcebiso, ukutya, kunye nezinye iikholamu; kunye noluhlu lukanomathotholo nomabonakude (iishedyuli zeenkqubo). Amaphephandaba aye ahlela amacandelo entengiso apho abantu kunye namashishini banokuthenga izibhengezo ezincinci zokuthengisa iimpahla okanye iinkonzo; ukusukela ngo-2013, ukonyuka kweewebhusayithi ze-Intanethi zokuthengisa iimpahla, ezifana neCraigslist kunye ne-eBay kukhokelele ekuthengisweni okungaphantsi kokuhlelwa kwamaphephandaba. [icatshulwa] 

Uninzi lwamaphephandaba ngamashishini, kwaye ahlawula iindleko zawo ngomxube wengeniso yokubhalisa, ukuthengiswa kweendaba, kunye nengeniso yentengiso (amanye amashishini okanye abantu bahlawula ukubeka iintengiso kumaphepha abo, iiklasi ezichazwe kwi-intanethi, kunye ne-equids). Amanye amaphephandaba alawulwa ngurhulumente okanye ubuncinane axhaswa ngemali ngurhulumente; ukuthembela kwabo kwingeniso yentengiso kunye nenzuzo ayibalulekanga kangako kubomi babo. Ngoko ke, ukuzimela geqe kwephephandaba kusoloko kuxhomekeke kwizinto anomdla kuzo umntu, nokuba ngabanini, ababhengezi okanye urhulumente. Amanye amaphephandaba anenkululeko yokuhlela ephezulu, umgangatho wobuntatheli obuphezulu, nosasazo olukhulu ajongwa njengamaphephandaba arekhodiweyo. 

Amaphephandaba amaninzi, ngaphandle kokuqesha abachola-choli beendaba ngemivuzo yabo, akwarhumela amaziko eendaba (iinkonzo zocingo) (njengeAssociated Press, iReuters, okanye iAgence France-Presse), eqesha iintatheli ukuba zikhangele, zidibanise, zize zinike ingxelo ngeendaba, emva koko zithengise umxholo kumaphephandaba awahlukahlukeneyo. Le yindlela yokuphepha ukuphinda-phinda iindleko zokunika ingxelo kwihlabathi jikelele. c. Ngo-2005, bekukho malunga nama-6,580 amaphephandaba emihla ngemihla ehlabathini athengisa ama-395 ezigidi zeekopi zoshicilelo ngosuku (e-US, izihloko ezili-1,450 ezithengisa iikopi ezizigidi ezingama-55).[1] Ngasekupheleni koo-2000-ekuqaleni kowama-2010 ukudodobala koqoqosho kwihlabathi, kudityaniswe nokukhula okukhawulezayo kweendlela ezizezinye zasimahla ezisekwe kwiwebhu, kuye kwanceda ukwehla kweentengiso kunye nokusasazwa, njengoko amaphepha amaninzi kuye kwafuneka adendwe imisebenzi ukuze kuncitshiswe ilahleko.[2] Ingeniso yonyaka yehlabathi jikelele isondele kwi-100 yeebhiliyoni zeedola ngo-2005-7, emva koko yahla ngexesha lobunzima bemali ka-2008. Ingeniso ngo-2016 yehla yaya kutsho kwi-53 yeebhiliyoni zeerandi kuphela, yenzakalisa wonke umshicileli omkhulu njengoko iinzame zabo zokufumana ingeniso ye-intanethi zawa phantsi kakhulu kwinjongo.[3]
 
Ukuhla kweengeniso zentengiso kuchaphazele zombini ushicilelo kunye nemidiya ye-intanethi kunye nazo zonke ezinye iindlela; intengiso yoshicilelo ibikhe yanengeniso kodwa yehle kakhulu, kwaye amaxabiso entengiso ye-intanethi ahlala esezantsi kunalawo angaphambili kushicilelo. Ngaphandle kokuhlengahlengisa intengiso, i-intanethi (ingakumbi iwebhu) iphinde yacela umngeni kwiimodeli zoshishino zexesha loshicilelo kuphela ngokuxhobisa ngokuthumela upapasho ngokubanzi (ukwabelana ngolwazi nabanye) kwaye, ngakumbi, ubuntatheli (umsebenzi wokufumana, ukudibanisa, kunye nokunika ingxelo ngeendaba). Ngaphandle koko, ukunyuka kwee-aggregators zeendaba, ezidibanisa amanqaku aqhagamshelwe kumaphephandaba amaninzi e-intanethi kunye neminye imithombo, ichaphazela ukuhamba kwe-web traffic. Ukonyuka kwe-paywalling kumaphephandaba e-intanethi kunokuba kuchasene nezo ziphumo. Elona phephandaba lidala lisapapashwa yi-Ordinari Post Tijdender, eyasekwa e-Stockholm ngo-1645. 

Iinkcazelo 
Amaphephandaba adla ngokuhlangabezana nemilinganiselo emine: [4] [5] 

Ukufikeleleka koluntu: Imixholo yayo ifikeleleka ngokufanelekileyo kuluntu, ngokwesiko ngephepha elithengiswayo okanye lihanjiswa kwiindawo zeendaba, iivenkile, kunye namathala eencwadi, kwaye, ekubeni i-intanethi ye-intanethi, yenziwe yafumaneka kwi-intanethi ye-199. Ngoxa amaphephandaba akwi-Intanethi ekwazi ukufikelela ngakumbi kumaphephandaba ngabantu abane-Intanethi, abantu abangenayo i-Intanethi okanye ikhompyutha (ngokomzekelo, abantu abangenamakhaya, abantu abahlwempuzekileyo nabantu abahlala kwiindawo ezisemaphandleni okanye ezisemaphandleni) basenokungakwazi ukungena kwi-Intanethi, baze ngaloo ndlela bangakwazi ukufunda iindaba ezikwi-Intanethi. Ukukwazi ukufunda nokubhala kukwangumba othintela abantu abangakwaziyo ukufunda ukuba bakwazi ukuxhamla ngokufunda amaphephandaba (iphepha okanye kwi-intanethi). 
Iperiodicity: Zipapashwa ngamaxesha aqhelekileyo, ngokwesiqhelo yonke imihla okanye ngeveki. Oku kuqinisekisa ukuba amaphephandaba anokubonelela ngolwazi ngamabali eendaba asandula ukuvela okanye iziganeko.
Imali: Ingcaciso yayo isexesheni njengoko ishedyuli yayo yokupapashwa ivuma. Iqondo lokuhlaziywa kwephephandaba elishicilelweyo lilinganiselwe yimfuno yexesha lokushicilela nokusasazwa kwephephandaba. Kwizixeko ezikhulu, kusenokubakho uhlelo lwakusasa nohlelo lwamva lwephepha losuku olunye, ukuze uhlelo lwamva luquke iindaba ezisasazayo eziye zenzeka ukususela ekushicilelweni kohlelo lwakusasa. Amaphephandaba akwi-Intanethi anokuhlaziywa rhoqo njengoko ulwazi olutsha lufumaneka, namaxesha aliqela ngemini, nto leyo ethetha ukuba ushicilelo lwe-intanethi lunokuhlaziywa kakhulu. 
Indalo iphela: Amaphephandaba agubungela uluhlu lwezihloko, ukusuka kwiindaba zezopolitiko nezoshishino ukuya kuhlaziyo lwenzululwazi nobuchwepheshe, ubugcisa, inkcubeko kunye nolonwabo.  IiGazethi 
zeMbali 
kunye neebhulethi
KwiRoma yaMandulo, kwaveliswa iActa Diurna, okanye izibhengezo zikarhulumente. Zazikrolwa ngentsimbi okanye ngelitye zize zixhonywe kwiindawo zikawonke-wonke. ETshayina, amaphepha eendaba awaveliswa ngurhulumente wamandulo, abizwa ngokuba yiDibao, ayesasazwa phakathi kwamagosa enkundla ebudeni bokuphela kobukhosi bukaHan (ngenkulungwane yesibini neyesithathu AD). Phakathi kwe-713 kunye ne-734, i-Kaiyuan Za Bao ("I-Bulletin yeNkundla") ye-Chinese Tang dynasty yapapasha iindaba zikarhulumente; yayibhalwe ngesandla kwisilika ize ifundwe ngamagosa karhulumente. Ngo-1582, kwabakho imbekiselo yokuqala kumaphepha eendaba apapashiweyo ngasese eBeijing, ngexesha lolawulo olungasekhoyo lweMing.[6] 

Ekuqaleni kweYurophu yanamhlanje, unxibelelwano olwandisiweyo lokuwela imida lwenza imfuno ekhulayo yolwazi eyahlangatyezwa ngamaphepha eendaba abhalwe ngesandla. Ngo-1556, urhulumente waseVenice waqala ukupapasha i-notizie scritte yenyanga, eyayibiza i-gazetta enye, ingqekembe encinane. Ezi avvisi yayiziincwadana zeendaba ezibhalwe ngesandla kwaye zazisetyenziselwa ukuhambisa iindaba zezopolitiko, ezomkhosi, kunye nezoqoqosho ngokukhawuleza nangokufanelekileyo kwizixeko zaseTaliyane (1500-1700) -ukwabelana ngeempawu ezithile zamaphephandaba nangona ngokuqhelekileyo engaqwalaselwa njengamaphephandaba okwenyaniso. Nangona kunjalo, akukho nalunye kolu papasho olufikelelayo ngokupheleleyo kwiikhrayitheriya zeklasiki zamaphephandaba afanelekileyo, njengoko ngokuqhelekileyo bezingenzelwanga uluntu ngokubanzi kwaye zithintelwe kuluhlu oluthile lwezihloko. 

Amaphephandaba 
Inqaku eliphambili: Imbali yokupapashwa kwephephandaba 
Bona kwakhona: Uluhlu lwamaphephandaba okuqala kunye nenkqubo yokuveliswa kwamaphephandaba 
eYurophu 
Jonga kwakhona: Imbali yamaphephandaba aseBritani 

Iphepha lesihloko likaJohann Carolus' Relation from 1609, the first newspaper 

Josef Danhauser's portrait's Newspaper readers, 1840
Ushicilelo lokuqala olungoomatshini nolushenxisekayo olwavumela ukuveliswa kweencwadi ezininzi olushicilelweyo lwenziwa nguJohann Gutenberg malunga nowe-1450. Kwiminyaka engama-50 emva kokuba uGutenberg eqalisile ukuprinta, kuqikelelwa ukuba kwasasazwa iincwadi ezingama-500,000, zashicilelwa koomatshini bokushicilela abamalunga ne-1 000 kwilizwekazi lonke. Ukuveliswa kukaGutenberg yayisisixhobo esilula, kodwa kwaqalisa inguqulelo ephawuleka ngokuhambela phambili ngokuphindaphindiweyo kwezobugcisa yaye, ngenxa yoko, ukusasazwa kweengcamango zenkululeko nenkululeko yokwabelana ngolwazi.[9] 
 
Ukuvela kwamajelo eendaba amatsha ngenkulungwane ye-17 kufuneka kubonwe ngokusondeleyo nokusasazwa komatshini wokushicilela apho ushicilelo lokushicilela lufumana igama lawo.[10] I-German-language Relation aller Fürnemmen und gedenckwürdigen Historien, yashicilelwa ukusuka ngo-1605 ukuya phambili ngu-Johann Carolus eStrasbourg kuBukhosi obuNgcwele baseRoma beSizwe saseJamani, idla ngokuvunywa njengephephandaba lokuqala.[11][12] Iphephandaba lesibini, i<em>German Avisa, lapapashwa ukususela ngowe-1609 eWolfenbüttel. Omabini amaphephandaba azahlula kwezinye izinto ezishicilelweyo ngokupapashwa rhoqo. Banike ingxelo ngeziganeko zangoku ezahlukeneyo kubaphulaphuli abaninzi. Kwiminyaka nje embalwa, amaphephandaba ayenokufumaneka kuzo zonke izixeko ezikhulu zaseYurophu, ukususela eVenice ukusa eLondon.

I-Dutch Courante uyt Italien, Duytslandt, & c. ("iCourant evela eItali, eJamani, njl.njl.") ka-1618 yaba yeyokuqala ukuvela kwiphepha- endaweni ye-quarto-size. IAmsterdam, iziko lorhwebo lwehlabathi, ngokukhawuleza yaba likhaya lamaphephandaba ngeelwimi ezininzi, ngokufuthi ngaphambi kokuba apapashwe kwilizwe lawo.[13] Iphephandaba lokuqala lesiNgesi, iCorrant out of Italy, Germany, etc., lapapashwa eAmsterdam ngowe-1620. Kwangaloo nyaka, iphephancwadi laseAntwerp elithi Nieuwe Tijdinghen[14] lapapashwa nguAbraham Verhoeven.[15] Ngo-1621, iCorante, okanye iindaba zeveki ngeeveki ezivela eItali, eJamani, eHungary, ePoland, eBohemia, eFransi naseMazantsi Countreys zapapashwa eNgilani yi-"NB" (ngokuqhelekileyo ekucingelwa ukuba nguNathaniel Butter okanye uNicholas Bourne) noThomas Archer.[16] Iphephandaba lokuqala eFransi lapapashwa ngo-1631, iLa Gazette (eyapapashwa ekuqaleni njengeGazette de France).[7] Iphephandaba lokuqala eItali, ngokungqinelana neyona nkupho indala isagciniweyo, yayiyiDi Genova eyapapashwa ngowe-1639 eGenoa.[17] Iphephandaba lokuqala ePortugal, A Gazeta da Restauração, lapapashwa ngo-1641 eLisbon.[18] Iphephandaba lokuqala leSpanish, iGaceta de Madrid, lapapashwa ngo-1661. 

I-Post- och Inrikes Tidningar (eyasekwa njenge-Ordinari Post Tijdender) yapapashwa okokuqala eSweden ngo-1645, kwaye lelona phephandaba lidala elisakhoyo, nangona ngoku lipapasha kuphela kwi-intanethi.[19] I-Opregte Haarlemsche Courant yaseHaarlem, eyapapashwa okokuqala ngo-1656, lelona phepha lidala lisaprintwayo. Kwanyanzeleka ukuba idityaniswe nephephandaba iHaarlems Dagblad ngowe-1942 xa iJamani yayithimba iNetherlands. Ukusukela ngoko i-Haarlems Dagblad ibonakala inesihlokwana esithi Oprechte Haerlemse Courant 1656. 

Americas 
Bona kwakhona: Imbali yamaphephandaba aseMelika 

Umzobo othandwayo wevenkile kaMarguerite Martyn eSt.
EBoston ngo-1690, uBenjamin Harris wapapasha i-Publick Occurrences Zombini eziNgaphandle kunye nezasekhaya. Eli ligqalwa njengephephandaba lokuqala kumathanga aseMerika nangona kwapapashwa uhlelo olunye ngaphambi kokuba iphepha licinezelwe ngurhulumente. Ngo-1704, irhuluneli yavumela ukuba i-Boston News-Letter ipapashwe kwaye yaba liphephandaba lokuqala elipapashwa ngokuqhubekayo kwiikoloni. Kungekudala emva koko, amaphepha eveki aqala ukupapashwa eNew York nasePhiladelphia. La maphephandaba amandulo ayelandela ifomathi yaseBritani kwaye ayedla ngokuba namaphepha amane ubude. Ubukhulu becala babephethe iindaba ezivela eBritani kwaye umxholo wawuxhomekeke kwizinto anomdla kuzo umhleli. Ngo-1783, i-Pennsylvania Evening Post yaba yi-American yokuqala yonke imihla. [21] 
Amanqaku aphambili: Shicilela imidiya eIndiya, amaphephandaba aseJapan, kunye neMbali yamaphephandaba aseTshayina

Ngo-1752, uJohn Bushell wapapasha iHalifax Gazette, ethi "liphephandaba lokuqala laseCanada". Noko ke, inzala yayo esemthethweni, iRoyal Gazette, yimpapasho karhulumente yezaziso ezisemthethweni nezibhengezo kunokuba ibe liphephandaba elifanelekileyo; Ngo-1764, iQuebec Gazette yaqala ukushicilelwa ngomhla wama-21 kuJuni ka-1764 kwaye iselelona phephandaba lidala elisapapashwa ngokuqhubekayo eMntla Melika njengeQuebec Chronicle-Telegraph. Ngoku ipapashwa njengolwimi lwesiNgesi qho ngeveki kwii-ofisi zayo e-1040 Belvédère, suite 218, Quebec City, Quebec, Canada. Ngo-1808, iGazeta do Rio de Janeiro [22] yaba nohlelo lwayo lokuqala, yashicilelwa ngezixhobo ezisuka eNgilani, ipapasha iindaba ezilungileyo kurhulumente waseUnited Kingdom yasePortugal, eBrazil naseAlgarves ukusukela oko yaveliswa yinkonzo yoshicilelo esemthethweni yesithsaba sesiPhuthukezi. 

Ngowe-1821, emva kokuphela kokuvalwa kokusasazwa kwephephandaba labucala, kubonakala ushicilelo lokuqala olungelulo lobukhosi olushicilelweyo, iDiário do Rio de Janeiro, nangona sele ikhona iCorreio Braziliense, epapashwe nguHipólito José da Costa ngaxeshanye neGazeta, kodwa isuka eLondon kwaye ithethe ngamandla ukubhengeza iintsilelo zezopolitiko kunye neembono ezigxekayo. Iphephandaba lokuqala ePeru laliyi-El Peruano, eyasekwa ngo-Oktobha 1825 kwaye isapapashwa nanamhlanje, kodwa ngokutshintsha kwamagama amaninzi. 

E-Asiya 
Ngexesha lolawulo lweTang eChina (618-906), iKaiyuan Za Bao yapapasha iindaba zikarhulumente; yayishicilelwe ephepheni. Maxa wambi ligqalwa njengelinye lawona maphephandaba okuqala ukupapashwa. Ilinge lokuqala elirekhodiweyo lokufumana iphephandaba eliluhlobo lwanamhlanje eMzantsi Asia yaba nguWilliam Bolts, umDatshi owayeqeshwe yiBritish East India Company ngoSeptemba 1768 eCalcutta. Noko ke, ngaphambi kokuba aqalise iphephandaba lakhe, wagxothwa wabuyela eYurophu. Ngowe-1780 ushicilelo lweendaba lokuqala kulo mmandla, i<em>Bengal Gazette kaHicky, yapapashwa yindoda yaseIreland, uJames Augustus Hicky. Wayisebenzisa njengendlela yokugxeka ulawulo lwaseBritane ngobuntatheli. [23] IJobo, ekwaxutyushwa ngayo kwi-Annals of the Joseon Dynasty, yapapashwa ngowe-1577 ngabaphathiswa bakaKumkani uSeonjo. Ekubeni uKumkani wayengazange ayinike imvume yokushicilela iindaba, uJobo wayekwa, baza abalungiseleli abangama-30 bagwetyelwa “isohlwayo esiqatha”. Yayishicilelwa yonke imihla, yaye igubungela imixholo emininzi, kuquka imozulu, amakroza, nemicimbi yakutshanje. Ngo-2017, imonki yaseKorea yabanga ukuba ifumene ikopi ekhoyo kaJobo.[24][25] Inqaku elikuMbindi 

Mpuma 
: Imbali yamaphephandaba akuMbindi Mpuma 
Imbali yamaphephandaba akuMbindi Mpuma ibuyela emva kwinkulungwane ye-19. Abahleli abaninzi babengezontatheli kuphela kodwa nababhali, iintanda-bulumko kunye nabezopolitiko. Ngamajenali angekho semthethweni, ezi ngqondi zazikhuthaza iintetho zikawonke-wonke ngezopolitiko kuBukhosi baseOttoman nasePersi.Iincwadi zoncwadi zazo zonke iindidi zahlelwa kwaye zapapashwa nakumaphepha-ndaba.
 
Amaphephandaba okuqala kwi-Ottoman Empire ayengawabantu basemzini ababehlala apho ababefuna ukwenza ipropaganda malunga nehlabathi laseNtshona.[26] Eyokuqala yashicilelwa ngowe-1795 yiPalais de France ePera. Ubuntatheli boMthonyama kuMbindi Mpuma baqala ngo-1828, xa uMuhammad Ali, uKhedive waseYiputa, wayalela ukuba kusekwe igazethi iVekâyi-i Mısriyye (iMicimbi yaseYiputa).[27] Yayiliphepha lokuqala elibhalwe ngesi-Ottoman Turkish kunye nesiArabhu kumaphepha achaseneyo, kwaye kamva ngesiArabhu kuphela, phantsi kwesihloko esithi "Al-Waqāʾiʿ al-Miṣriyya".[28] 

Iphephandaba lokuqala laseTurkey elingekho ngokusemthethweni, iCeride-i Havadis (iRegister of Events), yapapashwa yiNgesi, uWilliam Churchill, ngo-1840. Iphephandaba lokuqala labucala elipapashwe yintatheli yaseTurkey, uTercüman-ı Ahvâl (Utoliki weZiganeko), yasekwa ngu-İbrahim Şinasi kunye ne-Agah 986 kunye ne-Agah 98]. Iphephandaba lokuqala e-Iran, Kaghaz-e Akhbar (Iphephandaba), wadalelwa urhulumente Mirza Saleh Shirazi ngo 1837 [30]. Iijenali zokuqala kwi-Peninsula yase-Arabia zavela e-Hijaz, xa sele izimele kulawulo lwe-Ottoman, ngasekupheleni kweMfazwe Yehlabathi I. Omnye wabasetyhini bokuqala ukuba basayine amanqaku akhe kumaphephandaba ama-Arabhu ngugqirha obhinqileyo uGalila Tamarhan, owanikela amanqaku kwiphephancwadi lezonyango elibizwa ngokuba yi "Ya'asub al-Tib" (iNkokeli ye-318 kwi-Medicine). 

I-Industrial Revolution 

Iphepha elingaphambili le-Helsingin Sanomat (i-Helsinki Times) nge-7 kaJulayi, ngo-1904.
Ekuqaleni kwenkulungwane ye-19, izixeko ezininzi zaseYurophu, nakuMntla noMzantsi Merika, zapapasha iimpapasho eziluhlobo lwamaphephandaba nangona zingaphuhliswanga ngendlela efanayo zonke; umxholo wayilwa kakhulu kukhetho lwengingqi kunye nenkcubeko.[32] Inkqubela kubugcisa bokushicilela obunxulumene neNguquko YezoShishino yenza ukuba amaphephandaba abe yindlela yonxibelelwano esasazwe ngokubanzi ngakumbi, njengoko ubugcisa obutsha bokushicilela benza ukuba ukushicilela kungabizi mali ininzi yaye kusebenze ngakumbi. Ngowe-1814, iThe Times (eLondon) yafumana umatshini wokushicilela owawukwazi ukwenza izinto ezili-1 100 ngeyure.[33] Kungekudala, lo matshini wokushicilela walungiselelwa ukuba uprinte macala omabini ephepha ngaxeshanye. Olu tshintsho lwenze ukuba amaphephandaba angabizi mali yaneleyo yaye ngaloo ndlela afumaneka kubantu abaninzi ngakumbi. 

Ngo-1830, iphephandaba lokuqala elingabizi kakhulu "lokushicilela ngepeni" lafika emarikeni: i-Boston Transcript kaLynde M. Walter. [34] Amaphepha okushicilela kaPenny axabisa malunga nesinye kwisithandathu sexabiso lamanye amaphephandaba yaye abhenela kubaphulaphuli abaninzi, kuquka abantu abangafundanga kangako nabanomvuzo ophantsi.[35] EFransi, u-Émile de Girardin waqala iLa Presse ngo-1836, esazisa ngexabiso eliphantsi, elixhaswa yintengiso yemihla ngemihla eFransi. Ngo-1848, uAugust Zang, waseOstriya owayesazi uGirardin eParis, wabuyela eVienna ukwazisa iindlela ezifanayo kunye neDie Presse (eyathiywa kwaye yakhutshelwa ngokungafihlisiyo upapasho lukaGirardin).[36] 

Iindidi 
Nangona uninzi lwamaphephandaba lujolise kuluhlu olubanzi lwabafundi, ngokuqhelekileyo luchazwa ngokwejografi, abanye bagxininise kumaqela abafundi abachazwe ngakumbi ngomdla wabo kunendawo abakuyo: umzekelo, kukho amaphephandaba amashishini emihla ngemihla kunye neveki (umz., I-Wall Street Journal kunye ne-India Today) kunye namaphephandaba ezemidlalo. Iingcali ezingakumbi zisengamaphepha-ndaba eveki nganye, adla ngokusimahla kwaye asasazwe kwiindawo ezithile zengingqi; ezi zinokusebenza uluntu njengento ethile njengabantu abathile abavela kwamanye amazwe, uluntu lwasekuhlaleni lwama-gay okanye abathanda i-indie rock ngaphakathi kwesixeko okanye ummandla. 

I-Frequency 
Daily 
"Iphepha lemihla ngemihla" liqondisa kwakhona apha. Ngophawu, jonga iDaily Paper (impahla). 
"Uhlelo lwangeCawa" luqondisa kwakhona apha. Ngolunye usetyenziso, jonga uHlelo lwangeCawe (disambiguation). 
Iphephandaba lemihla ngemihla lishicilelwa yonke imihla, ngamanye amaxesha ngaphandle kweeCawe kwaye ngamanye amaxesha ngeMigqibelo (kunye neeholide ezinkulu). NgoMgqibelo kwaye, apho akhoyo, ushicilelo lwangeCawa lwamaphephandaba emihla ngemihla ludla ngokuba makhulu, lubandakanya amacandelo awodwa ngakumbi (umz., kubugcisa, imiboniso bhanyabhanya, ukonwabisa) kunye nokufakwa kweentengiso, kunye neendleko ezingaphezulu. Ngokuqhelekileyo, uninzi lwabasebenzi bala maphephandaba basebenza ngoMvulo ukusa ngoLwesihlanu, ngoko uhlelo lwangeCawa nolweMivulo ubukhulu becala luxhomekeke kumxholo owenziwe kwangaphambili okanye umxholo othunyelweyo.
 
Uninzi lwamaphephandaba emihla ngemihla athengiswa kusasa. Amaphepha asemva kwemini okanye ngorhatya, awayefudula exhaphakile kodwa ngoku enqabile, ajolise ngakumbi kubakhweli nakubasebenzi baseofisini. Uqheliselo (nangona oku kunokwahluka ngokwelizwe), iphephandaba lakusasa liyafumaneka kwiintlelo zakusasa ukususela ngaphambi kwasezinzulwini zobusuku kubusuku obungaphambi komhla walo ongaphandle, iinkupho ezingakumbi ziyashicilelwa zize zisasazwe ebusuku. Ushicilelo lwamva lunokubandakanya iindaba eziphambili ezathi zatyhilwa kuqala ngaloo mini, emva kokuba uhlelo lwakusasa lwalusele lushicilelwe. Uphononongo lwamaphephandaba angomso ludla ngokuba yinxalenye yeendaba zasebusuku, njengeNewsnight yaseUnited Kingdom. Ngo-1650, iphephandaba lokuqala lemihla ngemihla, i-Einkommende Zeitung, [37] elapapashwa ngu-Timotheus Ritzsch eLeipzig, eJamani. 

EUnited Kingdom nakwamanye amazwe amanyeneyo, ngokungafaniyo namanye amazwe amaninzi, amaphephandaba emihla ngemihla awapapashwa ngeeCawa. Ngaphambili bekukho amaphephandaba azimeleyo eCawa; kule mihla kwaloo mvakalisi mnye ngokufuthi uvelisa iphephandaba langeCawa, elahlukileyo ngeendlela ezininzi kusuku lwemihla ngemihla, ngokuqhelekileyo elinegama elihlobene nalo; umz., iThe Times kunye neThe Sunday Times ngamaphephandaba awohlukileyo aphethwe yinkampani enye, kwaye inqaku elipapashwe kwelamva alinakuze lifakwe kwiThe Times.

Kwezinye iimeko uhlelo lwangeCawa yinguqulelo eyandisiweyo yephephandaba evela kumpapashi omnye; kwezinye iimeko, ngakumbi eBritani, isenokuba lishishini elahlukileyo, umz., I-Observer, enganxulumananga nephephandaba lemihla ngemihla ukususela ekusekweni kwayo ngo-1791 de yafunyanwa yiThe Guardian ngo-1993. (ezifana neThe New York Times Magazine kunye neThe Sunday Times Magazine). 

Kwamanye amazwe amaphephandaba emihla ngemihla akapapashwa ngoSuku lweKrisimesi, kodwa amaphephandaba eveki nganye angalutshintsha usuku lwawo umz. amaphephandaba angeCawa apapashwa ngoMgqibelo we-24 kaDisemba, uBubusuku bangaphambi kweKrisimesi xa uSuku lweKrisimesi luba ngeCawa. 

Isiqingatha seveki 
Amanye amaphephandaba apapashwa kabini ngeveki kwaye aziwa njengopapasho oluphakathi kweveki. 

Nge-Triweekly 
Njengoko igama libonisa, i-triweekly ipapasha kathathu ngeveki. I-Meridian Star ingumzekelo wempapasho enjalo.[39] 
Inqaku eliphambili 

leVeki : Iphephandaba leVeki 
Amaphephandaba aphuma kanye ngeveki, kwaye athande ukuba mancinci kunamaphepha emihla ngemihla. 
Kabini ngeveki 
Ezinye iimpapasho zipapashwa, umzekelo, emva kweveki ezimbini (okanye kabini ngeveki ngolwimi lwaseMelika). Basenokuba notshintsho ukusuka kusuku oluqhelekileyo lweveki yeveki ngexesha leKrisimesi kuxhomekeke kumhla weveki uSuku lweKrisimesi luwela. 
Umda wejografi kunye nokuhanjiswa 
Kwengingqi okanye kwingingqi 
Eli candelo alichazi nayiphi na imithombo. Nceda uncede ukuphucula eli candelo ngokongeza izicatshulwa kwimithombo ethembekileyo. Izixhobo ezingasetyenziswanga zinokucelwa umngeni kwaye zisuswe. (Disemba 2018) (Funda indlela kwaye nini ukususa lo myalezo) 
Iphephandaba lasekuhlaleni likhonza ummandla onjengesixeko, okanye inxalenye yesixeko esikhulu. Phantse yonke imarike inephephandaba elinye okanye amabini alawula le ndawo. Amaphephandaba amakhulu eMetropolitan ahlala enothungelwano olukhulu losasazo, kwaye anokufumaneka ngaphandle kwendawo yawo eqhelekileyo, ngamanye amaxesha ngokubanzi, ngamanye amaxesha kwimithombo embalwa. 
Kuzwelonke 
Bona kwakhona: Uluhlu lwamaphephandaba esizwe 
Amaphephandaba ezizwe ngezizwe athengiswayo eParis 
Uninzi lwamazwe lunephephandaba elinye elijikeleza kwilizwe lonke: iphephandaba lesizwe. Amanye amaphephandaba esizwe, anjengeFinancial Times neThe Wall Street Journal, akhethekileyo (kule mizekelo, kwimibandela yemali). Maninzi amaphephandaba esizwe eUnited Kingdom, kodwa ambalwa eUnited States naseKhanada. ECanada, iGlobe kunye neMayile zithengiswa kulo lonke ilizwe. EUnited States, ukongezelela kumaphephandaba esizwe anjalo, iThe New York Times ifumaneka kulo lonke elo lizwe.[40]






Kukwakho neqaqobana lamaphephandaba anokuchazwa njengamaphephandaba ezizwe ngezizwe. Amanye, afana neThe New York Times International Edition, (eyayisakuba yi-International Herald Tribune) ibisoloko inaloo ngqwalasela, ngelixa amanye epakishwa kwakhona ngamaphephandaba esizwe okanye “uhlelo lwamazwe ngamazwe” lwamaphephandaba esizwe okanye amakhulu esixeko. Kwezinye iimeko, amanqaku anokuthi angabinamdla kuluhlu olubanzi lwabafundi akafakwanga kwiintlelo zamazwe ngamazwe; kwezinye, ezibangela umdla kubaphambukeli, iindaba ezibalulekileyo zelizwe ziyagcinwa. Njengoko isiNgesi saba lulwimi lwehlabathi loshishino nobuchwepheshe, amaphephandaba amaninzi ebepapashwa kuphela ngeelwimi ezingezizo ezesiNgesi nawo aphuhlise amahlelo olwimi lwesiNgesi. Kwiindawo ezahlukahlukeneyo njengeJerusalem neMumbai, amaphephandaba aprintelwa abantu basekhaya nabantetho isisiNgesi, kunye nabakhenkethi. Ukufika kwe-Intanethi kuye kwavumela amaphepha-ndaba angengawo awesiNgesi ukuba akhuphe inguqulelo yesiNgesi ethotyiweyo ukunika iphephandaba labo ukufikelela kwihlabathi jikelele. 

Ngokufanayo, kumazwe amaninzi anabemi abaninzi abathetha ulwimi lwasemzini okanye abakhenkethi abaninzi, amaphephandaba ngeelwimi ezingezizo ezolwimi lwesizwe apapashwa ekuhlaleni aze angeniswe kwamanye amazwe. Ngokomzekelo, amaphephandaba namaphephancwadi aphuma kumazwe amaninzi, namaphephandaba apapashwa ekuhlaleni ngeelwimi ezininzi, sele ekulungele ukufumaneka kwiindawo zokuthengisa iindaba kumbindi weLondon. Kwilizwe laseMelika laseFlorida, abakhenkethi abaninzi abavela kwiphondo laseKhanada elithetha isiFrentshi eQuebec batyelela ukuhlala ixesha elide ebusika ("iintaka zeqhwa") ukuba ezinye iindawo zeendaba kunye neevenkile zithengisa amaphephandaba aseFrentshi afana neLe Droit. 

Umba wesifundo 
Amaphephandaba ngokubanzi agubungela zonke izihloko, ngogxininiso olwahlukileyo. Ngelixa ubuncinci bekhankanya zonke izihloko, ezinye zinokuba nogutyulo oluhle lweziganeko zamazwe ngamazwe ezibalulekileyo; abanye basenokunikel’ ingqalelo ngakumbi kulonwabo lwelizwe okanye lwasekuhlaleni okanye kwezemidlalo. Amaphephandaba awodwa asenokunikela ingqalelo ngakumbi, ngokomzekelo, kwimibandela yemali. Kukho iimpapasho ezithetha ngezemidlalo kuphela, okanye imidlalo ethile, umdyarho wamahashe, iqonga 

lemidlalo yeqonga, njalo njalo, nangona zingasenakuze zibizwe ngokuba 
ngamaphephandaba 

. 
.
Kangangeenkulungwane amaphephandaba ayeshicilelwa ephepheni aze abonelelwe ngokwasemzimbeni kubafundi nokuba kukusasazwa kwasekuhlaleni okanye kwezinye iimeko ngeposi, umzekelo kubaphambukeli baseBritani abahlala eIndiya okanye eHong Kong ababhalisele amaphephandaba aseBritani. Amaphephandaba anokuhanjiswa kumakhaya ababhalisi kunye/okanye amashishini ngabantu abahambisa iphepha ngokwalo, athunyelwe ngeposi, athengiswa kwiindawo zeendaba, kwiivenkile ezithengisa ukutya, nakwiivenkile ezithengisa ukutya, kwaye asiwe kumathala eencwadi nakwiivenkile ezithengisa iincwadi. Imibutho yamaphephandaba idinga inkqubo enkulu yokuhambisa ukuhambisa amaphepha abo kwaba basasazi bahlukeneyo, nto leyo ebandakanya iilori zokuhambisa kunye nabantu bokuhambisa. Kwiminyaka yakutshanje, amaphephandaba kunye namanye amajelo eendaba aziqhelanise nemeko yetekhnoloji eguqukayo ngokuqalisa ukubonelela ngohlelo lwe-intanethi ukukhawulelana neemfuno zoluntu. Kwixesha elizayo, umkhwa wokuhanjiswa kweendaba nge-elektroniki uya kuqhubeka nokugxininiswa ngakumbi kwi-Intanethi, kwimidiya yoluntu kunye nezinye iindlela zokuhanjiswa kwe-elektroniki. Nangona kunjalo, ngelixa indlela yokuhanjiswa iguquka, iphephandaba kunye neshishini lisekhona niche kwihlabathi. Inqaku eliPhambili 

kwi-Intanethi 
: Iphephandaba elikwi-Intanethi 
Ukusukela ngo-2007, phantse onke amaphephandaba ashicilelweyo avelisa ushicilelo lwe-intanethi olusasazwa kwi-Intanethi, oluthi, ngokuxhomekeke kwilizwe, lulawulwe yimibutho yobuntatheli efana neKomishoni yeZikhalazo ze-Press e-UK.[41] Kodwa njengoko abanye abapapashi befumanisa ukuba iimodeli zabo ezisekwe kushicilelo zikhula ngokungazinzanga, [42] "amaphephandaba" asekwe kwiWebhu nawo sele eqalile ukuvela, njengeSouthport Reporter e-UK kunye neSeattle Post-Intelligencer, eyayeka ukupapasha ekushicileleni emva kweminyaka eyi-149 ngoMatshi ka-2009 kwaye yaba liphepha le-intanethi kuphela. 

Ukusukela ngo-2005 e-UK ngaphezulu kwamaphephandaba engingqi angama-200 avaliwe nto leyo ebangele ukwehla kwenani leentatheli zengingqi ngama-50%. Uphononongo luka-2016 olwenziwa yiKing's College, eLondon, lwafumanisa ukuba iidolophu eziphulukene namaphephandaba asekuhlaleni ziye zarhoxa kwizithethe zedemokhrasi zaza zaphulukana nokholo loluntu kwabasemagunyeni.[43] 

Indlela entsha yokupapasha amaphephandaba kukuqaliswa kokwenziwa komntu ngeteknoloji yoshicilelo olufunekayo okanye iiwebhusayithi ezidibanisa iindaba ezikwi-intanethi njengeendaba zikaGoogle. Amaphephandaba enzelwe wena avumela umfundi ukuba enze iphephandaba lakhe ngokukhetha amaphepha aphuma kupapasho oluninzi. Le "Igqwesileyo" yendlela ivumela ukuvuselelwa kwemodeli esekwe kushicilelo kwaye ivule umjelo omtsha wokusasaza ukwandisa ukuhanjiswa ngaphantsi kwemida eqhelekileyo yokusasazwa. Amaphephandaba enziwe ngokwezifiso kwi-intanethi anikezelwe nguMyYahoo, I-Google, CRAYON, ICurrent.com, Kibboko.com, Twitter. amaxesha kunye nabanye abaninzi. Ngala maphephandaba akwi-intanethi, umfundi unokuzikhethela ukuba lingakanani na kwicandelo ngalinye (lezopolitiko, ezemidlalo, ezobugcisa, njl.njl.) anqwenela ukulibona kwiindaba zabo. 

Umbutho kunye nabasebenzi 

Indlu yoshicilelo yeTelegraph eMacon, eGeorgia, c. 1876

Inkwenkwe yeendaba ethengisa iToronto Telegram eCanada ngo-1905 

Igumbi leendaba laseGazeta Lubuska eZielona Góra, ePoland 

Isakhiwo seofisi saseTyrvään Sanomat eSastamala, eFinland 
Ubusuku kwindlu yeendaba eDaily Nebraskan 
E-US, umphathi jikelele okanye umlawuli oyintloko wephephandaba ngumpapashi. [44] Kumaphepha-ndaba amancinane, umnini woshicilelo (okanye oyena mnini sabelo mkhulu kwiqumrhu elingumnini wempapasho) udla ngokuba ngumpapashi [ukucaphula] Uninzi lwamaphephandaba anamasebe amane aphambili azinikele ekupapasheni iphephandaba ngokwalo—elokuhlela, elokuvelisa/lokushicilela, ukujikeleziswa, kunye nentengiso, nangona esoloko ebhekiswa kuwo ngamanye amagama ahlukeneyo. Uninzi lwamaphepha lukwanamasebe angengawo amaphepha-ndaba afumaneka kwamanye amashishini anobungakanani obuthelekisekayo, njenge-accounting, ukuthengisa, izibonelelo zabasebenzi, kunye ne-IT. 

Kulo lonke ihlabathi elintetho isisiNgesi, umntu okhetha umxholo wephephandaba udla ngokubizwa ngokuba ngumhleli. Ukwahluka kwesi sihloko njengomhleli oyintloko, umhleli olawulayo, njalo njalo zixhaphakile. Kumaphepha-ndaba amancinci, umhleli omnye unokuba noxanduva kuzo zonke iinkalo zomxholo. Kumaphepha-ndaba amakhulu, oyena mhleli ukwinqanaba eliphezulu nguye ophethe upapasho, ngelixa abahleli abancinci abancinci banokugxila kwindawo enye, njengeendaba zasekhaya okanye imidlalo. La macandelo abizwa ngokuba zii-ofisi zeendaba okanye "iidesika", kwaye ngalinye lijongwa ngumhleli ochongiweyo. Uninzi lwabahleli bamaphephandaba bakhuphela amabali amabali abo kwicandelo labo lephephandaba, kodwa banokwabelana ngomsebenzi wabo nabahloli bamaxwebhu kunye nabahloli benyaniso. 

Iintatheli ziintatheli ezichaza izibakala eziye zaqokelela, kwaye abo babhala amanqaku amade, amanqaku angenamdla kangako kunokuthiwa ngababhali abaphambili. Abafoti kunye namagcisa egraphic abonelela ngemifanekiso kunye nemifanekiso ukuxhasa amanqaku. Abacholacholi beendaba badla ngokusebenza ngokukhethekileyo kumbandela othile, obizwa ngokuba sisingqisho, njengezemidlalo, unqulo okanye inzululwazi. Ababhali bemihla ngemihla ziintatheli ezibhala amanqaku rhoqo zibalisa ngezimvo zabo namava abo. Abashicileli kunye nabasebenzi bokushicilela baliprinta ngokwasemzimbeni iphephandaba. Ushicilelo lukhutshwa ngamaphephandaba amaninzi, ngokuyinxenye ngenxa yeendleko zomatshini wokushicilela we-offset (olona hlobo loshicilelo luxhaphakileyo olusetyenziselwa ukushicilela amaphephandaba), nangenxa yokuba ushicilelo lwephephandaba elincinane lusenokufuna ukusebenza okungaphantsi kweyure, nto leyo ethetha ukuba ukuba iphephandaba linoshicilelo lwalo beliya kuhlala lingasebenzi ixesha elininzi. Ukuba iphephandaba libonelela ngolwazi kwi-intanethi, abaphathi bewebhu kunye nabayili bewebhu banokuqeshwa ukuba bafake amabali kwiwebhusayithi yephephandaba.

Abasebenzi besebe lokusasaza banxibelelana nabathengisi abathengisa iphephandaba; thengisa imirhumo; kunye nokongamela ukuhanjiswa kwamaphephandaba ashicilelweyo ngeposi, ngabathuthi bamaphephandaba, kubathengisi nangoomatshini bokuthengisa. Amaphephandaba asimahla awawathengisi imirhumo, kodwa asenesebe lokusasaza elinoxanduva lokusasaza amaphephandaba. Abasebenzi bezentengiso kwisebe leentengiso abathengisi kuphela indawo yentengiso kubathengi abafana namashishini asekuhlaleni, kodwa bancedisa abathengi ukuyila nokucwangcisa amaphulo abo entengiso. Amanye amalungu esebe leentengiso anokubandakanya abayili begraphic, abayila iintengiso ngokweenkcukacha zabathengi kunye nemigaqo-nkqubo yesebe. Kwiphephandaba elingenazibhengezo, akukho candelo lezentengiso. 

Izowuni nezinye iinkupho 

Iphephandaba lakwaSirayeli lemihla ngemihla i-Haaretz kuhlelo lwalo lwesiHebhere nesiNgesi 
Amaphephandaba ahlala ecokisa ukusasazwa kweentengiso kunye neendaba ngokucandwa komhlaba nangohlelo. Ukucandwa komhlaba kwenzeka xa intengiso kunye nesiqulatho sokuhlela sitshintsha ukubonisa indawo apho imveliso isiwa khona. Umxholo wokuhlela unokutshintsha nje ukubonisa utshintsho kwintengiso-ubuninzi kunye noyilo oluchaphazela indawo ekhoyo yokuhlela-okanye inokuqulatha iindaba ezingqamene nommandla. Kwiimeko ezinqabileyo, intengiso isenokungatshintshi ukusuka kwenye indawo ukuya kwenye, kodwa kuya kubakho umxholo wokuhlela owahlukileyo wommandla othile. Njengoko umxholo unokwahluka ngokubanzi, amahlelo azowuniweyo ahlala eveliswa ngokuhambelanayo. Ukuhlelwa kwenzeka kumacandelo aphambili njengoko iindaba zihlaziywa ubusuku bonke. Intengiso ikholisa ukuba yinto enye kuhlelo ngalunye (ngaphandle kwemimandla ecandiweyo, apho kudla ngokuba licandelo 'B' leendaba zasekuhlaleni ezithi lenze utshintsho kwintengiso). Njengoko uhlelo ngalunye lumele iindaba zamva nje ezifumanekayo kushicilelo olulandelayo, olu hlelo luveliswa ngokomgca, ngohlelo olunye olugqityiweyo lukhutshelwa luze luhlaziywe kuhlelo olulandelayo. Uhlelo lwangaphambili luhlala lukhutshelwa ukugcina iPhepha leNdaba leRekhodi kunye nokubuyela emva ukuba ulungiso olukhawulezayo luyafuneka kumaphephandaba. Umzekelo, zombini iThe New York Times kunye neWall Street Journal zibonelela ngoshicilelo lwengingqi, oluprintwe ngonokontraka wasekhaya, kwaye iqulethe umxholo othile wendawo. Ikhadi leNtengiso leJenali linika umzekelo omhle wohlelo.[45] 

Bona kwakhona Los Angeles Times amacandelo suburban. 
IFomathi 

Yomiuri Shimbun, i-broadsheet eJapan inikwe imbeko yokuba nephepha-ndaba elikhulu elisasazwayo kwihlabathi 
Uninzi lwamaphephandaba anamhlanje[46] akwelinye lobukhulu obuthathu:
 
I-Broadsheets: 600 mm × 380 mm (23+1⁄2 in × 15 in), ngokubanzi enxulunyaniswa namaphephandaba akrelekrele ngakumbi, nangona amaphephandaba atshintshayo. Imizekelo ibandakanya iDaily Telegraph yaseUnited Kingdom.
I-Tabloids: isiqingatha sobukhulu be-broadsheets kwi-380 mm × 300 mm (15 in × 11+3⁄4 in), kwaye kaninzi ibonwa njenge-sensationalist ngokungafaniyo ne-broadsheets.[cating] Imizekelo ibandakanya i-Sun, i-National Enquirer, i-Star Magazine, i-New York Post, i-Chicago Sun-Times, kunye ne-The G. 
"I-Microdaily" ayifane isetyenziswe ukubhekisela kwiphephandaba lemihla ngemihla le-tabloid lasimahla elinikezela ngamaxabiso aphantsi entengiso kunalawo akhuphisana nawo nge-broadsheet 
. in) esetyenziswa ngamaphepha aseYurophu afana neLe Monde eFransi, iLa Stampa eItali, i-El País eSpain kwaye, ukusuka kwi-2005 ukuya kwi-2018, i-Guardian e-United Kingdom. 
I-Brazilian Vossa Senhoria ithi lelona phephandaba lincinane ehlabathini, elinomlinganiselo we-1.4 in. x 1 in (3.5 cm x 2.5 cm). 

Amaphephandaba adla ngokuprintwa kwiphepha eliphantsi, elingekho mhlophe elaziwa ngokuba yi-newsprint. Ukusukela ngeminyaka yee-1980s, ishishini lamaphephandaba liye lasuka ubukhulu becala kushicilelo olukumgangatho ophantsi we letterpress ukuya kudidi oluphezulu, inkqubo yemibala emine, ushicilelo lweoffset. Ukongeza, iikhompyuter zedesktop, isoftwe yokuseta amagama, isoftware yemizobo, iikhamera zedijithali kunye nobuchwepheshe bokucofa kwangaphambili kunye neteknoloji yokuseta iguqule inkqubo yokuvelisa amaphephandaba. Obu bugcisa buye benza ukuba amaphephandaba apapashe iifoto ezinemibala kunye nemizobo, kunye noyilo oluyilayo kunye noyilo olungcono. 

Ukuze imixholo yawo icace kumaziko eendaba, amanye amaphephandaba ashicilelwa kumaphepha eendaba anemibala. Umzekelo, iFinancial Times iprintwa kwiphepha elahlukileyo lesalmon elipinki, kwaye upapasho lwezemidlalo lweveki yeSheffield lufumana igama layo, iGreen 'Un, kumbala wemveli wephepha layo. Iphephandaba lezemidlalo lase-Italiya i-La Gazzetta dello Sport likwaprintwa kwiphepha elipinki ngelixa i-L'Équipe (eyayisakuba yi-L'Auto) ishicilelwe kwiphepha elityheli.
