Zombini ezi zamva zaphakamisa imidyarho yeebhayisikile ezinkulu kwaye imibala yazo yeendaba ibonakaliswe kwimibala yeejezi ezisetyenziswa ukubonisa inkokeli yogqatso; umzekelo inkokeli yaseGiro d'Italia inxiba ijezi epinki. 

Ukujikeleza kunye nokufunda 
Amanqaku aphambili: Uluhlu lwamaphephandaba ngokujikeleziswa, ukusasazwa kwamaphephandaba, kunye nokuguga kokufunda amaphephandaba
Inani leekopi ezisasaziweyo, mhlawumbi ngosuku oluqhelekileyo okanye ngeentsuku ezithile (ngokuqhelekileyo ngeCawa), libizwa ngokuba lusasazo lwephephandaba kwaye yenye yezinto eziphambili ezisetyenziselwa ukumisela amaxabiso entengiso. Ukusasazwa kweekopi akufani ngokuyimfuneko neekopi ezithengiswayo, ekubeni ezinye iikopi okanye amaphephandaba asasazwa ngaphandle kweendleko. Amanani okufunda anokuba phezulu kunamanani asasazwayo, kuba iikopi ezininzi zifundwa ngabantu abangaphezulu komnye, nangona oku kulungiswa linani leekopi ezisasaziweyo kodwa zingafundwa (ingakumbi ezo zisasazwe simahla). E-United States, i-Alliance ye-Audited Media igcina idatha yembali kunye nekhoyo ngoku kwi-avareji yokusasazwa kwamaphephandaba emihla ngemihla naweveki kunye namanye amaphepha-ndaba. 

Ngokutsho kweGuinness Book of Records, ukusasazwa kwemihla ngemihla kwephephandaba laseSoviet iTrud kwadlula ama-21 500 000 ngowe-1990, ngoxa i<em>Soviet weekly Argumenty i Fakty yaqhayisa ngokusasazwa kwama-33 500 000 ngowe-1991. izigidi. I<em>Bild yaseJamani, esasazwa isi-1,15 sezigidi, yayikuphela kwephepha elinye kolo didi. EUnited Kingdom, iLanga lelona lithengisiweyo liphezulu, malunga neekopi ezimalunga nezigidi ezisisi-1.2 ezisasazwa yonke imihla. E-US, i-Wall Street Journal inokuhanjiswa kwemihla ngemihla malunga ne-2.02 yezigidi, nto leyo eyenza ibe lelona phepha lisasazwe kakhulu kweli lizwe.[47] 

Ngelixa ukufunda okuhlawulwayo kwamaphephandaba ashicilelweyo kuye kwancipha ngokuthe ngcembe kumazwe aphuhlileyo e-OECD, iye yanyuka kwizizwe eziphuhlayo eziphambili (eBrazil, eIndiya, e-Indonesia, e-China naseMzantsi Afrika), ehlawulelwa ukuhanjiswa kwemihla ngemihla kudlula ezo zezizwe eziphuhlileyo okokuqala kwi-2008 [48]. EIndiya, [49] IThe Times of India lelona phephandaba lesiNgesi elisasazwa kakhulu, elineekopi ezizizigidi ezi-3.14 yonke imihla. NgokoPhando lwe-Indian Readership ka-2009, iDainik Jagran lelona phephandaba lifundwa kakhulu, ngolwimi lwasekhaya (isiHindi), elinabafundi abazizigidi ezingama-55.7.[50] Ngokutsho kukaTom Standage weThe Economist, i-Indiya ngoku isasazwa amaphephandaba mihla le iikopi ezizigidi ezili-110.[51]

Umlinganiselo oqhelekileyo wempilo yephephandaba kukungena kwiimarike, ochazwa njengepesenti yamakhaya afumana ikopi yephephandaba xa kuthelekiswa nenani lilonke lamakhaya akummandla worhwebo wephepha. Kwi-1920s, kwisiseko sesizwe e-US, amaphephandaba emihla ngemihla aphumelele ukungena kwimarike ye-123 yeepesenti (ithetha ukuba i-avareji yekhaya lase-US lifumene amaphephandaba e-1.23). Njengoko amanye amajelo eendaba ayeqalisa ukukhuphisana namaphephandaba, yaye njengoko ushicilelo lwalusiya lusiba lula yaye lungabizi mali ininzi nto leyo ebangela ukuba kubekho ushicilelo olwahlukileyo, ukungena kwiimarike kwaqalisa ukuhla. Kwakungekho de kwasekuqaleni kweminyaka yee-1970, nangona kunjalo, ukungena kwimarike kwehle ngaphantsi kwe-100 ekhulwini. Ngowama-2000, yayingama-53 ekhulwini yaye isehla.[52] Amaphephandaba amaninzi ahlawulelwayo anikezela ngezicwangciso ezahlukeneyo zokubhalisa. Ngokomzekelo, umntu usenokufuna kuphela iphepha langeCawa, okanye mhlawumbi ngeCawa nangoMgqibelo kuphela, okanye mhlawumbi umrhumo weveki yomsebenzi kuphela, okanye mhlawumbi umrhumo wemihla ngemihla. Inkoliso yamaphephandaba inikela inxalenye okanye yonke imixholo yawo kwi-Intanethi, ngaphandle kweendleko okanye ngentlawulo. Kwezinye iimeko, ukufikelela kwamahhala kufumaneka kuphela kwimiba yeentsuku okanye iiveki, okanye kwinani elithile lamanqaku ajongwayo, emva koko abafundi kufuneka babhalise kwaye banike idatha yomntu. Kwezinye iimeko, oovimba basimahla banikezelwa.

Intengiso 
 
eLondon
Iphephandaba likholisa ukwenza i-70-80% yengeniso yalo kwiintengiso, kunye nentsalela kwiintengiso nemirhumo.[53] Inxalenye yephephandaba engapapashiyo ibizwa ngokuba ngumxholo wokuhlela, umcimbi womhleli, okanye nje umhleli, nangona ixesha lokugqibela likwasetyenziselwa ukubhekisa ngokukodwa kuloo manqaku iphephandaba nababhali balo abaziindwendwe bavakalisa izimvo zabo. (Olu lwahlulo, nangona kunjalo, lwaphuhliswa ngokuhamba kwexesha - abapapashi bokuqala abafana noGirardin (eFransi) kunye neZang (Austria) abazange bahlale behlula izinto ezihlawulwayo kumxholo wokuhlela.). Imodeli yoshishino yokuba neentengiso ixhasa iindleko zokushicilela nokusasazwa kwamaphephandaba (kwaye, kusoloko kuthenjwa, ukwenziwa kwengeniso) kunokuba abantu abarhumayo bahlawule zonke iindleko zenziwa okokuqala, kubonakala ngathi, ngowe-1833 yiThe Sun, iphepha lemihla ngemihla elapapashwa kwisiXeko saseNew York. Kunokuba babize 6 iisenti ikopi nganye, ixabiso eqhelekileyo New York yonke imihla ngelo xesha, babiza 1-cent, kwaye kuxhomekeke intengiso ukwenza umahluko.[54]
 
Amaphephandaba kumazwe anokufikelela lula kwiwebhu aye enzakaliswa kukuncipha kwabathengisi abaninzi bemveli. Iivenkile zesebe kunye neevenkile ezinkulu bekunokuthenjelwa kuzo kwixesha elidlulileyo ekuthengeni amaphepha ezibhengezo zamaphephandaba, kodwa ngenxa yokumanyaniswa kweshishini mancinane kakhulu amathuba okwenza oko ngoku.[55] Ukongeza, amaphephandaba abona abathengisi bemveli betshintshela kumaqonga amatsha eendaba. Uluhlu oluhleliweyo lutshintshela kwiisayithi ezibandakanya iCraigslist, iiwebhusayithi zengqesho, kunye neendawo zemoto. Abathengisi belizwe batshintshela kwiintlobo ezininzi zomxholo wedijithali kubandakanya iiwebhusayithi, amaqonga eendaba atyebileyo, kunye neselula. 

Kwiminyaka yakutshanje, i-advertorial yavela. Iintengiso zidla ngokubonwa njengohlelo oluchaseneyo apho abantu besithathu bahlawula umrhumo wokuba ibandakanywe kwiphepha. Ababhengezi badla ngokubhengeza iimveliso ezintsha okanye ubuchule, njengoyilo olutsha lwezixhobo zegalufa, uhlobo olutsha lotyando lwelaser, okanye amayeza okunciphisa umzimba. Ithoni idla ngokusondela kushicilelo lweendaba kuneendaba zeendaba ezinenjongo. Amanqaku anjalo ahlala ehlulwa ngokucacileyo kumxholo wokuhlela ngokusebenzisa uyilo kunye noyilo lwephepha okanye ngeleyibhile ebhengeza inqaku njengentengiso. Nangona kunjalo, kukho inkxalabo ekhulayo malunga nokufiphala komgca phakathi kokuhlela kunye nomxholo wesibhengezo.[56] 

Ngo-1938 isibhengezo sephepha-ndaba lesiDatshi sempahla yabasetyhini ethengiswa kwiivenkile ze-C&A 
ngo-1938 isibhengezo sephepha-ndaba lesiDatshi sempahla yabasetyhini ethengiswa kwiivenkile ze-C&A ezithengisa 
 
ingeniso yephephandaba lase-US—I-Newspaper Association of America yapapasha idatha[57] 
ingeniso yentengiso yephephandaba lase-US—I-Newspaper Association of America yapapasha idata[57] 
Ubuntatheli 
Inqaku eliphambili: I-Journalism 

Inqaku lomhleli I-Journalism Thenyil9 Kray e-Russian
Ekubeni amaphephandaba aqala njengephephancwadi (ingxelo yeziganeko zangoku), umsebenzi owawubandakanyekile ekwenzeni amaphephandaba waqalisa ukubizwa ngokuba bubuntatheli. Ngexesha lobuntatheli obutyheli ngenkulungwane ye-19, amaphephandaba amaninzi eUnited States ayethembele kumabali achukumisayo awayenzelwe ukucaphukisa okanye ukuvuyisa uluntu, kunokuba axelele. Isimbo esithintelweyo sokunika ingxelo esixhomekeke ekujongweni kwenyani kunye nokuchaneka kuphinde kwaduma ngeMfazwe yesibini yeHlabathi. Ukugxekwa kobuntatheli kuyahluka kwaye ngamanye amaxesha kunomsindo. Ukuthembeka kuyabuzwa ngenxa yemithombo engaziwa; iimpazamo kwizibakala, upelo negrama; utyekelo lokwenyani okanye olubonwayo; kunye namahlazo abandakanya ukukopa kunye nokuyila. 

Ngaphambili, amaphephandaba ebesoloko engabanikazi bamaphephandaba, kwaye ayesetyenziselwa ukufumana ilizwi lezopolitiko. Emva ko-1920 uninzi lwamaphephandaba aphambili aba yinxalenye yamatyathanga aqhutywa ngamaqumrhu amakhulu eendaba afana neGannett, iMcClatchy Company, iHearst Corporation, iCox Enterprises, iLandmark Media Enterprises LLC, iMorris Communications, iThe Tribune Company, iHollinger International, iNews Corporation, iSwift Communications, njalo njalo. Iimpempe, kunye nabo “bavuza” amabali orhwaphilizo kwimibutho yezopolitiko basoloko bekhetha ukwazisa amaphephandaba phambi kwezinye iindlela zonxibelelwano, bexhomekeke ekucingeni ukuba abahleli bamaphepha-ndaba bazimisele ukubhentsisa iimfihlo kunye nobuxoki babo bangathanda ukuwagubungela. Nangona kunjalo, kuye kwakho iimeko ezininzi zokuzimela kwezopolitiko kwamaphephandaba kuncitshiswa. Uphando lwakutsha nje luphonononge iziphumo zokuvalwa kwephephandaba ekonyulweni kwakhona kwababambeleyo, abavoti, kunye nenkcitho yephulo. [58] 

Izimvo zabanye ababhali nabafundi zichazwe kwi-op-ed ("ichasana nephepha lokuhlela") kunye neeleta eziya kumacandelo abahleli bephepha. Ezinye iindlela amaphephandaba azame ngazo ukuphucula ukuthembeka kwawo zezi: ukutyumba i-ombudsmen, ukuphuhlisa imigaqo-nkqubo yeenqobo ezisesikweni noqeqesho, ukusebenzisa imigaqo-nkqubo yezilungiso engqongqo, ukunxibelelana ngeenkqubo zabo nengqiqo nabafundi, nokucela imithombo yolwazi ukuba iphonononge amanqaku emva kokuba epapashiwe. 

Ifuthe likamabonwakude ne-Intanethi 
Inqaku eliphambili: Ukuhla kwamaphephandaba 
Ulwazi oluthe kratya: Amaphephandaba akwi-Intanethi 

Ushicilelo lwephephandaba eLimoges, eFransi
Ngasekupheleni kwee-1990s, ukufumaneka kweendaba kumajelo omabonwakude weeyure ezingama-24 kunye nobukho obulandelayo bobuntatheli be-intanethi buze kube ngumngeni oqhubekayo kumzekelo woshishino wamaphepha-ndaba amaninzi kumazwe aphuhlileyo. Ukusasazwa kwamaphephandaba ahlawulwayo kuye kwancipha, ngelixa ingeniso yentengiso-ininzi yengeniso yamaphephandaba amaninzi-iye yatshintsha ukusuka kushicilelo ukuya kumajelo asekuhlaleni kunye neewebhusayithi zeendaba, okubangele ukuhla ngokubanzi. Omnye wemingeni kukuba inani leewebhusayithi zeendaba ezikwi-intanethi zikhululekile ukufikelela kuzo. Ezinye iisayithi zeendaba ze-intanethi zine-paywall kwaye zifuna umrhumo ohlawulelwayo ukuze ufikelele. Kumazwe angakhangayo kangako, ukushicilelwa nokusasazwa kwayo ngexabiso eliphantsi, ukwanda kolwazi lokufunda nokubhala, ukwanda kwabantu abakumgangatho ophakathi nezinye oothunywashe ziye zayibuyekeza ngokuvela kwezixhobo ze-elektroniki, yaye ukusasazwa kwamaphephandaba kusaqhubeka kusanda.[59]

NgoAprili ka-1995, iThe American Reporter yaba liphephandaba lokuqala lemihla ngemihla elisekelwe kwi-Intanethi kunye neentatheli zalo ezihlawulwayo kunye nomxholo wokuqala. [60] Ikamva lamaphephandaba kumazwe anamazinga aphezulu okufikelela kwi-Intanethi kuye kwaxoxwa kakhulu ngalo njengoko ishishini liye lajongana nokunyuka kwamaxabiso oshicilelo lweendaba, ukuhla kweentengiso zentengiso, ilahleko yeentengiso ezininzi ezihlelwayo, kunye nokwehla okukhawulezileyo kokujikeleza. Ukususela ekupheleni kweminyaka yee-1990, inani lamaphephandaba ekulindeleke ukuba livalwe, litshone, okanye lincitshiswe ngokuqatha—ingakumbi eUnited States, apho eli shishini liye lachitha isihlanu seentatheli zalo ukususela ngowama-2001.[61] Ingxelo kaJuni 2022 iqikelele ukuba amaphephandaba ama-2 afa ngeveki, kwaye atyhila ukuba i-US yehla ukusuka kumaphephandaba angama-8,891 ngo-2005 ukuya kwi-6,377 ekupheleni kukaMeyi 2022. Imisebenzi yobuntatheli yehla malunga ne-75,000 ngo-2006 ukuya kwi-31,000 ngo-2022. 

Ingxoxo-mpikiswano ingxamiseke kakhulu mva nje, njengoko ukudodobala koqoqosho kuka-2008-2009 kwacheba iingeniso zamaphephandaba kwaye ukukhula kwakanye kwaqhuma kwingeniso yewebhu kuye kwathabath' unyawo, kunqanda oko ishishini linethemba lokuba liya kuba ngumthombo obalulekileyo wengeniso.[63] Umba ngowokuba ingaba ishishini lephephandaba lijongene nomjikelo webhayisikile (okanye idiphu), okanye ingaba itekhnoloji entsha inikeze amaphephandaba ashicilelo ukuba aphelelwe lixesha. Ukusukela ngo-2017, ipesenti eyandayo yeminyaka eyiwaka ifumana iindaba zabo kwiiwebhusayithi zemidiya yoluntu. Kwiminyaka ye-2010, amaphephandaba amaninzi emveli aqalise ukubonelela "ii-digital editions", ezifumaneka ngeekhompyutha kunye nezixhobo eziphathwayo. Intengiso kwi-Intanethi ivumela iiwebhusayithi zeendaba ukuba zibonise iintengiso ezilungiselelwe, ngokusekelwe kwizinto ezinomdla wondwendwe. 

Oovimba 
Bona kwakhona: Uluhlu lwamaxwebhu ephepha-ndaba kunye namaPhepha-ndaba e-United States § Oovimba 
Kwixesha lewebhu, oovimba bedijithali bebesoloko bethatha indawo yogcino lwangaphambili lwemicroform kunye nekopi eprintiweyo, kwaye le mibini imidiya yokugqibela iye yafakwa kwidijithali ngokuskena umfanekiso, ngokwesiqhelo ngekonsathi kunye nokuqondwa koonobumba ababonakalayo.

Eli nqaku limalunga neempapasho. Ngolunye usetyenziso, jonga iMagazini (disambiguation). 
"Ngekota" isalathisa apha. Ngekota kwi-heraldry, bona i-Quartering (heraldry). 

Eli nqaku linemiba emininzi. Nceda uncede ukuyiphucula okanye uxoxe ngale miba kwiphepha lentetho. (Funda ukuba ungayisusa njani kwaye nini le miyalezo) 
Eli nqaku libandakanya uluhlu lweereferensi ngokubanzi, kodwa alinazo ngokwaneleyo izicatshulwa ezihambelanayo emgceni. (Januwari 2025) 
Eli nqaku lichaza imithombo yalo kodwa alinikeli maphepha eembekiselo. (Januwari 2025) 
Ukuchaneka kokwenyaniso kweenxalenye zeli nqaku (ezo zihlobene nelothe, nakulo lonke) kusenokubekwa esichengeni ngenxa yenkcazelo ephelelwe lixesha. Isizathu esinikiweyo sesi: inqaku liyasilela ukujongana, ngaphandle kokunyanzeliswa kunye namaxesha athile, impembelelo egqwesileyo kwaye ebhalwe kakuhle yenguqu yoshicilelo-kwidijithali yeshishini, enefuthe kulo lonke eli nqaku. (NgoJanuwari 2025) 

UHarper's Monthly, amandla oncwadi kunye nezopolitiko ngasekupheleni kwenkulungwane ye-19[icatshulwa] 
Imagazini[1] lupapasho lwamaxesha ngamaxesha, olushicilelweyo okanye lwedijithali, oluveliswe kwishedyuli eqhelekileyo, equlathe naluphi na uhlobo lomxholo osekelwe kwisifundo kunye neefom zomxholo obonwayo. Ngokuqhelekileyo amaphephancwadi axhaswa ngemali ngezibhengezo, ixabiso lokuthenga, imirhumo ehlawulwa kwangaphambili, okanye ngokudityaniswa kwezi zintathu. Zihlelwa ngokwamaxesha okupapashwa kwazo (okt, njengeeveki ngeeveki, ngenyanga, ngekota, njl.njl.), abantu ekujoliswe kubo (umzkl, iimagazini zabasetyhini kunye nezorhwebo), imixholo yazo (umz., isayensi edumileyo kunye nenkolo), kunye neethoni zabo okanye iindlela zokuthetha (umz., imisebenzi yokuhlekisa okanye ehlekisayo). Imbonakalo kuqweqwe lwamaphephancwadi ashicilelweyo ngokwembali yayiqondwa njengedlulisela indawo yembeko okanye umahluko kumntu okanye isiganeko. 

Igama imvelaphi kunye nengcaciso 
Imvelaphi 
I-etymology yegama elithi "magazine" icebisa ukuthatyathwa kwegama lesiArabhu makhāzin (مخازن), isininzi esaphukileyo se-makhzan (مخزن) elithetha "idepo, uvimba" (ekuqaleni uvimba womkhosi); leyo iza kwisiNgesi ngemagazini yaseMbindi yesiFrentshi kunye nemagazini yesiTaliyane.[2] Ngokwengqiqo yalo yantlandlolo, igama elithi "iphephancwadi" libhekisela kwindawo yokugcina okanye isixhobo.[2] 

Iinkcazelo 
[icon] 
Eli candelo lifuna ukwandiswa nge: iinkcazelo ezifunyenweyo, ukwenzela ukususa icandelwana kude neWP: OKANYE kunye nembono yomhleli/uluvo. Unokunceda ngokongeza kuyo. (Januwari 2025) 
Kwimeko yopapasho olubhaliweyo, ibhekisela kwingqokelela yamanqaku abhaliweyo; kungoko, upapasho lwamaphephancwadi lwabelana ngemoniker kunye neeyunithi zokugcina izixhobo zomkhosi ezifana nerhuluwa, iimagazini zemipu, kunye nemagazini yesiFrentshi nesiRashiya (ethathwe kwisiFrentshi, njenge магазин), abathengisi abafana neevenkile zesebe.[3]

Umahluko phakathi kweemagazini kunye neejenali ngabaphulaphuli bazo, injongo, kunye nenkqubo yopapasho. Amanqaku ejenali abhalwa ziingcaphephe ezilungiselelwe iingcaphephe, ngelixa amanqaku eemagazini ngokuqhelekileyo ejoliswe kuluntu ngokubanzi okanye ngokwedemografi. Iijenali ziqulethe uphando lwakutsha nje ngemimandla ethile, ngelixa iimagazini zijolise ekonwabisa, ukwazisa, okanye ukufundisa abaphulaphuli ngokubanzi ngemixholo emininzi. Iijenali zipapashwa yimibutho yezemfundo okanye yobungcali, kwaye zinokujongwa kwakhona ngoontangandini, ngelixa amanqaku emagazini eqhelekile kwaye efikeleleka ngakumbi kunamanqaku ejenali, ehlala ebhalwa ngendlela yobuntatheli.[4][5] 

Ukuhanjiswa 

Iimagazini zokuprinta zaseJamani 
Iimagazini eziprintiweyo zinokusasazwa ngeposi, ngokuthengiswa ziivenkile zeendaba, iivenkile zeencwadi, okanye abanye abathengisi, okanye ngokusasazwa simahla kwiindawo ezikhethiweyo zokuthatha [ukucaphula] Iindlela zokusasaza nge-elektroniki zingabandakanya imidiya yoluntu, i-imeyile, i-aggregators yeendaba, kunye nokubonakala kwewebhusayithi yopapasho kunye neziphumo ze-injini 

yokukhangela 
. imodeli, iphephancwadi lithengiswa kubafundi ngexabiso, mhlawumbi kwi-per-issue basis okanye ngokubhaliselwa, apho umrhumo wonyaka okanye ixabiso lenyanga lihlawulwe kwaye imiba ithunyelwa ngeposi kubafundi. Ujikelezo oluhlawulweyo luvumela iinkcukacha-manani zokufunda ezichaziweyo.[6][7] 

Ukujikeleziswa okungahlawulwanga 
Oku kuthetha ukuba akukho xabiso li-inshorensi kunye nemiba enikezelwayo, umzekelo kwiimpahla zasesitalatweni, kwiinkampani zeenqwelo-moya, okanye zibandakanywe nezinye iimveliso okanye ushicilelo. Ngenxa yokuba le modeli ibandakanya ukunika imiba kubantu abangachazwanga, amanani- 

nkcazo abandakanya kuphela inani lemiba esasaziweyo, hayi ukuba ngubani oyifundayo.
Lo ngumzekelo osetyenziswa ziimagazini ezininzi zorhwebo (amanqaku asekelwe kushishino) asasazwa kuphela kubafundi abafanelekileyo, amaxesha amaninzi simahla kwaye imiselwa luhlobo oluthile lophando. Ngenxa yeendleko (umzekelo, ukuprinta nokuposa) ezinxulumene noshicilelo, abapapashi abanako ukuhambisa iikopi simahla kuye wonke umntu ozicelayo (iinkokeli ezingenakufaneleka); endaweni yoko, basebenza phantsi kojikelezo olulawulwayo, begqiba ukuba ngubani onokufumana imirhumo yasimahla esekelwe kwisiqinisekiso somntu ngamnye njengelungu lorhwebo (kunye nokuba nokwenzeka kokuthenga, umzekelo, ukuba nokwenzeka kokuba negunya lokuthenga iqumrhu, njengoko kumiselwe yitayitile yomsebenzi). Oku kuvumela inqanaba eliphezulu lengqiniseko yokuba izibhengezo zentengiso ziya kufunyanwa ngabaphulaphuli ekujoliswe kubo bomthengisi,[8] kwaye inqanda ukumoshwa kweendleko zoshicilelo nokuhambisa. Le modeli yokugqibela yayisetyenziswa ngokubanzi phambi kokunyuka kweWebhu eBanzi yeHlabathi kwaye isasetyenziswa ngezinye izihloko. Ngokomzekelo, eUnited Kingdom, kukho amaphephancwadi aliqela asebenza ngekhompyutha asebenzisa le ndlela, kuquka iComputer Weekly neComputing, nakwimali iWaters Magazine. Kushishino lwemidiya yehlabathi, umzekelo iyakuba yiVideoAge International.[cating required] 

Imbali 

Eli candelo lifuna ucaphulo olongezelelweyo ukuze lingqinisiswe. Nceda uncede ukuphucula eli nqaku ngokongeza izicatshulwa kwimithombo ethembekileyo kweli candelo. Izixhobo ezingasetyenziswanga zinokucelwa umngeni kwaye zisuswe. (Janyuwari 2025) (Funda ukuba ungawususa njani kwaye nini lo myalezo) 

Iqweqwe langaphambili lomhla woku-1 kuOkthobha 1892 kuhlelo lweNdaba ze-Illustrated zaseLondon 
Umzekelo wokuqala weemagazini yayingu-Erbauliche Monaths Unterredungen, imagazini yoncwadi nefilosofi, eyasungulwa ngo-1663 eJamani.[9] IGentleman's Magazine, eyapapashwa okokuqala ngo-1741 eLondon yaba yimagazini yokuqala enomdla ngokubanzi.[10] U-Edward Cave, owahlela i-Gentleman's Magazine phantsi kwegama losiba "uSylvanus Urban", wayengowokuqala ukusebenzisa igama elithi "magazine", kuthelekiso lwendlu yokugcina impahla yasemkhosini, [11] isicatshulwa sithi: "ingqokelela yenyanga, ukuyigcina njengobutyebi njengemagazini".[12] Yasekwa nguHerbert Ingram ngo-1842, iThe Illustrated London News yaba liphephancwadi leendaba lokuqala elinemizobo leveki nganye.[10] 

EBritani 
Eyona magazini indala yabathengi isashicilelwa yiThe Scots Magazine, [13] eyapapashwa okokuqala ngo-1739, nangona utshintsho oluninzi kubunini kunye nezikhewu kupapasho ezingaphaya kweminyaka engama-90 zilenza buthathaka elo bango. ULuhlu lukaLloyd lwasekwa kwivenkile yekofu kaEdward Lloyd eNgilani ngowe-1734; nangona iqonga layo le-intanethi lisahlaziywa yonke imihla, alizange lipapashwe njengemagazini eprintiweyo ukususela ngo-2013, xa yaphela ukupapashwa emva kweminyaka engama-274 [14]. 

EFransi 
Amanqaku aphambili: Imbali yobuntatheli baseFransi kunye neMbali yobuntatheli 
 
Eli candelo lifuna izicatshulwa ezongezelelweyo zokuqinisekisa. Nceda uncede ukuphucula eli nqaku ngokongeza izicatshulwa kwimithombo ethembekileyo kweli candelo.Izixhobo ezingasetyenziswanga zinokucelwa umngeni kwaye zisuswe.
Fumana imithombo: "Iphephancwadi" - iindaba · amaphephandaba · iincwadi · umphengululi · JSTOR (ngoJanuwari 2025) (Funda indlela kwaye nini ukususa lo myalezo) 

La Gazette, 26 December 1786
Phantsi kweAncien Régime, awona maphephancwadi abalaseleyo yayiyiMercure de France, iJournal des sçavans, eyasekwa ngowe-1665 isenzelwa izazinzulu, neGazette de France, eyasekwa ngowe-1631. UJean Loret wayengomnye weentatheli zokuqala zaseFransi. Wasasaza iindaba zeveki zomculo, umdaniso kunye noluntu lwaseParis ukususela ngo-1650 ukuya kutsho ngo-1665 kwindinyana, kwinto awayeyibiza ngokuba yi-gazette burlesque, ehlanganiswe kwimiqulu emithathu yeLa Muse historique (1650, 1660, 1665). Ushicilelo lwaseFransi lwasilela isizukulwana emva kweBritane, kuba bona bajongana neemfuno zolawulo lwezihandiba, ngelixa oogxa baseBhritane batsha babejolise kwicala eliphakathi kunye neqela elisebenzayo 

. Babengazolanga kwaphela kwezobupolitika—kaninzi babekugxeka ukuphathwa kakubi kweCawa nokungabi nagunya kwabasemagunyeni. Babuxhasa ubukhosi yaye badlala indima encinane ekuvuseleleni inguqulelo.[16][iphepha elifunekayo] Ebudeni beMvukelo, amaphephancwadi amatsha adlala indima ephambili njengamaziko okusasaza amaqela ahlukahlukeneyo. UJean-Paul Marat (1743–1793) wayengoyena mhleli ubalaseleyo. I-L'Ami du peuple yakhe yayithethelela ngamandla amalungelo abantu abakumgangatho ophantsi ngokuchasene neentshaba zabantu uMarat azithiyileyo; lwavalwa xa wayebulawa. Emva komnyaka 

ka 1800 uNapoleon waphinda wamisela uqwalaselo olungqongqo. Bakhonza uluntu lwenkolo, lwenkcubeko kunye nezopolitiko. Ngamaxesha obunzima bezobupolitika bavakalisa baza bancedisa ekulungiseni iimbono zabafundi babo yaye ngaloo ndlela baba ngamalungu aphambili ekuguqukeni kwenkcubeko yezobupolitika.[18][iphepha elifunekayo] Ngokomzekelo, kwakukho amaphephancwadi asibhozo amaKatolika ngowe-1830 eParis. Akukho nanye eyayiyeyeCawa okanye eyayixhaswa ngokusemthethweni yaye yayibonisa uthotho lwezimvo phakathi kwamaKatolika afundileyo ngemibandela yangoku, njengeMvukelo kaJulayi yowe-1830 eyabhukuqa ubukhosi baseBourbon. Uninzi lwaba ngabaxhasi abomeleleyo bookumkani baseBourbon, kodwa bonke abasibhozo bacela inkxaso kurhulumente omtsha, bebeka izibheno zabo ngokugcina ucwangco. Babedla ngokuxubusha ngonxulumano phakathi kwecawa norhulumente. Ngokuqhelekileyo, babebongoza abefundisi ukuba banikele ingqalelo kwizinto zokomoya baze bangazibandakanyi nezobupolitika. Umbhali-mbali uM. Patricia Dougherty uthi le nkqubo idale umgama phakathi kweCawa kunye nokumkani omtsha kwaye yenza ukuba amaKhatholika aphuhlise ukuqonda okutsha kobudlelwane becawe-norhulumente kunye nomthombo wegunya 
lezopolitiko 

.
I-Moniteur Ottoman yayiyigazette ebhalwe ngesiFrentshi kwaye yaqala ukupapashwa ngo-1831 ngokomyalelo ka-Mahmud II. Yayiyi-gazette yokuqala esemthethweni yoBukhosi base-Ottoman, ehlelwe ngu-Alexandre Blacque ngeendleko ze-Sublime Porte. Igama layo mhlawumbi libhekisela kwiphephandaba laseFransi iLe Moniteur Universel. Yayikhutshwa ngeveki. I-Takvim-i vekayi yapapashwa kwiinyanga ezimbalwa kamva, ngenjongo yokuguqulela i-Moniteur kwi-Ottoman Turkish. Emva kokuba ihlelwe nguConsul wangaphambili waseDenmark "M. Franceschi", kwaye kamva ngu "Hassuna de Ghiez", yagqitywa ukuhlelwa nguLucien Rouet. Nangona kunjalo, ijongene nobutshaba boonozakuzaku, yavalwa ngeminyaka yoo-1840. [20] 

I-Satire 

Eli candelo alichazi nayiphi na imithombo. Nceda uncede ukuphucula eli candelo ngokongeza izicatshulwa kwimithombo ethembekileyo. Izixhobo ezingasetyenziswanga zinokucelwa umngeni kwaye zisuswe. (NgoJanuwari 2025) (Funda indlela kwaye nini ukususa lo myalezo) 
Iimagazini zeSatirical zaseTurkey zinesithethe eside. Enye yeemagazini zokuqala ze-satirical yayiyi-Diyojen eyasungulwa ngo-1869. Kukho malunga ne-20 yeemagazini ezihlekisayo; ezona ziphambili yiPenguen (isasazwa ngama-70,000 ngeveki), iLeMan (50,000) ne-Uykusuz. Imizekelo yembali iquka iphephabhuku lika-Oğuz Aral elithi Gırgır (eyafikelela kujikelezo lwe-500,000 kwiminyaka yoo-1970) kunye noMarko Paşa (eyasungulwa ngo-1946). Abanye baquka uL-Manyak kunye neLombak. 

eUnited States 
Ulwazi oluthe vetshe: Imbali yobuntatheli baseMelika kunye nosasazo lweMisa kunye nezopolitiko zaseMelika 
iKoloniyali yaseMelika 
[icon] 
Eli candelo lifuna ukwandiswa: ngenkcazo yobungcali yesi sihloko secandelwana, ephuma kwimithombo yolwazi ukongeza kumthombo wefashoni weVogue ovelayo. Unokunceda ngokongeza kuyo. (NgoJanuwari 2025) 
Ukupapasha yayilishishini elibiza kakhulu ngamaxesha olawulo lwamathanga. Iphepha kunye ne-inki yomshicileli zazirhafiswa kwimpahla ethunyelwa ngaphandle kwaye umgangatho wazo wawungangqinelani. Uluhlu lwamaxabiso aphakathi kwamazwe kunye nenkqubo yendlela engekho mgangathweni ithintele usasazo, nokuba kumlinganiselo wommandla. Kwaqaliswa amaphephancwadi amaninzi, amaninzi esilela kwiintlelo ezimbalwa, kodwa abavakalisi baqhubeka bezama. Kuthiwa uBenjamin Franklin waba nombono wenye yeemagazini zokuqala zamathanga aseMerika ngowe-1741, iGeneral Magazine kunye neHistorical Chronicle. I-Pennsylvania Magazine, ehlelwe nguThomas Paine, yahamba nje ixesha elifutshane kodwa yayiyimpapasho enempembelelo kakhulu ngexesha leMfazwe yeNguquko. Umba wokugqibela oqulethe umbhalo weSibhengezo seNkululeko wapapashwa ngowe-1776.[21][umthombo obhetele ofunekayo] 

Ngasekupheleni kwenkulungwane ye-19.
Phakathi kwinkulungwane ye-19, amaphephancwadi aphuma kanye ngenyanga aye aduma. Zazingumdla ngokubanzi ukuqalisa, ziqulethe ezinye iindaba, ii<em>vignettes, imibongo, imbali, iziganeko zobupolitika, neengxoxo zasentlalweni.[22][iphepha elifunekayo] Ngokungafaniyo namaphephandaba, yayingaphezulu kwengxelo yenyanga yeziganeko zangoku kunye namabali okonwabisayo, imibongo nemifanekiso. Amaphepha-ncwadi okuqala aphuma kwiindaba ayeyiHarper kunye neAtlantiki, egxile ekukhuthazeni ubugcisa. [23] [iphepha elifunekayo] Zombini iHarper kunye neAtlantiki zisaqhubeka unanamhla, kunye noHarper's imagazini yenkcubeko kunye neAtlantiki egxile kakhulu kwiziganeko zehlabathi. Upapasho lwangaphambili lukaHarper lude lwabamba imisebenzi edumileyo njengopapasho lokuqala lukaMoby Dick okanye iziganeko ezidumileyo ezinjengokubekwa kwentambo yocingo yokuqala yehlabathi yokuwela iAtlantiki; kunjalo, isininzi isiqulatho ekuqaleni kwaba trickle phantsi iziganeko British.[24] 

Ukuphuhliswa kwamaphephancwadi kwavuselela ukwanda kokugxekwa koncwadi kunye neengxoxo zezopolitiko, ukuya kwiingqungquthela ezingaphezulu kweengcamango ezivela kumaphephandaba anenjongo. [23] [iphepha elifunekayo] Ixesha elongezelelweyo phakathi koshicilelo kunye nenani elikhulu lesithuba sokubhala libonelele iqonga leengxoxo zoluntu ngabaphengululi kunye nabakhi-mkhanyo abagxekayo 

. yaba yincutshe ngakumbi 

kwaye ingxoxo ngokubanzi okanye iincwadana zenkcubeko ziye zanyanzeliswa ukuba ziqhelane nemarike yabathengi eyayilangazelela ukuhanjiswa kwemicimbi kunye neziganeko zasekuhlaleni 

. IiOlimpiki zasehlotyeni. 
Ulwazi oluthe vetshe: IMuckrakers kunye neMas media kunye nezopolitiko zaseMelika 
Iimagazini zokusasazwa kweMisa ziye zaxhaphaka ngakumbi emva ko-1900, ezinye zisasazwa kumakhulu amawaka ababhalisile. Abanye baphumelele isigidi-mark kwi-1920s. Yayilixesha lemithombo yeendaba. Ngenxa yokwanda okukhawulezayo kweentengiso zelizwe, ixabiso le-inshorensi lehla kakhulu laya kutsho malunga neesenti ezili-10.[26] Omnye unobangela yayikukubhengezwa kakhulu korhwaphilizo kwezopolitiko, oorhulumente basekhaya kunye namashishini amakhulu, ngakumbi ngabakwaMuckrakers. Babeziintatheli ezazibhalela amaphephancwadi adumileyo ukuba abhence izono neentsilelo zentlalo nezopolitiko. Bathembele kwingxelo yabo yobuntatheli obuphandayo; abarhwaphilizi bebesoloko besebenzela ukubhenca ububi bentlalo kunye norhwaphilizo lweshishini nezopolitiko. Iimagazini zeMuckraking–ngokukodwa iMcClure’s–zithabathele kulawulo lweshishini kunye noomatshini bezopolitiko abagqwethekileyo ngelixa besazisa uluntu ngentlupheko engapheliyo yasezidolophini, iimeko zokusebenza ezingakhuselekanga, kunye nemiba yasekuhlaleni efana nokuqeshwa kwabantwana.[27][iphepha elifunekayo]

Iintatheli ezigxile ekuvezeni inkunkuma, urhwaphilizo, kunye nesityholo esisebenza kwinqanaba likarhulumente nelasekhaya, njengoRay Stannard Baker, uGeorge Creel, kunye noBrand Whitlock. Abanye, kuquka uLincoln Steffens, babhenca ukunganyaniseki kwezobupolitika kwizixeko ezininzi ezikhulu; U-Ida Tarbell wahamba emva kweNkampani ye-Oli ye-John D. Rockefeller. USamuel Hopkins Adams ngo-1905 wabonisa ubuqhophololo obubandakanyekayo kumayeza amaninzi elungelo elilodwa lomenzi wechiza, inoveli ka-Upton Sinclair ka-1906 ethi The Jungle yanika umfanekiso owoyikekayo wendlela eyayipakishwe ngayo inyama, kwaye, nango-1906, uDavid Graham Phillips wakhupha isimangalo esibuhlungu seNdlu yeeNgwevu zase-US. Roosevelt 

wanika ezi ntatheli isiqhulo sazo xa wayekhalazela ukuba abancedi nganto 
ngokuqokelela 

bonke 
ubumdaka 
. I-Statista, ukuvalwa kweemagazini kuye kwaqalwa ngenani kuneziphehlelelo kuMntla Melika ngo-2009. Nangona omabini amanani ehlile ngo-2010-2015, iqalise ngokuvalwa okungaphezulu kwenani ngalinye kuloo minyaka, ngamanye amaxesha ngomlinganiselo we-3:1.[30] Ukugxininisa ngakumbi, iMediaFinder.com yafumanisa ukuba iimagazini ezintsha ze-93 zaqaliswa kwiinyanga ezintandathu zokuqala ze-2014, ngelixa i-30 kuphela ivaliwe ngelo xesha. Udidi oluvelise upapasho olutsha kakhulu "Umdla weNgingqi", apho kwaqaliswa iimagazini ezintandathu ezintsha, kubandakanywa i-12th & Broad kunye neCraft Beer & Brewing. Johnson Publishing kaThixo Jet wayeka ushicilelo imiba rhoqo, ukwenza utshintsho kwifomathi yedijithali, nangona nangoku ushicilelo edition yonyaka.[32] Ijenali yeLadies' Home iye yamisa ucwangciso lwabo lwenyanga nokuhanjiswa kwekhaya ukuze abarhumi babe lupapasho olunomdla olukhethekileyo lwekota kuphela.[33] 
Ngokwezibalo ukusuka ekupheleni kuka-2013, amanqanaba okubhalisela ama-22 aphezulu kwiimagazini ze-25 zehla ukusuka kwi-2012 ukuya kwi-2013, kunye nexesha nje, i-Glamour kunye ne-ESPN iMagazine ifumana amanani.[34] Nangona kunjalo, ngo-2024, ezinye izihloko, ngokukodwa iimagazini zangaphandle, zabonakala zikhula ngokuthandwa.[35] 
Iimagazini zabasetyhini



"Oodade abasixhenxe" bamaphephancwadi aseMelika abasetyhini yiLadies' Home Journal, ukugcinwa kakuhle kweNdlu, uMcCall's, uSuku loMfazi, iRedbook, iSangqa soSapho, kunye namaKhaya aNgcono kunye neeGadi. Ezinye iimagazini, phakathi kwazo i-Godey's Lady's Book kunye ne-Harper's Bazaar, zenzelwe kuphela abaphulaphuli ababhinqileyo, begxininisa iindima zesini zenkulungwane ye-19. Ukubandakanywa komxholo we-didactic malunga nokugcinwa kwendlu kusenokuba kwandisa umdla wephephancwadi kubaphulaphuli ababanzi babasetyhini kunye namadoda axhalabileyo malunga nokungabi nanto kwemagazini yefashoni.[21][ukuqinisekiswa okufunekayo] 

Iintlobo 
Kukho iintlobo ezininzi zeemagazini. Ngelixa ezinye zero kwizihloko ezinje ngeejenali zorhwebo ze-niche, uphando oluphambili, okanye iimagi zabasetyhini, ezinye zibandakanya izihloko ezifana nenkolo kunye nenkcubeko yepop. Oku kunokubandakanya ukuhlekisa okumnandi, ukugxeka okufileyo, okanye ukuhleka okuhlekisayo. 

Iindidi 
[umfanekiso] 
Eli candelo lifuna ukwandiswa ngolu hlobo: nokwahlulwa kweendidi ezidityanisiweyo zabaphulaphuli kunye nesihloko, kunye nokukhangela okunye kunye nemizekelo njengoko kufuneka, kwicandelwana ngalinye. Unokunceda ngokongeza kuyo. (Janyuwari 2025) 
Ngokusekelwe kumaxesha athile 
iiMagazini zidla ngokuhlelwa ngokweendlela zokupapashwa kwazo (oko kukuthi, ngeeveki, ngeenyanga, ngeekota, njalo njalo).[38] 

Ngokusekwe kubaphulaphuli ekujoliswe kubo kunye nesihloko 
sefashoni yabasetyhini 
Imagazini yokuqala yabasetyhini ejolise kubafazi noomama yapapashwa ngo-1852. [39] Ngeminyaka yoo-1920, iimagazini ezintsha zabhenela kubafazi abancinci baseJamani abanomfanekiso ovuselelayo kunye nezibhengezo zempahla efanelekileyo kunye nezixhobo abanokuthi bafune ukuzithenga. Amaphepha acwebezelayo e-Die Dame kunye no-Das Blatt der Hausfrau abonise i-"Neue Frauen", "Intombazana Entsha" - oko abantu baseMelika bakubiza ngokuba yi-flapper. Eli bhinqa liselula lifanelekileyo lalilungile, lizimele ngokwezimali, kwaye lithanda ukuthenga iifashoni zamva nje. Iimagazini zamgcina esazi ngefashoni, ubugcisa, imidlalo, nobugcisa bezi mini obunjengeemoto neemfonomfono.[40] 

Ukuba Ngumzali 
Amanye amaphephancwadi amabhinqa aye anempembelelo kwiimbono zobunina nokukhulisa abantwana ngokusebenzisa imihlathi yamacebiso, izibhengezo namanqaku aphathelele ukukhulisa abantwana.[41] Iimagazini zabasetyhini ezithengiswe ngobuninzi ziye zabumba kwaye zaguqula iinqobo zenkcubeko ezinxulumene nezenzo zobuzali. Ngaloo ndlela, iimagazini ezijolise kumabhinqa kunye nokuba ngumzali ziye zasebenzisa amandla nempembelelo kwiingcamango malunga nokuba ngumama nokukhulisa umntwana.[41] 

Unqulo 
Iimagazini zonqulo zinembali ende neyahlukahlukeneyo. EUnited States, amaphephancwadi onqulo aphakathi kwamaphephancwadi okuqala aphumayo, yaye umxholo wawo wanceda ekuxonxeni ukufunda nokubhala, imilinganiselo yokuziphatha neziganeko zobupolitika zeRiphabliki yamandulo. Kodwa kule minyaka ili-150 idluleyo, impembelelo yawo iye yehla.[42] 

Intlebendwane yodumo, umdla womntu
Iimagazini ezipapasha amabali neefoto zabantu abadumileyo nabantu abadumileyo kudala ziyinto ethandwayo eUnited States.[43] Ngo-2019, i-People Magazine ibekwe kwindawo yesibini emva kwe-ESPN Magazine ngokufikelela kuyo yonke i-98.51 yezigidi. 

Ubuchwephesha 

Umzekelo wemagazini yobuchwephesha luSasazo, olujoliswe kubafundi abakwishishini losasazo lukanomathotholo nomabonakude eUnited Kingdom 
Iimagazini zobuchwephesha, ezikwabizwa ngokuba ziimagazini zorhwebo, okanye iimagazini zeshishini ukuya kwishishini zijoliswe kubafundi abaqeshwe kumashishini athile. Ezi magazini zikholisa ukugubungela iintsingiselo zeshishini kunye neendaba ezinomdla kwiingcali zolu shishino. Imirhumo idla ngokuza nobulungu kumbutho weengcali. Iimagazini zobuchwephesha zinokufumana ingeniso kwiintengiso okanye kwiintengiso zeenkampani ezithengisa iimveliso kunye neenkonzo kubaphulaphuli abathile abaziingcali. Imizekelo ibandakanya uBudala beNtengiso, iiNdaba zeMoto, uSasazo, uMthengisi weencwadi, kunye neNqanaba.[45][46][47][48][49] 

Ngokusekwe kwithoni okanye kwindlela yokuthetha 
Iimagazini zinokuhlelwa ngokwethoni yazo okanye ngokwendlela yokufikela kuyo, umz., njengakwimisebenzi yamaxesha athile ephoxayo okanye ehlekisayo.[50] 

Ikhava 
Ulwazi oluthe vetshe: ubugcisa bokhuselo 

Eli candelo linemiba emininzi. Nceda uncede ukuyiphucula okanye uxoxe ngale miba kwiphepha lentetho. (Funda ukuba ungayisusa njani kwaye nini le miyalezo) 
Eli candelo alichazi nayiphi na imithombo. (Januwari 2025) 
Eli candelo lifuna ukwandiswa: umxholo ophuma kumthombo oxoxa ngentsingiselo, kunye nenjongo yobuntatheli kunye nefuthe lobugcisa bemagazini kunye nokufota. Unokunceda ngokongeza kuyo. (Janyuwari 2025) 
Ukuba kuqweqwe lwemagazini ngamanye amaxesha kuthathwa njengembeko, okanye njengembali;[51] imizekelo ziingxelo zexesha elinye ezibonisa ukuba umntu "ubonakale kuqweqwe lweXesha" okanye kwiLitye eliqengqelekayo, njalo njalo.[52][53]
