Ayinakubhidaniswa nopapasho lweDesktop. 

Eli nqaku lidinga izicatshulwa ezongezelelweyo zokuqinisekisa. Nceda uncede ukuphucula eli nqaku ngokongeza izicatshulwa kwimithombo ethembekileyo. Izixhobo ezingasetyenziswanga zinokucelwa umngeni kwaye zisuswe. 
Fumana imithombo yolwazi: "Upapasho lwe-elektroniki" - iindaba · amaphephandaba · iincwadi · isifundiswa · JSTOR (Aprili 2023) (Funda ukuba ungawususa njani kwaye nini lo myalezo) 
Upapasho lwe-elektroniki (elukwabizwa ngokuba lupapasho lwe-elektroniki, upapasho lwedijithali, okanye upapasho lwe-intanethi) luquka upapasho lwedijithali lwee-e-books, iimagazini zedijithali, kunye nophuhliso lweelayibrari zedijithali kunye neekhathalogu.[1] Ikwabandakanya ukuhlelwa kweencwadi, iijenali, kunye neemagazini eziza kufakwa kwiscreen (ikhompyutha, i-e-reader, ithebhulethi, okanye i-smartphone).[2] 

Isishwankathelo 
Upapasho lwe-elektroniki luyinto eqhelekileyo kupapasho lwezenzululwazi apho kuye kwaxoxwa ukuba iijenali zenzululwazi eziphononongwe ngoontanga zikwinkqubo yokuthatyathelwa indawo ngopapasho lwe-elektroniki. Kukwayinto eqhelekileyo ukuhambisa iincwadi, iimagazini, kunye namaphephandaba kubathengi ngokusebenzisa izixhobo zokufunda iithebhulethi, imarike ekhula ngezigidi ngonyaka, [3] iveliswa ngabathengisi be-intanethi abafana nevenkile yeencwadi ye-iTunes, ivenkile yeencwadi ye-Amazon ye-Kindle, kunye neencwadi kuGoogle Play Bookstore. Uphando lwemarike lucebise ukuba isiqingatha sawo onke amaphephancwadi kunye nokuhanjiswa kwephephandaba kuya kuba ngokuhanjiswa kwedijithali ekupheleni kuka-2015[4] kwaye isiqingatha sako konke ukufundwa eUnited States kuya kwenziwa ngaphandle kwephepha ngo-2015 [5]. 

Nangona ukusasazwa nge-Intanethi (ekwaziwa njengopapasho lwe-intanethi okanye upapasho lwewebhu xa lukuhlobo lwewebhusayithi) kule mihla lunxulunyaniswa ngamandla nopapasho lwe-elektroniki, zininzi iimpapasho ze-elektroniki ezingezizo ezothutho ezifana ne-encyclopedias kwi-CD kunye neDVD, kunye noshicilelo lobugcisa kunye nereferensi exhomekeke kubasebenzisi beselula kunye nabanye ngaphandle kokufikelela okuthembekileyo kunye nokufikelela ngokukhawuleza kwinethiwekhi. Upapasho nge-elektroniki luyasetyenziswa kwicandelo lokulungiselela uvavanyo ekuphuhliseni nasekuphuhliseni uqoqosho lwemfundo yabafundi (ngaloo ndlela ngokuyinxenye ithatha indawo yeencwadi eziqhelekileyo) - kuba yenza umxholo kunye nohlalutyo zidityanisiwe - ukuze kuxhamle abafundi. Ukusetyenziswa kopapasho lwe-elektroniki lweencwadi zesikhokelo kunokuba kuxhaphake ngakumbi nge-Apple Books evela kwi-Apple Inc. kunye nothethathethwano lwe-Apple kunye nabathengisi beencwadi abathathu abakhulu e-US[6]

Upapasho lwe-elektroniki luya luthandwa kakhulu kwimisebenzi yentsomi. Abapapashi be-elektroniki bayakwazi ukuphendula ngokukhawuleza kwiimfuno eziguqukayo zemarike, kuba iinkampani akufuneki ziodole iincwadi eziprintiweyo kwaye ziziswe. Upapasho lwe-E lwenza uluhlu olubanzi lweencwadi lufumaneke, kubandakanywa iincwadi abathengi abangayi kuzifumana kubathengisi beencwadi eziqhelekileyo, ngenxa yokungonelanga kwemfuno "yokuprinta". Upapasho lwe-E lwenza ukuba ababhali abatsha bakhuphe iincwadi ezingafane zibe nengeniso kubapapashi bemveli. Ngelixa igama elithi "ukupapashwa kwe-elektroniki" lisetyenziswa ngokuyintloko ngo-2010 ukubhekisa kubashicileli be-intanethi kunye ne-web-based, eli gama linembali yokusetyenziswa ukuchaza uphuhliso lweendlela ezintsha zokuvelisa, ukuhanjiswa, kunye nokusebenzisana komsebenzisi ngokubhekiselele kwimveliso esekelwe kwikhompyutheni yombhalo kunye neminye imithombo yeendaba ezisebenzisanayo.[7] 

I-History 
Digitization 
Inyathelo lokuqala lokufakwa kwedijithali lalingo-1971 nguMichael S. Hart, umfundi weYunivesithi yase-Illinois eChicago, owasungula iProjekthi Gutenberg, [8] eyilelwe ukwenza ukuba uncwadi lufikeleleke ngakumbi kuye wonke umntu, nge-intanethi. Kwathatha ixesha ukuphuhlisa, kwaye ngowe-1989 kwakukho imibhalo ye-10 kuphela eyakhutshelwa ngesandla kwikhompyutheni nguMichael S. Hart ngokwakhe kunye namavolontiya athile. Kodwa ngokubonakala kwe-Web 1.0 kwi-1991 kunye nokukwazi ukudibanisa amaxwebhu kunye namaphepha amileyo, iprojekthi yahamba ngokukhawuleza. Amavolontiya amaninzi ngakumbi ancedise ekuphuhliseni iprojekthi ngokunika ufikelelo kwiindawo zakudala zoluntu.[9] 

Ngeminyaka yee-1970, iZiko leSizwe loPhando lwezeNzululwazi laseFransi lafaka ekhompyutheni iwaka leencwadi kwimixholo eyahlukahlukeneyo, ubukhulu becala uncwadi kodwa nentanda-bulumko nenzululwazi, ezisusela kwinkulungwane ye-12 ukuza kuthi ga ngoku. Ngale ndlela kwakhiwa iziseko zesichazi-magama esikhulu, iTrésor de la langue française au Québec. Esi siseko se-e-texts, ebizwa ngokuba yi-Frantext, yapapashwa kwi-compact disc phantsi kwegama le-brand Discotext, kwaye emva koko kwiwebhu yehlabathi jikelele ngo-1998. 

Ukwenziwa kwedijithali ngobuninzi 
Ngo-1974, umqambi waseMelika kunye nengcali yekamva uRaymond Kurzweil wenze iskena esasixhotyiswe nge-software ye-Omnifont eyenza ukuqondwa koonobumba babona kugalelo lamanani.[Ingcaciso efunekayo] Iiprojekthi zedijithali ke ngoko zinokuba namabhongo ngakumbi kuba ixesha elifunekayo lokufakwa kwedijithali liye lehla kakhulu, kunye nethala leencwadi ledijithali. Ehlabathini lonke, iilayibrari ze-e-layibrari zaqala ukuvela [ukucaphula] 

I-ABU (i-Association des Bibliophiles Universels), yayiyiprojekthi yelayibrari yedijithali yoluntu eyenziwe yi-Cnam ngo-1993. Yayiyilayibrari yokuqala yaseFransi yedijithali kwinethiwekhi; yanqunyanyiswa ukususela ngo-2002, baphinda bavelisa ngaphezu kwekhulu lemibhalo esafumanekayo.[11]

Ngo-1992, i-Bibliothèque nationale de France yasungula inkqubo enkulu yokwenza idijithali. Umongameli uFrançois Mitterrand wayefuna ukususela ngo-1988 ukwenza ilayibrari entsha kunye nentsha yedijithali, kwaye yapapashwa ngo-1997 phantsi kwegama elithi Gallica. Ngo-2014, ithala leencwadi ledijithali lalinikezela nge-80 255 yeencwadi ze-intanethi kunye namaxwebhu angaphezu kwesigidi, kuquka iprints kunye nemibhalo yesandla.[13] 

Ngo-2003, i-Wikisource yaphehlelelwa, kwaye iprojekthi yayinqwenela ukwenza ithala leencwadi ledijithali kunye neelwimi ezininzi eliza kuba luncedo kwiprojekthi yeWikipedia. Ekuqaleni yayibizwa ngokuba yi "Project Sourceberg", njengomdlalo wamagama ukukhumbuza iProjekthi Gutenberg.[14] Ixhaswa yi-Wikimedia Foundation, i-Wikisource iphakamisa iitekisi ezifakwe ekhompyutheni eziye zaqinisekiswa ngamavolontiya.[15] 

NgoDisemba ka-2004, uGoogle wenza iincwadi zikaGoogle, iprojekthi yokwenza zonke iincwadi ezikhoyo emhlabeni zifakwe ekhompyutheni (ngaphezu kwezigidi ezili-130 zeencwadi) ukuze zifikeleleke kwi-intanethi.[16] Kwiminyaka eyi-10 kamva, iincwadi ezingama-25 000 000, ezivela kumazwe alikhulu neelwimi ezingama-400, ziseqongeni. Oku kwakunokwenzeka ngenxa yokuba ngelo xesha, iirobhothi zokuskena zazinokufakwa kwidijithali malunga neencwadi ezingama-6 000 ngeyure.[17] 

Kwi-2008, i-prototype ye-Europeana yasungulwa; kwaye ngo-2010, iprojekthi ibinikezela ukufikelela kwizinto ezidijithali ezingaphezu kwe-10 lezigidi. Ilayibrari Europeana yikhathalogu yaseYurophu ebonelela amakhadi index kwizigidi izinto zedijithali kunye namakhonkco kumathala eencwadi zabo zedijithali.[18] Kwangalo nyaka mnye, iHathiTrust yadalwa ukuze idibanise imixholo yeelayibrari ezininzi ze-eyunivesithi ezivela e-USA naseYurophu, kunye neeNcwadi zikaGoogle kunye noVimba we-Intanethi. Ngo-2016, ngaphezulu kwezigidi ezithandathu zabasebenzisi bebesebenzisa iHathiTrust.[19] 

Upapasho lwe-elektroniki 
Iiprojekthi zokuqala zokwenziwa kwedijithali bezigqithisela umxholo obonakalayo kwisiqulatho sedijithali. Upapasho lwe-elektroniki lujolise ekudibaniseni yonke inkqubo yokuhlela kunye nopapasho (ukuveliswa, ukucwangciswa, ukupapashwa) kwihlabathi ledijithali. 

UAlain Mille, kwincwadi ethi Pratiques de l'édition numérique (ehlelwe nguMichael E. Sinatra kunye noMarcello Vitali-Rosati), [20] uthi ukuqala kwe-Intanethi kunye neWebhu yeyona nto iphambili yokupapashwa kwe-elektroniki, kuba bazimisele kakhulu utshintsho olukhulu kwimveliso kunye neepateni zokusasaza. I-Intanethi inefuthe elithe ngqo kwimibuzo yokupapasha, ivumela abadali kunye nabasebenzisi ukuba baqhubele phambili kwinkqubo yemveli (umbhali-umhleli-indlu yopapasho).[21] 

Upapasho lwemveli, kwaye ngokukodwa inxalenye yokudala, yaqala yatshintshwa yi-desktop entsha epapasha iisoftwares ezibonakala ngoo-1980, kunye nogcino-lwazi olubhaliweyo lwenzelwe iencyclopedia kunye nezalathisi. Ngaxeshanye i-multimedia yayikhula ngokukhawuleza, idibanisa incwadi, i-audiovisual kunye neempawu zesayensi yekhompyutha. IiCD kunye neeDVD ziyavela, nto leyo evumela ukubonwa kwezi zichazi-magama kunye neencyclopedia kwiikhompyutha.[22]

Ukufika kunye nedemokhrasi ye-Intanethi kunika izindlu ezincinci zokupapasha ithuba lokupapasha iincwadi zazo ngokuthe ngqo kwi-Intanethi. Ezinye iiwebhusayithi, njengeAmazon, zivumela abasebenzisi bazo ukuba bathenge ii-eBooks; Abasebenzisi be-Intanethi banokufumana amaqonga okufundisa amaninzi (asimahla okanye hayi), iiwebhusayithi zeencyclopedic ezifana neWikipedia, kunye namaqonga eemagazini zedijithali. I-eBook ke iye ifikeleleke ngakumbi nangakumbi ngeenkxaso ezininzi ezahlukeneyo, njenge-e-reader kunye nee-smartphones. Incwadi yedijithali, kwaye isenayo, impembelelo ebalulekileyo kwizindlu zokupapasha kunye nemizekelo yazo yezoqoqosho; isengummandla oshukumayo, kwaye kusafuneka bazazi iindlela ezintsha zokupapasha kwixesha ledijithali.[23] 

Uhlelo olukwi-Intanethi 
Ngokusekwe kwiinkqubo ezintsha zonxibelelwano zewebhu 2.0 kunye noyilo olutsha lokuthatha inxaxheba, uhlelo lwe-intanethi luvula umnyango wentsebenziswano yoluntu ukuze kucaciswe ngakumbi kwaye kuphuculwe imixholo kwi-Intanethi, ngelixa ikwaphucula ukufunda ngokufunda ngokudibeneyo. Iwebhu 2.0 ayidibanisi amaxwebhu kuphela, njengoko yenza iwebhu 1.0, ikwadibanisa abantu kunye ngemidiya yoluntu: yiyo loo nto ibizwa ngokuba yiWebhu eThatha inxaxheba (okanye ethatha inxaxheba).[24] 

Izixhobo ezininzi zabekwa endaweni yokukhuthaza ukwabelana kunye nemixholo edibeneyo yokuyila. Enye yezininzi yiWikipedia encyclopedia, kuba ihleliwe, yalungiswa kwaye yandiswa zizigidi zabanegalelo. I-OpenStreetMap ikwasekwe kumgaqo ofanayo. Iiblogi kunye neenkqubo zokuphawula ziyaziwa ngoku njengohlelo lwe-intanethi kunye nopapasho, njengoko kunokwenzeka ngonxibelelwano olutsha phakathi kombhali nabafundi bayo, kwaye inokuba yindlela ebalulekileyo yokuphefumlelwa kodwa kunye nokubonakala.[25] 

Inkqubo 
Ulwazi oluthe vetshe: Upapasho lweDesktop 
Inkqubo yokupapasha nge-elektroniki ilandela imiba ethile yenkqubo yemveli yopapasho olusekwe ephepheni[26] kodwa iyahluka kupapasho lwemveli ngeendlela ezimbini: 1) ayibandakanyi ukusebenzisa umatshini wokushicilela we-offset ukuprinta imveliso yokugqibela kunye ne-2) inqanda ukuhanjiswa kwemveliso ebonakalayo (umzekelo, iincwadi zephepha, iimagazini zephepha, okanye iimagazini zephepha). Ngenxa yokuba umxholo ukwi-elektroniki, unokuhanjiswa kwi-Intanethi nakwiivenkile zeencwadi ze-elektroniki, kwaye abasebenzisi banokufunda imathiriyeli kuluhlu lwezixhobo zombane kunye nedijithali, kubandakanya iikhompyuter zedesktop, iilaptops, iikhompyuter zethebhulethi, ii-smartphones okanye iitafile ze-e-reader. Umthengi unokufunda umxholo opapashiweyo kwi-intanethi kwiwebhusayithi, kwisicelo kwisixhobo sethebhulethi, okanye kuxwebhu lwePDF ekhompyutheni. Kwezinye iimeko, umfundi unokuprinta umxholo ephepheni esebenzisa i-ink-jet yodidi lwabathengi okanye iprinta yelaser okanye ngenkqubo yokuprinta-kwimfuno. Abanye abasebenzisi bakhuphela umxholo wedijithali kwizixhobo zabo, nto leyo ebenza bakwazi ukufunda umxholo naxa isixhobo sabo singaqhagamshelwanga kwi-Intanethi (umz., xa bebhabha ngenqwelomoya).

Ukusasaza umxholo nge-elektroniki njengezicelo zesoftware ("ii-apps") sele zidumile kwi-2010s, ngenxa yokwamkelwa kwabathengi ngokukhawuleza kwee-smartphones kunye neetafile. Ekuqaleni, ii -apps zomthonyama zeqonga ngalinye eliphathwayo bekufuneka lifikelele kubo bonke abaphulaphuli, kodwa kumzamo wokuhambelana nesixhobo sehlabathi, ingqalelo iye yajika ekusebenziseni i-HTML5 ukwenza ii -apps zewebhu ezinokusebenza kuso nasiphi na isikhangeli kwaye zisebenze kwizixhobo ezininzi. Inzuzo yopapasho lwe-elektroniki ivela ekusebenziseni iimpawu ezintathu zobuchwepheshe bedijithali: iithegi ze-XML ukuchaza umxholo, [27] amaphepha esitayile ukuchaza inkangeleko yomxholo, kunye nemetadata (idatha malunga nedatha) ukuchaza umxholo weenjini zokukhangela, ngaloo ndlela inceda abasebenzisi ukuba bafumane kwaye bafune umxholo (umzekelo oqhelekileyo wemetadata lulwazi malunga nombhali wengoma wengoma, umqambi ohlanganisiweyo kunye neefayile ze-elektroniki ze-CD; imetadata yenza kube lula kubathandi bomculo ukufumana iingoma abazikhangelayo). Ngokusetyenziswa kweethegi, amaphepha esitayela, kunye nemethadatha, oku kwenza ukuba umxholo "owenziwe kwakhona" ulungelelanise nezixhobo zokufunda ezahlukeneyo (ithebhulethi, i-smartphone, i-e-reader, njl.) okanye iindlela zokuhanjiswa kwe-elektroniki. 

Ngenxa yokuba upapasho lwe-elektroniki luhlala lufuna ukuphawula okubhaliweyo (umzekelo, uLwimi lweMarkup ye-HyperText okanye olunye ulwimi lwe-markup) ukuphuhlisa iindlela zokuhanjiswa kwe-intanethi, iindima eziqhelekileyo zoomatshini bokubhala kunye nabayili beencwadi, abaye badala ukuseta ukushicilelwa kweencwadi zephepha, zitshintshile. Abaqulunqi bomxholo opapashwe ngedijithali kufuneka babe nolwazi olomeleleyo lweelwimi zokuphawula, iintlobo ngeentlobo zezixhobo zokufunda kunye neekhompyutha ezikhoyo, kunye neendlela abathengi abafunda ngazo, ukujonga okanye ukufikelela kumxholo. Nangona kunjalo, ngo-2010s, isoftware entsha yoyilo esebenzisekayo iyafumaneka ukuze abaqulunqi bapapashe umxholo kulo mgangatho ngaphandle kokufuna ukwazi iindlela ezineenkcukacha zokucwangcisa, ezinje ngeAdobe Systems' Digital Publishing Suite kunye neApple's iBooks Author. Eyona fomati yefayile ixhaphake yi.epub, esetyenziswa kwiifomati ezininzi ze-e-book. .epub ngumgangatho okhululekileyo novulekileyo okhoyo kwiinkqubo ezininzi zokupapasha. Enye ifomathi eqhelekileyo ithi .folio, esetyenziswa yi-Adobe Digital Publishing Suite ukwenza umxholo we-iPad tablets kunye ne-apps. 


Incwadi ye-ebook (ifutshane kwincwadi ye-elektroniki), ephinda ibhalwe njenge-e-book okanye i-eBook, yincwadi epapashiweyo eyenziwe yafumaneka ngohlobo lwe-elektroniki, equka umbhalo, imifanekiso, okanye zombini, efundeka kwiphaneli yephaneli ebonisa iikhompyutha okanye ezinye izixhobo zombane.[1] Nangona ngamanye amaxesha ichazwa "njengenguqulelo ye-elektroniki yencwadi eprintiweyo", [2] ezinye ii-e-books zikhona ngaphandle kokuprintwa okufanayo. Iincwadi ze-E-zinokufundwa kwizixhobo ezizinikeleyo zokufunda i-elektroniki, nakuso nasiphi na isixhobo sekhompyutha esinesikrini sokujonga esilawulekayo, kubandakanywa iikhompyutha zedesktop, iilaptops, iitafile kunye nee-smartphones.

Kwi-2000s, kwakukho umkhwa wokuprinta kunye ne-e-book yokuthengisa ehamba kwi-Intanethi, [3] apho abafundi bathenga iincwadi zephepha zemveli kunye ne-e-ncwadi kwiiwebhusayithi usebenzisa iinkqubo ze-e-commerce. Ngeencwadi eziprintiweyo, abafundi baya bekhangela ngakumbi kwimifanekiso yamaqweqwe eencwadi kumshicileli okanye kwiiwebhusayithi zevenkile yeencwadi kunye nokukhetha kunye nokuodola izihloko kwi-Intanethi. Emva koko iincwadi zamaphepha zisiwa kumfundi ngeposi okanye ngayo nayiphi na enye inkonzo yokuhanjiswa. Ngee-books, abasebenzisi banokukhangela ngezihloko kwi-intanethi, bakhethe kwaye baodole izihloko, emva koko i-e-book inokuthunyelwa kubo kwi-intanethi okanye umsebenzisi unokukhuphela i-e-book.[4] Ekuqaleni koo-2010, ii-e-books zaziqalisile ukudlula i-hardcover ngamanani apapashiweyo ngokubanzi e-US[5] 

Ezona zizathu ziphambili zokuba abantu bathenge i-e-books mhlawumbi ngenxa yamaxabiso aphantsi, ukonyuka kokukhululeka (njengoko benokuthenga ekhaya okanye ekuhambeni ngezixhobo eziphathwayo) kunye nokhetho olukhulu lwezihloko.[6] Ngee-books, "iibhukhimakhi ze-elektroniki zenza kube lula ukubhekisela, kwaye abafundi be-e-book banokuvumela umsebenzisi ukuba achaze amaphepha." "Nangona iincwadi ezingeyonyani nezingezontsomi ziza kwiifomathi ze-e-book, izinto zobugcisa zifaneleke ngokukodwa ukuhanjiswa kwe-e-book kuba zinokukhangelwa ngedijithali" kumagama angundoqo. Ukongeza, kwiincwadi zeprogram, imizekelo yekhowudi inokukhutshelwa.[7] E-US, inani le-e-ncwadi yokufunda liyenyuka. Ngo-2021, i-30% yabantu abadala baye bafunda i-e-book kunyaka odlulileyo, xa kuthelekiswa ne-17% kwi-2011. Ngo-2014, i-50% yabantu abadala baseMerika babe ne-e-reader okanye ithebhulethi, xa kuthelekiswa ne-30% ephethe izixhobo ezinjalo kwi-2013. [9] 

Ngaphandle kweencwadi ezipapashiweyo kunye neemagazini ezinokulingana kwedijithali, kukwakho neencwadi zokufunda zedijithali ezijoliswe ukuba zisebenze njengesicatshulwa seklasi kunye nokunceda kwimfundo esekelwe kubuchwepheshe. 

Ii-Teminology 
E-books zikwabizwa ngokuba zii-"ebooks", "e-books", "eBooks", "Ebooks", "e-Books", "e-journals", "e-editions", okanye "digital books". Isixhobo esenzelwe ngokukodwa ukufunda iincwadi ze-e-book kuthiwa yi-"e-reader", "ebook device", okanye "eReader". 

Imbali 
The Readies (1930) 
Abanye balanda ingqikelelo ye-e-reader, isixhobo esiya kwenza ukuba umsebenzisi abone iincwadi kwiscreen, kwimanifesto ka-1930 kaBob Brown, eyabhalwa emva kokubukela i-"talkie" yakhe yokuqala (ifilimu enesandi). Wayibiza ngokuba yiThe Readies, edlala ingcamango ye "talkie".[10] Kwincwadi yakhe, uBrown uthi iimuvi ziye zayigqitha incwadi ngokudala "iintetho" kwaye, ngenxa yoko, ukufunda kufuneka kufumane indlela entsha: 

Umatshini wokufunda olula endinokuthi ndiwuthwale okanye ndiwujikeleze, ndincamathele kuyo nayiphi na iplagi yombane endala kwaye ndifunde iinoveli zamagama alikhulu-waka kwimizuzu eli-10 ukuba ndiyafuna, kwaye ndiyafuna.

Ingcamango kaBrown, nangona kunjalo, yayigxile kakhulu ekuguquleni ukubhalwa kwe-orthography kunye nesigama, kunokuba kuphakathi. Uthi: "Lixesha lokukhupha isithinteli" kwaye uqalise "inguqu enegazi yegama," ukwazisa amanani amakhulu eesimboli ze-portmanteau ukubuyisela amagama aqhelekileyo, kunye neziphumlisi ukulinganisa isenzo okanye intshukumo, ngoko ke akucaci ukuba oku kuyangena kwimbali ye "e-books" okanye hayi. Kamva abafundi be-elektroniki abazange balandele imodeli kwaphela efana nekaBrown. Nangona kunjalo, wachaza ngokuchanekileyo i-miniaturization kunye nokuphatheka kwe-e-readers. Kwinqaku, uJennifer Schuessler ubhala athi: "Umatshini, uBrown wathi, uya kuvumela abafundi ukuba bahlengahlengise ubungakanani bohlobo, baphephe ukusika amaphepha kunye nokugcina imithi, ngelixa bekhawuleza imini xa amagama anokuthi 'abhalwe ngokuthe ngqo kwi-ether epholileyo. U-Schuessler uyinxulumanisa no-DJ ojikeleza amasuntswana eengoma ezindala ukwenza isingqi okanye ingoma entsha ngokupheleleyo, ngokuchaseneyo ne-remix yengoma eqhelekileyo.[11] 

Umqambi 
we-e-book yokuqala akuvunyelwana ngayo ngokubanzi. Abanye abaviwa abaphawulekayo baquka oku kulandelayo: 

URoberto Busa (1946-1970) 
I-e-book yokuqala ingaba yi-Index Thomisticus, i-index ye-elektroniki echazwe kakhulu kwimisebenzi kaThomas Aquinas, elungiselelwe nguRoberto Busa, SJ eqala ngo-1946 kwaye yagqitywa kwi-1970s [12]. Nangona ekuqaleni yayigcinwe kwikhompyutha enye, inguqulelo yeCD-ROM esasazwayo yavela ngowe-1989. Noko ke, lo msebenzi uyashiywa ngamanye amaxesha. Mhlawumbi oku kungenxa yokuba umbhalo ofakwe ekhompyutheni wawuyindlela yokufunda izicatshulwa ezibhaliweyo kunye nokuphuhlisa iikhonkodensi zolwimi, kunokuba ibe luhlelo olupapashiweyo ngokwalo.[13] Ngo-2005, i-Index yapapashwa kwi-intanethi.[14] 

U-Ángela Ruiz Robles (1949) 
Ngo-1949, u-Ángela Ruiz Robles, utitshala waseFerrol, eSpain, wafumana ilungelo elilodwa lomenzi kwi-Enciclopedia Mecánica, okanye i-Mechanical Encyclopedia, isixhobo somatshini esasisebenza emoyeni oxinanisiweyo apho okubhaliweyo kunye nemizobo yayiqulethwe kwii-spools ezithi abasebenzisi baziphonse ezijikelezayo. Umbono wakhe yayikukwenza isixhobo esiza kunciphisa inani leencwadi ezithwalwa ngabafundi bakhe xa besiya esikolweni. Esona sixhobo sokugqibela sasicetywe ukuba siquke izinto ezirekhodiweyo, iglasi yokukhulisa, isixhobo sokubala, nesibane sombane ukuze sifundwe ebusuku.[15] Isixhobo sakhe asizange sibekwe kwimveliso kodwa iprototype iboniswa kwiMyuziyam yeSizwe yeSayensi neTekhnoloji eA Coruña. [16]
 
UDouglas Engelbart kunye noAndries van Dam (1960s)
Ngaphandle koko, abanye ababhali-mlando bacinga ukuba iincwadi ze-elektroniki ziqale ekuqaleni kwe-1960s, kunye neprojekthi ye-NLS ekhokelwa nguDouglas Engelbart kwi-Stanford Research Institute (SRI), kunye ne-Hypertext Editing System kunye neeprojekthi ze-FRESS ezikhokelwa ngu-Andries van Dam kwiYunivesithi yaseBrown [17] [18] [19] Amaxwebhu e-FRESS aqhutywa kwi-IBM izakhelo eziphambili kwaye ajolise kulwakhiwo kunokuba ajolise kumgca. Zaye zafomathwa ngokuguquguqukayo kubasebenzisi abahlukeneyo, i-hardware yokubonisa, ubungakanani befestile, njalo njalo, kunye nokuba neetafile ezizenzekelayo zemixholo, izalathisi, njalo njalo. Zonke ezi nkqubo zikwabonelele ngonxibelelwano olubanzi, imizobo, kunye nobunye ubuchule. UVan Dam kucingelwa ukuba wayila igama elithi "incwadi ye-elektroniki", [20][21] kwaye yasekwa ngokwaneleyo ukuba isetyenziswe kwisihloko senqaku ngo-1985. 

I-FRESS yayisetyenziselwa ukufunda izicatshulwa eziphambili ezibanzi kwi-intanethi, kunye nochazo kunye neengxoxo ze-intanethi kwiikhosi ezininzi, kuquka i-English Poetry kunye ne-Biochemistry. Ifakhalthi kaBrown isebenzise kakhulu iFRESS. Umzekelo isithandi sobulumko uRoderick Chisholm wasisebenzisa ukuvelisa uninzi lweencwadi zakhe. Ngaloo ndlela kwiNtshayelelo kuMntu kunye neNjongo (1979) ubhala athi: "Le ncwadi yayingayi kugqitywa ngaphandle kwe-epoch-making File Retrieval and Editing System ..." [23] Umsebenzi weYunivesithi yaseBrown kwiinkqubo zeencwadi ze-elektroniki waqhubeka iminyaka emininzi, kubandakanywa iiprojekthi ezixhaswa ngemali yi-US Navy yokulungiswa kwe-electronic-manual; eyakha iDynaText, inkqubo yokuqala esekwe kwiSGML ye-e-reader; kunye nomsebenzi obanzi weQela leTekhnoloji yeScholar kumgangatho we-Open eBook. 

UMichael S. Hart (1971) 

uMichael S. Hart (ngasekhohlo) kunye noGregory Newby (ekunene) weProjekthi Gutenberg, kwiNkomfa ye-Hackers kwiPlanethi yoMhlaba (HOPE), ngo-2006 
Nangona imbali yangaphambili ebanzi, iimpapasho ezininzi zibika uMichael S. Hart njengomqambi we-e-book.[26][27][28] Kwi-1971, abaqhubi be-Xerox Sigma V mainframe kwiYunivesithi yase-Illinois banike iHart ixesha elide lekhompyutheni. Efuna ukusetyenziswa ngokufanelekileyo kwesi sixhobo, wenza uxwebhu lwakhe lokuqala lwe-elektroniki ngokuchwetheza iSibhengezo seNkululeko saseUnited States kwikhompyutha ngombhalo ocacileyo. UHart ucwangcise ukwenza amaxwebhu esebenzisa umbhalo ocacileyo ukuze kube lula kangangoko ukukhuphela nokujonga kwizixhobo. Emva kokuba uHart elungelelanise iSibhengezo seNkululeko sase-US kuxwebhu lwe-elektroniki ngo-1971, iProjekthi Gutenberg yasungulwa ukwenza iikopi ze-elektroniki zemibhalo emininzi, ngakumbi iincwadi.[29] 

Ukuphunyezwa kwehardware kwangoko
Izixhobo ze-hardware ezinikezelweyo zokufunda i-ebook zaqala ukuvela kwi-70s kunye ne-80s, ngaphezu kwesakhelo esiphambili kunye nezisombululo zelaptop, kunye nokuqokelelwa kwedatha nganye. Olunye ukuphunyezwa kwe-e-book kwasekuqaleni yayiyi-desktop yeprototype yekhompyuter ecetywayo, iDynabook, ngeminyaka yoo-1970 e-PARC: ikhompyuter yenjongo eqhelekileyo ephathwayo ekwaziyo ukubonisa iincwadi zokufunda.[30] Ngo-1980, iSebe lezoKhuselo lase-US laqala uphuhliso lwengqikelelo yesixhobo sokuhanjiswa kwe-elektroniki esiphathwayo solwazi logcino lobugcisa olubizwa ngokuba yiprojekthi iPEAM, i-Portable Electronic Aid for Maintenance. Iinkcukacha ezineenkcukacha zagqitywa ngo-FY 1981/82, kwaye uphuhliso lweprototype lwaqala nge-Texas Instruments kwangaloo nyaka. Iiprototypes ezine zaveliswa kwaye zanikezelwa ukuvavanywa kwi-1986, kwaye iimvavanyo zagqitywa ngo-1987. Ingxelo yokugqibela yesishwankathelo yaveliswa kwi-1989 yi-US Army Research Institute ye-Behavioral and Social Sciences, ebhalwe nguRobert Wisher kunye no-J. Peter Kincaid. Isicelo selungelo elilodwa lomenzi wechiza kwisixhobo sePEAM, [32] esinesihloko esithi "Izixhobo zokuzisa imiyalelo yohlobo lwenkqubo", sangeniswa yiTexas Instruments ngoDisemba 4, 1985, edwelisa uJohn K. Harkins noStephen H. Morriss njengabaqambi. 


Incwadi yokuqala ye-elektroniki ephathekayo, iSebe lezoKhuseleko lase-US "Uncedo lwe-elektroniki lobuqu kwi-Maintainance" 
Kwi-1992, u-Sony uqalise i-Data Discman, umfundi wencwadi ye-elektroniki onokufunda iincwadi ze-e-books ezigcinwe kwiiCD. Olunye upapasho lwe-elektroniki olwalunokudlalwa kwiDiscman yeDatha yayibizwa ngokuba yiThala leeNcwadi Lekamva.[33] Iincwadi ze-e-early zazibhalelwa iindawo ezikhethekileyo kunye nabaphulaphuli abambalwa, benzelwe ukufundwa kuphela ngamaqela amancinci kunye namaqela anomdla. Umda wemiba yesifundo sezi e-books ubandakanya iimanyuwali zobugcisa zehardware, ubuchule bokuvelisa, kunye nezinye izifundo. Kwiminyaka ye-1990, ukufumaneka ngokubanzi kwe-Intanethi kwenza ukuhanjiswa kweefayile ze-elektroniki kube lula kakhulu, kubandakanywa 

ne-e-books. Into ephawulekayo yayikukulandela umkhondo wephepha lokugqibela elifundiweyo ukuze xa ubuyela 'kwincwadi' ubuyiselwe apho ubuyeke ukufunda ngaphambili. Isihloko sesi sitaki sisenokuba sincede ekwenzeni igama elithi 'ebook' lidume. [34] 

Iifomathi ze-e-book 
Jonga kwakhona: Uthelekiso lweefomathi ze-e-book
 
Ibhinqa lifunda incwadi isebenzisa i-e-reader
Njengoko iifomathi ze-e-book zavela kwaye zanda, [ukucaphula] inkxaso efunyenweyo evela kwiinkampani ezinkulu zesoftware, njengeAdobe nefomathi yayo yePDF eyaziswa ngo-1993. [35] Ngokungafaniyo nezinye iifomathi ezininzi, amaxwebhu ePDF ahlala ebotshelelwe kubungakanani obuthile kunye noyilo, kunokuba ahlengahlengise ngokutshintshayo kwiphepha langoku, ifestile, okanye obunye ubungakanani. Izixhobo ezahlukeneyo ze-e-reader zilandele iifomathi ezahlukeneyo, uninzi lwazo lwamkela iincwadi ngefomathi enye okanye ezimbalwa, ngaloo ndlela zahlulahlula i-e-book market nangakumbi. Ngenxa yobubodwa kunye nomlinganiselo wokufunda we-e-books, imarike eyaphukileyo yabashicileli abazimeleyo kunye nababhali abakhethekileyo abazange bavumelane malunga nomgangatho wokupakisha kunye nokuthengisa iincwadi ze-e-books [icatshulwa] 

Ngelo xesha, abaphengululi baye baqulunqa i-Text Encoding Initiative, eyaphuhlisa izikhokelo zemvumelwano malunga neencwadi ze-encoding kunye nezinye izixhobo zokufunda kakuhle njengoko kuhlalutya umdla wokufunda. Iincwadi ezininzi kunye neminye imisebenzi iye yaphuhliswa kusetyenziswa indlela ye-TEI. Ekupheleni kweminyaka yoo-1990, kwasekwa iqumrhu lokuphuhlisa i-Open eBook ifomathi njengendlela yokuba ababhali nabapapashi babonelele ngomthombo omnye-uxwebhu olunokuthi luphathwe ngesoftware yokufunda iincwadi kunye namaqonga ehardware. Abaphengululi abaliqela abavela kwi-TEI babebandakanyeka ngokusondeleyo kuphuhliso lokuqala lwe-eBook evulekileyo, kuquka uAllen Renear, uElli Mylonas, noSteven DeRose, bonke baseBrown. Igxile ekuphatheni, Vula i-eBook njengoko kuchaziwe iiseti ezifunekayo ze-XHTML kunye neCSS; isethi yefomathi zemultimedia (ezinye zingasetyenziswa, kodwa kufuneka kwakhona kubekho ukubuyisela umva kwenye yeefomati ezifunekayo), kunye ne-XML schema ye "manifest", ukudwelisa amacandelo e-e-book enikeziweyo, ukuchonga uluhlu lweziqulatho, ubugcisa bokugubungela, njalo njalo. Iincwadi zikaGoogle ziguqule imisebenzi emininzi yoluntu kule fomati ivuliweyo.[36] 

Kwi-2010, iincwadi ze-e-books zaqhubeka zizuza kwiingcali zabo kunye neemarike eziphantsi komhlaba. Kwangaxeshanye, ababhali abaneencwadi ezingamkelwanga ngabapapashi banikela ngemisebenzi yabo kwi-intanethi ukuze ibonwe ngabanye. [37] Iikhathalogu zeencwadi ezingekho semthethweni (kwaye ngamanye amaxesha ezingagunyaziswanga) ziye zafumaneka kwiwebhu, kwaye iisayithi ezinikezelwe kwii-e-books zaqala ukusasaza ulwazi malunga ne-e-books eluntwini.[38] Phantse isibini kwisithathu se-US Consumer e-book publishing market ilawulwa yi "Big Five". Abapapashi be "Big Five" ngaba: Hachette, HarperCollins, Macmillan, Penguin Random House kunye noSimon & Schuster. [39] 

Amathala eencwadi
Amathala eencwadi ase-US aqala ukunikezela ngee-e-books zasimahla kuluntu ngo-1998 ngokusebenzisa iiwebhusayithi zabo kunye neenkonzo ezihambelanayo, [40] nangona iincwadi ze-e-books ubukhulu becala yayizizifundo, ubuchwephesha, okanye ubuchwephesha bendalo, kwaye zingenako ukukhutshelwa. Ngo-2003, amathala eencwadi aqala ukunikezela ngeencwadi ze-e-fiction ezikhutshelwayo simahla nezingezontsomi eluntwini, esungula imodeli yokuboleka i-e-ncwadi eyasebenza ngempumelelo kakhulu kumathala eencwadi oluntu. [41] Inani labahambisi beencwadi ze-e-ncwadi zethala leencwadi kunye nemifuziselo yokuboleka imali liqhubekile nokukhula kule minyaka imbalwa izayo. Ukususela ngo-2005 ukuya ku-2008, amathala eencwadi afumana ukukhula kwe-60% kwiiqoqo ze-e-book.[42] Ngo-2010, i-Public Library Funding and Technology Access Study yi-American Library Association [43] yafumanisa ukuba i-66% yamathala eencwadi oluntu e-US anikezela nge-e-books, [44] kunye nentshukumo enkulu kushishino lwamathala eencwadi yaqala ukuvavanya nzulu imiba enxulumene nokubolekwa kwe-e-book, ukuvuma "inqaku lokuphonononga" xa i-e-book iteknoloji iya kusekwa ngokubanzi. Isiqulatho esivela kumathala eencwadi oluntu sinokukhutshelwa kwi-e-readers kusetyenziswa isoftwe yesicelo efana ne-Overdrive kunye neHoopla.[46] 

ILayibrari yeSizwe yezoNyango yase-US iminyaka emininzi ibonelela nge-PubMed, i-bibliography ebanzi yoncwadi lwezonyango. Ekuqaleni kuka-2000, i-NLM yaseka indawo yokugcina i-PubMed Central, egcina iinguqulelo ezipheleleyo ze-e-book zamanqaku amaninzi ejenali yezonyango kunye neencwadi, ngokusebenzisana nabaphengululi kunye nabapapashi entsimini. I-Pubmed Central ikwabonelela ngogcino kunye nokufikelela kumanqaku angaphezu kwezigidi ezi-4.1, agcinwe kwifomathi eqhelekileyo yeXML eyaziwa ngokuba yiJournal Article Tag Suite (JATS).

Nangona ukwamkelwa ngokubanzi kweencwadi ze-e-books, abanye abapapashi kunye nababhali abazange bayivume ingcamango yokupapashwa kwe-elektroniki, bekhankanya imiba efunwa ngumsebenzisi, ukuphulwa kwelungelo lokushicilela kunye nemingeni kunye nezixhobo zobunikazi kunye neenkqubo. [47] Kuphando lwemali mboleko yamathala eencwadi (ILL), kwafunyaniswa ukuba ama-92% amathala eencwadi abamba ii-e-books kwingqokelela yawo kwaye ama-27% aloo mathala athethathethane ngamalungelo e-ILL kwezinye zeencwadi zawo ze-e-book. Olu phononongo lufumene imiqobo ebalulekileyo ekuqhubeni imali-mboleko yamathala eencwadi kwi-e-books.[48] I-Patron-driven acquisition (PDA) ikhona iminyaka eliqela kumathala eencwadi kawonke-wonke, ivumela abathengisi ukuba balungelelanise inkqubo yokufumana ngokunikezela ukutshatisa iprofayile yokhetho lwethala leencwadi kunye nezihloko ze-e-book yomthengisi. Ikhathalogu yethala leencwadi ke izaliswe ngeerekhodi zazo zonke ii-e-books ezihambelana neprofayile. Isigqibo sokuthenga itayitile sishiyelwa kubaxhasi, nangona ithala leencwadi linokubeka iimeko zokuthenga ezifana nexabiso eliphezulu kunye neekepusi zokuthenga ukuze imali enikezelweyo isetyenziswe ngokohlahlo lwabiwo-mali lwethala leencwadi.[49] Intlanganiso ka-2012 ye-Association of American University Presses yayiquka iphaneli kwi-PDA yeencwadi eziveliswe ngoomatshini bokushicilela baseyunivesithi, ngokusekelwe kwingxelo yokuqala kaJoseph Esposito, umcebisi wokushicilela wedijithali oye wafunda iimpembelelo zePDA kunye nesibonelelo esivela ku-Andrew W. Mellon Foundation.[50] 

Imingeni 
Nangona imfuno yeenkonzo ze-e-book kumathala eencwadi ikhule kumashumi amabini eminyaka okuqala enkulungwane yama-21, ubunzima bugcina amathala eencwadi ekuboneleleni ngeencwadi ze-imeyile kubathengi. Abapapashi baya kuthengisa iincwadi ze-e-books kumathala eencwadi, kodwa kwiimeko ezininzi baya kunika amathala eencwadi kuphela ilayisenisi elinganiselweyo kwisihloko, oku kuthetha ukuba ithala leencwadi alinayo itekisi ye-elektroniki kodwa ivumelekile ukuyijikeleza nokuba yithuba elithile lexesha, okanye inani elithile lokuphuma, okanye zombini. Xa ithala leencwadi lithenga ilayisenisi ye-e-book, ixabiso liphinda kathathu into ebeliya kuba yiyo kumthengi wobuqu.[51] Iilayisensi ze-E-book zibiza kakhulu kunohlelo lwefomathi yephepha kuba abapapashi banexhala lokuba incwadi ye-e-ncwadi ethengiswayo inokufundwa kunye/okanye ijongwe liqela elikhulu labasebenzisi, ukuthengisa okunokuba yingozi. Nangona kunjalo, ezinye izifundo zifumene umphumo ochaseneyo ukuba yinyani (umzekelo, uHilton noWikey 2010).[52] 

Ugcino loovimba 
Uvimba we-Intanethi kunye neThala leeNcwadi eliVulelekileyo zibonelela ngaphezulu kwezigidi ezithandathu ezifikeleleka ngokupheleleyo kwii-e-books zoluntu. IProjekthi Gutenberg ineencwadi ze-e-books ezifumaneka simahla kwidomeyini yoluntu. 

Abafundi behardware abazinikeleyo kunye nesoftware ephathwayo 
Inqaku eliphambili: I-E-reader 
Jonga kwakhona: Ukuthelekiswa kwe-e-readers 

IBEBook e-reader
I-e-reader, ekwabizwa ngokuba yi-e-book reader okanye i-e-book device, sisixhobo sombane esiphathwayo esenzelwe ngokukodwa injongo yokufunda ii-e-books kunye neeperiodical digital. I-e-reader ifana nefom, kodwa iyancipha ngakumbi kwinjongo kunethebhulethi. Xa kuthelekiswa namacwecwe, uninzi lwe-e-readers lungcono kuneetafile zokufunda ngenxa yokuba ziphathwa ngakumbi, zifundeka ngcono ekukhanyeni kwelanga kwaye zinobomi obude bebhetri. [53] NgoJulayi 2010, umthengisi weencwadi kwi-intanethi i-Amazon.com ibike ukuthengiswa kwe-e-books ye-Kindle yayo yobunikazi, ingaphezulu kweentengiso zeencwadi ezinoqweqwe olunzima okokuqala ngqa kwikota yesibini ye-2010, isithi ithengise ii-e-books ze-140 kuzo zonke iincwadi ze-100 ezinoqweqwe olulukhuni, kubandakanywa ii-hardcovers apho kwakungekho uhlelo lwedijithali.[54] NgoJanuwari 2011, ukuthengiswa kwe-e-book e-Amazon yayigqithise intengiso yayo yamaphepha. [55] Kuyo yonke imarike yase-US, ukuthengiswa kwencwadi yephepha kusenkulu kakhulu kunoqweqwe olulukhuni okanye i-e-ncwadi. I-American Publishing Association iqikelelwa ukuba i-e-books imele i-8.5% yeentengiso phakathi no-2010, ukusuka kwi-3% ngonyaka ngaphambili. [56] Ekupheleni kwekota yokuqala ka-2012, ukuthengiswa kwe-e-book e-United States kwadlula ukuthengiswa kwencwadi enoqweqwe olulukhuni okokuqala.[5] 

Kuze kube sekupheleni kuka-2013, ukusetyenziswa kwe-e-reader kwakungavumelekanga kwiinqwelomoya ngexesha lokuhamba kunye nokuhla yi-FAA. [57] NgoNovemba 2013, i-FAA ivumele ukusetyenziswa kwe-e-readers kwiinqwelomoya ngamaxesha onke ukuba ikwiModi yeenqwelomoya, oku kuthetha ukuba zonke iirediyo zicinyiwe, kwaye iYurophu yalandela esi sikhokelo kwinyanga ezayo. Kwi-2014, i-New York Times iqikelele ukuba ngo-2018 iincwadi ze-e-ncwadi ziza kwenza ngaphezu kwe-50% yengeniso yokushicilela abathengi eUnited States nase-Great Britain. [59] 

Izicelo 

Ukufundwa kwezicelo kwizixhobo ezahlukeneyo 
Abanye abathengisi beencwadi abaphambili kunye nabaphuhlisi abaninzi beqela lesithathu babonelela simahla (kwaye kwezinye iimeko zomntu wesithathu, intlawulo ehlawulwayo) usetyenziso lwesoftware ye-e-reader (ii-apps) zekhompyuter yeMac kunye nePC kunye ne-Android, iBlackberry, i-iPad, i-iPhone, iWindows Phone kunye nezixhobo zePalm OS ukuvumela ukufundwa kwe-e-ncwadi kunye namanye amaxwebhu ngokuzimeleyo kwizixhobo ezinikezelweyo ze-ebook. Imizekelo ziiapps zeAmazon Kindle,[60] Barnes & Noble Nook, iBooks, Kobo eReader kunye neSony Reader. 

Eli nqaku limalunga neempapasho. Ngolunye usetyenziso, jonga iMagazini (disambiguation). 
"Ngekota" isalathisa apha. Ngekota kwi-heraldry, bona i-Quartering (heraldry). 

Eli nqaku linemiba emininzi. Nceda uncede ukuyiphucula okanye uxoxe ngale miba kwiphepha lentetho. (Funda ukuba ungayisusa njani kwaye nini le miyalezo) 
Eli nqaku libandakanya uluhlu lweereferensi ngokubanzi, kodwa alinazo ngokwaneleyo izicatshulwa ezihambelanayo emgceni. (Januwari 2025) 
Eli nqaku lichaza imithombo yalo kodwa alinikeli maphepha eembekiselo. (Januwari 2025)
Ukuchaneka okuyinyani kweenxalenye zeli nqaku (ezo zinxulumene nelothe, kwaye kuyo yonke) zisenokuphazamiseka ngenxa yolwazi oluphelelwe lixesha. Isizathu esinikiweyo sesi: inqaku liyasilela ukujongana, ngaphandle kokunyanzeliswa kunye namaxesha athile, impembelelo egqwesileyo kwaye ebhalwe kakuhle yenguqu yoshicilelo-kwidijithali yeshishini, enefuthe kulo lonke eli nqaku. (NgoJanuwari 2025) 

UHarper's Monthly, amandla oncwadi kunye nezopolitiko ngasekupheleni kwenkulungwane ye-19[icatshulwa] 
Imagazini[1] lupapasho lwamaxesha ngamaxesha, olushicilelweyo okanye lwedijithali, oluveliswe kwishedyuli eqhelekileyo, equlathe naluphi na uhlobo lomxholo osekelwe kwisifundo kunye neefom zomxholo obonwayo. Ngokuqhelekileyo amaphephancwadi axhaswa ngemali ngezibhengezo, ixabiso lokuthenga, imirhumo ehlawulwa kwangaphambili, okanye ngokudityaniswa kwezi zintathu. Zihlelwa ngokwamaxesha okupapashwa kwazo (okt, njengeeveki ngeeveki, ngenyanga, ngekota, njl.njl.), abantu ekujoliswe kubo (umzkl, iimagazini zabasetyhini kunye nezorhwebo), imixholo yazo (umz., isayensi edumileyo kunye nenkolo), kunye neethoni zabo okanye iindlela zokuthetha (umz., imisebenzi yokuhlekisa okanye ehlekisayo). Imbonakalo kuqweqwe lwamaphephancwadi ashicilelweyo ngokwembali yayiqondwa njengedlulisela indawo yembeko okanye umahluko kumntu okanye isiganeko. 

Igama imvelaphi kunye nengcaciso 
Imvelaphi 
I-etymology yegama elithi "magazine" icebisa ukuthatyathwa kwegama lesiArabhu makhāzin (مخازن), isininzi esaphukileyo se-makhzan (مخزن) elithetha "idepo, uvimba" (ekuqaleni uvimba womkhosi); leyo iza kwisiNgesi ngemagazini yaseMbindi yesiFrentshi kunye nemagazini yesiTaliyane.[2] Ngokwengqiqo yalo yantlandlolo, igama elithi "iphephancwadi" libhekisela kwindawo yokugcina okanye isixhobo.[2] 

Iinkcazelo 
[icon] 
Eli candelo lifuna ukwandiswa nge: iinkcazelo ezifunyenweyo, ukwenzela ukususa icandelwana kude neWP: OKANYE kunye nembono yomhleli/uluvo. Unokunceda ngokongeza kuyo. (Januwari 2025) 
Kwimeko yopapasho olubhaliweyo, ibhekisela kwingqokelela yamanqaku abhaliweyo; kungoko, upapasho lwamaphephancwadi lwabelana ngemoniker kunye neeyunithi zokugcina izixhobo zomkhosi ezifana nerhuluwa, iimagazini zemipu, kunye nemagazini yesiFrentshi nesiRashiya (ethathwe kwisiFrentshi, njenge магазин), abathengisi abafana neevenkile zesebe.[3] 

Umahluko phakathi kweemagazini kunye neejenali ngabaphulaphuli bazo, injongo, kunye nenkqubo yopapasho. Amanqaku ejenali abhalwa ziingcaphephe ezilungiselelwe iingcaphephe, ngelixa amanqaku eemagazini ngokuqhelekileyo ejoliswe kuluntu ngokubanzi okanye ngokwedemografi. Iijenali ziqulethe uphando lwakutsha nje ngemimandla ethile, ngelixa iimagazini zijolise ekonwabisa, ukwazisa, okanye ukufundisa abaphulaphuli ngokubanzi ngemixholo emininzi. Iijenali zipapashwa yimibutho yezemfundo okanye yobungcali, kwaye zinokujongwa kwakhona ngoontangandini, ngelixa amanqaku emagazini eqhelekile kwaye efikeleleka ngakumbi kunamanqaku ejenali, ehlala ebhalwa ngendlela yobuntatheli.[4][5] 

Ukusasazwa
 
iimagazini ezishicilelweyo zesiJamani
Iimagazini zokuprinta zinokusasazwa ngeposi, ngokuthengiswa ziivenkile zeendaba, iivenkile zeencwadi, okanye abanye abathengisi, okanye ngokusasazwa simahla kwiindawo ezikhethiweyo zokuthatha [ukucaphula] Iindlela zokusasaza nge-elektroniki zingabandakanya imidiya yoluntu, i-imeyile, i-aggregators yeendaba, kunye nokubonakala kwewebhusayithi yopapasho kunye neziphumo ze-injini 
yokukhangela 

. abafundi ngexabiso, mhlawumbi ngokwesiseko semiba nganye okanye ngokurhuma, apho umrhumo wonyaka okanye ixabiso lenyanga lihlawulwe kwaye imiba ithunyelwa ngeposi kubafundi. Ujikelezo oluhlawulweyo luvumela iinkcukacha-manani zokufunda ezichaziweyo.[6][7] 

Ukujikeleziswa okungahlawulwanga 
Oku kuthetha ukuba akukho xabiso li-inshorensi kunye nemiba enikezelwayo, umzekelo kwiimpahla zasesitalatweni, kwiinkampani zeenqwelo-moya, okanye zibandakanywe nezinye iimveliso okanye ushicilelo. Ngenxa yokuba le modeli ibandakanya ukunika imiba kubantu abangachazwanga, amanani-manani abandakanya kuphela inani lemiba esasaziweyo, hayi ukuba ngubani oyifundayo.[icatshulwa] 

Ukuhanjiswa okulawulwayo 
Lo ngumzekelo osetyenziswa ngamaphephancwadi orhwebo amaninzi (amanqaku asekelwe kushishino) asasazwa kuphela kubafundi abafanelekileyo, ngokufuthi simahla kwaye kumiselwa luhlobo oluthile lophando. Ngenxa yeendleko (umzekelo, ukuprinta nokuposa) ezinxulumene noshicilelo, abapapashi abanako ukuhambisa iikopi simahla kuye wonke umntu ozicelayo (iinkokeli ezingenakufaneleka); endaweni yoko, basebenza phantsi kojikelezo olulawulwayo, begqiba ukuba ngubani onokufumana imirhumo yasimahla esekelwe kwisiqinisekiso somntu ngamnye njengelungu lorhwebo (kunye nokuba nokwenzeka kokuthenga, umzekelo, ukuba nokwenzeka kokuba negunya lokuthenga iqumrhu, njengoko kumiselwe yitayitile yomsebenzi). Oku kuvumela inqanaba eliphezulu lengqiniseko yokuba izibhengezo zentengiso ziya kufunyanwa ngabaphulaphuli ekujoliswe kubo bomthengisi,[8] kwaye inqanda ukumoshwa kweendleko zoshicilelo nokuhambisa. Le modeli yokugqibela yayisetyenziswa ngokubanzi phambi kokunyuka kweWebhu eBanzi yeHlabathi kwaye isasetyenziswa ngezinye izihloko. Ngokomzekelo, eUnited Kingdom, kukho amaphephancwadi aliqela asebenza ngekhompyutha asebenzisa le ndlela, kuquka iComputer Weekly neComputing, nakwimali iWaters Magazine. Kushishino lwemidiya yehlabathi, umzekelo iyakuba yiVideoAge International.[cating required] 

Imbali 

Eli candelo lifuna ucaphulo olongezelelweyo ukuze lingqinisiswe. Nceda uncede ukuphucula eli nqaku ngokongeza izicatshulwa kwimithombo ethembekileyo kweli candelo. Izixhobo ezingasetyenziswanga zinokucelwa umngeni kwaye zisuswe. (NgoJanuwari 2025) (Funda ukuba ungawususa njani kwaye nini lo myalezo)
 
Iqweqwe langaphambili lomhla woku-1 kuOkthobha 1892 kuhlelo lweThe Illustrated London News.
Owona mzekelo wamandulo wamaphephancwadi yayiyi-Erbauliche Monaths Unterredungen, iphephancwadi loncwadi nefilosofi, eyasungulwa ngo-1663 eJamani.[9] IGentleman's Magazine, eyapapashwa okokuqala ngo-1741 eLondon yaba yimagazini yokuqala enomdla ngokubanzi.[10] U-Edward Cave, owahlela i-Gentleman's Magazine phantsi kwegama losiba "uSylvanus Urban", wayengowokuqala ukusebenzisa igama elithi "magazine", kuthelekiso lwendlu yokugcina impahla yasemkhosini, [11] isicatshulwa sithi: "ingqokelela yenyanga, ukuyigcina njengobutyebi njengemagazini".[12] Yasekwa nguHerbert Ingram ngo-1842, iThe Illustrated London News yaba liphephancwadi leendaba lokuqala elinemizobo leveki nganye.[10] 

EBritani 
Eyona magazini indala yabathengi isashicilelwa yiThe Scots Magazine, [13] eyapapashwa okokuqala ngo-1739, nangona utshintsho oluninzi kubunini kunye nezikhewu kupapasho ezingaphaya kweminyaka engama-90 zilenza buthathaka elo bango. ULuhlu lukaLloyd lwasekwa kwivenkile yekofu kaEdward Lloyd eNgilani ngowe-1734; nangona iqonga layo le-intanethi lisahlaziywa yonke imihla, alizange lipapashwe njengemagazini eprintiweyo ukususela ngo-2013, xa yaphela ukupapashwa emva kweminyaka engama-274 [14]. 

France 
Amanqaku aphambili: Imbali yobuntatheli besiFrentshi kunye neMbali yobuntatheli 

Eli candelo lifuna izicatshulwa ezongezelelweyo zokuqinisekisa. Nceda uncede ukuphucula eli nqaku ngokongeza izicatshulwa kwimithombo ethembekileyo kweli candelo. Izixhobo ezingasetyenziswanga zinokucelwa umngeni kwaye zisuswe. 
Fumana imithombo: "Imagazini" - iindaba · amaphephandaba · iincwadi · isazi · JSTOR (ngoJanuwari 2025) (Funda indlela kwaye nini ukususa lo myalezo) 

La Gazette, 26 December 1786 
Ngaphantsi kwe-Ancien Régime, iimagazini ezibalaseleyo zaziyiMercure de France, Journal des sçavans, eyasungulwa kwi-163 ye-France, i-Gazette ye-Jean165 ifunyenwe kwi-166 ye-France. ULoret wayengomnye weentatheli zokuqala zaseFransi. Wasasaza iindaba zeveki zomculo, umdaniso kunye noluntu lwaseParis ukususela ngo-1650 ukuya kutsho ngo-1665 kwindinyana, kwinto awayeyibiza ngokuba yi-gazette burlesque, ehlanganiswe kwimiqulu emithathu yeLa Muse historique (1650, 1660, 1665). Ushicilelo lwaseFransi lwasilela isizukulwana emva kweBritane, kuba bona bajongana neemfuno zolawulo lwezihandiba, ngelixa oogxa baseBhritane batsha babejolise kwicala eliphakathi kunye neqela elisebenzayo 

. Babengazolanga kwaphela kwezobupolitika—kaninzi babekugxeka ukuphathwa kakubi kweCawa nokungabi nagunya kwabasemagunyeni. Babuxhasa ubukhosi yaye badlala indima encinane ekuvuseleleni inguqulelo.[16][iphepha elifunekayo] Ebudeni beMvukelo, amaphephancwadi amatsha adlala indima ephambili njengamaziko okusasaza amaqela ahlukahlukeneyo. UJean-Paul Marat (1743–1793) wayengoyena mhleli ubalaseleyo. I-L'Ami du peuple yakhe yayithethelela ngamandla amalungelo abantu abakumgangatho ophantsi ngokuchasene neentshaba zabantu uMarat azithiyileyo; lwavalwa xa wayebulawa. Emva kowe-1800 uNapoleon waphinda waphinda wamisela uqwalaselo olungqongqo.[17] [iphepha elifunekayo]

Iimagazini zanda emva kokuba uNapoleon emkile ngowe-1815. Uninzi lwazo lwaluzinze eParis yaye uninzi lwalugxininisa uncwadi, imibongo namabali. Bakhonza uluntu lwenkolo, lwenkcubeko kunye nezopolitiko. Ngamaxesha obunzima bezobupolitika bavakalisa baza bancedisa ekulungiseni iimbono zabafundi babo yaye ngaloo ndlela baba ngamalungu aphambili ekuguqukeni kwenkcubeko yezobupolitika.[18][iphepha elifunekayo] Ngokomzekelo, kwakukho amaphephancwadi asibhozo amaKatolika ngowe-1830 eParis. Akukho nanye eyayiyeyeCawa okanye eyayixhaswa ngokusemthethweni yaye yayibonisa uthotho lwezimvo phakathi kwamaKatolika afundileyo ngemibandela yangoku, njengeMvukelo kaJulayi yowe-1830 eyabhukuqa ubukhosi baseBourbon. Uninzi lwaba ngabaxhasi abomeleleyo bookumkani baseBourbon, kodwa bonke abasibhozo bacela inkxaso kurhulumente omtsha, bebeka izibheno zabo ngokugcina ucwangco. Babedla ngokuxubusha ngonxulumano phakathi kwecawa norhulumente. Ngokuqhelekileyo, babebongoza abefundisi ukuba banikele ingqalelo kwizinto zokomoya baze bangazibandakanyi nezobupolitika. 
Umbhali -mbali uM. Patricia Dougherty uthi le nkqubo idale umgama phakathi kweCawa kunye nokumkani omtsha kwaye yenza ukuba amaKatolika aphuhlise ukuqonda okutsha kobudlelwane becawa-norhulumente kunye nomthombo wegunya 

lezopolitiko 
. Yayiyigazethi yokuqala esemthethweni yoBukhosi base-Ottoman, ehlelwe ngu-Alexandre Blacque ngeendleko ze-Sub lime Porte. Igama layo mhlawumbi libhekisela kwiphephandaba laseFransi iLe Moniteur Universel. Yayikhutshwa ngeveki. I-Takvim-i vekayi yapapashwa kwiinyanga ezimbalwa kamva, ngenjongo yokuguqulela i-Moniteur kwi-Ottoman Turkish. Emva kokuba ihlelwe nguConsul wangaphambili waseDenmark "M. Franceschi", kwaye kamva ngu "Hassuna de Ghiez", yagqitywa ukuhlelwa nguLucien Rouet. Nangona kunjalo, ijongene nobutshaba boonozakuzaku, yavalwa ngeminyaka yoo-1840. [20] 
I-Satire 
Eli candelo alichazi nayiphi na imithombo. Nceda uncede ukuphucula eli candelo ngokongeza izicatshulwa kwimithombo ethembekileyo. Izixhobo ezingasetyenziswanga zinokucelwa umngeni kwaye zisuswe. (NgoJanuwari 2025) (Funda indlela kwaye nini ukususa lo myalezo) 
Iimagazini zeSatirical zaseTurkey zinesithethe eside. Enye yeemagazini zokuqala ze-satirical yayiyi-Diyojen eyasungulwa ngo-1869. Kukho malunga ne-20 yeemagazini ezihlekisayo; ezona ziphambili yiPenguen (isasazwa ngama-70,000 ngeveki), iLeMan (50,000) ne-Uykusuz. Imizekelo yembali iquka iphephabhuku lika-Oğuz Aral elithi Gırgır (eyafikelela kujikelezo lwe-500,000 kwiminyaka yoo-1970) kunye noMarko Paşa (eyasungulwa ngo-1946). Abanye baquka uL-Manyak kunye neLombak. 
EUnited States 
Ulwazi olongezelelekileyo: Imbali yobuntatheli baseMelika kunye nemidiya yoluntu kunye nezopolitiko zaseMelika 
iColonial America


 
[icon]
Eli candelo lifuna ukwandiswa: Inkcazo yesifundiswa yesi sihloko secandelwana, ephuma kwimithombo yolwazi ukongeza kumthombo wefashoni weVogue ovelayo. Unokunceda ngokongeza kuyo. (NgoJanuwari 2025) 
Ukupapasha yayilishishini elibiza kakhulu ngamaxesha olawulo lwamathanga. Iphepha kunye ne-inki yomshicileli zazirhafiswa kwimpahla ethunyelwa ngaphandle kwaye umgangatho wazo wawungangqinelani. Uluhlu lwamaxabiso aphakathi kwamazwe kunye nenkqubo yendlela engekho mgangathweni ithintele usasazo, nokuba kumlinganiselo wommandla. Kwaqaliswa amaphephancwadi amaninzi, amaninzi esilela kwiintlelo ezimbalwa, kodwa abavakalisi baqhubeka bezama. Kuthiwa uBenjamin Franklin waba nombono wenye yeemagazini zokuqala zamathanga aseMerika ngowe-1741, iGeneral Magazine kunye neHistorical Chronicle. I-Pennsylvania Magazine, ehlelwe nguThomas Paine, yahamba nje ixesha elifutshane kodwa yayiyimpapasho enempembelelo kakhulu ngexesha leMfazwe yeNguquko. Inkupho yokugqibela equlethe umbhalo weSibhengezo seNkululeko yapapashwa ngowe-1776.[21][umthombo obhetele ofunekayo] 

Ngasekupheleni kwenkulungwane ye-19 
Phakathi kwinkulungwane ye-19, amaphephancwadi aphuma kanye ngenyanga afumana ukuthandwa. Zazingumdla ngokubanzi ukuqalisa, ziqulethe ezinye iindaba, ii<em>vignettes, imibongo, imbali, iziganeko zobupolitika, neengxoxo zasentlalweni.[22][iphepha elifunekayo] Ngokungafaniyo namaphephandaba, yayingaphezulu kwengxelo yenyanga yeziganeko zangoku kunye namabali okonwabisayo, imibongo nemifanekiso. Amaphepha-ncwadi okuqala aphuma kwiindaba ayeyiHarper kunye neAtlantiki, egxile ekukhuthazeni ubugcisa. [23] [iphepha elifunekayo] Zombini iHarper kunye neAtlantiki zisaqhubeka unanamhla, kunye noHarper's imagazini yenkcubeko kunye neAtlantiki egxile kakhulu kwiziganeko zehlabathi. Upapasho lwangaphambili lukaHarper lude lwabamba imisebenzi edumileyo njengopapasho lokuqala lukaMoby Dick okanye iziganeko ezidumileyo ezinjengokubekwa kwentambo yocingo yokuqala yehlabathi yokuwela iAtlantiki; kunjalo, isininzi isiqulatho ekuqaleni kwaba trickle phantsi iziganeko British.[24] 

Ukuphuhliswa kwamaphephancwadi kwavuselela ukwanda kokugxekwa koncwadi kunye neengxoxo zezopolitiko, ukuya kwiingqungquthela ezingaphezulu kweengcamango ezivela kumaphephandaba anenjongo. [23] [iphepha elifunekayo] Ixesha elongezelelweyo phakathi koshicilelo kunye nenani elikhulu lesithuba sokubhala libonelele iqonga leengxoxo zoluntu ngabaphengululi kunye nabakhi-mkhanyo abagxekayo 

. yaba yincutshe ngakumbi 

kwaye ingxoxo ngokubanzi okanye iincwadana zenkcubeko ziye zanyanzeliswa ukuba ziqhelane nemarike yabathengi eyayilangazelela ukuhanjiswa kwemicimbi kunye neziganeko zasekuhlaleni 

. IiOlimpiki zasehlotyeni. 
Ulwazi oluthe vetshe: iMuckrakers kunye neMisa yeendaba kunye nezopolitiko zaseMelika
Amaphephancwadi asasazwa ngobuninzi axhaphaka ngakumbi emva kowe-1900, amanye ayesasazwa ngamakhulu amawaka abantu abarhumelayo. Abanye baphumelele isigidi-mark kwi-1920s. Yayilixesha lemithombo yeendaba. Ngenxa yokwanda okukhawulezayo kweentengiso zelizwe, ixabiso le-inshorensi lehla kakhulu laya kutsho malunga neesenti ezili-10.[26] Omnye unobangela yayikukubhengezwa kakhulu korhwaphilizo kwezopolitiko, oorhulumente basekhaya kunye namashishini amakhulu, ngakumbi ngabakwaMuckrakers. Babeziintatheli ezazibhalela amaphephancwadi adumileyo ukuba abhence izono neentsilelo zentlalo nezopolitiko. Bathembele kwingxelo yabo yobuntatheli obuphandayo; abarhwaphilizi bebesoloko besebenzela ukubhenca ububi bentlalo kunye norhwaphilizo lweshishini nezopolitiko. Iimagazini ze-Muckraking-ngokukodwa i-McClure's-ithathe i-monopolies yenkampani kunye noomatshini bezopolitiko abagwenxa ngelixa bephakamisa ulwazi loluntu ngentlupheko engapheliyo yasezidolophini, iimeko zokusebenza ezingakhuselekanga, kunye nemiba yentlalontle efana nokuqeshwa kwabantwana 

. Abanye, kuquka uLincoln Steffens, babhenca ukunganyaniseki kwezobupolitika kwizixeko ezininzi ezikhulu; U-Ida Tarbell wahamba emva kweNkampani ye-Oli ye-John D. Rockefeller. USamuel Hopkins Adams ngo-1905 wabonisa ubuqhophololo obubandakanyekayo kumayeza amaninzi elungelo elilodwa lomenzi wechiza, inoveli ka-Upton Sinclair ka-1906 ethi The Jungle yanika umfanekiso owoyikekayo wendlela eyayipakishwe ngayo inyama, kwaye, nango-1906, uDavid Graham Phillips wakhupha isimangalo esibuhlungu seNdlu yeeNgwevu zase-US. Roosevelt 

wanika ezi ntatheli isiqhulo sazo xa wayekhalazela ukuba abancedi nganto 
ngokuqokelela 

bonke 
ubumdaka 
. I-Statista, ukuvalwa kweemagazini kuye kwaqalwa ngenani kuneziphehlelelo kuMntla Melika ngo-2009. Nangona omabini amanani ehlile ngo-2010-2015, iqalise ngokuvalwa okungaphezulu kwenani ngalinye kuloo minyaka, ngamanye amaxesha ngomlinganiselo we-3:1.[30] Ukugxininisa ngakumbi, iMediaFinder.com yafumanisa ukuba iimagazini ezintsha ze-93 zaqaliswa kwiinyanga ezintandathu zokuqala ze-2014, ngelixa i-30 kuphela ivaliwe ngelo xesha. Udidi oluvelise upapasho olutsha kakhulu "Umdla weNgingqi", apho kwaqaliswa iimagazini ezintandathu ezintsha, kubandakanywa i-12th & Broad kunye neCraft Beer & Brewing. Johnson Publishing kaThixo Jet wayeka ushicilelo imiba rhoqo, ukwenza utshintsho kwifomathi yedijithali, nangona nangoku ushicilelo edition yonyaka.[32] Ijenali yeLadies' Home iye yamisa ucwangciso lwabo lwenyanga nokuhanjiswa kwekhaya ukuze abarhumi babe lupapasho olunomdla olukhethekileyo lwekota kuphela.[33]


Ngokwezibalo ukusuka ekupheleni kuka-2013, amanqanaba okubhalisela ama-22 aphezulu kwiimagazini ze-25 zehla ukusuka kwi-2012 ukuya kwi-2013, kunye nexesha nje, i-Glamour kunye ne-ESPN iMagazine ifumana amanani.[34] Nangona kunjalo, ngo-2024, ezinye izihloko, ngokukodwa iimagazini zangaphandle, zabonakala zikhula ngokuthandwa.[35] 

Iimagazini zabasetyhini 
"Oodade abasixhenxe" bamaphephancwadi aseMerika yiLadies' Home Journal, ukugcinwa kakuhle kweNdlu, uMcCall, uSuku loMfazi, iRedbook, iSangqa soSapho, kunye namaKhaya aNgcono kunye neeGadi. Ezinye iimagazini, phakathi kwazo i-Godey's Lady's Book kunye ne-Harper's Bazaar, zenzelwe kuphela abaphulaphuli ababhinqileyo, begxininisa iindima zesini zenkulungwane ye-19. Ukubandakanywa komxholo we-didactic malunga nokugcinwa kwendlu kusenokuba kwandisa umdla wephephancwadi kubaphulaphuli ababanzi babasetyhini kunye namadoda axhalabileyo malunga nokungabi nanto kwemagazini yefashoni.[21][ukuqinisekiswa okufunekayo] 

Iintlobo 
Kukho iintlobo ezininzi zeemagazini. Ngelixa ezinye zero kwizihloko ezinje ngeejenali zorhwebo ze-niche, uphando oluphambili, okanye iimagi zabasetyhini, ezinye zibandakanya izihloko ezifana nenkolo kunye nenkcubeko yepop. Oku kunokubandakanya ukuhlekisa okumnandi, ukugxeka okufileyo, okanye ukuhleka okuhlekisayo. 

Iindidi 
[umfanekiso] 
Eli candelo lifuna ukwandiswa ngolu hlobo: nokwahlulwa kweendidi ezidityanisiweyo zabaphulaphuli kunye nesihloko, kunye nokukhangela okunye kunye nemizekelo njengoko kufuneka, kwicandelwana ngalinye. Unokunceda ngokongeza kuyo. (Janyuwari 2025) 
Ngokusekelwe kumaxesha athile 
iiMagazini zidla ngokuhlelwa ngokweendlela zokupapashwa kwazo (oko kukuthi, ngeeveki, ngeenyanga, ngeekota, njalo njalo).[38] 

Ngokusekwe kubaphulaphuli ekujoliswe kubo kunye nesihloko 
sefashoni yabasetyhini 
Imagazini yokuqala yabasetyhini ejolise kubafazi noomama yapapashwa ngo-1852. [39] Ngeminyaka yoo-1920, iimagazini ezintsha zabhenela kubafazi abancinci baseJamani abanomfanekiso ovuselelayo kunye nezibhengezo zempahla efanelekileyo kunye nezixhobo abanokuthi bafune ukuzithenga. Amaphepha acwebezelayo e-Die Dame kunye no-Das Blatt der Hausfrau abonise i-"Neue Frauen", "Intombazana Entsha" - oko abantu baseMelika bakubiza ngokuba yi-flapper. Eli bhinqa liselula lifanelekileyo lalilungile, lizimele ngokwezimali, kwaye lithanda ukuthenga iifashoni zamva nje. Iimagazini zamgcina esazi ngefashoni, ubugcisa, imidlalo, nobugcisa bezi mini obunjengeemoto neemfonomfono.[40] 

Ukuba Ngumzali 
Amanye amaphephancwadi amabhinqa aye anempembelelo kwiimbono zobunina nokukhulisa abantwana ngokusebenzisa imihlathi yamacebiso, izibhengezo namanqaku aphathelele ukukhulisa abantwana.[41] Iimagazini zabasetyhini ezithengiswe ngobuninzi ziye zabumba kwaye zaguqula iinqobo zenkcubeko ezinxulumene nezenzo zobuzali. Ngaloo ndlela, iimagazini ezijolise kumabhinqa nokuba ngumzali ziye zasebenzisa amandla nempembelelo kwiingcamango malunga nokuba ngumama nokukhulisa umntwana.[41] 

Unqulo
Amaphephancwadi onqulo anembali ende neyahlukahlukeneyo. EUnited States, amaphephancwadi onqulo aphakathi kwamaphephancwadi okuqala aphumayo, yaye umxholo wawo wanceda ekuxonxeni ukufunda nokubhala, imilinganiselo yokuziphatha neziganeko zobupolitika zeRiphabliki yamandulo. Kodwa kule minyaka ili-150 idluleyo, impembelelo yawo iye yehla.[42] 

Intlebendwane yabantu abadumileyo, umdla wabantu 
Iimagazini ezipapasha amabali kunye neefoto zabantu abakumgangatho ophezulu kunye nosaziwayo kudala iyifomathi ethandwayo eUnited States. [43] Ngo-2019, i-People Magazine ibekwe kwindawo yesibini emva kwe-ESPN Magazine ngokufikelela kuyo yonke i-98.51 yezigidi. 

Ubuchwephesha 

Umzekelo wemagazini yobuchwephesha luSasazo, olujoliswe kubafundi abakwishishini losasazo lukanomathotholo nomabonakude eUnited Kingdom 
Iimagazini zobuchwephesha, ezikwabizwa ngokuba ziimagazini zorhwebo, okanye iimagazini zeshishini ukuya kwishishini zijoliswe kubafundi abaqeshwe kumashishini athile. Ezi magazini zikholisa ukugubungela iintsingiselo zeshishini kunye neendaba ezinomdla kwiingcali zolu shishino. Imirhumo idla ngokuza nobulungu kumbutho weengcali. Iimagazini zobuchwephesha zinokufumana ingeniso kwiintengiso okanye kwiintengiso zeenkampani ezithengisa iimveliso kunye neenkonzo kubaphulaphuli abathile abaziingcali. Imizekelo ibandakanya uBudala beNtengiso, iiNdaba zeMoto, uSasazo, uMthengisi weencwadi, kunye neNqanaba.[45][46][47][48][49] 

Ngokusekwe kwithoni okanye kwindlela yokuthetha 
Iimagazini zinokuhlelwa ngokwethoni yazo okanye ngokwendlela ezithetha ngayo, umz., njengakwimisebenzi yamaxesha athile ephoxayo okanye ehlekisayo. 

Imidiya yoluntu bubuchwepheshe beendaba obutsha obuququzelela ukuyilwa, ukwabelana kunye nokudityaniswa komxholo (ofana neengcinga, umdla, kunye nezinye iindlela zokuthetha) phakathi koluntu olubonakalayo kunye nothungelwano.[1][2] Iimpawu eziqhelekileyo zibandakanya: [2] 

Amaqonga e-Intanethi enza abasebenzisi benze kwaye babelane ngomxholo kwaye bathathe inxaxheba kwinethiwekhi yoluntu. [2] [3] [4] 
Umxholo owenziwe ngumsebenzisi-njengokubhaliweyo okanye izimvo, iifoto zedijithali okanye iividiyo, kunye nedatha eyenziwe ngonxibelelwano lwe-intanethi.[2][3] 
Iiprofayili ezikhethekileyo zenkonzo eziyilwe kwaye zigcinwe ngumbutho wemidiya yoluntu.[2][5] 
Imidiya yoluntu inceda uphuhliso lweintanethi zoluntu ngokudibanisa iprofayile yomsebenzisi nezo zabanye abantu okanye amaqela.[2][5] 
Igama elithi intlalo ngokumalunga nemithombo yeendaba licebisa ukuba amaqonga enze imisebenzi yoluntu. Imidiya yoluntu yongeza kwaye yandisa uthungelwano lwabantu.[6] Abasebenzisi bafikelela kumajelo asekuhlaleni ngokusebenzisa ii-apps ezisekwe kwiwebhu okanye usetyenziso lwesiko kwizixhobo eziphathwayo. La maqonga onxibelelwano avumela abantu, uluntu, amashishini, kunye nemibutho ukuba babelane, benze intsebenziswano, baxoxe, bathathe inxaxheba, kwaye balungise umxholo owenziwe ngumsebenzisi okanye ozilungiselele yena.[7][5][1] Imidiya yoluntu isetyenziselwa ukubhala iinkumbulo, ukufunda, nokwenza ubuhlobo.[8] Zisenokusetyenziswa ukukhuthaza abantu, iinkampani, iimveliso neembono.[8] Imidiya yoluntu ingasetyenziselwa ukutya, ukupapasha, okanye ukwabelana ngeendaba.

Iiplatifti zeendaba zoluntu zingahlelwa ngokusekelwe kumsebenzi wabo oyintloko. 

Iisayithi zenethiwekhi zoluntu ezifana ne-Facebook kunye ne-LinkedIn zigxile ekwakheni uqhagamshelwano lomntu kunye nobugcisa. 
Iiplatifomu ze-Microblogging, ezifana ne-Twitter (ngoku i-X), i-Threads kunye ne-Mastodon, igxininisa umxholo omfutshane kunye nokwabelana ngolwazi olukhawulezayo. 
Inethiwekhi yokwabelana ngemidiya, kubandakanya i-Instagram, iTikTok, iYouTube, kunye ne-Snapchat, ivumela abasebenzisi ukuba babelane ngemifanekiso, iividiyo kunye nemijelo ephilayo. 
Ingxoxo kunye neeforam zoluntu ezifana ne-Reddit, i-Quora, kunye ne-Discord ziququzelela iincoko, i-Q&A, kunye nokuzibandakanya koluntu. 
Amaqonga okusasaza ebukhoma, anje ngeTwitch, iFacebook Live, kunye neYouTube Live, yenza intsebenziswano yabaphulaphuli ngexesha lokwenyani. 
Iiplatifti zeendaba zoluntu ezifana neMastodon kunye neBluesky zijolise ekuboneleleni ngenethiwekhi yoluntu ngaphandle kokulawulwa kwenkampani, ukunika abasebenzisi ukuzimela ngakumbi kwidatha yabo kunye nokusebenzisana. 
Amaqonga eendaba ezentlalo adumileyo anabasebenzisi ababhalisiweyo abangaphezu kwezigidi ezili-100 babandakanya i-Twitter, i-Facebook, i-WeChat, i-ShareChat, i-Instagram, i-Pinterest, i-QZone, i-Weibo, i-VK, i-Tumblr, i-Baidu Tieba, i-Treads kunye ne-LinkedIn. Kuxhomekeke ekutolikweni, amanye amaqonga adumileyo adla ngokubizwa ngokuba ziinkonzo zosasazo zoluntu zibandakanya iYouTube, Letterboxd, QQ, Quora, Telegraph, WhatsApp, Signal, LINE, Snapchat, Viber, Reddit, Discord, kunye neTikTok. I-Wikis yimizekelo yokudala umxholo wentsebenziswano. 

Amajelo osasazo oluntu ahlukile kumajelo eendaba amadala (umzekelo, amaphephandaba, iTV, nosasazo lukanomathotholo) ngeendlela ezininzi, kuquka nomgangatho,[9] ukufikelela, ukuphindaphindeka, ukusebenziseka, ukufaneleka, kunye nokuba sisigxina.[10] Amajelo eendaba ezentlalo asebenza kwi-dialogic transmission system (imithombo emininzi kubantu abaninzi abafumanayo) ngelixa imidiya yemveli isebenza phantsi kwemodeli yokuhanjiswa kwe-monologic (umthombo omnye kubamkeli abaninzi). Ngokomzekelo, iphephandaba lisiwa kubantu abaninzi abarhumelayo, yaye isikhululo sikanomathotholo sisasaza iinkqubo ezifanayo kwisixeko.[11] 

Amajelo eendaba ezentlalo agxekwa ngoluhlu lweempembelelo ezingalunganga ebantwaneni nakulutsha, kubandakanywa ukuchanabeka kumxholo ongafanelekanga, ukuxhatshazwa ngabantu abadala, iingxaki zokulala, iingxaki zokuhoya, iimvakalelo zokungabandakanywa, kunye nezigulo ezahlukeneyo zempilo yengqondo.[12][13] Amajelo osasazo ezentlalo nawo afumene ukugxekwa njengokwanda kocalucalulo kwezopolitiko kunye nokujongela phantsi idemokhrasi. Imithombo yeendaba ezinkulu zihlala zinolawulo oluluqilima kwindawo yokuphepha kunye nokulungisa amabango obuxoki, kodwa iimpawu ezikhethekileyo zeendaba zoluntu zizisa umxholo wentsholongwane kunye nokungahoywa okuncinci. "Ii-algorithms ezilandelela ukubandakanyeka komsebenzisi ukubeka phambili oko kubonisiwe kuthanda ukuthanda umxholo ovuselela iimvakalelo ezingalunganga njengomsindo kunye nomsindo. Ngokubanzi, ulwazi oluninzi olungeyonyani lwe-intanethi luvela kwigcuntswana elincinci "labagqwesileyo," kodwa imidiya yoluntu ikhulisa ukufikelela kunye nefuthe 

labo 
. 
.
Inkqubo ye-PLATO yasungulwa kwi-1960 kwiYunivesithi yase-Illinois kwaye emva koko ithengiswa ngokurhweba yi-Control Data Corporation. Inike iifom zangaphambili zeempawu zemidiya yoluntu kunye nezinto ezintsha ezifana namanqaku, isicelo seforum ye-PLATO yomyalezo; I-TERM-intetho, uphawu lwayo lomyalezo okhawulezileyo; I-Talkomatic, mhlawumbi igumbi lokuqala lokuncokola kwi-intanethi; Ingxelo yeendaba, iphephandaba le-intanethi elixutywe ngabantu, kunye neblogi kunye noLuhlu lokuFikelela, okwenza umnini wefayile yenqaku okanye esinye isicelo ukuba anciphise ukufikelela kwisethi ethile yabasebenzisi, umzekelo, abahlobo kuphela, abafundi ofunda nabo, okanye osebenza nabo. 

I-ARPANET, eyafika kwi-intanethi ngo-1969, yaba ngasekupheleni kweminyaka yee-1970 yavumela ukutshintshiselana ngeengcamango ezingekho phantsi kukarhulumente / ishishini kunye nonxibelelwano, njengoko kungqinwa yi-network etiquette (okanye "i-netiquette") echazwe kwincwadi ye-1982 kwi-computing kwi-MIT's Artificial Intelligence Laboratory. [15] I-ARPANET yavela kwi-Intanethi ngeminyaka yoo-1990. [16] U-Usenet, owakhawulwa nguTom Truscott noJim Ellis ngo-1979 kwiYunivesithi yaseNorth Carolina e-Chapel Hill kunye neYunivesithi yaseDuke, yayiyi-app yokuqala ye-social media app, eyasungulwa ngo-1980 


. umbuzo 
I-precursor ye-electronic bulletin board system (BBS), eyaziwa ngokuba yi-Community Memory, yavela ngo-1973. I-BBSs eyi-Mainstream yafika kunye ne-Computer Bulletin Board System e-Chicago, eyasungulwa ngoFebruwari 16, 1978. Kungekudala, izixeko ezininzi zase-US zine-BBS engaphezu kweyodwa, esebenza kwi-TRS-80, i-Apple II, i-PC ye-Atari, i-8 ye-PC, i-Comsmodo I-8 Sinclair, nabanye. ICompuServe, iProdigy, kunye ne-AOL yayiziinkampani ezintathu ezinkulu ze-BBS kwaye yayingabokuqala ukufudukela kwi-Intanethi ngo-1990. Phakathi kwiminyaka yee-1980 naphakathi kwiminyaka yee-1990, ii-BBS zazibalelwa kumashumi amawaka kuMntla Merika kuphela.[17] Iiforum zemiyalezo ibiyinto ye-BBS yotyikityo kuyo yonke iminyaka yoo-1980 nasekuqaleni koo-1990. 

Kwi-1991, u-Tim Berners-Lee udibanise isoftware ye-HTML hypertext kunye ne-Intanethi, edala iWebhu ebanzi yehlabathi. Le mpumelelo ikhokelele kugqabhuko-dubulo lweeblogi, iiseva zoluhlu, kunye neenkonzo ze-imeyile. Iiforam zemiyalezo ziye zafudukela kwiwebhu, zaza zaguqukela kwiiforam ze-Intanethi, zixhaswa lufikelelo oluphantsi kunye nokukwazi ukuphatha abantu abaninzi kakhulu ngaxeshanye. 

Ezi nkqubo zokuqala ezisekwe kwiteksti zanda ukuze zibandakanye imifanekiso kunye nevidiyo kwinkulungwane yama-21, zincediswa ziikhamera zedijithali kunye neefowuni zekhamera.[18] 

Amaqonga eendaba ezentlalo 

i-SixDegrees, eyasungulwa ngo-1997, ihlala ithathwa njengendawo yokuqala yeendaba zoluntu. 
Ukuvela kweenkonzo ze-intanethi zaqhubela phambili ukusuka ekusebenzeni njengamatshaneli onxibelelwano lothungelwano ukuya ekubeni ngamaqonga onxibelelwano onxibelelwano loluntu ngokufika kweWeb 2.0.[6]

Imidiya yoluntu yaqala phakathi kwiminyaka yoo-1990 ngokuyilwa kwamaqonga afana neGeoCities, Classmates.com, kunye neSixDegrees.com.[19] Ngelixa umyalezo okhawulezileyo kunye nabathengi bencoko babekho ngelo xesha, i-SixDegrees yayikhethekile njengoko yayiyinkonzo yokuqala ye-intanethi eyilelwe ukuba abantu baqhagamshelane besebenzisa amagama abo okwenene endaweni yokungaziwa. Iqhayise ngeempawu ezinje ngeeprofayili, uluhlu lwabahlobo, kunye nobudlelwane besikolo, nto leyo eyenza ukuba ibe "yeyona ndawo yokuqala yenethiwekhi yoluntu".[19][20] Igama leqonga liphenjelelwe yingcamango "yokuhlukana kwamaqondo amathandathu", nto leyo ebonisa ukuba wonke umntu okwiplanethi uqhagamshelwe nje ezintandathu kude kuye wonke umntu.[21] 

Ekuqaleni koo-2000, amaqonga eendaba ezentlalo afumana ukuthandwa ngokubanzi ngeBlackPlanet (1999) eyandulela i-Friendster kunye neMyspace, [22][23] ilandelwa nguFacebook, YouTube, kunye ne-Twitter.[24] 

Uphando olusuka ku-2015 luxele ukuba kwihlabathi jikelele, abasebenzisi bachithe i-22% yexesha labo kwi-intanethi kwiintanethi zentlalo, [25] kusenokwenzeka ukuba bakhuthazwa kubukho bee-smartphones.[26] Ukusukela ngo-2023, abantu abamalunga ne-4.76 yeebhiliyoni basebenzise imidiya yoluntu[27] malunga nama-59% abantu behlabathi. 

Inkcazo 
Uphononongo luka-2015 luchonge iimpawu ezine ezikhethekileyo kwiinkonzo zemidiya yoluntu: [2] 

I-Web 2.0 yezicelo ezisekelwe kwi-Intanethi. [2] [3] 
Umxholo owenziwe ngumsebenzisi[2][3] 
Iiprofayile ezenzelwe ngumsebenzisi[2][5] 
Uthungelwano loluntu olwenziwe luqhakamshelwano phakathi kweeprofayile,[2][5] njengabalandeli, amaqela, kunye noluhlu. 
Ngo-2019, uMerriam-Webster wachaza amajelo eendaba ezentlalo “njengeendlela zonxibelelwano lwe-elektroniki (ezifana neewebhusayithi zenethiwekhi yoluntu kunye ne-microblogging) apho abasebenzisi benza khona uluntu olukwi-intanethi ukuze babelane ngolwazi, izimvo, imiyalezo yobuqu, kunye neminye imixholo (efana neevidiyo).
